tathā śatasahasrāṇi catvāriṃśacca pañca ca।
ahorātrātpataṅgasya gatireṣā vidhīyate ॥ 1.50.122 ॥
dakṣiṇādvinivṛtto'sau viṣuvastho yadā raviḥ।
kṣīrodasya samudrasya uttarāntā diśaścaran ॥ 1.50.123 ॥
maṇḍalaṃ viṣuvadyāpi yojanaistannibodhata।
tathā śatasahasrāṇāmaśītyekādhikā punaḥ ।
śravaṇe cottarāṃ kāṣṭāñcitrabhānuryadā bhavet ।
śākadvīpasya ṣaṣṭhasya uttarāntā diśaścaran ॥ 1.50.125 ॥
uttarāyāñca kāṣṭāyāṃ pramāṇaṃ maṇ‍ḍalasya ca।
yojanāgrātprasaṅkhyātā koṭirekā tu sā dvijaiḥ ॥ 1.50.126 ॥
aśītirniyutānīha yojanānāṃ tathaiva ca।
aṣṭapañcāśatañcaiva yojanānyadhikāni tu ॥ 1.50.127 ॥
nāgavīthyuttarāvīthī ajavīthī ca dakṣiṇā।
mūlaṃ caiva tathāṣāḍe hyajavīthyudayāstrayaḥ।
kāṣṭhayorantaraṃ yacca tadvakṣye yojanaiḥ punaḥ।
etacchatasahasrāṇāmekatriṃśottaraṃ śatam ॥ 1.50.129 ॥
trayastriṃśādhikāścānye trayastriṃśacca yojanaiḥ।
kāṣṭhayorantaraṃ hyetadyojanāgrāt pratiṣṭitam ॥ 1.50.130 ॥
kāṣṭhayorlekhayoścaiva antare dakṣiṇottare ।
te tu vakṣyāmi saṅkhyāya yojanaistannibodhata ॥ 1.50.131 ॥
ekaikamantarantasyā niyutānyekasaptatiḥ।
sahasrāṇyatiriktāśca tato'nyā pañcasaptatiḥ ॥ 1.50.132 ॥
lekhayoḥ kāṣṭhayoścaiva bāhyābhyantarayoḥ smṛtam।
abhyantarantu paryeti maṇḍalānyuttarāyaṇe ॥ 1.50.133 ॥
bāhyato dakṣiṇe caiva satatantu yathākramam।
maṇḍalānāṃ śataṃ pūrṇamaśītyadhikamuttaram ॥ 1.50.134 ॥
carate dakṣiṇe cāpi tāvadeva vibhāvasuḥ।
pramāṇaṃ maṇḍalasyātha yojanāgrānnibodhata ॥ 1.50.135 ॥
śate dve punarapyanye yojanānāṃ prakīrttite ॥ 1.50.136 ॥
ekaviṃśatibhiścaiva yojanairadhikairhi te।
etatpramāṇamākhyātaṃ yojanairmaṇḍalaṃ hi tat ॥ 1.50.137 ॥
viṣkambho maṇḍalasyaiṣa tiryak sa tu vidhīyate।
pratyahañcarate tāni sūryo vai maṇḍalakramam ॥ 1.50.138 ॥
kulālacakraparyanto yathā śīghraṃ nivarttate।
dakṣiṇe prakrame sūryastathā śīghraṃ nivarttate ॥ 1.50.139 ॥
tasmāt prakṛṣṭāṃ bhūmiñca kālenālpena gacchati।
trayodaśārddhamṛkṣāṇāmahnānucarate raviḥ।
muhūrttaistāvadṛkṣāṇi naktamaṣṭādaśaiścaran ॥ 1.50.141 ॥
kulālacakramadhyastu yathā mandaṃ prasarpati।
tathodagayane sūryaḥ sarpate mandavikramaḥ ॥ 1.50.142 ॥
trayodaśārddhamarddhena ṛkṣāṇāṃ carate raviḥ।
tasmāddīrgheṇa kālena bhūmimilpāṃ nigacchati ॥ 1.50.143 ॥
aṣṭādaśamuhūrttaistu uttarāyaṇapaścimam।
aharbhavati taccāpi carate mandavikramaḥ ॥ 1.50.144 ॥
trayodaśārddhamardhena ṛkṣāṇāñcarate raviḥ।
muhūrttaistāvadṛkṣāṇi naktamaṣṭādaśaiścaran ॥ 1.50.145 ॥
tato mandataraṃ tābhyāñcakraṃ bhramati vai yathā।
mṛtpiṇḍa iva madhyastho dhruvo bhramati vai yathā ॥ 1.50.146 ॥
triṃśanmuhūrttāne vāhurahorātraṃ dhruvo bhraman ।
ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayormadhye bhramate maṇḍalāni saḥ ॥ 1.50.147 ॥
kulālacakranābhistu yathā tatraiva varttate।
dhruvastathā hi vijñeyastatraiva parivarttate ॥ 1.50.148 ॥
ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayormadhye bhramato maṇḍalāni tu।
divā naktañca sūryasya mandā śīghrā ca vai gatiḥ ॥ 1.50.149 ॥
uttare prakrame tvindo rdivā mandā gatiḥ smṛtā।
tathaiva ca punarnaktaṃ śīghrā sūryasya vai gatiḥ ॥ 1.50.150 ॥
dakṣiṇe prakrame caiva divā śīghraṃ vidhīyate ।
gatiḥ sūryasya naktaṃ vai mandā cāpi tathā smṛtā ॥ 1.50.151 ॥
evaṃ gativiśeṣeṇa vibhajan rātryahāni tu।
tathā vicarate mārgaṃ samena viṣameṇa ca ॥ 1.50.152 ॥
lokāloke sthitā ye te lokapālāścaturdiśam।
agastyaścarate teṣāmupariṣṭājjavena tu ।
bhajannasāvahorātramevaṅgativiśeṣaṇaiḥ ॥ 1.50.153 ॥
dakṣiṇe nāgavīthyāyāṃ lokālokasya cottaram।
lokasantārako hyeṣa vaiśvānarapathādbahiḥ ॥ 1.50.154 ॥
pṛṣṭe yāvat prabhā sauhī purastāt samprakāśate।
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi daśorddvantūcchrito giriḥ।
prakāśaścāprakāśaśca sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ ॥ 1.50.156 ॥
nakṣatracandrasūryāśca grahāstārāgaṇaiḥ saha।
abhyantaraṃ prakāśante lokālokasya vai gireḥ ॥ 1.50.157 ॥
etāvāneva lokastu nirālokastvataḥ param।
lokālokantu sandhatte yasmāt sūryaḥ parigraham।
tasmātsandhyeti tāmāhuruṣāvyuṣṭyoryadantaram ।
uṣā rātriḥ smṛtā viprairvyuṣṭiścāpi tvahaḥ smṛtam ॥ 1.50.159 ॥
sūryaṃ hi grasamānānāṃ sandhyākāle hi rakṣasām।
prajāpatiniyogena śāpasteṣāṃ durātmanām ।
akṣayatvañca dehasya prāpitā maraṇaṃ tathā ॥ 1.50.160 ॥
tisraḥ koṭyastu vikhyātā mandehā nāma rākṣasāḥ।
prārthayanti sahasrāṃśumudayanti dine dine।
tāpayanto durātmānaḥ sūryamicchanti khāditum ॥ 1.50.161 ॥
atha sūryasya teṣāñca yuddhamāsīt sudāruṇam।
tato brahmā ca devāśca brāhmaṇāścaiva sattamāḥ।
oṅkārabrahmasaṃyuktaṃ gāyatryā cābhimantritam।
tataḥ punarmahātejā mahādyutiparākramaḥ.
yojanānāṃ saha srāṇi ūrddhvamuttiṣṭhate śatam ॥ 1.50.164 ॥
tataḥ prayāti bhagavān brāhmaṇaiḥ parivāritaḥ।
vālakhilyaiśca munibhiḥ kṛtārthaiḥ samarīcibhiḥ ॥ 1.50.165 ॥
kāṣṭā nimeṣā daśa pañca caiva triṃśacca kāṣṭā gaṇayet kalāntam ।
triṃśat kalāścaiva bhavenmuhūrttastaistriṃśatā rātryahanī samete ॥ 1.50.166 ॥
hrāsavṛddhī tvaharbhāgairdivasānāṃ yathākramam।
sandhyā muhūrtamānantu hrāse vṛddhau samā smṛtā ॥ 1.50.167 ॥
lekhāprabhṛtyathāditye trimuhūrttāgate tu vai।
prātastanaḥ smṛtaḥ kālo bhāgastvahnaḥ sa pañcamaḥ ॥ 1.50.168 ॥
tasmāt prātastanātkālāt trimuhūrttastu saṅgavaḥ।
madhyāhnastrimuhūrttastu tasmātkālācca saṅgavāt ॥ 1.50.169 ॥
tasmānmadhyandināt kālādaparāhna iti smṛtaḥ ।
aparāhne vyatīpāte kāla- sāyāhna ucyate।
daśapañcamuhūrttādvai muhūrttāstraya eva ca ॥ 1.50.171 ॥
daśapañcamuhūrttaṃ vai aharviṣuvati smṛtam।
vardhdhate hrasate caiva ayane dakṣiṇottare।
ahastu grasate rātriṃ rātristu grasate tvahaḥ ॥ 1.50.173 ॥
śaradvasantayormadhye viṣuvantadvibhāvyate।
ahorātraṃ kalāścaiva sapta somaḥ samaśrute ॥ 1.50.174 ॥
tathā pañcadaśāhāni pakṣa ityābhidhīyate।
dvau pakṣau ca bhavenmāso dvau māsāvantarāvṛtuḥ।
kalāyāstriṃśataḥ kāṣṭā mātrāghītidvayātmikā ॥ 1.50.176 ॥
dviṣaṣṭibhāk trayoviṃśanmātrāyāñca calā bhavet ॥ 1.50.177 ॥
catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi śatānyaṣṭau ca vidyutiḥ।
saptatiñcāpi tatraiva navatiṃ viddhi nisvaye ॥ 1.50.178 ॥
carāṃśo hyeṣa vijñeyo nālikā cātra kāraṇam ॥ 1.50.179 ॥
saṃvatsarādayaḥ pañca caturmānavikalpitāḥ।
niścayaḥ sarvakālasya yuga ityabhidhīyate ॥ 1.50.180 ॥
saṃvatsarastu prathamo dvitīyaḥ parivatsaraḥ।
idvatsarastṛtīyastu caturthaścānuvatsaraḥ।
pañcamo vatsarasteṣāṃ kālastu parisaṃjñitaḥ ॥ 1.50.181 ॥
viṃśaśataṃ bhavetpūrṇaṃ parvaṇāṃ tu raveryugam।
etānyaṣṭādaśastriṃśadudayo bhāskarasya ca ॥ 1.50.182 ॥
ṛtavastriṃśataḥ saurā ayanāni daśaiva tu।
pañcatriṃśat śataṃ cāpi ṣaṣṭirmāsāśca bhāskaraḥ ॥ 1.50.183 ॥
triṃśadeva tvahorātraṃ sa tu māsaśca bhāskaraḥ।
ekaṣaṣṭistvahorātrā danureko nibhāvyate ॥ 1.50.184 ॥
ahnāntu tryadhikāśītiḥ śataṃ cāpyadhikaṃ bhavet।
mānaṃ taccitrabhānostu vijñeyaṃ bhuvanasya tu ॥ 1.50.185 ॥
saurasaumyaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ nakṣatraṃ sāvanaṃ tathā।
khe tasyottarataścaiva śrṛṅgavānnāma parvataḥ।
trīṇi tasya tu śrṛṅgāṇi spṛśantīva nabhastalam ॥ 1.50.187 ॥
tasya vai sarvataḥ śrṛṅgaṃ madhyamantaddhiraṇmayam।
dakṣiṇaṃ rājatañcaiva śrṛṅgaṃ tu sphaṭikaprabham ॥ 1.50.189 ॥
sarvaratnamayaṃ caikaṃ śrṛṅgamuttaramuttamam।
evaṃ kūṭaisribhiḥ śailaiḥ śrṛṅgavāniti viśrutaḥ ॥ 1.50.190 ॥
yattadviṣuvataṃ śrṛṅgantadarkaḥ pratipadyate।
śaradvasantayormadhye madhyamāṃ gatimāsthitaḥ।
ahastulyāmatho rātriṃ karoti timirāpahaḥ ॥ 1.50.191 ॥
haritāśca hayā divyāste niyuktā mahārathe।
anuliptā ivābhānti pajharaktairgabhastibhiḥ ॥ 1.50.192 ॥
meṣānte ca tulānte ca bhāskarodayataḥ smṛtāḥ ।
muhūrttā daśa pañcaiva ahorātriśca tāvatī ॥ 1.50.193 ॥
kṛttikānāṃ yadā sūryaḥ prathamāṃśagato bhavet ।
viśākhānāṃ tathā jñeyaścaturthāṃśe niśākaraḥ॥ 1.50.194 ॥
viśākhāyāṃ yadā sūrya ścrateṃ'śaṃ tṛtīyakam।
tadā candraṃ vijānīyāt kṛttikāśirasi sthitam ॥ 1.50.195 ॥
viṣuvantaṃ tadā vidyādevamāhurmaharṣayaḥ।
sūryeṇa viṣuvaṃ vidyāt kālaṃ somena lakṣayet ॥ 1.50.196 ॥
samā rātrirahaścaiva yadā tadviṣuvadbhavet।
tadā dānāni deyāni pitṛbhyo viṣuvatyapi।
brāhmaṇebhyo viśeṣeṇa mukhametattu daivatam ॥ 1.50.197 ॥
ūnarātrādhimāsau ca kalākāṣṭāmuhūrttakāḥ।
paurṇamāsī tathā jñeyā amāvāsyā tathaiva ca।
sinīvālī kuhūścaiva rākā cānumati stathā ॥ 1.50.198 ॥
tapastapasyau madhumādhavau ca śukraḥ śuciścāyanamuttaraṃ syāt।
nabho nabhaśyo'tha iṣuḥ sahorjaḥ sahaḥsahasyāviti dakṣiṇaṃ syāt ॥ 1.50.199 ॥
tasmāttu ṛtavo jñeyā ṛtavo hyantarāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 1.50.200 ॥
tasmādanumukhā jñeyā amāvāsyāsya parvaṇaḥ.
tasmāttu viṣuvaṃ jñeyaṃ pitṛdaivahitaṃ sadā ॥ 1.50.201 ॥
tasmāt smṛtaṃ prajānāṃ vai viṣuvatsarvagaṃ sadā ॥ 1.50.202 ॥
lokapālāḥ sthitāstatra lokālokasya madhyataḥ ॥ 1.50.203 ॥
catvāraste mahātmānastiṣṭhantyābhūtasamplavāt।
sudhāmā caiva vairājaḥ karddamaḥ śaṅ‌kṛpastathā।
hiraṇyalomā parjjanyaḥ ketumān jātaniścayaḥ ॥ 1.50.204 ॥
nirdvandvā nirabhīmānā nistantrā niṣparigrahāḥ।
lokapālāḥ sthitā hyete lokāloke caturdiśam ॥ 1.50.205 ॥
uttaraṃ yadagastyasya ajavīthyāśca dakṣiṇam।
pitṛyāṇaḥ sa vai panthā vaiśvānarapathādbahiḥ ॥ 1.50.206 ॥
tatrāsate prajāvanto munayo hyagnihotriṇaḥ ।
lokasya santānakarāḥ pitṛyāṇe pathi sthitāḥ ॥ 1.50.207 ॥
bhūtārambha kṛtaṃ karma āśiṣā ṛtvigucyate ।
prārabhante lokakāmāsteṣāṃ panthāḥ sa dakṣiṇaḥ ॥ 1.50.208 ॥
calitante punarddharmaṃ sthāpayanti yuge yuge।
santatyā tapasā caiva maryādābhiḥ śrutena ca ॥ 1.50.209 ॥
jāyamānāstu pūrve vai paścimānāṃ gṛheṣu ca।
eva māvarttamānāste tiṣṭhantyābhūtasamplavāt ॥ 1.50.210 ॥
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi munīnāṃ gṛhamedhinām।
saviturddakṣiṇaṃ mārgaṃ śritā hyācandratārakam।
kriyāvatāṃ prasaṅkhyeyā ye śmaśānāni bhejire ॥ 1.50.211 ॥
lokaśaṃvyavahāreṇa bhūtārambhakṛtena ca।
icchādveṣaprakṛtyā ca maithunopagamena ca ॥ 1.50.212 ॥
tathā kāyakṛteneha sevanādviṣayasya ca।
etaistaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ siddhāḥ śmaśānāni hi bhejire।
prajaiṣiṇaste munayo dvāpareṣviha jajñire ॥ 1.50.213 ॥
nāgavīthyuttare yacca saptarṣibhyaśca dakṣiṇam ।
uttaraḥ savituḥ panthā devayānastu sa smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.50.214 ॥
yatra te vāsinaḥ siddhā vimalā brahmacāriṇaḥ।
satatante jugupsante tasmānmṛtyurjjitastu taiḥ ॥ 1.50.215 ॥
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi teṣāmapyūrddhvaretasām।
udakūpanthānamaryamṇaḥ śritā hyābhūtasamplavāt ॥ 1.50.216 ॥
ityetaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ śuddhaiste' matatvaṃ hi bhejire।
ābhūtasamplavasthānamamṛtatvaṃ vibhāvyate ॥ 1.50.217 ॥
trailokyasthitikālo'yamapunarmārgagāminaḥ।
brahmahatyāśvamedhābhyāṃ puṇyāpāpakṛto'param।
ābhūtasamplavānte tu kṣīyante hyūrddhvaretasaḥ ॥ 1.50.218 ॥
ūrddhvottaramṛṣibhyastu dhruvo yatrāsti vai smṛtam।
etadviṣṇupadaṃ divyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ vyomni bhāsvaram ॥ 1.50.219 ॥
tatra gatvā na śocanti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam।
dharmadhruvādyāstiṣṭhanti yatra te lokasādhakāḥ ॥ 1.50.220 ॥
svāyambhuve nisarge tu vyākhyātānyuttarāṇi tu।
bhaviṣyāṇi ca sarvāṇi teṣāṃ vakṣyāmyanukramam ॥ 1.51.1 ॥
etacchrutvā tu munayaḥ papracchurlomaharṣaṇam।
sūryācandramasoścāraṃ grahāṇāñcaiva sarvaśaḥ ॥ 1.51.2 ॥
bhramante kathametāni jyotīṃṣi divi maṇḍalam।
tiryagvyūhena sarvāṇi tathaivāsaṅkareṇa ca।
kaśca bhrāmayate tāni bhramanti yadi vā svayam ॥ 1.51.3 ॥
etadveditumicchāmastanno nigada sattam।
bhūtasammohanaṃ hyetad bruvato me nibodhata।
pratyakṣamapi dṛsyaṃ yattat saṃmohayate prajāḥ ॥ 1.51.5 ॥
yo'sau caturdiśaṃ pucche śiśumāre vyavasthitaḥ।
uttānapādaputro'sau meḍhībhūto dhruvo divi ॥ 1.51.6 ॥
sa hi bhraman bhrāmayate candrādityau grahaiḥ saha।
bhramantamanugacchanti nakṣatrāṇi ca cakravat ॥ 1.51.7 ॥
dhruvasya manasā cāsau sarpate bhagaṇaḥ svayam।
sūryācandramasau tārā nakṣatrāṇi grahaiḥ saha ॥ 1.51.8 ॥
vātānīkamayairbandhairdhruve baddhāni tāni vai।
teṣāṃ yogasva bhedāśca kālacārastathaiva ca ॥ 1.51.9 ॥
astodayau tathotpātā ayane dakṣiṇottare।
viṣuvad‌grahavarṇāśca dhruvātsarvaṃ pravarttate ॥ 1.51.10 ॥
varṣā dharmo himaṃ rātriḥ sandhyā caiva dinaṃ tathā ।
śubhāśubhaṃ prajānāñca dhruvātsarvaṃ pravarttate ॥ 1.51.11 ॥
dhruveṇādhikṛtāṃścaiva sūryo'pāvṛttya tiṣṭhati।
tadeṣa dīptakiraṇaḥ sa kālāgnirddivākaraḥ ॥ 1.51.12 ॥
parivartta kramādviprā bhābhirālokayan diśaḥ।
sūryaḥ kiraṇajālena vāyuyuktena sarvaśaḥ।
jagato jalamādatte kṛtsnasya dvijasattamāḥ ॥ 1.51.13 ॥
nāḍībhirvāyuyuktābhirlokādhānaṃ pravarttate ॥ 1.51.14 ॥
meghā vāyunighātena visṛjanti jalambhuvi ॥ 1.51.15 ॥
ekamutkṣipyate caiva patate ca punarjjalam।
sandhāraṇārthaṃ bhūtānāṃ māyaiṣā viśvanirmitā।
anayā māyayā vyāptaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ॥ 1.51.17 ॥
viśveśo lokakṛddevaḥ sahasrāṃśuḥ prajāpatiḥ।
dhātā kṛtsnasya lokasya prabhu rviṣṇurdivākaraḥ ॥ 1.51.18 ॥
somādhāraṃ jagatsarvametattathyaṃ prakīrtitam ॥ 1.51.19 ॥
sūryāduṣṇaṃ nisravate somācchītaṃ pravarttate।
śītoṣṇavīryau dvāvetau yuktau dhārayato jagat ॥ 1.51.20 ॥
somādhārā nadī gaṅgā pavitrā vimalodakā।
somaputrapurogāśca mahānadyo dvijottamāḥ ॥ 1.51.21 ॥
sarvabhūtaśarīreṣu āpo hyanugatāśca yāḥ ।
teṣu sandahyamāneṣu jaṅgamasthāvareṣu ca।
dhūmabhūtāstu tā āpo niṣkrāmantīha sarvaśaḥ ॥ 1.51.22 ॥
tena cābhrāṇi jāyante sthānamatrāmbhasāṃ smṛtam ।
ārkantejo hi bhūtebhyo hyādatte raśmibhirjalam ॥ 1.51.23 ॥
samudrādvāyusaṃyogādvahantyāpo gabhastayaḥ।
yatastvṛtuvaśāt kāle parivartto divākāraḥ।
yacchatyapo hi meghebyaḥ śuklāḥ śuklagabhastibhiḥ ॥ 1.51.24 ॥
abhrasthā prapatantyāpo vāyunā samudīritāḥ।
sarvabhūtahitārthāya vāyubhiśca samantataḥ ॥ 1.51.25 ॥
tato varṣati ṣaṇmāsān sarvabhūtavivṛddhaye।
vāyavyaṃ stanitañcaiva vaidyutañcāgnisaṃbhavam ॥ 1.51.26 ॥
mehanācca miherddhātormeghatvaṃ vyañjayanti ca।
na bhraśyanti yatastvāpastadabhraṃ kavayo viduḥ ॥ 1.51.27 ॥
meghānāṃ punarutpattistrividhā yonirucyate।
āgneyā brahmajāścaiva pakṣajāśca pṛthagvidhāḥ।
tridhā ghanāḥ samākhyātāsteṣāṃ vakṣyāmi sambhavam ॥ 1.51.28 ॥
āgneyāstvarṇajāḥ proktāsteṣāṃ tasmāt pravarttanam।
śītadurdinavātā ye svaguṇāste vyavasthitāḥ ॥ 1.51.29 ॥
mahiṣāśca varāhāśca mattamātaṅgagāminaḥ।
bhūtvā dharaṇimabhyetya vicaranti ramanti ca ॥ 1.51.30 ॥
jīmūtā nāma te meghā etebyo jīvasambhavāḥ।
vidyudguṇavihīnāśca jaladhārāvalambinaḥ ॥ 1.51.31 ॥
krośamātrācca varṣanti krośārddhādapi vā punaḥ ॥ 1.51.32 ॥
parvatāgranitambeṣu varṣanti ca ramanti ca।
balākāgarbhadāścaiva balākāgarbhadhāriṇaḥ ॥ 1.51.33 ॥
brahmajānāma te meghā brahmaniḥśvāsasambhavāḥ।
te hi vidyudguṇopetāḥ stanayanti svanapriyāḥ ॥ 1.51.34 ॥
teṣāṃ śabdapraṇādena bhūmiḥ svāṅgaruhodghamā।
rājñī rājñābhiṣikteva punaryauvanamaśrute।
teṣviyaṃ prītimāsaktā bhūtānāṃ jīvitodbhavā ॥ 1.51.35 ॥
jīmūtā nāma te meghāstebhyo jīvasya sambhavaḥ।
dvitīyaṃ pravahaṃ vāyuṃ meghāste tu samāśritāḥ ॥ 1.51.36 ॥
ete yojanamātrācca sārddhārddhānniṣkṛtādapi।
vṛṣṭisargastathā teṣāṃ dhārāsārāḥ prakīrttitāḥ।
puṣkarāvarttakā nāma ye meghāḥ pakṣasambhavāḥ ॥ 1.51.37 ॥
śakreṇa pakṣāśchinnā ye parvatānāṃ mahojasām।
kāmagānāṃ pravṛddhānāṃ bhūtānāṃ śivamicchatā ॥ 1.51.38 ॥
puṣkarā nāma te meghā bṛhantastoya matsarāḥ।
puṣkarāvarttakāstena kāraṇeneha śabditāḥ ॥ 1.51.39 ॥
nānārūpadharāścaiva mahāghoratarāśca te।
kalpāntavṛṣṭeḥ sraṣṭāraḥ saṃvarttāgnerniyāmakāḥ ॥ 1.51.40 ॥
varṣantyete yugānteṣu tṛtīyāste prakīrttitāḥ।
anekarūpasaṃsthānāḥ pūrayanto mahītalam ।
vāyuṃ paraṃ vahantaḥ syurāśritāḥ kalpasādhakāḥ ॥ 1.51.41 ॥
tasmādbrahmā samutpannaścaturvaktraḥ svayambhuvaḥ।
tānyevāṇḍakapālasya sarve meghāḥ prakīrttitāḥ ॥ 1.51.42 ॥
teṣāmāpyāyanaṃ dhūmaḥ sarveṣāmaviśeṣataḥ ।
teṣāṃ śreṣṭhastu parjjanyaścatvāraścaiva diggajāḥ ॥ 1.51.43 ॥
gajānāṃ parvatānāñca megānāṃ bhogibhiḥ saha।
kulamekaṃ pṛthagbhūtaṃ yonirekā jalaṃ smṛtam ॥ 1.51.44 ॥
parjanyo diggajāścaiva hemante śītasambhavāḥ।
tuṣāravṛṣṭiṃ varṣanti sarvasasyavivṛddhaye ॥ 1.51.45 ॥
śreṣṭhaḥ parivaho nāma teṣāṃ vāyurapāśrayaḥ।
yo'sau bibhartti bhagavān gaṅgāmākāśagocarām।
tasyāviṣpandajantoyaṃ diggajāḥ pṛthubhiḥ karaiḥ।
śīkaraṃ sampramuñcanti nīhāra iti sa smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.51.47 ॥
dakṣiṇena giriryo'sau hemakūṭa iti smṛtaḥ।
udag himavataḥ śailāduttarasya ca dakṣiṇe।
puṇḍraṃ nāma samākhyātaṃ nagaraṃ tatra vai smṛtam ॥ 1.51.48 ॥
tasminnipatitaṃ varṣaṃ yattuṣārasamudbhavam ।
tatastadāvaho vāyurhimaśailāt samudvahan।
ānayatyātmayogena siñcamāno mahāgirim ॥ 1.51.49 ॥
himavantamatikramya vṛṣṭiśeṣaṃ tataḥ param।
ihābhyeti tataḥ paścādaparāntavivṛddhaye ॥ 1.51.50 ॥
meghāvāpyāyataścaiva sarvametat prakīrttitam ।
sūrya eva tu vṛṣṭināṃ sraṣṭā samupadiśyate ॥ 1.51.51 ॥
dhruveṇā veṣṭitaḥ sūryastābyāṃ vṛṣṭiḥ pravarttate।
dhruveṇāveṣṭito vāyurvṛṣṭiṃ saṃharate punaḥ ॥ 1.51.52 ॥
grahānniḥsṛtya sūryāttu kṛtsne nakṣatramaṇḍale ।
vārasyānte viśatyarkaṃ dhruveṇa pariveṣṭitam ॥ 1.51.53 ॥
ataḥ sūryarathasyātha sanniveśaṃ nibodhata।
saṃsthitainaikacakreṇa pañcāreṇa trinābhinā ॥ 1.51.54 ॥
naṣṭavartmāndhakāreṇa ṣaṭ‌prakāraikaneminā।
cakreṇa bhāsvatā sūryaḥ syandanena prasarppati ॥ 1.51.55 ॥
daśa yojanasāhasro vistārāyāmataḥ smṛtaḥ।
dviguṇo'sya rathopasthādīṣādaṇḍapramāṇataḥ ॥ 1.51.56 ॥
sa tasya brahmaṇā sṛṣṭo ratho hyarthavaśena tu।
asaṅgaḥ kāñcano divyo yuktaḥ paramagairhayaiḥ ॥ 1.51.57 ॥
chandobhirvājirūpaistu yataḥ śukrastataḥ sthitaḥ।
varuṇasyandanasteha lakṣaṇaiḥ sadṛśastu saḥ।
te nā'sau sarpativyomni bhāsvatā tu divākaraḥ ॥ 1.51.58 ॥
athemāni tu sūryasya pratyaṅgāni rathasya tu।
saṃvatsarasyāvayavaiḥ kalpitāni yathā kramam ॥ 1.51.59 ॥
ahastu nābhiḥ sūryasya ekacakraḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ।
ārāḥ pañcarttavastasya nemiḥ ṣaḍhṛtavaḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 1.51.60 ॥
rathanīḍaḥ smṛto hyabdastvayane kūbarāvubhau ।
muhūrtā bandhurāstasya śamyā tasya kalāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 1.51.61 ॥
tasya kāṣṭāḥ smṛtā ghoṇā īṣādaṇḍaḥ kṣaṇāṃstu vai।
nimeṣāścānukarṣo'sya īṣā cāsya lavāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 1.51.62 ॥
rātrirvarūtho gharmo'sya dhvaja ūrddhvasamucchritaḥ।
yugākṣakoṭī te tasya arthakāmāvubhau smṛtau ॥ 1.51.63 ॥
saptāśvarūpāśchandāṃsi vahante vāmato dhurām।
gāyatrī caiva triṣṭupū ca anuṣṭub jagatī tathā ॥ 1.51.64 ॥
paṅktiśca bṛhatī caiva uṣṇik caiva tu saptamam।
akṣe cakraṃ nibaddhantu dhruve tvakṣaḥ samarpitaḥ ॥ 1.51.65 ॥
sahacakro bhramatyakṣaḥ sahākṣo bhramati dhruvaḥ।
akṣaḥ sahaiva cakreṇa bhramate'sau dhruveritaḥ ॥ 1.51.66 ॥
evamartha vaśāttasya sanniveśo rathasya tu।
tathā saṃyogabhāgena saṃsiddho bāsvaro rathaḥ ॥ 1.51.67 ॥
tenā'sau taraṇirdevastarasā sarpate divi।
yugākṣakoṭisambaddhau raśmī dvau syandanasya hi ॥ 1.51.68 ॥
dhruveṇa bhramato raśmī vicakrayugayostu vai।
bhramato maṇḍalāni syuḥ khecarasya rathasya tu ॥ 1.51.69 ॥
yugākṣakoṭī te tasya dakṣiṇe syandanasya tu।
dhruveṇa saṃgṛhīte vai dvicakraśvetarajjuvat ॥ 1.51.70 ॥
bhramantamanugacchetāṃ dhruvaṃ raśmī tu tāvubhau ।
yugākṣa koṭī te tasya vātormī syandanasya tu ॥ 1.51.71 ॥
kīlāsakto yathā rajjurbhramate sarvato diśam।
hrasatastasya raśmī tau maṇḍaleṣūttarāyaṇe ॥ 1.51.72 ॥
varddhete dakṣiṇe caiva bhramato maṇḍalāni tu।
dhruveṇa saṃgṛhītau tu rasmī vai nayato ravim ॥ 1.51.73 ॥
ākṛṣyete yadā tau vai dhruveṇa samadhiṣṭitau।
tadā so'bhyantaraṃ sūryo bhramate maṇḍalāni tu ॥ 1.51.74 ॥
aśītimaṇḍalaśataṃ kāṣṭhayorubhayoścaran ।
dhruveṇa mucyamānābhyāṃ raśmibhyāṃ punareva tu ॥ 1.51.75 ॥
tathaiva bāhyataḥ sūryo bhramate maṇḍalāni tu।
udveṣṭayan sa vegena maṇḍalāni tu gacchati ॥ 1.51.76 ॥
sa ratho'dhiṣṭito devairādityaiṛṣibhistathā।
gandharvairapsarobhiśca grāmaṇīsarparākṣasaiḥ ॥ 1.52.1 ॥
ete vasanti vai sūrye dvau dvau māsau krameṇa tu।
dhātāryamā pulastyaśca pulahaśca prajāpatiḥ ॥ 1.52.2 ॥
urago vāsukiścaiva saṅkīrṇāraśca tāvubhau।
rakṣo hetiḥ prahetiśca yātudhānāvudāhṛtau।
madhumādhavayoreṣa gaṇo vasati bhāskare ॥ 1.52.5 ॥
pauruṣeyo dhavaścaiva yātudhānāvudāhṛtau।
tataḥ sūrye punastvanyā nivasantīha devatāḥ।
indraścaiva vivasvāṃśca aṅgirā bhṛgureva ca ॥ 1.52.9 ॥
elāparṇastathā sarpaḥ śaṅkhapālaśca tāvubhau।
viśvāvasūgrasenau ca prātaścaivāruṇaśca ha ॥ 1.52.10 ॥
pramloceti ca vikhyātā nimloceti ca te ubhe।
yātudhānastathā sarpo vyāghraḥ śvetaśca tāvubhau।
nabhonabhasyayoreṣa gaṇo vasati bhāskare ॥ 1.52.11 ॥
śaradṛ-tau punaḥ śubhrā vasanti muni devatāḥ।
parjjanyaścātha pūṣā ca bharadvājaḥ sagautamaḥ ॥ 1.52.12 ॥
viśvāvasuśca gandharvāstathaiva surabhiśca yaḥ।
viśvācī ca ghṛtācī ca ubhe te śubhalakṣaṇe ॥ 1.52.13 ॥
nāga airāvataścaiva viśrutaśca dhanañjayaḥ।
senajicca suṣeṇaśacava senānīrgrāmaṇīśca tau ॥ 1.52.14 ॥
āpo vātaśca tāvetau yātudhānāvubhau smṛtau।
haimantikau tu dvau māsau vasanti tu divākare।
aṃśo bhagaśca dvāvetau kaśyapaśca ṛtuśca ha ॥ 1.52.16 ॥
bhujaṅgaśca mahāpajhaḥ sarpaḥ karkoṭakastathā।
citrasenaśca gandharva ūrṇāyuścaiva tāvubhau ॥ 1.52.17 ॥
urvaśī vipracittiśca tathaivāpsarasau śubhe।
tārkṣyaścāriṣṭanemiśca senānīrgrāmaṇīśca tau ॥ 1.52.18 ॥
vidyutsphūrjjaśca tāvugrau yātudhānāvudāhṛtau।
sahe caiva sahasye ca vasantyete divākare ॥ 1.52.19 ॥
tataḥ śaiśirayośvāpi māsayornivasanti vai।
tvaṣṭā viṣṇurjamadagnirviśvāmitrastathaiva ca ॥ 1.52.20 ॥
kādraveyau tathā nāgau kambalāśvatarāvubhau।
gandharvo dhṛtarāṣṭraśca sūryavarccāstathaiva ca ॥ 1.52.21 ॥
ete devā vasantyarke dvau māsau tu krameṇa tu ॥ 1.52.23 ॥
sthānābhimānino hyete gaṇā dvādaśa saptakāḥ।
sūryamāpyāyayantyete tejasā teja uttamam ॥ 1.52.24 ॥
gandharvāpsarasaścaiva gītanṛtyairupāsate ॥ 1.52.25 ॥
grāmaṇīyakṣabhūtāstu kurvate bhīmasaṃgraham।
sarpā vahanti sūryañca yātudhānānuyānti ca।
vālakhilyā nayantyastaṃ paricāryodayādravim ॥ 1.52.26 ॥
eteṣāmeva devānāṃ yatāvīryaṃ yathātapaḥ।
yathāyogaṃ yathāsatyaṃ yathādharmaṃ yatābalam ॥ 1.52.27 ॥
yathā tapatyasau sūryasteṣāṃ siddhastu tejasā।
ityete vai vasantīha dvau dvau māsau divākare ॥ 1.52.28 ॥
ṛṣayo devagandharvāḥ pannagāpsarasāṅgaṇāḥ ।
grāmaṇyaśca tathā yakṣā yātudhānāśca bhūriśaḥ ॥ 1.52.29 ॥
ete tapanti varṣanti bhānti vānti sṛjanti ca।
bhūtānāmaśubhaṃ karma vyapohantīha kīrtitāḥ ॥ 1.52.30 ॥
mānavānāṃ śubhaṃ hyete haranti duritātmanām।
duritaṃ hi pracārāṇāṃ vyapohanti vkacit vkacit ॥ 1.52.31 ॥
ete sahaiva sūryeṇa bhramanti divasānugāḥ ॥ 1.52.32 ॥
varṣantaśca tapantaśca hlādayantaśca vai prajāḥ।
gopāyanti tu bhūtāni sarvānīhāmanukṣayāt ॥ 1.52.33 ॥
sthānābhimānināmetat sthānaṃ manvantareṣu vai।
atītānāgatānāṃ vai varttante sāmpratantu ye ॥ 1.52.34 ॥
evaṃ vasanti vai sūrye saptakāste caturddiśam।
caturddaśasu sargeṣu gaṇā manvantareṣu ca ॥ 1.52.35 ॥
grīṣme hime ca varṣāsu muñcamānā gharmaṃ himañca varṣañca dinaṃ niśāñca।
kālena gacchatyṛtuvaśāt parivṛttaraśmi rdevān pitṝṃśca manujāṃśca tarpayan vai ॥ 1.52.36 ॥
prīṇāti devānamṛtena sūryaḥ somaṃ suṣumnena vivarddhayitvā ।
śukle tu pūrṇaṃ divasakrameṇa taṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe vibudhāḥ pibanti ॥ 1.52.37 ॥
pītantu somaṃ dvikālāvaśiṣṭaṃ kṛṣṇakṣaye raśmibhistaṃ kṣarantam।
sudhāmṛtaṃ tatpitaraḥ pibanti devāśca saumyāśca tathaiva kavyam ॥ 1.52.38 ॥
sūryeṇa gobhistu samuddhṛtābhiradbhiḥ punaścaiva samuddhṛtābhiḥ।
vṛṣṭyātivṛddhābhirathauṣadhībhirmartyāḥ kṣudhantvannapānairjayanti ॥ 1.52.39 ॥
annena śaśvattu dadhāti martyān sūryaḥ svayaṃ tacca bibharti gobhiḥ ॥ 1.52.40 ॥
ayaṃ haristairharibhisturaṅgamairayan hi cāpo haratīti raśmibhiḥ।
visargakāle visṛjaṃśca tāḥ punarbibharti śaśvat savitā carācaram ॥ 1.52.41 ॥
harirharidbhirhriyate turaṅgamaiḥ pibatyathāpo haribhiḥ sahasradhā।
tataḥ pramuñcatyapi tāstvasau hariḥ sa muhyamāno haribhisturaṅgamaiḥ ॥ 1.52.42 ॥
ityeṣa ekacakreṇa sūryastūrṇaṃ rathena tu।
bhadraistairakṣatairaśvaiḥ sarpate'sau divi kṣaye ॥ 1.52.43 ॥
ahorātrādrathaināsau ekacakreṇa tu bhraman।
saptadvīpasamudrāntaṃ saptabhiḥ saptabhirhayaiḥ ॥ 1.52.44 ॥
chandobhiraśvarūpaistairyataścakrantataḥ sthitaiḥ।
kāmarūpaiḥ sakṛdyuktairamitaistairmanojavaiḥ ॥ 1.52.45 ॥
haritairavyayaiḥ piṅgairīśvarairbrahmavādibhiḥ।
aśīti maṇḍalaśataṃ bhramantyabdena te hayāḥ ॥ 1.52.46 ॥
bāhyamabhyantarañcaiva maṇḍalaṃ divasakramāt ।
kalpādau samprayuktāste vahantyābhūtasamplavāt।
āvṛtā vālakhilyaiste bhramante rātryahāni tu ॥ 1.52.47 ॥
saivyate gītavṛtyaiśca gandharvairapsarogaṇaiḥ।
pataṅgaḥ pata gairaśvairbhramamāṇo divaspatiḥ ॥ 1.52.48 ॥
hrāsavṛddhī tathaivāsya raśmīnāṃ sūryavat smṛte ॥ 1.52.49 ॥
tricakrobhayapārśvastho vijñeyaḥ śaśino rathaḥ।
apāṃ garbhasamutpanno rathaḥ sāśvaḥ sasārathiḥ।
śatāraiśca tribhiścakrairyuktaḥ śulkairhayottamaiḥ ॥ 1.52.50 ॥
daśa bhistu kṛśairdivyairasaṅgaistairmanojavaiḥ।
sakṛdyukte rathe tasmin vahante cāyugakṣayāt ॥ 1.52.51 ॥
saṃgṛhīte rathe tasmin śvetaścakṣuḥśravāstu vai।
aśvā stamekavarṇāste vahante śaṅkhavarccasam ॥ 1.52.52 ॥
ityete nāmabhiḥ sarve daśa candramaso hayāḥ ।
ete candramasaṃ devaṃ vahanti divasakṣayāt ॥ 1.52.54 ॥
devaiḥ parivṛtaḥ saumyaḥ pitṛbhiścaiva gacchati।
somasya śukla pakṣādau bhāskare purataḥ sthite।
āpūryate purasyāntaḥ satataṃ divasakramāt ॥ 1.52.55 ॥
devaiḥ pītaṃ kṣaye somamāpyāyayati nityadā।
pītaṃ pañcadaśāhantu raśminaikena bhāskaraḥ ॥ 1.52.56 ॥
āpūrayan suṣumnena bhāgaṃ bhāgamahaḥkramāt ।
suṣumnāpyāyamānasya śuklā varddhanti vai kalāḥ ॥ 1.52.57 ॥
tasmāddhrasanti vai kṛṣṇe śukla āpyāyayanti ca।
ityevaṃ sūryavīryeṇa candrasyāpyāyitā tanuḥ ॥ 1.52.58 ॥
paurṇamāsyāṃ sa dṛśyeta śuklaḥ sampūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ ।
evamāpyāyitaḥ somaḥ śuklapakṣe dinakramāt ॥ 1.52.59 ॥
tato dvitīyāprabhṛti bahulasya caturddaśī।
apāṃ sāramayasyendo rasamātrātmakasya ca।
pibantyambumayaṃ devā madhu saumyaṃ sudhāma yam ॥ 1.52.60 ॥
sambhṛtañcārddhamāsena amṛtaṃ sūryatejasā ।
bhakṣārthamamṛtaṃ saumyaṃ paurṇamāsyāmupāsate ॥ 1.52.61 ॥
somasya kṛṣṇapakṣādau bhāskarābhimukhasya ca ॥ 1.52.62 ॥
kṣīyante tasmāt kṛṣṇe yāḥ śukle hyāpyāyayanti tāḥ ॥ 1.52.63 ॥
evaṃ dinakramātīte vibudhāstu niśākaram ।
pītvā'rddhamāsaṅgacchanti amāvāsyāṃ surottamāḥ ।
pitaraścopatiṣṭhanti amāvāsyāṃ niśākaram ॥ 1.52.64 ॥
tataḥ pañcadaśe bhāge kiñcicchiṣṭe kalātmake।
aparāhne pitṛgaṇairjaghanyaḥ paryupāsyate ॥ 1.52.65 ॥
niḥsṛtaṃ tadamāvāsyāṅgabhastibhyaḥ svadhāmṛtam।
tāṃ svadhāṃ māsatṛptyai tu pītvā gacchanti te'mṛtam ॥ 1.52.66 ॥
saumyā barhiṣadaścaiva agniṣvāttāstathaiva ca।
kavyāścaiva tu ye proktāḥ pitaraḥ sarva eva te ॥ 1.52.67 ॥
saṃvatsarāstu vai kavyāḥ pañcābdā ye dvijaiḥ smṛtāḥ।
saumyāstu ṛtavo jñeyā māsā barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ।
agniṣvāttārtavaścaiva pitṛsargā hi vai dvijāḥ ॥ 1.52.68 ॥
pitṛbhiḥ pīyamānasya pañcadaśyāṃ kalā tu vai।
yāvanna kṣīyate tasya bhāgaḥ pañcadaśa stu saḥ ॥ 1.52.69 ॥
amāvasyāntadā tasya antamāpūryate param।
vṛddhikṣayau vai pakṣādau ṣoḍaśyāṃ śaśinaḥ smṛtau ॥ 1.52.70 ॥
evaṃ sūryanimittaiṣā kṣayavṛddhi rniśākare।
tārāgrahāṇāṃ vakṣyāmi svarbhānośca rathaṃ punaḥ ॥ 1.52.71 ॥
toyatejomayaḥ śubhraḥ somaputrasya vai rathaḥ।
sopāsaṅgapatākastu sadhvajo meghasannibhaḥ ॥ 1.52.73 ॥
bhārgavasya rathaḥ śrīṇāṃstejasā sūryasannibhaḥ।
pṛthivīsambhavairyukto nānāvarṇairhayottamaiḥ ॥ 1.52.74 ॥
śvetaḥ piśaṅgaḥ sāraṅgo nīlaḥ pīto vilohitaḥ।
kṛṣṇaśca haritaścaiva pṛṣataḥ pṛṣṇireva ca।
daśabhi stairmahābhāgairakṛśairvātavegitaiḥ ॥ 1.52.75 ॥
aṣṭāśvaḥ kāñcanaḥ śrīmān somasyāpi ratho'bhavat।
asaṅgairlauhitairaśvaiḥ sarvagairagnisambhavaiḥ।
sarpate'sau kumāro vai ṛjuvakrānucakragaḥ ॥ 1.52.76 ॥
tatastvāṅgiraso vidvān devācāryo bṛhaspatiḥ।
śoṇairaśvaiḥ kāñcanena syandanena prasarpati ॥ 1.52.77 ॥
tataḥ śanaiśvaropyaśvaiḥ śabalairvyomasambhavaiḥ।
kārṣṇāyasaṃ samāruhya syandanaṃ yāti vai śanaiḥ ॥ 1.52.79 ॥
svarbhānostu tathaivāśvāḥ kṛṣṇā hyaṣṭau manojavāḥ।
rathantamomayantasya sakṛdyuktā vahantyuta ॥ 1.52.80 ॥
ādityānniḥsṛto rāhuḥ somaṃ gacchati parvasu।
ādityameti somācca punaḥ saureṣu parvasu ॥ 1.52.81 ॥
atha keturathasyāśvā aṣṭāṣṭau vātaraṃhasaḥ।
palāladhūmasaṅkāśāḥ śabalā rāsabhāruṇāḥ ॥ 1.52.82 ॥
ete vāhā grahāṇāṃ vai mayā proktā rathaiḥ saha।
sarve dhruvanibaddhāste prabaddhā vātaraśmibhiḥ ॥ 1.52.83 ॥
ete vai bhrāmyamāṇāstu yathā yogaṃ bhramanti vai।
vāyavyābhiradṛśyābhiḥ prabaddhā vātaraśmibhiḥ ॥ 1.52.84 ॥
paribhramanti tadbaddhāścandrasūryagrahā divi।
bhramantamanugacchanti dhruvante jyotiṣāṃ gaṇāḥ ॥ 1.52.85 ॥
yathā nadyudake naustu salilena sahohyate।
tathā devālayā hyete uhyante vātaraśmibhiḥ।
tasmātsarveṇa dṛsyante vyomni devagaṇāstu te ॥ 1.52.86 ॥
yāvantyaścaiva tārāstu tāvanto vātaraśmayaḥ।
sarvā dhruvanibaddhāstā bramantyo bhrāmayanti tam ॥ 1.52.87 ॥
tailapīḍākaraṃ cakraṃ bhramadbhrāmayate yathā।
tathā bhramanti jyotīṃṣi vāyabaddhāni sarvaśaḥ ॥ 1.52.88 ॥
alātacakravadyānti vātacakreritāni tu।
tasmājjyotīṃṣi vahate pravahaṃstena sa smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.52.89 ॥
evaṃ dhruvanibaddho'sau sarpate jyotiṣāṃ gaṇaḥ।
saiṣa tārāmayojñeyaḥ śiśumāro dhruvo divi।
yadahnā kurute pāpaṃ dṛṣṭavā taṃ niśi mucyate ॥ 1.52.90 ॥
yāvatyaścaiva tārāstāḥ śiśūmārāśritā divi।
tāvantyeva tu varṣāṇi jīvantyabhyadhikāni tu ॥ 1.52.91 ॥
uttānapādastasyātha vijñeyo hyuttaro hanuḥ ॥ 1.52.92 ॥
yajño'dharastu vijñeyo dharmo mūrddhānamāśritaḥ।
hṛdi nārāyaṇaḥ sādhyaḥ aśvinau pūrvapādayoḥ ॥ 1.52.93 ॥
varuṇaścāryamā caiva paścime tasya sasthini।
śiśraḥ saṃvatsarastasya mitro'pāne samāśritaḥ ॥ 1.52.94 ॥
pucche'gniśca mahendraśca marīciḥ kaśyapo dhruvaḥ।
tārakāḥ śiśumāraśca nāstameti catuṣṭayam ॥ 1.52.95 ॥
nakṣatracandrasūryāśca grahāstārāgaṇeḥ saha।
unmukhābhimukhāḥ sarve cakrībhūtāśritā divi ॥ 1.52.96 ॥
dhruveṇādhiṣṭitāḥ sarve dhruvameva pradakṣiṇam ।
prayāntīha varaṃ śreṣṭhamedhībhūtaṃ dhruvandivi ॥ 1.52.97 ॥
eka eva bhramatyeṣa meruparvatamūrddhani ॥ 1.52.98 ॥
jyotiṣāñcakrametaddhi sadā karṣatyavāṅmukhaḥ।
merumālokayatyeṣa prayātīha pradakṣiṇam ॥ 1.52.99 ॥
etacchrutvā tu munayaḥ punaste saṃśayānvitāḥ।
papracchuruttaraṃ bhūyastadā te lomaharṣaṇam ॥ 1.53.1 ॥
yadetaduktambhavatā gṛhāṇyetāni viśritam।
kathaṃ devagṛhāṇi syuḥ kathaṃ jyotīṃṣi varṇaya ॥ 1.53.2 ॥
etatsarvaṃ samācakṣva jyotiṣāñcaiva niścayam।
śrutvā tu vacanaṃ teṣāṃ tadā sūtaḥ samāhitaḥ ॥ 1.53.3 ॥
asminnarthe mahāprājñairyaduktaṃ jñānabuddhibhiḥ।
tadvo'haṃ sampravakṣyāmi sūryācandramasorbhavam।
yathā devagṛhāṇīha sūryācandramasorgṛham ॥ 1.53.4 ॥
ataḥ paraṃ trividhāgnervakṣye'hantu samudbhavam।
divyasya bhautikasyāgnerathāgneḥ pārthivasya ca ॥ 1.53.5 ॥
vyuṣṭāyāntu rajanyāṃ vai brahmaṇo'vyaktajanmanaḥ।
avyākṛtamidantvāsīnnaiśena tamasāvṛtam ॥ 1.53.6 ॥
yaścādau tapate sūrye śuciragnistu sa smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.53.7 ॥
vaidyutākhyastu vijñeyasteṣāṃ vakṣye'tha lakṣaṇam।
vaidyuto jāṭharaḥ sauro hyapāṅgarbhāstrayo'gnayaḥ।
tasmādapaḥ piban sūryo gobhidīrpyatyasau divi ॥ 1.53.8 ॥
vaidyutena samāviṣṭo vārkṣo nādbhiḥ praśāmyati ।
mānavānāñca kukṣistho nādbhiḥ śāmyati pāvakaḥ ॥ 1.53.9 ॥
yaścāyaṃ maṇḍalī śuklo nirūṣmā saṃprakāśate ॥ 1.53.10 ॥
prabhā hi saurī pādena hyastaṃ yāti divākare।
agnimāviśate rātrau tasmād‌dūrāt prakāśate ॥ 1.53.11 ॥
udyantañca punaḥ sūryamauṣṇyamāgneyamāviśat।
pādena pārthivasyāgnestasmādagnistapatyasau ॥ 1.53.12 ॥
prakāśaśca tathauṣṇyañca saurāgneye tu tejasī।
parasparānupraveśādāpyāyete divāniśam ॥ 1.53.13 ॥
uttare caiva bhūmyarddhe tasmādasmiṃśca dakṣiṇe।
uttiṣṭhati punaḥ sūrye rātrirāviśate tvapaḥ।
tasmāttāmrā bhavantyāpo divārātripraveśanāt ॥ 1.53.14 ॥
astaṃ yāti punaḥ sūrye aharvai praviśatyapaḥ।
tasmānnaktaṃ punaḥ śuklā āpo viśyanti bhāskare ॥ 1.53.15 ॥
etena kramayogena bhūmyarddhe dakṣiṇottare ।
udayāstamaye nityamahorātraṃ viśatyapaḥ ॥ 1.53.16 ॥
yaścāsau tapate sūrye pibannambho gabhastibhiḥ।
pārthivo hi vimiśro'sau divyaḥ śuciriti smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.53.17 ॥
sahasrapādaḥ so'gnistu vṛttaḥ kumbhanibhaḥ śuciḥ।
ādatte tattu raśmīnāṃ sahasreṇa samantataḥ ॥ 1.53.18 ॥
nādeyīścaiva sāmudrīḥ kaupyāścaiva sadhānvanīḥ।
tasya raśmisahasrantu varṣaśītoṣṇaniḥsravam ॥ 1.53.19 ॥
tāsāñcatuḥśatā nāḍyo varṣanti citramūrttayaḥ।
vandanāścaiva vandyaśca ṛtanā nūtanāstathā।
amṛtā nāmataḥ sarvvā raśmayo vṛṣṭisarjanāḥ ॥ 1.53.20 ॥
himavāhāśca tābhyo'nyā raśmayastriśatāḥ punaḥ।
dṛśyā medhyāśca vāhyāśca hrādinyo himasarjanāḥ ॥ 1.53.21 ॥
candrāstā nāmataḥ sarvāḥ pītābhāstu gabhastayaḥ।
śuklāśca kakubhaścaiva gāvo viśvabhṛtastathā ॥ 1.53.22 ॥
śuklāstā nāmataḥ sarvāstriśatā gharmasarjanāḥ।
samaṃ bibharti tābhistu manuṣyapitṛdevatāḥ ॥ 1.53.23 ॥
manuṣyānauṣadheneha svadhayā ca pitṝnapi।
amṛtena surān sarvāṃstrīṃstribhistarpayatyasau ॥ 1.53.24 ॥
vasante caiva grīṣme ca sataiḥ sutapate tribhiḥ।
varṣāsvatho śaradi ca caturbhiḥ samprakarṣati ॥ 1.53.25 ॥
hemante śiśire caiva himaṃ sa sṛja te tribhiḥ।
oṣadhīṣu balandhatte svadhayā ca pitṝnapi।
sūryo'maratvamamṛtatrayantriṣu niyacchati ॥ 1.53.26 ॥
evaṃ raśmisahasrantat sauraṃ lokārtha sādhakam।
bhidyate ṛtumāsādya jalaśītoṣṇaniḥsravam ॥ 1.53.27 ॥
ityetanmaṇḍalaṃ śuklaṃ bhāsvaraṃ sūryasaṃjñitam।
nakṣatragrahasomānāṃ pratiṣṭāyonireva ca।
ṛkṣacandragrahāḥ sarve nijñeyāḥ sūryasambhavāḥ ॥ 1.53.28 ॥
nakṣatrādhipatiḥ somo graharājo divākaraḥ।
śeṣāḥ pañcagrahā jñeyā īśvarāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ ॥ 1.53.29 ॥
paṭyate cāgnirāditya audakaścandramāḥ smṛtaḥ।
śeṣāṇāṃ prakṛtiṃ samyagvarṇyamānāṃ nibodhata ॥ 1.53.30 ॥
surasenāpati skandaḥ paṭyate'ṅgārako grahaḥ ।
nārāyaṇaṃ budhaṃ prāhurdevaṃ jñānavido viduḥ ॥ 1.53.31 ॥
rudro vaivasvataḥ sākṣāddharmo loke prabhuḥ svayam।
mahāgraho dvijaśreṣṭo mandagāmī śanaiścaraḥ ॥ 1.53.32 ॥
devāsuragurū dvau tu bhānumantau mahāgrahau।
prajāpatisutāvetāvubhau śukrabṛhaspatī।
ādityamūlamakhilaṃ trilokaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ।
bhavatyasya jagatkṛtsnaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ॥ 1.53.34 ॥
rudrendropendracandrāṇāṃ viprendrāstridivaukasām।
dyutirdyutimatāṃ kṛtsnā yattejaḥ sārvalaukikam ॥ 1.53.35 ॥
tataḥ saṃjāyate sarvaṃ tatra caiva pralīyate ॥ 1.53.36 ॥
bāvābhāvau hi lokānāmādityānniḥ sṛtau purā।
jagajjñeyo graho viprā dīptimān sugrāho raviḥ ॥ 1.53.37 ॥
yatra gacchanti nidhanaṃ jāyante ca punaḥ punaḥ।
kṣaṇā muhūrttā divasā niśāḥ pakṣāśca kṛtsnaśaḥ।
māsāḥ saṃvatsarāścaiva ṛtavo'ndayugāni ca ॥ 1.53.38 ॥
tadādityādṛte teṣāṃ kālasaṃkhyā na vidyate।
kālādṛte na nigamo na dīkṣā nāhnikakramaḥ ॥ 1.53.39 ॥
ṛtunāmavibhāgaśca puṣpamūlaphalaṃ kutaḥ।
kutaḥ sasyābhiniṣpattirguṇauṣadhigaṇādi vā ॥ 1.53.40 ॥
abhāvo vyavahārāṇāṃ devānāṃ divi ceha ca।
jagatpratāpanamṛte bhāskaraṃ vāritaskaram ॥ 1.53.41 ॥
sa eva kālaścāgniśca dvādaśātmā prajāpatiḥ।
tapatyeṣa dvijaśreṣṭāstrailokyaṃ sacarācaram ॥ 1.53.42 ॥
uttamaṃ mārgamāsthāya vāyobhābhiridañjagat।
pārśvamūrddhvamadhaścaiva tāpayatyeṣa sarvaśaḥ ॥ 1.53.43 ॥
raveraśmisahasraṃ yat prāṅmayā samudāhṛtam ।
teṣāṃ śreṣṭāḥ punaḥ sapta raśmayo grahayonayaḥ ॥ 1.53.44 ॥
suṣumno harikeśaśca viśvakarmā tathaiva ca।
viśvaśravāḥ punaśvānyaḥ sampadvasurataḥ param ।
arvāvasuḥ punaścānyomayā cātra prakīrttitaḥ ॥ 1.53.45 ॥
suṣumnaḥ sūryaraśmistu kṣīṇaṃ śaśinamedhayan।
tiryagūrddhvaprabhāvo'sau suṣumnaḥ parikīrtyate ॥ 1.53.46 ॥
harikeśaḥ purastvādyā ṛkṣayoniḥ prakīrtyate।
dakṣiṇe viśvakarmā tu raśmirvarddhayate budham ॥ 1.53.47 ॥
viśvaśravāstu yaḥ paścāt śukrayoniḥ smṛto budhaiḥ।
sampadvasuśca yo raśmiḥ sā yonirlohitasya ca ॥ 1.53.48 ॥
ṣaṣṭhastvarvāvasū raśmiryonistu sa bṛhaspateḥ।
śanaiścaraṃ punaścāpi raśmirāpyāyate svarāṭ ॥ 1.53.49 ॥
evaṃ sūryaprabhāveṇa grahanakṣatratārakāḥ।
varddhante viditāḥ sarvā viśvañcaidaṃ punarjagat ।
nakṣīyante punastāni tasmānnakṣatratā smṛtā ॥ 1.53.50 ॥
kṣetrāṇyetāni vai pūrvamāpatanti gabhastibhiḥ।
teṣāṃ kṣetrāṇyathādatte sūryo nakṣatratāṅgataḥ ॥ 1.53.51 ॥
tīrṇānāṃ sukṛteneha sukṛtānte grahāśrayāt ।
tārāṇāṃ tārakā hyetāḥ śuklatvāccaiva tārakāḥ ॥ 1.53.52 ॥
divyānāṃ pārthivānāñca naiśānāñcaiva sarvaśaḥ ।
ādānānnityamādityastamasāṃ tejasāṃ mahān ॥ 1.53.53 ॥
suvati spandanārthe ca dhātureṣa vibhāvyate।
savanāttejaso'pāñca tenāsau savitā mataḥ ॥ 1.53.54 ॥
bahvarthaścandra ityeṣa hlādane dhāturiṣyate ।
śuklatve cāmṛtatve ca śītatve ca vibhāvyate ॥ 1.53.55 ॥
suryācandramasordivye maṇḍale bhāsvare khage।
jvalattejomaye śukle vṛttakumbhanibhe śubhe ॥ 1.53.56 ॥
ghanatoyātmakaṃ tatra maṇḍalaṃ śaśinaḥ smṛtam।
ghanatejomayaṃ śuklaṃ maṇḍalaṃ bhāskarasya tu ॥ 1.53.57 ॥
viśanti sarvadevāstu sthānānyetāni sarvaśaḥ।
manvantareṣu sarveṣu ṛkṣasūryagrahāśrayāḥ ॥ 1.53.58 ॥
tāni devagṛhāṇyeva tadākhyāste bhavanti ca।
sauraṃ sūryo viśasthānaṃ saumyaṃ somastathaiva ca ॥ 1.53.59 ॥
śaukraṃ śukro viśasthānaṃ ṣoḍaśārcciḥ pratāpavān।
ādityaraśmisaṃyogāt saṃprakāśātmikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
navayojanasāhasro viṣkambhaḥ savituḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.53.61 ॥
triguṇastasya vistāro maṇḍalañca pramāṇataḥ।
dviguṇaḥ sūryavistārādvistāraḥ śaśinaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.53.62 ॥
tulyastayostu svarbhānurbhūtvādhastāt prasarpati।
uddhṛtya pārthivacchāyāṃ nirmito maṇḍalākṛtiḥ ॥ 1.53.63 ॥
svarbhānostu bṛhat sthānannirmitaṃ yattamomayam।
ādityāttacca niṣkramya somaṃ gacchati parvasu ॥ 1.53.64 ॥
ādityameti somācca punaḥ somañca parvasu।
svarbhāsānudate yasmāttataḥ svarbhānurucyate ॥ 1.53.65 ॥
candrasya ṣoḍaśo bhāgo bhārgavaśca nidhīyate।
viṣkambhānmaṇḍalāccaiva yojanāgrāt pramāṇataḥ ॥ 1.53.66 ॥
bhārgavātpādahīnastu vijñeyo vai bṛhaspatiḥ।
buhaspateḥ pādahīnau kujasaurāvubhau smṛtau ।
vistārānmaṇḍalāccaiva pādahīnastayorbudhaḥ ॥ 1.53.67 ॥
tārānakṣatrarūpāṇi svapuṣmantīha yāni vai।
budhena samatulyāni vistārānmaṇḍalādatha ॥ 1.53.68 ॥
prāyaśaścandrayogāni vidyādṛkṣāṇi tattvavit।
tārānakṣatrarūpāṇi hīnāni tu parasparam ॥ 1.53.69 ॥
śatāni pañca catvāri trīṇi dve caiva yojane।
pūrvāparanikṛṣṭāni tārakāmaṇḍalāni tu।
yojanānyarddhamātrāṇi tebhyo hrasvaṃ na vidyate ॥ 1.53.70 ॥
upariṣṭātrayasteṣāṃ grahā ye dūrasarpiṇaḥ।
sauro'ṅgirāśca vakraśca jñeyā mandavicāriṇaḥ ॥ 1.53.71 ॥
tebhyo'dhastāttu catvāraḥ punaranye mahāgrahāḥ।
sūryaḥ somo budhaścaiva bhārgavaścaiva śīghragāḥ ॥ 1.53.72 ॥
yāvantya stārakāḥ koṭyastāvadṛkṣāṇi sarvaśaḥ।
gatistāstveva sūryasya nīcoccatve'yanakramāt।
uttarāyaṇa mārgastho yadā parvasu candramāḥ।
baudhaṃ baudho'tha svarbhānuḥ svarbhānoḥ sthānamāsthitaḥ ॥ 1.53.74 ॥
nakṣatrāṇi ca sarvāṇi nakṣatrāṇi viśantyuta।
gṛhāṇye tāni sarvāṇi jyotīṃṣi sukṛtātmanām ॥ 1.53.75 ॥
kalpādau saṃpravṛttāni nirmitāni svayambhuvā।
sthānānyetāni tiṣṭhanti yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ॥ 1.53.76 ॥
manvantareṣu sarveṣu devatāyatanāni vai।
atītaistu sahātītā bhāvyābhāvyaiḥ surāsuraiḥ ।
varttante varttamānaiśca sthānāni svaiḥ suraiḥ saha ॥ 1.53.78 ॥
asmin manvantare caiva grahā vaimānikāḥ smṛtāḥ।
vivasvānaditeḥ putraḥ sūryo vaivasvate'ntare ॥ 1.53.79 ॥
tviṣimāndharmaputrastu somadevo vasuḥ smṛtaḥ।
śukro devastu vijñeyo bhārgavo'surarājakaḥ ॥ 1.53.80 ॥
bṛhattejāḥ smṛto devo devācāryo'ṅgiraḥsutaḥ।
budho manoharaścaiva tviṣiputrastu sa smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.53.81 ॥
agnirvikalpāt saṃjajñe yuvā'sau lohitādhipaḥ।
nakṣatrṛkṣagāminyo dākṣāyaṇyaḥ smṛtāstu tāḥ ॥ 1.53.82 ॥
svarbhānuḥ siṃhikāputro bhūtasantāpano'suraḥ।
somarkṣagrahasūrye tu kīrtitāstvabhimāninaḥ ॥ 1.53.83 ॥
sthānānyetānyathoktāni sthāninyaścaiva devatāḥ।
śuklamagnimayaṃ sthānaṃ sahasrāṃśorvivasvataḥ ॥ 1.53.84 ॥
sahasrāṃśostviṣaḥ sthānamammayaṃ śuklameva ca।
atha śyāmaṃ manojñasya pañcaraśmergṛhaṃ smṛtam ॥ 1.53.85 ॥
śukrasyāpyammayaṃ sthānaṃ sadma ṣoḍaśaraśmivat।
navaraśmestu yūno hi lohitasthānamammayam ॥ 1.53.86 ॥
hariścāpyaṃ bṛhaccāpi dvādaśāṃśorbṛhaspateḥ।
aṣṭa raśmergṛhaṃ proktaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ buddhasya ammayam ॥ 1.53.87 ॥
svarbhānostāmasaṃ sthānaṃ bhūtasantāpanālayam।
vijñeyāstārakāḥ sarvāstvammayāstvekaraśmayaḥ ॥ 1.53.88 ॥
āśrayāḥ puṇyakīrtīnāṃ suśuklāścaiva varṇataḥ।
ghanatoyātmikā jñeyāḥ kalpādau vedanirmitāḥ ॥ 1.53.89 ॥
uccatvāddṛśyate śīghramabhivyaktairgabhastibhiḥ।
bhūmilekhāvṛtaḥ sūryaḥ pūrṇāmāvāsyayostathā।
nadṛśyate yathākālaṃ śāghrato'stamupaiti ca ॥ 1.53.91 ॥
tasmāduttaramārgastho hyamāvāsyāṃ niśākaraḥ।
dṛśyate dakṣiṇe mārge niyamāddṛśyate na ca ॥ 1.53.92 ॥
jyotiṣāṃ gatiyogena sūryācandramasāvubhau।
samānakālāstamayau viṣuvatsu samodayau ॥ 1.53.93 ॥
uttarāsu ca vīthīṣu vyantarāstamayodayau।
pūrṇāmāvāsyayorjñeyau jyotiścakrānuvarttinau ॥ 1.53.94 ॥
dakṣiṇāyanamārgastho yadā bhavati raśmivān।
tadā sarvagrahāṇāṃ sa sūryo'dhastāt prasarpati ॥ 1.53.95 ॥
vistīrṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā tasyorddhvañcarate śaśī।
nakṣatramaṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ somādūrddhvaṃ prasarpati ॥ 1.53.96 ॥
nakṣatrebhyo budhaśvorddhvaṃ budhādūrddhvaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ।
tasmācchanaiścaraścorddhvaṃ tasmātsaptarṣimaṇḍalam ।
ṛṣīṇāñcaiva saptānāṃ dhruva ūrddhvaṃ vyavasthitaḥ ॥ 1.53.97 ॥
dviguṇeṣu sahasreṣu yojanānāṃ śateṣu ca।
tārāgrahāntarāṇi syurupariṣṭādyathākramam ॥ 1.53.98 ॥
grahāśca candrasūryau tu divi divyena tejasā।
nityamṛkṣeṣu yujyanti gacchanti niyamakramāt ॥ 1.53.99 ॥
grahanakṣatrasūryāstu nīcoccamṛdvavasthitāḥ।
samāgame ca bhede ca paśyanti yugapat prajāḥ ॥ 1.53.100 ॥
parasparasthitāḥ hyete yujyante ca parasparam।
asaṅkareṇa vijñeyasteṣāṃ yogastu vai budhaiḥ ॥ 1.53.101 ॥
ityeṣa sanniveśo vaḥ pṛthivyāṃ jyautiṣasya ca।
dvīpānāmudnadhīnāṃ ca parvatānāṃ tathaiva ca ॥ 1.53.102 ॥
varṣāṇāṃ ca nadīnāñca yeṣu teṣu vasanti vai।
ete caiva grahāḥ pūrvaṃ nakṣatreṣu samutthitāḥ ॥ 1.53.103 ॥
vivasvānaditeḥ putraḥ sūryo vai cākṣuṣe'ntare।
viśākhāsu samutpanno grahāṇāṃ prathamo grahaḥ ॥ 1.53.104 ॥
tviṣimān dharmmaputrastu somo viśvāvasustathā।
śītaraśmiḥ samutpannaḥ kṛttikāsu niśākaraḥ ॥ 1.53.105 ॥
ṣoḍaśārcirbhṛgoḥ putraḥ śukraḥ sūryādanantaram।
tārāgrahāṇāṃ pravarastiṣyakṣetre samutthitaḥ ॥ 1.53.106 ॥
grahaścāṅgirasaḥ putro dvādaśārccirbṛhaspatiḥ।
phālgunīṣu samutpannaḥ sarvāsu ca jagadguruḥ ॥ 1.53.107 ॥
navārcirlohitāṅgastu prajāpatisuto grahaḥ ।
āṣāḍhāsviha pūrvāsu samutpanna iti śrutiḥ ॥ 1.53.108 ॥
revatīṣveva saptārci stathā sauraśanaiścaraḥ।
rohiṇīṣu samutpannau grahau candrārkamarddanau ॥ 1.53.109 ॥
ete tārāgrahāścaiva boddhavyā bhārgavādaya।
janmanakṣatrapīḍāsu yānti vaiguṇyatāṃ yataḥ।
spṛśante tena doṣeṇa tatastā grahabhaktiṣu ॥ 1.53.110 ॥
sarvagrahāṇāmeteṣāmādirāditya ucyate।
tārāgrahāṇāṃ śukrastu ketūnāñcaiva dhūmavān ॥ 1.53.111 ॥
dhruvaḥ kālo grahāṇāṃ tu vibhaktānāṃ caturdiśam ।
nakṣatrāṇāṃ śraviṣṭā syādayanānāṃ tathottaram ॥ 1.53.112 ॥
varṣāṇāñcāpi pañcānāmādyaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ।
ṛtūnāṃ śiśirañcāpi māsānāṃ māgha eva ca ॥ 1.53.113 ॥
pakṣāṇāṃ śuklapakṣastu tithīnāṃ pratipattathā।
ahorātravibhāgānāmahaścāpi prakīrtitam ॥ 1.53.114 ॥
muhūrttānāṃ tathaivādirmuhūrtto rudradaivataḥ।
akṣṇoścāpi nimeṣādiḥ kālaḥ kālavido mataḥ ॥ 1.53.115 ॥
śravaṇāntaṃ śraviṣṭādiyugaṃ syāt pañcavārṣikam।
bhānorgativiśeṣeṇa cakravat parivarttate ॥ 1.53.116 ॥
divākaraḥ smṛtastasmātkālastaṃ viddhi ceśvaram।
caturvanidhānāṃ bhūtānāṃ pravarttakanivarttakaḥ ॥ 1.53.117 ॥
ityeṣa jyotiṣāmeva sanniveśo'rthaniścayāt।
lokasaṃvyavahārārthamīśvareṇa vinirmitaḥ ॥ 1.53.118 ॥
utpannaḥ śravaṇenāsau saṃkṣiptaśca dhruve tathā।
sarvato'nteṣu vistīrṇo vṛkṣākāra iti sthitiḥ ॥ 1.53.119 ॥
buddhipūrvambhagavatā kalpādau saṃprakīrtitaḥ।
sāśrayaḥ so'bhimānī ca sarvasya jyotirātmakaḥ।
viśvarūpaḥ pradhānasya pariṇāmo'yamadbhutaḥ ॥ 1.53.120 ॥
naiva śakyaṃ prasaṃkhyātuṃ yāthātathyena kenacit।
gatāgataṃ manuṣyeṣu jyotiṣāṃ māṃsacakṣuṣā ॥ 1.53.121 ॥
āgamādanumānācca pratyakṣādupapattitaḥ।
parīkṣya nipuṇaṃ bhaktyā śraddhātavyaṃ vipaścitā ॥ 1.53.122 ॥
cakṣuḥ śāstraṃ jalaṃ lekhyaṃ gaṇitaṃ buddhisattamāḥ।
pañcaite hetavo jñeyā jyotirgaṇavicintane ॥ 1.53.123 ॥
devabhaktā mahātmāno munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ।
tacchutvā bhāvitātmāno munayaḥ śaṃśitavratāḥ।
vālakhilyeti vikhyātāḥ pataṅgasahacāriṇaḥ ॥ 1.54.8 ॥
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi munīnāmūrddhvaretasām।
tasmāt pṛcchanti vai vāyuṃ vāyuparṇāmbubhojanāḥ ॥ 1.54.9 ॥
nīlakaṇṭeti yat proktaṃ tvayā pavanasattama।
etadduhyaṃ pavitrāṇāṃ puṇyaṃ puṇyakṛtāṃ varāḥ ॥ 1.54.10 ॥
tadvayaṃ śrotumicchāmastvatprasādātprabhañjana।
nīlatā yena kaṇṭhasya kāraṇenāmbikāpateḥ ॥ 1.54.11 ॥
śrotumicchā mahe samyak tava vakrādviśeṣataḥ।
varṇasthānagate vāyau vāgvidhiḥ saṃpravartate।
jñānaṃ pūrvamathotsāha stvatto vāyo pravartate ।। 54.13 .
tvayi niṣpandamāne tu śeṣā varṇapravṛttayaḥ।
yatra vāco nivartante dehabandhāśca durlabhāḥ ॥ 1.54.13 ॥
tatrāpi te'sti sadbhāvaḥ sarvagastvaṃ sadānila।
nānyaḥ sarvagato devastvadṛteśasti samīraṇa ॥ 1.54.14 ॥
eṣa vai jīvalokaste pratyakṣaḥ sarvato'nila।
vettha vācaspatiṃ devaṃ manonāyakamīsvaram ॥ 1.54.15 ॥
brūhi tatkaṇṭhadeśasya kiṃ kṛtā rūpavikriyā।
śrutvā vākyantatasteṣāmṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmānām।
pratyuvāca mahātejā vāyurloka namaskṛtaḥ ॥ 1.54.16 ॥
purā kṛtayuge vipro vedanirṇayatatparaḥ।
vasiṣṭo nāma dharmātmā mānaso vai prajāpateḥ ॥ 1.54.17 ॥
prapaccha kārtikeyaṃ vai mayūravaravāhanam।
mahiṣāsuranārīṇāṃ nayanāñjanataskaram ॥ 1.54.18 ॥
mahāsenaṃ mahātmānaṃ meghastanitaniḥsvanam।
umāmanaḥpraharṣeṇa bālakaṃ chajharūpiṇam ॥ 1.54.19 ॥
krauñcajīvitaharttāraṃ pārvatīhṛdi nandanam।
yadetaddṛśyate varṇaṃ śubhaṃ śubhrāñjanaprabham।
tatkimarthaṃ samutpannaṃ kaṇṭe kundendusaṃprabhe ॥ 1.54.24 ॥
kathāṃ maṅgalasaṃyuktāṃ pavitrāṃ pāpanāśinīm ।
matpriyārthaṃ mahābhāga vaktumarhasyaśeṣataḥ ॥ 1.54.25 ॥
śrutvā vākyaṃ tatastasya vasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ।
pratyuvāca mahātejāḥ surāribalasūdanaḥ ॥ 1.54.26 ॥
śrṛṇuṣva vadatāṃ śreṣṭha kathyamānaṃ vaco mama।
umotsaṅganiviṣṭena mayā pūrvaṃ yathāśrutam ॥ 1.54.27 ॥
pārvatyā saha saṃvādaḥ śarvasya ca mahātmanaḥ।
tadahaṅkīrttayiṣyāmi tvatpriyārthaṃ mahāmune ॥ 1.54.28 ॥
kailāsaśikhare ramye nānādhātuvicitrite।
nānādrumalatākīrṇe cakravākopaśobhite ॥ 1.54.29 ॥
ṣaṭ‌padodgītabahule dhārāsampātanādite।
mattakrauñcamayūrāṇāṃ nādairudghuṣṭakandare ॥ 1.54.30 ॥
apsarogaṇasaṅkīrṇe kinnaraiścopaśobhite ।
kokilārāvamadhure siddha cāraṇasevite।
saurabhaiyīninādāḍhye adhastanitaniḥsvane ॥ 1.54.32 ॥
vināyakabhayodvigne kuñjarairyuktakandare।
vīṇāvāditranirghoṣaiḥ śrotrendriyamanoramaiḥ ॥ 1.54.33 ॥
dolālambitasampāte vanitāsaṅghasevite।
dhvajairlambitadolānāṃ ghaṇṭānāṃ ninadākule ॥ 1.54.34 ॥
mukhamardalavāditrairbalināṃ sphoṭitaistathā।
krīḍāravavicārāṇāṃ nirghoṣaiḥ pūrṇamandire ॥ 1.54.35 ॥
dehagandhairvicitraiśca prakrīḍitagaṇeścaraiḥ ॥ 1.54.36 ॥
vajrasphaṭikasopāna citrapaṭṭiśilātalaiḥ।
vyādhrasiṃhamukhaiśacavānyairgajavājimukhaistathā ॥ 1.54.37 ॥
biḍālavadanaiścograiḥ kroṣṭukākāramūrtibhiḥ ।
hrasvairdīrghaiḥ kṛśaiḥ sthūlairlambodara mahodaraiḥ ॥ 1.54.38 ॥
hrasvajaṅghaiśca lamboṣṭaistālajaṅghaistathāparaiḥ।
gaukarṇairekakarṇaiśca mahākarṇairakarṇakaiḥ ॥ 1.54.39 ॥
bahupādairmahāpādairekapādairapādakaiḥ।
bahuśīrṣairmahāśīrṣairekaśīrṣairaśīrṣakaiḥ ॥ 1.54.40 ॥
bahunetrairmahānetrairekanaitrairanaitrakaiḥ ।
evaṃvidhairmahāyogibhūtairbhūtapatirvṛtaḥ ॥ 1.54.41 ॥
viśuddhamuktāmaṇiratnabhūṣite śilātale hemamaye manorame।
sukhopaviṣṭaṃ madanāṅganāśanaṃ provāca vākyaṃ girirājaputrī ॥ 1.54.42 ॥
bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa govṛṣāṅkitaśāsana।
tava kaṇṭe mahādeva bhrājate'mbudaśannibham ॥ 1.54.43 ॥
nātyulbaṇaṃ nātiśubraṃ nīlāñjanacayopamam।
kimidaṃ dīpyate deva kaṇṭe kāmāṅga nāśana ॥ 1.54.44 ॥
ko hetuḥ kāraṇaṃ kiñca kaṇṭe nīlatvamīśvaraḥ ।
etatsarvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ brūhi kautūhalaṃ hime ॥ 1.54.45 ॥
śrutvā vākyaṃ tatastasyāḥ pārvatyāḥ pārvatīpriyaḥ ।
kathāṃ maṅgalasaṃyuktāṃ kathayāmāsa śaṅkaraḥ ॥ 1.54.46 ॥
mathyamāne'mṛte pūrvaṃ kṣīrode suradānavaiḥ।
agre samutthitaṃ tasmin viṣaṃ kālānalaprabham ॥ 1.54.47 ॥
taṃ dṛṣṭvā surasaṅghāśca daityāścaiva varānane।
viṣaṇṇavadanāḥ sarve gatāste brahmaṇo'ntikam ॥ 1.54.48 ॥
dṛṣṭvā suragaṇān bhītān brahmo vāca mahādyutiḥ।
kimarthaṃ bho mahābhāgā bhītā udvignacetasaḥ ॥ 1.54.49 ॥
mayāṣṭaguṇamaiśvaryaṃ bhavatāṃ samprakalpitam।
kena vyāvarttitaiśvaryā yūyaṃ vai surasattamāḥ ॥ 1.54.50 ॥
trailokyasyeśvarā yūyaṃ sarve vai vigatajvarāḥ।
prajāsarge na so'stīha ājñāṃ yo me nivarttayet ॥ 1.54.51 ॥
vimānagāminaḥ sarve sarve svacchandagāminaḥ।
adhyātme cādhibhūte ca adhidaive ca nityaśaḥ।
prajāḥ karmavipākena śaktā yūyaṃ pravarttitum ॥ 1.54.52 ॥
tatkimarthaṃ bhayodvignā mṛgāḥ siṃhārditā iva।
kiṃ duḥkhaṃ kena santāpaḥ kulo vā bhayamāgatam।
etatsarvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ śīgramākhyātumarhatha ॥ 1.54.53 ॥
śrutvā vākyaṃ tatastasya brahmaṇo vai mahātmanaḥ।
ūcuste ṛṣibhiḥ sārdhdhaṃ suradaityendradānavāḥ ॥ 1.54.54 ॥
surāsurairmathyamāne pāthodhau ca mahātmabhiḥ।
bhujaṅgabhṛṅgasaṅkāśaṃ nīlajīmūtasannibham।
prādurbhūtaṃ viṣaṃ ghoraṃ saṃvartāgnisamaprabham ॥ 1.54.55 ॥
kālamṛtyurivodbhūtaṃ yugāntādityavarcasam।
trailokyotsādi sūryābhaṃ prasphurantaṃ samantataḥ ॥ 1.54.56 ॥
viṣeṇottiṣṭhamānena kālānalasamatviṣā।
nirdagdho raktagaurāṅgaḥ kṛtakṛṣṇo janārdanaḥ ॥ 1.54.57 ॥
dṛṣṭvā taṃ raktagaurāṅgaṃ kṛtakṛṣṇaṃ janārdanam।
bhītāḥ sarve vayaṃ devāstvāmeva śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ॥ 1.54.58 ॥
surāṇāmasurāṇāñca śrutvā vākyaṃ pitāmahaḥ।
pratyuvāca mahātejā lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ॥ 1.54.59 ॥
śrṛṇudhvaṃ devatāḥ sarve ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ।
yattadagre samutpannaṃ mathyamāne mahodadhau ॥ 1.54.60 ॥
viṣaṃ kālānalaprakhyaṃ kālakūṭeti viśrutam।
tasya viṣṇurahañcāpi sarve te surapuṅgavāḥ।
na śaknuvanti vai soḍhuṃ vegamanye tu śaṅkarāt ॥ 1.54.62 ॥
ityuktvā pajhagarbhābhaḥ pajhayonirayonijaḥ ।
tataḥ stotuṃ samārabdho brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ॥ 1.54.63 ॥
namastubhyaṃ virūpākṣa namaste'nekacakṣuṣe।
namaḥ pinākahastāya vajrahastāya vai namaḥ ॥ 1.54.64 ॥
namastrailokyanāthāya bhūtānāmpataye namaḥ।
namaḥ surārisaṃhartre tāpasāya tricakṣuṣe ॥ 1.54.65 ॥
brahamaṇe caiva rudrāya viṣṇave caiva te namaḥ।
sāṅkhyāya caiva yogāya bhūtagrāmāya vai namaḥ ॥ 1.54.66 ॥
manmatāṅgavināśāya kālakālāya vai namaḥ।
kapardine karālāya śaṅkarāya kapāline।
virūpāyaikarūpāya śivāya varadāya ca ॥ 1.54.67 ॥
tripuraghnāya vandyāya mātṝṇāmpataye namaḥ।
buddhāya caiva śuddhāya muktāya kevalāya ca ॥ 1.54.68 ॥
namaḥ kamalahastāya digvāsāya śikhaṇḍine ।
loka trayavalidhātre ca candrāya varuṇāya ca ॥ 1.54.69 ॥
agrāya caiva cogrāya viprāyānekacakṣuṣe।
rajase caiva sattvāya tamase'vyaktayonaye ॥ 1.54.70 ॥
nityāyānityarūpāya nityānityāya vai namaḥ।
vyaktāya caivāvyaktāya vyaktāvyaktāya vai namaḥ ॥ 1.54.71 ॥
cintyāya caivācintyāya cintyācintyāya vai namaḥ।
bhaktānāmārtināśāya naranārāyaṇāya ca ॥ 1.54.72 ॥
umāpriyāya śarvāya nandicakrāṅkitāya ca।
pakṣamāsārddhamāsāya namaḥ saṃvatsarāya ca ॥ 1.54.73 ॥
bahurūpāya muṇḍāya daṇḍine'tha varūthine।
namaḥ kapālahastāya digvāsāya śikhaṇiḍane ॥ 1.54.74 ॥
dhvajine rathine caiva yamine brahmacāriṇe।
ṛgyajuḥ sāmavedāya puruṣāyeśvarāya ca।
evaṃ stutastato devaiḥ praṇipatya varānane ॥ 1.54.76 ॥
jñātvā tu bhaktiṃ mama devadevo gaṅgājalāplāvitakeśadeśaḥ।
sūkṣmo'tiyogātiśayādacintyo na hi pluto vyaktamupaiti candraḥ ॥ 1.54.77 ॥
evaṃ bhagavatā pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇā।
stuto'haṃ vividhaiḥ stotrai rvedavedāṅgasambhavaiḥ ॥ 1.54.78 ॥
tato'haṃ sūkṣmayā vācā pitāmahamathābruvam ॥ 1.54.79 ॥
kiṃ kārye te mayā brahman karttavyaṃ vada suvrata ॥ 1.54.80 ॥
śrutvā vākyaṃ tato brahmā pratyuvācāmbujekṣaṇaḥ ।
bhūtabhavyabhavannātha śrūyatāṃ kāraṇeśvara ॥ 1.54.81 ॥
surāsurairmathyamāne payodhāvambujekṣaṇa।
bhagavanmegha saṅkāśaṃ nīlajīmūtasannibham ॥ 1.54.82 ॥
prādurbhūtaṃ viṣaṅghoraṃ saṃvarttāgnisamaprabham।
kālamṛtyurivodbhūtaṃ yugāntādityavarccasam ॥ 1.54.83 ॥
trailokyotsādi sūryābhaṃ visphurantaṃ samantataḥ।
agre samutthitaṃ tasmin viṣaṅkālānalaprabham ॥ 1.54.84 ॥
taṃ dṛṣṭvā tuṃ vayaṃ sarve bhītāḥ sambhrāntacetasaḥ।
tat pibasva mahādeva lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।
tvāmṛte'nyo mahādeva viṣaṃ soḍhuṃ na vidyate ।
evaṃ tasya vacaḥ śrutvā brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭinaḥ।
bāḍhamityeva tadvākyaṃ pratigṛhya varānane ॥ 1.54.87 ॥
tato'haṃ pātumārabdho viṣamantakasannibham।
pibato me mahāghoraṃ viṣaṃ surabhayaṅkaram।
kaṇṭhaḥ samabhavattūrṇaṃ kṛṣṇo me varavarṇini ॥ 1.54.88 ॥
taṃdṛṣṭvo tpalapatrābhaṃ kaṇṭe saktamivoragam ।
takṣakaṃ nāgarājānaṃ lelihānamiva sthitam ॥ 1.54.89 ॥
athovāca mahātejā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ।
śobhase tvaṃ mahādeva kaṇṭenānena suvrata ॥ 1.54.90 ॥
tatastasya vacaḥ śrutvā mayā girivarātmaje।
paśyatāṃ devasaṅgānāṃ daityānāñca varānane ॥ 1.54.91 ॥
yakṣagandharvabhūtānāṃ piśācoragarakṣasām।
dhṛtaṃ kaṇṭe viṣaṃ ghoraṃ nīlakaṇṭastato hyaham ॥ 1.54.92 ॥
tat kālakūṭaṃ viṣamugratejaḥ kaṇṭe mayā parvatarājaputri।
niveśyamānaṃ suradaityasaṅgho dṛṣṭvā paraṃ vismayamājagāma ॥ 1.54.93 ॥
tataḥ suragaṇāḥ sarve sadaityoragarākṣasāḥ।
ūcuḥ prāñcalayo bhūtvā mattamātaṅgagāmini ॥ 1.54.94 ॥
aho balaṃ vīryaparākramaste aho punaryogabalaṃ tavaiva।
tvameva viṣṇuścaturānanastvaṃ tvameva mṛtyu rvaradastvameva।
tvameva sūryo rajanīkaraśca tvameva bhūmiḥ salilaṃ tvameva ॥ 1.54.96 ॥
itīdamuktvā vacanaṃ surendrāḥ pragṛhya somaṃ praṇipatya mūrdnā।
gatā vimānairanigṛhya vegairmahātmano merumupetya sarve ॥ 1.54.99 ॥
ityetatparamaṃ guhyaṃ puṇyātpuṇyamahattaram।
yastu dhārayate nityamenāṃ brahmodbhavāṃ kathām।
tasyāhaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi phalaṃ vai vipulaṃ mahat ॥ 1.54.101 ॥
viṣaṃ tasya varārohe sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamantathā।
gātraṃ prāpya ca suśroṇi kṣipraṃ tat pratihanyate ॥ 1.54.102 ॥
śamayatyaśubhaṃ ghoraṃ duḥsvapnañcāpakarṣati।
strīṣu vallabhatāṃ yāti sabhāyāṃ pārthivasya ca ॥ 1.54.103 ॥
vivāde jayamāpnoti yuddhe śūratvameva ca।
gacchataḥ kṣemamadhvānaṃ gṛhe ca nityasampadaḥ ॥ 1.54.104 ॥
śarīrabhede vakṣyāmi gatiṃ tasya varānane।
nīlakaṇṭo haricchamaśruḥ śaśāṅkāṅkitamūrddhajaḥ ॥ 1.54.105 ॥
tryakṣastriśūlapāṇiśca vṛṣayānaḥ pinākadhṛk।
nandhitulyabalaḥ śrīmān nanditulyaparākramaḥ ॥ 1.54.106 ॥
vicaratyacirāt sarvān sarvalokānmamājñayā ।
na hanyate gatistasya anilasya yathāmbare।
mama tulyabalo bhūtvā tiṣṭhatyābhūtasamplavam ॥ 1.54.107 ॥
mama bhaktā varārohe ye ca śrṛṇvanti mānavāḥ।
teṣāṃ gatiṃ pravakṣyāmi iha loke paratra ca ॥ 1.54.108 ॥
brāhmaṇo vedamāpnoti kṣatriyo jayate mahīm।
vaiśyastu labhate lābhaṃ śūdraḥ sukhamavāpnuyāt ॥ 1.54.109 ॥
vyādhito mucyate rogādbaddho mucyeta bandhanāt।
gurviṇī labhate putraṃ kanyā vindati satpatim।
naṣṭañca labhate sarvamihaloke paratra ca ॥ 1.54.110 ॥
gavāṃ śatasahasrasya samyagdattasya yat phalam।
tat phalaṃ bhavati śrutvā vibhordivyāmimāṃ kathām ॥ 1.54.111 ॥
pādaṃ vā yadi vāpyarddhaṃ ślokaṃ ślokārddhameva vā।
yastu dhārayate nityaṃ rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ॥ 1.54.112 ॥
kathāmimāṃ puṇyaphalādiyuktāṃ nivedya devyāḥ śaśibaddha mūrddhajaḥ।
vṛṣasya pṛṣṭena sahomayā prabhurjagāma kiṣkindhaguhāṃ guhapriyaḥ ॥ 1.54.113 ॥
adhītya sarvaṃ tvakhilaṃ sulakṣaṇaṃ jagāma ādityapathaṃ dvijottamaḥ ॥ 1.54.114 ॥
śrotumicchāmahe samyagāścaryaṃ guṇavistaram ॥ 1.55.1 ॥
atrāpyudāharantīmamiti hāsaṃ purātanam ।
mahādevasya māhātmyaṃ vibhutvañca mahātmanaḥ ॥ 1.55.2 ॥
pūrvaṃ trailokyavijaye viṣṇunā samudāhṛtam।
baliṃ baddhvā mahaujāstu trailokyādhi patiḥ purā ॥ 1.55.3 ॥
praṇaṣṭeṣu ca daityeṣu prahṛṣṭe ca śacīpatau।
athājagmuḥ prabhuṃ draṣṭuṃ sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ ॥ 1.55.4 ॥
yatrāste viśvarūpātmā kṣīrodasya samī pataḥ।
siddhabrahmarṣayo yakṣā gandharvāpsarasāṅgaṇāḥ ॥ 1.55.5 ॥
nāgā devarṣayaścaiva nadyaḥ sarve ca parvatāḥ।
abhigamya mahātmānaṃ stuvanti puruṣaṃ harim ॥ 1.55.6 ॥
tvaṃ dhātā tvañca karttā'sya tvaṃ lokān sṛjasi prabho।
tvatprasādācca kalyāṇaṃ prāptaṃ trailokyamavyayam।
asurāśca jitāḥ sarve balirbaddhaśca vai tvayā ॥ 1.55.7 ॥
eva muktaḥ surairviṣṇuḥ siddhaiśca paramarṣibhiḥ।
pratyuvāca tato devān sarvāṃstān puruṣottamaḥ ॥ 1.55.8 ॥
śrūyatāmabhidhāsyāmi kāraṇaṃ surasattamāḥ।
yaḥ sraṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ kālaḥ kālakaraḥ prabhuḥ ॥ 1.55.9 ॥
yena hi brahmaṇā sārddhaṃ sṛṣṭā lokāśca māyayā।
tasyaiva ca prasādena ādau siddhatvamāgatam ॥ 1.55.10 ॥
purā tamasi cāvyakte trailokye grāsite mayā।
udarastheṣu bhūteṣu loke'haṃ śayitastadā ॥ 1.55.11 ॥
sahasraśīrṣā bhūtvā ca sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt।
śaṅkhacakragadā pāṇiḥ śayito vimale'mbhasi ॥ 1.55.12 ॥
etasminnantare dūrāt paśyāmi hyamitaprabham।
śatasūryapratīkāśaṃ jvalantaṃ svena tejasā ॥ 1.55.13 ॥
caturvakraṃ mahā yogaṃ puruṣaṃ kāñcanaprabham।
kṛṣṇājinadharaṃ devaṃ kamaṇḍaluvibhūṣitam।
nimeṣāntaramātreṇa prāpto'sau puruṣottamaḥ ॥ 1.55.14 ॥
tato māmabravīdbrahmā sarvaloka namaskṛtaḥ।
kastvaṃ kuto vā kiñceha tiṣṭhase vada me vibho ॥ 1.55.15 ॥
ahaṃ karttā'smi lokānāṃ svayambūrviśvatomukhaḥ।
evamuktastadā dena brahmaṇāhamuvāca tam ॥ 1.55.16 ॥
ahaṃ karttā ca lokānāṃ saṃharttā ca punaḥ punaḥ।
uttarāṃ diśamāsthāya jvālā dṛṣṭāpyadhiṣṭitā ॥ 1.55.17 ॥
jvālāntatastāmālokya vismittau ca tadānayoḥ ।
varddhamāne tadā vahnāvatyantaparamādbhute।
atidudrāva tāṃ jvālāṃ brahmā cāhañca satvaraḥ ॥ 1.55.19 ॥
divaṃ bhūmiñca viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhantaṃ jvālamaṇḍalam।
tasya jvālasya madhye tu paśyāvo vipulaprabham ॥ 1.55.20 ॥
prādeśamātramavyaktaṃ liṅgaṃ paramadīpitam।
na ca tatkāñcanaṃ madhye na śailaṃ na ca rājatam ॥ 1.55.21 ॥
anirddeśyamacintyañca lakṣyālakṣyaṃ punaḥ punaḥ।
jvālāmālāyataṃ nyastaṃ sarvabhūtabhayaṅkaram ॥ 1.55.22 ॥
ghora rūpiṇamatyarthaṃ bhindantamiva rodasī ॥ 1.55.23 ॥
tato māmabravīdbrahmā adho gaccha tvatandritaḥ।
antamasya vijānīmo liṅgasya tu mahātmanaḥ ॥ 1.55.24 ॥
ahamūrddhvaṃ gamiṣyāmi yāvadanto'sya dṛśyate।
tadā tau samayaṃ kṛtvā gatāvūrddhvamadhaśca ha ॥ 1.55.25 ॥
tato varṣasahasrantu ahaṃ punaradho gataḥ।
na ca paśyāmi tasyāntaṃ bhītaścāhaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ॥ 1.55.26 ॥
samāgato mayā sārddhaṃ tatraiva ca mahāmbhasi ॥ 1.55.27 ॥
tato vismayamāpannāvubhau tasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
māyayā mohitau tena naṣṭasaṃjñau vyavasthitau ॥ 1.55.28 ॥
tato dhyānagatantatra īśvaraṃ sarvatomukham।
prabhavaṃ nidhaऩñcaiva lokānāṃ prabhumavyayam ॥ 1.55.29 ॥
brahmāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā tasmai śarvāya śūline।
mahābhairavanādāya bhīmarūpāya daṃṣṭriṇe।
avyaktāya mahāntāya namaskāraṃ prakurmahe ॥ 1.55.30 ॥
namo'stu te lokasureśa deva namo'stu te bhūtapate mahāṃśca।
namo'stu te śāśvata siddhayone namo'stu te sarvajagatpratiṣṭha ॥ 1.55.31 ॥
parameṣṭī paraṃ brahma akṣaraṃ paramaṃ padam।
śreṣṭhastvaṃ vāmadevaśca rudraḥ skandaḥ śivaḥ prabhuḥ ॥ 1.55.32 ॥
tvaṃ yajñastvaṃ vaṣaṭ‌kārastvamoṅkāraḥ paraṃ padam।
svāhākāro namaskāraḥ saṃskāraḥ sarvakarmaṇām ॥ 1.55.33 ॥
svadhākāraśca jāpyaśca vratāni niyamāstathā।
vedā lokāśca devāśca bhagavāneva sarvaśaḥ ॥ 1.55.34 ॥
ākāśasya ca śabdastvaṃ bhūtānāṃ prabhavāvyayam।
bhūmergandho rasaśvāpāṃ tejorūpaṃ maheśvara ॥ 1.55.35 ॥
vāyoḥ ruparśaśca devaśca vapuścandramasastathā ।
budho jñānañca deveśa prakṛtau bījameva ca ॥ 1.55.36 ॥
tvaṃ karttā sarvabhūtānāṃ kālo mṛtyuryamo'ntakaḥ।
tvaṃ dhārayasi lokāstrīṃstvameva sṛjasi prabho ॥ 1.55.37 ॥
pūrveṇa vadanena tvamindratvañca prakāśase।
dakṣiṇena ca vakreṇa lokān saṃkṣīyase prabho ॥ 1.55.38 ॥
paścimena tu vakreṇa varuṇatvaṃ karoṣi vai।
uttareṇa tu vakreṇa saumyatvañca vyavasthitam ॥ 1.55.39 ॥
rājase bahudhā deva lokānāṃ prabhavāvyayaḥ।
ādityā vasavo rudrā marutaścāśvinīsutau ॥ 1.55.40 ॥
sādhyā vidyādharā nāgāśvāraṇāśca tapodhanāḥ.
vālakhilyā mahātmānastapaḥ siddhāśca suvratāḥ ॥ 1.55.41 ॥
tvattaḥ prasūtā deveśa ye cānye niyatavratāḥ।
umā sītā sinī vālī kuhūrgāyatrireva ca ॥ 1.55.42 ॥
lakṣmīḥ kīrttirdhṛtirmedhā lajjā kṣāntirvapuḥ svadhā।
tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ kriyā caiva vācāṃ devī sarasvatī।
tvattaḥ prasūtā deveśa sandhyā rātristathaiva ca ॥ 1.55.43 ॥
sūryāyutānāmayutaprabhā ca namo'stu te candrasahasragocara।
namo'stu te bhasmavibhūṣitāṅga namo'stu te kāmaśarīranāśana।
namo'stu te deva hiraṇyavāsase namo'stu te deva hiraṇyabāhave ॥ 1.55.46 ॥
namo'stu te deva hiraṇyarūpa namo'stu te deva hiraṇyanābha।
namo'stu te netrasahasracitra namo'stu te deva hiraṇyaretaḥ ॥ 1.55.47 ॥
namo'stu te deva hiraṇyavarṇa namo'stu te deva hiraṇyagarbha।
namo'stu te deva hiraṇyacīra namo'stu te deva hiraṇyadāyine ॥ 1.55.48 ॥
namo'stu te deva hiraṇyamāline namo'stu te deva hiraṇyavāhine।
namo'stu te deva hiraṇyacīra namo'stu te bhairavanādanādine ॥ 1.55.49 ॥
evaṃ saṃstūyamānastu vyakto bhūtvā mahāmatiḥ।
vakrakoṭisahasreṇa grasamāna ivāparam ॥ 1.55.52 ॥
ekagrīvastvekajaṭo nānābhūṣaṇbhūṣitaḥ।
nānācitravicitrāṅgo nānāmālyānulepanaḥ ॥ 1.55.53 ॥
pinākapāṇirbhagavān vṛṣabhāsanaśūladhṛk ।
vyālayajñopavītī ca surāṇāmabhayaṅkaraḥ।
dundubhisvananirghoṣaparjanyaninadopamaḥ।
mukto hāsastadā tena nabhaḥ sarvamapūrayat ॥ 1.55.55 ॥
tena śabdena mahatā vayaṃ bhītā mahātmanaḥ।
tadovāca mahāyogī prīto'haṃ surasattamau ॥ 1.55.56 ॥
paśyetāñca mahāmāyāṃ bhayaṃ sarvaṃ pramucyatām ।
yuvāṃ prasūtau gātreṣu mama pūrvasanātanau ॥ 1.55.57 ॥
ayaṃ me dakṣiṇo bāhurbrahmā lokapitāmahaḥ।
vāmo bāhuśca me viṣṇurnityaṃ yuddheṣu tiṣṭhati।
prīto'haṃ yuvayoḥ samyagvaraṃ dajhi yathepsitam ॥ 1.55.58 ॥
tataḥ prahṛṣṭamanasau praṇatau pādayoḥ punaḥ ।
yadi prītiḥ samutpannā yadi deyo varaśca nau।
bhaktirbhavatu nau nityaṃ tvayi deva sureśvara ॥ 1.55.60 ॥
evamastu mahābhāgau sṛjatāṃ vividhāḥ prajāḥ।
evamuktvā sa bhagavāṃstatraivāntaradhīyata ॥ 1.55.61 ॥
evameṣa mayokto vaḥ prabhāvastasya yoginaḥ।
etaddhi rūpamajñātamavyaktaṃ śivasaṃjñitam।
tasmai devādhipatyāya namaskāraṃ prayuṅkta ha।
yena sūkṣmamacintyañca paśyanti jñānacakṣuṣaḥ ॥ 1.55.64 ॥
mahādeva namaste'stu maheśvara namo'stu te।
etacchrutvā gatāḥ sarve surāḥ svaṃ svaṃ niveśanam।
namaskāraṃ prayuñjānāḥ śaṅkarāya mahātmane ॥ 1.55.66 ॥
imaṃ stavaṃ paṭedyastu īśvarasya mahātmanaḥ।
kāmāṃśca labhate sarvān pāpebhyastu vimucyate ॥ 1.55.67 ॥
etatsarvaṃ sadā tena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā।
mahādevaprasādena uktaṃ brahma sanātanam।
etadvaḥ sarvamākhyātaṃ mayā māheśvaraṃ balam ॥ 1.55.68 ॥
agātkathamamāvāsyāṃ māsi māsi divaṃ nṛpaḥ।
ailaḥ purūravāḥ sūta kathaṃ vā'tarpayat pitṝn ॥ 1.56.1 ॥
tasya cāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi prabhāvaṃ śāṃśapāyana।
ailasyādityasaṃyogaṃ somasya ca mahātmanaḥ ॥ 1.56.2 ॥
apāṃsāramayasyendoḥ pakṣayoḥ śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ।
hrāsavṛddhī pitṛmataḥ pakṣasya ca vinirṇayaḥ ॥ 1.56.3 ॥
somāccaivāmṛtaprāptiḥ pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ tathā।
kavyāgneścāttasomānāṃ pitṝṇāñcaiva darśanam ॥ 1.56.4 ॥
yathā purūravāścaila tarpayāmāsa vai pitṝn।
etatsarvaṃ pravakṣyāmi parvāṇi ca yathākramam ॥ 1.56.5 ॥
yadā tu candrasūryau tau nakṣatreṇa samāgatau।
amāvāsyānnivasata ekarātraikamaṇḍale ॥ 1.56.6 ॥
sa gacchati tadā draṣṭuṃ divākaraniśākarau।
amāvasyāmamāvāsyāṃ mātāmahapitāmahau।
abhivādya tadā tatra kālāpekṣaḥ pratīkṣyate ॥ 1.56.7 ॥
uvāste pitṛmantaṃ taṃ sasomaṃ sa divāsthitaḥ ॥ 1.56.8 ॥
dvilavaṃ kuhumātraṃ tu te ubhe tu vicārya saḥ।
sinīvālīpramāṇena sinīvālīmupāsakaḥ ॥ 1.56.9 ॥
kuhūmātrāṃ kalāñcaiva jñātvopāste kuhuṃ punaḥ।
sudhāmṛtaṃ kutaḥ somāt prasravenmāsatṛptaye।
daśabhiḥ pañcabhiścaiva sudhāmṛtaparisravaiḥ ॥ 1.56.11 ॥
kṛṣṇapakṣe tadā pītvā duhyamānaṃ tathāṃśubhiḥ।
sadyaḥ pakṣaratā tena saumyena madhunā ca saḥ ॥ 1.56.12 ॥
sudhāmṛtena rājendrastarpayāmāsa vai pitṝn।
saumyā barhiṣadaḥ kāvyā agniṣvāttāstathaiva ca ॥ 1.56.13 ॥
ṛturagnistu yaḥ proktaḥ sa tu saṃvatsaro mataḥ।
jajñire hyṛtavastasmādṛtubhyaścārttavāśca ye । 56.14 ।।
ārttavā hyarddhamāsākhyāḥ pitaro hyabdasūnavaḥ।
prapitāmahāstu vai devāḥ pañcābdā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ।
saumyāstu saumyajā jñeyāḥ kāvyā jñeyāḥ kaveḥ sutāḥ ॥ 1.56.15 ॥
upahūtāḥ smṛtāḥ devāḥ somajāḥ somapāstathā।
ājyapāstu smṛtāḥ kāvyāstṛpyanti pitṛjātayaḥ ॥ 1.56.16 ॥
kāvyā barhiṣadaścaiva agniṣvāttāśca te tridhā।
gṛhasthā ye ca yajvānā ṛturbarhiṣado dhruvam ॥ 1.56.17 ॥
gṛhasthāścāpi yajvānā agniṣvāttāstathārttavāḥ।
aṣṭakāpatayaḥ kāvyāḥ pañcābdāstānnibodhata ॥ 1.56.18 ॥
eṣāṃ saṃvatsaro hyagniḥ sūryastu parivatsaraḥ।
soma īdvatsaraḥ prokto vāyuścaivānuvatsaraḥ ॥ 1.56.19 ॥
rudrastu vatsarasteṣāṃ pañcābdā ye yugātmakāḥ।
leśāśvaivoṣmapāścaiva divākīrtyāśca te smṛtāḥ ॥ 1.56.20 ॥
ete pibantyamāvāsyāṃ māsi māsi sudhāṃ divi ।
tāṃstena tarpayāmāsa yāvadāsīt purūravāḥ ॥ 1.56.21 ॥
yasmāt prasravate somānmāsi māsi nibodhata।
tasmāt sudhāmṛtaṃ dvai pitṝṇāṃ somapāyinām ॥ 1.56.22 ॥
evaṃ tadamṛtaṃ saumyaṃ sudhā ca madhu caiva ha ।
kṛṣṇapakṣe yathā cendoḥ kalāḥ pañcadaśa kramāt ॥ 1.56.23 ॥
pibantyambumayīrde vāstrayastriṃśattu chandajāḥ।
pītvā ca māsaṃ gacchanti caturddaśyāṃ sudhāmṛtam ॥ 1.56.24 ॥
samāgacchadamāvāsyāṃ bhāge pañcadaśe sthitaḥ ।। 56.26।
suṣumnāpyāyitañcaiva amāvāsyāṃ yathākramam।
pibanti dvikalaṃ kālaṃ pitaraste sudhāmṛtam ॥ 1.56.25 ॥
niḥśeṣāyāṃ kalāyāntu somamāpyāyayat punaḥ।
suṣumnāpyāyamānasya bhāgaṃ bhāga mahaḥkramāt।
kalāḥ kṣīyanti tāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ śuklāścāpyāyayanti ca ॥ 1.56.27 ॥
evaṃ sūryasya vīryeṇa candrasyāpyāyitā tanuḥ।
dṛśyate paurṇamāsyāṃ vai śuklaḥ sampūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ।
saṃsiddhirevaṃ somasya pakṣayoḥ śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ ॥ 1.56.28 ॥
krāntaḥ paṃcadaśaiḥ sārddhaṃ sudhā mṛtaparisravaiḥ ॥ 1.56.29 ॥
ataḥ parvāṇi vakṣyāmi parvaṇāṃ sandhayastathā।
granthimanti yathā parvāṇīkṣuveṇvorbhavantyuta ॥ 1.56.30 ॥
tathārddhamāsaparvāṇi śuklakṛṣṇāni vai viduḥ।
pūrṇāmāvāsyayorbhedairgranthiryā sandhayaśca vai ।
arddhamāsāstu parvāṇi tṛtīyāprabhṛtīni tu ॥ 1.56.31 ॥
agnayādhānakriyā yasmāt kriyate parvasandhiṣu।
sāyāhne pratipaccaiva sa kālaḥ paurṇamāsikaḥ ॥ 1.56.32 ॥
vyatīpāte sthite sūrye lesorddhantu yugāntare।
yugāntarodite caiva lekhorddhaṃ śaśinaḥ kramāt ॥ 1.56.33 ॥
paurṇamāse vyatīpāte yadīkṣete parasparam।
yasminkāle sa sīmānte sa vyatīpāta eva tu ॥ 1.56.34 ॥
kālaṃ sūryasya nirddeśaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṅkhyā tu sarpati।
pūrṇendoḥ pūrṇapakṣe tu rātrisandhiṣu pūrṇimā।
yasmāttāmanupaśyanti pitaro daivataiḥ saha।
tasmādanumatirnāma pūrṇimā prathamā smṛtā ॥ 1.56.36 ॥
atyarthaṃ bhrājate yasmāt paurṇamāsyānniśākaraḥ।
rañjanāccaiva candrasya rāketi kavayo viduḥ ॥ 1.56.37 ॥
amā vasetāmṛkṣe tu yadā candradivākarau।
ekāṃ pañcadaśīṃ rātrimamāvāsyā tataḥ smṛtā ॥ 1.56.38 ॥
yadīkṣate vyatīpāte divā pūrṇe parasparam।
candrārkāvaparāhne tu pūrṇātmānau tu pūrṇimā ॥ 1.56.39 ॥
vicchinnāṃ tāmamāvāsyāṃ paśyataśca samāgatau।
anyonyaṃ candrasūryau tau yadā taddarśa ucyate ॥ 1.56.40 ॥
dvau dvau lavāvamāvāsyāṃ yaḥ kālaḥ parvasandhiṣu।
divasārddhena rātryarddhaṃ sūryaṃ prāpya tu candramāḥ.
sūryeṇa sahasā muktiṃ gatvā prātastanotsavau ।
dvau kālau saṅgamaścaiva madhyāhne niṣpatedraviḥ ॥ 1.56.42 ॥
pratipacchuklapakṣasya candramāḥ sūryamaṇḍalāt।
nirmucyamānayormadhye tayormaṇḍalayostu vai ॥ 1.56.43 ॥
sa tadā hyāhuteḥ kālo darśasya ca vaṣaṭkriyā।
etadṛtumukhaṃ jñeyamamāvāsyāsya parvaṇaḥ ॥ 1.56.44 ॥
divā parvaṇyamāvāsyāṃ kṣīṇendau bahule tu vai।
tasmāddivā hyamāvāsyāṃ gṛhyate'sau divākaraḥ।
gṛhyate vai divā hyasmādamāvāsyāṃ divikṣayaiḥ ॥ 1.56.45 ॥
tithīnāṃ nāma dheyāni vidvadbhiḥ saṃjñitāni vai ॥ 1.56.46 ॥
darśayetāmathānyonyaṃ sūryācandramasāvubhau ।
niṣkrāmatyatha tenaiva kramaśaḥ sūryamaṇḍalāt ॥ 1.56.47 ॥
dvilavena hyaho rātraṃ bhāskaraṃ spṛśate śaśī।
sa tadā hyāhuteḥ kālo darśasya ca vaṣaṭ‌kriyā ॥ 1.56.48 ॥
tatkālasaṃjñitā yasmādamāvāsyā kuhuḥ smṛtā ॥ 1.56.49 ॥
sinīvālīpramāṇena kṣīṇaśeṣo niśākaraḥ।
amāvāsyāṃ viśatyarkaṃ sinīvālī tataḥ smṛtā ॥ 1.56.50 ॥
candrasūryavyatīpāte ubhe te pūrṇime smṛte ॥ 1.56.51 ॥
pratipatpañcadaśyośca parvakālo dvimātrakaḥ।
arkāgnimaṇḍale some parvakālaḥ kalāśrayaḥ।
evaṃ sa śukrapakṣo vai rajanyāḥ parvasandhiṣu ॥ 1.56.53 ॥
sampūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ śrīmāṃścandramā uparajyate।
yasmādāpyāyate somaḥ pañcadaśyāntu pūrṇimā ॥ 1.56.54 ॥
daśabhiḥ pañcabhiścaiva kalābhirdivasakramāt।
tasmāt kalā pañcadaśī some nāsti tu ṣoḍaśī।
tasmātsomasya bhavati pañcadaśyāṃ mahākṣayaḥ ॥ 1.56.55 ॥
ityete pitaro devāḥ somapāḥ somavarddhanāḥ।
ataḥ pitṝn pravakṣyāmi māsaśrāddhabhujastu ye।
teṣāṃ gatiñca sattvañca gatiṃ śrāddhasya caiva hi ॥ 1.56.57 ॥
na mṛtānāṃ gatiḥ śakyā vijñātuṃ punarāgatiḥ।
tapasāpi prasiddhena kiṃ punarmāṃsacakṣuṣā ॥ 1.56.58 ॥
devāste pitaraḥ sarve devāstān bhāvayantyuta।
manuṣyāḥ pitaraścaiva tebhyo'nye laukikāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 1.56.60 ॥
pitā pitāmahaścaiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ।
yajvāno ye tu some na somavantastu te smṛtāḥ ॥ 1.56.61 ॥
agniṣvāttāḥ smṛtāsteṣāṃ homino yājyayājinaḥ।
ye vāpyāśramadharmeṇa prasthāneṣu vyavasthitāḥ ॥ 1.56.63 ॥
brahmacaryeṇa tapasā yajñena prajayā ca vai ॥ 1.56.64 ॥
śraddhayā vidyayā caiva pradānena ca saptadhā।
karmasveteṣu ye yuktā bhavantyā devapātanāt ॥ 1.56.65 ॥
devaistaiḥ pitṛbhiḥ sārddhaṃ sūkṣmakaiḥ somapāyakaiḥ।
svargatā divi modante pitṛmantamupāsate ॥ 1.56.66 ॥
teṣāṃ nivāpadattānnaṃ tatkulīnaiśca bāndhavaiḥ ॥ 1.56.67 ॥
māsaṃ śrāddhabhujastṛpti labhante somalaukikāḥ।
ete manuṣyāḥ pitaro māsi śrāddha bhujastu te ॥ 1.56.68 ॥
tebhyo'pare tu ye cānye saṅkīrṇāḥ karmayoniṣu।
bhraṣṭāścāśramadharmebhyaḥ svadhāsvāhāvivarjitāḥ ॥ 1.56.69 ॥
bhinnadehā durātmanaḥ pretabhūtā yamakṣaye।
svakarmāṇyeva śocanti yātanāsthānamāgatāḥ ॥ 1.56.70 ॥
dīrghāyuṣo'tiśuṣkāśca vivarṇāśca vivāsasaḥ।
kṣutpipāsāparītāśca vidravanti itastataḥ ॥ 1.56.71 ॥
saritsarastaḍāgāni vāpiścaiva jalepsavaḥ।
parānnāni ca lipsante kampamānāstatastataḥ ॥ 1.56.72 ॥
śālmalau vaitaraṇyāñca kumbhīpākeṣu teṣu ca ॥ 1.56.73 ॥
karambhavālukāyāñca asipatravane tathā।
śilāsampeṣaṇe caiva pātyamānāḥ svakarmabhiḥ ॥ 1.56.74 ॥
tatra sthānāni teṣāṃ vai duḥkhānāmapyanākavat।
teṣāṃ lokāntarasthānāṃ vividhairnāmagotrataḥ ॥ 1.56.75 ॥
bhūmyāpasavyadarbheṣu dattvā piṇḍatrayantu vai।
pati tāṃstarpayante ca pretasthāneṣvadhiṣṭitāḥ ॥ 1.56.76 ॥
aprāptā yātanāsthānaṃ sṛṣṭā ye bhuvi pañcadhā।
nānārūpāsu jātīṣu tiryagyoniṣu cātiṣu।
yadāhārā bhavantyete tāsu tāsviha yoniṣu।
tasmistasmiṃstadāhāraṃ śrāddhadattopatiṣṭhati ॥ 1.56.78 ॥
kāle nyāyāgataṃ pātraṃ vidhinā pratipāditam।
prāpnotyannaṃ yathā dattaṃ bandhuryatrāvatiṣṭhate ॥ 1.56.79 ॥
yathā goṣu pranaṣṭāsu vatso vindati mātaram।
tathā śrāddhe tadiṣṭānāṃ mantraḥ prāpayate pitṝn ॥ 1.56.80 ॥
evaṃ hyavikalaṃ śrāddhaṃ śrāddhadattantu mantrataḥ।
sanatkumāraḥ provāca paśyan divyena cakṣuṣā।
bahvīkāsvoṣmapāścaiva divākīrtyāśca te smṛtāḥ।
kṛṣṇapakṣastvahasteṣāṃ śuklaḥ svaprāya śarvarī ॥ 1.56.82 ॥
itye te pitaro devā devāśca pitaraśca vai।
ete tu pitaro devā mānuṣāḥ pitaraśca ye।
prīteṣu teṣu prīyante śraddhāyuktena karmaṇā ॥ 1.56.84 ॥
ityevaṃ pitaraḥ proktāḥ pidṝṇāṃ somapāyinām।
etat pitṛmatatvaṃ hi purāṇe niścayo mataḥ ॥ 1.56.85 ॥
ityarkapitṛ somānāmailasya ca samāgamaḥ।
sudhāmṛtasya cāvāptiḥ pitṝṇāñcaiva tarpaṇam ॥ 1.56.86 ॥
pūrṇimāvāsyayoḥ kālaḥ pitṝṇāṃ sthānameva ca।
samāsātkīrttitastubhyameṣa sargaḥ sanātanaḥ ॥ 1.56.87 ॥
vaiśvarūpyantu sarvasya kathitañcaikadeśikam।
na śakyaṃ parisaṅkhyātuṃ śraddheyaṃ bhūtimicchatā ॥ 1.56.88 ॥
svāyambhuvasya hītyeṣa sargaḥ krānto mayātra vai।
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca bhūyaḥ kiṃ varṇayāmyaham ॥ 1.56.89 ॥
caturyugāni yānyāsan pūrvaṃ svāyambhuve'ntare ।
teṣāṃ nisargaṃ tattvañca śrotumicchāmi vistarāt ॥ 1.57.1 ॥
pṛthivyādiprasaṅgena yanmayā prāgudāhṛtam।
teṣāñcaturyugaṃ hyetat pravakṣyāmi nibodhata ॥ 1.57.2 ॥
saṅkhyayeha prasaṅkhyāya vistārāccaiva sarvaśaḥ।
yugañca yugabhedañca yugadharmantathaiva ca ॥ 1.57.3 ॥
yugasandhyaṃśakañcaiva yugasandhānameva ca।
ṣaṭ‌prakārayugākhyānāṃ pravakṣyāmīha tattvataḥ ॥ 1.57.4 ॥
laukikena pramāṇena vibuddho'bdastu mānuṣaḥ।
tenābdena prasaṅkhyāya vakṣyāmīha caturyugam ।। 57.5 .
nimeṣakālatulyaṃ hi vidyāllaghvakṣarañcayat ॥ 1.57.5 ॥
kāṣṭā nimeṣā daśa pañca caiva triṃśacca kāṣṭā gaṇayet kalāstāḥ।
triṃśat kalāścaiva bhavenmuhūrttāstatrtriṃśatā rātryahanī samete ॥ 1.57.6 ॥
ahorātre vibhajate sūryo mānuṣadaivike।
tatrāhaḥ karmaceṣṭāyāṃ rātriḥ svapnāya kalpyate ॥ 1.57.7 ॥
pitrye rātryahanī māsaḥ pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ।
kṛṣṇa pakṣastvahasteṣāṃ śuklaḥ svapnāya śarvarī ॥ 1.57.8 ॥
triṃśacca mānuṣā māsāḥ pitryo māsaśca sa smṛtaḥ।
śatāni trīṇi māsānāṃ ṣaṣṭayā cāpyadhikāni vai।
pitryaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa vibhāvyate ॥ 1.57.9 ॥
mānuṣeṇaiva mānena varṣāṇāṃ yacchataṃ bhavet ।
pidṝṇāṃ trīṇi varṣāṇi saṅkhayātānīha tāni vai।
lokikenaiva mānena abdo yo mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ।
etaddivyamahorātraṃ śāstre'smin niśvayo mataḥ ॥ 1.57.11 ॥
divye rātryahanī varṣaṃ pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ ।
ahastatrodagayanaṃ rātriḥ syāddakṣiṇāyanam ॥ 1.57.12 ॥
ye te rātryahanī divye prasaṅkhayāte tayoḥ punaḥ।
triṃśacca tāni varṣāṇi divyo māsastu sa smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.57.13 ॥
mānuṣañca śataṃ viddhi divyamāsāstrayastu te।
daśa caiva tathāhāni divyo hyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.57.14 ॥
trīṇi parṣaśatānyeva ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇi yāni ca।
divyaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa prakīrttitaḥ ॥ 1.57.15 ॥
trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi mānuṣeṇa pramāṇataḥ।
triṃśadyāni tu varṣāṇi mataḥ saptarṣivatsaraḥ ॥ 1.57.16 ॥
nava yāni sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।
anyāni navatiścaiva krauñcaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.57.17 ॥
ṣaṭ‌triṃśattu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।
varṣāṇāntu śataṃ jñeyaṃ divyo hyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.57.18 ॥
trīṇyeva niyutānyeva varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi ca।
ṣaṣṭiścaiva sahasrāṇi saṅkhyātāni tu saṅkhyayā।
divyavarṣasahasrantu prāhuḥ saṅkhyāvido janāḥ ॥ 1.57.19 ॥
ityevamṛṣibhirgītaṃ divyayā saṅkhyayānvitam।
divyenaiva pramāṇena yugasaṅkacāprakalpanam ॥ 1.57.20 ॥
catvāri bhārate varṣe yugāni kavayo viduḥ।
pūrvaṃ kṛtayugaṃ nāma tatastretā vidhīyate।
dvāparaśca kali ścaiva yugānyetāni kalpayet ॥ 1.57.21 ॥
catvāryāhuḥ sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāntu kṛtaṃ yugam।
ita rāsu ca sandhyāsu sandhyāṃśeṣu ca vai triṣu ।
ekāpāyena varttante sahasrāṇi śatāni ca ॥ 1.57.23 ॥
tasyāpi dviśatī sandhyā sandhayāṃśaḥ sandhyayā samaḥ ॥ 1.57.25 ॥
kaliṃ varṣasahasrantu yugamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ।
eṣā dvādaśasāhasrī yugākhyā parikīrttitā।
kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparañca kaliścaiva catuṣṭayam ॥ 1.57.27 ॥
atra saṃvatsarāḥ sṛṣṭā mānuṣeṇa pramāṇataḥ।
sahasrāṇāṃ śatānyatra caturdaśa tu saṅkhyayā।
evaṃ caturyugaḥ kālo vinā sandhyāṃśakaiḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 1.57.30 ॥
catvāriṃśatrtrīṇi caiva niyutāni ca saṅkhyayā ।
viṃśatiśca sahasrāṇi sasandhyāṃśaścaturyugaḥ ॥ 1.57.31 ॥
evaṃ caturyugākhyā tu sādhikā hyekasaptatiḥ।
kṛtatretādiyuktā sā manorantaramucyate ॥ 1.57.32 ॥
manvantarasya saṅkhyā tu varṣāgreṇa nibodhata।
triṃśatkoṭyastu varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣeṇa prakīrtitāḥ ॥ 1.57.33 ॥
saptaṣaṣṭistathānyāni niyutānyadhikāni tu।
viṃśatiśca sahasrāṇi kālo'yaṃ sādhikāṃ vinā ॥ 1.57.34 ॥
manvantarasya saṅkhyaiṣā saṅkhyāvidbhirdvijaiḥ smṛtā।
manvantarasya kālo'yaṃ yugaiḥ sārddhaṃ prakīrtitaḥ ॥ 1.57.35 ॥
catuḥ sahasrayuktaṃ vai prathamantat kṛtaṃ yugam।
tretāvaśiṣṭaṃ vakṣyāmi dvāparaṃ kalimeva ca ॥ 1.57.36 ॥
yugapatsamavetārtho dvidhā vaktuṃ na śakyate।
kramāgataṃ mayā hyetattubhyaṃ proktaṃ yugadvayam।
ṛṣivaṃśaprasaṅgena vyākulatvāttathaiva ca ॥ 1.57.37 ॥
tatra tretāyugasyādau manuḥ saptarṣayaśca te।
śrautaṃ smārttañca dharmañca brahmaṇā ca pracoditam ॥ 1.57.38 ॥
dārāgnihotrasaṃyogamṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃjñitam।
ityādilakṣaṇaṃ śrautaṃ dharmaṃ saptarṣayo'bruvan ॥ 1.57.39 ॥
parasparāgataṃ dharmaṃ smārttañcācāralakṣaṇam।
varṇāśramācārayutaṃ manuḥ svāyambhuvo'bravīt ॥ 1.57.40 ॥
satyena brahmacaryeṇa śrutena tapasā ca vai।
teṣāṃ sutaptatapasāmārṣeyeṇa krameṇa tu ॥ 1.57.41 ॥
saptarṣīṇāṃ manoścaiva ādye tretāyugasya tu ।
abuddhipūrvakaṃ teṣāmakriyāpūrvameva ca ॥ 1.57.42 ॥
abhivyaktāstu te mantrāstārakādyairnidarśanaiḥ।
ādikalpe tu devānāṃ prādurbhūtāstu te svayam ॥ 1.57.43 ॥
praṇāśe tvatha siddhīnāmapyāsāñca pravarttanam।
āsan mantrā vyatīteṣu ye kalpeṣu sahasraśaḥ।
temantrā vai punasteṣāṃ pratibhāsasamutthitāḥ ॥ 1.57.44 ॥
ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni mantrāścātharvaṇāni ca।
saptarṣibhistu te proktāḥ smārtaṃ dharmaṃ manurjagau ॥ 1.57.45 ॥
tretādau saṃhitā vaidāḥ kevalā dharmaśeṣataḥ।
saṃrodhādāyuṣaścaivavyasyante dvāpareṣu te ॥ 1.57.46 ॥
anādinidhanā divyāḥ pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭāḥ svayambhuvā ॥ 1.57.47 ॥
sadharmāḥ saprajāḥ sāṅgā yathādharmaṃ yuge yuge।
vikrīḍante samānārthā vedavādā yathāyugam ॥ 1.57.48 ॥
ārambhayajñā kṣatrasya haviryajñā viśāmpateḥ।
paricāra yajñāḥ śūdrāstu japayajñā dvijottamāḥ ॥ 1.57.49 ॥
tathā pramuditā varṇāstretāyāṃ dharmapālitāḥ।
kriyāvantaḥ prajāvantaḥ samṛddhāḥ sukhinastathā ॥ 1.57.50 ॥
brāhmaṇānanuvarttante kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriyān viśaḥ।
vaiśyānuvartinaḥ śūdrāḥ parasparamanuvratāḥ ॥ 1.57.51 ॥
śubhāḥ pravṛttayasteṣāṃ dharmā varṇāśramāstathā।
saṅkalpitena manasā vācoktena svasarmaṇā।
tretāyuge tvavikalaḥ karmmārambhaḥ prasiddhyati ॥ 1.57.52 ॥
āyurmedhā balaṃ rūpamārogyaṃ dharmaśīlatā।
sarvasādhāraṇā hyete tretāyāṃ vai bhavantyuta ॥ 1.57.53 ॥
varṇāśramavyavasthānaṃ teṣāṃ brahmā tathākarot ।
punaḥ prajāstu tā mohāttān dharmānna hyapālayan ॥ 1.57.54 ॥
parasparavirodhena manuntāḥ punaranvayuḥ।
manuḥ svāyambhuvo dṛṣṭvā yāthātathyaṃ prajāpatiḥ ॥ 1.57.55 ॥
dhātā tu śatarūpāyāḥ pumān sa udapādayat।
priyavratottānapādau pradhamantau mahīpatī ॥ 1.57.56 ॥
tataḥ prabhṛti rājāna utpannā daṇḍadhāriṇaḥ।
prajānāṃ rañjanāccaiva rājānastvabhavannṛṣāḥ ॥ 1.57.57 ॥
varṇānāṃ pravibhāgāśca tretāyāṃ saṃprakīrtitāḥ।
saṃhitāśca tato mantrā ṛṣabhirbrahmaṇaistu te ॥ 1.57.59 ॥
yajñaḥ pravartitaścaiva tadā hyevantu daivataiḥ।
sārddhaṃ viśvabhujā caiva devendreṇa mahaujasā।
svāyambhuve'ntare devairyajñāste prāk pravartitāḥ ॥ 1.57.61 ॥
satyaṃ japastapo dānaṃ tretāyāṃ dharma ucyate।
prajāyante tataḥ śūrā āyuṣmanto mahābalāḥ।
nyastadaṇḍamahābhāgā yajvāno brahmavādinaḥ ॥ 1.57.63 ॥
padma patrāyatākṣāśca pṛthūraskāḥ susaṃhitāḥ।
siṃhāntakā mahāsattvā mattamātaṅgagāminaḥ ॥ 1.57.64 ॥
mahādhanurddharāścaiva tretāyāṃ cakravartinaḥ।
sarvalakṣaṇasampannā nyagrodhaparimaṇḍalāḥ ॥ 1.57.65 ॥
nyagrodhau tau smṛtau bāhū vyāmo nyagrodha ucyate।
vāmenaivocchrayādyasya sama ūrddhvantu dehinaḥ।
samucchrayaḥ parīṇāho jñeyo nyagrodhamaṇḍalaḥ ॥ 1.57.66 ॥
cakraṃ ratho maṇirbhāryā nidhiraścāgajāstathā।
saptātiśayaratnāni sarveṣāñcakravarttinām ।। 57.68 ।
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi dvāparasya vidhiṃ punaḥ।
tatra tretāyuge kṣīṇe dvāparaṃ pratipadyate ॥ 1.58.1 ॥
dvāparādau prajānāntu siddhistratāyuge tu yā।
parivṛtte yuge tasmiṃstataḥ sā saṃpraṇaśyati ॥ 1.58.2 ॥
tataḥ pravarttate tāsāṃ prajānāṃ dvāpare punaḥ।
lobho'dhṛtirvaṇigyuddhaṃ tattvānāmaviniścayaḥ ॥ 1.58.3 ॥
tambhedaścaiva varṇānāṃ kāryāṇāñcā vinirṇayaḥ।
yajñauṣadheḥ paśordaṇḍo mado dambho'kṣamā balam।
eṣāṃ rajastamoyuktā pravṛttirdvāpare smṛtā ॥ 1.58.4 ॥
ādye kṛte ca dharmo'sti tretāyāṃ samprapadyate।
dvāpare vyākulībhūtvā praṇaśyati kalau yuge ॥ 1.58.5 ॥
varṇānāṃ viparidhvaṃsaḥ saṃkīrttyate tathāśramaḥ।
dvaidhāt śruteḥ smṛteścaiva niścayo nādhigamyate।
aniścayādigamanāddharmatattvaṃ nigadyate।
dharmatattve tu bhinnānāṃ matibhedo bhavennṛṇām ॥ 1.58.7 ॥
parasparavibhinnaistairdṛṣṭīnāṃ vibhrameṇa ca।
ayaṃ dharmo hyayaṃ neti niścayo nābhigamyate ॥ 1.58.8 ॥
matibhede ca teṣāṃ vai dṛṣṭīnāṃ vibhramo bhavet ॥ 1.58.9 ॥
tato dṛṣṭivibhinnaistaiḥ kṛtaṃ śāstrakulantvidam।
eko vedaśvatuṣpādastretāsviha vidhīyate ॥ 1.58.10 ॥
saṃrodhādāyuṣaścaiva dṛśyate dvāpareṣu ca ।
vedavyāsaiścaturdhā tu vyasyate dvāparādiṣu ॥ 1.58.11 ॥
ṛṣiputraiḥ punarvedā bhidyante dṛṣṭivibhramaiḥ।
mantrabrāhmaṇavinyāsaiḥ svaravarṇaviparyayaiḥ ॥ 1.58.12 ॥
saṃhitā ṛgyajuḥsāmnāṃ saṃhanyante śrutarṣibhiḥ।
sāmānyādvaikṛtāccaiva dṛṣṭibhinnaiḥ vkacitvkacit ॥ 1.58.13 ॥
brāhmaṇaṃ kalpasūtrāṇi mantrapravacanāni ca।
anye tu prahitāstīrthaiḥ kecittān pratyavasthitāḥ ॥ 1.58.14 ॥
sāmānyaviparītārthaiḥ kṛtaṃ śāstrakulantvidam।
ādhvaryavasya prastāvairbahudhā vyākulaṃ kṛtam ॥ 1.58.16 ॥
tathaivātharvṛksāmnāṃ vikalpaiścāpyasaṃkṣayaiḥ।
vyākulaṃ dvāpare bhinne kriyate bhinnadarśanaiḥ ॥ 1.58.17 ॥
taiṣāṃ bhedāḥ prabhedāśca vikalpaiścāpyasaṃkṣayāḥ ।
dvāpare sampravartante vinaśyanti punaḥ kalau ॥ 1.58.18 ॥
teṣāṃ viparyayāścaiva bhavanti dvāpare punaḥ।
avṛṣṭirmaraṇañcaiva tathaiva vyādhyupadvavāḥ ॥ 1.58.19 ॥
vāṅmanaḥkarmajairduḥkhairnirvedo jāyate punaḥ ।
nirvedājjāyate teṣāṃ duḥkhamokṣa vicāraṇā ॥ 1.58.20 ॥
vicārāṇācca vairāgyaṃ vairāgyāddopadarśanam।
doṣāṇāṃ darśanāccaiva dvāpare jñānasambhavaḥ ॥ 1.58.21 ॥
teṣāñca mānināṃ pūrvamādye svāyambhuve'ntare।
utpadyante hi śāstrāṇāṃ dvāpare paripanthinaḥ ॥ 1.58.22 ॥
āyurvedavikalpāśca aṅgānāṃ jyautiṣasya ca।
arthaśāstravikalpaśca hetuśāstravikalpanam ॥ 1.58.23 ॥
smṛtiśāstraprabhedāśca prasthānāni pṛthak pṛthak।
dvāpareṣvabhivarttante matibhedāstathā nṛṇām ॥ 1.58.24 ॥
manasā karmaṇā vācā kṛcchrā dvārttā prasiddhyati।
dvāpare sarvabhūtānāṃ kāyakleśapuraskṛtā ॥ 1.58.25 ॥
vedaśāstrapraṇayanaṃ dharmāṇāṃ saṅkarastathā ॥ 1.58.26 ॥
dvāpareṣu pravarttante rogo lobho vadhastathā।
varṇāśramaparidhvaṃsāḥ kāmadveṣau tathaiva ca ॥ 1.58.27 ॥
pūrṇe varṣasahasre dve paramāyustuthā nṛṇām।
niḥśepe dvāpare tasmin tasya sandhyā tu pādataḥ ॥ 1.58.28 ॥
pratiṣṭhate guṇairhīno dharmo'sau dvāparasya tu ।
dvāparasya ca varṣe yā tiṣyasya tu nibodhata।
dvāparasyāṃśaśeṣe tu pratipattiḥ kalerataḥ ॥ 1.58.30 ॥
hiṃsāsūyānṛtaṃ māyā vadhaścaiva tapasvinām।
ete svabhāvāstiṣyasya sādhayanti ca vai prajāḥ ॥ 1.58.31 ॥
eṣa dharmaḥ kṛtaḥ kṛtsno dharmaśca parihīyate।
manasā karmaṇā stutyā vārttā siddhyati vā na vā ॥ 1.58.32 ॥
kalau pramārako rogaḥ satataṃ kṣudbhayāni vai।
anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ ghoraṃ darśanañca viparyayam ॥ 1.58.33 ॥
na pramāṇaṃ smṛterasti tiṣye loke yuge yuge।
garbhastho mriyate kaścidyauvanasthastathāparaḥ ।
sthāvire madhyakaumāre mriyante vai kalau prajāḥ ॥ 1.58.34 ॥
duriṣṭairduradhītaiśca durācārairdurāgamaiḥ।
viprāṇāṃ karmadoṣaistaiḥ prajānāṃ jāyate bhayam ॥ 1.58.36 ॥
hiṃsā māyā tatherṣyā ca krodho'sūyākṣamānṛtam।
tiṣye bhavanti jantūnāṃ rāgo lobhaśca sarvaśaḥ ॥ 1.58.37 ॥
saṃkṣobho jāyate'tyarthaṃ kalimāsādya vai yugam।
nādhīyante tadā vedā na yajante dvijātayaḥ।
utsīdanti narāścaiva kṣatriyāḥ saviśaḥ kramāt ॥ 1.58.38 ॥
kṣudrāṇāmantyayonestu sambandhā brāhmaṇaiḥ saha।
bhavantīha kalau tasmin śayanāsanabhojanaiḥ ॥ 1.58.39 ॥
rājānaḥ śūdrabhūyiṣṭā pāṣaṇḍānāṃ pravartakāḥ।
āyurmedhā balaṃ rūpaṃ kulañcaiva prahīyate।
śūdrāśca brāhmaṇācārāḥ śūdrācārāśca brāhmaṇāḥ ॥ 1.58.41 ॥
rājavṛtte sthitāścaurāścauravṛttāśca pārthivāḥ।
aśīlinyo'vratāścāpi striyo madyāmiṣapriyāḥ।
śvāpadaprabalatvañca gavāñcaivāpyupakṣayaḥ।
sādhūnāṃ vinivṛttiśca vidyāttasmin kalau yuge ॥ 1.58.44 ॥
caturāśramaśaithilyāddharmaḥ pravicaliṣyati ॥ 1.58.45 ॥
arakṣitāro harttāro balibhāgasya pārthivāḥ।
yugānteṣu bhaviṣyanti svarakṣaṇaparāyaṇāḥ ॥ 1.58.48 ॥
akṣatriyāśca rājāno viśaḥ śūdropajīvinaḥ।
śūdrābhivādinaḥ sarve yugānte dvijasattamāḥ ॥ 1.58.49 ॥
patayaśca bhaviṣyanti bahavo'smin kalau yuge।
sarve vāṇijakāścāpi bhaviṣyantyadhame yuge।
bhūyiṣṭhaṃ kūṭamānaiśca paṇyavikrītatejanaiḥ ॥ 1.58.51 ॥
kuśīlacaryā pāṣaṇḍairvṛthārūpaiḥ samāvṛtam।
puruṣālpaṃ bahustrīkaṃ yugānte paryupasthite ॥ 1.58.52 ॥
bahuyācanako loko bhaviṣyati parasparam।
kravyādanaḥ krūravākyo nārjavo nānasūyakaḥ ॥ 1.58.53 ॥
na kṛte pratikartā ca kṣīṇo loko bhaviṣyati।
aśaṅkā caiva patite tadyugāntasya lakṣaṇam ॥ 1.58.54 ॥
goptāraścāpyagoptāraḥ prabhaviṣyantyaśāsanāḥ ॥ 1.58.56 ॥
harttāraḥ pararatnānāṃ paradārapradharṣakāḥ।
kāmātmāno durātmāno hyadharmāt sāhasapriyāḥ ॥ 1.58.57 ॥
ūnaṣoḍaśavarṣāśca prajāyante yugakṣaye ॥ 1.58.58 ॥
śukladantā jitākṣāśca muṇḍāḥ kāṣāyavāsasaḥ।
śūdrā dharmañcariṣyanti yugānte paryupasthite ॥ 1.58.59 ॥
jñānakarmaṇyuparate loke niṣkriyatāṅgate ।
kīṭamūṣikasarpāśca dharṣayiṣyanti mānavān ॥ 1.58.61 ॥
subhikṣaṃ kṣemamārogyaṃ sāmarthyaṃ durlabhaṃ bhavet।
kauśikāḥ prativatsyanti deśān kṣudbhayapīḍitān ॥ 1.58.62 ॥
duḥkhenābhiplutānāñca paramāyuḥ śataṃ bhavet।
dṛśyante na ca dṛśyante vedāḥ kaliyuge'khilāḥ ॥ 1.58.63 ॥
utsīdanti tathā yajñāḥ kevalā dharmapīḍitāḥ।
kaṣāyiṇaśca nirgranthāstathā kāpālinaśca ha ॥ 1.58.64 ॥
vedavikrayiṇaścānye tīrthavikrayiṇo'pare ।
varṇāśramāṇāṃ ye cānye pāṣaṇḍāḥ paripanthinaḥ ॥ 1.58.65 ॥
utpadyante tathā te vai saṃprāpte tu kalau yuge।
nādhīyante tadā vedāḥ śūdrā dharmārthakovidāḥ ॥ 1.58.66 ॥
yajante nāśvamedhena rājānaḥ śūdrayonayaḥ।
strīvadhaṃ govadhaṃ kṛtvā hatvā caiva parasparam।
upahanyustadānyonyaṃ sādhayanti tathā prajāḥ ॥ 1.58.67 ॥
prajā tu bhrūṇahatyāyāmatha vai sampravarttate।
tasmādāyurbalaṃ rūpaṃ kaliṃ prāpya prahīyate।
duḥkhenābhiplutānāṃ vai paramāyuḥ śataṃ nṛṇām ॥ 1.58.69 ॥
dṛśyante nābhidṛśyante vedāḥ kaliyuge'khilāḥ।
utsīdante tadā yajñāḥ kovalā dharmapīḍitāḥ ॥ 1.58.70 ॥
tadā tvalpena kālena siddhiṃ yāsyanti mānavāḥ।
dhanyā dharmañcariṣyanti yugānte dvijasattamāḥ ॥ 1.58.71 ॥
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ ye carantyanasūyakāḥ.
tretāyāṃ vārṣiko dharmo dvāpare māsikaḥ smṛtaḥ।
yathāśaktiṃ caran prājñastadahnā prāpruyāt kalau ॥ 1.58.72 ॥
eṣā kaliyuge'vasthā sandhyāṃśantu nibodha me ।
yuge yuge tu hīyante trīṃstrīn pādāṃśca siddhayaḥ ॥ 1.58.73 ॥
yugasvabhāvātsandhyāstu tiṣṭhantīmāstu pādaśaḥ।
sandhyāsvabhāvāccāṃśeṣu pādaśaste pratiṣṭitāḥ ॥ 1.58.74 ॥
evaṃ sandhyāṃśake kāle samprāpte tu yugāntike।
teṣāṃ śāstā hyasādhūnāṃ bhṛgūṇāṃ nidhanotthitaḥ ॥ 1.58.75 ॥
gotreṇa vai candramaso nāmnā pramitirucyate।
mādhavasya tu soṃśena pūrvaṃ svāyambhuve'ntare ॥ 1.58.76 ॥
