sāttvikī pauruṣī yā tu sānugrahakarī smṛtā ॥ 2.5.99 ॥
rājasyā brahmaṇoṃ'śena marīciḥ kaśyapo'bhavat।
trailokye tāḥ smṛtāstisrastanavastu svayambhuvaḥ ॥ 2.5.101 ॥
ityetāḥ kathitā stisrastanavastu svayambhuvaḥ।
prajāpatyā ca raudrī ca vaiṣṇavī caiva tāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.5.104 ॥
ekā tanuḥ smṛtā vede dharmaśāstre purātane।
sāṅkhyayogapare vīraiḥ pṛthaktvaikatvadarśibhiḥ।
abhijātaprabhāvajñaiṛṣibhistattvadarśibhiḥ ॥ 2.5.105 ॥
ekatve ca pṛthaktve ca tāsu bhinnāḥ prajāstviha ।
idaṃ paramidaṃ neti bruvato bhinnadarśanāḥ ॥ 2.5.106 ॥
brahmāṇaṃ kāraṇaṃ kecit kecit prāhuḥ prajāpatim।
kecicchivaṃ paratvena prāhurviṣṇuṃ tathā'pare।
kāraṇañca smṛtā hyetā nānārtheṣviha devatāḥ ॥ 2.5.108 ॥
ekaṃ nindati yasteṣāṃ sarvānena sa nindati।
ekaṃ praśasamānastu sarvāneva praśaṃsati।
adveṣastu sadā kāryo devatāsu vijānatā।
na śakyamīśvaraṃ jñātumaiśvaryeṇa vyavasthitam ॥ 2.5.110 ॥
ekātmā sa tridhā bhūtvā saṃmohayati yaḥ prajāḥ।
eteṣāñca trayāṇāntu vicarantyantaraṃ janāḥ ॥ 2.5.111 ॥
idaṃ paramidaṃ neti vadanti bhinnadarśinaḥ ॥ 2.5.112 ॥
guṇamātrātmikābhistu tanubhirmohayan prajāḥ।
teṣvekaṃ yajate yastu sa tadā yajate trayam ॥ 2.5.114 ॥
tasmāddevāstrayo hyete nairantarye vyavasthitāḥ।
tasmāt pṛthaktvamekatvasaṅkhyā saṅkhyāgatāgatam।
ekatvaṃ vā bahutvaṃ vā teṣu ko jñātumarhati ॥ 2.5.115 ॥
yasmāt sṛṣṭvānugṛhṇīte grasate caiva te prajāḥ ।
guṇātmakatvātrtraikālye tasmādekaḥ sa ucyate ॥ 2.5.116 ॥
rudraṃ brah‌māṇamindrañca loka pālān ṛṣīn danūn।
devaṃ tamekaṃ bahudhā prāhurnārāyaṇaṃ dvijāḥ ॥ 2.5.117 ॥
prājāpatyā tanuryā ca tanuryā caiva vaiṣṇavī।
manvantare ca kalpe ca āvarttante punaḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.5.118 ॥
tejasā yaśasā buddhyā śrutena ca balena ca ।
jāyante tatsamāścaiva tānapīha nibodhata ॥ 2.5.119 ॥
rājasyā brāhmaṇoṃ'śena marīciḥ kaśyapo'bhavat।
tāmasyāstasya cāṃśena kālātmā rudra ucyate ।
triṣu kāleṣu tasyaitā brahmaṇastanavoṃ'śajāḥ।
kālo bhūtvā punaścāsau rudraḥ saṃharate prajāḥ ॥ 2.5.121 ॥
samprāpte caiva kalpānte saptaraśmirddivākaraḥ।
tasyāntasyāmavasthāyāṃ tattadutpattikāraṇam ॥ 2.5.123 ॥
sattvodriktā tu yā proktā brahmaṇaḥ pauruṣī tanuḥ।
ākūtyāṃ manaso deva utpannaḥ prathame vibhuḥ ।. 5.125 ।।
tataḥ punaḥ sa vai devo prāpte svārociṣe'ntare।
tuṣitāyāṃ samutpanno hyatītastuṣitaiḥ saha ॥ 2.5.124 ॥
satyāyāmabhavatsatyaḥ satyaiḥ saha surottamaiḥ।
tāmasasyāntare cāpi samprāpte punareva hi।
bhāryāyāṃ haribhiḥ sārddhaṃ harireva babhūva ha ॥ 2.5.126 ॥
vaikuṇṭāyāmasau jajñe hyābhūtarajasaiḥ saha।
mārīcāt kaśyapādviṣṇuradityāṃ sambamūva ha।
pratyapādayadindrāya devebhyaścaiva sa prabhuḥ।
ityetāsatanavastasya vyatītāḥ sapta saptasu।
manvantareṣvatīteṣu yābhiḥ saṃrakṣitāḥ prajāḥ ॥ 2.5.130 ॥
tāsāntāstejasā buddhyā śrutena ca balena ca।
yadyadvibhūtimatsattvaṃ śrīmadūrjitameva vā।
tattadevāvagacchaghvaṃ viṣṇostejoṃ'śasambhavam ॥ 2.5.134 ॥
sa evaṃ jāyateṃ'śena kecidicchanti mānavāḥ।
evaṃ vivadamānāste dṛṣṭvā tānvai bruvanti ha।
manvantareṣu sarveṣu prajāḥ sthāvarajaṅgamāḥ।
sargādau sakṛdutpannāstiṣṭhantīha praśaṃsayā ॥ 2.5.138 ॥
prāpte prāpte tu kalpānte rudraḥ saṃharati prajāḥ।
jāyante mohayanto'nyānīśvarā yogamāyayā ॥ 2.5.139 ॥
tasmāddoṣapracāreṣu yuktāyuktaṃ na vidyate ॥ 2.5.140 ॥
bhūtāpavādino duṣṭā madhyasthā bhūtabhāvinaḥ।
bhūtāpavādinaḥ śaktāstrayo vedāḥ pravādinām ॥ 2.5.141 ॥
śrutajñaiḥ kāraṇairetaiścaturbhiḥ parikīrttyate ॥ 2.5.144 ॥
imau codāharantyatra ślokau yogeśvaraṃ prati ॥ 2.5.145 ॥
kuryādyogabalamprāpya taiśca sarvaiḥ sahācaret ॥ 2.5.146 ॥
prāpnuyādviṣayāścaiva tathaivogratapaścaran ।
saṃharecca punaḥ sarvān sūryatejo guṇāniva ॥ 2.5.147 ॥
etacchrutvā vacastasya naimiṣeyāstapasvinaḥ।
vrahmaṇo vai mukhāt sṛṣṭā yathā devāḥ prajepsayā।
sarva mantraśarīrāste smṛtā manvatareṣviha ॥ 2.6.4 ॥
darśaśca paurṇamāsaśca bṛhadyacca rathantaram।
vittiścaiva suvittiśca ākūtiḥ kūtireva ca।
vijñātiścaiva vijñāto mānavo ye ca dvādaśa ॥ 2.6.6 ॥
evamuktvā tu taṃ vrahmā tatraivāntaradhīyata ॥ 2.6.8 ॥
tataste nābhyanandanta tadvākyaṃ parameṣṭinaḥ।
ya evāpyavatiṣṭhante doṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā tu karmasu।
kṣayātiśayayuktantu te dṛṣṭvā karmaṇāṃ phalam ॥ 2.6.10 ॥
jugupsantaḥ prasūtiñca nistandrā nirmamābhavan।
ajasraṃ kāṃkṣamāṇāste viraktā doṣadarśinaḥ ॥ 2.6.11 ॥
arthaṃ dharmañca kāmañca hitvā te vai vyavasthitāḥ।
pauruṣaṃ jñānamāsthāya tejaḥ saṃkṣipya cāsthitāḥ ॥ 2.6.12 ॥
teṣāñca tamabhiprāyaṃ jñātvā brahmā cukopa ha।
tānabravīttadā brahmā nirutsāhāt surānatha ॥ 2.6.13 ॥
prajārthamiha yūyaṃ vai prajāsraṣṭā'smi nānyathā।
prasūyadhvaṃ jayaghvañcetyuktavānasmi yat purā ॥ 2.6.14 ॥
yasmādvākyamanādṛtya mama vairāgyamāsthitāḥ।
jugupsamānāḥ svaṃ janma santatiṃ nābhi nandatha ॥ 2.6.15 ॥
karmaṇāñca kṛto nyāso hyamṛtattvābhikāṃkṣayā।
te śaptā brahmaṇā devā jayāstaṃ vai prasādayan।
kṣamāsmākaṃ mahādeva yadajñānāt kṛtaṃ vibho ॥ 2.6.17 ॥
praṇipatya sānunayaṃ brahmā tānabravīt punaḥ।
loke mayānanujñātaḥ kaḥ svātantryamihārhasi ॥ 2.6.18 ॥
mayā parigataṃ sarvaṃ kathamacchandato mama।
pratipatsyanti bhūtāni śubhaṃ vā yadi vā'śubham ॥ 2.6.19 ॥
buddhyātmanā mayā vyāptaṃ ko māṃ loke'tisandhayet ॥ 2.6.20 ॥
bhūtānāṃ tarkitaṃ yacca yaccāpyeṣāṃ vidhāritam।
tathā vicāritaṃ yacca tatsarvaṃ viditaṃ mama ॥ 2.6.21 ॥
mayā sthitamidaṃ sarvaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam।
āśāmayena tattvena kathaṃ chettumihotsahe ॥ 2.6.22 ॥
iha karmāṇyanārabhya ko me chandādvimokṣyate ॥ 2.6.23 ॥
yasmātsa viphalo'yanno hyapārastveṣa yaḥ kṛtaḥ।
bhavitā'taḥ sukhodarko devā bhāveṣu jāyatām ॥ 2.6.25 ॥
ātmacchandena vo janma bhaviṣyati surottamāḥ।
vaivasvatānteṣu surāstathā svāyambhuvādiṣu।
tān jñātvā brahmaṇā tatra śloko gītaḥ purātanaḥ ॥ 2.6.27 ॥
sa evaṃ slokaṃ dṛṣṭvā tu jayā devānathābravīt।
vaivasvate'ntare'tīte matsamīpamiheṣyatha ॥ 2.6.29 ॥
evamuktvā tu tān brahmā tatraivāntaradhīyata ॥ 2.6.30 ॥
tato devāstirobhūte īśvare hyakutobhayam।
prapannā aṇimādyaiśca yuktā yogabalānvitāḥ ॥ 2.6.31 ॥
jayā iti samākhyātā jātā ścodadhisannibhāḥ ॥ 2.6.32 ॥
tataḥ svāyambhuve tasmin sargete jajñire surāḥ।
svāyambhuve'ntare pūrve tataḥ svārociṣe punaḥ।
tuṣitāyāṃ samutpannāḥ punaḥ putrāḥ svarociṣaḥ ॥ 2.6.35 ॥
uttamasya tu te putrāḥ satyāyāṃ jajñire śubhāḥ।
tataḥ satyāḥ smṛtā devā uttame cāntare tadā ॥ 2.6.37 ॥
harṣā ye tamasaḥ putrā jajñire dvādaśaiva tu ।
harayo nāma te devā yajñabhājastathā'bhavan ॥ 2.6.39 ॥
tataste harayo devāḥ prāpte cāriṣṇave'ntare।
vaikuṇṭā nāma te devāḥ pañcamasyāntare manoḥ ॥ 2.6.40 ॥
tataste vai punarddevā vaikuṇṭāḥ prāpya cākṣuṣam।
tataste vai punaḥ sādhyāḥ saṃkṣīṇe cākṣuṣe'ntare ।
upasthite manoḥ sarge punarvaivasvatasya ha ॥ 2.6.42 ॥
aṃśena sādhyāste'dityāṃ mārīcāt kaśyapāt punaḥ ॥ 2.6.43 ॥
jajñire dvādaśādityā varttamāne'ntare punaḥ।
yadā tvete samutpannāścākṣuṣasyāntare manoḥ ॥ 2.6.44 ॥
tataḥ svāyambhuve sādhyā jajñire dvādaśāmarāḥ।
paṭedyaḥ śraddhayā yuktaḥ pratvāyaṃ na gacchati ॥ 2.6.46 ॥
ityete bhūtayaḥ sapta jayānāṃ saptalakṣaṇāḥ।
parikrāntā mayā cādya kimbhūyaḥ śrotumicchatha ॥ 2.6.47 ॥
daityānāṃ dānavānāñca gandharvoragarakṣasām।
sarvabhūtapiśācānāṃ paśūnāṃ pakṣivīrudhām।
utpattiṃ nidhanañcaiva vistarāt kathayasva naḥ ॥ 2.6.48 ॥
evamuktastadā sūta uvāca ṛṣisattamān ।
kaśyapasyātmajau tau vai sarvebhyaḥ pūrvajau smṛtau।
sūtye'hanyatirātrasya kaśyapasyāśvamedhike ॥ 2.6.50 ॥
hiraṇyakaśipurnāma prathamaṃ ṛtvigāsanam।
dityā garbhādviniḥsṛtya tatrāsīnoccasaṃsadi।
hiraṇyakaśipustasmāt karmaṇā tena sa smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.6.51 ॥
hiraṇyakaśipornāma janma caiva mahātmanaḥ।
prabhāvañcaiva daityasya vistarādbrūhi naḥ prabho ॥ 2.6.52 ॥
kaśyapasyāśvamedho'bhūt puṇyo vai puṣkare purā।
ṛṣibhirddevatābhiśca gandharvai rupaśobhitaḥ ॥ 2.6.53 ॥
utkṛṣṭenaiva vidhinā ākhyānādau yathāvidhi।
āsanānyupaklṛptāni kāñcanāni tu pañca vai ॥ 2.6.54 ॥
kuśapūtāni trīṇyatra kūrcaphalakameva ca।
mukhyārtvijaśca catvārasteṣāntānyupakalpayet ॥ 2.6.55 ॥
upaklṛptāsanaṃ yattu hoturarthe hiraṇmayam।
niṣasāda sagarbho'tra tatrāsīnaḥ śaśaṃsa ca ॥ 2.6.58 ॥
ākyānapañcamān vedān maharṣiḥ kāśyapo yathā।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā munayastasya nāmākurvaṃstu tadvidham ॥ 2.6.59 ॥
hiraṇyakaśipustasmāt karmaṇā tena viśrutaḥ।
hiraṇyākṣo'nujastasya siṃhikā tasya cānujā।
rāhoḥ sā jananī devī vipracitteḥ parigrahāt ॥ 2.6.60 ॥
hiraṇyakaśipurddaityaścacāra paramaṃ tapaḥ।
śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ nirāhāro hyadhaḥśirāḥ ॥ 2.6.61 ॥
sarvāmaratvaṃ viprebhyaḥ sarvabhūtebhya eva ca।
yogāddevān vinirjitya sarvadevatvamāsthitaḥ ॥ 2.6.62 ॥
hiraṇyakaśipurdaityaḥ ślokairgītaḥ purātanaiḥ ॥ 2.6.64 ॥
rājā hiraṇyakaśipuryāṃ yāmāśāṃ niṣevate।
tasyāstasyā diśo devā namaścakrurmaharṣibhiḥ ॥ 2.6.65 ॥
tasyāsīnnarasiṃhaḥ sa viṣṇurmṛtyuḥ purā kila।
hiraṇyākṣasutāḥ pañca vikrāntāḥ sumahā balāḥ।
utkuraḥ śakuniścaiva kālanābhastathaiva ca ॥ 2.6.67 ॥
mahānābhaśca vikrānto bhūtasantāpanastathā।
hiraṇyākṣasutāḥ hyete devairapi durāsadāḥ ॥ 2.6.68 ॥
teṣāṃ putrāśca pautrāśca bāḍeyaḥ sagaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ।
śatantāni sahasrāṇi nihatāstārakāmaye ॥ 2.6.69 ॥
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putrāścatvārastu mahābalāḥ।
prahlādaḥ pūrvajasteṣāmanuhlādastathaiva ca।
saṃhrādaśca hradaścaiva hradaputrānnibodhata ॥ 2.6.70 ॥
hrādo nisundaśca tatā hradaputrau babhūvatuḥ।
brahmaghnastu mahāvīryo mūkastu hradadāyinaḥ।
mārīcaḥ sundaputrastu tāḍakāmupapadyate ॥ 2.6.72 ॥
tāḍakā nihatā sā'tha rāghaveṇa balīyasā।
mūko vinihataścāpi kirāte savyasācinā ॥ 2.6.73 ॥
utpannā mahatā caiva tapasā bhāvitāḥ svayam।
avadhyā devatānāṃ vai nihatāḥ savyasācinā ॥ 2.6.74 ॥
śumbhaścaiva niśumbhaśca viṣvakseno mahaujasaḥ ॥ 2.6.77 ॥
gaveṣṭinaḥ sutā hyete jambhasya śatadundubhiḥ।
bāṣkalasya sutā hyete kālanemisutān śrṛṇu ॥ 2.6.79 ॥
brahmajit kṣatrajiccaiva devāntakanarāntakau ।
kālanemisutā hyete śambhostu śrṛṇuta prajāḥ ॥ 2.6.80 ॥
gavākṣaścaiva gomāṃśca śambhoḥ putrāḥ prakīrttitāḥ ॥ 2.6.81 ॥
virocanasya putrastu balirekaḥ pratāpavān।
baleḥ putraśataṃ jajñe rājānaḥ sarva eva te ॥ 2.6.82 ॥
teṣāṃ pradhānāścatvāro vikrāntāḥ sumahābalāḥ।
śakunī pūtanā caiva kanye dve tu baleḥ sute।
baleḥ putrāśca pautrāśca śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ ॥ 2.6.84 ॥
baliryo nāmavikhyāto gaṇo vikrāntapauruṣaḥ।
ditirvinaṣṭaputrā vai toṣayāmāsa kaśyapam।
sa kaśyapaḥ prasannātmā samyagārādhitastayā ।
vareṇa cchandayāmāsa sā ca vavre varaṃ tataḥ ॥ 2.6.86 ॥
sa tu tasyai varaṃ prādāt prārthitaṃ bhagavan prabhuḥ।
mārīcaṃ kaśyapaṃ tuṣṭaṃ bhartāraṃ prāñjalistathā।
hataputrāsmi bhagavān ādityaistava sūnubhiḥ ॥ 2.6.88 ॥
śakrahantāramiccheyaṃ putraṃ dīrghatapo'nvitam।
ahaṃ tapaścariṣyāmi garbha mādhātumarhasi ॥ 2.6.89 ॥
tasyāstadvacanaṃ śrutvā mārīcaḥ kaśyapastathā।
pratyuvāca mahātejā ditiṃ paramaduḥkhitām ॥ 2.6.90 ॥
evaṃ bhavatu bhadrante śucirbhava tapodhane।
janayiṣyasi satputraṃ śakrahantāramāhave ॥ 2.6.91 ॥
pūrṇaṃ varṣaśataṃ tāvat śuciryadi bhaviṣyasi ।
putraṃ trilokapracaramathatvaṃ janayiṣyasi ॥ 2.6.92 ॥
tāmāliṅgya tribhuvanaṃ jagāma bhagavānṛṣiḥ ॥ 2.6.93 ॥
gate bharttari sā devī ditiḥ paramaharṣitā।
kuśalaṃ vanamāsādya tapastepe sudāruṇam ॥ 2.6.94 ॥
śakraḥ sarveṣu (lokeṣu) kāleṣu ditiṃ paricacāra ha ।
prītā te'haṃ suraśreṣṭha daśavarṣāṇi putraka।
avaśiṣṭāni bhadrānte bhrātaraṃ drakṣyase tataḥ ॥ 2.6.98 ॥
trailokyavijayaṃ pūtra prāpsyāmi saha tena vai ॥ 2.6.99 ॥
evamuktvā ditiḥ śakraṃ madhyaṃ prāpte divākare ।
praviśya cāmitaṃ dṛṣṭvā garbhamindro mahaujasam।
ruroda sasvaraṃ bhīmaṃ vepamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
taṃ garbhaṃ saptadhābhūtaṃ hyekaikaṃ saptadhā punaḥ।
kuliśena bibhedendrastato ditirabudhyata ॥ 2.6.104 ॥
na hantavyo na hantavya ityevaṃ ditirabravīt ।
niṣpapātodarādvajrī māturvacanagauravāt।
prāñjalirvajrasahito ditiṃ śakro'bhyabhāṣata ॥ 2.6.105 ॥
aśucirdevi suptāsi pādayorgatamūrddhajā।
bhinnavān garbhametante bahudhā kṣantumarhasi ॥ 2.6.106 ॥
tasmistu viphale garbhe ditiḥ paramaduḥkhitā।
mamāparādhādgarbho'yaṃ yadi te viphalīkṛtaḥ।
nāparādho'sti deveśa ṛṣiputra mahābala ॥ 2.6.108 ॥
śatrorvadhe na doṣo'sti tena tvāṃ na śapāmi bhoḥ।
priyantu karttumicchāmi śreyo garbhasya me kuru ॥ 2.6.109 ॥
bhavantu mama putrāṇāṃ sapta sthānāni vai divi।
vātaskandhānimān sapta carantu mama putrakāḥ।
marutaśceti vikhyātā gaṇāste sapta saptakāḥ ॥ 2.6.110 ॥
pṛthivyāṃ prathamaskandho dvitīyaścaiva bhāskare।
some tṛtīyo vijñeyaścaturtho jyotiṣāṃ gaṇe ॥ 2.6.111 ॥
graheṣu pañcamaścaiva ṣaṣṭhaḥ saptarṣimaṇḍale।
dhruve tu saptamaścaiva vātaskandhaḥ parastu saḥ ॥ 2.6.112 ॥
tānyete vicarantvadya kāle kāle mamātmajāḥ।
vātaskandhānimān bhūtvā carantu mama putrakāḥ ॥ 2.6.113 ॥
pṛthivyāṃ prathamaskandho amedhyebhyo ya āvahaḥ।
dvitīyaścāpi medhyebhya āsūryāt pravahastu yaḥ।
somādūrddhvaṃ tatharkṣebhyaścaturthaḥ suvahastu yaḥ।
caturtho mama putrāṇāṃ gaṇastu caratāṃ vibho ॥ 2.6.117 ॥
yakṣebhyaśca tathaivorddhvamāgrahādvivahastu yaḥ।
vāta skandhaḥ parivahastatra tiṣṭhantu me sutāḥ ॥ 2.6.120 ॥
etat sarvaṃ carantvete kāle kāle mamātmajāḥ।
tatra tena ca nāmnā vai bhavantu marutastvime ॥ 2.6.121 ॥
sattvajyotistathādityaḥ satyajyotistathā'paraḥ।
prathamastu gaṇaḥ prokto dvitīyaṃ me nibodhata।
ṛtajitsatyajiccaiva suṣeṇaḥ senajittathā ॥ 2.6.124 ॥
satmitro'bhimitraśca harimitrastathā'paraḥ।
gaṇa eṣa dvitīyastu tṛtīyaṃ me nibodhata ॥ 2.6.125 ॥
dhvāntaścaiva dhuniścaiva hyugro bhīmastathaiva ca।
abhiyuḥ sakṣipaścaivamāhvayaśca gaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.6.126 ॥
(?) samitiścaiva saṃrambhaśca tathā gaṇaḥ ॥ 2.6.127 ॥
īdṛk ca puruṣaścaiva anyādṛkṣācca cetasaḥ।
ete hyeko napañcāśanmaruto nāmataḥ smṛtāḥ।
prasaṃkhyātāstathā tābhyāṃ dityā candreṇa caiva hi ॥ 2.6.129 ॥
śrutvā teṣāntu nāmāni ditirindramuvāca ha।
vicarantu ca bhadrante devaiḥ saha mamātmajāḥ ॥ 2.6.130 ॥
tasyāstadvacanaṃ śrutvā sahasrākṣaḥ purandaraḥ।
uvāca prāñjalirbhūtvā mātarbhavatu tattathā ॥ 2.6.131 ॥
sarvametadyathoktante bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ।
devabhūtā mahātmānaḥ kumārā devasaṃmatāḥ।
devaiḥ saha bhaviṣyanti yajña bhājastathātmajāḥ ॥ 2.6.132 ॥
tasmātte maruto devāḥ sarve cendrānujāmarāḥ।
vijñeyāścāmarāḥ sarve ditiputrāstapasvinaḥ ॥ 2.6.133 ॥
evaṃ tau niścayaṃ jñātvā mātāputrau tapodhanau।
marutāṃ hi śubhaṃ janma śrṛṇuyādyaḥ paṭeta vā।
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi danuputrānnibodhata।
abhavan danuputrāstu vaṃśe khyātā mahāsurāḥ ॥ 2.7.1 ॥
vipracittipradhānāste śataṃ tīvraparākramāḥ।
sarve labdhavarāścaiva sutaptatapasastathā ॥ 2.7.2 ॥
satyasandhāḥ parākrāntāḥ krūrā māyāvinaśca te ।
kīrttyamānānmayā sarvān prādhānyena nibodhata ॥ 2.7.3 ॥
dvimūrddhā śaṅkuvarṇaśca tathā śaṅkunirāmayaḥ।
śaṅkukarṇo mahāviśvo gaveṣṭirdundubhistathā ॥ 2.7.4 ॥
vikṣobhyaśca suketuśca suvīryaḥ suhṛdastathā।
ekacakraḥ subāhuśca tārakaśca mahābalaḥ।
vaiśvānaraḥ pulomā ca pravīṇo'tha mahāśirāḥ ॥ 2.7.7 ॥
svarbhānurvṛṣaparvā ca muṇḍakaśca mahāsuraḥ।
dhṛtarāṣṭraśca sūryaśca candra indraśca tāpinaḥ ॥ 2.7.8 ॥
sūkṣmaścaiva nicandraśca ūrṇanābho mahāgiriḥ।
asilomā sukeśaśca sadaśca balako daśa ॥ 2.7.9 ॥
tathā gaganamūrddhā ca kumbhanābhā mahodaraḥ।
pramodāhaśca kupatho hayagrīvaśca vīryavān ॥ 2.7.10 ॥
ajo hiraṇmayaścaiva śatamāyuśca śambaraḥ ॥ 2.7.11 ॥
śarabhaḥ śalabhaścaiva sūryācandramasāvubhau।
asurāṇāṃ surāvetau surāṇāṃ sāmpratāvimau ॥ 2.7.12 ॥
iti putrā danorvaṃśāḥ pradhānāḥ parikīrtitāḥ।
teṣāmaparisaṅkhyeyaṃ putrapautrādyanantakam ।। 7.13 ।।
ityete tvasurāḥ proktā daiteyā dānavāśca ye।
ime tu vaṃśānugatā danoḥ putrāstu ye smṛtāḥ ।। 7.14 ।।
gaveṣṭiśca gavākṣaśca tālaketuśca vīryavān।
ete manuṣyadharmāstu danoḥ putrā mayā smṛtāḥ ।। 7.16 ।।
daityadānavasaṃharṣe jātā bhīmaparākramāḥ।
siṃhikāyāmathotpannā vipracittisutāstvime ।। 7.17 ।।
saiṃhikeyā iti khyātāścaturddaśa mahāsurāḥ।
haraḥ kalpaḥ kālanābho bhaumaśca narakastathā ।। 7.19 ।।
rāhurjyaṣṭhastu teṣāṃ vai candrasūryapramardanaḥ।
ityete siṃhikāputrā devairapi durāsadāḥ ।। 7.20 ।।
dāruṇābhijanāḥ krūrāḥ sarve brahmadviṣaśca te।
daśānyāni sahasrāṇi saiṃhikeyo gaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 7.21 ।।
nihato jāmadagnyena bhārgaveṇa balīyasā।
svarbhānostu prabhā kanyā pulomno'tha śacī tathā ।। 7.22 ।।
pulomā kālikā caiva vaiśvānarasute ubhe ।। 7.23 ।।
prabhāyā nahuṣaḥ putro jayantaśca śacīsutaḥ।
puruṃjajñe'tha śarmiṣṭā duṣmantamupadānavī ।। 7.24 ।।
vaiśvānarasute hyete pulomā kālikā ubhe ।
ubhe hyapi tu te kanye mārīcasya parigrahe । 7.25 ।।
tābhyāṃ putrasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭirdānavapuṅgavāḥ।
caturdaśa tathānyāni hiraṇyapuravāsinām ।। 7.26 ।।
paulomāḥ kālakeyāśca dānavāḥ sumahābalāḥ।
avadhyā dānavānāṃ te nihatāḥ savyasācinā ।। 7.27 ।।
māyāvī dundubhiścaiva vṛṣaśca mahiṣastathā ।। 7.28 ।।
bāliko vajrakarṇaśca kanyā mandodarī tathā।
daityānāṃ dānavānāñca sarga eṣa prakīrttitaḥ ।। 7.29 ।।
danāyuṣāyāḥ putrāstu smṛtāḥ pañca mahābalāḥ।
aruro stanayaḥ krūro dhundhurnāma mahāsuraḥ।
nihataḥ kuvalāśvena uttaṅkavacanāt kila ।। 7.31 ।।
baleḥ putrau mahāvīryau tejasāpratimāvubhau।
kumbhilaścakravarmā ca sa karṇaḥ pūrvajanmani ।। 7.32 ।।
virakṣasyāpi putrau dvau kālakaśca varaśca tau।
viṣasya tvabhavan putrāścatvāraḥ krūrakarmaṇaḥ।
śrāddhahā yajñahā caiva brahmahā paśuhā tathā ।। 7.33 ।।
krāntā danāyuṣāputrā vṛtrasyāpi nibodhata।
jajñire śvasanāddhorādvṛtrasyendreṇa yudhyataḥ ।। 7.34 ।।
bharttāro manasā khyātā rākṣasāḥ sumahābalāḥ ।
śataṃ tāni sahasrāṇi mahendrānucarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 7.35 ।।
sarve brahmavidaḥ saumyā dhārmikāḥ sūkṣmamūrttayaḥ।
prajāsvantargatāḥ sarve nivasanti sudhārmikāḥ ।। 7.36 ।।
daityānāṃ dānavānāñca sarga eṣa prakīrttitaḥ।
ityete devagandharvā vijñeyāḥ parikīrttitāḥ ।। 7.39 ।।
gandharvāpsarasaḥ puṇyā mauneyāḥ parikīrttitāḥ।
dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ pulomā ca sūryavarccāstathaiva ca।
trayodaśo bhramiśirāḥ parjanyaśca caturdaśaḥ।
kaliḥ pañcadaśaśvaiva nāradaścaiva ṣoḍaśaḥ।
ityete devagandharvā mauneyāḥ parikīrttitāḥ ॥ 2.8.3 ॥
catustriṃśadyavīyasyasteṣāmapsarasaḥ śubhāḥ ।
miśrakeśī tathā śācī parṇinī vāpyalambuṣā।
mārīcī putrikā caiva vidyudvarṇā tilottamā ॥ 2.8.5 ॥
adrikā lakṣaṇā caiva devī rambhā manoramā।
puṇḍarīkā sugandhā ca sudantā surasā tathā।
gandharvāpsaraso hyetā mauneyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ॥ 2.8.8 ॥
pracetasaḥ sutā yakṣāsteṣāṃ nāmāni me śrṛṇu ॥ 2.8.11 ॥
utpāditā mahāvīryā mahāgandharvanāyakāḥ ॥ 2.8.18 ॥
ṣaṣṭhastu tumburusteṣāṃ tato viśvāvasuḥ smṛtaḥ।
suṣuve'ṣṭau mahābhāgā variṣṭā devapūjitāḥ।
manovatī sukeśā ca tumburostu sute ubhe।
pañcacūḍāstvimā divyā daivikyo'psaraso daśa ॥ 2.8.49 ॥
menakā sahajanyā ca parṇinī puñjikasthalā।
ghṛtasthalā ghṛtācī ca viśvācī pūrvacītyapi।
pramlocetyabhivikhyātānumlocantī tathaiva ca ॥ 2.8.50 ॥
anādinidhanasyātha jajñe nārāyaṇasya yā।
ūroḥ sarvānavadyāṅgī urvaśyekādaśī smṛtā ॥ 2.8.51 ॥
sarvāśca brahma vādinyo mahāyogāśca tāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.8.52 ॥
gaṇā apsarasāṅkhyātāḥ puṇyāste vai caturddaśa।
āhūtāḥ śobhayantaśca gaṇā hyete caturddaśa ॥ 2.8.53 ॥
vegavantyastvariṣṭāyā ūrjjāyāścāgnisambhavāḥ ॥ 2.8.54 ॥
vārijā hyamṛtotpannā amṛtā nāmataḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.8.55 ॥
vidyutaśca ruco nāma mṛtyoḥ kanyāśca bhairavāḥ ॥ 2.8.56 ॥
śobhayantyaḥ kāmaguṇā gaṇāḥ proktāścaturddaśa।
ityete bahusāhasraṃ bhāsvarā hyapsarogaṇāḥ।
devatānāmṛṣīṇāñca patnyastā mātaraśca ha ॥ 2.8.61 ॥
sugandhāścampavarṇāśca sarvāścāpsarasaḥ samāḥ।
parvatastatra saṃbhūto nāradaścaiva tāvubhau।।
tayoryavīyasī caiva tṛtīyārandhatī smṛtā।
vinatāyāstu putrau dvāvaruṇo garuḍaśca ha।
gāyatryādīni cchandāṃsi sauparṇeyāśca pakṣiṇaḥ।
kadrūrnāgasahasraṃ vai carā caramajījanat ।
anekaśirasāṃ teṣāṃ khecarāṇāṃ mahātmanām।
bahudhānāmadheyānāṃ prāyaśastu nibodhata ॥ 2.8.65 ॥
teṣāṃ pradhānanāgāśca śeṣavāsukitakṣakāḥ।
airāvatamahāpajhau kambalāśvatarāvubhau।
ailapatraśca śaṅkhaśca karkoṭakadhanañjayau ॥ 2.8.67 ॥
mahākarṇo mahānīlo dhṛtarāṣṭrabalāhakau।
kumāraḥ puṣpadantaśca sumukho durmukhastathā ॥ 2.8.68 ॥
śilīmukho dadhimukhaḥ kālīyaḥ śālipiṇḍakaḥ ।
kapilaścāmbarīṣaśca dhṛtapādaśca kacchapaḥ ।
nahuṣaḥ khararomā ca maṇirityevamādayaḥ।
kādraveyā mayā khyātāḥ khaśāyāṃstu nibodhata ॥ 2.8.71 ॥
khaśā vijajñe putrau dvau viśrutau puruṣādakau।
jyeṣṭhaṃ paścimasaṅkhyāyāṃ pūrvasyāṃ manujāstathā ॥ 2.8.72 ॥
vilohitaṃ vikarṇañca pūrvaṃ sā'janayat sutam।
caturbhujaṃ catuṣpādaṃ dvimūrddhānaṃ dvidhāgatim ॥ 2.8.73 ॥
sarvāṅgakeśaṃ sthūlāṅgaṃ tuṅganāsaṃ mahodaram।
sthūlaśīrṣaṃ mahākarṇaṃ muñjākeśaṃ manoratham ॥ 2.8.74 ॥
hastyoṣṭhaṃ dīrghajaṅghañca aśvadaṃṣṭraṃ mahāhanum।
guhyakaṃ śitikarṇañca mahānandaṃ mahāmukham।
evaṃvidhaṃ khaśāputraṃ vijajñe sā'tibhīṣaṇam ॥ 2.8.76 ॥
tasyānujaṃ dvitīyantu khaśā caiva vyajāyata।
triśīrṣañca tripādañca trihastaṃ kṛṣṇalocanam ॥ 2.8.77 ॥
ūrddhvakeśaṃ haricchmaśruṃ śilāsaṃhananaṃ dṛḍham ।
hrasva kāyaṃ subāhuñca mahākāyaṃ mahābalam ॥ 2.8.78 ॥
ākarṇadāritāsyañca lambabhrūṃ sthūlanāsikam।
sthūloṣṭhamaṣṭadaṃṣṭrañca dvijihvaṃ śaṅkukarṇakam ॥ 2.8.79 ॥
piṅgalodvṛttanayanaṃ jaṭilaṃ piṅgalaṃ tathā।
sadyaḥ prasūyamātrau tu vivṛddhau ca pramāṇataḥ।
upabhogasamarthābhyāṃ śarīrābhyāmupasthitau।
sadyojātavivṛddhāṅgau mātaraṃ paryabhūṣyatām ॥ 2.8.81 ॥
jyāyāṃstayostu yaḥ krūro mātaraṃ so'bhyakarṣata।
nyaṣedhayat punarhyenaṃ jyāyāṃsantu kaniṣṭhakaḥ।
bāhubhyāṃ parigṛhyainaṃ mātaraṃ tāṃ vyamocayat ॥ 2.8.83 ॥
etasminneva kāle tu prādurbhūtastayoḥ pitā ।
tau dṛṣṭvā vikṛtākārau vasatāṃ hītyabhāṣata ॥ 2.8.84 ॥
tau tu taṃ pitaraṃ dṛṣṭvā balavantau tvarānvitau ।
mātureva punasvāṅke pralapetāṃ svamāyayā ॥ 2.8.85 ॥
atho'bravīdṛṣirbhāryāmāvābhyāmuktavatyasi ।
pūrvamācakṣva tattvena tathaivābhyāṃ vyatikramam ॥ 2.8.86 ॥
mātulaṃ bhajate putraḥ pitṝn bhajati kanyakā।
yathāśīlā bhavenmātā tathāśīlo bhavet sutaḥ ॥ 2.8.87 ॥
yadvarṇā tu bhavedbhūmistadvarṇaṃ salilaṃ dhruvam।
mātṝṇāṃ śīladoṣeṇa tathā śīlaguṇaiḥ punaḥ।
vibhinnāstu prajāḥ sarvāstathā khyātivaśena ca ॥ 2.8.88 ॥
krodhaśīlā tathā kadrūḥ krodhenāsukhaśīlakā ॥ 2.8.91 ॥
ityevamuktvā bhagavān khaśāmapratimāṃ tadā।
mātrā yathā samākhyātaṃ karma tābhyāṃ pṛthak pṛthak।
tena dhātvarthayogena tattvadarśī cakāra ha ॥ 2.8.96 ॥
yakṣayetyuktavān yasmāt tasmādyakṣo bhavatyayam ॥ 2.8.97 ॥
rakṣa ityeṣa dhāturyaḥ pālane sa vibhāvyate।
uktavāṃścaiva yasmāttu rakṣa me mātaraṃ khaśām।
nāmnā'yaṃ rākṣasastasmāt bhaviṣyati tavātmajaḥ ॥ 2.8.98 ॥
tayoḥ prādiśadāhāraṃ prajāpatirasṛgvase ॥ 2.8.99 ॥
pitā tau kṣudhitau dṛṣṭvā varañcemaṃ tayordadau।
yuvayorhastasaṃsparśo naktamena tu sarvaśaḥ ॥ 2.8.100 ॥
naktāhāravihārau ca divā svapnopabhoginau।
naktañcaiva balīyāṃsau divā suptāvubhau yuvām ॥ 2.8.101 ॥
mātaraṃ rakṣatañcaiva dharmaścaivānuśiṣyatām।
ityuktvā kaśyapaḥ putrau tatraivāntaradhīyata ॥ 2.8.102 ॥
gate pitari tau vīrau nisargādeva dāruṇau।
viparyayeṇa varttantau kimbhakṣau prāṇihiṃsakau ॥ 2.8.103 ॥
mahābalau mahāsattvau mahākāyau durāsadau।
māyāvinau ca dṛśyau tāvantarddhānagatāvubhau ॥ 2.8.104 ॥
tau kāmarūpiṇau ghorau vikṛtājñau svabhāvataḥ।
devā surānṛṣīṃścaiva gandharvān kinnarānapi।
piśācāṃśca manuṣyāṃśca pannagān pakṣiṇaḥ paśūn ॥ 2.8.106 ॥
bhakṣārthamapi lipsantau sarvatastau niśācarau।
yakṣastu na kadācidvai niśīthai hyekakaściram।
āhāraṃ sa parīpsan vai śabdenānucacāra ha ॥ 2.8.108 ॥
āsasāda piśācau dvau jantucaṇḍau ca tāvubhau।
piṅgākṣāvūrddhvaromāṇau vṛttākṣau tu sudārūṇau ॥ 2.8.109 ॥
kanyābhyāṃ sahitau tau tu tābhyāṃ priyacikīrṣayā ॥ 2.8.110 ॥
dve kanye kāmarūpiṇyau tadācāre ca te śubhe।
sahasā sannipāte tu dṛṣṭvā caiva parasparam ॥ 2.8.112 ॥
rakṣamāṇau tato'nyonyaṃ parasparajighṛkṣavaḥ।
pitarāvūcatuḥ kanye yuvāmānayata drutam ॥ 2.8.113 ॥
jīvagrāhaṃ vigṛhyainaṃ visphurantaṃ pade pade।
tataḥ samabhisṛtyainaṃ kanye jagṛhatustadā।
gṛhītvā hastayostābhyāmānīte pitṛsaṃsadi ॥ 2.8.114 ॥
pṛcchatāṃ ko'si kasya tvaṃ sa ca sarvamabhāṣata ॥ 2.8.115 ॥
ajañca śaṇḍaṃ tasyaite pratyapādayatāṃ sute।
tau tuṣṭau karmaṇā tasya kanye dve dadatuḥ sute ॥ 2.8.116 ॥
paiśāceva vivāhena sudatyā buddhavāhanaḥ।
ajaḥ khaṇḍaśca tābhyāṃ tau tadāśrāvayatāṃ dhanam ॥ 2.8.117 ॥
iyaṃ brahmadhanā nāma mama kanyā hyalomikā ।
brahmasattvadhanāhārā iti khaṇḍobhyabhāṣata ॥ 2.8.118 ॥
iyaṃ jantudhanā nāma kanyā sarvāṅgasundarī।
sarvāṅgakeśī nāmnā ca kanyā jantudhanā tathā।
akarṇāntāpyaromā ca kanyā brahmadhanā tu yā ॥ 2.8.120 ॥
evaṃ piśācakanye te mithune dve prasūyatām।
tayoḥ prajāvisargañca bruvato me nibodhata ॥ 2.8.121 ॥
hetiḥ prahetirugraśca pauruṣeyo vadhastathā।
visphūrjiścaiva vātaśca āpo vyāghrastathaiva ca ॥ 2.8.122 ॥
sarpaśca rākṣasā hyete yātudhānātmajā daśa।
mālyavāṃśca sumālī ca prahetitanayān śrṛṇu।
prahetitanayaḥ śrīmān pulomā nāma viśrutaḥ ॥ 2.8.124 ॥
vyāghraputro nirānando jantūnāṃ vighnakārakaḥ।
svasāro brahmarākṣasyasteṣāñcemāḥ sudāruṇāḥ ॥ 2.8.128 ॥
raktakarṇā mahājihvā'kṣayā caivopahāriṇī।
etāsāmanvaye jātāḥ pṛthivyāṃ brahmarākṣasāḥ ॥ 2.8.129 ॥
ityete rākṣasāḥ krāntā yakṣasyāpi nibodhata ॥ 2.8.130 ॥
cakame'psarasaṃ yakṣa pañcasthūlāṃ kratusthalīm।
vaibhrājaṃ surabhiñcaiva tathā caitrarathañca yat।
dṛṣṭavān nandane tasminnapsarobhiḥ sahāsatīm ॥ 2.8.132 ॥
nopāyaṃ vindate tatra tasyā lābhāya cintayan।
dūṣitaḥ svena rūpeṇa karmmaṇā tena dūṣitaḥ ॥ 2.8.133 ॥
tatkathaṃ nāma cārvaṅgīṃ prāpnuyāmahamaṅganām ॥ 2.8.134 ॥
dṛṣṭvopāyaṃ tataḥ so'tha śīghrakārī vyavarttata।
tataḥ so'psarasāṃ madhye tāṃ jagrāha kratusthalīm ॥ 2.8.135 ॥
buddhvā ca suruciṃ taṃ sā bhāvenaivābhyavarttata।
saṃvṛtaḥ sa tayā sārddhaṃ dṛśyamāno'psarogaṇaiḥ ॥ 2.8.136 ॥
rājāhamiti nābhirhi pitaraṃ so'bhyabhāṣata।
tavātra jāte na bhītiḥ pitā taṃ pratyuvāca ha ॥ 2.8.138 ॥
mātrānurūpo rūpeṇa piturvīryeṇa jāyate।
jāte sa tasmin harṣeṇa svarūpaṃ pratyapadyata ॥ 2.8.139 ॥
svabhāvaṃ pratipadyante bṛhanto yakṣarākṣasāḥ ।
tato'bravīdapsarasaḥ smayamānaḥ sa guhyakaḥ।
ityuktvā sahasā tañca dṛṣṭvā svaṃ rūpamāsthitam।
gacchantīranvagacchadyā putrastāṃ sāntvayan girā।
gandharvāpsarasāṃ madhyetāṃ nītvā sa nyavarttata ॥ 2.8.143 ॥
tāñca dṛṣṭvā samutpattiṃ yakṣasyāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ।
yakṣāṇāṃ tvaṃ janitrīti procustāṃ vai kratusthalīm ॥ 2.8.144 ॥
jagāma saha putreṇa tato yakṣaḥ svamālayam।
tasmānnivāso yakṣāṇāṃ nyagrodhaḥ sarvataḥ priyaḥ ॥ 2.8.145 ॥
yakṣo rajatanābhastu guhyakānāṃ pitāmahaḥ।
anuhrādasya daityasya bhadrāmativarāṃ sutām।
upayeme sa bhadrāyāṃ yasyāṃ maṇivaro vaśī ॥ 2.8.146 ॥
jajñe sā maṇibhadrañca śakratulyaparākramam।
tayoḥ patnyau bhaginyau tu kratusthalyātmaje śubhe ॥ 2.8.147 ॥
nāmnā puṇyajanī caiva tathā devajanī ca yā।
vijajñe maṇibhadrāttu putrān puṇyajanī śubhān ॥ 2.8.148 ॥
siddhārthaṃ sūryatejañca sumantaṃ nandanaṃ tathā।
sarvānubhūtaṃ śaṅkhañca piṅgākṣaṃ bhīrumeva ca।
catvāro viṃśatiścaiva putrāḥ puṇyajanāḥ śubhāḥ ।
jajñire maṇibhadrasya te sarve puṇyalakṣaṇāḥ ।
teṣāṃ putrāśca pautrāśca yakṣā puṇyajanāḥ śubhāḥ ॥ 2.8.152 ॥
vijajñe devajananī putrān maṇivarātmajāt ।
pūrṇabhadraṃ hemarathaṃ maṇimannandivarddhanau ॥ 2.8.153 ॥
kustumburuṃ piśaṅgābhaṃ sthūlakarṇaṃ mahājayam।
śvetañca vipulañcaiva puṣpavantaṃ bhayāvaham ॥ 2.8.154 ॥
padmavarṇaṃ sunetrañca yakṣaṃ bālaṃ bakaṃ tathā।
kumudaṃ kṣemakañcaiva varddhamānaṃ tathā damam ॥ 2.8.155 ॥
padmanābhaṃ varāṅgañca suvīraṃ vijayaṃ kṛtim।
pūrṇamāsaṃ hiraṇyākṣaṃ surūpañcaivamādayaḥ ॥ 2.8.156 ॥
putrā maṇivarasyaite yakṣā vai guhyakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
surūpāśca virūpāśca sragviṇaḥ priyadarśanāḥ।
teṣāṃ putrāśca pautrāśca śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ ॥ 2.8.157 ॥
khaśāyāstvapare putrā rākṣasāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ ।
teṣāṃ yathā pradhānān vai varṇyamānānnibodhata ॥ 2.8.158 ॥
lālāviḥ kuthano bhīmaḥ sumālī madhureva ca।
visphūrjjito vidyujjihvo mātaṅgo dhūmritastatā ॥ 2.8.159 ॥
candrārkaḥ sukaro budhnaḥ kapilomā prahāsakaḥ।
krīḍaḥ paraśunābhaśca cakrākṣaśca niśācaraḥ ॥ 2.8.160 ॥
triśirāḥ śatadaṃṣṭraśca tuṇḍakeśaśca rākṣasaḥ।
ityete rākṣasavarā vikrāntā gaṇarūpiṇaḥ.
sarvalokacarāste tu tridaśānāṃ samakramāḥ ॥ 2.8.162 ॥
sapta cānyā duhitarastāḥ śrṛṇudhvaṃ yathākramam।
tāsāñca yaḥ prajāsargo yena cotpāditā gaṇāḥ ॥ 2.8.163 ॥
ālambā utkacā kṛṣṇā niṛto kapilā śivā।
keśinī ca mahābhāgā bhaginyaḥ sapta yāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.8.164 ॥
tābhyo lokāmiṣādaśca hantāro yuddhadurmadāḥ।
udīrṇā rākṣasagaṇā ime utpāditāḥ śubhāḥ ॥ 2.8.165 ॥
ālambeyo gaṇaḥ krūra utkaceyo gaṇastathā।
tathā kārṣṇeyaśaiveyā rākṣasā hyuttamā gaṇāḥ ॥ 2.8.166 ॥
tathaiva naiṛto nāma tryambakānucareṇa ha।
utpāditaḥ prajāsargo gaṇeśvaracareṇa tu ॥ 2.8.167 ॥
utpāditā balavatā udīrṇā yakṣarākṣasāḥ ।
vikrāntāḥ śauryasampannā naiṛtā devarākṣasāḥ।
yeṣāmadhipatiryukto nāmnā khyāto virūpakaḥ ॥ 2.8.168 ॥
teṣāṃ gaṇaśatānekā uddhṛtānāṃ mahātmanām।
prāyeṇānucarantyete śaṅkaraṃ jagataḥ prabhum ॥ 2.8.169 ॥
daityarājena kumbhena mahākāyā mahātmanā ।.
utpāditā mahāvīryā mahābalaparākramāḥ ॥ 2.8.170 ॥
kapileyā mahāvīryā udīrṇā daityarākṣasāḥ।
kampanena ca yakṣeṇa keśinyāste pare janāḥ ॥ 2.8.171 ॥
utpāditā mahāvātā udīrṇā yakṣarākṣasāḥ।
ālambeyena janitā naikāḥ surasikena hi।
nailā iti samākhyātā durjayā ghoravikramāḥ ॥ 2.8.173 ॥
caranti pṛtivīṃ kṛtsnāṃ tatra te devalaukikāḥ।
bahutvāccaiva sargasya teṣāṃ vaktuṃ na śakyate ॥ 2.8.174 ॥
tasyāstvapi ca nīlāyā vikacā nāma rākṣasī।
utpāditāḥ surā ghorāḥ śrṛṇu tāstvanupūrvaśaḥ ॥ 2.8.176 ॥
daṃṣṭrākarālavikṛtā mahākarṇā mahodarāḥ।
hārakā bhīṣakāścaiva tathaiva krāmakāḥ pare ॥ 2.8.177 ॥
bhūmirākṣasakā hyete mandāḥ puruṣavikramāḥ ॥ 2.8.178 ॥
carantyadṛṣṭapūrvāśca nānākārā hyanekaśaḥ।
utkṛṣṭa balasattvā ye te ca vai khecarāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.8.179 ॥
lakṣamātreṇa cākāśaṃ svalpāḥ svalpaṃ caranti vai ।
etairvyāptamimaṃ lokaṃ śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ ॥ 2.8.180 ॥
bhūmī rākṣasakaiḥ sarvairanekaiḥ kṣudrarākṣasaiḥ।
nānāprakārairākrāntā nānādeśāḥ samantataḥ ॥ 2.8.181 ॥
samāsābhihatāśvaiva hyaṣṭau rākṣasamātaraḥ।
aṣṭau vibhāgā hyeṣāṃ hi vikhyātā anupūrvaśaḥ ॥ 2.8.182 ॥
bhadrakā nikarāḥ kecidyajñaniṣpattihetukāḥ।
sahasrasatasaṅkhyātā marttyalokavicāriṇaḥ ॥ 2.8.183 ॥
pūtanā mātṛsāmānyāstathā bhūtabhayaṅkarāḥ।
bālānāṃ mānuṣe loke grahā vaimānahetukāḥ ॥ 2.8.184 ॥
kaumārāste tu vijñeyā bālānāṃ grahavṛttayaḥ ॥ 2.8.185 ॥
skandagrahaviśeṣāṇāṃ māyikānāṃ tathaiva ca।
pūtanānāmabhūtānāṃ ye ca lokavināyakāḥ ॥ 2.8.186 ॥
sahasraśata saṅkhyānāṃ martyalokavicāriṇām।
evaṃ gaṇaśatānyeva caranti pṛthivīmimām ॥ 2.8.187 ॥
yakṣāṇāṃ rākṣasānāñca paulastyāgastyayaśca ye ।
yakṣā dṛṣṭvā pibantīha nṛṇāṃ māṃsamasṛgvasām।
rakṣāṃsyanupraveśena piśācāḥ paripīḍanaiḥ ॥ 2.8.191 ॥
sarvalakṣaṇasampannāḥ samakṣetrāśca daivataiḥ।
bhāsvarā balavantaśca īśvarāḥ karāmarūpiṇaḥ ॥ 2.8.192 ॥
anābhibhakṣā vikrāntāḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtāḥ।
sūkṣmāścaujasvino medhyā varadā yajñiyāśca ye ॥ 2.8.193 ॥
gandharvebhyastribhiḥ pādairhīnā vai sarvaguhyakāḥ।
aiśvaryahīnā yakṣebhyaḥ piśācāstri guṇaṃ punaḥ ॥ 2.8.195 ॥
evaṃ dhanena rūpeṇa āyuṣā ca balena ca।
dharmaiśvaryeṇa buddhyā ca tapaḥśrutaparākramaiḥ ॥ 2.8.196 ॥
devāsurebhyo hīyante trīn pādān vai parasparam।
gandharvādyāḥ piśācāntāścatasro devayonayaḥ ॥ 2.8.197 ॥
ataḥ śrṛṇuta bhadraṃ vaḥ prajāḥ krodhavaśatmakāḥ ।
krodhāyāṃ kanyakā jajñe dvādaśa hyātmasambhavāḥ।
tā bhāryāḥ pulahasyāsannāmatastā nibodhata ॥ 2.8.198 ॥
mṛgī ca mṛgamandā ca haribhadrā irāvatī।
bhūtā ca kapiśā daṃṣṭrā niśā tiryā tathaiva ca।
śvetā caiva svarā caiva surasā ceti viśrutāḥ ॥ 2.8.199 ॥
mṛgyāstu hariṇāḥ putrā mṛgāścānye śaśāstathā।
nyaṅkavaḥ śarabhā ye ca ruravaḥ pṛṣatāśca ye ॥ 2.8.200 ॥
mṛgarājā mṛgamandāyā gavayāścāpare tathā।
mahiṣoṣṭravarāhāśca khaḍgagauramukhāstathā ॥ 2.8.201 ॥
harestu harayaḥ putrā golāṅgulatarakṣavaḥ ।
vānarāḥ kinnarāścaiva vyāghrāḥ kimpuruṣāstathā।
sūryasyāṇḍakapāle dve samānīya tu bhauvanaḥ।
hastābhyāṃ parigṛhyātha rathantaramagāyata ॥ 2.8.203 ॥
sāmnā prasūyamānena sadya eva gajo'bhavat।
sa prāyacchadirāvatyai putrārthaṃ sa tu bhauvanaḥ ॥ 2.8.204 ॥
irāvatyāḥ suto yasmāttasmādairāvataḥ smṛtaḥ ।
devarājopavāhyatvāt prathamaḥ sa mataṅgarāṭ।
śubhrābhrabhāścaturddaṃṣṭraḥ śrīmānairāvato gajaḥ ॥ 2.8.205 ॥
apsujasyaikamūlasya suvarṇābhasya hastinaḥ ।
ṣaḍdantasya hi bhadrasya aupāvāhyaśca vai balaḥ ॥ 2.8.206 ॥
tasya putro'ñjanaścaiva supratīko'tha vāmanaḥ।
padmaścaiva caturtho'bhūddhastinī cābhramustathā ॥ 2.8.207 ॥
bhadraṃ mṛgañca mandaṃ ca saṅkīrṇaṃ caturaḥ sutān ॥ 2.8.208 ॥
bhadro yaḥ supratīkastu haritaḥ sa hyapāmpateḥ ॥ 2.8.209 ॥
padmo mandastu yo gauro dvipo hyailavilasya saḥ।
mṛgaḥ śyāmastu yo hastī upavāhyaḥ sa pāvakaiḥ ॥ 2.8.210 ॥
udagrabhāvenopetā jāyante tasya cānvaye।
śvetabālanakhāḥ piṅgā varṣmavanto mataṅgajāḥ।
mataṅgajān pravakṣyāmi nāgānanyānapi kramāt ॥ 2.8.212 ॥
kapilaḥ puṇḍarīkaśca sumanābho rathāntaraḥ।
jātau nāmnā sutau tābhyāṃ supratiṣṭhapramarddanau ॥ 2.8.213 ॥
śūlāḥ sthūlāḥ śirodāntāḥ śuddhabālanakhāstathā।
balinaḥ śaktinaścaiva smṛtāstvākulikā gajāḥ ॥ 2.8.214 ॥
puṣpadanto bṛhatsāmā ṣaḍdanto danta puṣpavān।
tāmravarṇaśca tatputraḥ sahacāriviṣāṇitaḥ ॥ 2.8.215 ॥
anvaye cāsya jāyante lamboṣṭāścārudarśinaḥ।
vāmadevo'ñjanaśyāmaḥ sāmno jajñe'tha vāmanaḥ।
bhāryā caivāṅgadā tasya nīlavallakṣaṇau sutau ॥ 2.8.217 ॥
caṇḍaścātraśiro grīvā vyūḍhoraskāstarasvinaḥ।
narairbaddhāḥ kule teṣāṃ jāyante vikṛtā gajāḥ ॥ 2.8.218 ॥
tasya prahārī sampātī pṛthuścittisutāstrayaḥ ॥ 2.8.219 ॥
paśavo dīrghatālvauṣṭāḥ suvibhaktaśirodarāḥ।
jāyante mṛdusambhūtā vaṃśe tasya mataṅgajāḥ ॥ 2.8.220 ॥
añjanādañjanā sāmno vijajñe cāñjanāvatī।
mahāvibhaktaśirasaḥ snigdhajīmūtasannibhāḥ।
sudarśanāḥ suvarṣmāṇaḥ padmābhāḥ parimaṇḍalāḥ।
śūnāḥ pītāyatamukhā gajāstasyānvaye'bhavan ॥ 2.8.222 ॥
jajñe candramasaḥ sāmnaḥ piṅgalā kumudadyutiḥ।
piṅgalāyāḥ sutau tasyā mahāpadmormimālinau ॥ 2.8.223 ॥
hastiyuddhe priyānnāgān viddhi tasya kulodbhavān ॥ 2.8.224 ॥
etān devāsure yuddhe jayārthe jagṛhuḥ surāḥ।
kṛtārthaiśca visṛṣṭāstaiḥ pūrvoktāḥ prayayurdiśaḥ ॥ 2.8.225 ॥
eteṣāmanvaye jātān vinītāṃstridaśā daduḥ ।
aṅgāya lomapādāya sūtrakārāya vai dvipān ॥ 2.8.226 ॥
varaṇādvāraṇo dantī dantābhyāṃ garjanādgajaḥ ॥ 2.8.227 ॥
mataṅgāditi mātaṅgo dvipo dvābhyāmapi smṛtaḥ।
sāmajaḥ sāmajātatvāditi nirvacanakramaḥ ॥ 2.8.228 ॥
eṣāṃ jihvāparāvṛttirivāktaṃ hyagniśāpajam।
balasyānavato yā tu yā caiṣāṃ gūḍhamuṣkatā।
devadānavagandharvāḥ piśācoragarākṣasāḥ।
kanyāsu jātā diṅnāgairnānāsāttvāstato gajāḥ ॥ 2.8.230 ॥
sambhūtiśca prabūtiśca nāmanirvacanaṃ tathā।
etadgajānāṃ vijñeyaṃ yeṣāṃ rājā vibhāvasuḥ ॥ 2.8.231 ॥
uttarā tasya vindhyasya gaṅgāyā dakṣiṇañca yat।
gaṅgodbhedātkarūṣebhyaḥ supratīkasya tadvanam ॥ 2.8.233 ॥
ekabhūtātmanosyaitadvāmanasya vanaṃ smṛtam ॥ 2.8.234 ॥
apareṇa tu lauhityamāsindhoḥ paścimena tu।
yamasyaitadvanaṃ proktamanuparvatameva tat ॥ 2.8.235 ॥
sthūlān kṛśāṃśca dīrghāṃśca vāmanān hrasvakān samān ॥ 2.8.236 ॥
lambakarṇān pralamboṣṭān lambajihvāstanodarān।
ekarūpān dvirūpāṃśca lambasphiksthūlapiṇḍikān ॥ 2.8.237 ॥
babhrūn vai śabalān dhūmrān kadrūn rāsabhadārūṇān।
bahuśīrṣān viśīrṣāṃśca ekaśīrṣāṃśca śīrṣakān ॥ 2.8.240 ॥
sarovarasamudrādinadīpulinasevinaḥ।
ekakarṇān mahākarṇān śaṅkukarṇānakarṇikān ॥ 2.8.242 ॥
daṃṣṭriṇo nakhinaścaiva nirddantāṃśca dvijihvakān।
ekahastān dvihastāṃśca trihastāṃścāpyahastakān ॥ 2.8.243 ॥
ekapādān dvipādāṃśca tripādān bahupādakān ।
mahāyogān mahāsattvān sutapakvān mahābalān ॥ 2.8.244 ॥
sarvatragānapratighān brahmajñān kāmarūpiṇaḥ ।
hastādāṃśca mukhādāṃśca śirodāṃśca kapālinaḥ ॥ 2.8.246 ॥
dhanvino mudgaradharānasiśūladharāṃstathā।
rātrisandhyācarān ghorān vkacitsaumyān divācarān।
paratve ca bhayaṃ daiva sarve te gatamānasāḥ।
naiṣāṃ bhāryā'sti putro vā sarve te hyūrddhvaretasaḥ ॥ 2.8.249 ॥
śatantāni sahasrāṇi bhūtānāmātmayoginām।
kapiśatvāt piśācāste sarve ca piśitāśanāḥ ॥ 2.8.251 ॥
yugmāni ṣoḍaśānyāni varttamānāstadanvayāḥ।
chagalaśchagalī caiva vakro vakramukhī tathā।
anarkaśca anarkā ca kukhaṇḍaśca kukhaṇḍikā।
pāṇipātraḥ pāṇipātrī pāṃśuḥ pāṃśumatī tathā ॥ 2.8.255 ॥
nituṇḍaśca nituṇḍī ca nipuṇā nipuṇastathā।
ṣoḍaśānāṃ piśācānāṃ gaṇāḥ proktāstu ṣoḍaśa ॥ 2.8.256 ॥
ajāmukhā vakramukhāḥ pūriṇaḥ skandinastathā।
vipādāṅgārikāścaiva kumbhapātrāḥ prakundakāḥ ॥ 2.8.257 ॥
sūcīmukhoccheṣaṇādāḥ kulānyetāni ṣoḍaśa।
ityetā hyabhijātāstu kūṣmāṇḍānāṃ prakīrtitāḥ ॥ 2.8.259 ॥
bībhatsaṃ vikṛtācāraṃ putrapautramanantakam।
atasteṣāṃ piśācānāṃ lakṣaṇañca nibodhata ॥ 2.8.260 ॥
sarvāṅgakeśā vṛttākhyā daṃṣṭriṇo nakhinastathā।
tiryaṅgāḥ puruṣādāśca piśācāste hyadhomukhāḥ ॥ 2.8.261 ॥
akeśakā hyaromāṇastvagvasāścarmavāsasaḥ।
kūṣmāṇḍikāḥ piśācāste tilabhakṣāḥ sadāmiṣāḥ ॥ 2.8.262 ॥
vakrāṅgahastapādāśca vakraśīlāgatāstathā।
jñeyā vakrapiśācāste vakragāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ ॥ 2.8.263 ॥
lambodarāstuṇḍanāśā hrasvakāyaśirobhujāḥ।
nitundakāḥ piśācāste tilatakṣāḥ priyaśravāḥ ॥ 2.8.264 ॥
vāmanākṛtayaścaiva vācālāḥ plutagāminaḥ।
piśācānarkamarkāste vṛkṣavāsādanapriyāḥ ॥ 2.8.265 ॥
ūrddhvabāhūrddhvaromāṇa ūrddhvavṛkṣāstathālayāḥ।
muñcanti pāṃśūnaṅgebhyaḥ piśācāḥ pāṃśavaśca te ॥ 2.8.266 ॥
dhamanīmatakāḥ śuṣkāḥ śmaśrulāścīravāsasaḥ।
upavīrāḥ piśācāśca śmaśānāyatanāstathā ॥ 2.8.267 ॥
viṣṭabdhākṣā mahājihvā lelihānā hyudūkhalāḥ।
hastyuṣṭrasthūlaśiraso viratā baddhapiṇḍakāḥ ॥ 2.8.268 ॥
piśācāḥ sumbhapātrāste adṛṣṭānnāni bhuñjate।
sūkṣmāstu romaśāḥ piṅgā dṛṣṭādṛṣṭāścaranti vai ॥ 2.8.269 ॥
ayuktāśca viśantīha nipuṇāste piśācakāḥ.
ākarṇa dāritāsyāśca lambaśrūsthūlanāsikāḥ ॥ 2.8.270 ॥
hastapādākrāntagaṇā hrasvakāḥ kṣitidṛṣṭayaḥ।
bālādāste piśācā vai sūtikāgṛhasevinaḥ ॥ 2.8.271 ॥
pṛṣṭhataḥ pāṇipādāśca hrasvakā vātaraṃhasaḥ।
piśitādāḥ piśācāste saṃgrāme rudhirāśinaḥ ॥ 2.8.272 ॥
piśācāḥ skandinaste vai anyā ucchusanāśinaḥ ।
ṣoḍaśa jātayasteṣāṃ piśācānāṃ prakīrttitāḥ ॥ 2.8.273 ॥
evaṃvidhānpiśācāṃstu dīnāndṛṣṭvānukampayā।
tebhyo brahmā varaṃ prādātkāruṇyādalpacetasaḥ।
antarddhānaṃ prajāsteṣāṃ kāmarūpatvameva ca ॥ 2.8.274 ॥
gṛhāṇi yāni bhagnāni śūnyānyalpajanāni ca ॥ 2.8.275 ॥
vidhvastāni ca yāni syuranācāroṣitāni ca।
asaṃspṛṣṭopa liptāni saṃskārairvarjitāni ca ॥ 2.8.276 ॥
rājamārgoparathyāśca niṣkuṇṭāścatvarāṇi ca।
dvārāṇyaṣṭālakāścaiva nirmamānsaṃkramāṃstathā ॥ 2.8.277 ॥
patho nadyo'tha tīrthāni caityavṛkṣānmahāpathān ।
piśācā viniviṣṭā vai sthāneṣveteṣu sarvaśaḥ ॥ 2.8.278 ॥
varṇāśramāḥ saṅkarikāḥ kāruśilpijanāstathā ॥ 2.8.279 ॥
etairanyaiśca bahubiranyāyopārjjitairdhanaiḥ ।
ārabhante kriyā yāstu piśācāstatra devatāḥ ॥ 2.8.280 ॥
madhumāṃsaudanairdadhnā tilacūrṇasurāsavaiḥ।
dhūpairhāridrakṛśaraistailabhadraguḍaudanaiḥ ॥ 2.8.281 ॥
kṛṣṇāni caiva vāsāṃsi dhūpāḥ sumanasastathā।
evaṃ yuktāḥ subalayasteṣāṃ vai parvasandhiṣu।
piśācānāmanujñāya brahmā so'dhipatirdadau ॥ 2.8.282 ॥
sarvabhūtapiśācānāṃ giriśaṃ śūlapāṇinam ।
dṛṣṭvā tvajanayanputrānvyāghrānsiṃhāṃśca bhāminī ॥ 2.8.283 ॥
dvipinaśca sutāstasyā vyāleyāścāmiṣāśinaḥ।
ṛṣayaścāpi kārtsnyena prajāsargaṃ nibodhata।
tasyā duhitaraḥ pañca tāsāṃ nāmāni me śrṛṇu ॥ 2.8.284 ॥
mīnā mātā tathā vṛttā parivṛttā tathaiva ca।
anuvṛttā tu vijñeyā tāsāṃ vai śrṛṇuta prajāḥ ॥ 2.8.285 ॥
sahasradantā makarāḥ pāṭīnāstāmarohitāḥ।
ityevamādirhi gaṇo maino vistīrṇa ucyate ॥ 2.8.286 ॥
vṛttā kūrmavikārāṇi naikāni jalacāriṇām।
tathā śaṅkhavikārāṇi janayāmāsa naikaśaḥ ॥ 2.8.288 ॥
maṇḍūkānāṃ vikārāṇi anuvṛttā vyajāyata।
aiṇeyānāṃ vikārāṇi śambūkānāṃ tathaiva ca ॥ 2.8.289 ॥
tathā śuktivikārāṇi varāṭakakṛtāni ca।
tathā śaṅkhavikārāṇi parivṛttā vyajāyata ॥ 2.8.290 ॥
kālakūṭavikārāṇi jalaukavihitāni ca ।
ityeṣa hi ṛṣervaṃśaḥ pañcaśākhāḥ prakīrttitāḥ ॥ 2.8.291 ॥
tiryagaṃ hetukamādyādurbahulaṃ vaṃśavistaram।
saṃsvedajavikārāṇi yathā yebhyo bhavanti ha ॥ 2.8.292 ॥
manuṣyāḥ svedamalajāḥ uśanā nāma jantavaḥ।
nānāpipīlikagaṇāḥ kīṭakā baddhapādakāḥ ॥ 2.8.293 ॥
śaṅkhopalavikārāṇi kīlakācārakāṇi ca।
ityevamādibahulāḥ svedajāḥ pārthivā gaṇāḥ ॥ 2.8.294 ॥
tathā gharmāditaptābhyastvadbhayo vṛṣṭibhya eva ca।
naikā mṛgaśarīrebhyo jāyante jantavastvime ॥ 2.8.295 ॥
nīlacitrāśca jāyante hyalakā bahuvistarāḥ ॥ 2.8.296 ॥
jalajāḥ svedajāścaiva jāyante jantavastvime।
kāśāto yañjakāḥ kīṭanaladā bahupādakāḥ ॥ 2.8.297 ॥
sihalā romalāścaiva picchalāḥ parikīrttitāḥ।
ityemādirhi gaṇo jalajaḥ svedajaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.8.298 ॥
sarpirbhyo māṣamudgānāṃ jāyante kramaśastathā।
jambubilvāmrapūgebhyaḥ phalebhyaścaiva jantavaḥ ॥ 2.8.299 ॥
mudgebhyaḥ panasebhyaśca taṇḍulebhyastathaiva ca।
tathā koṭaraśuṣkebhyo nihitebhyo bhavanti hi ॥ 2.8.300 ॥
anyebhyo'pi ca jāyante na hi tebhyaściraṃ sadā।
jantavasturagādibhyo viṣādibhyastathaiva ca ॥ 2.8.301 ॥
bahūnyahāni niḥkṣipte sambhavanti ca gomaye।
jāyante kṛmayo viprā kāṣṭebhyaśca ghuṇādayaḥ ॥ 2.8.302 ॥
saṃsvedajāśca jāyante vṛścikāḥ śuṣkagomayāt ॥ 2.8.304 ॥
gobhyo hi mahiṣebhyaśca jāyante jantavaḥ prabho।
matsyādayaśca vividhā aṇḍakukṣau viśeṣataḥ ॥ 2.8.305 ॥
caivīrikāśca jāyante tathā gojākulāni ca।
tathānyāni ca sūkṣmāṇi jalaukādīni jātayaḥ ॥ 2.8.306 ॥
makṣikāṇāṃ vikārāṇi jāyante jāta yo'pare ।
prāyeṇa tu vasantyasminnucchiṣṭodakakarddame ॥ 2.8.307 ॥
maśakānāṃ vikārāṇi bhramarāṇāṃ tathaiva ca।
maṇicchedāstathā vyālāḥ potajāḥ parikīrttitāḥ।
śataverivikārāṇi karīṣebhyo bhavantiha ॥ 2.8.309 ॥
evamādirasaṅkhyāto gaṇaḥ saṃsvedajo mayā।
samāsābhihito hyeṣa prākkarmavaśajaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.8.310 ॥
tathā'nye naiṛtāḥ sattvāste smṛtā upasargajāḥ।
pūtāstu yonijāḥ kecitkecidautpattikāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.8.311 ॥
prāyeṇa devāḥ sarve vai vijñeyā hyupapattijāḥ ।
kecittu yonijā devāḥ kecidevānimittataḥ ॥ 2.8.312 ॥
tamobahula ityeṣa gaṇaḥ krodhavaśātmakaḥ ॥ 2.8.315 ॥
pulahasyātmajā sargastāmrāyāstannibodhata।
bahvanyāstvabivikhyātāstāmrāyāśca vijajñire ॥ 2.8.316 ॥
sampātiñca jaṭāyuñca prasūtā pakṣisattamau ॥ 2.8.317 ॥
jaṭāyuṣaśca ye putrāḥ kāka gṛdhrāścakarṇinaḥ ॥ 2.8.318 ॥
bhāryā garutmataścāpi bhāsī krauñcī tathā śukī।
śukī garutmataḥ putrān suṣuve ṣaṭ pariśrutān ।
triśaṅkhanetraṃ sumukhaṃ surūpaṃ surasaṃ balam।
eṣāṃ putrāśca pautrāśca garuḍānāṃ mahātmanām ॥ 2.8.321 ॥
caturdaśa sahasrāṇi krūrāṇāṃ pannagāśinām।
putrapautravisargācca teṣāṃ vai vaṃśavistaraḥ ॥ 2.8.322 ॥
vyāptāni yāni deśāni tāni vakṣye yathākramam।
śālmalidvīpamakhilaṃ devakūṭañca parvatam ॥ 2.8.323 ॥
maṇimantañca śailendraṃ sahasraśikharaṃ tathā।
parṇamālaṃ sukeśañca śataśrṛṅgaṃ tathācalam ॥ 2.8.324 ॥
kaurajaṃ pañcaśikharaṃ hemakūṭañca parvatam।
pracaṇḍavāyuprabhavairdīpitaiḥ pajharāgibhiḥ ॥ 2.8.325 ॥
śailajālāni vyāptāni gāruḍaistairmahātmabhiḥ ।
bhāsīputrāḥ smṛtā bhāsā ulūkā kākakukkuṭāḥ ॥ 2.8.326 ॥
mayūrāḥ kalaviṅkāśca kapotā lāvatittirāḥ।
krauñcī vārddhīṇasān śyenī kurarānsārasānbakān ॥ 2.8.327 ॥
ityevamādayonye'pi kravyādā ye ca pakṣiṇaḥ।
dhṛtarāṣṭrī ca haṃsāṃśca kalahaṃsāṃśca bhāminī ॥ 2.8.328 ॥
cakravākāṃśca vihagānsarvāṃścaivādakān dvijān।
garuḍasyātmajāḥ proktā irāyāḥ śrṛṇuta prajāḥ।
irā prajajñe kanyā vaitisraḥ kamalalocanāḥ ॥ 2.8.330 ॥
vana spatīnāṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ vīrudhāñcaiva mātaraḥ।
latā vanaspatīñjajñe hyapuṣpān pulinasthitān ।
vīrudhā tadapatyāni vaṃśaścātra samāpyate ॥ 2.8.333 ॥
ete kaśyapadāyādā vyākhyātāḥ sthāṇujaṅgamāḥ ।
teṣāṃ putrāśca pautrāśca yairidaṃ pūritaṃ jagat ॥ 2.8.334 ॥
iti sargaikadeśasya kīrtito'vayavo mayā।
mārīco'yaṃ prajā sargaḥ samāsena prakīrtitaḥ।
na śakyaṃ vyāsato vaktumapi varṣaśatairdvijāḥ ।। 8.335 ।।
aditirdharmaśīlā tu balaśīlā ditiḥ smṛtā।
tapaḥśīlā tu surabhi rmāyāśīlā danuḥ smṛtā ।। 8.336 ।।
irā grahaṇaśīlā tu danāyurbhakṣaṇe ratā ।। 8.337 ।।
vāhaśīlā tu vinatā tāmrā vai pāśaśālinī।
svabhāvā lokamātṝṇāṃ śīlānyetāni sarvaśaḥ ।। 8.338 ।।
dharmataḥ śīlato buddhyā kṣamayā balarūpataḥ।
rajaḥ sattvatamo vṛttā dhārmikādhārmikāstu vai ।। 8.339 ।।
devatāsuragandharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ।
piśācāḥ paśavaścaiva mṛgāḥ pataṅgavīrudhaḥ ।। 8.340 ।।
yasmāddākṣāyaṇīṣvete jajñire mānuṣīṣviha।
manvantareṣu sarveṣu tasmācchreṣṭāstu mānuṣāḥ ।। 8.341 ।।
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāḥ sādhakāstu vai।
tato'dhaḥ srotasaste vai utpadyante surāsurāḥ ।। 8.342 ।।
jāyante kāryasiddhayarthaṃ mānuṣeṣu punaḥ punaḥ।
ityevaṃ vaṃśaprabhavaḥ prasaṅkhyātastapasvinām ।। 8.343 ।।
surāṇāmasurāṇāñca gandharvāpsarasāṃ tathā।
yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācānāṃ suparṇoragapakṣiṇām ।। 8.344 ।।
vyālānāṃ śikhināñcaiva oṣadhīnāñca sarvaśaḥ।
kṛmikīṭapataṅgānāṃ kṣudrāṇāṃ jalajāśca ye।
paśūnāṃ brāhṇānāñca śrīmatāṃ puṇyalakṣaṇam ।। 8.345 ।।
āyuṣyaścaiva dhanyaśca śrīmān hitasukhāvahaḥ।
śrotavyaścaiva satataṃ grāhyaścaivānusūyatā ।। 8.346 ।।
imantu vaṃśaṃ niyamena yaḥ paṭenmahātmanāṃ brāhṇavaidyasaṃsadi ।
apatyalābhaṃ hi labetsupuṣkalaṃ śriyaṃ dhanaṃ pretya ca śobhanāṃ gatim ।। 8.347 ।।
evaṃ prajāsu sṛṣṭāsu kaśyape na mahātmanā।
pratiṣṭitāsu sarvāsu sthāvarāsu carāsu ca ॥ 2.9.1 ॥
abhiṣicyādhipatyeṣu teṣāṃ mukhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ।
tataḥ krameṇa rājyāni vyādeṣṭumupacakrame ॥ 2.9.2 ॥
dvijātīnāṃ vīrudhāñca nakṣatrāṇāṃ grahaiḥ saha।
yajñānāṃ tapasāñcaiva somaṃ rājye'bhyaṣecayata ॥ 2.9.3 ॥
bṛhaspatiṃ tu viśveṣāṃ dadāvaṅgirasāṃ patim।
bhṛgūṇāmadhipañcaiva kāvyaṃ rājye'bhyaṣecayat ॥ 2.9.4 ॥
ādityānāṃ punarviṣṇuṃ vasūnāmatha pāvakam ।
prajāpatīnāṃ dakṣañca marutāmatha vāsavam ॥ 2.9.5 ॥
daityānāmatha rājānaṃ prahlādaṃ ditinandanam।
nārāyaṇaṃ tu sādhyānāṃ rudrāṇāṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam ॥ 2.9.6 ॥
vipracittiñca rājānaṃ dānavānāmathādiśat।
apāṃ tu varuṇaṃ rājye rājñāṃ vaiśravaṇaṃ patim।
yakṣāṇāṃ rākṣasānāñca pārthivānāṃ dhanasya ca ॥ 2.9.7 ॥
vaivasvataṃ pitṝṇāñca yamaṃ rājye'bhyaṣecayat।
sarvabhūtapiśācānāṃ giriśaṃ śūlapāṇinam ॥ 2.9.8 ॥
śailānāṃ himavantañca nadīnāmatha sāgaram।
gandharvāṇāmadhipatiṃ cakre citrarathaṃ tadā ॥ 2.9.9 ॥
uccaiḥśravasamaśvānāṃ rājānañcābhyaṣecayat।
mṛgāṇāmatha śārdūlaṃ govṛṣañca catuṣpadām ॥ 2.9.10 ॥
pakṣiṇāmatha sarveṣāṃ garuḍaṃ patatāṃ varam।
gandhānāṃ mātulañcaiva bhūtānāmaśarīriṇām ॥ 2.9.11 ॥
śabdākāśabalānāñca vāyuṃ balavatāṃ varam।
sarveṣāṃ daṃṣṭriṇāṃ śeṣaṃ nāgānāmatha vāsukim ॥ 2.9.12 ॥
sarīsṛpāṇāṃ sarpāṇāṃ nāgānāñcaiva takṣakam।
sāgarāṇāṃ nadīnāñca meghānāṃ vraṣitasya ca।
ādityānāmanyatamaṃ parjanyamabhiṣiktavān ॥ 2.9.13 ॥
sarvāpsarogaṇānāñca kāmadevaṃ tathaiva ca।
ṛtūnāmatha māsānāmārttavānāṃ tathaiva ca ॥ 2.9.14 ॥
pakṣāṇāñca vipakṣāṇāṃ muhūrttānāñca parvaṇām।
kalākāṣṭāpramāṇānāṃ gate rayanayostathā।
gaṇitasyātha yogasya cakre saṃvatsaraṃ prabhum ॥ 2.9.15 ॥
prajāpatirvai rajasaḥ pūrvasyāndiśi viśrutam।
putraṃ nāmnā sudhāmānaṃ rājānaṃ so'bhyaṣecayat ॥ 2.9.16 ॥
paścimāyāṃ diśi tathā rajasaḥ putramacyutam।
ketumantaṃ mahātmānaṃ rājānaṃ so'bhyaṣecayat ॥ 2.9.17 ॥
manuṣyāṇāmadhipatiṃ cakre caiva sutaṃ manum।
tairiyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā sapattanā ।
yathāpradeśamadyāpi dharmeṇa paripālyate ॥ 2.9.18 ॥
svāyambhuve'ntare pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā te'bhiṣecitāḥ।
nṛpā hyete'bhiṣicyante manavo ye bhavanti vai ॥ 2.9.19 ॥
manvantareṣvatīteṣu gatā hyeteṣu pārthivāḥ।
evamanye'bhiṣicyante prāpte manvantare punaḥ।
atītānāgatāḥ sarve smṛtā manvantareśvarāḥ ॥ 2.9.20 ॥
rājasūye'bhiṣiktaśca pṛthurebhirnarottamaiḥ।
vedadṛṣṭena vidhinā kṛto rājā pratāpavān ॥ 2.9.21 ॥
etānutpādya putrāṃstu prajāsantānakāraṇāt ।
punareva mahābhāgaḥ prajānāṃ patirīśvaraḥ ॥ 2.9.22 ॥
kaśyapo gotrakāmastu cacāra paramaṃ tapaḥ ।
putrau gotrakarau mahyaṃ bhavetāmityacintayat ॥ 2.9.23 ॥
tasya pradhyāyamānasya kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ।
brahmaṇoṃ'śau sutau paścāt prādurbhūtau mahaujasau ॥ 2.9.24 ॥
vatsāraścāsitaścaiva tāvubhau brahmavādinau।
vatsārānnidhruvo jajñe raibhyaśca sa mahāyaśāḥ ॥ 2.9.25 ॥
raibhyasya raibhyā vijñeyā nidhruvasya nibodhata।
cyavanasya sukanyāyāṃ sumedhāḥ samapadyata ॥ 2.9.26 ॥
nidhruvasya tu yā patnī mātā vai kuṇḍapāyinām।
asitasyaikaparṇāyāṃ brahmiṣṭhaḥ samapadyata ॥ 2.9.27 ॥
śāṇḍilyānāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā devalaḥ sumahāyaśāḥ।
nidhruvāḥ śāṇḍilyā raibhyāstrayaḥ paścāttu kaśyapāḥ ॥ 2.9.28 ॥
varaprabhṛtayo devā devalasya prajāstvimāḥ।
caturyuge tvatikrānte manorhyekādaśe prajāḥ।
athāvaśiṣṭe tasmistu dvāpare sampravartate ॥ 2.9.29 ॥
mānasasya cariṣyantastasya putro damaḥ kila।
tretāyugamukhe rājā tṛtīye sambabhūva ha।
bṛhaspaterbṛhatkīrttirdevācāryasya kīrttitaḥ ।
kanyāṃ tasyopayeme sa nāmnā vai devavarṇinīm ॥ 2.9.33 ॥
kaikasīṃ mālinaḥ kanyāṃ tāsāntu śrṛṇuta prajāḥ ॥ 2.9.34 ॥
jyeṣṭhaṃ vaiśravaṇaṃ tasya suṣuve devavarṇinī।
divyena vidhinā yuktamārṣeṇaiva śrutena ca।
rākṣasena ca rūpeṇa āsureṇa balena ca ॥ 2.9.35 ॥
tripādaṃ sumahākāyaṃ sthūlaśīrṣaṃ mahātanum।
aṣṭadaṃṣṭraṃ haricchmaśruṃ śaṅkukarṇaṃ vilohitam ॥ 2.9.36 ॥
hrasva bāhuṃ prabāhuñca piṅgalaṃ suvibhīṣaṇam।
vaivartajñānasampannaṃ sambuddhaṃ jñānasampadā ॥ 2.9.37 ॥
pitā dṛṣṭvābravīttatra kubero'yamiti svayam ॥ 2.9.38 ॥
kutsāyāṃ kvitiśabdo'yaṃ śarīraṃ beramucyate ।
kuberaḥ kuśarīratvānnāmnā tena ca so'ṅkitaḥ ॥ 2.9.39 ॥
yasmādviśravaso'patyaṃ sādṛśyādviśravā iva।
tasmādvaiśravaṇo nāma nāmnā loke bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.9.40 ॥
ṛddhyāṃ kubero'janayadviśrutaṃ nalakūbaram।
rāvaṇaṃ kumbhakarṇañca kanyāṃ śūrpaṇakhāntathā।
vibhīṣaṇaṃ caturthāṃstānkaikasyajanayetsutān ॥ 2.9.41 ॥
śaṅkukarṇo daśagrīvaḥ piṅgalo raktamūrddhajaḥ।
catuṣpādviṃśatibujo mahākāyo mahā balaḥ ॥ 2.9.42 ॥
jātyāñjananibho daṃṣṭro lohitagrīva eva ca।
rājaseno jayayukto rūpeṇa ca balena ca ॥ 2.9.43 ॥
satyabuddhirdṛḍhatanū rākṣasaireva rāvaṇaḥ ।
nisargāddāruṇaḥ krūro rāvaṇādrāvaṇastu saḥ ॥ 2.9.44 ॥
hiraṇyakaśipustvāsītsa rājā pūrvajanmani।
caturyugāni rājātra trayodaśa sa rākṣasaḥ ॥ 2.9.45 ॥
tāḥ pañcakoṭyo varṣāṇāmākhyātāḥ saṅkhyayā dvijaiḥ।
ṣaṣṭiśatasahasrāṇi varṣāṇāntu sa rāvaṇaḥ ।
devatānāṃ ṛṣīṇāñca ghoraṃ kṛtvā prajāgaram ॥ 2.9.47 ॥
tretāyuge caturviṃśe rāvaṇastapasaḥ kṣayāt।
rāmaṃ dāśarathiṃ prāpya sagaṇaḥ kṣayamīyivān ॥ 2.9.48 ॥
mahodayaḥ prahastaśca mahāpāṃśukharastathā।
puṣpotkaṭāyāḥ putrāste kanyā kumbhīnasī tathā ॥ 2.9.49 ॥
triśirā dūṣaṇaścaiva vidyujjihvaśca rākṣasaḥ।
kanyā hyasalikā caiva vākāyāḥ prasavāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.9.50 ॥
ityete krūrakarmāṇaḥ paulastyā rākṣasā daśa।
dāruṇābijanāḥ sarve devairapi durāsadāḥ ॥ 2.9.51 ॥
sarve labdhavarāścaiva putrapautrasamanvitāḥ।
yakṣāṇāñcaiva sarveṣāṃ paulastyā ye ca rākṣasāḥ ॥ 2.9.52 ॥
āgastyavaiśvāmitrāṇāṃ krūrāṇāṃ brahmarakṣasām।
vedādhyayanaśīlānāṃ tapovrataniṣeviṇām ॥ 2.9.53 ॥
teṣāmaiḍaviḍo rājā paulastyaḥ savyapiṅgalaḥ।
itare vai yajñamukhāstena rakṣogaṇāstrayaḥ ॥ 2.9.54 ॥
yātu dhānā brahmadhānā vārttāścaiva divācarāḥ ।
niśācaragaṇāsteṣāṃ catvāraḥ kavibhiḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.9.55 ॥
paulastyā naiṛtāścaiva āgatsyāḥ kauśikāstathā।
ityetāḥ sapta teṣāṃ vai jātayo rākṣasāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.9.56 ॥
teṣāṃ rūpaṃ pravakṣyāmi svabhāvena vyavasthitam।
vṛttākṣāḥ piṅgalāścaiva mahākāyā mahodarāḥ ॥ 2.9.57 ॥
aṣṭadaṃṣṭrā śaṅkukarṇā ūrddhvaromāṇa eva ca।
ākarṇadāritāsyāśca muñjadhūmorddhvamūrddhajāḥ ॥ 2.9.58 ॥
sthūlaśīrṣāḥ sitābhāśca hrasvakāśca pravāhukāḥ।
tāmrāsyā lambajihvauṣṭā lambabhūsthūlanāsikāḥ ॥ 2.9.59 ॥
nīlāṅgā lohitagrīvā gambhīrākṣā vibīṣaṇāḥ ।
mahāghorasvarāścaiva vikaṭā baddhapiṇḍikāḥ ॥ 2.9.60 ॥
sthūlāśca tuṅganāsāśca śilāsaṃhananā dṛḍhāḥ।
dāruṇābhijanāḥ krūrāḥ prāyaśaḥ kliṣṭakarmiṇaḥ ॥ 2.9.61 ॥
sakuṇḍalāṅgadāpīḍā mukuṭoṣṇīṣadhāriṇaḥ।
vicitra vastrābharaṇāścitrasraganulepanāḥ ॥ 2.9.62 ॥
annādāḥ piśitādāśca puruṣādāśca te smṛtāḥ।
ityetadrūpasādharmyaṃ rākṣasānāṃ budhaiḥ smṛtam।
pulahasya mṛgāḥ putrāḥ sarve vyālāśca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ ।
bhūtāḥ piśācāḥ sarpāśca bhramarā hastinastathā ॥ 2.9.64 ॥
vānarāḥ kinnarāścaiva yamakimpuruṣāstathā।
anapatyaḥ kratustasmin smṛto vaivasvate'ntare।
na tasya putraḥ pautro vā tejaḥ saṃkṣipya vā sthitaḥ ।। 9.66।
atrervaṃśaṃ pravakṣyāmi tṛtīyasya prajāpateḥ।
tasya patnyaśca sundaryo daśaivāsanpativratāḥ ॥ 2.9.66 ॥
bhadrāśvasya dhṛtācyāṃ vai daśāpsarasi sūnavaḥ।
bhadrā śūdrā ca madrā ca śaladā maladā tathā ॥ 2.9.67 ॥
velā khalā ca saptaitā yā ca gocapalā smṛtā ।
tathā mānarasā caiva ratnakṛṭā ca tā daśa ॥ 2.9.68 ॥
bhadrāyāṃ janayāmāsa somaṃ putraṃ yaśasvinam ॥ 2.9.69 ॥
svarbhānunā hate sūrye patamāno divo mahīm।
tamo'bhibhūte loke'smin prabhā yena pravarttitā ॥ 2.9.70 ॥
svasti te'stviti coktaḥ sa patanniha divākaraḥ।
brahmarṣervacanāttasya na papāta divo mahīm ॥ 2.9.71 ॥
atriśreṣṭāni gotrāṇi yaścakāra mahātapāḥ ।
yajñeṣvatrighanaścaiva surairyaśca pravarttitaḥ ॥ 2.9.72 ॥
daśa tāsveva mahatā tapasā bhāvitaprabhā ॥ 2.9.73 ॥
svastyātreyā iti khyātā ṛṣayo vedapāragāḥ ।
teṣāṃ vikhyātayaśasau brahmiṣṭau sumahaujasau ॥ 2.9.74 ॥
yavīyasī sutā tasyā mabalā brahmavādinī।
atrāpyudāharantīmaṃ ślokaṃ paurāṇikāḥ purā ॥ 2.9.75 ॥
atreḥ putraṃ mahātmānaṃ śāntātmānamakalmaṣam।
dattātreyaṃ tanuṃ viṣṇoḥ purāṇajñāḥ pracakṣate ॥ 2.9.76 ॥
tasya gotrānvaye jātāścatvāraḥ prathitā bhuvi।
ete nṛṇāntu catvāraḥ smṛtāḥ pakṣā mahaujasām ॥ 2.9.77 ॥
kaśyapānnāradaścaiva parvato'rundhatī tathā।
nāradastu vasiṣṭāyārundhatīṃ pratyapādayat।
ūrddhvaretā mahātejā vṛkṣaśāpāttu nāradaḥ ॥ 2.9.79 ॥
purā devāsure tasminsaṃgrāma tārakāmaye।
anāvṛṣṭyā hate loke vyagre śakre suraiḥ saha।
vasiṣṭhastapasā dhīmāndhārayāmāsa vai prajāḥ ॥ 2.9.80 ॥
tāstena jīvayāmāsa kāruṇyādoṣadhena tu ॥ 2.9.81 ॥
arundhatyāṃ vasiṣṭhastu śaktimutpādayaddvijāḥ।
sāgarañjanayacchakteradṛśyantī parāśaram ॥ 2.9.82 ॥
kālī parāśarājjajñe kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ prabhum।
dvaipāyanādaraṇyāṃ vai śuko jajñe guṇānvitaḥ ॥ 2.9.83 ॥
utpadyante ca pīvaryāṃ ṣaḍime śukasūnavaḥ।
bhūriśravāḥ prabhuḥ śambhuḥ kṛṣṇo gauraśca pañcamaḥ ॥ 2.9.84 ॥
kanyā kīrtimatī caiva yogamātā dṛḍhavratā।
jananī brahmadattasya patnī sattvaguhasya ca ॥ 2.9.85 ॥
śvetāḥ kṛṣṇāśca gaurāśca śyāmā dhūmrāḥ samūlikāḥ।
ūṣmapā dārakāścaiva nīlāścaiva parāśarāḥ।
parāśarāṇāmaṣṭau te pakṣāḥ proktā mahātmanām ॥ 2.9.86 ॥
ata ūrddhvaṃ nibodhadhvamindrapratimasambhavam।
vasiṣṭhasya kapiñjalyāṃ ghṛtācyāṃ samapadyata।
kuśītiyaḥ samākhyāta indrapratima ucyate ॥ 2.9.87 ॥
pṛthoḥ sutāyāḥ sambhūtaḥ putrastasyā bhavadvasuḥ।
upamanyuḥ sutastasya yasyeme upamanyavaḥ ॥ 2.9.88 ॥
mitrāvaruṇayoścaiva kuṇḍino ye pariśrutāḥ।
ekārṣeyāstathaivānye vasiṣṭā nāma viśrutāḥ।
ete pakṣā vasiṣṭānāṃ smṛtā ekādaśeva tu ॥ 2.9.89 ॥
ityete brahmaṇaḥ putrā mānasā hyaṣṭa viśrutāḥ।
bhrātaraḥ sumahābhāgā teṣāṃ vaṃśāḥ pratiṣṭitāḥ ॥ 2.9.90 ॥
trīṃllokāndhārayantīmāndevarṣigaṇasaṅkulān ।
teṣāṃ putrāśca pautrāśca śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ।
yairvyāptā pṛthivī sarvā sūryyasyeva gabhastibhiḥ ॥ 2.9.91 ॥
etacchrutvā vacastasya sutasya viditātmanaḥ।
            ।।śāṃśapāyana uvāca।।
kathaṃ dvitīyamutpannā bhavānī prāksatī tu yā।
āsīddākṣāyaṇī pūrvamumā kathama jāyata ॥ 2.10.2 ॥
menāyāṃ pitṛkanyāyāṃ janayāmāsa śailaruṭ।
kecaite pitaraścaiva yeṣāṃ menā tu mānasī ॥ 2.10.3 ॥
mainākaścaiva dauhitro dauhitrī ca tathā hyumā।
ekaparṇā tathā caiva tathā yā caikapāṭalā ॥ 2.10.4 ॥
gaṅgā caiva saricchreṣṭā sarvāsāṃ pūrvajā tathā।
śrotumicchāmi bhadrante śrāddhasya ca paraṃ vidhim ॥ 2.10.6 ॥
putrāśca te smṛtāḥ keṣāṃ kathañca pitarastu te ।
svarge tu pitaro'nye ye devānāmapi devatāḥ।
evaṃ vai śrotumicchāmi pitṝṇāṃ sargamuttamam।
yathāvaddattamasmābhiḥ śrāddhaṃ prīṇāti vai pitṝn ॥ 2.10.8 ॥
yadarthaṃ tena dṛśyante tatra kiṃ kāraṇaṃ smṛtam।
svarge hi ke tu varttante pitaro narake tu ke ॥ 2.10.9 ॥
abhisandhāya pitaraṃ pituśca pitaraṃ tathā।
pituḥ pitāmahañcaiva triṣu piṇḍeṣu nāmataḥ ॥ 2.10.10 ॥
kāni śrāddhāni deyāni kathaṃ gacchanti vai pitṝn ।
kathañca śaktāste dātuṃ narakasthāḥ phalaṃ punaḥ ॥ 2.10.11 ॥
ke ceha pitaro nāma kān yajāmo vayaṃ punaḥ ।
devā api putṝn svarge yajantīti hi naḥ śrutam ॥ 2.10.12 ॥
etadicchāmi vai śrotuṃ vistareṇa bahuśruta।
spaṣṭābhidhānamarthaṃ vai tadbhavānvaktumarhati ॥ 2.10.13 ॥
atra vo varṇayiṣyāmi yathāprajñaṃ yathāśrutam।
manvantareṣu jāyante pitaro devasūnavaḥ ॥ 2.10.15 ॥
atītānāgate jyeṣṭāḥ kaniṣṭāḥ kramaśastu te।
devaiḥ sārddhaṃ purātītāḥ pitaro ye'ntareṣu vai।
varttante sāmprataṃ ye tu tānvai vakṣyāmi niścayāt ॥ 2.10.16 ॥
devānasṛjan brahmā nāyakṣanniti vai punaḥ ।
tamutsṛjya tadātmānamasṛjaṃste phalārthinaḥ ॥ 2.10.17 ॥
te śaptā brahmaṇā mūḍhā naṣṭasaṃjñā bhaviṣyatha।
te bhūyaḥ praṇatāḥ sarve yācanti sma pitāmaham।
anugrahāya lokānāṃ punastānabravītprabhuḥ ॥ 2.10.19 ॥
prāyaścittaṃ caradhvaṃ vai vyabhicāro hi yaḥ kṛtaḥ ।
putrānsvānparipṛcchadhvaṃ tato jñānamavāpsyatha ॥ 2.10.20 ॥
tataste svānsutāṃścaiva prāyaścittajighṛkṣavaḥ।
apṛcchan saṃyatātmāno vidhivacca mitho mithaḥ ॥ 2.10.21 ॥
tebhyaste niyatātmānaḥ putrāḥ śaṃsuranekadhā।
prāyaścittāni dharmajñā vāṅmanaḥ karmmajāni tu ॥ 2.10.22 ॥
te putrānabruvanprītā labdhasaṃjñā divaukasaḥ।
yūyaṃ vai pitaro'smākaṃ ye vayaṃ pratibodhitāḥ।
dharmajñānañca kāmaśca ko varo vaḥ pradīyatām ॥ 2.10.23 ॥
punastānabravīdbrahmā yūyaṃ vai satyavādinaḥ।
tasmādyaduktaṃ yuṣmābhistattathā na tadanyathā ॥ 2.10.24 ॥
uktañca pitaro'smākamiti vai tanayāḥ svakāḥ।
pitaraste bhaviṣyanti tebhyo'yaṃ dīyatāṃ varaḥ ॥ 2.10.25 ॥
tenaiva vacasā putrā brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭinaḥ।
putrāḥ pitṛttvamājagmuḥ putratvaṃ pitaraḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.10.26 ॥
tasmātte pitaraḥ putrāḥ pitṛtve teṣu tatsmṛtam ।
evaṃ smṛtvā pitṝn putrānputrāśca pitarastathā।
vyājahāra punarbrahmā pidṝnātmavivṛddhaye ॥ 2.10.27 ॥
yo hyaniṣṭvā pitṝñchrāddhe kriyāṃ kāñicitkariṣyati।
rākṣasā dānavāścaiva phalaṃ prāpsyanti tasya tat ॥ 2.10.28 ॥
śrāddhairāpyāyitāścaiva pitaraḥ somamavyayam।
āpyāyyamānā yuṣmābhirvarddhayiṣyanti nityaśaḥ ॥ 2.10.29 ॥
śrāddhairāpyāyitaḥ somo lokānāpyāyayiṣyati ।
kṛtsraṃ saparvatavanaṃ jaṅgamājaṅgamairvṛtam ॥ 2.10.30 ॥
śrāddhāni puṣṭikāmāśca ye kariṣyanti mānavāḥ।
tebhyaḥ puṣṭiṃ prajāścaiva dāsyanti pitaraḥ sadā ॥ 2.10.31 ॥
śrāddhe yebhyaḥ pradāsyanti trīn piṇḍān nāmagotrataḥ।
sarvatra varttamānāste pitaraḥ prapitāmaham।
teṣāmāpyāyayiṣyanti śrāddhadānena vai prajāḥ ॥ 2.10.32 ॥
evamājñā kṛtā pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā parameṣṭinā।
tenaitatsarvathā siddhaṃ dānamadhyayanaṃ tapaḥ ॥ 2.10.33 ॥
te tu jñānapradātāraḥ pitaro vo na saṃśayaḥ।
ityete pitaro devā devāśca pitaraḥ punaḥ ।
anyonyaṃ pitaro hyete devāśca pitaraśca ha ॥ 2.10.34 ॥
etadbrahmavacaḥ śrutvā sūtasya vihitātmanaḥ ।
papracchurmunayo bhūyaḥ sūtaṃ tasmādyaduttaram ॥ 2.10.35 ॥
kiyanto vai pitṛgaṇāḥ kasminkāle ca te gaṇāḥ ।
varttante devapravarā devānāṃ somavarddhanāḥ ॥ 2.10.36 ॥
etadvo'haṃ pravakṣyāmi pitṛsargamanuttamam।
śaṃyuḥ papraccha yatpūrvaṃ pitaraṃ vai bṛhaspatim ॥ 2.10.37 ॥
bṛhaspatimupāsīnaṃ sarvajñānārthakovidam।
putraḥ śaṃyurimaṃ praśnaṃ papraccha vinayānvitaḥ ॥ 2.10.38 ॥
ka ete pitaro nāma kiyantaḥ ke ca nāmataḥ।
samudbhūtāḥ kathañcaite pitṛtvaṃ samupāgatāḥ ॥ 2.10.39 ॥
kasmācca pitaraṃ pūrvaṃ yajñe yujyanti nityaśaḥ।
kriyāśca sarvā varttante śrāddhapūrvā mahātmanām ॥ 2.10.40 ॥
kasmai śrāddhāni deyāni kiñca dattaṃ mahāphalam।
keṣu vāpyakṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ tīrtheṣu ca nadīṣu ca ॥ 2.10.41 ॥
keṣu vai sarvamāpnoti śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā dvijottamaḥ।
kaśca kālo bhaveccrāddhe vidhiḥ kaścānuvarttate ॥ 2.10.42 ॥
etadicchāmi bhagavan vistareṇa yathātatham।
vyākhyātumānupūrvyeṇa yatra codāhṛtaṃ mayā ॥ 2.10.43 ॥
bṛhaspatiridaṃ samyagevaṃ pṛṣṭo mahāmatiḥ।
vyājahārānupūrvyeṇa praśnaṃ praśnavidāṃ varaḥ ॥ 2.10.44 ॥
          ।।bṛhaspatiruvāca।।
kathayiṣyāmi te tāta yanmāṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi।
vinayena yathānyāyaṃ gambhīraṃ praśnamuttamam ॥ 2.10.45 ॥
dyaurantarikṣaṃ pṛthivī nakṣatrāṇi diśastathā।
sūryācandramasau caiva tathāhorātrameva ca ॥ 2.10.46 ॥
na babhūvustadā tāta tamobhūtamidaṃ jagat।
brahmaiko duścaraṃ tatra cacāra paramaṃ tapaḥ ॥ 2.10.47 ॥
śaṃyustamabravīdbhūyaḥ pitaraṃ brahmavittamam।
sarvadaiva vratasnātaṃ sarvajñānavidāṃvaram ॥ 2.10.48 ॥
kīdṛśaṃ sarvabhūte śastapastepe prajāpatiḥ।
sarveṣāṃ tapasāṃ yuktistapoyogamanuttamam।
dhyāyaṃstadā tadbhagavāṃstena lokanavāsṛjat ॥ 2.10.50 ॥
bhūtabhavyāni jñānāni lokānvedāṃśca kṛtsnaśaḥ।
yogamāviśya tatsṛṣṭaṃ brahmaṇā yogacakṣuṣā ॥ 2.10.51 ॥
lokāḥ sāntānikā nāma yatra tiṣṭhanti bhāsvarāḥ।
te vairājā iti khyātā devānāṃ divi devatāḥ ॥ 2.10.52 ॥
yogena tapasā yuktaḥ pūrvameva tadā prabhuḥ।
devānasṛjata brahmā yogaṃ yuktvā sanātanam ॥ 2.10.53 ॥
ādidevā iti khyātā mahāsattvā mahaujasaḥ।
sarvakāmapradāḥ pūjyā devadānavamānavaiḥ ॥ 2.10.54 ॥
teṣāṃ sapta samākhyātā gaṇāstrailokyapūjitāḥ ।
amūrttayastrayasteṣāṃ catvārastu sumūrttayaḥ ॥ 2.10.55 ॥
upariṣṭātrayasteṣāṃ varttante bhāvamūrttayaḥ।
teṣāmadhastādvarttante catvāraḥ sūkṣamamūrttayaḥ ॥ 2.10.56 ॥
tato devāstato bhūmireṣā lokaparamparā।
loke varttanti te hyasmiṃstebhyaḥ parjanyasambhavaḥ ।
āpyāyayanti te yasmātsomañcānnañca yogataḥ।
ūcustānvai pitṝṃstasmāllokānāṃ lokasattamāḥ ॥ 2.10.58 ॥
manojavāḥ svadhābhakṣāḥ sarvakāmaparicchadāḥ।
lobhamohabhayāpetā niścitāḥ śokavarjitāḥ ॥ 2.10.59 ॥
ete yogaṃ parityajya prāptā lokānsudarśanān।
divyāḥ puṇyā mahātmāno vipāpmāno bhavantyuta ॥ 2.10.60 ॥
tato yugasahasrānte jāyante brahmavādinaḥ।
pratilabhya punaryogaṃ mokṣaṃ gacchantyamūrttayaḥ ॥ 2.10.61 ॥
vyaktāvyaktaṃ parityajya mahāyogabalena vā ।
naśyantyulkeva gagane kṣīṇavidyutprabheva ca ॥ 2.10.62 ॥
utsṛjya dehajātāni mahāyogabalena ca।
nirākhyopākhyatāṃ yānti saritaḥ sāgare yathā ॥ 2.10.63 ॥
kriyayā gurupūjābhirye ca kurvanti nityaśaḥ।
śrāddhe prītāḥ punaḥ somaṃ pitaro yogamāsthitāḥ।
āpyāyayanti yogena trailokyaṃ yena jīvati ॥ 2.10.65 ॥
tasmācchrāddhāni deyāni yogibhyo yatnataḥ sadā।
pitṝṇāṃ hi balaṃ yogo yogātsomaḥ pravarttate ॥ 2.10.66 ॥
sahasraśastu viprānvai bhojayedyāvadāgatān ।।
ekastu yogavitprītaḥ sarvānarhati tacchṛṇu ॥ 2.10.67 ॥
kalpitānāṃ sahasreṇa snātakānāṃ śatena ca।
yogācāryeṇa yadbhuktaṃ trāyate mahato bhayāt ॥ 2.10.68 ॥
gṛhasthānāṃ sahasreṇa vānaprasthaśatena ca।
brahmacārisahasreṇa yogī hyeko viśiṣyate ॥ 2.10.69 ॥
nāstiko vā vikarmā vā saṅkīrṇastaskaro'pi vā।
nānyatra kāraṇaṃ dānaṃ yogeṣvāha prajāpatiḥ ॥ 2.10.70 ॥
pitarastasya tuṣyanti suvṛṣṭeneva karṣakāḥ।
putro vāpyatha vā pautro dhyāninaṃ bhojayiṣyati ॥ 2.10.71 ॥
alābhe dhyānibhikṣūṇāṃ bhojayedbrahmacāriṇau ।
tadalābhepyudāsīnaṃ gṛhasthamapi bhojayet ॥ 2.10.72 ॥
yastiṣṭedekapādena vāyubhakṣaḥ śataṃ samāḥ ।
dhyānayogī parastasmāditi brahmānuśāsanam ॥ 2.10.73 ॥
siddhā hi viprarūpeṇa caranti pṛthivīmimām।
tasmādatithimāyāntamabhigacchetkṛtāñjaliḥ ॥ 2.10.74 ॥
ūrvoḥ sāgaraparyantāṃ devā yogeśvarāḥ sadā।
nānārūpaiścarantyete prajā dharmeṇa pālayan ॥ 2.10.75 ॥
pradānāni pravakṣyāmi phalañcaiṣāṃ tathaiva ca ॥ 2.10.76 ॥
ādya eṣa gaṇaḥ proktaḥ pitṝṇāmamitaujasām।
bhāvayansaptakālānvai sthita eṣa gaṇastadā ॥ 2.10.78 ॥
ata ūraddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvān pitṛgaṇānpunaḥ ।
santatiṃ saṃsthitiñcaiva bhāvanāñca yathākramam ॥ 2.10.79 ॥
sapta medhāvatāṃ śreṣṭāḥ svarge pitṛgaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ।
catvāro mūrtimantaśca trayasteṣāmamūrttayaḥ।
teṣāṃ lokavisargantu kīrttayiṣye nibodhata ॥ 2.11.1 ॥
yā vai duhitarasteṣāṃ dohitrāścaiva ye smṛtāḥ।
lokā virajaso nāmnā yatra tiṣṭhanti bhāsvarāḥ ॥ 2.11.3 ॥
amūrttayaḥ pitṛgaṇāḥ putrāste vai prajāpateḥ।
virajasya dvijāḥ śreṣṭā vairājā iti viśrutāḥ ।
teṣāntu mānasī kanyā menā nāma mahāgireḥ।
patnī himavataḥ śubhra yasyāṃ maināka ucyate ॥ 2.11.5 ॥
tisraḥ kanyāstu menāyāṃ janayāmāsa śailarāṭ।
aparṇāmekaparṇāñca tṛtīyāmekapāṭalām ॥ 2.11.7 ॥
āśrite dve hyaparṇā tu aniketā tapo'carat।
nyagrodhamekaparṇī tu pāṭalāmekapāṭalā।
śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇi duścaraṃ devadānavaiḥ ṣa॥ 2.11.8 ॥
āhāramekaparṇena ekaparṇī samācarat।
pāṭalenaiva caikena vidadhyādekapāṭalā ॥ 2.11.9 ॥
pūrṇe pūrṇe sahasre dve āhāraṃ vai prajakratuḥ ।
ekā tatra nirāhārā tāṃ mātā pratyabhāṣata ॥ 2.11.10 ॥
niṣedhayantī hyumeti mātā srehena duḥkhitā।
sā tathoktatayā devī mātrā duścaracāriṇī ॥ 2.11.11 ॥
umeti sā mahābhāgā triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā ।
tatheti nāmnā tenāsau niruktā karmaṇā śubhā ॥ 2.11.12 ॥
etāsāṃ tapasā dṛptaṃ yāvadbhūmiddhariṣyati ॥ 2.11.13 ॥
tapaḥśarīrāstāḥ sarvāstisro yogabalānvitāḥ।
devyastāḥ sumahābhāgāḥ sarvvāśca sthirayauvanāḥ ॥ 2.11.14 ॥
sarvāśca brahmavādinyaḥ sarvā ścaivorddhvaretasaḥ।
umā tāsāṃ variṣṭā ca śreṣṭā ca varavarṇinī ॥ 2.11.15 ॥
mahāyogabalopetā mahādevamupasthitā।
dantakāṇvośanā tasyāḥ putro vai bhṛgu nandanaḥ ॥ 2.11.16 ॥
asitasyaikaparṇī tu patnī sādhvī dṛḍhavratā।
dattā himavatā tasmai yogācāryāya dhīmate।
devalaṃ suṣuve sā tu brahmiṣṭhaṃ mānasaṃ sutam ॥ 2.11.17 ॥
yā caitāsāṃ kumārīṇāṃ tṛtīyā tvekapāṭalā।
putraṃ śataśilākasya jaigīṣavyamupasthitā ॥ 2.11.18 ॥
tasyāpi śaṅkhalikhitau smṛtau putrāvayonijau।
ityetā vai mahābhāgāḥ kanyā himavataḥ śubhāḥ ॥ 2.11.19 ॥
rudrāṇī sā tu pravarā svaguṇairatiricyate।
anyonyaprītiranayorumāśaṅkarayoryathā ॥ 2.11.20 ॥
śleṣaṃ saṃsaktayorjñātvā śaṅkitaḥ kila vṛtrahā।
tābhyāṃ maithunasaktābhyāmapatyodbhavabhīruṇā।
tayoḥ sakāśamindreṇa preṣito havyavāhanaḥ ॥ 2.11.21 ॥
anayo rativighnañca tvamācara hutāśana।
sarvatra gata eva tvaṃ na doṣo vidyate tadā ॥ 2.11.22 ॥
ityevamukte tu tathā vahninā ca tathā kṛtam।
umādehaṃ samutsṛjya śukraṃ bhūmau visarjitam ॥ 2.11.23 ॥
idaṃ coktavatī vahniṃ roṣagadghadayā girā ॥ 2.11.24 ॥
yasmānmayyavitṛptāyāṃ rativighnaṃ hutāśana।
kṛtavānasyakarttavyaṃ tasmāttvamasi durmate ॥ 2.11.25 ॥
yadevaṃ vibhṛtaṃ garbhaṃ raudraṃ śukraṃ mahāprabham।
garbhaṃ tvaṃ dhārayasvaivameṣā te daṇḍadhāraṇā ॥ 2.11.26 ॥
sa śāparoṣādrudrāṇyā antargarbho hutāśanaḥ।
bahūnvarṣagaṇān garbhaṃ dhārayāmāsa vai dvijāḥ ॥ 2.11.27 ॥
sa gaṅgāmupagamyāha śrūyatāṃ sariduttame।
sumahān parikhedo me garbhadhāraṇakāraṇāt ॥ 2.11.28 ॥
maddhitārthamimaṃ garbhamato dhāraya nimnage।
matprasādācca khedo vai mandastava bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.11.29 ॥
tathetyuktvā tadā sā tu samprahṛṣṭa mahānadī।
taṃ garbhaṃ dhārayāmāsa dahyamānena cetasā ॥ 2.11.30 ॥
sāpi kṛcchreṇa mahatā khidyamānā mahānadī।
tatra taṃ vyasṛjadgarbhaṃ dīpyamānāmivānalam ॥ 2.11.32 ॥
rudrāgnigaṅgātanayastatra jāto'ruṇaprabhaḥ ।
ādityaśatasaṅkāśo mahātejāḥ pratāpavān ॥ 2.11.33 ॥
tasmiñjāte mahābhāge kumāre jāhnavīsute।
vimānayānairākāśaṃ patatribhirivāvṛtam ॥ 2.11.34 ॥
devadundubhayo nedurākāśe madhurasvarāḥ।
mumucuḥ puṣpavarṣañca khacarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ ॥ 2.11.35 ॥
jagurgandharvvamukhyāśca sarvvaśastatra tatra ha।
yakṣā vidyādharāḥ siddhāḥ kinnarāścaiva sarvaśaḥ ॥ 2.11.36 ॥
mahānāga sahasrāṇi pravarāśca patatriṇaḥ ।
upatasthurmahābhāgamāgneyaṃ śaṅkarātmajam।
prabhāveṇa tadā tena daityadānavarākṣasāḥ ॥ 2.11.37 ॥
saha saptarṣibhāryābhirādāve vāgnisambhavaḥ।
abhiṣekaprayātābhirdṛṣṭo varjya tvarundhatīm ॥ 2.11.38 ॥
tābhiḥ sa bālārkanibho raudraḥ parivṛtaḥ prabhuḥ ।
snihyamānābhiratyarthaṃ svakābhiriva mātṛbhiḥ ॥ 2.11.39 ॥
yugapatsarvadevīrhi didṛkṣurjāhnavīsutaḥ।
tena jātena mahatā devānāmasahiṣṇavaḥ।
skanditā dānavagaṇāstasmātskandaḥ pratāpavān ॥ 2.11.42 ॥
kṛttikābhistu yasmāt saṃvarddhitaḥ sa purātanaḥ।
kārttikeya iti khyātastasmādasurasūdanaḥ ॥ 2.11.43 ॥
jṛmbhatastasya daityārerjvālāmālākulāttadā।
mukhādvinirgatā tasya svaśaktiraparājitā ॥ 2.11.44 ॥
krīḍārthañcaiva skandasya viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā।
garuḍāditi sṛṣṭau hi pakṣiṇau hi prabhadrakau ॥ 2.11.45 ॥
mayūraḥ kukkuṭaścaiva patākā caiva vāyunā।
yasya dattā sarasvatyā mahāvīṇā mahāsvanā।
ajaḥ svayambhuvā datto meṣo dattaśca śambhunā ॥ 2.11.46 ॥
māyā viharaṇe viprā girau krauñce nipātite।
tārake cāsuravare samudīrṇe nipātite ॥ 2.11.47 ॥
sendropendrairmahābhāgairdevaraignisutaḥ prabhuḥ ।
senāpatyena daityārirabhiṣiktaḥ pratāpavān ॥ 2.11.48 ॥
devasenāpatistvevaṃ paṭyate naranāyakaḥ।
devāriskandanaḥ skandaḥ sarvalokeśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ॥ 2.11.49 ॥
pramathairvividhairdavaistathā bhūta gaṇairapi ।
mātṛbhirvividhābhiśca vināyakagaṇaistathā ॥ 2.11.50 ॥
sā tvapaśyadvimānāni patantī sā divaścyutā ।
susūkṣmānaparityaktānagnīnagniṣvivāhitān।
trāyadhvamityuvācātha patantī tānavākśirāḥ ॥ 2.11.52 ॥
tairuktā sā tu mābhaiṣīrityuktādhiṣṭitābhavat।
tataḥ prāsādayatsā vai pitṝṃstān dīnayā girā ॥ 2.11.53 ॥
ūcuste pitaraḥ kanyāṃ bhraṣṭaiśvaryāṃ vyatikramāt।
bhraṣṭaiśvaryā svadoṣeṇa tapasi tvaṃ śucismite ॥ 2.11.54 ॥
taireva tatkarmaphalaṃ prāpnuvantīha devatāḥ ॥ 2.11.55 ॥
sadyaḥ phalanti karmāṇi devatve pretya mānuṣe।
ityuktyā vai pitaraḥ punaste tu prasāditāḥ।
dhyātvā prasādaṃ sañcakrustasyāste tvanukampayā ॥ 2.11.57 ॥
avaśyambhāvinaṃ dṛṣṭvā hyarthamūcustataḥ surāḥ ।
somapāḥ pitaraḥ kanyāṃ rājñaścaiva hyamāvasoḥ ॥ 2.11.58 ॥
utpannasya pṛthivyāṃ tu mānuṣatve mahātmanaḥ।
kanyā bhūtvā tvimāँllokānpunaḥ prāpsyasi svāniti ॥ 2.11.59 ॥
aṣṭāviṃśe bhavitrī tvaṃ dvāpare matsyayonijā।
asyaiva rājño duhitā adrikāyāṃ hyamāvasoḥ ॥ 2.11.60 ॥
parāśarasya dāyādaṃ ṛṣestvaṃ janayiṣyasi।
sa vedamekaṃ viprarṣiścaturdhā vai kariṣyati ॥ 2.11.61 ॥
mahābhiṣasya putrau dvau śantanoḥ kīrttivarddhanau।
vicitravīryyaṃ dharmajñaṃ tvamevotpādayiṣyasi ॥ 2.11.62 ॥
etānutpādya putraṃ svaṃ punarlokānavāpsyasi ॥ 2.11.63 ॥
vyatikramātpitṝṇāṃ tvaṃ prāpsyase janma kutsitam।
tasyaiva rājñastvaṃ kanyā adrikāyāṃ bhaviṣyasi ॥ 2.11.64 ॥
kanyā bhūtvā tataśca tvamimān lokānavāpsyasi।
evamuktā tu dāśeyī jātā satyavatī tu sā ॥ 2.11.65 ॥
adrikāyāṃ sutā matsyāṃ sutā jātā hyamāvasoḥ।
adri kāmatsyasambhūtā gaṅgāyāmanusaṅgame ॥ 2.11.66 ॥
tasya rājño hi sā kanyā rājño vīryye sadaiva hi।
virajā nāma te lokā divi rocanti te gaṇāḥ ॥ 2.11.67 ॥
agniṣvāttāḥ smṛtāstatra pitaro bhāsvaraprabhāḥ ।
eteṣāṃ mānasī kanyā pīvarī nāma viśrutā।
yoginī yogapatnī ca yogamātā tathaiva ca ॥ 2.11.70 ॥
bhavitā dvāparaṃ prāpya aṣṭāviṃśantu daivatam।
parāśarakulodbhūtaḥ śuko nāma mahātapāḥ ॥ 2.11.71 ॥
śrīmānyogī mahāyogī yogastasmāddvijottamaḥ।
vyāsādaraṇyāṃ sambhūto vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ ॥ 2.11.72 ॥
kṛṣṇaṃ gauraṃ prabhuṃ śambhuṃ tathā bhūriśrutaṃ vavau ॥ 2.11.73 ॥
kanyāṃ kīrttimatīñcaiva yoginīṃ yogamātaram ।
brahmadattasya jananī mahiṣī tvaṇuhasya tu ॥ 2.11.74 ॥
ādityakiraṇopetaṃ tvapunarbhāvamāsthitaḥ।
sarvavyāpi vinirmukto bhaviṣyati mahāmuniḥ ॥ 2.11.76 ॥
utpannāste svadhāyāstu kanyā hyagneḥ kaveḥ sutāḥ ॥ 2.11.78 ॥
pitaro devalokeṣu jyotirbhāsiṣu bhāsvarāḥ।
sarvakāmasamṛddheṣu dvijā stānbhāvayantyuta ॥ 2.11.79 ॥
eteṣāṃ mānasī kanyā gaurnāma divi viśrutā।
dattasenā kumāreṇa śukrasya mahiṣī priyā ॥ 2.11.80 ॥
marīcigarbhāste lokāḥ samāvṛtya divi sthitāḥ ॥ 2.11.81 ॥
ete hyaṅgirasaḥ putrāḥ sādhyaiḥ saha vivarddhitāḥ।
upahūtāḥ smṛtāste tu pitaro bhāsvarā divi।
tānkṣatriyagaṇāndṛṣṭvā bhāvayanti phalārthinaḥ ॥ 2.11.82 ॥
eteṣāṃ mānasī kanyā yaśodā nāma viśrutā।
rājarṣerjananī devī khaṭvāṅgasya mahātmanaḥ।
yasya yajñe purā gītā gāthā gītairmaharṣibhiḥ ॥ 2.11.84 ॥
agnerjanma tathā dṛṣṭvā śāṇḍilyasya mahātmanaḥ।
yajamānaṃ dilīpaṃ ye paśyanti susamāhitāḥ।
satyavrataṃ mahātmānaṃ te svargajayino'marāḥ ॥ 2.11.85 ॥
ājyapā nāma pitaraḥ kardamasya prajāpateḥ ।
samutpannasya pulahādutpannāstasya vai punaḥ ॥ 2.11.86 ॥
lokeṣveteṣu varttante kāmageṣu vihaṅgamāḥ ।
etānvaiśyagaṇāḥ śrāddhe bhāvayanti phalārthinaḥ ॥ 2.11.87 ॥
eteṣāṃ mānasī sanyā virajā nāma viśrutā ।
yayāterjananī sādhvī patnī sā nahuṣasya tu ॥ 2.11.88 ॥
sukālā nāma pitaro vasiṣṭhasya prajāpateḥ ।
hiraṇyagarbhasya sutāḥ śūdrāstānbāvayantyuta ॥ 2.11.89 ॥
mānasā nāma te lokā vahante yatra te divi।
eteṣāṃ mānasī kanyā narmadā saritāṃ varā ॥ 2.11.90 ॥
sā bhāvayati bhūtāni dakṣiṇāpathagāminī ।
jananī trasaddasyorhi purukutsaparigrahaḥ ॥ 2.11.91 ॥
eteṣāmabhyupagamānmāturmanvantareśvaraḥ ।
manvanta rādau śrāddhāni pravarttayati sarvaśaḥ ॥ 2.11.92 ॥
pidṝṇāmānupūrvyeṇa sarveṣāṃ dvijasattamāḥ ।
tasmādiha svadharmeṇa śrāddhaṃ deyantu śraddhayā ॥ 2.11.93 ॥
sarveṣāṃ rājataiḥ pātrairapi vā rajatānvitaiḥ।
dattaṃ svadhāṃ purodhāya tathā prīṇāti vai pitṝn ॥ 2.11.94 ॥
somasyāpyāyanaṃ kṛtvā hyagnervaivasvatasya ca।
pitṝn prīṇāti vai bhaktyā pitaraḥ prīṇayanti tam।
pitaraḥ puṣṭikāmasya prajākāmasya vā punaḥ।
puṣṭiṃ prajāṃ ca svargaṃ prayacchanti na saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.11.96 ॥
devakāryyādapi sadā pitṛkāryyaṃ viśiṣyate।
devatābhyaḥ pitṝṇāṃ hi pūrvvamāpyāyanaṃ smṛtam ॥ 2.11.97 ॥
na hi yogagatiḥ sūkṣmā pitṝṇāmapi tṛptayaḥ।
tapasā hi prasiddhena dṛśyante māṃsacakṣuṣā ॥ 2.11.98 ॥
ityete pitaraścaiva lokā duhitaraśca vai।
dauhitrā yajamānāśca proktā ye bhāvayanti tān ॥ 2.11.99 ॥
catvāro mūrttimantaśca trayasteṣāmamūrttayaḥ।
tebhyaḥ śrāddhāni satkṛtya devāḥ kurvvanti yatnataḥ ॥ 2.11.100 ॥
bhaktāḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve sendrāstadghatamānasāḥ।
viśve ca sikatāścaiva pṛśnijāḥ śrṛṅgiṇastathā ॥ 2.11.101 ॥
kṛṣṇāḥ śvetāstvajāścaiva vidhivatpūjayantyuta।
prajāstā vātaraśanā divākīrttyāstathaiva ca ॥ 2.11.102 ॥
lekhāśca marutaścaiva brahmādyāśca divaukasaḥ।
atribhṛgvaṅgirādyāśca ṛṣayaḥ sarvva eva ca ॥ 2.11.103 ॥
yakṣā nāgāḥ suparṇāśca kinnarā rākṣasaiḥ saha।
pitṝṃstvapūjayansarve nityameva phalārthinaḥ ॥ 2.11.104 ॥
evamete mahātmānaḥ śrāddhe satkṛtya pūjitāḥ।
sarvānkāmānprayacchanti śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ ॥ 2.11.105 ॥
hitvā trailokyasaṃsāraṃ jarāmṛtyubhayaṃ tathā।
mokṣopāyamathaiśvaryyaṃ sūkṣmadehāśca devatāḥ।
kṛtsnaṃ vairāgyamānantyaṃ prayacchanti pitāmahāḥ ॥ 2.11.107 ॥
aiśvaryyaṃ vihitaṃ yogamaiśvaryyaṃ vittamuttamam।
yogaiśvaryyadṛte mokṣaḥ kathañcinnopapadyate ॥ 2.11.108 ॥
apakṣasyaiva gamanaṃ gagane pakṣiṇo yathā ।
variṣṭhaḥ sarvadharmmāṇāṃ mokṣo dharmmaḥ sanātanaḥ ॥ 2.11.109 ॥
vimānānāṃ sahasrāṇi yuktānyapsarasāṃgaṇaiḥ।
sarvakāmaprasiddhāni prayacchanti pitāmahāḥ ॥ 2.11.110 ॥
prajñā puṣṭiḥ smṛtirmedhā rājyamārogyameva ca।
pitṝṇāṃ hi prasādena prāpyate sumahātmanā ॥ 2.11.111 ॥
muktāvaiḍhūryyavāsāṃsi vājināgāyutāni ca।
koṭiśaścāpi ratnāni prayacchanti pitāmahāḥ ॥ 2.11.112 ॥
haṃsabarhiṇayuktāni muktāvaiḍhūryyavanti ca।
kiṅkiṇījālanaddhāni sadā puṣpaphalāni ca।
prītyā nityaṃ prayacchanti manuṣyāṇāṃ pitāmahāḥ ॥ 2.11.113 ॥
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ pitṝṇāṃ pātramucyate।
rajataṃ rajatāktaṃ vā pitṝṇāṃ pātramucyate ॥ 2.12.1 ॥
rajatasya tathā cāpi darśanaṃ dānameva ca।
anantamakṣayaṃ svargyaṃ pitṝṇāṃ dānamucyate।
pitṝnetena dānena satputrāstārayantyuta ॥ 2.12.2 ॥
rājate hi svadhā dugdhā pātre'sminpitṛbhiḥ purā।
svadhādāyārthibhistāta tasmindatte tadakṣayam ॥ 2.12.3 ॥
kṛṣṇājinasya sānnidhyaṃ darśanaṃ dānameva vā।
rakṣoghnaṃ brahmavarccasyaṃ pitṝṃstattadvitārayet ॥ 2.12.4 ॥
kāñcanaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ dauhitraṃ kutapastilāḥ।
vastrañca pāvanīyāni tridaṇḍo yogameva ca ॥ 2.12.5 ॥
śrāddhakarmaṇyayaṃ śreṣṭo vidhirbrāhyaḥ sanātanaḥ।
āyuḥ kīrttiḥ prajāścaiva prajñāsantativarddhanaḥ ॥ 2.12.6 ॥
diśi dakṣiṇapūrvasyāṃ vidikūsthānaṃ viśeṣataḥ।
sarvatoratnimātrantu caturasraṃ susaṃhitam ॥ 2.12.7 ॥
vakṣyāmi vidhivatsthānaṃ pitṝṇāmanuśāsanāt।
dhanyamārogyamāyuṣyaṃ balavarṇavivarddhanam ॥ 2.12.8 ॥
tatra garttāstrayaḥ kāryyāstrayo daṇḍāśca khādirāḥ।
ratnimātrāstu te kāryyā rajatena vibhūṣitāḥ।
tevitastyāyatāḥ kāryyāḥ sarvvataścaturaṅgulāḥ ॥ 2.12.9 ॥
adbhiḥ pavitrapūtābhiḥ plāvayetsatataṃ śuciḥ ॥ 2.12.10 ॥
payasā hyājagavyena śodhanaṃ vāgbhireva tu।
evaṃ triṣavaṇasnāto yo'rcayeta pitṝnsadā ।
mantreṇa vidhivatsamyagaśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ॥ 2.12.12 ॥
tatsthāpayedamāvāsyāṃ gartte bhūcaturaṅgule ।
triḥsaptasaṃjñāste yajñāstrailokyaṃ dhāryyate tu vai ॥ 2.12.13 ॥
tasya puṣṭirathaiśvaryyamāyuḥ santatireva ca।
vicitrā bhajate lakṣmīrmokṣaṃ ca labhate kramāt ॥ 2.12.14 ॥
pāpmāpahaṃ pāvanīyamaśvamedhaphalaṃ tathā।
aśvamedhaphalaṃ hyetaddvijaiḥ satkṛtya pūjitam।
mantraṃ vakṣyāmyahaṃ tasmādamṛtaṃ brahmanirmitam ॥ 2.12.15 ॥
devatābhyaḥ pitṛbhyaśca mahāyogibhya eva ca।
namaḥ svadhāyai svāhāyai nityameva bhavantyuta ॥ 2.12.16 ॥
ādyāvasāne śrāddhasya trirāvarttaṃ japetsadā।
piṇḍanirvapaṇe caiva japedetatsamāhitaḥ।
pitaraḥ kṣipramāyānti rākṣasāḥ pradravanti ca ॥ 2.12.17 ॥
pitṝṃstatrtriṣu lokeṣu mantro'yaṃ tārayatyuta।
paṭyamānaḥ sadā śrāddhe niyataṃ brah‌mavādibhiḥ ॥ 2.12.18 ॥
rājyakāmo japedenaṃ sadā mantramatandritaḥ।
vīryyaśaucārthasattvañca śrīrāyurbalavarddhanam ॥ 2.12.19 ॥
prīyante pitaro yena japyena niyamena ca।
saptārcciṣaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvakāmapradaṃ śubham ॥ 2.12.20 ॥
amūrtānāṃ samūrtānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ dīpta tejasām।
namasyāmi sadā tebhyo dhyānibhyo yogacakṣuṣā ॥ 2.12.21 ॥
indrādīnāṃ janayitāro bhṛgumārīcayostathā।
saptarṣīṇāṃ pitṝṇāñca tānnamasyāmi kāmadān ॥ 2.12.22 ॥
manvādīnāṃ sureśānāṃ sūryyācandramasostathā।
dyāvāpṛthivyośca tathā namasyāmi kṛtāñjaliḥ ॥ 2.12.24 ॥
devarṣīṇāñjanayitṝṃśca sarvalokanamaskṛtān।
yogayogeśvarebhyaśca namasyāmi kṛtāñjaliḥ ॥ 2.12.26 ॥
pitṛgaṇebhyaḥ saptabhyo namo lokeṣu saptasu।
svayambhuve namaścaiva brahmaṇe yogacakṣuṣe ॥ 2.12.27 ॥
etaduktaṃ sasaptarṣibrahmarṣigaṇapūjitam ।
pavitraṃ paramaṃ hyetacchrīmadrakṣovināśanam ॥ 2.12.28 ॥
anena vidhinā yuktastrīnvarān labhate naraḥ।
annamāyuḥ sutāṃścaiva dadate pitaro bhuvi ॥ 2.12.29 ॥
bhaktyā paramayā yuktaḥ śraddadhāno jitendriyaḥ।
saptārcciṣaṃ japedyastu nityameva samāhitaḥ।
saptadvīpasamudrāyāṃ pṛthivyāmekarāḍbhavet ॥ 2.12.30 ॥
yatkiṃcitpacyate gehe bhakṣyaṃ vā bhojyameva ca।
anivedya na bhoktavyaṃ tasminnāyatane sadā ॥ 2.12.31 ॥
kramaśaḥ kīrttayiṣyāmi balipātrāṇyataḥ param।
yeṣu yacca phalaṃ proktaṃ tanme nigadataḥ śrṛṇu ॥ 2.12.32 ॥
sarvabhūtādhipatyaṃ ca plakṣe nityamudāhṛtam ॥ 2.13.1 ॥
rakṣoghnaṃ ca yaśasyaṃ ca kāśmaryyaṃ pātramucyate ॥ 2.13.2 ॥
saubhāgyamuttamaṃ loke madhuke samudāhṛtam।
phalgupātre ca kurvāṇaḥ sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt ॥ 2.13.3 ॥
parā dyutiratho karttuḥ prākāśyaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
bilve lakṣmīstathā medhā nityamāyuṣyameva ca ॥ 2.13.4 ॥
kṣetrārāmataḍāgeṣu sarvasasyeṣu caiva hi।
varṣedajasraṃ parjanyo veṇupātreṣu kurvvataḥ ॥ 2.13.5 ॥
sakṛdapyatra yajñānāṃ sarveṣāṃ phalamucyate ॥ 2.13.6 ॥
sadā dadyācchriyā yuktaḥ sa vibhāti divākaraḥ ॥ 2.13.7 ॥
guggulādīṃstathā dhūpān pitṛbhyo yaḥ prayacchati।
saṃyuktānmadhusarpirbhyāṃ so'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ॥ 2.13.8 ॥
dhūpaṃ gandhaguṇopetaṃ kāntaṃ pitṛparāyaṇam।
labhate strīṣvapatyāni iha cāmutra cobhayoḥ।
dadyādeva pitṛbhyastu nityameva hyatandritaḥ ॥ 2.13.9 ॥
dīpaṃ pitṛbhyaḥ prayataḥ sadā yastu prayacchati।
tejasā yaśamā caiva kāntyā caiva balena ca।
bhuvi prakāśo bhavati bhrājate ca triviṣṭape।
apsarobhiḥ parivṛto vimānāgre sa modate ॥ 2.13.11 ॥
phalamūlanamaskāraiḥ pidṝṇāṃ prayataḥ śuciḥ।
pūrva kṛtvā dvijānpaśvātpūjayedannasampadā ॥ 2.13.12 ॥
śrāddhakāle tu satataṃ vāyubhūtāḥ pitāmahāḥ।
āviśanti dvijāndṛṣṭvā tasmādetadbravīmi te ॥ 2.13.13 ॥
vastrairannaiḥ pradānaistairbhakṣyapeyaistathaiva ca।
gobhiraśvaistathā grāmaiḥ pūjayitvā dvijottamān ॥ 2.13.14 ॥
bhavanti pitaraḥ prītāḥ pūjiteṣu dvijātiṣu।
tasmādannena vidhivat pūjayeddvijasattamān ॥ 2.13.15 ॥
savyottarābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ kuryyādullekhanaṃ dvijaḥ।
prokṣaṇañca tathā kuryācchrāddhakarmmaṇyatandritaḥ ॥ 2.13.16 ॥
darbhānpiṇḍāṃstathā bhakṣyānpuṣpāṇi vividhāni ca।
gandhadānamalaṅkāramekaikaṃ nirvapedvudhaḥ ॥ 2.13.17 ॥
poṣayitvā janaṃ samyagvaiśvaḥ syāduttaro dvijaḥ।
abhyaṅga darbhapiñjālaistribhiḥ kuryādyathāvidhi ॥ 2.13.18 ॥
apasavyaṃ pitṛbhyaśca dadyādannamanuttamam।
tamuccāryyātha sarveṣāṃ vastrārthaṃ sūtrameva ca ॥ 2.13.19 ॥
khaṇḍanaṃ poṣaṇaṃ caiva tathaivollekhanaṃ tathā।
sakṛdeva hi devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ tribhirucyate ॥ 2.13.20 ॥
ekaṃ pavitraṃ hastena pitṝnsarvānsakṛtsakṛt।
cailamantreṇa piṇḍebhyo dattvā darśanajaṃ hitam ॥ 2.13.21 ॥
sadā sarpistilairyuktāṃ strīn piṇḍānnirvapedbhuvi।
jānuṃ kṛtvā tathā savyaṃ bhūmau pitṛparāyaṇaḥ ॥ 2.13.22 ॥
pitṝn pitāmahāṃścaiva tathaiva prapitāmahān।
āhūya ca pitṝn prāñcān pitṛtīrthena yatnataḥ।
piṇḍānparikṣipetsamyagapasavyamatandritaḥ ॥ 2.13.23 ॥
annenādbhiśca puṣpaiśca bhakṣyaiścaiva pṛthagvidhaiḥ।
pṛthag mātāmahānāntu kecidicchanti mānavāḥ ॥ 2.13.24 ॥
trīn piṇḍānānupūrvvyeṇa sāṅguṣṭānpuṣṭivarddhanān ।
jānvantarābhyāṃ yatnena piṇḍān dadyādyathākramam ॥ 2.13.25 ॥
namo vaḥ pitaraḥ sūkṣmaiḥ sadā hyevamatandritaḥ ॥ 2.13.26 ॥
dakṣiṇasyāntu pāṇibhyāṃ prathamaṃ piṇḍamutsṛjet।
namo vaḥ pitaraḥ saumyāḥ paṭhannityamatandritaḥ ॥ 2.13.27 ॥
savyottarābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ dharme sarvvamatandritaḥ।
ulūkhalasya lekhāyā mudapātrācca sevanam ॥ 2.13.28 ॥
kṣaumasūtraṃ navaṃ dadyācchoṇaṃ kārpāsikaṃ tathā।
patrorṇaṃ pitṛsūtrañca kauśeyaṃ parivarjayet ॥ 2.13.29 ॥
varjayettaddaśāṃ yajñe yadapyahatavastrajām।
na prīṇanti tathaitāni dāturāpyāyato bhavet ॥ 2.13.30 ॥
śreṣṭhamāhustrikakudamañjanaṃ nityameva ca।
candanāguruṇī cobhe tamālośīrapajhakam।
śuklāḥ sumanasaḥ śreṣṭāstathā pajhotpalāni ca।
puṣpāṇi varjanīyāni śrāddhakarmaṇi nityaśaḥ ॥ 2.13.34 ॥
yāni gandhādapetāni upagandhīni yāni ca।
varjanīyāni puṣpāṇi bhūtimanvicchatā tadā ॥ 2.13.35 ॥
dvijātayastathānviṣṭā niyatāḥ syurudaṅmukhāḥ।
pūjayedyajamānastu vidhivaddakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ॥ 2.13.36 ॥
teṣāmabhimukho dadyāddarbhānpiṇḍāṃśca yatnataḥ।
anena vidhinā sākṣādarccayet svān pitāmahān ॥ 2.13.37 ॥
haritā vai sapiñjalyāḥ puṣpasnigdhāḥ samāhitāḥ।
ratnimātrapradānena pitṛtīrthena saṃsthitāḥ ॥ 2.13.38 ॥
tathā śmāmākanīvārā durvārāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ ॥ 2.13.39 ॥
tasya vālā nipatitā bhūmau cākāśamārgataḥ ॥ 2.13.40 ॥
tasmānmedhyā samākāśāḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi pūjitāḥ ।
piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ teṣu karttavyaṃ bhūtimicchatā ॥ 2.13.41 ॥
bhavanti rucirā nityaṃ vipāpmāno'ghavarjitāḥ ॥ 2.13.42 ॥
sakṛdevāstareddarbhān piṇḍārthaṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ।
prāgdakṣiṇāgraniyato vidhiñcāpyanuvakṣyati ॥ 2.13.43 ॥
na dīno vāpi vā kruddho na caivānyamanā naraḥ।
ekāgramādhāya manaḥ śrāddhaṃ kuryyātsadā budhaḥ ॥ 2.13.44 ॥
nihanmi sarvvaṃ yadamedhyavadbhaved hatāśca sarvve suradānavā mayā।
rakṣāṃsi yakṣāśca piśācasaṅghā hatā mayā yātudhānāśca sarvve ॥ 2.13.45 ॥
evaṃ pitre dṛṣṭamannaṃ hi yasya tasyāsurā varjayantīha sarvve।
yasmindeśe paṭyate eṣa mantrastaṃ vai deśaṃ rākṣasā varjayanti ॥ 2.13.46 ॥
anena vidhinā nityaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryyāddvijaḥ sadā।
manasā kāṅkṣitaṃ yadyattattaddadyuḥ pitāmahāḥ ॥ 2.13.47 ॥
pitaro hṛṣṭamanaso rakṣāṃsi vimanāṃsi ca।
bhavantyeva kṛte śrāddhe nityameva prayatnataḥ ॥ 2.13.48 ॥
śūdrāḥ śrāddhe kṣīravāśu balvajāstaravastathā।
evamādīnyathānyāni tṛṇāni parivarjayet ॥ 2.13.49 ॥
kāśaiḥ punarbhavaiḥ kāryyaṃ sarvvameva phalaṃ bhavet ॥ 2.13.50 ॥
kāśāḥ punarbhavā ye ca barhaṇā upabarhaṇāḥ।
atha te pitaro devā devāśca pitaraḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.13.51 ॥
puṣpagandhādidhūpānāmeṣa mantra udāhṛtaḥ।
āhṛtya dakṣiṇāyāntu homārthe viprayatnataḥ ॥ 2.13.52 ॥
somāya vai pitṛmate svadhā aṅgirase namaḥ।
asvargyaṃ laukikaṃ vāpi juhuyātkarmmasiddhaye ॥ 2.13.53 ॥
antarādhāya samidhaṃ tathā homo vidhīyate।।
samāhitena manasā prayatāgniḥ prayatnataḥ ॥ 2.13.54 ॥
agnaye kavyavāhāya svadhā aṅgirase namaḥ।
yamāya caivāṅgirase svadhā nama iti bruvan ॥ 2.13.55 ॥
ityete vai homamantrā mantrāṇāmanu pūrvvaśaḥ।
dakṣiṇāto'gnaye nityaṃ somāyāntaratastathā ॥ 2.13.56 ॥
etayorantaraṃ nityaṃ juhuyādvai vivasvate।
upacāraṃ svadhākāraṃ tathaivollekhanañca yat ॥ 2.13.57 ॥
homajapye namaskāraḥ prokṣaṇañca viśeṣataḥ।
añjanābhyañjane caiva piṇḍasaṃvapanaṃ tathā ॥ 2.13.58 ॥
kriyāḥ sarvvā yatho ddiṣṭāḥ prayatnena samācaret ॥ 2.13.59 ॥
bahuhavyatvamevāgnau susamiddhe viśeṣataḥ।
vidhūme lelihāne ca hotavyaṃ karmasiddhaye ॥ 2.13.60 ॥
aprabuddhe sadhūme ca juhuyādyo hutāśane।
yajamāno bhavedandhaḥ so'putra iti naḥ śrutam ॥ 2.13.61 ॥
alpendhano vā rūkṣo vā visphuliṅgaśca sarvvaśaḥ ।
jvālā dhūmopasevyaśca sa tu vahnirna siddhaye ॥ 2.13.62 ॥
durgandhaścaiva nīlaśca kṛṣṇaścaiva viśeṣataḥ।
bhūmiṃ vigāhate yatra tatra vidyātparābhavam ॥ 2.13.63 ॥
arciṣmān piṇḍitaśikhaḥ sarpiḥkāñcanasambhavaḥ।
snigdhaḥ pradakṣiṇaścaiva vahniḥ syātkāryyasiddhaye ॥ 2.13.64 ॥
naranārīgaṇebhyaśca pūjāṃ prāpnoti śāśvatīm।
akṣayāḥ pūjitāstena bhavanti pitaro'vyayāḥ ॥ 2.13.65 ॥
sthālyudumbarapātrāṇi phalāni samidhastathā।
śrāddhe cātipavitrāṇi medhyānīti viśeṣataḥ ॥ 2.13.66 ॥
pavitraṃ vā dvijaśreṣṭha śuddhaye janmakarmmasu।
pātreṣu phalamuddiṣṭaṃ yanmayā śrāddhakarmaṇi ॥ 2.13.67 ॥
tadeva kṛtsnaṃ vijñeyaṃ samitsu ca yathākramam।
kṛtvā samāhitaṃ cittamagraye vai karomyaham ॥ 2.13.68 ॥
anujñātaḥ kuruṣveti tathaiva dvijasattamaiḥ।
patnīmādāya putrāṃśca juhuyāddhavyavāhanam ॥ 2.13.69 ॥
samānaplakṣanyagrodhaplakṣāśvatthavikaṅkatāḥ।
udumbarāstathā bilvacandanā yajñiyāśca te ॥ 2.13.70 ॥
saralo devadāruśca śālaśca khadirastathā।
samidarthaṃ praśastāḥ syurete vṛkṣā viśeṣataḥ ॥ 2.13.71 ॥
grāmyāḥ kamṭakinaścaiva yajñiyā yena kena ca।
pūjitāḥ samidarthe tu pitṝṇāṃ vacanaṃ tathā ॥ 2.13.72 ॥
