samidbhiḥ kalkaleyābhirjjuhuyādyo hutāśanam ।
phalaṃ yat karmaṇastasya tanme nigadataḥ śrṛṇu ॥ 2.13.73 ॥
āyasaṃ sarvvakāmīyamaśvamedhaphalaṃ hi tat।
śleṣmātako naktamālaḥ kapitthaḥ śālmalistathā ॥ 2.13.74 ॥
śakunānāṃ nivāsaśca varjayecca mahīruhān।
svadheti caiva mantrānte pitṝṇāṃ vacanaṃ tathā।
svāheti caiva devānāṃ yajñakarmaṇyudāhṛtam ॥ 2.13.76 ॥
devāśca pitaraścaiva tebhyo'nye pitarastathā।
ātharvaṇavidhirhyeṣa pratyuvāca bṛhaspatiḥ ॥ 2.14.1 ॥
devebhyo'pi pitṛn pūrvamarcayantīha yatnataḥ ॥ 2.14.2 ॥
prakhyātāstriṣu lokeṣu sarvvalokanamaskṛtāḥ।
samastāste mahātmānaśverurugraṃ mahattapaḥ ॥ 2.14.4 ॥
himavacchikhare ramye devagandharvasevite।
varaṃ vṛṇīdhvaṃ prītāḥsma kaṃ kāmaṃ karavāmahe ॥ 2.14.6 ॥
evamukte tu pitṛbhistadā trailokyabhāvanaḥ।
mahātejā mahādevastapasā taistu tāpitaḥ।
evamuktāstadā viśve brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇā।
ūcuste sahitāḥ sarvve brahmāṇaṃ lokabhāvinam ॥ 2.14.9 ॥
śrāddhe'smākaṃ bhavedaṃśo hyeṣa naḥ kāṃkṣito varaḥ ।
pratyuvāca tato brahmā tānvai tridivapūjitān ॥ 2.14.10 ॥
bhaviṣyatyevameveti kāṃkṣito vo varastu yaḥ।
pitṛbhistu tathetyuktvā evametanna saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.14.11 ॥
sahāsmābhistu vo bhāvyaṃ yatkiñcit kriyate tviha।
asmākaṃ kalpite śrāddhe yuṣmānagrāsanaṃ ha vai ॥ 2.14.12 ॥
bhaviṣyati manuṣyeṣu satyametadbravīmi te।
mālyairgandhaistathānnena yuṣmānagrerjayiṣyati ॥ 2.14.13 ॥
pradātā ceti yuṣmākamasmākaṃ dāsyate tataḥ।
visarjanamathāsmākaṃ pūrvvaṃ paścāttu devatāḥ ॥ 2.14.14 ॥
rakṣaṇañcaiva śrāddhasya ātithyañca vidhidvayam।
evaṃ dattvā varaṃ teṣāṃ brahmā pitṛgaṇaiḥ saha।।
vede pañca mahāyajñā narāṇāṃ samudāhṛtāḥ ।
etānpañca mahāyajñānnirvapetsatataṃ naraḥ ॥ 2.14.17 ॥
yatra yāsyanti dātāraḥ saṃsthānaṃ vai nibhodhata।
nirbhayaṃ nirahaṅkāraṃ niḥśokaṃ nirvyathaklamam।
brahmasthānamavāpnoti sarvakāmapuraskṛtam ॥ 2.14.18 ॥
śūdreṇāpi prakarttavyāḥ pañcaite mantravarjitāḥ।
ato'nyathā tu yo bhuṅkte sa ṛṇaṃ nityamaśnute ॥ 2.14.19 ॥
ṛṇañca bhuṅkte pāpātmā yaḥ pacedātmakāraṇāt।
tasmānnirvarttayetpañca mahāyajñānsadā budhaḥ ॥ 2.14.20 ॥
naivedyaṃ kecidicchanti jīvatyapi prayatnataḥ।
udakpūrvvaṃ baliṃ kuryādudakumbhaṃ tathaiva ca ॥ 2.14.21 ॥
baliṃ suviditaṃ kuryāduccāduccataraṃ kṣipet ।
paraśrṛṅgagavāṃ pūrvva baliṃ sūkṣmaṃ samutkṣipet ॥ 2.14.22 ॥
na vinedyo bhavet piṇḍaḥ pitṝṇāṃ yastu jīvati।
iṣṭenānnena bhakṣyaiśca bhojayeta yathāvidhi।
devadevā mahātmāno hyetepi pitaro hyuta।
icchanti kiñcidācāryyāḥ paścāt piṇḍanivedanam ॥ 2.14.24 ॥
pūjanañcaiva viprāṇāṃ sarvvameva hi nityaśaḥ।
taddhi dharmārthakuśalānityuvāca bṛhaspatiḥ ॥ 2.14.25 ॥
pūrvvaṃ nivedayetpiṇḍaṃ paścādviprāṃśca bhojayet।
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ pitaro yoga sambhavāḥ।
somamāpyāyayantyete pitaro yogamāsthitāḥ ॥ 2.14.26 ॥
tasmāddadyāc‌chuciḥ piṇḍān yogibhyastatparāyaṇaḥ ।
pitṝṇāṃ hi bhavedetatsākṣādiva hutaṃ haviḥ ॥ 2.14.27 ॥
yajamānañca bhoktṝṃśca naurivāmbhasi tārayet ॥ 2.14.28 ॥
asatāṃ pragraho yatra satāñcaiva vimānanā।
daṇḍo devakṛtastatra sadyaḥ patati tāruṇaḥ ॥ 2.14.29 ॥
hitvāgamaṃ sadharmāṇaṃ bāliśaṃ yatra bhojayet।
ādikarma samutsṛjya dātā tatra vinaśyati ॥ 2.14.30 ॥
piṇḍamagnau sadā dadyādbhogārthī tu prayatnataḥ ।
uttamāṃ dyutimanvicchan goṣu nityaṃ prayacchati।
prārthayandīrghamāyuśca vāyasebhyaḥ prayacchati।
saukumāryamathānvicchan kukkuṭebhyaḥ prayacchati ॥ 2.14.33 ॥
evametatsamuddiṣṭaṃ piṇḍanirvapaṇāt phalam।
ākāśaṃ śamayedvāpi sthitau sudakṣiṇāmukhaḥ।
pitṝṇāṃ sthānamākāśaṃ dakṣiṇā caiva digbhavet ॥ 2.14.34 ॥
ekaṃ viprāḥ punaḥ prāhuḥ piṇḍoddharaṇamagrataḥ।
anujñāte tu tairviprairvānamudviyatāmiti ॥ 2.14.35 ॥
puṣpāṇāṃ caphalānāṃ ca bhakṣyāṇāmannatastathā।
agramuddhṛtya sarveṣāṃ juhuyājjātavedasi ॥ 2.14.36 ॥
bhakṣyamannaṃ tathā peyamanuttamaphalāni ca।
hutvā cāgnau tataḥ piṇḍānnirvapeddakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ॥ 2.14.37 ॥
ekāgraḥ paryupāsīta prayataḥ prāñjaliḥ sthitaḥ।
tatparaḥ śraddadhānaśca kāmānāpnoti mānavaḥ ॥ 2.14.38 ॥
akṣudratvaṃ kṛtajñatvaṃ dākṣiṇyaṃ satkṛtañca yat।
tato yajñañca dānañca prayacchanti pitāmahāḥ ॥ 2.14.39 ॥
ataḥ paraṃ vidhiṃ saumyaṃ bhuktavatsu dvijātiṣu।
ānupūrvyeṇa vidhinā tanme nigadataḥ śrṛṇu ॥ 2.14.40 ॥
prokṣya bhūmimathoddhṛtya pūrvaṃ pitṛparāyaṇaḥ।
tato'tra vikiraṃ kuryāt vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ॥ 2.14.41 ॥
svadhāṃ vācya tato viprā vidhivadbhūri dakṣiṇān।
annaśeṣamanujñāpya satkṛtya dvijasattamān ।
prāñjaliḥ prayataścaiva anugamya visarjayet ॥ 2.14.42 ॥
sakṛdabhyarcitāḥ prītā bhavanti pitaro'nyayāḥ।
yogātmāno mahātmāno vipāpmāno mahaujasaḥ ॥ 2.15.1 ॥
pretya ca svargalābhāya kāmaiśvaryaṃ suvistaram ।
yeṣāṃ cāpyanugṛhṇanti mokṣaprāptikrameṇa tu ॥ 2.15.2 ॥
tāni vakṣyāmyahaṃ saumyāḥ sarāṃsi saritastathā।
tīrthāni caiva puṇyāni deśāñjailāṃstathāśramān ॥ 2.15.3 ॥
puṇyo yastriṣu lokeṣvamarakaṇṭakaparvataḥ।
parvataḥ pravaraḥ puṇyaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitaḥ ॥ 2.15.4 ॥
yatra varṣasahasrāṇi prayutānyarbudāni ca।
tapaḥ suduścaraṃ tepe bhagavānaṅgirāḥ purā ॥ 2.15.5 ॥
yatra mṛtyorgatirnāsti tathaivāsurarakṣasām।
na bhayaṃ caiva vā'lakṣmīryāvadbhūmirdhariṣyati ॥ 2.15.6 ॥
tejasā yaśasā caiva bhrājate sa nagottamaḥ।
śrṛṅgamālyavato nityaṃ vahniḥ saṃvartako yathā ॥ 2.15.7 ॥
mṛdavaśca sugandhāśca hemābhāḥ priyadarśanāḥ ।
śāntāḥ kuśā iti khyātāḥ pibandakṣiṇanarmadām ॥ 2.15.8 ॥
dṛṣṭavān svargasopānaṃ bhagavānaṅgirāḥ purā।
agnihotre mahātejāḥ prastarārthakuśottamān ॥ 2.15.9 ॥
teṣu darbheṣu yaḥ piṇḍānamarakaṇṭakaparvate।
dadyātsakṛdapi prājñastasya vakṣyāmi yatphalam ॥ 2.15.10 ॥
tadbhavatyakṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ prītivarddhanam ।
antarddhānaṃ ca gacchanti kṣetramāsādya tatsadā ॥ 2.15.11 ॥
tatra jvālārasaḥ puṇyo dṛśyate'dyāpi sarvaśaḥ।
saśalyānāṃ ca sattvānāṃ viśalyakaraṇī nadī ॥ 2.15.12 ॥
prāgdakṣiṇā tu sāvarttā vāpī sā parvatottame।
siddhakṣetramṛṣiśreṣṭā yaduktaṃ paramaṃ bhuvi।
sammato devadaityānāṃ ślokamapyuśanā jagau ॥ 2.15.14 ॥
dhanyāste puruṣā loke ye prāpyāmarakaṇṭakam।
pitṝnsantarpayiṣyanti śrāddhe pitṛparāyaṇāḥ ॥ 2.15.15 ॥
alpena tapasā siddhiṃ gamiṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ।
sakṛdevārcitāstatra svargamamarakaṇṭake ॥ 2.15.16 ॥
mahendraparvate ramye puṇyaṃ śakraniṣevitam।
tatrāruhya bhavet prītiḥ śrāddhaṃ caiva mahatphalam ॥ 2.15.17 ॥
bilvādhaḥśikhare yuktā divyaṃ cakṣuḥ pravarttate।
adṛśyaṃ caiva bhūtānāṃ devavaccarate mahīm ॥ 2.15.18 ॥
saptagodāvare caiva gokarṇe ca tapovane।
aśvamedhaphalaṃ tatra snātvā ca labhatenaraḥ ॥ 2.15.19 ॥
dhūtapāpasthalaṃ prāpya pūtaḥ snātvā bhavennaraḥ।
rudrastatra tapastepe devadevo maheśvaraḥ ॥ 2.15.20 ॥
gokarṇe varṇitaṃ viprairnastikānāṃ nidarśanam।
abrāhmaṇasya sāvitrī paṭhataḥ sampraṇaśyati ॥ 2.15.21 ॥
devarṣibhavane śrṛṅge siddhacāraṇasevite।
āruhya taṃ tu niyamāttato yānti triviṣṭapam ॥ 2.15.22 ॥
divyaiśvandanavṛkṣaiśca pādapairupaśobhitam।
nadī pravarttate tābhyastāmraparṇīti nāmataḥ।
yoṣeva samahākhedā dakṣiṇaṃ yāti sāgaram ॥ 2.15.24 ॥
nadyāstasyāstu yā āpo mūrcchamānā mahodadhau।
śaṅkhā bhavanti muktāśca jāyante śaṅkhamuktikāḥ ॥ 2.15.25 ॥
udakānayanaṃ kṛtvā śaṅkhamauktikasaṃyutam।
ādhibhirvyādhibhiścaiva muktā yāntyamarāvatīm ॥ 2.15.26 ॥
candanebhyaḥ prayuktānāṃ śaṅkhānāṃ mauktikasya ca।
pāpa kartṝnapi pitṝṃśtārayanti yathā śrutiḥ ॥ 2.15.27 ॥
candratīrthe kumāryyāntu kāveryyāṃ prabhave'kṣaye।
śrīparvatasya tīrtheṣu vaikṛte ca tathā girau ॥ 2.15.28 ॥
ekasthā yatra dṛśyante vṛkṣā hyośiraparvate।
pālāśāḥ khādirā bilvā plakṣāśvatthavikaṅkatāḥ ॥ 2.15.29 ॥
etaddhi maṇḍalaṃ siddhaṃ yajñīyaṃ dvijasattamāḥ।
asmin muktvā jano'ṅgāni kṣipraṃ yātyamarāvatīm ॥ 2.15.30 ॥
karmāṇi svaprayuktāni sidhyanti prabhavātyaye ।
duṣprasaktāni pitṛṣu prayuktāni bhavantyuta ॥ 2.15.31 ॥
pitṝṇāṃ duhitā puṇyā narmadā saritāṃ varā।
tatra śrāddhāni dattāni akṣayāṇi bhavantyuta ॥ 2.15.32 ॥
māṭharasya vane puṇye siddhacāraṇasevite।
antarddhānaṃ na gacchanti sattāstasminmahāgirau ॥ 2.15.33 ॥
vindhye caiva girau puṇye dharmādharmanidarśanam।
pāpadhārāṃ na paśyanti dhārāṃ paśyanti sādhavaḥ ॥ 2.15.34 ॥
tasyāṃ na dṛśyate pāpaṃ keṣāñcit pāpakarmaṇām।
kauśalāyāṃ mataṅgasya vāpī pāpaniṣūdanī।
snātāstasyāṃ divaṃ yānti kāmacāravihaṅgamāḥ ॥ 2.15.36 ॥
kumārakośalātīrthe parvate pālapañjare।
pāṇḍu kūle samudrānte paṇḍārakavane tathā ॥ 2.15.37 ॥
vimale ca vipāpe ca satkṛtya prabhave'bhaye।
bhīvṛkṣe gṛdhrakūṭe ca jambūmārge ca nityaśaḥ ॥ 2.15.38 ॥
asitasya guroḥ puṇye yogācāryasya dhīmataḥ।
tatrāpi śrāddhamānantyamasitāyāñca nityaśaḥ ॥ 2.15.39 ॥
puṣkareṣvakṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ tapaścaiva mahāphalam।
mahodadhau prabhāse ca tasmādevaṃ vinirddiśet ॥ 2.15.40 ॥
devikāyāṃ vṛṣo nāma kūpaḥ siddhaniṣevitaḥ।
samutpatanti tasyāpo gavāṃ śabdena nityaśaḥ ॥ 2.15.41 ॥
yogeśvaraiḥ sadā juṣṭaḥ sarvapāpabahiṣkṛtaiḥ।
dadyācchrāddhantu yastasmiṃstasya vakṣyāmi yatphalam ॥ 2.15.42 ॥
akṣayaṃ sārvakāmīyaṃ śrāddhaṃ prīṇāti vai pitṝn।
jātavedaḥ śilā tatra sākṣādagneḥ sanātanī ॥ 2.15.43 ॥
yastvāgniṃ praviśettatra nākapṛṣṭe sa modate।
agniḥ śāntaḥ punarjātastasmindattaṃ tadakṣayam ॥ 2.15.44 ॥
daśāśvamadike tīrthe tīrthe pañcāśvamedhike।
yathoddiṣṭaṃ phalaṃ teṣāṃ kratūnāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.15.45 ॥
khyātaṃ hayaśiro nāma tīrthaṃ sadyo varapradam।
śrāddhaṃ tatra tadākṣayyaṃ dattvā svarge ca modate ॥ 2.15.46 ॥
śrāddhaṃ tatrākṣayaṃ proktaṃ japyahomatapāṃsi ca ॥ 2.15.47 ॥
ajhatuṅge śubhe tīrthe tarpayetsatataṃ pitṝn।
dṛśyate parvasu cchāyā yatra nityaṃ divaukasām।
pṛthivyāmakṣayaṃ dattaṃ nirujā yatra pāṇḍavāḥ ॥ 2.15.48 ॥
yogeśvaraiḥ sadā juṣṭaṃ sarvapāpabahiṣkṛtaiḥ।
dadyācchrāddhantu yastasmistasya vakṣyāmi yatphalam ॥ 2.15.49 ॥
arcitāstena vai sākṣādbhavanti pitaraḥ sadā।
asmiँlloke vaśī yaḥ syātpretya svarge sa modate ॥ 2.15.50 ॥
prāyaśaḥ pravaraḥ puṇyaḥ śivo nāma hradastathā।
tatra vyāsasaraḥ puṇyaṃ divyaṃ brahmasarastathā ॥ 2.15.51 ॥
ujjantaḥ parvataḥ puṇyo vasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ।
ṛgyajuḥsāmaśirasaḥ kāpotaḥ puṣpasāhvayaḥ।
ākhyātaḥ pañcamo vedaḥ sṛṣṭvā hyeteṣu brahmaṇā ॥ 2.15.52 ॥
gatvaitān mucyate pāpāddvijo vahniḥ sanātanaḥ ।।
śrāddhañcānantyameteṣu japya homatapāṃsi ca ॥ 2.15.53 ॥
puṇḍarīke mahātīrthe puṇḍarīkasamaṃ phalam।
sindhusāgarasambhede tadā pañcanade'kṣayam ।
kīrakātmā tataḥ puṇyo maṇḍavāyāṃ ca parvate ॥ 2.15.55 ॥
deyaṃ saptahrade śrāddhaṃ mānase ca viśeṣataḥ।
mahākūṭe ca vande ca girau trirau trikakude tathā ॥ 2.15.56 ॥
sandhyāyāṃ ca mahāvedyāṃ dṛśyate mahadadbhutam।
aśraddadhānānnābhyeti sābhyeti ca dhṛtavratān ॥ 2.15.57 ॥
jātavedaḥ śilā tatra sākṣādagneḥ sanātanī।
śrāddhāni cāgnikāryaṃ ca tatra kuryāt sadākṣayam ॥ 2.15.58 ॥
saṃśrayitvaikamekena sāyāhnaṃ prati nityaśaḥ।
tasmindeyaṃ sadā śrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāmakṣayārthinā ॥ 2.15.59 ॥
kṛtātmā vā'kṛtātmā vā yatra vijñāyate naraḥ।
svargyamārgapradaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ sadyo varapradam।
vairāṇyutsṛjya tasmistu divaṃ saptarṣayo gatāḥ ॥ 2.15.60 ॥
adyāpi tāni dṛśyante vairāṇyeva gatāni tu।
snātvā svargamavāpnoti tasmistīrthottame naraḥ ॥ 2.15.61 ॥
khyātamāyatanaṃ tatra nandisiddha niṣevitam।
nandīśvarasya yā mūrttirdurājārairna dṛśyate ॥ 2.15.62 ॥
dṛśyante kāñcanā yūpāḥ sañciṣye bhāskarodaye।
kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ te tu gacchantyantarhitā divam ॥ 2.15.63 ॥
sarvataśca kurukṣetraṃ sutīrthañca viśeṣataḥ।
puṇyaṃ sanatkumārasya yogeśasya mahātmanaḥ।
kīrttyate ca tilāndattvā pitṝṇāṃ vai sadā'kṣayam ॥ 2.15.64 ॥
ojase cākṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ dharmarājaniveśane।
śrāddhaṃ dattamamāvasyāṃ vidhinā ca yathākramam ॥ 2.15.65 ॥
punaḥ sannihitānāṃ vai kurukṣetre viśeṣataḥ।
arcayedvā pitṝṃstatra satputrastvanṛṇo bhavet ॥ 2.15.66 ॥
vinaśane sarasvatyāṃ plakṣapraśravaṇe tathā।
vyāsatīrthe sarasvatyāṃ brahmakṣetre viśeṣataḥ ॥ 2.15.67 ॥
deyamoṅkārapaṭhanaiḥ śrāddhamakṣayamicchatā।
sarvataścaiva gaṅgyāṃ maināke ca nagottame ॥ 2.15.68 ॥
yamunāprabhave caiva sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।
atyuṣṇāścātiśītāśca āpastatra nidarśanam ॥ 2.15.69 ॥
yamasya bhaginī puṇyā mārttaṇḍaduhitā tathā।
tatrākṣayaṃ tadā śrāddhaṃ pitṛbhiḥ pūrvakīrttitam ॥ 2.15.70 ॥
brahmānugahrade snātvā sadyo bhavati brāhmaṇaḥ।
tasmin hi śrāddhamānantyaṃ japahomatapāṃsi ca ॥ 2.15.71 ॥
sthāṇubhūtaścaraṃstatra vasiṣṭo vai mahātapāḥ।
adyāpi yatra dṛśyante pādapā maṇicarccitāḥ ॥ 2.15.72 ॥
tulā tu dṛśyate yatra dharmādharmapradarśinī।
yayā vai tulitaṃ vipraistīrthānāṃ phalamuttamam ॥ 2.15.73 ॥
pitṝṇāṃ duhitā yogā gandhakālīti viśrutā।
caturtho brahmaṇaścāṃśaḥ parāśarakulodvahaḥ ॥ 2.15.74 ॥
vyasya tvekaṃ caturddhā tu vedaṃ dhīmān mahāmuniḥ।
mahāyogaṃ mahātmānaṃ yo vyāsaṃ janayiṣyati ॥ 2.15.75 ॥
acchodakaṃ nāma saro yatrācchodā samucchritā ।
matsyayonau punarjātā niyogādvāraṇena tu ॥ 2.15.76 ॥
tasyā yatrāśramaḥ puṇyaḥ puṇyakṛdbhirniṣevitaḥ।
sakṛddattaṃ tu vai śrāddhamakṣayaṃ samudāhṛtam।
tasyāṃ yoga samādhāne dattaṃ yugapadudbhavet ॥ 2.15.77 ॥
siddhaistu sevitā nityaṃ dṛśyate nākṛtātmabhiḥ।
anivarttanaṃ tu nandāyāṃ vedyāṃ prāguttare diśi ॥ 2.15.79 ॥
siddhakṣetraṃ tu vai juṣṭaṃ yatprāpya na nivarttate।
mahālaye padaṃ nyastaṃ mahādevena dhīmatā ॥ 2.15.80 ॥
devyālaye tapastaptvā ekapādena īśvaraḥ।
nīhāraśca yugaṃ divyamumātuṅge sthitaṃ jalam ॥ 2.15.81 ॥
umā tuṅge bhṛgostuṅge brahmatuṅge mahālaye।
kādravatyāṃ ca śāṇḍilyāṃ guhāyāṃ vāmanasya ca ॥ 2.15.82 ॥
gatvā caitāni pūtaḥ syācchrāddhamakṣayameva ca।
japo homastathā dhyānaṃ yatkicitsukṛtaṃ bhavet ॥ 2.15.83 ॥
brahmacaryaṃ yajante vai gurubhaktāḥ śataṃ samāḥ ।
kumāradhārā tatraiva dṛṣṭā pāpapraṇāśanī।
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ devavaccarate mahīm ॥ 2.15.86 ॥
kāśyapasya mahātīrthaṃ kālasarpiriti śrutam।
tatra śrāddhāni deyāni nityamakṣayamicchatā ॥ 2.15.87 ॥
kāśyapasya mahātīrthaṃ kālasarpiriti śrutam।
tatra śrāddhāni deyāni nityamakṣayamicchatā ॥ 2.15.88 ॥
akṣayaṃ tu bhavecchrāddhaṃ śālagrāmasamantataḥ।
dṛṣṭyā na dṛśyate tatra pratyakṣamakṛtātmanā ॥ 2.15.89 ॥
pratyādeśo hyaśiṣṭānāṃ śiṣṭānāṃ ca niveśanam ।
piṇḍaṃ gṛhṇāti hisatāṃ na gṛhṇātyasatāṃ hi saḥ।
atipradīptairbhujagairbhoktumannaṃ na śakyate ॥ 2.15.91 ॥
pratyakṣaṃ dṛśyate dharmastīrthayoranayordvayoḥ।
devadāruvane cāpi cārayestaṃ nidarśanam ॥ 2.15.92 ॥
vidhūtāni tu pāpāni dṛśyante sukṛtātmanā ।
bhāgīrathyāṃ prayāge ca nityamakṣayyamucyate ॥ 2.15.93 ॥
kālañjare daśārṇāyāṃ naimiṣe kurujāṅgale।
vārāṇasyāṃ nagaryāṃ tu deyaṃ śrāddhaṃ tu yatnataḥ ॥ 2.15.94 ॥
tasyāṃ yogeśvaro nityaṃ tattasyāṃ dattamakṣayam।
dattvā caiteṣu pūtaḥ syācchrāddhamānantyameva ca ॥ 2.15.95 ॥
tapo homastathā dhyānaṃ yat kiñcitsukṛtaṃ bhavet।
lauhitye vaitaraṇyāṃ vai svarṇavedyāṃ tathaiva ca ॥ 2.15.96 ॥
gayāyāṃ dharmapṛṣṭe ca sarasi brahmaṇastathā ॥ 2.15.97 ॥
gayāyāṃ gṛdhrakūṭe ca śrāddhaṃ dattaṃ mahāphalam।
himañca patate tatra samantāt pañcayojanam ॥ 2.15.98 ॥
bharatasyāśrame puṇye'raṇyaṃ puṇyatamaṃ smṛtam ।
khyāpitaṃ dharmmasarvvasvaṃ lokasyāsya nidarśanam।
evaṃ pañcavanaṃ puṇyaṃ puṇyakṛdbhirniṣevitam।
yasminpāṇḍuviśāleti tīrthaṃ sadyo nidarśanam ॥ 2.15.100 ॥
tulāmānaistathā cāpaiḥ śāstraiśca vividhaistathā।
unmajjanti tathā lagne ye vai pāpakṛto janāḥ ॥ 2.15.101 ॥
tṛtīyāyāṃ tathā pāde niḥsvare pāvamaṇḍale।
mahāhrade vai kauśikyāṃ dattaṃ śrāddhaṃ mahāphalam ॥ 2.15.102 ॥
muṇḍapṛṣṭe padaṃ nyastaṃ mahādevena dhīmatā।
bahūndaveyugāṃstaptvā tapastīvraṃ suduścaram ॥ 2.15.103 ॥
alpenāpyatra kālena naro dharmmaparāyaṇaḥ।
pāpmānamutsṛjatyāśu jīrṇatvacamivoragaḥ ॥ 2.15.104 ॥
siddhānāṃ prītijananaiḥ pāpā nāñca bhayaṅkaraiḥ।
nāmnā kanakanandīti tīrthaṃ trailokyaviśrutam।
udīcyāṃ muṇḍapṛṣṭhasya devarṣi gaṇasevitam।
tatra srātvā divaṃ yānti kāmacārā vihaṅgamāḥ ॥ 2.15.106 ॥
dattaṃ cāpi tathā śrāddhamakṣayaṃ samudāhṛtam।
tīre tu sarasastatra devasyāyatanaṃ mahat।
āruhya tajjapaṃstatra siddho yāti divaṃ tataḥ ॥ 2.15.108 ॥
uttaraṃ mānasaṃ gatvā siddhiṃ prāpnotyanuttamām ।
divaścyutā mahābhāgā hyantarikṣe virājate ॥ 2.15.111 ॥
ākāśe dṛśyate tatra toraṇaṃ sūryyasannibham ॥ 2.15.112 ॥
jāmbūnadamayaṃ divyaṃ svargadvāramivāyatam।
yataḥ pravarttate bhūyaḥ pūrvvasāgaramantimam ॥ 2.15.113 ॥
pāvanī sarvvabhūtānāṃ dharmajñānāṃ viśeṣataḥ।
candrabhāgā ca sindhuśca ubhau mānasasannibhau।
sāgaraṃ paścimaṃ yāti divyasindhurnadīvaraḥ ॥ 2.15.114 ॥
parvvato himavānnāma nānādhātuvibhūṣitaḥ।
siddhacāraṇasaṅkīrṇaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitaḥ।
tatra puṣkariṇī ramyā suṣumnā nāma viśrutā ॥ 2.15.116 ॥
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi tatra jātastu jīvati।
śrāddhaṃ bhavati cānantyaṃ tasyāṃ dattaṃ mahodayam।
tārayecca yadā śrāddhaṃ daśapūrvvāndaśāparān ॥ 2.15.117 ॥
samudragāḥ samudrāśca sarvve puṇyāḥ samantataḥ ॥ 2.15.118 ॥
evamādiṣu sarvveṣu śrāddhaṃ nirvarttayedbudhaḥ ।
pūto bhavati snātvā nu dattvā dattvā tathaiva ca ॥ 2.15.119 ॥
śailasānuṣu tuṅgeṣu kandareṣu guhāsu ca।
upahvaranitambeṣu tathā prasravaṇeṣu ca ॥ 2.15.120 ॥
pulineṣvāpagānāṃ ca tathaiva prabhave yuge।
mahodadhau gavāṃ goṣṭe saṅgameṣu vaneṣu ca ॥ 2.15.121 ॥
gomayenopalipteṣu vivikteṣu gṛheṣu ca ॥ 2.15.122 ॥
kuryyācchrāddhamathaiteṣu nityameva yathāvidhi।
pradakṣiṇaṃ diśaṃ gatvā sarvvakāmacikīrṣavaḥ ॥ 2.15.123 ॥
evameteṣu sarvveṣu śrāddhaṃ kuryyādatandritaḥ।
evameva tu medhāvī brāhmīṃ siddhimavāpnuyāt ॥ 2.15.124 ॥
kopasthānasya saṃtyāgātprāpyate pitṛpūjanam ॥ 2.15.125 ॥
kṛtapāpaśca śuddhyeta kiṃ punaḥ śubhakarmmakṛt ॥ 2.15.126 ॥
tiryagyoniṃ na gacchecca kudeśe na ca jāyate।
svargī bhavati vai vipro mokṣopāyaṃ ca vindati ॥ 2.15.127 ॥
gurutīrthe parā siddhistīrthānāṃ paramaṃ padam ।
dhyānaṃ tīrthaparaṃ tasmādbrahmatīrthaṃ sanātanam ॥ 2.15.129 ॥
upavāsātparaṃ dhyānamindriyāṇāṃ nivarttanam।
upavāsanibaddhā hi prāṇairiha punaḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.15.130 ॥
buddhiṃ manasi saṃyamya sarvveṣāṃ tu nivarttanam ॥ 2.15.131 ॥
pratyāhāraṃ punarviddhi mokṣopāyamasaṃśayam।
indriyāṇāṃ mano ghoraṃ buddhyādīnāṃ pravarttanam ॥ 2.15.132 ॥
anāhārātkṣayaṃ yāti vidyādanaśanaṃ tapaḥ।
nigrahādbuddhimanaso ramyā buddhistu jāyate ॥ 2.15.133 ॥
kṣīṇeṣu sarvvapāpeṣu kṣīṇeṣvevendriyeṣu ca।
parinirvāti śuddhātmā yathā vahnirnirindhanaḥ ॥ 2.15.134 ॥
kāraṇebhyo guṇebhyo'tha vyaktāvyaktasya kṛtsnaśaḥ।
viyojayati kṣetrajñaṃ tebhyo yogena yogavit ॥ 2.15.135 ॥
tasya nāsti gatisthānaṃ vyaktāvyaktaṃ na saṃśayaḥ।
āsannaḥ sadasannaiva naiva kiñcit sthita iti ॥ 2.15.136 ॥
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte śrāddhakalpe tīrthayātrā nāma pañcadaśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 15 ।। *
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dānāni ca phalāni ca।
śrāddhakarmmāṇi medhyāni varjanīyāni yāni ca ॥ 2.16.1 ॥
himaprapatane kuryyādāharedvā himantataḥ।
naktantu varjayecchrāddhaṃ rāhoranyatra darśanāt।
sarvvasvenāpi karttavyaṃ kṣipraṃ vai rāhudarśane ॥ 2.16.3 ॥
uparāge na kuryyādyaḥ paṅke gauriva sīdati।
kurvāṇastūddharetpāpānmagnānnauriva sāgare ॥ 2.16.4 ॥
viśvadevañca saumyañca bahumāṃsaparaṃ haviḥ ।
tvaṣṭā vai vāryyamāṇastu deveśena mahātmanā।
pibañchacīpateḥ somaṃ pṛthivyāmapatatpurā ॥ 2.16.6 ॥
śyāmākāstu tathotpannāḥ pitrarthamapi pūjitāḥ।
vipruṣastasya nāsābhyāmasaktābhyāṃ tathaiva ca ॥ 2.16.7 ॥
śleṣmāṇaḥ śītalā hṛdyā madhurāśca tathekṣavaḥ।
śyāmākairikṣubhiścaiva pitṝṇāṃ sārvvakāmikam।
kuryyādāgrayaṇaṃ yastu sa śīghraṃ siddhimāpnuyāt ॥ 2.16.8 ॥
evamātīni cānyāni svādūni madhurāṇi ca ।
nāgaraṃ cātra vai deyaṃ dīrghamūlakameva ca ॥ 2.16.10 ॥
vaṃśīkarīrāḥ surasāḥ sarjjakaṃ bhūstṛṇāni ca।
varjanīyāni vakṣyāmi śrāddhakarmmaṇi nityaśaḥ ॥ 2.16.11 ॥
laśunaṃ gṛñjanañcaiva palāṇḍuḥ piṇḍamūlakam।
karambhādyāni cānyāni hīnāni rasagandhataḥ ॥ 2.16.12 ॥
śrāddhakarmmaṇi varjyāni kāraṇañcātra vakṣyate।
purā devāsure yuddhe nirjitasya baleḥ suraiḥ ॥ 2.16.13 ॥
tata etāni varjyāni śrāddhakarmmaṇi nityaśaḥ ॥ 2.16.14 ॥
atha vedoktaniryāsān lavaṇānyūṣaraṇāni ca।
śrāddha karmmaṇi varjyāni yāśca nāryo rajasvalāḥ ॥ 2.16.15 ॥
durgandhaṃ phenilaṃ caiva tathā vai palvalodakam।
na labhedyatra gaustṛptiṃ naktaṃ yaccaiva gṛhyate ॥ 2.16.16 ॥
āvikaṃ mārgamauṣṭraṃ ca sarvvamekaśaphaṃ ca yat।
māhiṣañcāmarañcaiva payo varjyaṃ vijānatā ॥ 2.16.17 ॥
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi varjyān deśān prayatnataḥ।
na draṣṭavyaṃ ca yaiḥ śrāddhaṃ śaucāśaucaṃ ca kṛtsnaśaḥ ॥ 2.16.18 ॥
vanyamūlaphalāhāraiḥ śrāddhaṃ kuryyāttu śraddhayā।
aniṣṭa śabdasaṅkīrṇaṃ jantuvyāptamathāpi vā।
pūtigandhāṃ tathā bhūmiṃ śrāddhakarmmaṇi varjayet ॥ 2.16.20 ॥
nadyaḥ sāgaraparyyantā dvāraṃ dakṣiṇapūrvvataḥ ।
triśaṅkuṃ varjayed deśaṃ sarvvaṃ dvādaśayojanam ॥ 2.16.21 ॥
uttareṇa mahānadyā dakṣiṇena ca kaikaṭāt।
deśastraiśaṅkavo nāma varjitaḥ śrāddhakarmmaṇi ॥ 2.16.22 ॥
kāraṅkarāḥ kaliṅgāśca sindhoruttarameva ca।
pranaṣṭāśramadharmmāśca varjyā deśāḥ prayatnataḥ ॥ 2.16.23 ॥
nagnādayo na paśyeyuḥ śrāddhameva vyayasthitam।
gacchanti taistairdṛṣṭāni na pitṝnna pitāmahān ॥ 2.16.24 ॥
nagnādīn bhagavan samyaṅmamādya paripṛcchataḥ।
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ trayīsaṃvaraṇaṃ smṛtam ॥ 2.16.26 ॥
pralīyate naro yaḥ syānnirālambaśca yo vṛṣaḥ ॥ 2.16.27 ॥
vṛṣaṃ yaśca parityajya mokṣamanyatra mārgati ।
vṛṣo vedasamastasmin yo vai samyaṅna paśyati ॥ 2.16.28 ॥
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā vṛṣalāścaiva sarvvaśaḥ।
purā devāsure yuddhe nirjitairasuraistadā ॥ 2.16.29 ॥
ye dharmmaṃ nānuvarttante te vai nagnādayo janāḥ।
vṛthājaṭī vṛthāmudrī vṛthānagnaśca yo dvijaḥ ॥ 2.16.31 ॥
vṛthāvratī vṛthā jāpī te vai nagnādayo janāḥ।
kṛtakarmmākṣitāstvete kupathāḥ parikīrttitāḥ।
ebhirnirvṛttaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vā śrāddhaṃ gacchanti mānavāḥ ॥ 2.16.33 ॥
brahmaghnaśca kṛtaghnaśca nāstikā gurutalpagāḥ।
ye cānye pāpa karmmāṇaḥ sarvvāṃstān parivarjayet।
asurān yātudhānāṃśca dṛṣṭamebhirvrajantyuta।
brāhmaṃ kṛtayugaṃ proktaṃ tretā tu kṣatriyaṃ smṛtam ॥ 2.16.36 ॥
vaiśyaṃ dvāparamityāhuḥ śūdraṃ kaliyugaṃ smṛtam ।।
yuddhāni dvāpare nityaṃ pāṣaṇḍāśca kalau yuge।
apamānāpavitraśca kukkuṭo grāmasūkaraḥ ॥ 2.16.38 ॥
śāvasūtakasaṃspṛṣṭo dīrgharogibhireva ca ॥ 2.16.39 ॥
malinaiḥ patitaiścaiva na draṣṭavyaṃ kathañcana।
annaṃ paśyeyurete vai naitatsyāddhavyakavyayoḥ ॥ 2.16.40 ॥
haviṣāṃ saṃhatānāṃ tu pūrvvameva vivarjitam।
mṛtsaṃyuktābhiradbhiśca prokṣaṇaṃ ca vidhīyate ॥ 2.16.41 ॥
siddhārthakaiḥ kṛṣṇatilaiḥ kāryyaṃ vāpyavakīraṇam।
gurusūryyāgnivastūnāṃ darśanaṃ vāpi yatnataḥ ॥ 2.16.42 ॥
āsanārūḍhamāneṣu pādopahatameva ca।
amedhyairjaṅgamairdṛṣṭaṃ śuṣkaṃ paryuṣitaṃ ca yat ॥ 2.16.43 ॥
asitaṃ pariduṣṭaṃ ca tathaivāgrāvalehitam।
śarkarākeśapāṣāṇaiḥ kīṭairyaccāpyupadrutam ॥ 2.16.44 ॥
piṇyākamathitaṃ caiva tathā tilayavādiṣu।
siddhākṣatāśca ye bhakṣyāḥ pratyakṣalavaṇīkṛtāḥ ॥ 2.16.45 ॥
vāsasā cāvadhūtāni varjyāni śrāddhakarmaṇi।
santi vedavirodhena kecidvijñānamāninaḥ ॥ 2.16.46 ॥
dadhi śākaṃ tathā'bhakṣyāḥ śuktaṃ caiva vivarjitam ॥ 2.16.47 ॥
vārtākuṃ varjayeddadyātsarvānabhiṣavānapi।
saindhavaṃ lavaṇaṃ yacca tathā mānasasambhavam ॥ 2.16.48 ॥
pavitraṃ paramaṃ hyetat pratyakṣamapi varttate।
agnau nikṣipya badhnīyāddhastau prakṣipya yatnataḥ ॥ 2.16.49 ॥
gamayenmastakaṃ caiva brahmatīrthaṃ hi tatsmṛtam।
dravyāṇāṃ prokṣaṇaṃ kāryyaṃ tathaivāvapanaṃ punaḥ ॥ 2.16.50 ॥
nidhāya cādbhiḥ siñceta tathaivāpsu niveśanam।
vidalānāñca sarvveṣāṃ dharmavacchaucamiṣyate।
tathā dantāsthidārūṇāṃ śrṛṅgāṇāñcāvalekhanam ॥ 2.16.52 ॥
sarveṣāṃ mṛnmayānāntu punardāha udāhṛtaḥ।
siddhārthakānāṃ kalkena tilakalkena vā punaḥ ।
syācchaucaṃ sarvavālānāmāvikānāñca sarvaśaḥ ॥ 2.16.54 ॥
 āvi kānāñca sarvveṣāṃ mṛdbhiradbhirvidhīyate।
ādyantayostu śaucānāmadbhiḥ prakṣālanaṃ punaḥ ॥ 2.16.55 ॥
tathā kārppāsikānāñca bhasmanā samudāhṛtam।
phalapuṣpa śalākānāṃ plāvanañcādbhiriṣyate ॥ 2.16.56 ॥
niṣkramya bāhyato grāmādvāyupūtā vasundharā ॥ 2.16.57 ॥
evameṣa samuddiṣṭaḥ śaucānāṃ vidhiruttamaḥ।
kuryyātpurīṣaṃ śirovaguṇṭya na ca spṛśettatra śiraḥ kareṇa ॥ 2.16.59 ॥
śuṣkaistṛṇairvā kāṣṭairvā patrairveṇudalena vā।
uddhṛtodakamādāya mṛttikāñcaiva vāgyataḥ।
divā udaṅmukhaḥ kuryyādrātrau vai dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ॥ 2.16.61 ॥
dakṣiṇena ca hastena gṛhṇīyādvai kamaṇḍalum।
śaucañca vāmahastena gude tisrastu mṛttikāḥ ॥ 2.16.62 ॥
daśa cāpi punardadyādvāmahastakrameṇa tu ।
dvābhyāṃ vāpi punardadyāddhastānāṃ pañca mṛttikāḥ ॥ 2.16.63 ॥
mṛdā prakṣālya pādau ca ācamya ca yathāvidhi।
asatkāryaṃ kāryametairyathāvatpādadhāvanam ॥ 2.16.65 ॥
ācamanaṃ dvitīyena devakāryaṃ tataḥ param।
upavāsa strirātrantu duṣṭahaste hyudāhṛtaḥ ॥ 2.16.66 ॥
viprakṛṣṭena kṛcchreṇa prāyaścittamudāhṛtam।
spṛṣṭvā śvānaṃ śvapākaṃ vā taptakṛcchraṃ samācaret ॥ 2.16.67 ॥
mānuṣāsthīni saṃspṛśya upoṣyaṃ śuddhikāraṇam ।
trirātramuktaṃ sasnehamekarātramato'nyathā ॥ 2.16.68 ॥
kāraskarāḥ pulindāśca tathāndhaśabarādaya।
pītvā cāpobhūtilaye gatvā caiva yugandharām ॥ 2.16.69 ॥
sindhoruttaraparyyantaṃ tathā divyantare śatam।
pāpadeśāśca ye kecitpāparadhyuṣitā janaiḥ ॥ 2.16.70 ॥
śiṣṭaiśca varjitā ye ca brāhmaṇairvedapāragaiḥ।
gatvā deśānapuṇyāṃstu kṛtsnaṃ pāpaṃ samaśnute ॥ 2.16.71 ॥
vikhyāpanañca śaucānāṃ nityamajñānameva ca ॥ 2.16.72 ॥
atonyathā tu yaḥ kuryyānmohācchaucasya saṅkaram।
piśācān yātudhānāṃśca phalaṃ gacchatyasaṃśayam ॥ 2.16.73 ॥
śaucamaśraddadhānaśca mlecchajātiṣu jāyate।
ayajñāścaiva pāpo vā tiryyagyonigato'pi vā ॥ 2.16.74 ॥
śaucena mokṣaṃ kurvāṇaḥ svargavāsī bhavennaraḥ।
śucikāmā hi devā vai devairetadudāhṛtam ॥ 2.16.75 ॥
bībhatsamaśuciñcaiva varjayanti surāḥ sadā।
trīṇi śaucāni kurvanti nyāyataḥ śubhakarmaṇaḥ ॥ 2.16.76 ॥
brahmaṇyāyātitheyāya śaucayuktāya dhīmate।
pitṛbhaktāya dāntāya sānukrośāya ca dvijāḥ ॥ 2.16.77 ॥
taistaiḥ prītāḥ prayacchanti pitaro yogavarddhanāḥ।
manasā kāṃkṣitān kāmāṃstrailokyaprabhavāniti ॥ 2.16.78 ॥
aho dhīmaṃstvayā sūta śrāddhakalpastu kīrtitaḥ।
śruto naḥ śrāddhakalpo vai ṛṣibhiḥ parikīrtitaḥ ॥ 2.17.1 ॥
atīva vistaro yasya viśeṣeṇa prakīrtitaḥ।
vada śeṣaṃ mahāprājña ṛṣestasya yathāmatam ॥ 2.17.2 ॥
kīrtayiṣyāmi te viprā ṛṣestasya matantu tat।
śrāddhaṃ prati mahābhāgāstanme śrṛṇuta vistarāt ॥ 2.17.3 ॥
uktaṃ śrāddhaṃ mayā pūrvaṃ vidhiśca śrāddhakarmmaṇi।
pariśiṣṭaṃ pravakṣyāmi brāhmaṇānāṃ yathākramam ॥ 2.17.4 ॥
na mīmāṃsyāḥ sadā viprāḥ pavitraṃ hyetaduttamam।
daive pitrye ca satataṃ śrūyate vai parīkṣaṇam ॥ 2.17.5 ॥
yasmin doṣāḥ pradṛśyeran sadbhirvā varjitastu yaḥ।
jānīyādvāpi saṃvāsādvarjjayettaṃ prayatnataḥ ॥ 2.17.6 ॥
avijñātaṃ dvijaṃ śrāddhe parīkṣeta sadā budhaḥ ।
siddhā hi viprarūpeṇa caranti pṛthivīmimām ॥ 2.17.7 ॥
tasmādatithimāyāntamabhigacchet kṛtāñjaliḥ।
pūjayeccāpi pādyena pādābhyañjanabhojanaiḥ ॥ 2.17.8 ॥
urvīṃ sāgaraparyantāṃ devā yogeśvarāstathā।
nānā rūpaiścarantyete prajā dharmmeṇa pālayan ॥ 2.17.9 ॥
vyañjanāni ca bhakṣyāṇi phalaṃ teṣāṃ tathaiva ca ॥ 2.17.10 ॥
tatprāpnuyācchraddadhāno naro vai sarvaiḥ kāmairbhojayedyastu viprān।
sarvārthadaḥ sarvaviprātithau yaḥ phalaṃ bhuṅkte sarvamedhasya nityam ॥ 2.17.12 ॥
yastu śrāddhe'tithiṃ prāpya daive vāpyavamanyate।
taṃ vai devā viśvayanti hotā yadvat parāṃ vasum ॥ 2.17.13 ॥
devāśca pitaraścaiva vahniścaiva hi tān dvijān ।
āviśya bhuñjate tadvai lokānugrahakāraṇāt ॥ 2.17.14 ॥
apūjitā dahantyete dadyuḥ kāmāṃśca pūjitāḥ।
sarvasvenāpi tasmādvai pūjayedatithīn sadā ॥ 2.17.15 ॥
vānaprastho gṛhasthaśca gṛhamabhyāgato'thavā।
abhyāgato yācakaḥ syādatithiḥ syādayācakaḥ।
atitheratithiḥ śreṣṭhaḥ so'tithiryoga ucyate ॥ 2.17.17 ॥
na ghoro nāpi saṅkīrṇo nāvidyo na viśeṣavit।
na ca santo na samṛddho na sevī nācaro'tithiḥ ॥ 2.17.18 ॥
pipāsitāya śrāntāya bhrāntāyātibubhukṣate।
tasmai satkṛtya dātavyaṃ yajñasya phalamicchatā ॥ 2.17.19 ॥
āruhya bhṛgutuṅgoṣu gatvā puṇyāṃ sarasvatīm।
āpagāṃ tu nadī puṇyāṃ gaṅgā devī mahānadī ॥ 2.17.20 ॥
himavatprabhavā nadyo yāścānyā ṛṣipūjitāḥ ।
gatvaitān mucyate pāpaiḥ svarge nityaṃ mahīyate।
daśarātramaśaucantu proktaṃ vai mṛtasūtake ॥ 2.17.22 ॥
udakyā sarvavarṇānāṃ trirātreṇa tu śuddhayati।
udakyāṃ sūtikāñcaiva śvānamantyāvasāyinam ॥ 2.17.24 ॥
nagnādīn mṛtahārāṃśca spṛṣṭvā'śaucaṃ vidhīyate।
etadeva bhavecchaucaṃ maithune navabhistathā।
mṛdā prakṣālya hastau tu kuryācchaucavidhinnaraḥ ॥ 2.17.26 ॥
evaṃ śauca vidhirdṛṣṭaḥ sarvavarṇeṣu nityadā।
paridadyānmṛdastisro hastapādāvasecanam ॥ 2.17.28 ॥
āraṇyaṃ śaucametattu grāmyaṃ vakṣyāmyataḥ param।
mṛdaḥ pañcadaśāmedhye hastādīnāṃ vibhāgaśaḥ।
anirṇikte mṛdaṃ dadyānmṛdante tvadbhireva tu ॥ 2.17.30 ॥
akṛtvā pādayoḥ śaucamācānto'pyaśucirbhavet ॥ 2.17.31 ॥
prakṣālya pātraṃ niḥkṣipya ācamyābhyukṣaṇaṃ punaḥ।
dravyasyānyasya tu tathā kuryādabhyukṣaṇaṃ punaḥ ॥ 2.17.32 ॥
puṣpādīnāṃ tṛṇānāñca prokṣaṇaṃ haviṣāntathā।
parāhṛtānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ nidhāyābhyukṣaṇaṃ tathā ॥ 2.17.33 ॥
uttareṇa haredvedyāṃ dakṣiṇena visarjayet ॥ 2.17.34 ॥
vicchinnaṃ syādviparyāse daive pitrye tathaiva ca।
dakṣiṇena tu hastena dakṣiṇāṃ vedimālikhet ॥ 2.17.35 ॥
karābhyāmeva devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ vikaraṃ śubham।
kṣubhitasvapnayoścaiva tathā mūtrapurīṣayoḥ ॥ 2.17.36 ॥
niṣṭīvite yathā vyakte bhuktvā viparidhāya ca।
ucchiṣṭasya ca saṃsparśe tathā pādāvasecane ॥ 2.17.37 ॥
sandeheṣu ca sarveṣu śikhāṃ muktvā tathaiva ca ॥ 2.17.38 ॥
vinā yajñopavītena mohāttu yadyupaspṛṣet।
auṣṭhasya dantasaṃsparśe darśane cāntyavāsinām ॥ 2.17.39 ॥
jiṅvayā caiva saṃspṛśya dantāsaktaṃ tathaiva ca।
yaścādharme sthito mohādāyānto'pyaśucirbhavet।
upaviśya śucau deśe praṇataḥ prāgudaṅmukhaḥ ॥ 2.17.41 ॥
pādau prakṣālya hastau tu antarjānurupa spṛśet।
prasannāstriḥ pibeccāpaḥ prayataḥ susamāhitaḥ ॥ 2.17.42 ॥
dvireva mārjanaṃ kuryātsakṛdabhyukṣaṇaṃ tataḥ।
khāni mūrddhānamātmānaṃ hastau pādau tathaiva ca ॥ 2.17.43 ॥
abhyukṣaṇaṃ tathā tasya yadyamīmāṃsitaṃ bhavet।
evamācamanaṃ tasya vedā yajñāstapāṃsi ca ॥ 2.17.44 ॥
dānāni brahmacaryañca bhavanti saphalāstathā।
kriyāṃ yaḥ kurute mohādanācamyaiva nāstikaḥ ॥ 2.17.45 ॥
bhavanti ca vṛthā tasya kriyā hyetā na saṃśayaḥ।
medhyānyetāni jñeyāni duṣṭamebhyo viparyayaḥ।
na vaktavyaḥ sadā vipraḥ kṣudhito nāsti kiñcana ॥ 2.17.47 ॥
ekāntaśīlaṃ hrīmantaṃ sadā śrāddheṣu bhojayet ।
api jātiśataṃ gatvā na sa mucyeta kilbiṣāt।
viṣamaṃ bhojayedviprānekapaṃktyā ca yo naraḥ ॥ 2.17.50 ॥
pāpena gṛhyate kṣipramiṣṭāpūrttaṃ ca naśyati ॥ 2.17.51 ॥
yatistu sarvvaviprāṇāṃ sarvveṣāmagrya utsave।
trivedo'nantarastasya dvivedastadanantaraḥ ॥ 2.17.53 ॥
ya ete pūrvvanirddiṣṭāḥ sarvve te hyanupūrvvaśaḥ।
ṣaḍaṅgī vinayī yogī sarvvatantrastathaiva ca ॥ 2.17.55 ॥
yāyāvaraśca pañcaite vijñeyāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ ।
aṣṭādaśānāṃ vidyānāmekasmin pārago'pi yaḥ ॥ 2.17.56 ॥
yathāvadvarttamānaśca sarve te paṅktipāvanāḥ।
triṇāciketāstraividyo yaśca dharmmān paṭeddvijaḥ ॥ 2.17.57 ॥
bārhaspatye tathā śāstre pāraṃ yaśca dvijo gataḥ।
sarva te pāvanā viprāḥ paṅktīnāṃ samudāhṛtāḥ ॥ 2.17.58 ॥
āmantritastu yaḥ śrāddhe yoṣitaṃ sevate dvijaḥ।
pitarastasya taṃ māsaṃ tasya retasi śerate ॥ 2.17.59 ॥
tasmādatithaye deyaṃ bhojayedbrahmacāriṇam।
dhyānaniṣṭāya dātavyaṃ sānukrośāya dhārmikam ॥ 2.17.61 ॥
yatiṃ vā vālakhilyān vā bhojayecchrāddhakarmmaṇi।
vānaprasthopakurvvāṇaḥ pūjāmātreṇa toṣitaḥ ॥ 2.17.62 ॥
gṛhasthaṃ bhojayedyastu viśvedevāstu pūjitāḥ।
vānaprasthena ṛṣayo vālakhilyaiḥ purandaraḥ ॥ 2.17.63 ॥
catvāra āśramāḥ pūjyāḥ śrāddhe daive tathaiva ca।
caturāśramabāhyebhyaḥ śrāddhaṃ naiva pradāpayet ॥ 2.17.65 ॥
ayati rmokṣavādī ca ubhau tau paṅktidūṣakau ॥ 2.17.66 ॥
vṛthāmuṇḍāśca jaṭilāḥ sarve kārppaṭikāstathā।
nirghṛṇān bhinnavṛttāṃśca sarvabhakṣān vivarjayet ॥ 2.17.67 ॥
kārukādīnanācārān sarvavedabahiṣkṛtān।
gāyanān devavṛttāṃśca havyakavyeṣu varjayet ॥ 2.17.68 ॥
eteṣu varttate yaśca kṛtsvavarṇaṃ sa gacchati।
yo'śnāti saha śūdreṇa sarve te paṅktidūṣakāḥ ॥ 2.17.70 ॥
vyāpādanaṃ śaktinibarhaṇaṃ kṛṣirvāṇijyakāryyaṃ paśupālanaṃ ca।
ye tu viprāḥ sthitā nityaṃ jñānino dhyāninastathā।
upapātakasaṃyuktāḥ pātakaiśca viśeṣataḥ ॥ 2.17.73 ॥
vede niyogadātāro lobhamohaphalārthinaḥ।
brahmavikrayiṇaścaiva śrāddhakarmmaṇi varjitāḥ ॥ 2.17.74 ॥
na niyogo'sti vedānāṃ yo niyuṅkte sa pāpakṛt।
bhoktā vedaphalādbhraśyeddātā dānaphalāttathā ॥ 2.17.75 ॥
bhṛto'dhyāpayate yastu bhṛtakādhyāpitastu yaḥ ।
nārhatastāvapi śrāddhaṃ brahmaṇaḥ kriyavikrayī ॥ 2.17.76 ॥
vṛttireṣā tu vaiśyasya brāhmaṇasya tu pātakam ॥ 2.17.77 ॥
ubhau tau nārhataḥ śrāddhaṃ putrikāpatireva ca ॥ 2.17.78 ॥
vṛthā dārāṃśca yo gacchedyo yajeta vṛthādhvare।
nārhatastāvapi śrāddhaṃ dvijo yaścaiva nāstikaḥ ॥ 2.17.79 ॥
striyo naktaṃparā yeṣāṃ paradāraratāśca ye।
arthakāma ratāścaiva na tān śrāddheṣu bhojayet ॥ 2.17.81 ॥
varṇāśramāṇāṃ dharmmeṣu viruddhāḥ śrāddhakarmmaṇi।
stenaśca sarvayājī ca sarve te paṅktidūṣakāḥ ॥ 2.17.82 ॥
yaśca sūkaravadbhuṅkte yaśca pāṇitale dvijaḥ।
na tadaśnanti pitaro yaśca vāmaṃ samaśnute ॥ 2.17.83 ॥
strīśūdrāyānupetāya śrāddhocchiṣṭaṃ na dāpayet।
anyatra dadhisarpirbhyāṃ śiṣye putrāya nānyathā ॥ 2.17.85 ॥
puṣpamūlaphalairvāpi tuṣṭiṃ gacchanti cānnataḥ ॥ 2.17.86 ॥
tāvadaśnanti pitaro yāvadaśnanti vāgyatāḥ ॥ 2.17.87 ॥
dānaṃ pratigraho homo bhojanaṃ balireva ca।
sāṅguṣṭena tathā kāryyaṃ nāsurebhyo yathā bhavet ॥ 2.17.88 ॥
etānyeva ca sarvvāṇi dānādīni viśeṣataḥ।
antarjānvaviśeṣeṇa tadvadācamanaṃ bhavet ॥ 2.17.89 ॥
muṇḍāñjaṭilakāṣāyān śrāddhakāle'pi varjjayet।
ye tu vrate sthitā nityaṃ jñānino dhyāninastathā।
devabhaktā mahātmānaḥ punīyurdarśanādapi ॥ 2.17.91 ॥
sarvvaṃ yogeśvarairvyāptaṃ trailokyaṃ vai nirantaram ।
tasmāt paśyanti te sarve yatkiñcijjagatīgatam ॥ 2.17.92 ॥
vyaktāvyaktaṃ vaśīkṛtya sarvvasyāpi ca yatparam।
sarvvajñānāni dṛṣṭāni mokṣādīni mahātmanām।
ṛco hi yo veda sa veda vedān yajūṃṣi yo veda sa veda yajñam।
sāmāni yo veda sa veda brahma yo mānasaṃ veda sa veda sarvvam ॥ 2.17.95 ॥
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte śrāddhakalpe brāhmaṇaparīkṣā nāma saptadaśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 17 ।। *
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dānāni ca phalāni ca।
tāraṇaṃ sarvvabhūtānāṃ svargamārgaṃ sukhāvaham ॥ 2.18.1 ॥
loke śreṣṭhatamaṃ svargyamātman ścāpi yat priyam।
sarvvaṃ pitṝṇāṃ dātavyaṃ teṣāmevākṣayārthinā ॥ 2.18.2 ॥
jāmbūnadamayaṃ divyaṃ vimānaṃ sūryyasannibham।
divyāpsarobhiḥ saṅkīrṇamannado labhate phalam ॥ 2.18.3 ॥
ācchādanantu yo dadyādāhataṃ śrāddhakarmmaṇi।
āyuḥ prakāmamaiśvaryyaṃ rūpañca labhate sutam ॥ 2.18.4 ॥
upavītantu yo dadyācchrāddhakāleṣu dharmavit ।
pānañca sarvaviprāṇāṃ brahmadānasya yat phalam ॥ 2.18.5 ॥
kṛtaṃ vipreṣu yo dadyāchrāddhakāle kamaṇḍalum।
madhukṣīrasravā dhenurdātāramupatiṣṭhati ॥ 2.18.6 ॥
cakrāviddhaṃ tu yo dadyācchrāddhakāle kamaṇḍalum।
dhenuṃ sa labhate divyāṃ payodāṃ kāmyadohinīm ॥ 2.18.7 ॥
prāsādo hyuttamo bhūtvā gacchantamanugacchati ॥ 2.18.8 ॥
bhavanaṃ ratnasampūrṇaṃ saśayyāsanabhojanam।
śrāddhe dattvā yatibhyastu nākapṛṣṭe sa modate ॥ 2.18.9 ॥
muktā vaiḍhūryyavāsāṃsi ratnāni vividhāni ca।
vāhanāni ca divyāni ayutānyarbbudāni ca ॥ 2.18.10 ॥
sumahajjvalanaprakhyaṃ ratnakāmasamanvitam ।
sūryyacandra prabhaṃ divyaṃ vimānaṃ labhate'kṣayam ॥ 2.18.11 ॥
apsarobhiḥ parivṛtaṃ kāmagaṃ tu manojavam।
vasate sa vimānāgre stūyamānaḥ samantataḥ ॥ 2.18.12 ॥
lakṣaṇāni suvarṇāni śrāddhe pātrāṇi dāpayet।
rasāstamupatiṣṭhanti gavāṃ puṣṭistathaiva ca ॥ 2.18.19 ॥
pātraṃ vai taijasaṃ dadyānmanojñaṃ śrāddhabhojane।
pātraṃ bhavati kāmānāṃ rūpasya ca dhanasya ca ॥ 2.18.20 ॥
rājataṃ kāñcanaṃ vāpi dadyācchrāddhe tu karmmaṇi।
dhenuṃ śrāddhe tu yo dadyāt vṛṣṭi kumbhopadohanām।
gāvastamupatiṣṭhanti gavāṃ puṣṭistathaiva ca ॥ 2.18.22 ॥
indhanāni tu yo dadyāddvijebhyaḥ śiśi rāgame ॥ 2.18.23 ॥
nityaṃ jayati saṃgrāme śriyā yuktaścadīpyate।
surabhīṇi ca mālyāni gandhavanti tathaiva ca ॥ 2.18.24 ॥
pūjayitvā tu pātrāṇi śrāddhe satkṛtya dāpayet।
gandhavāhā mahānadyaḥ sukhāni vividhāni ca ॥ 2.18.25 ॥
dātāramupatiṣṭhanti yuvatyaśca manoramāḥ।
śayanāsanāni ramyāṇi bhūmayo vāhanāni ca ॥ 2.18.26 ॥
śrāddhe'pyetāni yo dadyādaśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet।
sarpiṣpūrṇāni pātrāṇi śrāddhe satkṛtya dāpayet ॥ 2.18.28 ॥
śrāddhe yathepsitaṃ dattvā puṇḍarīkasya yatphalam।
vanaṃ puṣpaphalopetaṃ dattvā saurabhamaśnute।
kūpārāmataḍāgāni kṣetraghoṣagṛhāṇi ca ॥ 2.18.31 ॥
dattvaitān modate svarge nityamācandratārakam।
āstīrṇaśayanaṃ dattvā śrāddhe ratnavibhūṣitam ॥ 2.18.32 ॥
pitarastasya tuṣyanti svargaṃ cānantyamaśnute।
rājabhiḥ pūjyate cāpi dhanadhānyaiśca varddhate ॥ 2.18.33 ॥
ajinaṃ kāñcanaṃ paṭṭaṃ praveṇī mṛgalomakam ॥ 2.18.34 ॥
prāpnoti śraddadhānastu vājapeyaśataṃ phalam ॥ 2.18.35 ॥
vaśe tiṣṭhanti bhūtāni asmiँlloke tvanāmayam ॥ 2.18.36 ॥
kauśeyaṃ kṣaumakārpāsaṃ dukūlasahitaṃ tathā।
śrāddheṣvetāni yo dadyāt kāmānāpnoti puṣkalān ॥ 2.18.37 ॥
bhrājate sa vimānāgre nakṣatreṣviva candramāḥ ॥ 2.18.38 ॥
vāso hi sarvadaivatyaṃ sarvadevaistvabhiṣṭutam।
vastrābhāve kriyā nāsti yajñā vedāstapāṃsi ca ॥ 2.18.39 ॥
tasmādvastrāṇi deyāni śrāddhakāle viśeṣataḥ।
nityaṃ śrāddheṣu yo dadyāt prayatastatparāyaṇaḥ ।
sarvān kāmānavāpnoti sarvaṃ rājyaṃ tathaiva ca ॥ 2.18.41 ॥
sarvakāmasamṛddhasya yajñasya phalamaśnute।
dadhi gavyamasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ bhakṣyā nānāvidhāstathā।
tadannaṃ śocati śrāddhe varṣāsu ca maghāsu ca ॥ 2.18.44 ॥
ghṛtena bhojayedviprān ghṛtaṃ bhūmau samutsṛjet।
gayāyāṃ hastinaścaiva dattvā śrāddhe na śocati ॥ 2.18.45 ॥
odanaṃ pāyasaṃ sarpirmadhumūlaphalāni ca।
bhakṣyāṃśca vividhāndattvā pretya ceha ca modate ॥ 2.18.46 ॥
śarkarākṣīrasaṃyuktaṃ pṛthukaṃ nityamakṣayam।
saktulājāstathā pūpāḥ kulmāṣavyañjanaistathā।
sārpeḥsnigdhāni hṛdyāni dadhnā saktūṃstu bhojayet।
śrāddheṣvetāni yo dadyāt pajhāni labhate nidhim ॥ 2.18.48 ॥
navasasyāni yo dadyācchrāddhe satkṛtya yatnataḥ।
sarvabhogānavāpnoti pūjyate ca divaṃ gataḥ ॥ 2.18.49 ॥
bhakṣyabhojyāni coṣyāṇi peyalehyavarāṇi ca।
vaiśvadevaṃ ca saumyaṃ ca khāḍgamāṃsaṃ paraṃ haviḥ।
viṣāṇaṃ varjjayet khāḍgamasūyāṃ nāśayāmahe ॥ 2.18.51 ॥
bhojane'grāsanaṃ dadyādatithibhyaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ ।
sarvayajñakriyāṇāṃ sa phalaṃ prāpnotyanuttamam ॥ 2.18.52 ॥
kṣipramatyuṣṇa makliṣṭaṃ dadyāccānnaṃ bubhukṣate।
vayañjanaṃ ca tathā snigdhaṃ bhaktyā satkṛtya yatnataḥ ॥ 2.18.53 ॥
taruṇādityasaṅkāśaṃ vimānaṃ haṃsavāhanam।
annado labhate tisraḥ kalpakoṭīstathaiva ca ॥ 2.18.54 ॥
jīvadānāt paraṃ dānaṃ na kiñcidiha vidyate।
anne lokāḥ pratiṣṭhanti lokadānasya tatphalam ।
annaṃ prajāpatiḥ sākṣāttena sarvvamidaṃ tatam।
tasmādannasamaṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.18.57 ॥
yāni ratnāni medinyāṃ vāhanāni striyastathā।
kṣipraṃ prāpnoti tat sarvaṃ pitṛbhakto hi mānavaḥ ॥ 2.18.58 ॥
pratiśrayaṃ sadā dadyādatithibhyaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ।
devāste saṃpratīkṣante divyātithyaiḥ sahasraśaḥ ॥ 2.18.59 ॥
sarvāṇyetāni yo dadyāt pṛthivyāmekarāḍ bhavet।
tribhirdvābhyāmathaikena dānena tu sukhī bhavet ॥ 2.18.60 ॥
dānāni paramo dharmmaḥ sadbhiḥ satkṛtya pūjitaḥ।
trailokyasyādhipatyaṃ hi dānādeva vyavasthitam ॥ 2.18.61 ॥
rājā tu labhate rājyamadhanaścottamaṃ dhanam।
kṣīṇāyurlabhate cāyuḥ pitṛbhaktaḥ sadā naraḥ।
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi śrāddhakarmmaṇi pūjitam।
kāmyanaimittikājasraṃ śrāddhakarmmaṇi nityaśaḥ ॥ 2.19.1 ॥
putra dāradhanamūlā aṣṭakāstisra eva ca।
prājāpatyā dvitīyā syāt tṛtīyā vaiśvadevikī।
ādyā pūpaiḥsadā kāryā māsairanyā bhavetsadā ॥ 2.19.3 ॥
śākairanyā tṛtīyā syādevaṃ dravyagato vidhiḥ ।
anvaṣṭakā pitṝṇāṃ vai nityameva vidhīyate ॥ 2.19.4 ॥
yadyanyā ca caturthī syāttāñca kuryyādviśeṣataḥ।
tāsu śrāddhaṃ budhaḥ kuryyāt sarvvasvenāpi nityaśaḥ ॥ 2.19.5 ॥
pūjakānāṃ sadotkarṣo nāstikā nāmadho gatiḥ ॥ 2.19.6 ॥
pitaraḥ sarvvakāleṣu tithikāleṣu devatāḥ।
sarvve puruṣamāyānti nipānamiva dhenavaḥ ॥ 2.19.7 ॥
mā sma te pratigaccheyuraṣṭakāḥ surapūjitāḥ ।
devāṃstu dāyino yānti tiryyaggacchantyadāyinaḥ।
prajāṃ puṣṭiṃ smṛtiṃ medhāṃ putrānaiśvaryyameva ca ॥ 2.19.9 ॥
kurvvāṇaḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ ca pūrvvaṃ pūrṇaṃ samaśnute।
pratipaddhanalābhāya labdhaṃ cāsya na naśyati ॥ 2.19.10 ॥
dvitīyāyāṃ tu yaḥ kuryyāddvipadādhipatirbhavet।
varārthinā tṛtīyā tu śatrughnī pāpanāśinī ॥ 2.19.11 ॥
caturthyāṃ kurute śrāddhaṃ śatrośchidrāṇi paśyati।
pañcamyāṃ vai prakurvāṇaḥ prāpnoti mahatīṃ śriyam ॥ 2.19.12 ॥
ṣaṣṭyāṃ śrāddhāni kurvāṇaṃ dvijāstaṃ pūjayantyuta।
kurute yastu saptamyāṃ śrāddhāni satataṃ naraḥ ॥ 2.19.13 ॥
mahāsatramavāpnoti gaṇānāmadhipo bhavet।
sampūrṇāmṛddhimāpnoti yo'ṣṭamyāṃ kurute naraḥ ॥ 2.19.14 ॥
śrāddhaṃ navamyāṃ kurvāṇa aiśvaryyaṃ kāṃkṣitāṃ striyam।
kurvan daśamyāṃ tu naro brāhmīṃ śriyamavāpnuyāt ॥ 2.19.15 ॥
vedāṃścaivāpnuyāt sarvān praṇāśamenasastathā।
ekādaśyāṃ paraṃ dānamaiśvaryyaṃ satataṃ tathā ॥ 2.19.16 ॥
dvādaśyāṃ rāṣṭralābhaṃ tu jayamāhurvasūni ca ।
prajāṃ buddhiṃ paśūn medhāṃ svātantryaṃ puṣṭimuttamām ।
dīrghamāyurathaiśvaryyaṃ kurvāṇastu trayodaśīm ॥ 2.19.17 ॥
śastreṇa tu hatā ye vai teṣāṃ dadyāccaturdaśīm ॥ 2.19.18 ॥
tathā viṣamajātānāṃ yamalānāṃ tu sarvaśaḥ ।
amāvāsyāṃ prayatnena śrāddhaṃ kuryyācchuciḥ sadā ॥ 2.19.19 ॥
sarvvān kāmānavāpnoti svargamānantyamaśnute ।
pratyakṣamarcitāstena bhavanti pitaraḥ sadā ॥ 2.19.24 ॥
pitṝdevā maghā yasmāt tasmāttāsvakṣayaṃ smṛtam।
yamastu yāni śrāddhāni provāca śaśa(śiva)bindave।
tāni me śrṛṇu kārtsnyena nakṣatreṣu pṛthak pṛthak ॥ 2.20.1 ॥
śrāddhaṃ yaḥ kṛttikāyoge karoti satataṃ naraḥ।
apatyakāmo rohiṇyāṃ saumyenaujasvitā bhavet ।
prāyaśaḥ krūrakarmmā tu cārdrāyāṃ śrāddhamācaret ॥ 2.20.3 ॥
kṣetrabhāgī bhavet putrī śrāddhaṃ kurvvan punarvvasau।
tuṣṭikāmaḥ punastiṣye śrāddhaṃ kurvīta mānavaḥ।
āśleṣāsu pitṝnārcya vīrān putrānavāpnuyāt ॥ 2.20.5 ॥
phalgunīṣu pitṝnārcya saubhāgyaṃ labhate naraḥ ॥ 2.20.6 ॥
pradhānaśīlaḥ sāpatya uttarāsu karoti yaḥ।
sa satsu mukhyo bhavati haste yastarpayetpitṝn ॥ 2.20.7 ॥
citrāyāṃ caiva yaḥ kuryāt paśyedrūpavataḥ sutān।
svātinā caiva yaḥ kuryādvidvāँllābhamavāpnuyāt ॥ 2.20.8 ॥
putrārthantu viśākhāsu śrāddhamīheta mānavaḥ।
anurādhāsu kurvvāṇo naraścakraṃ pravarttayet ॥ 2.20.9 ॥
ādhipatyaṃ labhecchraiṣṭyaṃ jyeṣṭāyāṃ satataṃ tu yaḥ।
mūlenārogyamicchanti āṣāḍhāsu mahadyaśaḥ ॥ 2.20.10 ॥
śravaṇāyāṃ sulokeṣu prāpruyāt paramāṃ gatim ॥ 2.20.11 ॥
rājyabhāgvai dhaniṣṭāsu prāpnuyādvipulaṃ dhanam।
nakṣatre vāruṇe kurvvan bhiṣaksiddhimavāpnuyāt।
uttarāsvanatikramya vindedghā vai sahasraśaḥ।
bahurūpakṛtaṃ dravyaṃ vindet kurvvaṃstu revatīm।
imaṃ śrāddhavidhiṃ kurvvañchaśabindurmahīmimām।
kiñciddattaṃ pitṝṇāṃ tu dhinoti vadatāṃ vara ।
kiṃ hi sviccirarātrāya kiñcānantyāya kalpate ॥ 2.21.1 ॥
havīṃṣi śrāddhakāle tu yāni śrāddhavido viduḥ।
tāni me śrṛṇu sarvāṇi phalaṃ caiṣāṃ yathābalam ॥ 2.21.2 ॥
tilairvrīhiyavairmāṣairadbhirmūlaphalena ca।
dattena māsaṃ prīyante śrāddhena tu pitāmahāḥ ॥ 2.21.3 ॥
matsyaiḥ prīṇanti dvau māsau trīnmāsānhāriṇena tu।
śāśantu caturo māsān pañca prīṇāti śākunam ॥ 2.21.4 ॥
vārāheṇa tu ṣaṇmāsāñchāgalaṃ sāptamāsikam।
aṣṭamāsikamityuktaṃ yacca pārṣatakaṃ bhavet ॥ 2.21.5 ॥
rauraveṇa tu prīyante navamāsān pitāmahāḥ।
gavayasya tu māṃsena tṛptiḥ syāddaśamāsikī ॥ 2.21.6 ॥
kūrmasya caiva māṃsena māsānekādaśaiva tu ।
ānantyāya bhavedyuktaṃ khāḍgamāṃsaiḥ pitṛkṣaye।
atra gāthāḥ pitṛgītāḥ kīrttayanti purāvidaḥ।
tāste'haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yathāvatsannibodhata ॥ 2.21.10 ॥
api naḥ svakule jāyādyo'nnaṃ dadyātrtrayodaśīm।
pāyasaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ chāyāyāṃ kuñjarasya tu ॥ 2.21.11 ॥
ājena sarvalohena varṣāsu ca maghāsu ca।
eṣṭavyā bahavaḥ putrā yadyeko'pi gayāṃ vrajet।
gaurīṃ vāpyudvahedbhāryyāṃ nīlaṃ vā vṛṣamutsṛjet ॥ 2.21.12 ॥
gayādīnāṃ phalaṃ tāta prabrūhi samapṛcchataḥ।
pitṝṇāṃ caiva yatpuṇyaṃ nikhilena bravīhi me ॥ 2.21.13 ॥
gayāyāmakṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ japahomatapāṃsi ca।
pitṛṅayāhe te putra tasmāttatrākṣayaṃ smṛtam ॥ 2.21.14 ॥
punīyādekaviṃśantu gauryāmutpāditaḥ sutaḥ।
phalaṃ vṛṣasya vakṣyāmi gadato me nibodhata।
vṛṣotsraṣṭā punātyeva daśātītān daśāvarān ॥ 2.21.16 ॥
yatkiñcit spṛśyate toyairuttīrṇena jalānmahīm।
vṛṣotsarge pitṝṇāṃ tu hyakṣayaṃ sa mudāhṛtam ॥ 2.21.17 ॥
yadyaddhi saṃspṛśettoyaṃ lāṃgūlādibhirantataḥ।
sarvaṃ tadakṣayaṃ tasya pitṝṇāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.21.18 ॥
śrṛṅgaiḥ khurairvā yadbhūmimillikhatya niśaṃ vṛṣaḥ।
madhukulyāḥ pitṝṃstasya akṣayāstā bhavanti vai ॥ 2.21.19 ॥
sahasranalvamātreṇa taḍāgena yathā śrutiḥ।
yo dadāti guḍhairmiśrāṃstilān vai śrāddhakarmaṇi।
na brāhmaṇān parīkṣeta sadā deye tu mānavaḥ।
daive karmaṇi pitrye ca śrūyate vai parīkṣaṇam ॥ 2.21.22 ॥
sarvavedavratasnātāḥ paṅktīnāṃ pāvanā dvijāḥ।
ye ca bhāṣya vido mukhyā ye ca vyākaraṇe ratāḥ ॥ 2.21.23 ॥
adhīyate purāṇaṃ ca dharmmaśāstraṃ tathaiva ca।
triṇāciketapañcāgnistrisuparṇaḥ ṣaḍaṅgavit ॥ 2.21.24 ॥
brahmadeya sutaścaiva chandogo jyeṣṭhasāmagaḥ।
mukhyeṣu yeṣu satreṣu bhavantyavabhṛthaśrutāḥ।
ye ca sadyovratā nityaṃ svakarmaniratāśca ye ॥ 2.21.26 ॥
akrodhanāḥ śāntiparāstān vai śrāddhe nimantrayet।
eteṣu dattamakṣayyamete vai paṅktipāvanāḥ।
trayo'pi pūjitāstena brahmaviṣṇu maheśvarāḥ ॥ 2.21.29 ॥
pitṛbhiḥ saha lokāśca yo hyetān pūjayennaraḥ।
pavitrāṇā pavitrañca maṅgalānāṃ ca maṅgalam ॥ 2.21.30 ॥
prathamaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ yogadharmo nigadyate ।
apāṅkteyāṃstu vakṣyāmi gadato me nibodhata ॥ 2.21.31 ॥
kitavo madyapo yakṣmī paśupālo nirākṛtiḥ।
grāmapreṣyo vārddhuṣiko gāyano vaṇijastathā ॥ 2.21.32 ॥
agāradāhī garadaḥ kuṇḍāśī somavikrayī।
pitrā vivadamānaśca yasya copapatirgṛhe।
abhiśastastathā stenaḥ śilpairyaścopajīvati ॥ 2.21.34 ॥
gaṇayācanakaścaiva nāstiko vedavarjitaḥ ॥ 2.21.35 ॥
naṣṭaṃ syānnāstike dattaṃ kṛtaghne caiva śaṃsake ॥ 2.21.37 ॥
yacca vāṇijake caiva neha nāmutra tadbhavet।
tathā vāṇijake caiva kāruke dharmmavarjite।
bhasma nīva hutaṃ havyaṃ dattaṃ paunarbhave dvije ॥ 2.21.40 ॥
ṣaṣṭiṃ kāṇaḥ śataṃ ṣaṇḍaḥ śvitrī yāvat prapaśyati।
pāparogī sahasrasya dāturnāśayate phalam ॥ 2.21.41 ॥
bhraśyate satphalāttasmāddātā yasya tu bāliśaḥ।
yo veṣṭitaśirā bhuṅkte yo bhuṅkte dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ॥ 2.21.42 ॥
sopānatkaśca yo bhuṅkte yacca dadyāttiraskṛtam ।
sarvaṃ tadasurendrāṇāṃ brahmā bhāgamakalpayat ॥ 2.21.43 ॥
tasmātparivṛtiṃ dadyāttilaiścānvavakīrayan ॥ 2.21.44 ॥
rākṣasānāṃ tilāḥ proktāḥ śunāṃ parivṛtistathā।
darśanātsūkaro hanti pakṣapātena kukkuṭaḥ ॥ 2.21.45 ॥
rajasvalānusparśena kruddho yaśca prayacchati।
nadītīreṣu ramyeṣu saritsu ca sarassu ca।
vivikteṣu ca prīyante datteneha pitāmahāḥ ॥ 2.21.47 ॥
na cāśruṃ pātayejjātu na yukto vācamīrayet।
pitṝṇāṃ nirvvapedbhūmau śūrpe vā darbhasaṃstare ॥ 2.21.50 ॥
kṛṣṇapakṣe'parāhne tu rauhiṇaṃ na vilaṅghayet ॥ 2.21.51 ॥
evamete mahātmāno mahā yogā mahaujasaḥ।
sadā vai pitaraḥ pūjyā draṣṭāro deśakālayoḥ ॥ 2.21.52 ॥
dhyānena mokṣaṃ gacchanti hitvā karma śubhāśubham ॥ 2.21.53 ॥
yajñahetoryaduddhṛtya mohayitvā jagattadā।
guhāyāṃ nihataṃ yogaṃ kaśyapena mahātmanā ॥ 2.21.54 ॥
amṛtaṃ guhyamṛddhṛtya yogaṃ yogavidāṃ vara।
devānāṃ paramaṃ guhyamṛṣīṇāṃ ca parāyaṇam।
prayatnātprāpnuyāttatra sarvameva na saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.21.57 ॥
yasmai śrāddhāni deyāni yacca dattaṃ mahāphalam।
yeṣu vāpyakṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ tīrthaṣu ca nadīṣu ca ।
yeṣu ca svargamāpnoti tatte proktaṃ sasaṃgraham ॥ 2.21.58 ॥
sa majjennarake ghore nāstikastamasāvṛtaḥ ॥ 2.21.59 ॥
parivādo na karttavyo yogināṃ ca viśeṣataḥ।
parivādāt kṛmirbhūtvā tatraiva parivarttate ॥ 2.21.62 ॥
sa gacchennarakaṃ ghoraṃ śrotā yaśca na saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.21.63 ॥
āvṛtaṃ tamasā sarvaṃ narakaṃ ghoradarśanam।
yogīśvaraparī vādānniścayaṃ yāti mānavaḥ ॥ 2.21.64 ॥
yogeśvarāṇāmākrośaṃ śrṛṇuyādyo yatātmanām।
sa hi kālaṃ ciraṃ majjet kumbhīpāke na saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.21.65 ॥
manasā karmaṇā vācā dveṣaṃ yogiṣu varjjayet।
pretyānyaṃ tatphalaṃ bhuṅkte iha caiva na saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.21.66 ॥
na pārago vindati pāramātmanastrilokamadhye carati svakarmabhiḥ।
ṛco yajuḥsāmatadaṅgapārago vikārameva hyanavāpya sīdati ॥ 2.21.67 ॥
vikārapāraḥ prakṛteśca pāragastrayī guṇānāṃ triguṇāntapāragā।
kṛtsnaṃ yathā tattvavisargamātmanastathaiva bhūyaḥ pralayaṃ sadātmanaḥ।
pratyāharedyogabalena yogavit sa sarvapārakramayānagocaraḥ ॥ 2.21.69 ॥
vedasya veditā yo vai vedyaṃ vindati yogavit।
taṃ vai vedavidaṃ prāhustaṃ prāhurvedapāragam ॥ 2.21.70 ॥
vedyaṃ ca veditavyaṃ ca viditvā vai yathāvidhi।
yajñān vedāṃstathā kāmāñjñānāni vividhāni ca।
prāpnotyāyuḥ prajāścaiva pitṛbhakto dhanāni ca ॥ 2.21.72 ॥
śrāddhe yaḥ śrāddhakalpaṃ vai paścimaṃ niyataṃ paṭet।
sarvāpyetānyavāpnoti tīrthe dānaphalāni ca ॥ 2.21.73 ॥
sa paṅktipāvanaścaiva dvijānāmagrabhug bhavet।
anasūyo jitakrodho lobhamohavivarjitaḥ ॥ 2.21.75 ॥
tīrthānāṃ ca phalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ dānādīnāṃ tathaiva ca।
iha cāpi parā tuṣṭistasmātkurvīta yatnataḥ ॥ 2.21.76 ॥
imaṃ vidhiṃ yo hi paṭedatandritaḥ samāhitaḥ saṃsadi parvasandhiṣu ।
apatyabhāgbhavati pareṇa tejasā divau kasāṃ sa vrajate salokatām ॥ 2.21.77 ॥
yena proktastvayaṃ kalpo namastasmai svayambhuve।
mahāyogeśvarebhyaśca sadā ca praṇato hyaham ॥ 2.21.78 ॥
ityetepitara stāta devānāmapi devatāḥ।
saptasveteṣu te nityaṃ sthāneṣu pitaro'vyathāḥ ॥ 2.21.79 ॥
prajāpatisutā hyete sarve caiva mahātmanaḥ।
ādyo gaṇastu yogānāṃ sa nityo yogavarddhanaḥ ॥ 2.21.80 ॥
dvitīyo devatānāṃ tu tṛtīyo devatā'riṇām।
śeṣāstu varṇināṃ jñeyā iti sarve prakīrtitāḥ ॥ 2.21.81 ॥
devāstvetān yajante vai sarveṣveteṣvavasthitāḥ।
āśramāstu yajantyetāṃścatvārastu yathākramam ॥ 2.21.82 ॥
varṇāścāpi yajantyetāṃścatvārastu yathāvidhi।
tathā saṅkarajātāśca mlecchāścaiva yajanti vai ॥ 2.21.83 ॥
pitṝṃśca yo yajedbhaktyā pitaraḥ pūjayanti tam।
pitaraḥ puṣṭikāmasya prajākāmasya vā punaḥ।
puṣṭiṃ prajāśca svargaṃ ca prayacchanti pitāmahāḥ ॥ 2.21.84 ॥
devakāryādapi sūnoḥ pitṛkāryaṃ viśiṣyate।
devatānāṃ hi pitaraḥ pūrvamāpyāyanaṃ svayam ॥ 2.21.85 ॥
na hi yogagatiḥ sūkṣmā pitṝṇāṃ ca parā gatiḥ।
tapasā viprakṛṣṭena dṛśyate māṃsacakṣuṣā ॥ 2.21.86 ॥
sarveṣāṃ rājataṃ pātramathavā rajatānvitam।
pāvanaṃ hyuttamaṃ proktaṃ devānāṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha ॥ 2.21.87 ॥
yeṣāṃ dāsyanti piṇḍāṃstrīn bāndhavā nāmagotrataḥ।
bhūmau kuśottarāyāñca apasavyavidhānataḥ ॥ 2.21.88 ॥
sarvatra varttamānāste piṇḍāḥ prīṇanti vai pitṝn।
yadāhāro bhavejjanturāhāraḥ so'sya jāyate ॥ 2.21.89 ॥
yathā goṣṭe pranaṣṭāṃ vai vatso vindati mātaram ।
tathā taṃ nayate mantro janturyatrāvatiṣṭhate ॥ 2.21.90 ॥
māna gotraṃ ca mantraśca dattamannaṃ nayanti tam।
api yoniśataṃ prāptāṃ stṛptistānanugacchati ॥ 2.21.91 ॥
evameṣā sthitā saṃsthā brahmaṇā parameṣṭinā ।
pitṝṇāmādisargastu lokānāmakṣayārthinām ॥ 2.21.92 ॥
ityete pitaro devā devāśca pitaraḥ punaḥ।
dauhitrā yajamānāśca proktāścaiva mayā'naghāḥ ॥ 2.21.93 ॥
lokā duhitaraścaiva dauhitrāśca sutāstathā।
dānāni saha śaucena tīrthāni ca phalāni ca ॥ 2.21.94 ॥
akṣayatvaṃ dvijāścaiva yāyāvaravidhistathā ।
satre vai vitate pūrvaṃ tadā varṣasahasrike ।
ślokāścātra purā gītā ṛṣibhirbrahmavādibhiḥ ॥ 2.21.98 ॥
dīkṣitasya tadā satre brahmaṇaḥ paramātmanaḥ।
tatraiva jātamatyugraṃ pitṝṇāmakṣayārthinā।
lokānāṃ ca hitārthāya brahmaṇā parameṣṭinā ॥ 2.21.99 ॥
evaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ pūrvaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ putrtreṇa dhīmatā।
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi varuṇasya nibodhata ॥ 2.21.100 ॥
ṛṣayaścaivamuktāstu paraṃ harṣamupāgatāḥ।
paraṃ śuśrūṣavo bhūyaḥ papracchustadanantaram ॥ 2.22.1 ॥
vaṃśānāmānupūrvyeṇa rājñāñcāmitatejasām।
sthitiñcaiṣāṃ prabhāvañca brūhi naḥ paripṛcchatām ॥ 2.22.2 ॥
evamuktastataḥ sūtastathā'sau lomaharṣaṇaḥ।
śuśrūṣāmuttarākhyāne ṛṣīṇāṃ vākyakovidaḥ ॥ 2.22.3 ॥
ākhyānakuśalo bhūyaḥ paraṃ vākyamuvāca ha ।
bruvato me nibodhasva ṛṣirāha yathā mama ॥ 2.22.4 ॥
vaṃśānāmānupūrvyeṇa rājñāñcāmitatejasām।
sthitiṃ caiṣāṃ prabhāvañca bruvato me nibedhata ॥ 2.22.5 ॥
varuṇasya patnī sāmudrī śunodevītyudāhṛtā ।
tasyāḥ putrau kalirvaidyaḥ sutā ca surasundarī ॥ 2.22.6 ॥
kali putrau mahāvīryau jayaśca vijayaśca ha।
vaidyaputrau ghṛṇiścaiva muniścaiva mahābalau ॥ 2.22.7 ॥
prajānāmattukāmānāmanyonyasya prabhakṣiṇau।
bhakṣayitvā tāvanyonyaṃ vināśaṃ samavāpatuḥ ॥ 2.22.8 ॥
kaliḥ surāyāṃ sañjajñe tasya putro madaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
tvāṣṭrī hiṃsā kalerbhāryyā jyeṣṭā yā nikṛtiḥ smṛtā ॥ 2.22.9 ॥
asūtānyān kaleḥ putrāṃścaturaḥ puruṣādakān।
nākaṃ vighnaṃ ca vikhyātaṃ sadramaṃ vidhamantathā ॥ 2.22.10 ॥
aśiraskastayorvighno nākaścaivāśarīravān।
sadramaścaika hasto'bhūdvidhamaścaikapātsmṛtaḥ ॥ 2.22.11 ॥
sadramasya tathā patnī tāmasī pūtanā smṛtā ।
revatī vidhamasyāpi tayoḥ putrāḥ sahasraśaḥ ॥ 2.22.12 ॥
nākasya śakuniḥ patnī vighnasya ca ayomukhī।
rākṣasāstu mahāśīrṣāḥ sandhyādvayavicāriṇaḥ ॥ 2.22.13 ॥
revatīpūtanāputrā naiṛtā nāmataḥ smṛtāḥ।
grahāste rākṣasāḥ sarve bālānāntu viśeṣataḥ।
skandasteṣāmadhipatirbrahmaṇo'numate prabhuḥ ॥ 2.22.14 ॥
bṛhaspateryā bhaginī varastrī brahmacāriṇī।
yogasiddhā jagatkṛtsnamasaktā carate sadā ॥ 2.22.15 ॥
prabhāsasya tu sā bhāryā vasūnāmaṣṭamasya tu।
viśvakarmā sutastasyā jātaḥ śilpiprajāpatiḥ ॥ 2.22.16 ॥
tvaṣṭā virājo rūpāṇāṃ dharmmapautra udāradhīḥ।
karttā śilpasahasrāṇāṃ tridaśānāñca vāstukṛt ॥ 2.22.17 ॥
yaḥ sarveṣāṃ vimānāni devatānāñcakāra ha।
mānuṣāścopajīvanti yasya śilpaṃ mahātmanaḥ ॥ 2.22.18 ॥
virocanasya bhaginī mātā triśirasastu sā ॥ 2.22.19 ॥
devācāryasya mahato viśvakarmasya dhīmataḥ।
viśvakarmātmajaścaiva viśvakarmamayaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.22.20 ॥
sureṇuriti vikhyātā svasā tasya yavīyasī।
tvāṣṭrī sā saviturbhāryyā punaḥ saṃjñeti viśrutā ॥ 2.22.21 ॥
sā tu gatvā kurūn devī vaḍavārūpadhāriṇī।
savituścāśvarūpasya nāsikābhyāṃ tu tau smṛtau ॥ 2.22.23 ॥
asūta sā mahābhāgā tvantarikṣe'śvinau kila।
nāsatyañcaiva dasrañca mārttaṇḍasyātmajāvubhau ॥ 2.22.24 ॥
kasmānmārttaṇḍa ityeṣa vivasvānucyate budhaiḥ।
kimarthaṃ sā'śvarūpā vai nāsikābhyāmasūyata।
etadveditumicchāmastattvaṃ vibrūhi pṛcchatām ॥ 2.22.25 ॥
cirotpannamatirbhinnamaṇḍaṃ tvaṣṭrā vidāritam।
aṇḍe dvidhākṛte tvaṇḍaṃ dṛṣṭvā tvaṣṭāramabravīt।
naitadaṇḍaṃ bhavānnūnaṃ mārttaṇḍastvaṃ bhavānagha ॥ 2.22.27 ॥
na khalvayaṃ mṛto'ṇḍe ca iti snehāt pitā'bravīt।
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā nāmānvarthamudāharat ॥ 2.22.28 ॥
yanmārttaṇḍo bhavetyuktaḥ pitrā'ṇḍe vai dvidhā kṛte।
tasmādvivasvānmārttaṇḍaḥ purāṇajñairvibhāṣyate ॥ 2.22.29 ॥
tataḥ prajāḥ pravakṣyāmi mārttaṇḍasya vivasvataḥ।
śanaiścaraśca saptaite mārttaṇḍasyātmajāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.22.31 ॥
vivasvān kaśyapājjajñe dākṣāyaṇyāṃ mahāyaśāḥ।
sureṇuriti vikhyātā punaḥ saṃjñeti viśrutā ॥ 2.22.32 ॥
sā tu bhāryā bhagavato mārttaṇḍasyātitejasaḥ।
na khalvayaṃ mṛto hyaṇḍe iti snehāttamabravīt ।
ajñānaḥ kaśyapaḥ snehānmārttaṇḍa iti cocyate ॥ 2.22.35 ॥
tejastvabhyadhikaṃ tasya nityameva vivasvataḥ।
yenāpi tāpayāmāsa trīlloँkān kaśyapātmajaḥ ॥ 2.22.36 ॥
trīṇyapatyāni saṃjñāyāṃ janayāmāsa vai raviḥ ।
dvau sutau tu mahāvīryau kanyāṃ kālindimeva ca ॥ 2.22.37 ॥
manurvivasvato jyeṣṭhaḥ śrāddhadevaḥ prajāpatiḥ।
tato yamo yamī caiva yamajau saṃbabhūvatuḥ ॥ 2.22.38 ॥
śāntavarṇantu tadrūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃjñā vivasvataḥ।
asahantī svakāṃ jāyāṃ savarṇāṃ nirmame punaḥ ॥ 2.22.39 ॥
mahīmayī tu sā nārī tasyāśchāyāsamudgatā।
prāñjaliḥ prayatā bhūtvā punaḥ saṃjñāmabhāṣata ॥ 2.22.40 ॥
vadasva kiṃ mayā kāryaṃ sā saṃjñā tāmathābravīt।
ahaṃ yāsyāmi bhadrante svameva bhavanaṃ pituḥ ॥ 2.22.41 ॥
tvayeha bhavane mahyaṃ vastavyaṃ nirviśaṅkayā।
imau ca bālakau mahyaṃ kanyā ca varavarṇinī ॥ 2.22.42 ॥
bhartre vai naivamākhyeyamidaṃ bhagavate tvayā।
tvaṣṭuḥ samīpamagamadvrīḍiteva tapasvinī ॥ 2.22.45 ॥
pitā tāmāgatāṃ dṛṣṭvā kruddhaḥ saṃjñāmathābravīt।
bhartuḥ samīpaṃ gaccha tvaṃ niyuktā ca punaḥ punaḥ।
agamadvaḍavā bhūtvācchādya rūpamaninditā।
uttarān sā kurūn gatvā tṛṇānyatha cacāra sā ॥ 2.22.48 ॥
dvitīyāyāntu saṃjñāyāṃ saṃjñeyamiti cintyatām।
ādityo janayāmāsa putrāvādityavarcasau ॥ 2.22.49 ॥
pūrvajasya manostulyau sādṛśyena tu tau prabhū ।
śrutaśravā manuḥ so'pi sāvarṇirvaibhaviṣyati।
śrutakarmmā tu vijñeyo graho vai yaḥ śanaiścaraḥ ॥ 2.22.51 ॥
saṃjñā tu pārthivī sā vai svasya putrasya vai tadā ॥ 2.22.52 ॥
cakārābhyadhikaṃ snehaṃ na tathā pūrvajeṣu vai।
manustaccākṣamatsarvaṃ yamastadvai na cākṣamat ॥ 2.22.53 ॥
bahuśo yasyamānastu sāpatnyādatiduḥkhitaḥ।
tāṃ vai roṣācca bālyācca bhāvino'rthasya vai balāt ॥ 2.22.54 ॥
sā śaśāva tataḥ krodhāt savarṇā jananī yamam ॥ 2.22.55 ॥
padā tarjayase yasmāt pitṛbhāryāṃ yaśasvinīm।
tasmāttavaiṣa caraṇaḥ patiṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.22.56 ॥
yamastu tena śāpena bhṛśaṃ pīḍitamānasaḥ।
manunā saha dharmmātmā pituḥ sarvvaṃ nyavedayat ॥ 2.22.57 ॥
bhṛśaṃ śāpabhayodvignaḥ saṃjñāvākyairvinirjitaḥ।
bālyādvā yadi vā mohānmāṃ bhavāṃstrātumarhati ॥ 2.22.58 ॥
śapto'hamasmiँllokeśa jananyā tapatāṃ vara।
tava prasādo nastrātuṃ hyetasmānmahato bhayāt ॥ 2.22.59 ॥
vivasvānevamuktastu yamaṃ provāca vai prabhuḥ।
asaṃśayaṃ putra mahadbhaviṣyaṃ tatra kāraṇam ॥ 2.22.60 ॥
yena tvāmāviśatkrodho dharmmajñaṃ satyavādinam।
na śakyametanmithyā tu karttuṃ māturvacastava ॥ 2.22.61 ॥
kṛmayo māṃsamādāya yāsyanti tu mahīṃ tava।
tataḥ pādaṃ mahāprājña punaḥ saṃprāpsyase sukham ॥ 2.22.62 ॥
kṛtamevaṃ vacaḥ satyaṃ mātustava bhaviṣyati।
śāpasya parihāreṇa tvaṃ ca trātā bhaviṣyasi ॥ 2.22.63 ॥
ādityastvabravīt saṃjñāṃ kimarthaṃ tanayeṣu vai।
tulyeṣvapyadhikaḥ sneha ekasmin kriyate tvayā ॥ 2.22.64 ॥
sā tatpariharantī vai nācacakṣe vivasvataḥ।
ātmanā sa samādhāya yogantathyamapaśyata ॥ 2.22.65 ॥
tāṃ śaptukāmo bhagavān nāśāya kupitaḥ prabhuḥ ।
sā tatsarvaṃ yathātattvamācacakṣe vivasvataḥ ॥ 2.22.66 ॥
vivasvānatha tacchrutvā kruddhastvaṣṭāramabhyayāt।
tvaṣṭā tu taṃ yathānyāyamarcayitvā vibhāvasum ॥ 2.22.67 ॥
nirddagdhukāmaṃ roṣeṇa sāntvayāmāsa vai śanaiḥ।
tavātitejasā yuktamidaṃ rūpaṃ na śobhate ॥ 2.22.68 ॥
asahantī tu tat saṃjñā vane carati śādvale।
drakṣyate tāṃ bhavānadya svāṃ bhāryāṃ śubhacāriṇīm ॥ 2.22.69 ॥
ślāghyāṃ yauvanasampannāṃ yogamāsthāya gopate।
anukūlaṃ bhavedevaṃ yadi syāt samayo mataḥ ॥ 2.22.70 ॥
rūpaṃ vivarttayedante ādyaṃ śreṣṭhamarindama।
rūpaṃ vivasvatastvāsīttiryagūrdhvamadhastathā ॥ 2.22.71 ॥
tenāsau vrīḍito devo rūpeṇa tu divaspatiḥ।
anujñātastatastvaṣṭā rūpanirvarttanāya tu।
tato'bhyupagamāttvaṣṭā mārttaṇḍasya vivasvataḥ ॥ 2.22.73 ॥
bhramimāropya tattejaḥ śātayāmāsa tasya vai।
tattu nirbhāsitantejastejasāpahṛtena tu ॥ 2.22.74 ॥
dadarśa yogamāsthāya svāmbhāryāṃ vaḍavāṃ tathā ॥ 2.22.75 ॥
adṛśyāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tejasā niyamena ca।
aśvarūpeṇa mārttaṇḍastāṃ mukhe samabhāvayat ॥ 2.22.76 ॥
maithunāya viceṣṭantī parapuṃsopaśaṅkayā।
devau tasmādajāyetāmaśvinau bhiṣajāṃ varau ।
nāsatyaścaiva dasraśca smṛtau dvāvaśvināviti ॥ 2.22.78 ॥
mārttaṇḍasya sutāvetāvaṣṭamasya prajāpateḥ।
tāntu rūpeṇa kāntena darśayāmāsa bhāskaraḥ ॥ 2.22.79 ॥
sā taṃ dṛṣṭvāttadā bhāryā tutoṣa ca mumoha ca।
yamastu tena śāpena bhṛśampīḍitamānasaḥ ॥ 2.22.80 ॥
dharmmeṇa rañjayāmāsa dharmmarājastatastu saḥ ।
so'labhat karmaṇā tena śubhena paramadyutiḥ ॥ 2.22.81 ॥
pitṝṇāmādhipatyañca lokapālatvameva ca।
manuḥ prajāpatiścaiva sāvarṇiḥ sa mahāyaśāḥ ॥ 2.22.82 ॥
bhāvyasau nāgate tasmin manuḥ sāvarṇike'ntare।
merupṛṣṭe suramye vai adyāpi carate prabhuḥ ॥ 2.22.83 ॥
bhrātā śanaiścarastatra grahatvaṃ sa tu labdhavān।
tvaṣṭā'nu tena rūpeṇa viṣṇoścakramakalpayat।
yavīyasī tayoryā tu yamunā ca yaśasvinī।
abhavat sā saricchreṣṭā yamunā lokabhāvinī ॥ 2.22.85 ॥
yastu jyeṣṭo mahātejāḥ sargo yasya tu sāmpratam।
vistaraṃ tasya vakṣyāmi manorvaivasvatasya ha ॥ 2.22.86 ॥
idaṃ tu janma devānāṃ śrṛṇuyādvā paṭeta vā।
vaivasvatasya putrāṇāṃ saptānāntu mahaujasām।
āpadaṃ prāpya mucyeta prāpnuyācca mahadyaśaḥ ॥ 2.22.87 ॥
tato manvantare'tīte cākṣuṣe daivataiḥ saha।
vaivasvatāya mahate pṛthivīrājyamādiśat ॥ 2.23.1 ॥
tasya vaivasvato vakṣye sāmpratasya mahātmanaḥ।
manoḥ prathamajasyāsan navaputrāstu tatsamāḥ ॥ 2.23.3 ॥
ikṣvākurnahuṣaścaiva dhṛṣṭaḥ śaryātireva ca।
nariṣyantastathā prāṃśu rnābhāgo'riṣṭa eva ca।
karūṣaśca pṛṣadhraśca navaite mānavāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.23.4 ॥
brahmaṇā tu manuḥ pūrvaṃ coditastu nibodhata।
athākarotputrakāmaḥ parāmiṣṭiṃ prajāpatiḥ।
mitrāvaruṇayoraṃśe manurāhutimāvapat ॥ 2.23.6 ॥
tatra divyāmbaradharā divyābharaṇabhūṣitā।
divyasannahanā caiva iḍā jajñe iti śrutiḥ ॥ 2.23.7 ॥
tāmiletyatha hovāca manurddaṇḍadharaḥ smṛtaḥ।
anugacchāmi bhadrante tamilā pratyuvāca ha ॥ 2.23.8 ॥
dharmmayuktamidaṃ vācyaṃ putrakāmaṃ prajāpatim।
mitrāvaruṇayoraṃśe jātāsmi vadatāṃ vara ॥ 2.23.9 ॥
tayoḥ sakaśaṃ yāsyāmi mā no dharmo hato'vadhīt।
saivamuktvā punarddevī tayorantikamāgamat ॥ 2.23.10 ॥
gatvāntikaṃ varārohā prāñjalirvākyamabravīt ।
aṃśe'sminyuvayorjātā devau kiṃ karavāṇi ca ॥ 2.23.11 ॥
manunaivāhamuktāsmi anugacchasva māmiti।
tathā tu vadatīṃ sādhvīmiḍāmāśritya tāvubhau ॥ 2.23.12 ॥
devau ca mitrāvaruṇāvidaṃ vacanamūcatuḥ ।
anena tava dharmajñe praśrayeṇa damena ca ॥ 2.23.13 ॥
satyena caiva suśroṇi prītau svo varavarṇini।
āvayostvaṃ mahābhāge khyātiṃ kanyā prayāsyasi ॥ 2.23.14 ॥
sudyumna iti vikhyātastriṣu lokeṣu pūjitaḥ।
jagatpriyo dharmmaśīlo manorvaṃśa vivarddhanaḥ ॥ 2.23.15 ॥
mānavaḥ sa tu sudyumnaḥ strībhāvamagamat prabhuḥ।
sā tu devī varaṃ labdhvā nivṛttā pitaraṃ prati ॥ 2.23.16 ॥
budhenāntaramāsādya maithunāyopamantritā।
somaputrādbudhāccāsyā ailo jajñe purūravāḥ ॥ 2.23.17 ॥
budhāt sā janayitvā tu sudyumnaṃ punarāgatā।
sudyumnasya ca dāyādāstrayaḥ paramadhārmmikāḥ ॥ 2.23.18 ॥
utkalaśca gayaścaiva vinatāśvastathaiva ca।
utkalasyotkalaṃ rāṣṭraṃ vinatāśvasya paścimam ।
dikṣu vātasya rājarṣergayasya tu gayā purī ॥ 2.23.19 ॥
pravisṛṣṭe manau tasmin prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā divākaraḥ।
daśadhā taddadhat kṣetramakarot pṛthivīmimām ॥ 2.23.20 ॥
kanyābhāvāttu sudyumno nainaṃ bhāgamavāpnuyāt ॥ 2.23.21 ॥
vasiṣṭhavacanāccāsīt pratiṣṭāno mahādyutiḥ।
pratiṣṭā dharmarājasya sudyumnasya mahātmanaḥ ॥ 2.23.22 ॥
mānavaḥ sa tu sudyumnaḥ strībhāvamagamat punaḥ ॥ 2.23.23 ॥
etacchrutvā tu ṛṣayaḥ papracchustadanantaram ।
mānavaḥ sa tu sudyumnaḥ strībhāvamagamat katham ॥ 2.23.24 ॥
provāca vacanaṃ devī priyahetoḥ priyaṃ priyā ।
sa me mamāśrame deva yaḥ pumān saṃpravekṣyati।
bhaviṣyati dhruvaṃ nārī sā tulyāpsarasāṃ śubhā ॥ 2.23.25 ॥
tatra sarvāṇi bhūtāni piśācāḥ paśavaśca ye।
strībhūtāḥ saha rudreṇa krīḍantyapsaraso tathā ॥ 2.23.26 ॥
umāvanaṃ praviṣṭastu sa rājā mṛgayāṃ gataḥ।
saha piśācairbhūtaistu rudraiḥ strībhāvamāsthitaḥ ॥ 2.23.27 ॥
tasmāt sa rājā sudyumnaḥ strībhāvaṃ labdhavān punaḥ ।
mahādevaprasādācca gāṇapatya mavāpnuyāt ॥ 2.23.28 ॥
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte vaivasvatamanoḥ sṛṣṭikathanaṃ nāma trayoviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 23 ।।
nisargaṃ manu putrāṇāṃ vistareṇa nibodhata।
pṛṣadhro hisayitvā tu gurorgāvamabhakṣayat ॥ 2.24.1 ॥
śāpācchūdratvamāpannaścyavanasya mahātmanaḥ।
karūṣasya tu kārūṣaḥ kṣatriyo yuddhadurmadaḥ ॥ 2.24.2 ॥
sahasrakṣatriyagaṇavikrāntaḥ saṃbabhūva ha।
nābhāgāriṣṭaputrastu vidvānāsīdbhalandanaḥ ॥ 2.24.3 ॥
bhalandanasya putro'bhūt prāṃśurnāma mahābalaḥ।
prāṃśoreko'bhavat putraḥ prajāniriti viśrutaḥ ॥ 2.24.4 ॥
saṃvarttena divaṃ nītaḥ sasuhṛt saha bāndhavaiḥ ॥ 2.24.9 ॥
vivādo'tra mahānāsīt saṃvarttasya bṛhaspateḥ।
ṛddhiṃ dṛṣṭvā tu yajñasya kruddhastasya bṛhaspatiḥ ॥ 2.24.10 ॥
saṃparttena hṛte yajñe cukopa subhṛśantadā।
lokānāṃ sa hi nāśaya daivatairhi prasāditaḥ ॥ 2.24.11 ॥
maruttaścakravarttī sa nariṣyantamavāptavān।
nariṣyantasya dāyādo rājā daṇḍadharo damaḥ ॥ 2.24.12 ॥
tasya putrastu vikrānto rājāsīdrāṣṭravarddhanaḥ ।
sudhṛtī tasya putrastu naraḥ sudhṛtinaḥ sutaḥ ॥ 2.24.13 ॥
kevalastasya putrastu bandhumān kevalātmajaḥ।
atha bandhumataḥ putro dharmātmā vegavān nṛpaḥ ॥ 2.24.14 ॥
budho vegavataḥ putra stṛṇabindurbudhātmajaḥ।
tretāyugamukhe rājā tṛtīye saṃbabhūva ha ॥ 2.24.15 ॥
kanyā tu tasya draviḍā mātā viśravaso hi sā।
putraścāsya viśālo'bhūd rājā paramadhārmikaḥ ॥ 2.24.16 ॥
viśālasya suto rājā hemacandro mahābalaḥ ॥ 2.24.17 ॥
sucandra iti vikhyāto hemacandrādanantaram।
sucandratanayo rājā dhūmrāśca iti viśrutaḥ ॥ 2.24.18 ॥
dhūmrāśvatanayo vidvān sṛñjayaḥ samapadyata।
sṛñjayasya sutaḥ śrīmān sahadevaḥ pratāpavān ॥ 2.24.19 ॥
kṛśāśvaḥ sahadevasya putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ।
kṛśāśvasya mahātejāḥ somadattaḥ pratāpavān ॥ 2.24.20 ॥
somadattasya rājarṣeḥ sutobhūjjanamejayaḥ।
janamejayātmajaścaiva pramatirnāma viśrutaḥ ॥ 2.24.21 ॥
tṛṇabinduprasādena sarve vaiśālakā nṛpāḥ ।
dīrghāyuṣo mahātmāno vīryavantaḥ sudhārmikāḥ ॥ 2.24.22 ॥
śaryātermithunaṃ tvāsīdānārto nāma viśrutaḥ।
putraḥ sukanyā kanyā na bhāryāyā cyavanasya tu ॥ 2.24.23 ॥
ānārttasya tu dāyādo revo nāmnā tu vīryavān।
ānartto viṣayo yasya purī cāpi kuśasthalī ॥ 2.24.24 ॥
revasya raivataḥ putraḥ kakujhī nāma dhārmikaḥ।
jyeṣṭo bhrātṛśatasyāsīdrājā prāpya kuśasthalīm ॥ 2.24.25 ॥
kanyayā saha śrutvā ca gandharvaṃ brahmaṇo'ntike।
muhūrttaṃ devadevasya mārtyaṃ bahuyugaṃ vibhoḥ ॥ 2.24.26 ॥
ājagāma yuvā caiva svāṃ purīṃ yādavairvṛtām।
kṛtāṃ dvāravatīṃ nāma bahudvārāṃ manoramām ॥ 2.24.27 ॥
bhojavṛṣṭyandhakairguptāṃ vasudevapurogamaiḥ।
tāṅkathāṃ raivataḥ śrutvā yathātattvamarindamaḥ ॥ 2.24.28 ॥
kanyā tu baladevāya suvratāṃ nāma revatīm।
dattvā jagāma śikharaṃ merostapasi saṃsthitaḥ ॥ 2.24.29 ॥
reme rāmaśca dharmātmā revatyā sahitaḥ kila।
tāṃ kathāmṛṣayaḥ śrutvā papracchustadanantaram ॥ 2.24.30 ॥
kathaṃ bahuyuge kāle vyatīte sūtanandana।
na jarā kṣutpipāsā vā na ca mṛtyubhayaṃ tataḥ।
na ca rogaḥ prabhavati brahmalokagatasya hi ॥ 2.24.34 ॥
gāndharvvaṃ prati yaccāpi pṛṣṭastu munisattamāḥ।
tato'haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yāthātathyena suvratāḥ ॥ 2.24.35 ॥
sapta svarāstrayo grāmā mūrcchanāstvekaviṃśatiḥ।
tālāścaikonapañcāśadityetat svaramaṇḍalam ॥ 2.24.36 ॥
ṣaḍjarṣabhau ca gāndhāro madhyamaḥ pañcamastathā।
dhaivataścāpi vijñeyastathā cāpi niṣādavān ॥ 2.24.37 ॥
sauvīrī madhyamagrāmo hariṇāsyā tathaiva ca।
mdhyamagrāmikīḥ khyātāḥ ṣaḍjagrāmaṃ nibodhata ॥ 2.24.39 ॥
uttaramandrā rajanī tathā yā cottarāyatā।
gāndhāragrāmi kāṃścānyān kīrtyamānān nibodhata।
āgniṣṭomikamādyantu dvitīyaṃ vājapeyikam ॥ 2.24.41 ॥
saptamaṃ gosavaṃ nāma mahāvṛṣṭikamaṣṭamam।
brahmadānañca navamaṃ prājāpatyamanantaram ॥ 2.24.43 ॥
nāgapakṣāśrayaṃ vidyādgotarañca tathaiva ca।
hayakrāntaṃ mṛgakrāntaṃ viṣṇukrāntaṃ manoharam ॥ 2.24.44 ॥
sāvitramarddhasāvitraṃ sarvvato madrameva ca ॥ 2.24.45 ॥
sāgaraṃ vijayañcaiva sarvabhūtamanoharam ॥ 2.24.46 ॥
manoharamadhātryañca gandharvānugataśca yaḥ ॥ 2.24.47 ॥
alambuṣeṣṭaśca tathā nāradapriya eva ca।
kathito bhīmasenena nāgarāṇāṃ yathā priyaḥ ॥ 2.24.48 ॥
karopanīta vinatā śrīrākhyo bhārgavapriyaḥ।
uttarādisvarasyaiva brahmā vai devatā'tra ca।
harideśasamutpannā hariṇāsyā vyajāyata।
manudeśasamutpannā mūrcchanā śuddhamadhyam।
mūrcchanā yojanā hyeṣā rajasā rajanī tataḥ ॥ 2.24.55 ॥
tasmāduttaratālañca prathamaṃ svāyataṃ viduḥ।
apānāduttaratvācca dhaivatasyottarāyaṇaḥ।
syādiyaṃ mūrcchanā hyevaṃ pitaraḥ śrāddhadevatāḥ ॥ 2.24.57 ॥
śuddhaṣaḍjasvaraṃ kṛtvā yasmādagniṃ maharṣayaḥ।
yakṣīṇāṃ mūrcchanā sā tu yākṣikā mūrcchanā smṛtā ॥ 2.24.59 ॥
nāgadṛṣṭirviṣā gītā nopasarpanti mūrcchanām।
nānāsādhāraṇāścaiva ṣaḍevānuvidastathā ॥ 2.24.66 ॥
pūrvvācāryyamataṃ buddhvā pravakṣyāmyanupūrvvaśaḥ।
triṃśataṃ vai alaṅkārāṃstān me nigadataḥ śrṛṇu ॥ 2.25.1 ॥
alaṅkārāstu vaktavyāḥ svaiḥsvairvarṇaiḥ prahetavaḥ।
saṃsthānayogaiśca tathā pādānāṃ cānvavekṣayā ॥ 2.25.2 ॥
vākyārthapadayogārthairalaṅkārasya pūraṇam।
padāni gītakasyāhuḥ purastāt pṛṣṭhato'thavā ॥ 2.25.3 ॥
eteṣu triṣu sthāneṣu pravṛtto vidhiruttamaḥ ॥ 2.25.4 ॥
catvāraḥ prakṛtau varṇāḥ pravicāraścaturvidhaḥ।
vikalpamaṣṭadhā caiva devāḥ ṣoḍaśadhā viduḥ ॥ 2.25.5 ॥
sthāyī varṇaḥ prasaṃcārī tṛtīyamavarohaṇam।
ārohaṇaṃ caturthantu varṇaṃ varṇavido viduḥ ॥ 2.25.6 ॥
tatraikaḥ saṃcarasthāyī sacarāstacarībhavan।
atha rohaṇavarṇānāmavarohaṃ vinirdiśet ॥ 2.25.7 ॥
ārohaṇena cārohavarṇaṃ varṇavido viduḥ।
eteṣāmeva varṇānāmalaṅkārānnibodhata ॥ 2.25.8 ॥
alaṅkārāstu catvāraḥ sthāpanī kramarejinaḥ।
pramādaścāpramādaśca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ॥ 2.25.9 ॥
visvaroṣṭrakalāścaiva sthānādekāntaraṃ gatāḥ।
āvarttasyākramotpattī dve kāryye parimāṇataḥ ॥ 2.25.10 ॥
kumāramaparaṃ vidyādvistaraṃ vamanaṃ gatam।
eṣa vai cāpyapāṅgastu kutārekaḥ kalādhikaḥ ॥ 2.25.11 ॥
tasmiṃścaiva svare vṛddhistiṣṭhate tadvilakṣaṇā ॥ 2.25.12 ॥
śyenastu aparohastu uttaraḥ parikīrttitaḥ।
viparyayasvaro'pi syādyasya durghaṭito'pi na ॥ 2.25.14 ॥
ekāntarā tu vādyantu ṣaḍjataḥ paramaḥ svaraḥ।
ākṣepāskandanaṃ kāryyaṃ kākasyevoccapuṣkalam ॥ 2.25.15 ॥
santārau tau tu sañcāryau kāryaṃ vā kāraṇaṃ tathā।
ākṣiptamavarohyāpi prokṣamadyantathaiva ca ॥ 2.25.16 ॥
dvādaśañca kalāsthānamekāntaragatantataḥ।
preṅkholitamalaṅkāramevaṃ svarasamanvitam ॥ 2.25.17 ॥
prakṣiptameva kalayā pādānītarayorbhavet ॥ 2.25.18 ॥
dvikalaṃ vā yathā bhūtaṃ yattad hrāsitamucyate।
uccārādvisvarārūḍhā tathā cāṣṭasvarāntaram ॥ 2.25.19 ॥
ekāntarahitā hyete tameva svaramantataḥ ॥ 2.25.20 ॥
makṣipracchedano nāma catuṣkalagaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ।
alaṅkārā bhavantyete triṃśadye vai prakīrttitāḥ।
varṇasthānaprayogeṇa kalāmātrā pramāṇataḥ ॥ 2.25.21 ॥
saṃsthānañca pramāṇaṃ ca vikāro lakṣaṇantathā।
caturvidhamidaṃ jñeyamalaṅkāraprayojanam ॥ 2.25.22 ॥
yathātmano hyalaṅkāro viparyasto'tigarhitaḥ।
varṇamevāpyalaṃkarttuṃ viṣamaṃ hyātmasambhavāt ॥ 2.25.23 ॥
nānābharaṇasaṃyogādyathā nāryā vibhūṣaṇam।
varṇasya caivālaṅkāro viparyasto'tigarhitaḥ ॥ 2.25.24 ॥
na pāde kuṇḍale dṛṣṭe na kaṇṭe rasanā yathā।
evameva hyalaṅkāro viparyasto vigarhitaḥ ॥ 2.25.25 ॥
kriyamāṇo'pyalaṅkāro rāgaṃ yaścaiva darśayet।
yathoddiṣṭasya mārgasya karttavyasya vidhīyate ॥ 2.25.26 ॥
yāthātathyena vakṣyāmi māsedbhavamukhodbhave ॥ 2.25.27 ॥
gorūpāṇāṃ purastāttu madhyamāṃśastu paryyayaḥ।
tayorvibhāgo gītānāṃ lāvaṇyamārgasaṃsthitaḥ ॥ 2.25.31 ॥
anuṣaṅgaṃ mayoddiṣṭaṃ svasārañca svarāntaram।
paryyayaḥ saṃpravartteta saptasvarapadakramam ॥ 2.25.32 ॥
pañcamo madhyamaścaiva dhaivate tu niṣādajaiḥ।
ṣaḍjarṣabhaiśca jānīmo mandrakeṣveva nāntare ॥ 2.25.33 ॥
prākṛte vaiṇavaiścaiva gāndhārāṃśe prayujyate ॥ 2.25.34 ॥
gāndhārāṃśena kārtsnyena paryayasya vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।
evañcaiva kramoddiṣṭo madhyamāṃśasya madhyamaḥ ॥ 2.25.35 ॥
yāni gītāni proktāni rūpeṇa tu viśeṣataḥ।
tattu saptasvaraṃ kāryyaṃ saptarūpañca kauśikam ॥ 2.25.36 ॥
aṅgadarśanamityāhurmāne dve samake tathā।
uttare ca prakṛtyevaṃ mātrā tallīyate tathā ।
pādenaikena mātrāyāṃ pādonāmati vīraṇā।
saṃkhyāyāścopahananaṃ tatra yānamiti smṛtam ॥ 2.25.39 ॥
dvitīyaṃ pādabhaṅgañca graheṇābhipratiṣṭitam।
pādabhāgaṃ sapādaṃ tu prakṛtyāmapi saṃsthitam ॥ 2.25.41 ॥
caturthamuttare caiva madravatyāṃ ca madrake।
madrake dakṣiṇasyāpi yathoktā varttate kalā ॥ 2.25.42 ॥
pūrvvamevānuyogantu dvitīyā buddhiriṣyate।
pādau cāharaṇaṃ cāsmat pāraṃ nātra vidhīyate ॥ 2.25.43 ॥
ekatvamupayogasya dvayoryaddhi dvijottama।
anekasamavāyastu patākāhariṇaṃ smṛtam ॥ 2.25.44 ॥
tisṝṇāṃ caiva vṛttīnāṃ vṛttau vṛttā ca dakṣiṇā।
aṣṭau tu samavāyāste sauvīrā mūrcchanā tathā।
kakujhinastu taṃ lokaṃ raivatasya gatasya ha।
hatāḥ puṇyajanaiḥ sarvvā rākṣasaiḥ sā kuśasthalī ॥ 2.26.1 ॥
tadvai bhrātṛśataṃ tasya dhārmmikasya mahātmanaḥ।
nibadhyamānā rakṣobhirdiśaḥ saṃprādravan bhayāt ॥ 2.26.2 ॥
anvavāyastu sumahān mahāṃstatra dvijottamāḥ ॥ 2.26.3 ॥
prayatā iti vikhyātā dikṣu sarvvāsu dhārmmikāḥ।
dhṛṣṭasya dhārṣṭakaṃ kṣatraṃ raṇadhṛṣṭaṃ babhūva ha ॥ 2.26.4 ॥
trisāhasrantu sagaṇaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahātmanām।
nabhagasya ca dāyādo nābhāgo nāma vīryyavān ॥ 2.26.5 ॥
ambarīṣastu nābhāgirvirūpastasya cātmajaḥ।
pṛṣadaśvo virūpasya tasya putro rathītaraḥ ॥ 2.26.6 ॥
ete kṣatraprasūtā vai punaścāṅgirasaḥ smṛtāḥ ।
rathītarāṇāṃ pravarāḥ kṣātropetā dvijātayaḥ ॥ 2.26.7 ॥
kṣuvatastu manoḥ pūrvvamikṣyākurabhiniḥsṛtaḥ ।
tasya putraśataṃ tvāsīdikṣvākorbhūridakṣiṇam ॥ 2.26.8 ॥
teṣāṃ jyeṣṭo vikukṣiśca nemirdaṇḍaśca te trayaḥ।
śakunipramukhāstasya putrāḥ paṃcāśatastu te ॥ 2.26.9 ॥
uttarāpathadeśasya rakṣitāro mahīkṣitaḥ।
catvāriṃśattathāṣṭau ca dakṣiṇasyāñca te diśi ॥ 2.26.10 ॥
viṃśatipramukhāste tu dakṣiṇāpatharakṣiṇaḥ।
ikṣvākustu vikukṣiṃ vai aṣṭakāyāmathādiśet ॥ 2.26.11 ॥
māṃsamānaya śrāddheyaṃ mṛgān hatvā mahābala।
śrāddhamadya nu kartavyamaṣṭakāyāṃ na saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.26.12 ॥
sa gatastu mṛgavyāṃ vai vacanāttasya dhīmataḥ।
mṛgān sahasraśo hatvā pariśrāntaśca vīryyavān।
bhakṣayacchaśakantatra vikukṣirmṛgayāṅgataḥ ॥ 2.26.13 ॥
āgate sa vikukṣau tu samāṃse sahasainike।
vasiṣṭhañcodayāmāsa māṃsaṃ prokṣayatāmiti ॥ 2.26.14 ॥
tatheti codito rājñā vidhivatsamupasthitaḥ।
sa dṛṣṭvopahataṃ māṃsaṃ kruddho rājānamabravīt ॥ 2.26.15 ॥
śūdreṇopahataṃ māṃsaṃ putreṇa tava pārthiva।
śaśabhakṣādabhojyaṃ vai tava māṃsaṃ mahādyute ॥ 2.26.16 ॥
śaśo durātmanā pūrvamaraṇye bhakṣito'nagha।
tena māṃsamidaṃ duṣṭaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nṛpasattama ॥ 2.26.17 ॥
ikṣvākustu tataḥ kruddho vikukṣimidamabravīt।
pitṛkarmmaṇi nirddiṣṭo mayā tvaṃ mṛgayāṅkataḥ।
śaśaṃ bhakṣayase'raṇye nirghṛṇaḥ pūrvvamadya nu ॥ 2.26.18 ॥
tasmātparityajāmi tvāṃ gaccha tvaṃ svena karmmaṇā।
evamikṣvākunā tyakto vasiṣṭhavacanāt sutaḥ ॥ 2.26.19 ॥
ikṣvākau saṃsthite tasmiñchaśī sa pṛthivīmimām ।
prāptaḥ paramadharmmātmā sa cāyodhyādhipo'bhavat ॥ 2.26.20 ॥
tadākarotsa rājyaṃ vai vasiṣṭhaparinoditaḥ।
tataḥ stenena sā pūrṇo rājyāvasthā mahīpateḥ ॥ 2.26.21 ॥
jñātvaivametadākhyānaṃ nā vidhirbhakṣayettu vai ॥ 2.26.22 ॥
māṃ sabhakṣayitāmutra yasya māṃsamihājyaham।
etanmāṃsasya māṃsatvaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ॥ 2.26.23 ॥
śaśādasya tu dāyādaḥ kakutstho nāma vīryyavān।
indrasya vṛṣabhūtasya kakutstho jāyate purā ॥ 2.26.24 ॥
pūrvvamāḍībake yuddhe kakutsthastena sa smṛtaḥ ।
anenāstu kakutsthasya pṛthuromā ca sa smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.26.25 ॥
vṛṣadaśvaḥ pṛthoḥ putrastasmādandhrastu vīryyavān ।
āndhrastu yavanāśvastu śrāvastastasya cātmajaḥ ॥ 2.26.26 ॥
jajñe śrāvastako rājā śrāvastī yena nirmitā।
śrāvastasya tu dāyādo bṛhadaśvo mahāyaśāḥ ॥ 2.26.27 ॥
bṛhadaśvasutaścāpi kubalāśca iti śrutiḥ।
yaḥ sa dhundhuvadhādrājā dhundhumāratvamāgataḥ ॥ 2.26.28 ॥
dhundhuvadhaṃ mahāprājña śrotumicchami vistarāt।
yadarthaṃ kubalāśvaḥ sa dhundhumāratvamāgataḥ ॥ 2.26.29 ॥
bṛhadaśvasya putrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇyekaviṃśatiḥ ।
sarve vidyāsu niṣṇātā balavanto durāsadāḥ ॥ 2.26.30 ॥
babhūvurddhārmikāḥ sarve yajvāno bhūridakṣiṇāḥ।
kubalāśvaṃ mahāvīryaṃ śūramuttamadhārmikam ॥ 2.26.31 ॥
bṛhadaśvo'bhyaṣiñcattaṃ tasmin rāṣṭre narādhipaḥ।
putrasaṃkrāmitaśrīstu vanaṃ rājā viveśa ha ॥ 2.26.32 ॥
bṛhadaśvaṃ mahārājaṃ śūramuttamadhārmmikam ।
prayātaṃ tamuttaṅkastu brahmarṣiḥ pratyavārayat ॥ 2.26.33 ॥
bhavato rakṣaṇaṃ kāryyaṃ tattāvat kartumarhati।
nirudvignastapaḥ kartuṃ na hi śaknomi pārthiva ॥ 2.26.34 ॥
samudro vālukāpūrṇastatra tiṣṭhati bhūpate ॥ 2.26.35 ॥
devatānāmavadhyastu mahākāyo mahābalaḥ।
antarbhūmigatastatra vālukāntarhito mahān ॥ 2.26.36 ॥
sa manostanayaḥ krūro dhundhurnāma sudāruṇaḥ।
śataṃ lokavināśāya tapa āsthāya dāruṇam ॥ 2.26.37 ॥
saṃvatsarasya paryyante sa niḥśvāsaṃ pramuñcati।
yadā tadā mahī tatra calitā sma sakānanā ॥ 2.26.38 ॥
tasya niḥśvāsavātena raja uddhūyate mahat।
ādityapathamāvṛtya saptāhaṃ bhūmikampanam ॥ 2.26.39 ॥
savisphuliṅgaṃ sajvālaṃ sadhūmamatidāruṇam ।
tena rājanna śaknomi tasmin sthātuṃ sva āśrame ॥ 2.26.40 ॥
taṃ vāraya mahābāho lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā।
tejaste sumahāviṣṇustejasāpyāyayiṣyati ॥ 2.26.41 ॥
lokāḥ svasthā bhavantvadya tasmin vinihate'sure ।
tvaṃ hi tasya vadhāyādya samarthaḥ pṛthivīpate ॥ 2.26.42 ॥
viṣṇunā ca varo datto mama pūrvvaṃ tato'nagha।
na hi dhundhurmahāvīryyastejasālpena śakyate ॥ 2.26.43 ॥
nirddagdhuṃ pṛthivīpāla api varṣa śatairiha।
vīryyaṃ hi sumahattasya devairapi durāsaham ॥ 2.26.44 ॥
evamuktastu rājarṣiruttaṅkena mahātmanā।
kubalāśvaṃ sutaṃ prādāttasmin dhundhunivāraṇe ॥ 2.26.45 ॥
rājā saṃnyastaśastro'hamayantu tanayo mama।
bhaviṣyati dvijaśveṣṭha dhundhumāro na saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.26.46 ॥
sa taṃ vyādiśya tanayaṃ dhundhumāraṇamudyatam।
jagāma parvvatāyaiva tapase śaṃsitavrataḥ ॥ 2.26.47 ॥
kubalāśvastu dharmmātmā piturvacanamāsthitaḥ।
sahasrairekaviṃśatyā putrāṇāṃ saha pārthivaḥ।
prāyāduttaṅka sahito dhundhostasya nivāraṇe ॥ 2.26.48 ॥
tamāviśattato viṣṇurbhagavān svena tejasā।
uttaṅkasya niyogāttu lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ॥ 2.26.49 ॥
tasmin prayāte durddharṣe divi śabdo mahānabhūt।
adyaprubhṛtyeṣa nṛpo dhundhumāro bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.26.50 ॥
sagatvā puruṣa vyāghrastanayaiḥ saha vīryyavān ॥ 2.26.51 ॥
samudraṃ khanayāmāsa vālukārṇavamavyayam।
tasya putraiḥ khanadbhiśca vālukāntarhitastadā ॥ 2.26.53 ॥
dhundhurāsāditastatra diśamāśritya paścimām।
mukhajenāgninā kruddho lokānudvarttayanniva ॥ 2.26.54 ॥
vāri śuśrāva yogena mahodadhirivodaye।
somasya somapaśreṣṭha dhārormikalilo mahān ॥ 2.26.55 ॥
tasya vārimayaṃ vegamapibat sa narādhipaḥ।
yogī yogena vahniṃ vā śamayāmāsa vāriṇā ॥ 2.26.57 ॥
nirasyattaṃ mahākāyaṃ balenodakarākṣasam।
uttaṅkaṃ darśayāmāsa kṛtakarmmā narādhipaḥ ॥ 2.26.58 ॥
uttaṅkaśca varaṃ prādāttasmai rājñe mahātmane।
adāttasyākṣayaṃ vittaṃ śatrubhiścāpyadhṛṣyatām ॥ 2.26.59 ॥
dharmme ratiñca satataṃ svarge vāsaṃ tathākṣayam।
putrāṇāṃ cākṣayāँllokān svarge ye rākṣasā hatāḥ ॥ 2.26.60 ॥
tasya putrāstrayaḥ śiṣṭā dṛḍhāśvo jyeṣṭha ucyate।
bhadrāśvaḥ kapilāśvaśca kanīyāsau tu tau smṛtau ॥ 2.26.61 ॥
dhaundhumārirdṛḍhāśvastu haryaśvastasya cātmajaḥ।
haryaśvasya nikumbho'bhūt kṣatradharmarataḥ sadā ॥ 2.26.62 ॥
saṃhatāśvo nikumbhasya śruto raṇaviśāradaḥ ।
kṛśāśvaścākṣayāśvaśca saṃhatāśca sutāvubhau ॥ 2.26.63 ॥
tasya patnī haimavatī satāṃ matidṛṣadvatī।
vikhyātā triṣu lokeṣu putrastasyāḥ prasenajit ॥ 2.26.64 ॥
yuvanāśvaḥ sutastasya triṣu lokeṣvatidyutiḥ।
atyantadhārmiko gaurī tasya patnī pativratā ॥ 2.26.65 ॥
abhiśastā tu sā bhartrā nadī sā bāhudā kṛtā ।
tasyāstu gaurikaḥ putra ścakravarttī babhūva ha ॥ 2.26.66 ॥
māndhātā yauvanāśvo vai trailokyavijayī nṛpaḥ।
atrāpyudāharantīmau ślokau paurāṇikī dvijāḥ ॥ 2.26.67 ॥
yāvatsūrya udayati yāvacca pratitiṣṭhati।
sarvaṃ tadyauvanāśvasya māndhātuḥ kṣetramucyate ॥ 2.26.68 ॥
atrāpyudāharantīmaṃ ślokaṃ vaṃśavido janāḥ ।
māndhātā tu tanurviṣṇoḥ purāṇajñāḥ prajakṣate ॥ 2.26.69 ॥
tasya caitrarathī bhāryyā śaśabindoḥ sutā'bhavat।
sādhvī bindumatī nāma rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvi ॥ 2.26.70 ॥
pativratā ca jyeṣṭā ca bhrātṝṇāmayutasya sā।
tasyāmutpādayāmāsa māndhātā trīn sutān prabhuḥ ॥ 2.26.71 ॥
purukutsamambarīṣaṃ mucukundañca viśrutam।
ambarīṣasya dāyādo yuvanāśvo'paraḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.26.72 ॥
narmadāyāṃ samutpannaḥ sambhūtastasya cātmajaḥ ॥ 2.26.74 ॥
sambhūtasyātmajaḥ putro hyanaraṇyaḥ pratāpavān।
rāvaṇena hato yena trilokīvijaye purā ॥ 2.26.75 ॥
trasadaśvo'naraṇyasya haryyaśvastasya cātmajaḥ ।
haryyaśvāttu dṛṣadvatyāṃ jajñe vasumato nṛpaḥ ॥ 2.26.76 ॥
tasya putro'bhavadrājā tridhanvā nāma dhārmmikaḥ।
āsīt traidhanvanaścāpi vidvāṃstrayyāṃ raṇaprabhuḥ ॥ 2.26.77 ॥
tasya satyavrato nāma kumāro'bhūnmahābalaḥ।
tena bhāryyā vidarbhasya hṛtā hatvā divaukasaḥ ॥ 2.26.78 ॥
pāṇigrahaṇamantreṣu niṣṭāṃ samprāpitoṣviha।
kāmādbalācca mohācca saṅkarṣaṇabalena ca।
bhāvino'rthasya ca balāt tatkṛtaṃ tena dhīmatā ॥ 2.26.80 ॥
tamadharmmeṇa saṃyuktaṃ pitā trayīguṇo'tyajat।
apadhvaṃseti bahuśo'vadat krodhasamanvitaḥ ॥ 2.26.81 ॥
pitaraṃ so'bravīdekaḥ kva gacchāmīti vai muhuḥ।
pitā cainamathovāca śvapākaiḥ saha varttaya ॥ 2.26.82 ॥
nāhaṃ putreṇa putrārthī tvayādya kulapāṃsana।
ityuktaḥ sa nirākrāmannagarādvacanādvibho ॥ 2.26.83 ॥
na cainaṃ dhārayāmāsa vasiṣṭo bhagavānṛṣiḥ।
sa tu satyavrato dhīmāñchvapākāvasathāntikam।
pitrā mukto'vasadvīraḥ pitā cāsya vanaṃ yayau ॥ 2.26.84 ॥
tasmiṃstu viṣaye tasya nāvarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ।
samā dvādaśa saṃpūrṇāstenādharmmeṇa vai tadā ॥ 2.26.85 ॥
dārāṃstu tasya viṣaye viśvāmitro mahātapāḥ।
saṃnyasya sāgarānūpe cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ ॥ 2.26.86 ॥
tasya patnī gale baddhvā madhyamaṃ putramaurasam।
śikhayā bharaṇārthāya vyakrīṇādghośatena vai ॥ 2.26.87 ॥
taṃ tu baddhaṃ gale dṛṣṭvā vikrītaṃ taṃ narottamaḥ।
maharṣiputraṃ dharmmātmā mokṣayāmāsa suvrataḥ ॥ 2.26.88 ॥
satyavrato mahābuddhirbharaṇaṃ tasya cākarot ।
viśvāmitrasya tuṣṭyarthamanukampārthameva ca ॥ 2.26.89 ॥
so'bhavadghālavo nāma gale baddho mahātapāḥ।
maharṣiḥ kauśikastātastena vīryeṇa mokṣitaḥ ॥ 2.26.90 ॥
tasya vratena bhaktyā ca kṛpayā ca pratijñayā।
viśvāmitrakalatrañca babhāra vinaye sthitaḥ ॥ 2.26.91 ॥
hatvā mṛgān varāhāṃśca mahiṣāṃśca vanecarān।
viśvāmitrāśramābhyāśe tanmāṃsamapacattataḥ ॥ 2.26.92 ॥
upāṃśuvratamāsthāya dīkṣāṃ dvādaśavārṣikīm।
piturniyogātabhajannṛpe tu vanamāsthite ॥ 2.26.93 ॥
ayodhyāñcaiva rājyañca tathaivāntaḥpuraṃ muniḥ।
yājyopādhyāyasaṃyogādvasiṣṭhaḥ parirakṣitaḥ ॥ 2.26.94 ॥
satyavratastu bālyāttu bhāvino'rthasya vai balāt।
vasiṣṭe'bhyādhikaṃ manyuṃ dhārayāmāsa manyunā ॥ 2.26.95 ॥
pitrā rudaṃstadā rāṣṭrāt parityaktaṃ svamātmajam।
na vārayāmāsa munirvasiṣṭhaḥ kāraṇena vai ॥ 2.26.96 ॥
pāṇigrahaṇamantrāṇāṃ niṣṭā syāt saptame pade।
evaṃ satyavratastān vai kṛtavān saptame pade ॥ 2.26.97 ॥
jānan dharmmān vasiṣṭhastu na ca mantrānihecchati।
iti satyavrate roṣaṃ vasiṣṭo manasākarot ।। 26.98 ।।
gururbuddhyā tu bhagavān vasiṣṭhaḥ kṛtavāṃstadā।
na tu satyavrato buddhyā upāṃśuvratamasya vai ।। 26.99 ।।
tasmiṃścoparate yo yatpiturāsīnmahāmanāḥ।
tena dvādaśavarṣāṇi nāvarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ ।। 26.100 ।।
tena tvidānīṃ bahudhā dīkṣāṃ tāṃ durbalāṃ bhuvi।
kulasya niṣkṛtiḥ svasya kṛteyañca bhavediti ।। 26.101 ।।
tato vasiṣṭo bhagavān pitrā tyaktaṃ nyavārayat।
abhiṣekṣyāmyahaṃ rājye paścādenamiti prabhuḥ ।। 26.102 ।।
sa tu dvādaśavarṣāṇi dīkṣāntāmudvahan balī।
avidyamāne māṃse tu vasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ ।। 26.103 ।।
sarvvakāmadughāṃ dhenuṃ saṃdadarśa nṛpātmajaḥ।
tāṃ vai krodhācca mohācca śramāccaiva kṣudhānvitaḥ ।। 26.104 ।।
dasyudharmmaṃ gato dṛṣṭvā jaghāna balināṃ varaḥ।
sa tu māṃsaṃ svayaṃ caiva viśvāmitrasya cātmajān ।। 26.105 ।।
bhojayāmāsa tacchrutvā vasiṣṭhastaṃ tadātyajat।
provāca caiva bhagavān vasiṣṭhastaṃ nṛpātmajam ।। 26.106 ।।
yadi te trīṇi śaṃkūni na syurhi puruṣādhama ।। 26.107 ।।
pituścāparitoṣeṇa gurordogdhrīvadhena ca।
aproṣitopayogācca trividhaste vyatikramaḥ ।। 26. 108 ।।
evaṃ sa trīṇi śaṃkūni dṛṣṭvā tasya mahā tapāḥ।
triśaṅkuriti hovāca triśaṅkustena sa smṛtaḥ ।। 26.109 ।।
viśvāmitrastu dārāṇāmāgato bharaṇe kṛte।
tatastasmai varaṃ prādāttadā prītastriśaṅkave ।। 26.110 ।।
chandyamāno vareṇātha guruṃ vrave nṛpātmajaḥ।
anāvṛṣṭibhaye tasmin gate dvādaśavārṣike ।। 26.111 ।।
abhiṣicya rājye pitrye yājayāmāsa taṃ muniḥ।
miṣatāṃ daivatānāñca vasiṣṭhasya ca kauśikaḥ।
saśarīraṃ tadā taṃ vai divamāropayat prabhuḥ ।। 26.112 ।।
miṣatastu vasiṣṭhasya tadadbhutamivābhavat।
atrāpyudāharantīmau ślokau paurāṇikā janāḥ ।। 26.113 ।।
viśvāmitraprasādena triśaṅkurdivi rājate ।
devai sārddhaṃ mahātejānugrahāttasya dhīmataḥ ।। 26.114 ।।
tasya satyaratā nāma bhāryyā kekayavaṃśajā।
kumāraṃ janayāmāsa hariścandramakalmaṣam ।। 26.116 ।।
sa tu rājā hariścandrastraiśaṅkava iti śrutaḥ ।
āharttā rājasūyasya samrāḍiti pariśrutaḥ ।। 26.117 ।।
hariścandrasya tu suto rohito nāma vīryyavān।
harito rohitasyātha caṃcuhārīta ucyate ।। 26.118 ।।
vijayaśca sudevaśca caṃcuputrau babhūvatuḥ।
jetā sarvvasya kṣatrasya vijayastena sa smṛtaḥ ।। 26.119 ।।
rurukastanayastatra rājā dharmmārthakovidaḥ।
rurukāddhṛtakaḥ putrastasmādbāhuśca jajñivān ।। 26.120 ।।
haihayaistālajaṅghaiśca nirasto vyasanī nṛpaḥ।
śakairyavanakāmbojaiḥ pāradaiḥ pahlavaistathā ।। 26.121 ।।
nātyarthaṃ dhārmmiko'bhūt sa dharmmye satyayuge tathā।
sagarastu suto bāhorjajñe saha gareṇa vai।
bhṛgorāśramamāsādya turveṇa parirakṣitaḥ ।। 26.122 ।।
āgneyamastraṃ labdhvā tu bhārgavāt sagaro nṛpaḥ।
jaghāna pṛthivīṅgatvā tālajaṃghān sahaihayān ।। 26.123 ।।
śakānāṃ pahlavānāñca dharmmānnirasadacyutaḥ।
kṣatriyāṇāṃ tathā teṣāṃ pāradānāñca dharmmavit ।। 26.124 ।।
kathaṃ sa sagaro rājā gareṇa saha jajñivān।
kimarthañca śakādīnāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahaujasām।
dharmmān kulocitān kruddho rājā nirasadacyutaḥ ।। 26.125 ।।
bāhorvyasaninastasya hṛtaṃ rājyaṃ purā kila।
haihayaistālajaṃvaiśca śakaiḥ sārddhaṃ samāgataiḥ ।। 26.126 ।।
yavanāḥ pāradāścaiva kāmbojāḥ pahlavāstathā।
haihayārthaṃ parākrāntā ete pañcagaṇāstadā ।। 26.127 ।।
hṛtarājyastadā bāhuḥ saṃnyasya nu tadā nṛpaḥ।
vanaṃ praviśya dharmmātmā saha patnyā tapo'carat ।। 26.128 ।।
kasyacittvatha kālasya toyārthaṃ prasthito nṛpaḥ।
vṛddhatvāddurbbalatvācca antarā sa mamāra ca ।। 26.129 ।।
patnī tu yādavī tasya sagarbhā pṛṣṭhato'nvagāt ।
sapatnyā tu garastasyai datto garbhajighāṃsayā ।। 26.130 ।।
sā tu bhartuścitāṃ kṛtvā vahnau taṃ samarohayat।
