aurvastāṃ bhārgavo dṛṣṭvā kāruṇyādvinyavarttayat ।। 26.131 ।।
tasyāśrame tu taṅgarbhaṃ sāgareṇa tadā saha।
vyajāyata mahābāhuṃ sagaraṃ nāma dhārmikam ।। 26.132 ।।
aurvastu jātakarmādīn kṛtvā tasya mahātmanaḥ।
adhyāpya vedaśāstrāṇi tato'straṃ pratyapādayat ।। 26.133 ।।
tataḥ śakān sayavanān kāmbojān pāradāṃstathā।
pahlavāṃścaiva niḥśeṣān kartuṃ vyavasito nṛpaḥ ।। 26.135 ।।
te vadhyamānā vīreṇa sagareṇa mahātmanā।
vasiṣṭhaṃ śaraṇaṃ sarvve prapannāḥ śaraṇaiṣiṇaḥ ।। 26.136 ।।
sagaraṃ vārayāmāsa teṣāndattvā'bhayantadā ।। 26.137 ।।
sagaraḥ svāmpratijñāñca gurorvāsyaṃ niśamya ca।
dharmmaṃ jaghāna teṣāṃ vai veṣānyatvaṃ cakāra ha ।। 26.138 ।।
arddhaṃ śakānāṃ śiraso muṇḍayitvā vyasarjayat।
yavanānāṃ śiraḥ sarvaṃ kāmbojānāntathaiva ca।। 26.139 ।।
pāradā muktakeśāśca pahlavāḥ śmaśru dhāriṇaḥ।
niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkārāḥ kṛtāstena mahātmanā ।। 26.140 ।।
śakā yavanakāmbojāḥ pahlavāḥ pāradaiḥ saha।
kelisparśā māhiṣikā dārvāścolāḥ khasāstathā ।। 26.141 ।।
sarvve te kṣatriyagaṇā dharmmasteṣāṃ nirākṛtaḥ।
vasiṣṭhavacanātpūrvaṃ sagareṇa mahātmanā ।। 26.142 ।।
sa dharmavijayī rājā vijityemāṃ vasundharām।
aśvaṃ vicārayāmāsa vājimedhāya dīkṣitaḥ ।। 26.143 ।।
tasya cārayataḥ so'śvaḥ samudre pūrvadakṣiṇe।
velāsamīpe'pahṛto bhūmiñcaiva praveśitaḥ ।। 26.144 ।।
sa tandeśaṃ sutaiḥ sarvaiḥ khanayāmāsa pārthivaḥ।
āseduśca tatastasmiṃstadantaste mahārṇave ।। 26.145 ।।
tamādipuruṣaṃ devaṃ hariṃ kṛṣṇaṃ prajāpatim।
viṣṇuṃ kapilarūpeṇa haṃsaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum ।। 26.146 ।।
tasya cakṣuḥ samāsādya tejastat pratipadyate।
dagdhāḥ putrāstadā sarve catvārastvavaśeṣitāḥ ।। 26.147 ।।
barhiketuḥ saketuśca tathā dharmmaratastrayaḥ।
śūraḥ pañcavanaścaiva tasya vaṃśakarāḥ prabho ।। 26.148 ।।
prādācca tasya bhagavān harirnārāyaṇo varān।
akṣayatvaṃ svavaṃśasya vājimedhaśataṃ tathā।
vibhuṃ putraṃ samudrañca svarge vāsaṃ tathākṣayam ।। 26.149 ।।
sa samudro'śvamādāya vandade (?) saritāṃpatiḥ।
sāgaratvaṃ ca lebhe sa karmaṇā tena tasya vai ।। 26.150 ।।
taṃ cāśvamedhikaṃ so'śvaṃ samudrāt prāpya pārthivaḥ।
ājahārāśvamedhānāṃ śataṃ caiva punaḥ punaḥ ।। 26.151 ।।
teṣāṃ nārāyaṇaṃ tejaḥ praviṣṭānāṃ mahātmanām।
putrāṇāntu sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭistu iti naḥ śrutam ।। 26.152 ।।
sagarasyātmajā rājñaḥ kathaṃ jātā mahābalāḥ।
vikrāntāḥ ṣaṣṭisāhasrā vidhinā kena vā vada ।। 26.153 ।।
dve patnyau sagarasyāstāṃ tapasā dagdhakilbiṣe।
jyeṣṭā vidarbhaduhitā keśinī nāma nāmataḥ ।। 26.154 ।।
kanīyasī tu yā tasya patnī paramadharmiṇī।
ariṣṭanemiduhitā rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvi ।। 26.155 ।।
aurvastābhyāṃ varaṃ prādāt tapasārādhitaḥ prabhuḥ।
ekā janiṣyate putraṃ vaṃśakarttāramīpsitam।
ṣaṣṭiputraṃ sahasrāṇi dvitīyā janayiṣyati ।। 26.156 ।।
munestu vacanaṃ śrutvā keśinī putramekakam।
vaṃśasya kāraṇaṃ śreṣṭā jagrāha nṛpasaṃsadi ।। 26.157 ।।
ṣaṣṭiputrasahasrāṇi suparṇabhaginī tathā।
atha kāle gate jyeṣṭā jyeṣṭhaṃ putraṃ vyajāyata।
asamañja iti khyātaṃ kākutsthaṃ sagarātmajam ।। 26.159 ।।
sumatistvapi jajñe vai garbhantumbaṃ yaśasvinī।
ṣaṣṭiputrasahasrāṇi tumbamadhyādviniḥsṛtāḥ ।। 26.160 ।।
ghṛtapūrṇeṣu kumbheṣu tān garbhān nyadadhattataḥ।
dhātrīścaikaikaśaḥ prādāt tāvatīḥ poṣaṇe nṛpaḥ ।। 26.161 ।।
tato navasu māseṣu samuttasthuryathāsukham।
kumārāste mahābhāgāḥ sagaraprītivarddhanāḥ ।। 26.162 ।।
asamañja iti khyāto barhiketurmahābalaḥ ।। 26.164 ।।
paurāṇāmahite yuktaḥ pitrā nirvāsitaḥ purā।
tasya putroṃ'śumānnāma asamañjasya vīryavān ।। 26.165 ।।
tasya putrastu dharmātmā dilīpa iti viśrutaḥ।
dilīpāttu mahātejā vīro jāto bhagīrathaḥ ।। 26.166 ।।
yena gaṅgā saricchreṣṭā vimānairupaśobhitā ।
atrāpyudāharantīmaṃ ślokaṃ paurāṇikā janāḥ ।। 26.167 ।।
bhagīrathastu tāṃ gaṅgāmānayāmāsa karmabhiḥ ।
tasmādbhāgīrathī gaṅgā kathyate vaṃśavittamaiḥ ।। 26.168 ।।
bhagīrathasutaścāpi śruto nāma babhūva ha।
nābhāgastasya dāyādo nityaṃ dharmaparāyaṇaḥ ।। 26.169 ।।
ambarīṣaḥ sutastasya sindhudvīpastato'bhavat।
evaṃ vaṃśapurāṇajñā gāyantīti pariśrutam ।। 26.170 ।।
nābhāgerambarīṣasya bhujābhyāṃ paripālitā।
babhūva vasudhātyarthaṃ tāpatrayavivarjitā ।। 26.171 ।।
ayutāyuḥ sutastasya sindhudvīpasya vīryavān।
ayutāyostu dāyāda ṛtuparṇo mahāyaśāḥ ।। 26.172 ।।
divyākṣahṛdajño'sau rājā nalasakho balī।
nalau dvāviti vikhyātau purāṇeṣu dṛḍhavratau ।। 26.173 ।।
vīrasenātmajaścaiva yaścekṣvākukulodvahaḥ।
ṛtuparṇasya putro'bhūt sarvvakāmo janeśvaraḥ ।। 26.174 ।।
sudāsastasya tanayo rājā haṃsamukho'bhavat।
sudāsasya sutaḥ proktaḥ saudāso nāma pārthivaḥ ।। 26.175 ।।
khyātaḥ kalmāṣapādo vai nāmnā mitrasahaśca saḥ ।
vasiṣṭhastu mahātejāḥ kṣetre kalmāṣapādake।
aśmakaṃ janayāmāsa ikṣvākukulavṛddhaye ।। 26.176 ।।
aśmakasyorakāmastu mūlakastatsuto'bhavat।
atrāpyudāharantīmaṃ mūlakaṃ vai nṛpaṃ prati ।। 26.177 ।।
sa hi rāmabhayādrājā strībhiḥ parivṛto'vasat।
vivastrastrāṇamicchan vai nārīkavacamīśvaraḥ ।। 26.178 ।।
mūlakasyāpi dharmātmā rājā śatarathaḥ smṛtaḥ।
tasmācchatarathājjajñe rājā caiḍiviḍo balī ।। 26.179 ।।
āsīttvaiḍiviḍaḥ śrīmān kṛtaśarmā pratāpavān।
putro viśvamahattasya putrīkasya vyajāyata ।। 26.180 ।।
dilīpastasya putro'bhūt khaṭvāṅga iti viśrutaḥ।
yena svargādihāgamya muhūrttaṃ prāpya jīvitam।
trayo'bhisaṃhitā lokā buddhyā satyena caiva hi ।। 26.181 ।।
dīrgabāhuḥ sutastasya raghustasmādajāyata।
ajaḥ putro raghoścāpi tasmājjajñe sa vīryavān।
rājā daśaratho nāma ikṣvākukulanandanaḥ ।। 26.182 ।।
rāmo dāśarathirvīro dharmajño lokaviśrutaḥ।
bharato lakṣmaṇaścaiva śatrughnaśca mahābalaḥ ।। 26.183 ।।
mādhavaṃ lavaṇaṃ hatvā gatvā madhuvanañca tat।
śatrughnena purī tasya mathurā sanniveśitā ।। 26.184 ।।
subāhuḥ śūrasenaśca śatrughnasahitāvubhau।
pālayāmāsatuḥ sūnū vaidehyau mathurāṃ purīm ।। 26.185 ।।
aṅgadaścāndraketuśca lakṣmaṇasyātmajāvubhau।
himavatparvatābhyāśe sphītau janapadau tayoḥ ।। 26.186 ।।
ahgadasyāṅgadīyā tu deśe kārapathe purī।
candraketostu mallasya candravaktā purī śubhā ।। 26.187 ।।
bharatasyātmajau vīrau takṣaḥ puṣkara eva ca।
gāndhāraviṣaye siddhe tayoḥ puryau mahātmanoḥ ।। 26.188 ।।
takṣasya dikṣu vikhyātā ramyā takṣaśilā purī।
puṣkarasyāpi vīrasya vikhyātā puṣkarāvatī ।। 26.189 ।।
gāthāṃ caivātra gāyanti ye purāṇavido jatāḥ।
rāme nibaddhāssattvārthā māhātmyāttasya dhīmataḥ ।। 26.190 ।।
śyāmo yuvā lohitākṣo dīptāsyo mitabhāṣitaḥ।
ājānubāhuḥ sumukhaḥ siṃhaskandho mahābhujaḥ ।। 26.191 ।।
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi rāmo rājyamakārayat।
ṛksāmayajuṣāṃ ghoṣo jyāghoṣaśca mahāsvanaḥ ।। 26.192 ।।
avicchinno'bhavadrāṣṭre dīyatāṃ bhujyatāmiti।
janasthāne vasan kāryaṃ tridaśānāñcakārasaḥ ।। 26.193 ।।
tamāgaskāriṇaṃ pūrvaṃ paulastyaṃ manujarṣabhaḥ।
sītāyāḥ padamanvicchan nijaghāna mahāyaśāḥ ।। 26.194 ।।
sattvavān guṇasampanno dīpyamānaḥ sva tejasā।
atisūryañca vahniñca rāmo dāśarathirbabhau ।। 26.195 ।।
kuśasya kośalā rājyaṃ purī vāpi kuśasthalī।
ramyā niveśitā tena vindhyaparvatasānuṣu ।। 26.198 ।।
uttarākośale rājyaṃ lavasya ca mahātmanaḥ।
śrāvastī lokavikhyātā kuśavaṃśaṃ nibodhata ।। 26.199 ।।
kuśasya putro dharmātmā hyatithiḥ supriyātithiḥ।
atitherapi vikhyāto niṣadho nāma pārthivaḥ ।। 26.200 ।।
niṣadhasya nalaḥ putro nabhaḥ putro nalasya tu।
nabhasaḥ puṇḍarīkastu kṣemadhanvā tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 26.201 ।।
kṣemadhanvasuto rājā devānīkaḥ pratāpavān।
āsīdahīnagurnāma devānī kātmajaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 26.202 ।।
ahīnagostu dāyādaḥ pāriyātro mahāyaśāḥ।
dalastasyātmajaścāpi tasmājjajñe balo nṛpaḥ ।। 26.203 ।।
auṅko nāma sa dharmātmā balaputro babhūva ha।
vajranābhaḥ sutastasya śaṅkhaṇastasya cātmajaḥ ।। 26.204 ।।
śaṃkhaṇasya suto vidvān dhyuṣitāśca iti śrutaḥ ।
dhyuṣitāśca sutaścāpi rājā viśvasahaḥ kila ।। 26.205 ।।
hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo vasiṣṭhastatsuto'bhavat।
śatāni saṃhitānāntu pañca yo'dhītavāṃstataḥ।
tasmādadhigato yogo yājñavalkyena dhīmatā ।। 26.207 ।।
puṣyastasya suto vidvān dhruvasandhiśca tatsutaḥ।
sudarśanastasya suto agnivarṇaḥ sudarśanāt ।। 26.208 ।।
agnivarṇasya śīghrastu śīghrakasya manuḥ smṛtaḥ।
manustu yogamāsthāya kalāpagrāmamāsthitaḥ।
ekonaviṃśaprayuge kṣatraprāvarttakaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 26.209 ।।
prasuśruto manoḥ putraḥ susandhistasya cātmajaḥ।
susandheśca tathāmarṣaḥ sahasvānnāma nāmataḥ ।। 26.210 ।।
āsītsahasvataḥ putro rājā viśrutavāniti।
tasyāsīdviśrutavataḥ putro rājā bṛhadbalaḥ ।। 26.211 ।।
ete ikṣvākudāyādā rājānaḥ prāyaśaḥ smṛtāḥ।
vaṃśe pradhānā ye te'smin prādhānyena tu kīrttitāḥ ।। 26.212 ।।
paṭhan samyagimāṃ sṛṣṭimādityasya vivasvataḥ।
prajāvāneti sāyujyaṃ manorvaivasvatasya saḥ ।। 26.213 ।।
śrāddhadevasya devasya prajānāṃ puṣṭidasya ca।
vipāpmā virajāścaiva āyuṣmān bhavate'cyutaḥ ।। 26.214 ।।
anujasya vikukṣestu nimervaṃśaṃ nibodhata।
yo'sau niveśayāmāsa purandevapuropamam ॥ 2.27.1 ॥
jayantamitivikhyātaṃ gautamasyāśramābhitaḥ।
yasyānvavāye yajñe vai janakādṛṣisattamāt ॥ 2.27.2 ॥
nemirnāma sudharmātmā sarvasatvanamaskṛtaḥ।
āsīt putro mahāprājña ikṣvākorbhūritejasaḥ ॥ 2.27.3 ॥
sa śāpena vasiṣṭhasya videhaḥ samapadyata।
tasya putro mithirnāma janitaḥ parvabhistribhiḥ ॥ 2.27.4 ॥
araṇyāṃ mathyamānāyāṃ prādurbhūto mahāyaśāḥ।
nāmnā mithiriti khyāto jananājjanako'bhavat ॥ 2.27.5 ॥
mithirnāma mahāvīryo yenāsau mithilābhavat।
rājāsau janako nāma janakāccāpyudāvasuḥ ॥ 2.27.6 ॥
udāvasoḥ sudharmātmā janito nandivarddhanaḥ।
nandivarddhanataḥ śūraḥ suketurnāma dhārmikaḥ ॥ 2.27.7 ॥
suketorapi dharmātmā devarāto mahābalaḥ।
devarātasya dharmātmā bṛhaduccha iti śrutiḥ ॥ 2.27.8 ॥
bṛhaducchasya tanayo mahāvīryaḥ pratāpavān ।
mahāvīryasya dhṛtimān sudhṛtistasya cātmajaḥ ॥ 2.27.9 ॥
sudhṛterapi dharmātmā dhṛṣṭaketuḥ parantapaḥ।
dhṛṣṭaketu sutaścāpi haryaśvo nāma viśrutaḥ ॥ 2.27.10 ॥
haryaśvasya maruḥ putro maroḥ putraḥ pratitvakaḥ।
pratitvakasya dharmātmā rājā kīrttirathaḥ sutaḥ ॥ 2.27.11 ॥
putraḥ kīrttirathasyāpi devamīḍha iti śrutaḥ ।
devamīḍhasya vibudho vibudhasya suto dhṛtiḥ ॥ 2.27.12 ॥
mahādhṛtisuto rājā kīrttirājaḥ pratāpavān ।
kīrtti rājātmajo vidvān mahārometi viśrutaḥ ॥ 2.27.13 ॥
mahāromṇastu vikhyātaḥ svarṇaromā vyajāyata।
svarṇaromātmajaścāpi hrasvaromābhavanṛpaḥ ॥ 2.27.14 ॥
hrasvaromātmajo vidvān sīradhvaja iti śrutiḥ।
udbhinnā kṛṣatā yena sītā rājñā yaśasvinī।
rāmasya mahiṣī sādhvī suvratātipativratā ॥ 2.27.15 ॥
kathaṃ sītā samutpannā kṛṣyamāṇā yaśasvinī।
kimarthañcākṛṣadrājā kṣetraṃ yasmin babhūva ha ॥ 2.27.16 ॥
agnikṣetre kṛṣyamāṇe aśvamedhe mahātmanaḥ।
vidhinā suprayuktena tasmātsā tu samutthitā ॥ 2.27.17 ॥
sīradhvajāttu jātastu bhānumānnāma maithilaḥ।
bhrātā kuśadhvajastasya sa kāśyadhipatirnṛpaḥ ॥ 2.27.18 ॥
tasya bhānumataḥ putraḥ pradyumnaśca pratāpavān।
munistasya sutaścāpi tasmādūrjavahaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.27.19 ॥
ūrjavahāt sutadvājaḥ śakunistasya cātmajaḥ।
svāgataḥ śakuneḥ putraḥ suvarccāstatsutaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.27.20 ॥
śruto yastasya dāyādaḥ suśrutastasya cātmajaḥ।
suśrutasya jayaḥ putro jayasya vijayaḥ sutaḥ ॥ 2.27.21 ॥
vijayasya ṛtaḥ putra ṛtasya sunayaḥ smṛtaḥ।
sunayādvītahavyastu vītahavyātmajo dhṛtiḥ ॥ 2.27.22 ॥
dhṛtestu bahulāśvo'bhūdbahulāśvasutaḥ kṛtiḥ।
tasmin santiṣṭate vaṃśo janakānāṃ mahātmanām।
ityete maithilāḥ proktāḥ somasyāpi nibodhata ॥ 2.27.23 ॥
pitā somasya vaiviprā jajñe'trirbhagavānṛṣiḥ।
karmaṇā manasā vācā śubhānyeva samācaran।
kāṣṭhakuḍyaśilābhūta ūrddhvabāhurmahādyutiḥ ।। 28.2 ।।
suduścaraṃ nāma tapo yena taptaṃ mahatpurā।
trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi divyānīti hi naḥ śrutam ।। 28.3 ।।
tasyorddhvaretasastatra sthitasyānimiṣaspṛham।
somatvantanurāpede mahābuddhiḥ sa vai dvijaḥ ।। 28.4 ।।
ūrddhvamācakrame tasya somatvaṃ bhāvitātmanaḥ।
taṃ garbhaṃ vidhinādiṣṭā daśa devyo dadhustadā।
sametya dhārayāmāsurna ca tāḥ samaśaknuvan ।। 28.6 ।।
sa tābhyaḥ sahasaivātha digbhyo garbhaḥ prabhānvitaḥ।
yathāvabhāsayaṃllokāñjhītāṃśuḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ ।। 28.7 ।।
yadā na dhāraṇe śaktāstasya garbhasya tāḥ striyaḥ।
tataḥ sa tābhiḥ śītāṃśurnipapāta vasundharām ।। 28.8 ।।
patantaṃ somamālokya brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ।
rathamāropayāmāsa lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। 28.9 ।।
sa hi devamayo viprā dharmmārthī satyasaṅgaraḥ।
yukto vājisahasreṇa siteneti hi naḥ śrutam ।। 28.10 ।।
tasminnipatite devāḥ putre'treḥ paramātmani।
tuṣṭuvurbrahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ mānasāḥ sapta viśrutāḥ ।। 28.11 ।।
tatraivāṅgirasastasya bhṛgoścaivātmajastathā।
ṛgbhiryajurbhirbahubhiratharvāṅgirasairapi ।। 28.12 ।।
tataḥ saṃstūyamānasya tejaḥ somasya bhāsvataḥ।
āpyāyamānaṃ lokāṃstrīn bhāvayāmāsa sarvvaśaḥ ।। 28.13 ।।
samena rathamukhyena sāgarāntāṃ vasundharām।
triḥsaptakṛtvo vipula ścakārābhipradakṣiṇam ।। 28.14 ।।
tasya yaccāpi tattejaḥ pṛthivīmanvapadyata।
oṣadhyastāḥ samudbhūtāstejasā saṃjvalantyuta ।। 28.15 ।।
tābhirdhāryatyayaṃ lokān prajāścāpi caturvidhāḥ।
poṣṭā hi bhagavān somo jagato hi dvijottamāḥ ।। 28.16 ।।
sa labdhatejāstapasā saṃstavaistaiśca karmmabhiḥ।
tapastepe mahābhāgaḥ pajhānāṃ daśatīrdaśa ।। 28.17 ।।
hiraṇyavarṇā yā devyo dhārayantyātmanā jagat।
vibhustāsāmbhavetsomaḥ prakhyātaḥ svena karmmaṇā ।। 28.18 ।।
tatastasmai dadau rājyaṃ brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥ।
bījauṣadhiṣu viprāṇāmapāñca dvijasattamāḥ ।। 28.19 ।।
so'bhiṣikto mahātejā mahārājyena rājarāṭ ।
lokānāṃ bhāvayāmāsa svabhāvāttapatāṃ varaḥ ।। 28.20 ।।
saptaviṃśatirindostu dākṣāyaṇyo mahāvratāḥ।
dadau prācetaso dakṣo nakṣatrāṇīti yā viduḥ ।। 28.21 ।।
sa tatprāpya mahadrājayaṃ somaḥ somavatāṃ prabhuḥ।
samājajñe rājasūyaṃ sahasraśatadakṣiṇam ।। 28.22 ।।
hiraṇyagarbhaścodgātā brahmā brahmatvameyivān।
sadasyastatra bhagavān harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।
sanatkumārapramukhairādyairbrahmarṣibhirvṛtaḥ ।। 28.23 ।।
dakṣiṇāmadadatsomastrīlloँkāniti naḥ śrutam।
tebhyo brahmarṣimukhyebhyaḥ sadasyebhyaśca vai dvijāḥ ।। 28.24 ।।
taṃ sinī ca kuhūścaiva vapuḥ puṣṭiḥ prabhāvasuḥ।
kīrttirdhṛtiśca lakṣmīśca nava devyaḥ siṣevire ।। 28.25 ।।
prāpyāvabhṛthamavyagraḥ sarvvadevarṣipūjitaḥ।
atirājātirājendro daśadhātāpayaddiśaḥ ।। 28.26 ।।
tadā tat prāpya duṣprāpamaiśvaryamṛṣisaṃstutam।
bṛhaspateḥ sa vai bhāryāntārāṃ nāma yaśasvinīm।
jahāra sahasā sarvvānavamatyāṅgiraḥsutān ।। 28.28 ।।
sa yācyamāno devaiśca tathā devarṣibhiśca ha।
naiva vyasarjayattārāṃ tasmāyāṅgirase tadā ।। 28.29 ।।
uśanāstasya jagrāha pārṣṇimaṅgiraso dvijāḥ।
sa hi śiṣyo mahātejāḥ pituḥ pūrvaṃ bṛhaspateḥ ।। 28.30 ।।
tena snehena bhagavān rudrastasya bṛhaspateḥ।
pārṣṇigrāho'bhavaddevaḥ pragṛhyājagavandhanuḥ ।। 28.31 ।।
tena brahmarṣimukhyebhyaḥ paramāstraṃ mahātmanā।
uddiśya devānutsṛṣṭaṃ yenaiṣāṃ nāśitaṃ yaśaḥ ।। 28.32 ।।
tatra tadyuddhamabhavat pratyakṣantārakāmayam।
devānāṃ dānavānāñca lokakṣayakaraṃ mahat ।। 28.33 ।।
tatra śiṣṭāstrayo devāstuṣitāścaiva ye smṛtāḥ।
brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmurādidevaṃ pitāmaham ।। 28.34 ।।
tato nivāryośanasaṃ rudraṃ jyeṣṭhañca śaṅkaram।
dadāvāṅgirase tārāṃ svayameva pitāmahaḥ ।। 28.35 ।।
antarvatnīṃ ca tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tārāntārādhipānanām।
garbhamutsṛjase na tvaṃ vipraḥ prāha bṛhaspatiḥ ।। 28.36 ।।
madīyāyāṃ tanau yonau garbho dhāryaḥ kathañcana।
jātamātro'tha bhagavān devānāmākṣipadvapuḥ ।। 28.38 ।।
tataḥ saṃśayamāpannāstārāmakathayan surāḥ।
satyaṃ brūhi sutaḥ kasya somasyātha bṛhaspateḥ ।। 28.39 ।।
hrīyamāṇā yadā devānnāha sā sādhvasādhu vā ।
tadā tāṃ śaptumārabdhaḥ kumāro dasyuhantamaḥ ।। 28.40 ।।
yadatra tathyantad‌brūhi tāre kasya sutastvayam ।। 28.41 ।।
sā prāñjaliruvācedaṃ brahmāṇaṃ varadaṃ prabhum।
somasyeti mahātmānaṃ kumārandasyuhantamam ।। 28.42 ।।
tataḥ sa tamupāghāya somo dātā prajāpatiḥ।
budha ityakaronnāma tasya putrasya dhīmataḥ ।। 28.43 ।।
pratipūrvvañca gamane samabhyuttiṣṭhate budhaiḥ।
utpādayāmāsa tadā putraṃ vai rājaputrikā ।। 28.44 ।।
tasya putro mahātejā babhūvailaḥ purūravāḥ ।
urvaśyāṃ jajñire tasya putrāḥ ṣaṭ sumahaujasaḥ ।। 28.45 ।।
prasahya dharṣitastatra vivaśo rājayakṣmaṇā ।
tato yakṣmābhibhūtastu somaḥ prakṣīṇamaṇḍalaḥ ।
jagāma śaraṇāyātha pitaraṃ so'trimeva tu ।। 28.46 ।।
tasya tatpāpaśamanaṃ cakārātrirmahāyaśāḥ।
sa rājayakṣmaṇā muktaḥ śriyā jajvāla sarvvaśaḥ ।। 28.47 ।।
etatsomasya vai janma kīrttitaṃ dvijasattamāḥ।
vaṃśantasya dvijaśreṣṭāḥ kīrtyamānaṃ nibodhata ।। 28.48 ।।
dhanyamārogyamāyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ kalmaṣaśodhanam।
somasya janma śrutvaiva sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। 28.49 ।।
somasya tu budhaḥ putro budhasya tu purūravāḥ।
tejasvī dānaśīlaśca yajvā vipuladakṣiṇaḥ ।। 29.1 ।।
brahmavādī parākrāntaḥ śatrubhiryudhi durjayaḥ।
āharttā cāgnihotrasya yajvanāñca dadau mahīm ।। 29.2 ।।
satyavāk karmmabuddhiśca kāntaḥ saṃvṛtamaithunaḥ।
atīva putro lokeṣu rūpeṇāpratimo'bhavat ।। 29.3 ।।
taṃ brahmavādinaṃ dāntaṃ dharmajñaṃ satyavādinam।
urvaśī varayāmāsa hitvā mānaṃ yaśasvinī ।। 29.4 ।।
tayā sahāvasadrājā daśavarṣāṇi cāṣṭa ca।
sapta ṣaṭ sapta cāṣṭau ca daśa cāṣṭau ca vīryavān ।। 29.5 ।।
vane caitrarathe ramye tathā mandākinītaṭe।
alakāyāṃ viśālāyāṃ nandane ca vanottame ।। 29.6 ।।
gandhamādanapādeṣu meruśrṛṅge nagottame।
uttarāṃśca kurūn prāpya kalāpagrāmameva ca ।। 29.7 ।।
eteṣu vanasukhyeṣu surairācariteṣu ca।
urvaśyā sahito rājā reme paramayā mudā ।। 29.8 ।।
gandharvā corvaśī devī rājānaṃ mānuṣaṃ katham।
brahmaśāpābhibhūtā sā mānuṣaṃ samupasthitā।
ātmanaḥ śāpamokṣārthaṃ niyamaṃ sā cakāra tu ।
anagnadarśanañcaiva akāmāta saha maithunam ।। 29.11 ।।
dvau meṣau śayanābhyāśe sa tāvad vyavatiṣṭhate।
ghṛtamātraṃ tathāhāraḥ kālamekantu pārthiva ।। 29.12 ।।
yadyeṣa samayo rājan yāvatkālañca te dṛḍham।
tāvatkālantu vatsyāmi eṣa naḥ samayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। 29.13 ।।
tasyāstaṃ samayaṃ sarvaṃ sa rājā paryapālayat।
varṣāṇyatha catuḥṣaṣṭiṃ tadbhaktyā śāpamohitā।
urvaśī mānuṣaṃ prāptā gandharvvā ścintayānvitāḥ ।। 29.15 ।।
cintayadhvaṃ mahābhāgā yathā sā tu varāṅganā।
āgacchettu punarddevānurvaśī svargabhūṣaṇā ।। 29.16 ।।
eko'gniḥ pūrvamāsīdvai ailastrīṃstānakalpayat ।। 29.45 ।।
evaṃprabhāvo rājāsīdailastu dvijasattamāḥ।
deśe puṇyatame caiva maharṣibhiralaṃkṛte ।। 29.46 ।।
rājyaṃ sa kārayāmāsa prayāge pṛthivī patiḥ।
uttare yāmune tīre pratiṣṭāne mahāyaśāḥ ।। 29.47 ।।
tasya putrā babhūvurhi ṣaḍindropamatejasaḥ।
gandharvvaloke viditā āyurddhīmānamāvasuḥ ।। 29.48 ।।
viśvāyuśca śatāyuśca gatāyuścorvaśīsutāḥ।
amāvasostu vai jāto bhīmo rājātha viśvajit ।। 29.49 ।।
śrīmān bhīmasya dāyādo rājāsītkāñcanaprabhaḥ।
vidvāṃstu kāñcanasyāpi suhotro'bhūnmahābalaḥ ।। 29.50 ।।
suhotrasyābhajjahnuḥ keśikāgarbhasambhavaḥ।
pratigatya tato gaṅgā vitato yajñakarmmaṇi ।। 29.51 ।।
plāvayāmāsa taṃ deśaṃ bhāvino'rthasya darśanāt।
gaṅgayā plāvitaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñavāṭaṃ samantataḥ ।। 29.52 ।।
rājarṣiṇā tataḥ pītāṃ gaṅgāṃ dṛṣṭvā surarṣayaḥ ।। 29.54 ।।
upaninyurmahābhāgā duhitṛtvena jāhnavīm।
yauvanāśvasya pautrīntu kāverīñjahnurāvahat ।। 29.55 ।।
yuvanāśvasya śāpena gaṅgā yena vinirmame ।
kāverīṃ saritāṃ śreṣṭāṃ jahnubhāryyāmaninditām ।। 29.56 ।।
jahnuśca dayitaṃ putraṃ suhotraṃ nāma dhārmikam।
kāveryyāṃ janayāmāsa ajakastasya cātmajaḥ ।। 29.57 ।।
ajakasya tu dāyādo balākāśvo mahāyaśāḥ।
babhūvuśca gayaḥ śīlaḥ kuśastasyātmajaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 29.58 ।।
kuśaputrā babhūvuśca catvāro vedavarcasaḥ।
kuśāśvaḥ kuśanābhaśca amūrttārayaśovasuḥ ।। 29.59 ।।
kuśastambastapastepe putrārthī rājasattamaḥ।
pūrṇe varṣasahasre vai śatakratumapaśyata ।। 29.60 ।।
tamugratapasaṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasrākṣaḥ purandaraḥ।
samarthaḥ putrajanane svayamevāsya śāśvataḥ ।। 29.61 ।।
putratvaṃ kalpayāmāsa svayameva purandaraḥ।
gādhirnāmābhavatputraḥ kauśikaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ ।। 29.62 ।।
paurukutsābhavadbhāryā gādhistasyāmajāyata।
pūrvvaṃ kanyāṃ mahābhāgāṃ nāmnā satyavatīṃ śubhām।
tāṃ gādhiputraḥ kāvyāya ṛcīkāya dadau prabhuḥ ।। 29.63 ।।
tasyāṃ putrastu vai bharttā bhārgavo bhṛgunandanaḥ।
putrārthe sādhayāmāsa caruṃ gādhestathaiva ca ।। 29.64 ।।
upayojyaścarurayaṃ tvayā mātrā ca teśubhe ।। 29.65 ।।
tasyāṃ janiṣyate putro dīptimān kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ।
ajeyaḥ kṣatriyairyuddhe kṣatriyarṣabhasūdanaḥ ।। 29.66 ।।
tavāpi putraṃ kalyāṇi dhṛtintaṃ tapodhanam।
śamātmakaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ carureṣa vidhāsyati ।। 29.67 ।।
evamuktvā tu tāṃ bhāryyāmṛcīko bhṛgunandanaḥ।
tapasyābhirato nityamaraṇyaṃ praviveśa ha ।। 29.68 ।।
gādhiḥ sadārastu tadā ṛcīkāśramamabhyagāt।
tīrthayātrāprasaṅgena sutāṃ draṣṭuṃ nareśvaraḥ ।। 29.69 ।।
carudvayaṃ gṛhītvā tu ṛṣeḥ satyavatī sadā।
bhartturvacanamavyagrā hṛṣṭā mātre nyavedayat ।। 29.70 ।।
mātā tu tasyai daivena duhitre svaṃ caruṃ dadau ।
tasyāścarumathājñānādātmanaḥ sā cakāra ha ।। 29.71 ।।
atha satyavatī garbhaṃ kṣatriyāntakaraṃ śubham।
dhārayāmāsa dīptena vapuṣā ghoradarśanā ।। 29.72 ।।
tamṛcīkastato dṛṣṭvā yogenāpyanumṛśya ca।
tadābravīddvijaśreṣṭhaḥ svāṃ bhāryyāṃ varavarṇinīm ।। 29.73 ।।
janiṣyati hi putraste krūrakarmātidāruṇaḥ ।। 29.74 ।।
mātā janiṣyate vāpi tathābhūtaṃ tapodhanam ।
viśvaṃ hi brahma tapasā mayā tatra samarpitam ।। 29.75 ।।
evamuktā mahābhāgā bhartrā satyavatī tadā।
prasādayāmāsa patiṃ suto me nedṛśo bhavet।
brāhmaṇāpasadastvanya ityukto munirabravīt ।। 29.76 ।।
naiṣa saṅkalpitaḥ kāmo mayā bhadre tathā tvayā ।
ugrakarmā bhavet putraḥ piturmātuśca kāraṇāt ।। 29.77 ।।
punaḥ satyavatī vākyamevamuktābravīdidam।
icchaँllokānapi mune sṛjethāḥ kiṃ punaḥ sutam ।। 29.78 ।।
śamātmakamṛjuṃ bharttaḥ putraṃ me dātumarhasi।
kāmamevaṃvidhaḥ putro mama syāttu vada prabho ।। 29.79 ।।
mayyanyathā na śakyaṃ vai kartumeva dvijottama।
tataḥ prasādamakarot sa tasyāstapaso balāt ।। 29.80 ।।
putre nāsti viśeṣo me pautre vā varavarṇini।
tvayā yathoktaṃ vacanaṃ tathā bhadre bhaviṣyati ।। 29.81 ।।
tasmāt satyavatī putraṃ janayāmāsa bhārgavam।
tapasyabhiratandāntaṃ jamadagniḥ śamātmakam ।। 29.82 ।।
bhṛgoścaruviparyāse raudravaiṣṇavayoḥ purā।
yamanādvaiṣṇavasyāgnerjamadagnirajāyata ।। 29.83 ।।
viśvāmitraṃ tu dāyādaṃ gādhiḥ kuśikanandanaḥ।
prāpya brahmarṣisahito (savitā) jagāma brahmaṇāvṛtaḥ ।। 29.84 ।।
sā hi satyavatī puṇyā satyavrataparāyaṇā।
kauśikīti samākhyātā pravṛtteyaṃ mahānadī ।। 29.85 ।।
parisrutā mahābhāgā kauśikī saritāṃ varā।
ikṣvākuvaṃśe tvabhavatsuveṇurnāma pārthivaḥ ।। 29.86 ।।
tasya kanyā mahābhāgā kāmalī nāma reṇukā।
ārcīko janayāmāsa jamadagniḥ sudāruṇam ।। 29.87 ।।
sarvavidyāntagaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dhanurvedasya pāragam।
rāmaṃ kṣatriya hantāraṃ pradīptamiva pāvakam ।। 29.88 ।।
aurvvasyaivamṛcīkasya satyavatyāṃ mahāmanāḥ।
jamadagnistato vīryyājjajñe brahmavidāṃ varaḥ।
madhyamaśca śunaḥśephaḥ śunaḥpucchaḥ kaniṣṭhakaḥ ।। 29.89 ।।
viśvāmitrastu dharmātmā nāmnā viśvarathaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
jajñe bhṛguprasādena kauśikādvaṃśavarddhanaḥ ।। 29.90 ।।
viśvāmitrasya putrastu śunaḥśepho'bhavanmuniḥ।
hariścandrasya yajñe tu paśutve niyutaḥ savai।
devairdattaḥ sa vai yasmāddevarātastato'bhavat ।। 29.91 ।।
viśvāmitrasya putrāṇāṃ śunaḥ śepho'grajaḥ smṛtaḥ।
madhucchando nayaścaiva kṛtadevau dhruvāṣṭakau ।। 29.92 ।।
kacchapaḥ pūraṇaścaiva viśvāmitrasutāstu vai।
teṣāṃ gotrāṇi bahudhā kauśikānāṃ mahātmanām ।। 29.93 ।।
pārthivā devarātāśca yājñavalkyā samarṣaṇāḥ ।
lohiṇyo reṇavaścaiva tathā kārīṣavaḥ smṛtāḥ।
babhravaḥ pāṇinaścaiva dhyāvajapyāstathaiva ca ।। 29.95 ।।
śālāvatyā hiraṇyākṣāḥ syaṅkṛtā gālavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
devalā yāmadūtāśca śālaṅkāyanabāṣkalāḥ ।। 29.96 ।।
dadāti bādarāścānye viśvāmitrasya dhīmataḥ।
ṛṣyantaravivāṅyāste bahavaḥ śauśikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 29.97 ।।
kauśikāsośrumāścaiva tathānye saidhavāyanāḥ।
pauroravasya puṇyasya brahmarṣeḥ kauśikasya tu ।। 29.98 ।।
dṛṣadvatīsutaścāpi viśvāmitrāttathāṣṭakaḥ।
aṣṭakasya suto yo hi prokto jahnugaṇomayā ।। 29.99 ।।
kiṃ lakṣaṇena dharmeṇa tapaseha śrutena vā।
brāhmaṇyaṃ samanuprāptaṃ viśvāmitrādibhirnṛpaiḥ ।। 29.100 ।।
yena yonābhidhā nena brāhmaṇyaṃ kṣatriyā gatāḥ ।
viśeṣaṃ jñātumicchāmi tapasā dānatastathā ।। 29.101 ।।
evamuktastato vākyamabravīdidamarthavat।
anyāyopagatairdravyairāhṛtya yajane dhiyā।
dharmābhikāṃkṣī yajate na dharmaphalamaśnute ।। 29.102 ।।
japaṃ kṛtvā tathā tīvraṃ dhanalobhānniraṅkuśaḥ।
rāgamohānvito hyante pāvanārthaṃ dadāti yaḥ ।। 29.104 ।।
tena dattāni dānāni aphalāni bhavantyuta।
tasya dharmmapravṛttasya hiṃsakasya durātmanaḥ ।। 29.105 ।।
evaṃ labdhvā dhanaṃ mohāddadato yajataśca ha।
sakliṣṭakarmaṇo dānaṃ na tiṣṭhati durātmanaḥ ।। 29.106 ।।
nyāyāgatānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ tīrthe sampratipādanam।
kāmānanabhisandhāya yajate ca dadāti ca ।। 29.107 ।।
sa dānaphalamāpnoti tacca dānaṃ sukhodayam।
dānena bhogānāpnoti svargaṃ satyena gacchati ।। 29.108 ।।
tapasā tu sutaptena lokān viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhati ।
saṃnyāsastapasaḥ śreyāṃstasmājjñānaṃ guruḥ smṛtam ।। 29.110 ।।
śrṛyante hi tapaḥsiddhāḥ kṣātropetā dvijātayaḥ।
viśvāmitro narapatirmāndhātā saṃkṛtiḥ kapiḥ ।। 29.111 ।।
ārṣṭiṣeṇo'mīḍhaśca bhāgānyonyastathaiva ca ।। 29.112 ।।
rathītaraśca rundaśca viṣṇuvṛddhādayo nṛpāḥ ।। 29.113 ।।
kṣātropetāḥ smṛtā hyete tapasā ṛṣitāṅgatāḥ ।
ete rājarṣayaḥ sarvve siddhiṃ sumahatīṅgatāḥ।
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi ayorvaṃśaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।। 29.114 ।।
pitā somasya vaiviprā jajñe'trirbhagavānṛṣiḥ।
karmaṇā manasā vācā śubhānyeva samācaran।
kāṣṭhakuḍyaśilābhūta ūrddhvabāhurmahādyutiḥ ॥ 2.28.2 ॥
suduścaraṃ nāma tapo yena taptaṃ mahatpurā।
trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi divyānīti hi naḥ śrutam ॥ 2.28.3 ॥
tasyorddhvaretasastatra sthitasyānimiṣaspṛham।
somatvantanurāpede mahābuddhiḥ sa vai dvijaḥ ॥ 2.28.4 ॥
ūrddhvamācakrame tasya somatvaṃ bhāvitātmanaḥ।
taṃ garbhaṃ vidhinādiṣṭā daśa devyo dadhustadā।
sametya dhārayāmāsurna ca tāḥ samaśaknuvan ॥ 2.28.6 ॥
sa tābhyaḥ sahasaivātha digbhyo garbhaḥ prabhānvitaḥ।
yathāvabhāsayaṃllokāñjhītāṃśuḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ ॥ 2.28.7 ॥
yadā na dhāraṇe śaktāstasya garbhasya tāḥ striyaḥ।
tataḥ sa tābhiḥ śītāṃśurnipapāta vasundharām ॥ 2.28.8 ॥
patantaṃ somamālokya brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ।
rathamāropayāmāsa lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ॥ 2.28.9 ॥
sa hi devamayo viprā dharmmārthī satyasaṅgaraḥ।
yukto vājisahasreṇa siteneti hi naḥ śrutam ॥ 2.28.10 ॥
tasminnipatite devāḥ putre'treḥ paramātmani।
tuṣṭuvurbrahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ mānasāḥ sapta viśrutāḥ ॥ 2.28.11 ॥
tatraivāṅgirasastasya bhṛgoścaivātmajastathā।
ṛgbhiryajurbhirbahubhiratharvāṅgirasairapi ॥ 2.28.12 ॥
tataḥ saṃstūyamānasya tejaḥ somasya bhāsvataḥ।
āpyāyamānaṃ lokāṃstrīn bhāvayāmāsa sarvvaśaḥ ॥ 2.28.13 ॥
samena rathamukhyena sāgarāntāṃ vasundharām।
triḥsaptakṛtvo vipula ścakārābhipradakṣiṇam ॥ 2.28.14 ॥
tasya yaccāpi tattejaḥ pṛthivīmanvapadyata।
oṣadhyastāḥ samudbhūtāstejasā saṃjvalantyuta ॥ 2.28.15 ॥
tābhirdhāryatyayaṃ lokān prajāścāpi caturvidhāḥ।
poṣṭā hi bhagavān somo jagato hi dvijottamāḥ ॥ 2.28.16 ॥
sa labdhatejāstapasā saṃstavaistaiśca karmmabhiḥ।
tapastepe mahābhāgaḥ pajhānāṃ daśatīrdaśa ॥ 2.28.17 ॥
hiraṇyavarṇā yā devyo dhārayantyātmanā jagat।
vibhustāsāmbhavetsomaḥ prakhyātaḥ svena karmmaṇā ॥ 2.28.18 ॥
tatastasmai dadau rājyaṃ brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥ।
bījauṣadhiṣu viprāṇāmapāñca dvijasattamāḥ ॥ 2.28.19 ॥
so'bhiṣikto mahātejā mahārājyena rājarāṭ ।
lokānāṃ bhāvayāmāsa svabhāvāttapatāṃ varaḥ ॥ 2.28.20 ॥
saptaviṃśatirindostu dākṣāyaṇyo mahāvratāḥ।
dadau prācetaso dakṣo nakṣatrāṇīti yā viduḥ ॥ 2.28.21 ॥
sa tatprāpya mahadrājayaṃ somaḥ somavatāṃ prabhuḥ।
samājajñe rājasūyaṃ sahasraśatadakṣiṇam ॥ 2.28.22 ॥
hiraṇyagarbhaścodgātā brahmā brahmatvameyivān।
sadasyastatra bhagavān harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।
sanatkumārapramukhairādyairbrahmarṣibhirvṛtaḥ ॥ 2.28.23 ॥
dakṣiṇāmadadatsomastrīlloँkāniti naḥ śrutam।
tebhyo brahmarṣimukhyebhyaḥ sadasyebhyaśca vai dvijāḥ ॥ 2.28.24 ॥
taṃ sinī ca kuhūścaiva vapuḥ puṣṭiḥ prabhāvasuḥ।
kīrttirdhṛtiśca lakṣmīśca nava devyaḥ siṣevire ॥ 2.28.25 ॥
prāpyāvabhṛthamavyagraḥ sarvvadevarṣipūjitaḥ।
atirājātirājendro daśadhātāpayaddiśaḥ ॥ 2.28.26 ॥
tadā tat prāpya duṣprāpamaiśvaryamṛṣisaṃstutam।
bṛhaspateḥ sa vai bhāryāntārāṃ nāma yaśasvinīm।
jahāra sahasā sarvvānavamatyāṅgiraḥsutān ॥ 2.28.28 ॥
sa yācyamāno devaiśca tathā devarṣibhiśca ha।
naiva vyasarjayattārāṃ tasmāyāṅgirase tadā ॥ 2.28.29 ॥
uśanāstasya jagrāha pārṣṇimaṅgiraso dvijāḥ।
sa hi śiṣyo mahātejāḥ pituḥ pūrvaṃ bṛhaspateḥ ॥ 2.28.30 ॥
tena snehena bhagavān rudrastasya bṛhaspateḥ।
pārṣṇigrāho'bhavaddevaḥ pragṛhyājagavandhanuḥ ॥ 2.28.31 ॥
tena brahmarṣimukhyebhyaḥ paramāstraṃ mahātmanā।
uddiśya devānutsṛṣṭaṃ yenaiṣāṃ nāśitaṃ yaśaḥ ॥ 2.28.32 ॥
tatra tadyuddhamabhavat pratyakṣantārakāmayam।
devānāṃ dānavānāñca lokakṣayakaraṃ mahat ॥ 2.28.33 ॥
tatra śiṣṭāstrayo devāstuṣitāścaiva ye smṛtāḥ।
brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmurādidevaṃ pitāmaham ॥ 2.28.34 ॥
tato nivāryośanasaṃ rudraṃ jyeṣṭhañca śaṅkaram।
dadāvāṅgirase tārāṃ svayameva pitāmahaḥ ॥ 2.28.35 ॥
antarvatnīṃ ca tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tārāntārādhipānanām।
garbhamutsṛjase na tvaṃ vipraḥ prāha bṛhaspatiḥ ॥ 2.28.36 ॥
madīyāyāṃ tanau yonau garbho dhāryaḥ kathañcana।
jātamātro'tha bhagavān devānāmākṣipadvapuḥ ॥ 2.28.38 ॥
tataḥ saṃśayamāpannāstārāmakathayan surāḥ।
satyaṃ brūhi sutaḥ kasya somasyātha bṛhaspateḥ ॥ 2.28.39 ॥
hrīyamāṇā yadā devānnāha sā sādhvasādhu vā ।
tadā tāṃ śaptumārabdhaḥ kumāro dasyuhantamaḥ ॥ 2.28.40 ॥
yadatra tathyantad‌brūhi tāre kasya sutastvayam ॥ 2.28.41 ॥
sā prāñjaliruvācedaṃ brahmāṇaṃ varadaṃ prabhum।
somasyeti mahātmānaṃ kumārandasyuhantamam ॥ 2.28.42 ॥
tataḥ sa tamupāghāya somo dātā prajāpatiḥ।
budha ityakaronnāma tasya putrasya dhīmataḥ ॥ 2.28.43 ॥
pratipūrvvañca gamane samabhyuttiṣṭhate budhaiḥ।
utpādayāmāsa tadā putraṃ vai rājaputrikā ॥ 2.28.44 ॥
tasya putro mahātejā babhūvailaḥ purūravāḥ ।
urvaśyāṃ jajñire tasya putrāḥ ṣaṭ sumahaujasaḥ ॥ 2.28.45 ॥
prasahya dharṣitastatra vivaśo rājayakṣmaṇā ।
tato yakṣmābhibhūtastu somaḥ prakṣīṇamaṇḍalaḥ ।
jagāma śaraṇāyātha pitaraṃ so'trimeva tu ॥ 2.28.46 ॥
tasya tatpāpaśamanaṃ cakārātrirmahāyaśāḥ।
sa rājayakṣmaṇā muktaḥ śriyā jajvāla sarvvaśaḥ ॥ 2.28.47 ॥
etatsomasya vai janma kīrttitaṃ dvijasattamāḥ।
vaṃśantasya dvijaśreṣṭāḥ kīrtyamānaṃ nibodhata ॥ 2.28.48 ॥
dhanyamārogyamāyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ kalmaṣaśodhanam।
somasya janma śrutvaiva sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ॥ 2.28.49 ॥
somasya tu budhaḥ putro budhasya tu purūravāḥ।
tejasvī dānaśīlaśca yajvā vipuladakṣiṇaḥ ॥ 2.29.1 ॥
brahmavādī parākrāntaḥ śatrubhiryudhi durjayaḥ।
āharttā cāgnihotrasya yajvanāñca dadau mahīm ॥ 2.29.2 ॥
satyavāk karmmabuddhiśca kāntaḥ saṃvṛtamaithunaḥ।
atīva putro lokeṣu rūpeṇāpratimo'bhavat ॥ 2.29.3 ॥
taṃ brahmavādinaṃ dāntaṃ dharmajñaṃ satyavādinam।
urvaśī varayāmāsa hitvā mānaṃ yaśasvinī ॥ 2.29.4 ॥
tayā sahāvasadrājā daśavarṣāṇi cāṣṭa ca।
sapta ṣaṭ sapta cāṣṭau ca daśa cāṣṭau ca vīryavān ॥ 2.29.5 ॥
vane caitrarathe ramye tathā mandākinītaṭe।
alakāyāṃ viśālāyāṃ nandane ca vanottame ॥ 2.29.6 ॥
gandhamādanapādeṣu meruśrṛṅge nagottame।
uttarāṃśca kurūn prāpya kalāpagrāmameva ca ॥ 2.29.7 ॥
eteṣu vanasukhyeṣu surairācariteṣu ca।
urvaśyā sahito rājā reme paramayā mudā ॥ 2.29.8 ॥
gandharvā corvaśī devī rājānaṃ mānuṣaṃ katham।
brahmaśāpābhibhūtā sā mānuṣaṃ samupasthitā।
ātmanaḥ śāpamokṣārthaṃ niyamaṃ sā cakāra tu ।
anagnadarśanañcaiva akāmāta saha maithunam ॥ 2.29.11 ॥
dvau meṣau śayanābhyāśe sa tāvad vyavatiṣṭhate।
ghṛtamātraṃ tathāhāraḥ kālamekantu pārthiva ॥ 2.29.12 ॥
yadyeṣa samayo rājan yāvatkālañca te dṛḍham।
tāvatkālantu vatsyāmi eṣa naḥ samayaḥ kṛtaḥ ॥ 2.29.13 ॥
tasyāstaṃ samayaṃ sarvaṃ sa rājā paryapālayat।
varṣāṇyatha catuḥṣaṣṭiṃ tadbhaktyā śāpamohitā।
urvaśī mānuṣaṃ prāptā gandharvvā ścintayānvitāḥ ॥ 2.29.15 ॥
cintayadhvaṃ mahābhāgā yathā sā tu varāṅganā।
āgacchettu punarddevānurvaśī svargabhūṣaṇā ॥ 2.29.16 ॥
eko'gniḥ pūrvamāsīdvai ailastrīṃstānakalpayat ॥ 2.29.45 ॥
evaṃprabhāvo rājāsīdailastu dvijasattamāḥ।
deśe puṇyatame caiva maharṣibhiralaṃkṛte ॥ 2.29.46 ॥
rājyaṃ sa kārayāmāsa prayāge pṛthivī patiḥ।
uttare yāmune tīre pratiṣṭāne mahāyaśāḥ ॥ 2.29.47 ॥
tasya putrā babhūvurhi ṣaḍindropamatejasaḥ।
gandharvvaloke viditā āyurddhīmānamāvasuḥ ॥ 2.29.48 ॥
viśvāyuśca śatāyuśca gatāyuścorvaśīsutāḥ।
amāvasostu vai jāto bhīmo rājātha viśvajit ॥ 2.29.49 ॥
śrīmān bhīmasya dāyādo rājāsītkāñcanaprabhaḥ।
vidvāṃstu kāñcanasyāpi suhotro'bhūnmahābalaḥ ॥ 2.29.50 ॥
suhotrasyābhajjahnuḥ keśikāgarbhasambhavaḥ।
pratigatya tato gaṅgā vitato yajñakarmmaṇi ॥ 2.29.51 ॥
plāvayāmāsa taṃ deśaṃ bhāvino'rthasya darśanāt।
gaṅgayā plāvitaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñavāṭaṃ samantataḥ ॥ 2.29.52 ॥
rājarṣiṇā tataḥ pītāṃ gaṅgāṃ dṛṣṭvā surarṣayaḥ ॥ 2.29.54 ॥
upaninyurmahābhāgā duhitṛtvena jāhnavīm।
yauvanāśvasya pautrīntu kāverīñjahnurāvahat ॥ 2.29.55 ॥
yuvanāśvasya śāpena gaṅgā yena vinirmame ।
kāverīṃ saritāṃ śreṣṭāṃ jahnubhāryyāmaninditām ॥ 2.29.56 ॥
jahnuśca dayitaṃ putraṃ suhotraṃ nāma dhārmikam।
kāveryyāṃ janayāmāsa ajakastasya cātmajaḥ ॥ 2.29.57 ॥
ajakasya tu dāyādo balākāśvo mahāyaśāḥ।
babhūvuśca gayaḥ śīlaḥ kuśastasyātmajaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.29.58 ॥
kuśaputrā babhūvuśca catvāro vedavarcasaḥ।
kuśāśvaḥ kuśanābhaśca amūrttārayaśovasuḥ ॥ 2.29.59 ॥
kuśastambastapastepe putrārthī rājasattamaḥ।
pūrṇe varṣasahasre vai śatakratumapaśyata ॥ 2.29.60 ॥
tamugratapasaṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasrākṣaḥ purandaraḥ।
samarthaḥ putrajanane svayamevāsya śāśvataḥ ॥ 2.29.61 ॥
putratvaṃ kalpayāmāsa svayameva purandaraḥ।
gādhirnāmābhavatputraḥ kauśikaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ ॥ 2.29.62 ॥
paurukutsābhavadbhāryā gādhistasyāmajāyata।
pūrvvaṃ kanyāṃ mahābhāgāṃ nāmnā satyavatīṃ śubhām।
tāṃ gādhiputraḥ kāvyāya ṛcīkāya dadau prabhuḥ ॥ 2.29.63 ॥
tasyāṃ putrastu vai bharttā bhārgavo bhṛgunandanaḥ।
putrārthe sādhayāmāsa caruṃ gādhestathaiva ca ॥ 2.29.64 ॥
upayojyaścarurayaṃ tvayā mātrā ca teśubhe ॥ 2.29.65 ॥
tasyāṃ janiṣyate putro dīptimān kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ।
ajeyaḥ kṣatriyairyuddhe kṣatriyarṣabhasūdanaḥ ॥ 2.29.66 ॥
tavāpi putraṃ kalyāṇi dhṛtintaṃ tapodhanam।
śamātmakaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ carureṣa vidhāsyati ॥ 2.29.67 ॥
evamuktvā tu tāṃ bhāryyāmṛcīko bhṛgunandanaḥ।
tapasyābhirato nityamaraṇyaṃ praviveśa ha ॥ 2.29.68 ॥
gādhiḥ sadārastu tadā ṛcīkāśramamabhyagāt।
tīrthayātrāprasaṅgena sutāṃ draṣṭuṃ nareśvaraḥ ॥ 2.29.69 ॥
carudvayaṃ gṛhītvā tu ṛṣeḥ satyavatī sadā।
bhartturvacanamavyagrā hṛṣṭā mātre nyavedayat ॥ 2.29.70 ॥
mātā tu tasyai daivena duhitre svaṃ caruṃ dadau ।
tasyāścarumathājñānādātmanaḥ sā cakāra ha ॥ 2.29.71 ॥
atha satyavatī garbhaṃ kṣatriyāntakaraṃ śubham।
dhārayāmāsa dīptena vapuṣā ghoradarśanā ॥ 2.29.72 ॥
tamṛcīkastato dṛṣṭvā yogenāpyanumṛśya ca।
tadābravīddvijaśreṣṭhaḥ svāṃ bhāryyāṃ varavarṇinīm ॥ 2.29.73 ॥
janiṣyati hi putraste krūrakarmātidāruṇaḥ ॥ 2.29.74 ॥
mātā janiṣyate vāpi tathābhūtaṃ tapodhanam ।
viśvaṃ hi brahma tapasā mayā tatra samarpitam ॥ 2.29.75 ॥
evamuktā mahābhāgā bhartrā satyavatī tadā।
prasādayāmāsa patiṃ suto me nedṛśo bhavet।
brāhmaṇāpasadastvanya ityukto munirabravīt ॥ 2.29.76 ॥
naiṣa saṅkalpitaḥ kāmo mayā bhadre tathā tvayā ।
ugrakarmā bhavet putraḥ piturmātuśca kāraṇāt ॥ 2.29.77 ॥
punaḥ satyavatī vākyamevamuktābravīdidam।
icchaँllokānapi mune sṛjethāḥ kiṃ punaḥ sutam ॥ 2.29.78 ॥
śamātmakamṛjuṃ bharttaḥ putraṃ me dātumarhasi।
kāmamevaṃvidhaḥ putro mama syāttu vada prabho ॥ 2.29.79 ॥
mayyanyathā na śakyaṃ vai kartumeva dvijottama।
tataḥ prasādamakarot sa tasyāstapaso balāt ॥ 2.29.80 ॥
putre nāsti viśeṣo me pautre vā varavarṇini।
tvayā yathoktaṃ vacanaṃ tathā bhadre bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.29.81 ॥
tasmāt satyavatī putraṃ janayāmāsa bhārgavam।
tapasyabhiratandāntaṃ jamadagniḥ śamātmakam ॥ 2.29.82 ॥
bhṛgoścaruviparyāse raudravaiṣṇavayoḥ purā।
yamanādvaiṣṇavasyāgnerjamadagnirajāyata ॥ 2.29.83 ॥
viśvāmitraṃ tu dāyādaṃ gādhiḥ kuśikanandanaḥ।
prāpya brahmarṣisahito (savitā) jagāma brahmaṇāvṛtaḥ ॥ 2.29.84 ॥
sā hi satyavatī puṇyā satyavrataparāyaṇā।
kauśikīti samākhyātā pravṛtteyaṃ mahānadī ॥ 2.29.85 ॥
parisrutā mahābhāgā kauśikī saritāṃ varā।
ikṣvākuvaṃśe tvabhavatsuveṇurnāma pārthivaḥ ॥ 2.29.86 ॥
tasya kanyā mahābhāgā kāmalī nāma reṇukā।
ārcīko janayāmāsa jamadagniḥ sudāruṇam ॥ 2.29.87 ॥
sarvavidyāntagaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dhanurvedasya pāragam।
rāmaṃ kṣatriya hantāraṃ pradīptamiva pāvakam ॥ 2.29.88 ॥
aurvvasyaivamṛcīkasya satyavatyāṃ mahāmanāḥ।
jamadagnistato vīryyājjajñe brahmavidāṃ varaḥ।
madhyamaśca śunaḥśephaḥ śunaḥpucchaḥ kaniṣṭhakaḥ ॥ 2.29.89 ॥
viśvāmitrastu dharmātmā nāmnā viśvarathaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
jajñe bhṛguprasādena kauśikādvaṃśavarddhanaḥ ॥ 2.29.90 ॥
viśvāmitrasya putrastu śunaḥśepho'bhavanmuniḥ।
hariścandrasya yajñe tu paśutve niyutaḥ savai।
devairdattaḥ sa vai yasmāddevarātastato'bhavat ॥ 2.29.91 ॥
viśvāmitrasya putrāṇāṃ śunaḥ śepho'grajaḥ smṛtaḥ।
madhucchando nayaścaiva kṛtadevau dhruvāṣṭakau ॥ 2.29.92 ॥
kacchapaḥ pūraṇaścaiva viśvāmitrasutāstu vai।
teṣāṃ gotrāṇi bahudhā kauśikānāṃ mahātmanām ॥ 2.29.93 ॥
pārthivā devarātāśca yājñavalkyā samarṣaṇāḥ ।
lohiṇyo reṇavaścaiva tathā kārīṣavaḥ smṛtāḥ।
babhravaḥ pāṇinaścaiva dhyāvajapyāstathaiva ca ॥ 2.29.95 ॥
śālāvatyā hiraṇyākṣāḥ syaṅkṛtā gālavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
devalā yāmadūtāśca śālaṅkāyanabāṣkalāḥ ॥ 2.29.96 ॥
dadāti bādarāścānye viśvāmitrasya dhīmataḥ।
ṛṣyantaravivāṅyāste bahavaḥ śauśikāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.29.97 ॥
kauśikāsośrumāścaiva tathānye saidhavāyanāḥ।
pauroravasya puṇyasya brahmarṣeḥ kauśikasya tu ॥ 2.29.98 ॥
dṛṣadvatīsutaścāpi viśvāmitrāttathāṣṭakaḥ।
aṣṭakasya suto yo hi prokto jahnugaṇomayā ॥ 2.29.99 ॥
kiṃ lakṣaṇena dharmeṇa tapaseha śrutena vā।
brāhmaṇyaṃ samanuprāptaṃ viśvāmitrādibhirnṛpaiḥ ॥ 2.29.100 ॥
yena yonābhidhā nena brāhmaṇyaṃ kṣatriyā gatāḥ ।
viśeṣaṃ jñātumicchāmi tapasā dānatastathā ॥ 2.29.101 ॥
evamuktastato vākyamabravīdidamarthavat।
anyāyopagatairdravyairāhṛtya yajane dhiyā।
dharmābhikāṃkṣī yajate na dharmaphalamaśnute ॥ 2.29.102 ॥
japaṃ kṛtvā tathā tīvraṃ dhanalobhānniraṅkuśaḥ।
rāgamohānvito hyante pāvanārthaṃ dadāti yaḥ ॥ 2.29.104 ॥
tena dattāni dānāni aphalāni bhavantyuta।
tasya dharmmapravṛttasya hiṃsakasya durātmanaḥ ॥ 2.29.105 ॥
evaṃ labdhvā dhanaṃ mohāddadato yajataśca ha।
sakliṣṭakarmaṇo dānaṃ na tiṣṭhati durātmanaḥ ॥ 2.29.106 ॥
nyāyāgatānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ tīrthe sampratipādanam।
kāmānanabhisandhāya yajate ca dadāti ca ॥ 2.29.107 ॥
sa dānaphalamāpnoti tacca dānaṃ sukhodayam।
dānena bhogānāpnoti svargaṃ satyena gacchati ॥ 2.29.108 ॥
tapasā tu sutaptena lokān viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhati ।
saṃnyāsastapasaḥ śreyāṃstasmājjñānaṃ guruḥ smṛtam ॥ 2.29.110 ॥
śrṛyante hi tapaḥsiddhāḥ kṣātropetā dvijātayaḥ।
viśvāmitro narapatirmāndhātā saṃkṛtiḥ kapiḥ ॥ 2.29.111 ॥
ārṣṭiṣeṇo'mīḍhaśca bhāgānyonyastathaiva ca ॥ 2.29.112 ॥
rathītaraśca rundaśca viṣṇuvṛddhādayo nṛpāḥ ॥ 2.29.113 ॥
kṣātropetāḥ smṛtā hyete tapasā ṛṣitāṅgatāḥ ।
ete rājarṣayaḥ sarvve siddhiṃ sumahatīṅgatāḥ।
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi ayorvaṃśaṃ mahātmanaḥ ॥ 2.29.114 ॥
ete putrā mahātmānaḥ pañcaivāsan mahābalāḥ।
svarbhānutanayā viprāḥ prabhāyāṃ jajñire nṛpāḥ ॥ 2.30.1 ॥
nahuṣaḥ prathamasteṣāṃ putradharmmā tataḥ smṛtaḥ।
dharmmavṛddhātmajaścaiva sutahotro mahāyaśāḥ ॥ 2.30.2 ॥
sutahotrasya dāyādāstrayaḥ paramadhārmmikāḥ।
kāśaḥ śalaśca dvāvetau tathā gṛtsamadaḥ prabhuḥ ॥ 2.30.3 ॥
putro gṛtsamadasyāpi śunako yasya śaunakaḥ।
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāścaiva vaiśyāḥ śūdrāstathaiva ca ॥ 2.30.4 ॥
etasya vaṃśe sambhūtā vicitraiḥ karmmabhirdvijāḥ।
śalātmajo hyārṣṭiṣeṇaścarantastasya cātmajaḥ ॥ 2.30.5 ॥
śaunakāścārṣṭiṣeṇāśca kṣātropetā dvijātayaḥ।
kāśasya kāśayo rāṣṭaḥ putro dīrghatapāstathā ॥ 2.30.6 ॥
dharmmaśca dīrghatapaso vidvān dhanvantaristataḥ।
tapasā sumahātejā jāto vṛddhasya dhīmataḥ।
athainamṛṣayaḥ procuḥ sūtaṃ vākyamimaṃ punaḥ ॥ 2.30.7 ॥
kathaṃ dhanvantarirddevo mānuṣeṣviha jajñivān।
etadveditumicchāmastato brūhi priyaṃ tathā ॥ 2.30.8 ॥
dhanvantareḥ sambhavo'yaṃ śrūyatāmiha vai dvijāḥ।
sa sambhūtaḥ samudrānte mathyamāne'mṛte purā ॥ 2.30.9 ॥
utpannaḥ sakalāt pūrvvaṃ sarvvataśca śriyāvṛtaḥ।
sarvvasaṃsiddhakāyaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā viṣṭambhitaḥ sthitaḥ।
ajastvamiti hovāca tasmādajastu saḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.30.10 ॥
ajaḥ provāca viṣṇuṃ taṃ tanayo'smi tava prabho।
vidhatsva bhāgaṃ sthānañca mama loke surottama ॥ 2.30.11 ॥
evamuktaḥ sudṛṣṭvā tu tathā provāca sa prabhuḥ ।
kṛto yajñavibhāgastu yajñiyaurhe suraistathā ॥ 2.30.12 ॥
vedeṣu vidhiyuktañca vidhihotraṃ maharṣibhiḥ।
na śakyamiha homo vai tulyaṃ karttuṃ kadācana ॥ 2.30.13 ॥
arvāksuto'si he deva nāmamantro'si vai prabho।
dvitīyāyāntu sambhūtyāṃ loke khyātiṅgamiṣyasi ॥ 2.30.14 ॥
tenaiva ca śarīreṇa devatvaṃ prāpsyasi prabho।
cārumantrairghṛtairgandhairyakṣyanti tvāṃ dvijātayaḥ ॥ 2.30.15 ॥
atha ca tvaṃ punaścaiva āyurvedaṃ vidhāsyasi।
avaśyambhāvī hyartho'yaṃ prāgdiṣṭastvabjayoninā ॥ 2.30.16 ॥
dvitīyaṃ dvāparaṃ prāpya bhavitā tvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ।
tasmāt tasmai varaṃ dattvā viṣṇurantardaghe tataḥ ॥ 2.30.17 ॥
dvitīye dvāpare prāpte saunahotraḥ sa kāśirāṭ।
putrakāma stapastepe nṛpo dīrghatapāstathā ॥ 2.30.18 ॥
ajaṃ devantu putrārthe hyārirādhayiṣurnṛpaḥ।
vareṇa cchandayāmāsa prīto dhanvantarirnṛpam ॥ 2.30.19 ॥
bhagavan yadi tuṣṭastvaṃ putro me dhṛtimān bhava।
tatheti samanujñāya tatraivāntaradhīyata ॥ 2.30.20 ॥
tasya gehe samutpanno devo dhanvantaristadā।
kāśirājo mahārājaḥ sarvvarogapraṇāśanaḥ ॥ 2.30.21 ॥
āyurvedaṃ bharadvājaścakāra sabhiṣakkriyam।
tamaṣṭadhā punarvyasya śiṣyebhyaḥ pratyapādayat ॥ 2.30.22 ॥
dhanvantarisutaścāpi ketumāniti viśrutaḥ।
atha ketumataḥ putro vibho bhīmaratho nṛpaḥ।
divodāsa iti khyāto vārāṇasyadhipo'bhavat ॥ 2.30.23 ॥
etasminneva kāle tu purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ purā।
śūnyāṃ viveśayāmāsa kṣeṇako nāma rākṣasaḥ ॥ 2.30.24 ॥
śaptā hi sā purī pūrvvaṃ nikumbhena mahātmanā।
śūnyā varṣasahasraṃ vai bhavitrīti punaḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.30.25 ॥
tasyāntu śaptamātrāyāṃ divodāsaḥ prajeśvaraḥ।
viṣayānte purīṃ ramyāṃ gomatyāṃ sannyaveśayat ॥ 2.30.26 ॥
vārāṇasīṃ kimarthantāṃ nikumbhaḥ śaptavān purā।
nikumbhaścāpi dharmmātmā siddhakṣetraṃ śaśāpa yaḥ ॥ 2.30.27 ॥
divodāsastu rājarṣirnagarīṃ prāpya pārthivaḥ।
vasate sa mahātejāḥ sphītāyāṃ vai narādhipaḥ ॥ 2.30.28 ॥
etasminneva kāle tu kṛtadāro maheśvaraḥ।
devyāḥ sa priyakāmastu vasānaśca surāntike ॥ 2.30.29 ॥
devājñayā pāriṣadā viśvarūpāstapodhanāḥ।
pūrvoktai rūpaviśeṣastoṣayanti maheśvarīm ॥ 2.30.30 ॥
hṛṣyati tairmahādevo menā naiva tu hṛṣyati।
jugupsate sā nityañca devaṃ devīṃ tathaiva ca ॥ 2.30.31 ॥
mama pārśve tvanācārastava bharttā maheśvaraḥ।
mātrā tathoktā vacasā strīsvabāvānnacākṣamat।
smitaṃ kṛtvā tu varadā harapārśvamathāgamat ॥ 2.30.33 ॥
viṣaṇṇavadanā devī mahādevamabhāṣata।
neha vatsyāmyahaṃ deva naya māṃ svaṃ niveśanam ॥ 2.30.34 ॥
tathoktastu mahādevaḥ sarvāṃllokānavekṣya ha।
vāsārthaṃ rocayāmāsa pṛthivyāṃ tu dvijottamāḥ।
vārāṇasīṃ mahātejāḥ siddhakṣetraṃ maheśvaraḥ ॥ 2.30.35 ॥
divo dāsena tāṃ jñātvā niviṣṭānnagarīṃ bhavaḥ।
pārśvāsthaṃ sa samāhūya gaṇeśaṃ kṣemakaṃ bravīt ॥ 2.30.36 ॥
gaṇeśvara purīṅgatvā sūnyāṃ vārāṇasīṃ kuru।
mṛdunā cābyupāyena ativīryaḥ sa pārthivaḥ ॥ 2.30.37 ॥
tato gatvā nikumbhastu purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ purā ।
svapne sandarśayāmāsa maṅkanaṃ nāma nāpitam ॥ 2.30.38 ॥
śreyaste'haṃ kariṣyāmi sthānaṃ me rocayānagha।
madrūpāṃ pratimāṃ kṛtvā nagaryyante niveśaya ॥ 2.30.39 ॥
tathā svapne yathā dṛṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ kāritavān dvijāḥ।
nagarīdvāryanujñāpya rājānantu yathāvidhi ॥ 2.30.40 ॥
pūjā tu mahatī caiva nityameva prayujyate।
gandhairdhūpaiśca mālyaiśca prekṣaṇīyaistathaiva ca ॥ 2.30.41 ॥
annapradānayuktaiśca atyadbhutamivābhavat।
evaṃ sampūjyate tatra nityameva gaṇeśvaraḥ ॥ 2.30.42 ॥
tato varasahasrāṇi nagarāṇāṃ prayacchati ।
putrān hiraṇyamāyūṃṣi sarvvakāmāṃstathaiva ca ॥ 2.30.43 ॥
rājñastu mahiṣī śreṣṭā suyaśā nāma viśrutā।
putrārthamāgatā sādhvī rājñā devī pracoditā ॥ 2.30.44 ॥
pūjāntu vipulāṃ kṛtvā devī putrānayācata।
punaḥ punarathāgamya bahuśaḥ putrakāraṇāt ॥ 2.30.45 ॥
na prayacchati putrāṃstu nikumbhaḥ kāraṇena tu।
atha dīrgheṇa kālena krodho rājānamāviśat।
bhūtaṃ tvidaṃ mahādvāri nagarāṇāṃ prayacchati ॥ 2.30.47 ॥
māmakaiḥ pūjyate nityaṃ nagaryāṃ mama caiva tu ॥ 2.30.48 ॥
tatrārccitaśca bahuśo devyā me tatra kāraṇāt ।
na dadāti ca putraṃ me kṛtaghno bahubhojanaḥ ॥ 2.30.49 ॥
ato nārhati pūjāntu matsakāśāt kathañcana।
tasmāttu nāśayiṣyāmi tasya sthānaṃ durātmanaḥ ॥ 2.30.50 ॥
evaṃ tu saviniścitya durātmā rāja kilbiṣī।
sthānaṃ gaṇapatestasya nāśayāmāsa durmatiḥ ॥ 2.30.51 ॥
bhagnamāyatanaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājānamagamat prabhuḥ।
yasmādṛte'parādhaṃ me tvayā sthānaṃ vinā śitam ॥ 2.30.52 ॥
akasmāt tu purī śūnyā bhavitrī te narādhipa।
tatastena tu śāpena śūnyā vārāṇasī tathā ॥ 2.30.53 ॥
śaptāṃ purīṃ nikumbhastu mahādevamathānayat।
śūnyāṃ purīṃ mahādevo nirmmame paramātmanā ॥ 2.30.54 ॥
tulyāṃ devavibhūtyāstu devyāścaiva mahātmanaḥ।
devyāḥ krīḍārthamīśāno devo vākyamathābravīt ॥ 2.30.56 ॥
nāhaṃ veśma vimokṣyāmi avimuktaṃ hi me gṛham।
prahasyaināmathovāca avimuktaṃ hi me gṛham ॥ 2.30.57 ॥
tasmāttadavimuktaṃ hi proktaṃ devena vai svayam ॥ 2.30.58 ॥
evaṃ vārāṇasī śaptā avimuktaṃ ca kīrttitam।
yasmin vasati vai devaḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ।
yugeṣu triṣu dharmātmā saha devyā maheśvaraḥ ॥ 2.30.59 ॥
antarddhānaṃ kalau yāti tatpurantu mahātmanaḥ।
antarhite pure tasmin purī sā vasate punaḥ ॥ 2.30.60 ॥
evaṃ vārāṇasī śaptā niveśaṃ punarāgatā।
bhadraśreṇyasya putrāṇāṃ śatamuttamadhanvinām ॥ 2.30.61 ॥
hatvā niveśayāmāsa divodāso narādhipaḥ।
bhadraśreṇyasya rājyantu hṛtantena balīyasā ॥ 2.30.62 ॥
bhadraśreṇyasya putrastu durdamo nāma nāmataḥ।
divodāsena bāleti ghṛṇayā sa vivarjitaḥ ॥ 2.30.63 ॥
divodāsādṝṣadvatyāṃ vīro jajñe pratarddanaḥ।
tena putreṇa bālena prahṛtaṃ tasya vai punaḥ ॥ 2.30.64 ॥
vairasyāntaṃ mahārājñā tadā tena vidhatsatā।
pratarddanasya putrau dvau vatso gargaśca viśrutaḥ ॥ 2.30.65 ॥
vatsaputro hyalarkastu sannatistasya cātmajaḥ ।
alarkaṃ prati rājarṣirgītaślokau purātanau ॥ 2.30.66 ॥
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭivarṣaśatāni ca।
yuvā rūpeṇa sampanno hyalarkaḥ kāśisattamaḥ ॥ 2.30.67 ॥
lopāmudrā prasādena paramāyuravāptavān ॥ 2.30.68 ॥
śāpasyānte mahābāhurhatvā kṣemakarākṣasam।
ramyāmāvāsayāmāsa purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ nṛpaḥ ॥ 2.30.69 ॥
sannaterapi dāyādaḥ sunītho nāma dhārmikaḥ।
sunīthasya tu dāyādaḥ suketurnāma dhārmmikaḥ ॥ 2.30.70 ॥
suketutanayaścāpi dharmaketuriti śrutiḥ।
dharmaketostu dāyādaḥ satyaketurmahārathaḥ ॥ 2.30.71 ॥
satyaketusutaścāpi vibhurnāma prajeśvaraḥ।
suvibhustu vibhoḥ putraḥ sukumārastataḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.30.72 ॥
sukumārasya putrastu dhṛṣṭaketuḥ sa dhārmmikaḥ।
dhuṣṭaketostu dāyādo veṇuhotraḥ prajeśvaraḥ ॥ 2.30.73 ॥
veṇuhotrasutaścāpi gārgyo vai nāma viśrutaḥ।
gārgyasya gargabhūmistu vātsyo vatsasya dhīmataḥ ॥ 2.30.74 ॥
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāścaiva tayoḥ putrāḥ sudhārmmikāḥ।
vikrāntā balavantaśca siṃhatulyaparākramāḥ ॥ 2.30.75 ॥
ityete kāśyapāḥ proktā rajerapi nibodhata।
rajeḥ putraśatānyāsan pañca vīryavato bhuvi।
rājeyamiti vikhyātaṃ kṣatramindrabhayāvaham ॥ 2.30.76 ॥
tadā daivāsure yuddhe samutpanne sudāruṇe।
devāścaivāsurāścaiva pitāmahamathābruvan ॥ 2.30.77 ॥
āvayorbhagavān yuddhe vijetā ko bhaviṣyati।
brūhi naḥ sarvvalokeśa śrotumicchāmahe vayam ॥ 2.30.78 ॥
yeṣāmarthāya saṃgrāme rajirāttāyudhaḥ prabhuḥ।
yotsyate te vijeṣyanti trīlloँkānnātra saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.30.79 ॥
rajiryatastato lakṣmīryato lakṣmīstato dhṛtiḥ।
yato dhṛtistato dharmo yato dharmastato jayaḥ ॥ 2.30.80 ॥
taddevā dānavāḥ sarve tataḥ śrutvā rajerjayam।
abhyayurjayamicchantaḥ stuvanto rājasattamam ॥ 2.30.81 ॥
te hṛṣṭamanasaḥ śarve rājānaṃ devadānavāḥ।
ūcurasmajjayāya tvaṃ gṛhāṇa varakārmukam ॥ 2.30.82 ॥
ahañjeṣyāmi no yuddhe devān śakrapurogamān।
indro bhavāmi dharmātmā tato yotsyāmi saṃyuge ॥ 2.30.83 ॥
asmākamindraḥ prahlādastasyārthe vijayāmahe।
asmistu samaye rājaṃstiṣṭethādeva no'diteḥ ॥ 2.30.84 ॥
sa tatheti bruvanneva devairapyabhicoditaḥ।
bhaviṣyasīndro jitveti devairapi nimantritaḥ ॥ 2.30.85 ॥
jaghāna dānavān sarvvān samakṣaṃ vajrapāṇinaḥ।
sa vipranaṣṭāṃ devānāṃ paramaśrīḥ śriyaṃ vaśī ॥ 2.30.86 ॥
nihatya dānavān sarvvān vyājahāra rajiḥ prabhuḥ।
taṃ tathā tu rajhiṃ tatra devaissaha śatakratuḥ ॥ 2.30.87 ॥
rajiputro'hamityuktvā punarevābravīdvacaḥ।
īndro'si rājan devānāṃ sarveṣānnātra saṃśayaḥ।
yasyāhamindraputraste khyātiṃ yāsyāmi śatruhan ॥ 2.30.88 ॥
sa tu śakravacaḥ śrutvā vañcitastena māyayā।
tathetyevābravīdrājā prīyamāṇaḥ śatakratum ॥ 2.30.89 ॥
tasmiṃstu devasadṛśe divaṃ prāpte mahīpatau।
dāyādyamindrādājahrurācāraṃ tanayā rajeḥ ॥ 2.30.90 ॥
tāni putraśatānyasya tacca sthānaṃ śacīpateḥ।
samakrāmanta bahudhā svargalokaṃ triviṣṭapam ॥ 2.30.91 ॥
tataḥ kāle bahutithe satīte mahābalaḥ।
hṛtarājyo'bravīcchakro hṛtabhāgo bṛhaspatim ॥ 2.30.92 ॥
badarīphalamātraṃ vai puroḍāśaṃ vidhatsva me।
brahmarṣe yena tiṣṭeyaṃ tejasāpyāyitastataḥ ॥ 2.30.93 ॥
brahman kṛśo'yaṃ vimanā hṛtarājyo hṛtāśanaḥ।
hataujā durbalo mūḍho rajiputraiḥ prasīda me ॥ 2.30.94 ॥
yadyevaṃ coditaḥ śakra tvayā syāṃ pūrvvameva hi।
nābhaviṣyat tvatpriyārthaṃ nākarttavyaṃ mamānagha ॥ 2.30.95 ॥
prayatiṣyāmi devendra taddhitārthaṃ mahādyute।
yathā bhāgañca rājyañca acirāt pratipatsyase ॥ 2.30.96 ॥
tathā śakra gamiṣyāmi mābhūtte viklavaṃ manaḥ।
tataḥ karmma cakārāsya tejaḥsaṃvarddhanaṃ mahat ॥ 2.30.97 ॥
teṣāñca buddhisaṃmohamakarodbuddhisattamaḥ।
brahmadviṣaśca saṃvṛttā hatavīryyaparākramāḥ।
tato lebhe suraiśvaryamaindrasthānaṃ tathottamam ॥ 2.30.99 ॥
hatvā rajisutān sarvānkāmakrodhaparāyaṇān।
ya idaṃ pāvanaṃ sthānaṃ pratiṣṭānaṃ śatakratoḥ।
śrṛṇuyādvā rajervāpi na sa daurātmyamāpnuyāt ॥ 2.30.100 ॥
marutena kathaṃ kanyā rājñe dattā mahātmanā।
kiṃvīryāśca mahātmāno jātā marutakanyakāḥ ॥ 2.31.1 ॥
āhavan taṃ marutsomamannakāmaḥ prajeśvaram।
māsi māsi mahātejāḥ ṣaṣṭisaṃvatsarānnṛpaḥ ॥ 2.31.2 ॥
tena te marutastasya marutsomena toṣitāḥ।
akṣayyānnaṃ daduḥ prītāḥ sarvakāmaparicchadam ॥ 2.31.3 ॥
annaṃ tasya sakṛtpakvamahorātre na kṣīyate।
koṭiśo dīyamānaṃ ca sūryyasyodayanādapi ॥ 2.31.4 ॥
mitrājyotistu kanyāyāṃ marutasya ca dhīmataḥ।
tasmājjātā mahāsattvā dharmajñā mokṣadarśinaḥ ॥ 2.31.5 ॥
saṃnyasya gṛhadharmāṇi vairāgyaṃ samupasthitāḥ।
yatidharmamavāpyeha brahmabhūyāya te gatāḥ ॥ 2.31.6 ॥
kṣatradharmastato jātaḥ pratipakṣo mahātapāḥ ॥ 2.31.7 ॥
pratipakṣasutaścāpi sañjayo nāma viśrutaḥ।
sañjayasya jayaḥ putro vijayastasya jagmivān ॥ 2.31.8 ॥
vijayasya jayaḥ putrastasya haryandvataḥ smṛtaḥ ।
haryandutastato rājā sahadevaḥ pratāpavān ॥ 2.31.9 ॥
sahadevasya dharmātmā adīna iti viśrutaḥ।
adīnasya jayatsenastasya putro'tha saṃkṛtiḥ ॥ 2.31.10 ॥
saṃkṛterapi dharmātmā kṛtadharmā mahāyaśāḥ।
ityete kṣatra dharmāṇo nahuṣasya nibodhata ॥ 2.31.11 ॥
nahuṣasya tu dāyādāḥ ṣaḍindropamatejasaḥ।
yatirjyeṣṭhastu teṣāṃ vai yayātistu tato'varaḥ ॥ 2.31.13 ॥
kākutsthakanyāṃ gāṃ nāma lebhe patnīṃ yatistadā।
saṃyātirmo kṣamāsthāya brahmabhūto'bhavanmuniḥ ॥ 2.31.14 ॥
teṣāṃ madhye tu pañcānāṃ yayātiḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ।
devayānimuśanasaḥ sutāṃ bhāryāmavāpa ha ॥ 2.31.15 ॥
śarmiṣṭā māsurīṃ caiva tanayāṃ vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ।
yaduṃ ca turvasuṃ caiva devayānirvyajāyata ॥ 2.31.16 ॥
druhyuñcānuñca pūruñca śarmiṣṭā vārṣaparvaṇī ।
ajījananmahāvīryān sutāndevasutopamān ॥ 2.31.17 ॥
rathantasmai dadau rudraḥ prītaḥ paramabhāsvaram।
asaṅgaṃ kāñcanaṃ divyamakṣayau ca maheṣudhī ॥ 2.31.18 ॥
yuktaṃ mano javairaśvairyena kanyāṃ samudvahat।
sa tena rathamukhyena jigāya ca tato mahīm ॥ 2.31.19 ॥
yayātiryudhi durddharṣo devadānavamānavaiḥ ।
pauravāṇāṃ nṛpāṇāñca sarveṣāṃ so'bhavadrathaḥ ॥ 2.31.20 ॥
yovatsudeśaprabhavaḥ kauravo janamejayaḥ।
kuroḥ putrasya rājñastu rājñaḥ pārikṣitasya ha।
jagāma sa ratho nāśaṃ śāpādgārgyasya dhīmataḥ ॥ 2.31.21 ॥
gārgyasya hi sutaṃ bālaḥ sa rājā janamejayaḥ।
durbuddhirhiṃsayāmāsa lohagandhaṃ narādhipam ॥ 2.31.22 ॥
sa lohagandho rājarṣiḥ paridhāvannitastataḥ।
paurajānapadaistyakto na lebhe śarma karhicit ॥ 2.31.23 ॥
tataḥ sa duḥkhasantapto nālabhatsaṃvidaṃ kvacit।
śaśāpa hetukamṛṣiṃ śaraṇyaṃ vyathitastadā ॥ 2.31.24 ॥
īndroto nāma vikhyāto yo'sau munirudāradhīḥ।
yojayāmāsa cendrotaḥ śaunako janamejayam।
aśvamedhena rājānaṃ pāvanārthaṃ dvijottamaḥ ॥ 2.31.25 ॥
sa lohagandho vyanaśattasyāvasathametya ha।
sa ca divyo rathastasmādvasoścedipatestathā ॥ 2.31.26 ॥
tataḥ śakreṇa tuṣṭena lebhe tasmādbṛhadrathaḥ।
tato hatvā jarāsandhaṃ bhīmastaṃ rathamuttamam।
pradadau vāsudevāya prītyā kauravanandanaḥ ॥ 2.31.27 ॥
sa jarāṃ prāpya rājarṣiryayātirnahuṣātmajaḥ।
putraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ variṣṭhañca yadumityabravīdvacaḥ ॥ 2.31.28 ॥
jarāvalī ca māṃ tāta palitāni ca paryaguḥ ।
kāvyasyośanasaḥ śāpānna ca tṛpto'smi yauvane ॥ 2.31.29 ॥
tvaṃ yado pratipadyasva pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha।
jarāṃ me pratigṛhṇīṣva taṃ yaduḥ pratyuvāca ha ॥ 2.31.30 ॥
anirdiṣṭā mayā bhikṣā brāhmaṇasya pratiśrutā ।
sā ca vyāyāmasādhyā vai na grahīṣyāmi te jarām ॥ 2.31.31 ॥
jarāyā bahavo doṣā pānabhojanakāriṇaḥ।
tasmājjarānna te rājan grahītumahamutsahe ॥ 2.31.32 ॥
sitaśmaśrudharo dīno jarayā śithilīkṛtaḥ।
balī sannatagātraśca durddaśo durbalākṛtiḥ ॥ 2.31.33 ॥
aśaktaḥ kāryakaraṇe paribhūtastu yauvane।
mahopabhītibhiścaiva tāṃ jarānnābhikāmaye ॥ 2.31.34 ॥
santi te bahavaḥ putrā mattaḥ priyatarā nṛpa।
pratigṛhṇantu dharmajña putramanyaṃ vṛṇīṣva vai ॥ 2.31.35 ॥
sa evamukto yadunā tīvrakopasamanvitaḥ।
uvāca vadatāṃ śreṣcho jyeṣṭhaṃ taṃ garhayan sutam ॥ 2.31.36 ॥
āśramaḥ kaśca vānyo'sti ko vā dharmavidhistava।
māmanādṛtya durbuddhe yadāttha navadeśika ॥ 2.31.37 ॥
evamuktvā yaduṃ rājā śaśāpainaṃ sa manyumān ।
yastvaṃ me hṛdayājjāto vayaḥ svaṃ na prayacchasi ॥ 2.31.38 ॥
tasmānna rājyabhāg mūḍha prajā te vai bhaviṣyati।
turvaso pratipadyasva pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha ॥ 2.31.39 ॥
na kāmaye jarāṃ tāta sāmabhogapraṇāśinīm।
jarāyā bahavo doṣāḥ pānabhojanakāriṇaḥ।
tasmājjarāṃ na te rājan grahītumahamutsahe ॥ 2.31.40 ॥
yastvaṃ me hṛdayājjāto vayaḥ svanna prayacchasi।
tasmāt prajā samucchedaṃ turvaso tava yāsyati ॥ 2.31.41 ॥
asaṅkīrṇā ca dharmeṇa pratilomavareṣu ca।
piśitādiṣu cānyeṣu mūḍha rājā bhaviṣyasi ॥ 2.31.42 ॥
guru dāraprasakteṣu tiryagyonigateṣu vā।
paśudharmeṣu mleccheṣu bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.31.43 ॥
evantu turvasuṃ śaptvā yayātiḥ sutamātmanaḥ।
śarmiṣṭāyāḥ sutaṃ druhyumidaṃ vacanamabravīt ॥ 2.31.44 ॥
druhyo tvaṃ pratipadyasva varṇarūpavināśinīm।
jarāṃ varṣasahasraṃ vai yauvanaṃ svandadasva me ॥ 2.31.45 ॥
pūrṇe varṣasahasre te pratidāsyāmi yauvanam।
svañcādāsyāmi būyo'haṃ pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha ॥ 2.31.46 ॥
na gajaṃ na rathaṃ nāśvaṃ jīrṇo bhuṅkte na ca striyam ।।
na saṅgaścāsya bhavati na jarāṃ tena kāmaye ॥ 2.31.47 ॥
yastvaṃ me hṛdayājjāto vayaḥ svanna prayacchasi।
tasmād druhyo priyaḥ kāmo na te sampatsyate kvacit ॥ 2.31.48 ॥
nauplavottarasañcārastatra nityaṃ bhaviṣyati।
arājabhrājavaṃśastvaṃ tatra nityaṃ bhaviṣyasi ॥ 2.31.49 ॥
ano tvaṃ pratipadyasva pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha।
evaṃ varṣasahasrantu careyaṃ yauvanena te ॥ 2.31.50 ॥
jīrṇaḥ śiśuvaraṃ datte jarayā hyaśuciḥ sadā।।
na juhoti sa kāle'gni tāṃ jarānnābikāmaye ॥ 2.31.51 ॥
yastvaṃ me hṛdayājjāto vayaḥ svanna prayacchasi।
jarādoṣastvayokto'yaṃ tasmātte pratipatsyate ॥ 2.31.52 ॥
prajā ca yauvanaṃ prāptā vinaśiṣyatyatastava।
agnipraskandanaparastvaṃ cāpyeva bhaviṣyasi ॥ 2.31.53 ॥
pūro tvaṃ pratipadyasva pāpmānañjarayā saha।
jarāvalī ca māntāta palitāni ca paryaguḥ ॥ 2.31.54 ॥
kāvyasyośanasaḥ śāpānna ca tṛpto'smi yauvane।
kañcitkālañjareyaṃ vai viṣayān vayasā tava ॥ 2.31.55 ॥
pūrṇeṃ varṣasahasre te pratidāsyāmi yauvanam।
svañcaiva pratipatsyāmi pāpmānañjarayā saha ॥ 2.31.56 ॥
evamuktaḥ pratyuvāca putraḥ pitaramañjasā।
yathānumanyase tāta kariṣyāmi tathaiva ca ॥ 2.31.57 ॥
pratipatsyāmi te rājan pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha।
gṛhāṇa yauvanaṃ mattaścara kāmān yathepsitān ॥ 2.31.58 ॥
jarayāhaṃ praticchanno vayorūpadharastava।
yauvanaṃ bhavate dattvā cariṣyāmi yathārtavat ॥ 2.31.59 ॥
pūro prīto'smi bhadrante prītaścedaṃ dadāmi te।
sarvakāmasamṛddhā te prajā rājye bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.31.60 ॥
pūroranumato rājā yayātiḥ svāṃ jarāntataḥ।
saṃkrāmayāmāsa tadā prasādādbhārgavasya tu ॥ 2.31.61 ॥
yauvanenātha vayasā yayātiranahuṣātmajaḥ ।
prītiyukto naraśreṣṭhaścacāra viṣayān svakān ॥ 2.31.62 ॥
yathākāmaṃ yathotsāhaṃ yathākālaṃ yathāsukham।
dharmmāvirodhādrājendro yathārhati sa eva hi ॥ 2.31.63 ॥
devānatarpayadyajñaiḥ pitṝñchrāddhaistathaiva ca।
dīnāṃścānugrahairiṣṭaiḥ kāmaiśca dvijasattamān ॥ 2.31.64 ॥
atithīnannapānaiśca vaiśyāṃśca paripālanaiḥ।
ānṛśaṃsyena śūdrāṃśca dasyūn saṃnigraheṇa ca ॥ 2.31.65 ॥
dharmmeṇa ca prajāḥ sarvvā yathāvadanurañjayan।
yayātiḥ pālayāmāsa sākṣādindra ivāparaḥ ॥ 2.31.66 ॥
sa rājā siṃhavikrānto yuvā viṣayagocaraḥ।
avirodhena dharmasya cacāra sukhamuttamam ॥ 2.31.67 ॥
sa mārgamāṇaḥ kāmānāmantardoṣanidarśanāt।
viśvāsaheto reme vai vaibrāje nandane vane ॥ 2.31.68 ॥
apaśyatsa yadā tāṃ vai varddhamānāṃ nṛpastadā।
gatvā pūroḥ sakāśaṃ vai svāṃ jarā pratyapadyata ॥ 2.31.69 ॥
sa samprāpya tu tān kāmāṃstṛptaḥ khinnaśca pārthivaḥ।
kālaṃ varṣasahasraṃ vai sasmāra manujādhipaḥ। ॥ 2.31.70 ॥
parisaṅkhyāya kālañca kalākāṣṭāstathaiva ca।
pūrṇaṃ mattvā tataḥ kālaṃ pūruṃ putramuvāca ha ॥ 2.31.71 ॥
yathāsukhaṃ yathotsāhaṃ yathākālamariṃdama।
sevitā viṣayāḥ putra yauvanena mayā tava ॥ 2.31.72 ॥
pūro prīto'smi bhadraṃ te gṛhāṇa tvaṃ svayauvanam।
brāhmaṇapramukhā varṇā idaṃ vacanamabruvan ॥ 2.31.73 ॥
pratipede jarāṃ rājā yayātirnahuṣātmajaḥ।
yauvanaṃ pratipede ca pūruḥ svaṃ punarātmanaḥ ॥ 2.31.74 ॥
abhiṣektukāmañca nṛpaṃ pūruṃ putraṃ kanīyasam।
brāhmaṇapramukhā varṇā idaṃ vacanamabruvan ॥ 2.31.75 ॥
kathaṃ śukrasya naptāraṃ devayānyāḥ sutaṃ prabho।
śreṣṭhaṃ yadumatikramya pūro rājyaṃ pradāsyasi ॥ 2.31.76 ॥
yadurjyeṣṭhastava suto jātastamanu turvasuḥ।
śarmiṣṭāyāḥ suto druhyustano'nuḥ pūrureva ca ॥ 2.31.77 ॥
kathaṃ jyeṣṭānatikramya kanīyān rājyamarhati ।
ataḥ sambodhayāmi tvāṃ dharmmaṃ samanupālaya ॥ 2.31.78 ॥
brāhmaṇapramukhā varṇāḥ sarve śrṛṇvantu me vacaḥ।
jyeṣṭaṃ prati yathā rārṣṭraṃ na deyaṃ me kathañcana ॥ 2.31.79 ॥
mātā pitrorvacanakṛtsa hi putraḥ praśasyate ।
mama jyeṣṭena yadunā niyogo nānupālitaḥ ॥ 2.31.80 ॥
pratikūlaṃ pituryaśca na sa putraḥ satāṃ mataḥ।
sa putraḥ putravad yaśca varttate pitṛmātṛṣu ॥ 2.31.81 ॥
yadunāhamavajñātastathā turvasunāpi ca।
druhyuṇā cānunā caivamapyavajñā kṛtā bhṛśam ॥ 2.31.82 ॥
pūruṇā tu kṛtaṃ vākyaṃ mānitaśca viśeṣataḥ।
kanīyān mama dāyādo jarā yena dhṛtā mama।
sarvakāmaḥ sarvakṛtaḥ pūruṇā putrakāriṇā ॥ 2.31.83 ॥
śukreṇa ca varo dattaḥ kāvye nośanasā svayam।
putro yastvānuvartteta sa rājā te mahāmate ॥ 2.31.84 ॥
bhavato'numatopyevaṃ pūru rāṣṭre'bhiṣicyatām ।
yaḥputro guṇasampanno mātāpitrorhitaḥ sadā।
sarvamarhati kalyāṇaṃ kanīyānapi sa prabhuḥ ॥ 2.31.85 ॥
varadānena śukrasya na śakyaṃ vaktumuttaram ॥ 2.31.86 ॥
paurajānapadaistuṣṭairityukto nāhuṣastadā।
abhiṣicya tataḥ pūruṃ svarāṣṭre sutamātmanaḥ ॥ 2.31.87 ॥
diśi dakṣiṇapūrvasyāṃ turvasuṃ tu nyaveśayat।
dakṣiṇāparato rājā yaduṃ śreṣṭhaṃ nyaveśayat ॥ 2.31.88 ॥
pratīcyāmuttarasyāñca druhyuñcānuñca tāvubhau।
saptadvīpāṃ yayātistu jittvā pṛthvīṃ sasāgarām।
vyabhajat pañcadhā rājā putrebhyo nāhuṣastadā ॥ 2.31.89 ॥
tairiyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā sapattanā।
yathāpradeśaṃ dharmajñairdharmmeṇa pratipālyate ॥ 2.31.90 ॥
evaṃ visṛjya pṛthivīṃ putrebhyo nāhuṣastadā।
putrasaṃkrāmitaśrīstu prītimānabhavannṛpaḥ ॥ 2.31.91 ॥
dhanurnyasya pṛṣatkāṃśca rājyañcaiva suteṣu tu।
prītimānabhavadrājā bhāramāveśya bandhuṣu ॥ 2.31.92 ॥
atra gāthā mahārājñā purā gītā yayātinā।
yo'bhipretyāharan kāmān kūrmoṅgānīva sarvaśaḥ ॥ 2.31.93 ॥
na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānāmupabhogena śāmyati।
haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivarddhate ॥ 2.31.94 ॥
yat pṛthivyāṃ vrīhiyavaṃ hiraṇyaṃ paśavaḥ striyaḥ ।
nālamekasya tatsarvamiti paśyanna muhyati ॥ 2.31.95 ॥
yadā tu kurute bhāvaṃ sarvvabhūteṣu pāvakam।
karmmaṇā manasā vācā brahma sampadyate tadā ॥ 2.31.96 ॥
yadā parānna bibheti yadā tvasmānna bibhyati।
yadā necchati na dveṣṭi brahma sampadyate tadā ॥ 2.31.97 ॥
yā dustyajā durmmatibhiryā na jīryati jīryyataḥ।
doṣāprāṇāntiko rāgastāṃ tṛṣṇāntyajataḥ sukham ॥ 2.31.98 ॥
jīryyanti jīryataḥ kośā dantā jīryanti jaryitaḥ।
jīvitāśā dhanāśā ca jīryyatopi na jīryati ॥ 2.31.99 ॥
yaccākāmasukhaṃ loke yacca divyaṃ mahat sukham।
tṛṣṇāsya ca sukhasyaiva kalāṃ nārhati ṣoḍaśīm ॥ 2.31.100 ॥
evamuktvā sa rājarṣiḥ sadāraḥ prasthito vanam।
bhṛgutuṅge tapastaptvā tatraiva ca mahāyaśāḥ।
pālayitvā vrataśataṃ tatraiva svargamāpnuyāt ॥ 2.31.101 ॥
tasya vaṃśāstu pañcaite puṇyā devarṣisatkṛtāḥ।
yairvyāptā pṛthivī kṛtsnā sūryasyeva gabhastibhiḥ ॥ 2.31.102 ॥
dhanyaḥ prajāvānāyuṣmān kīrtimāṃśca bhavennaraḥ।
yayāteścaritaṃ sarvaṃ paṭhañchṛṇvan dvijottamaḥ ॥ 2.31.103 ॥
yadorvaṃśaṃ pravakṣyāmi śreṣṭhasyottamatejhasaḥ।
vistareṇānupūrvyeṇa gadato me nibodhata ॥ 2.32.1 ॥
yadoḥ putrā babhūvurhi pañca devasutopamāḥ।
sahasrajidatha śreṣṭhaḥ kroṣṭurnīlo jito laghuḥ ॥ 2.32.2 ॥
sahasrajitsutaḥ śrīmāñchatajinnāma pārthivaḥ।
satajitsutā vikhyā tāstrayaḥ paramadhārmikāḥ ॥ 2.32.3 ॥
haihayaśca hayaścaiva rājā veṇuhayaśca yaḥ।
haihayasya tu dāyādo dharmmatattva iti śrutiḥ ॥ 2.32.4 ॥
dharmmatantrastu kīrttistu saṃjñeyastasya cātmajaḥ।
saṃjñeyasya tu dāyādo mahiṣmānnāma pārthivaḥ ॥ 2.32.5 ॥
āsīnmahiṣmataḥ putro bhadraśreṇyaḥ pratāpavān।
vārāṇasyadhipo rājā kathitaḥ pūrva eva hi ॥ 2.32.6 ॥
bhadraśreṇyasya dāyādo durmado nāma pārthivaḥ।
durmadasya tato dhīmān kanko nāma viśrutaḥ ॥ 2.32.7 ॥
kanakasya tu dāyādāścatvāro lokaviśrutāḥ।
kṛta vīryaḥ kārtavīryaḥ kṛtavarmā tathaiva ca ॥ 2.32.8 ॥
kṛto jātaścaturtho'bhūtkṛtaviryāttato'rjunaḥ।
jajñe bāhusahasreṇa saptadvīpeśvaro nṛpaḥ ॥ 2.32.9 ॥
sa hi varṣāyutaṃ taptvā tapaḥ paramaduścaram।
dattamārādhayāmāsa kārttavīryo'trisambhavam ॥ 2.32.10 ॥
tasmai datto varān prādāccaturo bhūritejasaḥ।
pūrvvaṃ bāhusahasrantu sa vavre prathamaṃ varam ॥ 2.32.11 ॥
adharmme dīyamānasya sadbhistasmānnivāraṇam।
dharmmeṇa pṛthivīñjitvā dharmmeṇaivānupālanam ॥ 2.32.12 ॥
saṃgrāmāṃstu bahūn jittvā hatvā cārīn sahasraśaḥ।
saṃgrāme yuddhayamānasya vadhaḥ syādadhikādraṇe ॥ 2.32.13 ॥
teneyaṃ pṛthivī kṛtsnā saptadvīpā sapattanā ।
saptodadhiparikṣiptā kṣātreṇa vidhinā janāḥ ॥ 2.32.14 ॥
tasya bāhusahasrantu yuddhyataḥ kila dhīmataḥ।
sarve yajñā mahābāhostasyāsan bhūritejasaḥ।
sarve kāñcanavedīkāḥ sarve yūpaiśca kāñcanaiḥ ॥ 2.32.17 ॥
sarve devairmmāhābhāgairvimānasthairalaṃkṛtāḥ।
gandharvvairapsarobhiśca nityamevopaśobhitāḥ ॥ 2.32.18 ॥
tasya rājño jagau gāthāṃ gandharvo nāradastathā।
caritaṃ tasya rājarṣermahimānaṃ nirīkṣya ca ॥ 2.32.19 ॥
na nūnaṃ kārttavīryasya gatiṃ yāsyanti mānavāḥ।
yajñairdānaistapobhiśca vikrameṇa śrutena ca ॥ 2.32.20 ॥
dvīpeṣu saptasu sa vai khaḍgī varaśarāsanī।
rathī rājāpyanucaro'nyo'gāccaivānudṛśyate ॥ 2.32.21 ॥
anaṣṭadravyaścaivāsīnna śoko na ca vibhramaḥ।
prabhāveṇa mahārājñaḥ prajā dharmmeṇa rakṣataḥ ॥ 2.32.22 ॥
pañcāśītisahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ sa narādhipaḥ।
sapta sapta vārān samrāṭ cakravarttī babhūva ha ॥ 2.32.23 ॥
sa eva paśupālo'bhūt kṣetrapālastathaiva ca।
sa eva vṛṣṭyā parjanyo yogitvādarjjuno'bhavat ॥ 2.32.24 ॥
sa vai bāhusahasreṇa jyāghātakaṭinena ca ।
bhāti raśmisahasreṇa śāradeneva bhāskaraḥ ॥ 2.32.25 ॥
sa hi nāgasahasreṇa māhiṣmatyāṃ narādhipaḥ।
karkoṭakasabhāñjitvā purīṃ tatra nyaveśayat ॥ 2.32.26 ॥
sa vai vege samudrasya prāvṛṭkālāmbujekṣaṇaḥ ।
krīḍanniva sukhodvignaḥ prāvṛṭkālañcakāra ha ॥ 2.32.27 ॥
lulitā krīḍatā tena hemasragdāmamālinī।
ūrmmibhrūkuṭisannādā śaṅkitābhyeti narmadā ॥ 2.32.28 ॥
tasya bāhu sahasreṇa kṣobhyamāṇe mahādadhau।
bhavanti līnā niśceṣṭāḥ pātālasthā mahāsurāḥ ॥ 2.32.30 ॥
cūrṇīkṛtamahāvīcilīnamīnamahāviṣāḥ।
patitā viddhaphenaughamāvarttakṣiptadussaham ॥ 2.32.31 ॥
cakāra kṣobhayanrājā doḥsahasreṇa sāgaram।
devāsuraparikṣiptaṃ kṣīrodamiva sāgaram ॥ 2.32.32 ॥
sahasotpāditā bhītā bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpottamam ॥ 2.32.33 ॥
nataniścalamūrddhāno babhūvuśca mahoragāḥ।
sāyāhne kadalīṣaṇḍā nirvātastimitā iva ॥ 2.32.34 ॥
laṅkāyāṃ mohayitvā tu sabalaṃ rāvaṇaṃ balāt।
nirjitya baddhvā cānīya māhiṣmatyāṃ babandha tam ॥ 2.32.35 ॥
tato gatvā pulastyastu arjunaṃ ca prasādayat।
mumoca rājā paulastyaṃ pulastyenānupālitam ॥ 2.32.36 ॥
tasya bāhusahasrasya babhūva jyātalasvanaḥ।
yugānte'mbudavṛkṣasya sphuṭitasyāśaneriva ॥ 2.32.37 ॥
aho mṛdhe mahāvīryaṃ bhārgavo yasya so'cchinat।
mṛdhe sahasraṃ bāhūnāṃ hematālavanaṃ yathā ॥ 2.32.38 ॥
tṛṣitena kadācitsa bhikṣitaścitrabhānunā।
sapta dvīpāṃścitrabhānoḥ prādādbhikṣāṃ viśāmpatiḥ ॥ 2.32.39 ॥
purāṇi ghoṣān grāmāṃśca pattanāni ca sarvvaśaḥ।।
jajvāla tasya bāṇeṣu citrabhānurdidhakṣayā ॥ 2.32.40 ॥
sa tasya puruṣendrasya prabhāveṇa mahāyaśāḥ।
dadāha kārtavīryasya śailāṃścāpi vanāni ca ॥ 2.32.41 ॥
sa śūnyamāśramaṃ sarvaṃ varuṇasyātmajasya vai।
dadoha savanadvīpāṃścitrabhānuḥ sahaihayaḥ ॥ 2.32.42 ॥
saṃlebhe varuṇaḥ putraṃ purā bhāsvinamuttamam।
vasiṣṭhanāmā sa muniḥ khyātaścāpaḥ śritaḥ śrutaḥ ॥ 2.32.43 ॥
tatrāpadastadā krodhādarjunaṃ śaptavānvibhuḥ।
yasmānna varjitamidaṃ vanaṃ te mama haihaya ॥ 2.32.44 ॥
tasmāt te duṣkaraṃ karmma kṛtamanyo haniṣyati।
arjuno nāma kaunteyo na ca rājā bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.32.45 ॥
arjuna tvāṃ mahāvīryo rāmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ।
chittvā bāhusahasraṃ vai pramathya tarasā balīṃ ॥ 2.32.46 ॥
tapasvī brāhmaṇaścaiva vadhiṣyati mahābalaḥ।
tasya rāmastadā hyāsīnmṛtyuśāpena dhīmataḥ ॥ 2.32.47 ॥
rājñā tena varaścaiva svayameva vṛtaḥ purā।
tasya putraśataṃ hyāsīt pañca tatra mahārathāḥ ॥ 2.32.48 ॥
kṛtāstrā balinaḥ śūrā dharmmātmāno yaśasvanaḥ ।
śūraśca śūrasenaśca vṛṣṭyādyaṃ vṛṣa eva ca ॥ 2.32.49 ॥
jayadhvajasya putrastu tālajaṅghaḥ pratāpavān ॥ 2.32.50 ॥
tasya putraśataṃ hyeva tālajaṅghā iti śrutam।
teṣāṃ pañca gaṇāḥ khyātā haihayānāṃ mahātmanām ॥ 2.32.51 ॥
tuṇḍikerāśca vikrāntāstālajaṅghāstathaiva ca ॥ 2.32.52 ॥
vīrahotrasutaścāpi ananto nāma pārthivaḥ।
durjayastasya putrastu babhūvāmitradarśanaḥ ॥ 2.32.53 ॥
anaṣṭadravyatā caiva tasya rājño babhūva ha।
prabhāveṇa mahārājaḥ prajāstāḥ paryyapālayat ॥ 2.32.54 ॥
na tasya vittanāśaśca naṣṭaṃ pratilabheta saḥ।
kārtavīryasya yo janma kathayediha dhīmataḥ ॥ 2.32.55 ॥
yathā tvaṣṭā yathā dātā tathā svarge mahīyate ॥ 2.32.56 ॥
kimarthaṃ bhuvanaṃ dagdhamapavasyaṃ mahātmanām।
kārtavīryeṇa vikramya tannaḥ prabrūhi pṛcchatām ॥ 2.33.1 ॥
rakṣitā sa tu rājarṣiḥ prajānāmiti naḥ śrutam।
kathaṃ sa rakṣitā bhūtvānāśayattattapovanam ॥ 2.33.2 ॥
etasminneva kāle tu apo nilayamāśritaḥ।
aikṣākī tvabhavadbhāryā sattvastasyāmajāyata।
teṣāṃ hi sargāścatvāraḥ śrṛṇudhvaṃ vistareṇa vai ॥ 2.34.2 ॥
bhajamānasya śrṛñjayyāṃ bāhyaścopari bāhyakaḥ।
śrṛñjayasya sute dve tu bāhyakaste udāvahat ॥ 2.34.3 ॥
tasya bhārye bhaginyau te prāsūteti sutān bahūn।
nimiśca paṇavaścaiva vṛṣṇiḥ parapurañjayaḥ ॥ 2.34.4 ॥
ye bāhyakāryyaśrṛñjayyāṃ bhajamānādvijajñire।
bāhyakāryyābhaginyāṃ ye bhajamānā dvijajñire।
teṣāṃ devāvṛdho rājā cacāra paramaṃ tapaḥ ॥ 2.34.6 ॥
putraḥ sarvaguṇopeto mama bhūyāditi sma ha।
saṃyojyātmānamevaṃ savarṇā sā jalamaspṛśat ॥ 2.34.7 ॥
sā copasparśanāttasya cakāra ṛṣimāpagā।
kalyāṇañca narapatestasya sā nimnagottamā ॥ 2.34.8 ॥
cintayābhiparītāṅgā jagāmātha viniścayam।
nādhigacchāmi tāṃ nārīṃ yasyāmevaṃvidhaḥ sutaḥ ॥ 2.34.9 ॥
bhavetsarvaguṇopeto rājño devāvṛdhasya hi।
tasmādasya svayaṃ cāhaṃ bhavāmyadya sahavratā।
jajñe tasyāḥ svayaṃ hasto bhāvastasya yatheritaḥ ॥ 2.34.10 ॥
atha bhūtvā kumārī tu sāvitrī paramaṃ vacaḥ।
cintayāmāsa rājānaṃ tāmiyeṣa sa parthivaḥ ॥ 2.34.11 ॥
tasyāmādhatta garbhaṃ sa tejasvinamudāradhīḥ।
atha sā navame māsi suṣuve saritāṃvarā ॥ 2.34.12 ॥
tatra vaṃśe purāṇajñā gāthāṃ gāyanti vai dvijāḥ ॥ 2.34.13 ॥
guṇān devāvṛdhasyāpi kīrttayanto mahātmanaḥ।
yathaiva śrṛṇute dūrāt saṃpaśyati tathāntikāt ॥ 2.34.14 ॥
babhruḥ śreṣṭo manuṣyāṇāṃ devairdevāvṛdhaḥ samaḥ।
puruṣāḥ pañcaṣaṣṭiśca sahasrāṇi ca saptatiḥ।
ye'mṛtatvamanuprāptā babhrurdevāvṛdhādapi ॥ 2.34.15 ॥
yajvā dānapatirvīro brahmaṇyaḥ satya vāg budhaḥ।
kīrttimāṃśca mahābhāgaḥ sāttvatānāṃ mahārathaḥ ॥ 2.34.16 ॥
gāndhārī caiva mādrī ca vṛṣṇerbhāryye babhūvatuḥ ॥ 2.34.17 ॥
gāndhārī janayāmāsa sumitraṃ mitranandanam।
anamitraṃ sutañcaiva tāvubhau puruṣottamau।
anamitrasuto nighno nighnasya dvau babhūvatuḥ ॥ 2.34.19 ॥
prasenaśca mahābhāgaḥ śakrajicca sutāvubhau।
tasya śakrajitaḥ pūrvaḥ sakhā prāṇasamo'bhavat ॥ 2.34.20 ॥
sa kadācinniśāpāye rathena rathināṃvaraḥ।
toyakūlādapaḥ spraṣṭumupasthātuṃ yayau ravim ॥ 2.34.21 ॥
tasyopatiṣṭhataḥ sūryo vivasvānagrataḥ sthitaḥ।
aspaṣṭamūrtirbhagavāṃ stejomaṇḍalavān vibhuḥ ॥ 2.34.22 ॥
atha rājā vivasvantamuvāca sthitamagrataḥ।
yathaiva vyomni paśyāmi tvāmahaṃ jyotiṣāmpate ॥ 2.34.23 ॥
tejomaṇḍalinañcaiva tathaivāpyagrataḥ sthitam।
ko viśeṣo vivasvaṃste sākṣādupagatena vai ॥ 2.34.24 ॥
etacchrutvā sa bhagavān maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam।
svakaṇṭādavamucyātha babandha nṛpatestadā ॥ 2.34.25 ॥
tato vigrahavantaṃ taṃ dadarśa nṛpatistadā।
pratimāmatha tāṃ dṛṣṭvā muhūrttaṃ kṛtavāṃstathā ॥ 2.34.26 ॥
tamatiprasthitaṃ bhūyo vivasvantaṃ sa śakrajit।
provācāgnisavarṇaṃ tvaṃ yena lokān prayāsyati।
syamantakaṃ nāma maṇiṃ dattavāṃstasya bhāskaraḥ।
sa tamābaddhya nagaraṃ praviveśa mahīpatiḥ ॥ 2.34.28 ॥
taṃ prasenijite divyaṃ maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam।
dadau bhrātre narapatiḥ premṇā śakrajiduttamam ॥ 2.34.30 ॥
syamantako nāma maṇiryasya rāṣṭre sthito bhevat ।
kālavarṣī ca parjanyo na ca vyādhibhayaṃ tadā ॥ 2.34.31 ॥
lipsāṃ cakre prasenāttu maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam।
govindo na ca taṃ lebhe śakto'pi na jahāra ca ॥ 2.34.32 ॥
kadā cinmṛgayāṃ yātaḥ prasenastena bhūṣitaḥ।
syamantakakṛte siṃhādvadhaṃ prāptaḥ sudāruṇam ॥ 2.34.33 ॥
jāmbavānṛkṣarājastu taṃ siṃhaṃ nijaghāna vai ।
ādāya ca maṇiṃ divyaṃ svaṃ bilaṃ praviveśa ha ॥ 2.34.34 ॥
tatkarma kṛṣṇasya tato vṛṣṇyandhakamahattarāḥ।
maṇaugṛdhnuntu manvānāstameva viśaśaṅkire ॥ 2.34.35 ॥
mithyābhiśastiṃ tebhyastāṃ balavānarisūdanaḥ।
amṛṣyamāṇo bhagavān vanaṃ sa vicacāra ha ॥ 2.34.36 ॥
sa tu prasenamṛgayāmacarattatra cāpyatha।
prasenasya padaṃ gṛhya puruṣai rāptakāribhiḥ ॥ 2.34.37 ॥
ṛkṣavantaṃ girivaraṃ vindhyañca nagamuttamam।
anveṣaṇapariśrāntaḥ sa dadarśa mahāmanāḥ ॥ 2.34.38 ॥
sāśvaṃ hataṃ prasenaṃ taṃ nāvindattatra vai maṇim।
atha siṃhaḥ prasenasya śarīrasyāvidūrataḥ ॥ 2.34.39 ॥
ṛkṣeṇa nihato dṛṣṭaḥ pādaiṛkṣasya sūcitām।
padairanveṣayāmāsa guhāmṛkṣasya yādavaḥ ॥ 2.34.40 ॥
mahatyatibile vāṇīṃ śuśrāva pramaderitām।
dhātryā kumāramādāya sutaṃ jāmbavato dvijāḥ।
prītimatyātha maṇinā mārodīrityudīritām ॥ 2.34.41 ॥
prasenamavadhīt siṃhaḥ siṃho jāmbavatā hataḥ।
sukumāraka mārodīstava hyeṣa syamantakaḥ ॥ 2.34.42 ॥
vyaktīkṛtañca śabdaṃ taṃ tūrṇaṃ so'pi yayau bilam।
apaśyacca vilābhyāśe prasenamavadāritam॥ 2.34.43 ॥
praviśya cāpi bhagavāstadṛkṣabilamañjasā।
dadarśa ṛkṣarājānaṃ jāmbavantamudāradhīḥ ॥ 2.34.44 ॥
yuyudhe vāsudevastu bile jāmbavatā saha।
bāhubhyāmeva govindo divasānekaviṃśatim ॥ 2.34.45 ॥
praviṣṭe ca bilaṃ kṛṣṇe vāsudeva puraḥsarāḥ ।
punardvāravatīmetya hataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ nyavedayan ॥ 2.34.46 ॥
vāsudevastu nirjitya jāmbavantaṃ mahābalam।
lebhe jāmbavatīṃ kanyāmṛkṣarājasya sammatām ॥ 2.34.47 ॥
bhagavattejasā grasto jāmbavān prasabhaṃ maṇim।
sutāṃ jāmbavatīmāśu viṣvaksenāya dattavān ॥ 2.34.48 ॥
maṇiṃ syamantakaṃ caiva jagrāhātma viśuddhaye।
anunīya ṛkṣarājaṃ niryayau ca tadā bilāt ॥ 2.34.49 ॥
evaṃ sa maṇimādāya viśoddhyātmānamātmanā।
dadau satrājite taṃ vai maṇiṃ sātvatasannidhau ॥ 2.34.50 ॥
kanyāṃ punarjāmbavatīmuvāca madhusūdanaḥ।
imāṃ mithyābhiśastiṃ yaḥ kṛṣṇasyeha vyapohitām।
veda mithyābhiśasteḥ sa nābhiśasyati karhicit ॥ 2.34.52 ॥
khyātimantastrayasteṣāṃ bhaṅgakārastu pūrvvajaḥ।
vīro vratapatiścaiva hyapasvāntaśca supriyaḥ ॥ 2.34.53 ॥
atha dvāravatī nāma bhaṅgakārasya suprajā।
suṣuve sā kumārīstu tisro rūpaguṇānvitāḥ ॥ 2.34.54 ॥
satya bhāmottamā strīṇāṃ vratinīva dṛḍhavratā।
tathā tapasvinī caiva pitā kṛṣṇasya tāṃ dadau ॥ 2.34.55 ॥
yattat satrājite kṛṣṇo maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam।
prādāttadāharadratnaṃ bhojena śatadhanvanā ॥ 2.34.56 ॥
tadā hi prārthayāmāsa satyabhāmāmaninditām।
akrūro ratnamanvicchan maṇiñcaiva syamantakam ॥ 2.34.57 ॥
bhadrakāraṃ tato hatvā śatadhanvā mahābalaḥ।
rātrau taṃ maṇimādāya tato'krūrāya dattavān ॥ 2.34.58 ॥
akrūrastu tadā ratnamādāya sa nararṣabhaḥ।
samayaṃ kāraṇaṃ cakre bodhyo nānyaistvayetyuta ॥ 2.34.59 ॥
vayamabhyupapatsyāmaḥ kṛṣṇena tvaṃ pradharṣitaḥ।
mama ca dvārakāḥ sarvā vaśe tiṣṭantyasaṃśayam ॥ 2.34.60 ॥
hate pitari duḥśārttā satyabhāmā yaśasvinī।
prayayau rathamāruhya nagaraṃ vāraṇāvatam ॥ 2.34.61 ॥
satyabhāmā tu tadvṛttaṃ bhojasya śatadhanvanaḥ।
bharturnivedya duḥkhārttā pārśvasthāśrūṇyavartayat ॥ 2.34.62 ॥
pāṇḍavānāntu dagdhānāṃ hariḥ kṛtvodakakriyām ।
tulyārthe caiva bhrātṝṇāṃ niyojayati sātyakim ॥ 2.34.63 ॥
tata stvaritamāgamya dvārakāṃ madhusūdanaḥ।
pūrvvajaṃ halinaṃ śrīmānidaṃ vacanamabravīt ॥ 2.34.64 ॥
hataḥ prasenaḥ siṃhena satrājicchatadhanvanā।
syamantakamahaṃ mārge tasya prahara he prabho ॥ 2.34.65 ॥
tadāroha rathaṃ śīghraṃ bhojaṃ hatvā mahābalam।
syamantako mahābāho tadāsmākaṃ bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.34.66 ॥
tataḥ pravṛtte yuddhe tu tumule bhojakṛṣṇayoḥ।
śatadhanvā na cākrūramavaikṣat sarvato diśi ॥ 2.34.67 ॥
anaṣṭāśvāvarohantu kṛtvā bhojajanārdanau।
śakto'pi sādhyādvārddhakyānnākrūro'bhyupapadyata ॥ 2.34.68 ॥
apayāne tato buddhiṃ bhūyaścakre bhayānvitaḥ।
yojanānāṃ śataṃ sāgraṃ yayā ca pratyapadyata ॥ 2.34.69 ॥
vijñātahṛdayā nāma śatayojanagāminī।
bhojasya vaḍhavādityo yayā kṛṣṇamayodhayat ॥ 2.34.70 ॥
tatastasya hayāste tu śramāt khedācca vai dvijāḥ।
khamutpetū rathaprāṇāḥ kṛṣṇo rāmamathābravīt ॥ 2.34.72 ॥
tiṣṭhasveha mahābāho dṛṣṭadoṣā mayā hayāḥ।
padybhāṃ gatvā hariṣyāmi maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam ॥ 2.34.73 ॥
padbhyāmeva tato gatvā śatadhanvānamacyutaḥ।
mithilādhipatiṃ taṃ vai jaghāna paramāstravit ॥ 2.34.74 ॥
syamantakaṃ na cāpaśyaddhatvā bhojaṃ mahābalam।
nivṛttaṃ cābravīt kṛṣṇaṃ ratnaṃ dehīti lāṅgalī ॥ 2.34.75 ॥
nāstīti kṛṣṇaścovāca tato rāmo ruṣānvitaḥ।
dhikchabdamasakṛt pūrvvaṃ pratyuvāca janārddanam ॥ 2.34.76 ॥
bhrātṛtvānmarṣayāmyeṣa svasti te'stu vrajāmyaham।
kṛtyaṃ na me drārakayā na tvayā na ca vṛṣṇibhiḥ ॥ 2.34.77 ॥
praviveśa tato rāmo mithilāmarimarddanaḥ।
sarvvakāmairupahṛtairmaithilenaiva pūjitaḥ ॥ 2.34.78 ॥
etasminneva kāle tu babhrurmatimatāṃvaraḥ।
nānārūpān kratūn sarvvānājahāra nirargalān ॥ 2.34.79 ॥
dīkṣāmayaṃ sakavacaṃ rakṣārthaṃ praviveśa ha।
syamantakakṛte rājā gādhiputro mahāyaśāḥ ॥ 2.34.80 ॥
akrūrayajña ityete khyātāstasya mahātmanaḥ।
bahvannadakṣiṇāḥ sarvve sarvvakāmapradāyinaḥ ॥ 2.34.82 ॥
atha duryyodhano rājā gatvā'tha mithilāṃ prabhuḥ।
gadāśikṣāṃ tato divyāṃ balabhadrādavāptavān ।। 34.83।
prasādya tu tato viprā vṛṣṇyandhakamahārathaiḥ।
ānīto dvārakāmeva kṛṣṇena ca mahātmanā ॥ 2.34.83 ॥
akrūramandhakaiḥ sārddhamupāyāt puruṣarṣabhaḥ।
yuddhe hatvā tu śatrugnaṃ saha bandhumatā balī ॥ 2.34.84 ॥
śvaphalkatanayāyāntu narāyāṃ narasattamau।
bhaṅgakārasya tanayo viśrutau sumahābalau ॥ 2.34.85 ॥
jajñāte'ndhakamukhyasya śatrughno bandhumāṃśca tau।
vadhārthaṃ bhaṅgakārasya kṛṣṇo na prītimān bhavet ॥ 2.34.86 ॥
jñāti bhedabhayādbhītaḥ samupekṣitavāṃstathā।
apayāte tathākrūre nāvarṣatpākaśāsanaḥ ॥ 2.34.87 ॥
anāvṛṣṭyā hataṃ rāṣṭramabhavattadvaghodyatam।
tataḥ prasādayāmāsurakrūraṃ kukurāndhakāḥ ॥ 2.34.88 ॥
punardvāravatīṃ prāpte tadā dānapatau tathā।
pravavarṣa sahasrākṣaḥ kukṣau jalanidhestataḥ ॥ 2.34.89 ॥
kanyāñca vāsudevāya svasāraṃ śīlasammatām।
akrūraḥ pradadau śrīmān prītyarthaṃ yadupuṅgavaḥ ॥ 2.34.90 ॥
ata vijñāya yogena kṛṣṇo babhrugataṃ maṇim।
sabhāmadhye tadā prāha tamakrūraṃ janārdanaḥ ॥ 2.34.91 ॥
yacca ratnaṃ maṇivaraṃ tava hastagataṃ prabho।
tatprayacchasva mānārha vimatiñcātra mā kṛthāḥ ॥ 2.34.92 ॥
ṣaṣṭivarṣagate kāle yadroṣo'bhūttadā mama।
susaṃrūḍhaḥ sakṛt prāptastatkālāśritya sa mahān ॥ 2.34.93 ॥
tataḥ kṛṣṇasya vacanāt sarvvasātvatasaṃsadi।
pradadau taṃ maṇiṃ babhrurakleśena mahāmatiḥ ॥ 2.34.94 ॥
tata ārjjavasaṃprāptababhruhastādarindamaḥ।
dadau prahṛṣṭamanasā taṃ maṇiṃ babhrave punaḥ ॥ 2.34.95 ॥
sa kṛṣṇahastāt saṃprāpya maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam।
ābaddhya gāndinīputro virarājāṃśumāniva ॥ 2.34.96 ॥
imāṃ mithyābhiśastiṃ yo viśuddhāmapi cottamām ।
veda mithyābhi śastiṃ sa na vrajecca kathañcana ॥ 2.34.97 ॥
animitrācchinirjajñe kaniṣṭādvṛṣṇinandanāt ॥ 2.34.98 ॥
satyavāk satyasampannaḥ satyakastasya cātmajaḥ।
sātyakiryuyudhānasya tasya bhūtiḥ suto'bhavat ॥ 2.34.99 ॥
bhūteryugandharaḥ putra iti bhautyāḥ prakīrttitāḥ।
jajñāte tanayau pṛśreḥ śvaphalkaścitrakaśca yaḥ ॥ 2.34.100 ॥
śvaphalkastu mahārājo dharmātmā yatra varttate।
nāsti vyādhibhayaṃ tatra na cāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ tathā ॥ 2.34.101 ॥
kadācit kāśirājasya vibhostu dvijasattamāḥ।
trīṇi varṣāṇi viṣaye nāvarṣatpākaśāsanaḥ ॥ 2.34.102 ॥
sa tatra vāsayāmāsa śvaphalkaṃ paramārcitam।
śvaphalkaparivāsena prāvarṣatpākaśāsanaḥ ॥ 2.34.103 ॥
śvaphalkaḥ kāśirājasya sutāṃ bhāryāmaninditām।
gāndinīṃ nāma gāṃ sā hi dadau viprāya nityaśaḥ ॥ 2.34.104 ॥
sā māturudarasthā vai bahuvarṣa śatān kila।
vasati sma na vai jajñe sarbhasthāntāṃ pitābravīt ॥ 2.34.105 ॥
jāyasva śīghraṃ bhadrante kimarthaṃ cāpi tiṣṭhasi।
provāca cainaṃ garbha sthā sā kanyā gaurdine dine ॥ 2.34.106 ॥
tathetyuvāca tāṃ tasyāḥ pitā kāmamapūpurat ॥ 2.34.107 ॥
dātā yajvā ca śūraśca śrutavānatithipriyaḥ।
tasyāḥ putraḥ smṛto'krūraḥ śvaphalko bhūridakṣiṇaḥ ॥ 2.34.108 ॥
upamaṅgustathā maṅgurmṛduraścārimejayaḥ।
girirakṣastatā yakṣaḥ śatrughno vārimarddanaḥ ॥ 2.34.109 ॥
āvāhaprativāhau ca vasudevā varāṅganā ॥ 2.34.110 ॥
akrūrādugrasenyāntu sutau dvau kulanandinau।
devaścānupadevaśca jajñāte devasaṃmitau ॥ 2.34.111 ॥
citrakasyābhavan putrāḥ pṛthurvipṛthureva ca।
aśvagrīvo'śvabāhuśca supārśvakagaveṣaṇau ॥ 2.34.112 ॥
ariṣṭanemiraśvaśca suvarmā varmacarmabhṛt ।
abhūmirbahubhūmiśca śraviṣṭāśravaṇe striyau ॥ 2.34.113 ॥
satyakāt kāśiduhitā lebhe sā caturaḥ sutān।
kakudaṃ bhajamānañca śamīkabalabarhiṣau ॥ 2.34.114 ॥
kakudasya suto vṛṣṭirvṛṣṭestu tanayo'bhavat।
kapotaromā tasyātha revato'bhavadātmajaḥ ॥ 2.34.115 ॥
tasyāsīttumburusakhā vidvān putro'bhavatkila।
khyāyate yasya nāmnā sa candanodakadundubhiḥ ॥ 2.34.116 ॥
tasmāccābhijitaḥ putra utpannastu punarvasuḥ।
aśvamedhantu putrārthe ājahāra narottamaḥ ॥ 2.34.117 ॥
tasya madhye'tirātrasya sadomadhyātsamutthitam।
tatastu vidvān dharmajño dātā yajvā punarvasuḥ ॥ 2.34.118 ॥
tasyāpi putramithunaṃ bāhubāṇājitaḥ kila।
āhukaścāhukī caiva khyātau matimatāṃvarau ॥ 2.34.119 ॥
imāṃścodāharantyatra ślokān prati tamāhukam।
sopāsaṅgānukarṣāṇāṃ sadhvajānāṃ varūthinām ॥ 2.34.120 ॥
rathānāṃ meghaghoṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi daśaiva tu।
nāsatyavādī tvāsīttu nāyajvā nāsahasradaḥ ॥ 2.34.121 ॥
nāśucirnāpyadharmātmā nāvidvānna kṛśo'bhavat।
āhukasya dhṛtiḥ putra ityevamanu śuśrumaḥ ॥ 2.34.122 ॥
śvetena paricāreṇa kiśorapratimān hayān।
aśītiyuktaniyutānyāhukapratimo'vrajat ॥ 2.34.123 ॥
pūrvasyāndiśi nāgānāṃ bhojasya pratirejire।
rūpyakāñcanakakṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇyekaviṃśatiḥ ॥ 2.34.124 ॥
tāvantyeva sahasrāṇi uttarasyāntathā diśi।
bhūmipālasya bhojasya uttiṣṭet kiṅkiṇī kila ॥ 2.34.125 ॥
āhukaścāhukāndhāya svasāraṃ tvāhukīndadau।
āhukāndhasya duhitā dvau putrau sambabhūvatuḥ ॥ 2.34.126 ॥
devakaścograsenaśca devagarbhasamāvubhau ।
devakasya sutā vīrā jajñire tridaśopamāḥ ॥ 2.34.127 ॥
devānāmapi devaśca sudevo devarañjitā।
teṣāṃ svasāraḥ saptāsan vasudevāya saṃdadau ॥ 2.34.128 ॥
vṛkadevopadevā ca tathānyā devarakṣitā।
śrīdevā śāntidevā ca mahādevā tathāparā ॥ 2.34.129 ॥
saptamī devakī tāsāṃ sunāmā cārudarśanā।
navograsenasya sutāḥ kaṃsasteṣāntu pūrvajaḥ ॥ 2.34.130 ॥
nyagrodhaśca sunāmā ca kadvaśaṃkuśca bhūmayaḥ।
sūtanū rāṣṭrapālaśca yuddhatuṣṭaḥ supuṣṭimān ॥ 2.34.131 ॥
teṣāṃ svasāraḥ pañcaiva karmadharmavatī tathā।
śatāṅkrū rāṣṭrāpālā ca kaṅvā caiva varāṅganā ॥ 2.34.132 ॥
ugraseno mahāpatyo vikhyātaḥ kukurodbhavaḥ।
kukurāṇāmimaṃ vaṃśaṃ dhārayannamitaujasām।
ātmano vipulaṃ vaṃśaṃ prajāvāṃśca bhavennaraḥ ॥ 2.34.133 ॥
bhajamānasya putrastu rathimukhyo vidūrathaḥ।
rājyādhidevaḥ śūraśca viduraśca suto'bhavat ॥ 2.34.134 ॥
tasya śūrasya tu sutā jajñire balavattarāḥ ।
vātaścaiva nivātaśca śoṇitaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ ॥ 2.34.135 ॥
śamī ca gadavarmā ca nidātaḥ śakraśakrajit।
śamiputraḥ pratikṣiptaḥ pratikṣiptasya cātmajaḥ ॥ 2.34.136 ॥
svayambhojaḥ svayambhojāddhṛdikaḥ sambabhūva ha।
hṛdikasya sutāstvāsan daśa bhīmaparākramāḥ ॥ 2.34.137 ॥
kṛtavarmā kṛtasteṣāṃ śatadhanvā tu madhyamaḥ।
sudāntaśca dhiyāntaśca nakavān kanakodbhavaḥ।
devārhasya suto vidvān jajñe kambalabarhiṣaḥ ॥ 2.34.139 ॥
asamaujāḥ sutastasya sumahaujāśca viśrutaḥ।
ajāvaputrāya tataḥ pradadāvasamaujase।
sudaṃṣṭrañca surūpañca kṛṣṇa ityandhakāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.34.140 ॥
andhakānāmimaṃ vaṃśaṃ kīrttayānastu nityaśaḥ।
ātmāno vipulaṃ vaṃśaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ॥ 2.34.141 ॥
asmakyāṃ janayāmāsa śūro vai devamānuṣim।
māṣyāntu janayāmāsa śūro vai devamīḍhuṣam ॥ 2.34.142 ॥
bhāṣyāntu jajñire śūrādbhojāyāṃ puruṣā daśa।
vasudevo mahābāhuḥ pūrvamānakadundubhiḥ ॥ 2.34.143 ॥
jajñe tasya prasūtasya dundubhiḥ prāṇadaddivi।
ānakānāñca saṃhrādaḥ sumahānabhavaddivi ॥ 2.34.144 ॥
papāta puṣpavarṣañca śūrasya bhavane mahat।
manuṣyaloke kṛtsne'pi rūpe nāsti samo bhuvi ॥ 2.34.145 ॥
yasyāsīt puruṣāgryasya kīrttiścandramaso yathā।
devabhāgastato jajñe tato devaśravāḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.34.146 ॥
śyāmaḥ śamīko gaṇḍūṣaḥ catasrastu varāṅganāḥ ॥ 2.34.147 ॥
pṛthā ca śrutavedā ca śrutakīrttiḥ śrutaśravāḥ।
rājādhidevī ca tathā pañcaitā vīramātaraḥ ॥ 2.34.148 ॥
tasmāt kuntīti vikhyātā kuntībhojātmajā pṛthā।
kuruvīraḥ pāṇḍumukhyastasmādbhāryāmavindata ॥ 2.34.150 ॥
pṛthā jajñe tataḥ putrān trīnagnisamatejasaḥ।
loke'pratirathān vīrān śakratulyaparākramān ॥ 2.34.151 ॥
dharmādyudhiṣṭiraṃ putraṃ mārutācca vṛkodaram।
īndrāddhanañjayañcaiva pṛthā putrānajījanat ॥ 2.34.152 ॥
mādravatyāntu janitāvāśvināviti viśrutam।
nakulaḥ sahadevaśca rūpasattvaguṇānvitau ॥ 2.34.153 ॥
jajñe ca śrutadevāyāṃ tanayo vṛddhaśarmaṇaḥ।
karūṣādhipatirvīro dantavakro mahābalaḥ ॥ 2.34.154 ॥
kaikeyāṃ śrutakīrtyāntu jajñe santardanaḥ punaḥ।
cekitānabṛhatkṣatrau tathaivānyau mahābalau ॥ 2.34.155 ॥
vindānuvindāvāvantyau bhrātarau sumahābalau।
śrutaśravāyāṃ caidyastu śiśupālo babhūva ha ॥ 2.34.156 ॥
damaghoṣasya rājarṣeḥ putro vikhyātapauruṣaḥ।
yaḥ purāsīddaśagrīvaḥ saṃbabhūvārimardanaḥ ॥ 2.34.157 ॥
pauravī rohiṇī caiva madirā cāparā tathā।
tathaiva bhadrā vaiśākhī devakī saptamī tathā ॥ 2.34.159 ॥
sugandhirvanarājī ca dve cānye paricārike।।
rohiṇī pauravī caiva vālmīkasyātmajābhavat ॥ 2.34.160 ॥
jyeṣṭā patnī mahābhāgā dayitānakadundubheḥ ।
jyeṣṭhaṃ lebhe sutaṃ rāmaṃ sāraṇaṃ niśavaṃ tathā ॥ 2.34.161 ॥
durddamaṃ damanaṃ śubhraṃ piṇḍārakakuśītakau।
citrāṃ nāma kumārīñca rohiṇyaṣṭau vyajāyata ॥ 2.34.162 ॥
pautrau rāmasya jajñāte vijñātau niśitotsukau।
pārśvī ca pārśvanandī ca śiśuḥ satyadhṛtistathā ॥ 2.34.163 ॥
mandabāhyo'tha rāmāṇagirikau gira eva ca।
śuklagulmeti gulmaśca daridrāntaka eva ca ॥ 2.34.164 ॥
kumāryaścāpi pañcādyā nāmatastā nibodhata।
arciṣmatī sunandā ca surasā suvacāstathā ॥ 2.34.165 ॥
tathā śatabalā caiva sāraṇasya sutāstvimāḥ।
bhadrāśvo bhadraguptiśca bhadravighnastathaiva ca ॥ 2.34.166 ॥
bhadrabāhurbhadraratho bhadrakalpastathaiva ca।
supārśvakaḥ kīrttimāṃśca rohitāśvaśca bhadrajaḥ ॥ 2.34.167 ॥
durmmadaścābhibhūtaśca rohiṇyāḥ kulajāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
nandopanantadau mitraśca kukṣimitrastathācalaḥ ॥ 2.34.168 ॥
citropa citre kanye ca sthitaḥ puṣṭirathāparaḥ।
madirāyāḥ sutā hyete sudevo'tha vijajñire ॥ 2.34.169 ॥
upabimbo'tha bimbaśca sattvadantamahaujasau।
catvāra ete vikhyātā bhadrāputrā mahābalāḥ ॥ 2.34.170 ॥
vaiśākhyāṃ samadācchauriḥ putraṃ kauśikamuttamam।
devakyāṃ jajñire śauriḥ suṣeṇaḥ kīrtimānapi ॥ 2.34.171 ॥
tadayo bhadrasenaśca yajudāyaśca pañcamaḥ।
ṣaṣṭo bhadravidekaśca kaṃsaḥ sarvāñjaghāna tān ॥ 2.34.172 ॥
atha tasyāmavasthāyāmāyuṣmān saṃbabhūva ha।
loka nāthaḥ punarviṣṇuḥ pūrvakṛṣṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ ॥ 2.34.173 ॥
