anujātā'bhavat kṛṣṇā subhadrā bhadrabhāṣiṇī।
kṛṣṇā subhadreti punarvyākhyātā vṛṣṇinandinī ॥ 2.34.174 ॥
subhadrāyāṃ rathī pārthādabhimanyurajāyata।
vasudevasya bhāryāsu mahābhāgāsu saptasu।
ye putrā jajñireśūrā nāmatastānnibodhata ॥ 2.34.175 ॥
śārṅgadevājanattambuṃ śaurī jajñe kulodvaham ॥ 2.34.176 ॥
upasaṅgaṃ vasuñcāpi tanayau devarakṣitau।
evaṃ daśa sutāstasya kaṃsastānapyaghātayat ॥ 2.34.177 ॥
gaveṣaṇaṃ mahābhāgaṃ saṅgrāme citra yodhinam ॥ 2.34.180 ॥
śaibyāyāmadadacchauriḥ putraṃ kauśikamavyayam ॥ 2.34.181 ॥
sugandhī vanarājī ca śaurerāstāṃ parigrahaḥ।
puṇḍraśca kapilaścaiva vasudevātmajau hi tau।
tayo rājā'bhavat puṇḍraḥ kapilastu vanaṃ yayo ॥ 2.34.182 ॥
tasyāṃ samabhavadvīro vasudevātmajo balī।
rājā nāma niṣādo'sau prathamaḥ sa dhanurddharaḥ ॥ 2.34.183 ॥
vikhyāto devarātasya mahābhāgaḥ suto'bhavat।
paṇḍitānāṃ mataṃ prāhurdevaśravasamudbhavam ॥ 2.34.184 ॥
asmakyāṃ labhate putramanādṛṣṭiṃ yaśasvinam।
nivarttaḥ śakraśatrughnaṃ śrāddhadevaṃ mahābalam ॥ 2.34.185 ॥
ajāyata śrāddhadevo niṣadhādiryataḥ śrutaḥ।
ekalavyo mahāvīryo niṣādaiḥ parivarddhitaḥ ॥ 2.34.186 ॥
gaṇḍūṣāyānapatyāya kṛṣṇastuṣṭo'dadat sutau।
cārudeṣṇañca sāmbañca kṛtāstrau śastalakṣaṇau ॥ 2.34.187 ॥
tantijastantimālaśca svaputrau kanakasya tu।
vastāvanestvaputrāya vasudevaḥ pratāpavān।
sautirdadau sutaṃ vīraṃ śauriṃ kauśikameva ca ॥ 2.34.188 ॥
anapatyo'bhavacchyāmaḥ śyāmakastu vanaṃ yayau।
jugupsamāno bhojatvaṃ rājarṣitvamavāpnuyāt ॥ 2.34.189 ॥
ya idaṃ janma kṛṣṇasya paṭhate niyatavrataḥ।
śrāvayedbrāhmaṇañcāpi sumahatsukhamāpnuyāt ॥ 2.34.190 ॥
devadevo mahātejāḥ pūrvvaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
vihārārthaṃ manuṣyeṣu jajñe nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ॥ 2.34.191 ॥
devakyāṃ vasudevena tapasā puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ।
caturbāhuḥ sa vijñeyo divyarūpaḥ śriyānvitaḥ ॥ 2.34.192 ॥
prakāśo bhagavān yogī kṛṣṇo mānuṣamāgataḥ।
avyakto'vyaktaliṅgasthaḥ sa eva bhagavān prabhuḥ ॥ 2.34.193 ॥
nārāyaṇo yataścakre prabhavaṃ cāvyayo hi saḥ।
devo nārāyaṇo bhūtvā harirāsītsanātanaḥ ॥ 2.34.194 ॥
yo'sṛjaccādipuruṣaṃ purā cakre prajāpatim।
aditerapi putratvametya yādavanandanaḥ।
devo viṣṇuriti khyātaḥ śakrādavarajo'bhavat ॥ 2.34.195 ॥
vadhārthaṃ suraśatrūṇāṃ daityadānavarakṣasām ॥ 2.34.196 ॥
yayātivaṃśajasyātha vasudevasya dhīmataḥ।
kulaṃ puṇyaṃ yataḥ karma bheje nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ॥ 2.34.197 ॥
sāgarāḥ samakampanta celuśca dharaṇīdharāḥ।
jajvaluścāgnihotrāṇi jāyamāne janārdane ॥ 2.34.198 ॥
śivāśca pravavurvātāḥ praśāntimabhavadrajaḥ।
jyotīṃṣyabhyadhikaṃ rejurjāyamāne janārdane ॥ 2.34.199 ॥
abhijinnāma nakṣatraṃ jayantī nāma śarvarī।
muhūrtto vijayo nāma yatra jāto janārdanaḥ ॥ 2.34.200 ॥
avyaktaḥ śāśvataḥ kṛṣṇo harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ।
ākāśāt puṣpavṛṣṭīśca vavarṣa tridaśeśvaraḥ।
gīrbhirmaṅgalayuktābhiḥ stuvanto madhusūdanam।
maharṣayaḥ sagandharvā upatasthuḥ sahasraśaḥ ॥ 2.34.202 ॥
vasudevastu taṃ rātrau jātaṃ putramadhokṣajam।
śrīvatsalakṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā divi divyaiḥ sulakṣaṇaiḥ।
uvāca vasudevaḥ svaṃ rūpaṃ saṃhara vai prabho ॥ 2.34.203 ॥
bhīto'haṃ kaṃsatastāta etadeva bravīmyaham।
mama putrā hatāstena jyeṣṭāste'dbhutadarśanāḥ ॥ 2.34.204 ॥
vasudevavacaḥ śrutvā rūpaṃ sa hṛtavān prabhuḥ।
anujñātaḥ pitā tvenaṃ nandagopagṛhaṃ gataḥ।
ugrasenamate tiṣṭhan yaśodāyai tadā dadau ॥ 2.34.205 ॥
tulyakālantu garbhiṇyau yaśodā devakī tathā।
yaśodā nandagopasya patnī sā nandagopateḥ ॥ 2.34.206 ॥
yāmeva rajanīṃ kṛṣṇo jajñe vṛṣṇikulaprabhuḥ।
tāmeva rajanīṃ kanyāṃ yaśodāpi vyajāyata ॥ 2.34.207 ॥
taṃ jātaṃ rakṣamāṇastu vasudevo mahāyaśāḥ।
prādāt putraṃ yaśodāyai kanyāntu jagṛhe svayam ॥ 2.34.208 ॥
dattvainaṃ nandagopasya rakṣamāmiti cābravīt।
sutaste sarvvakalyāṇo yādavānāṃ bhaviṣyati।
ayaṃ sa garbho devakyā asmatkleśān haniṣyati ॥ 2.34.209 ॥
ugrasenātmajāyāñca kanyāmānakadundubheḥ।
nivedayāmāsa tadā kanyeti śubhalakṣaṇā ॥ 2.34.210 ॥
svāsāyāṃ tanayaṃ kaṃso jātaṃ naivāvadhārayat।
atha tāmapi duṣṭātmā hyutsasarja mudānvitaḥ ॥ 2.34.211 ॥
kanyā sā vavṛdhe tatra vṛṣṇisadmani pūjitā ॥ 2.34.212 ॥
tāmeva vidhinotpannāmāhuḥ kanyāṃ prajāpatim ॥ 2.34.213 ॥
ekādaśā tu jajñe vai rakṣārthaṃ keśavasya ha।
tāṃ vai sarve sumanasaḥ pūjayiṣyanti yādavāḥ।
devadevo divyavapuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ saṃrakṣito'nayā ॥ 2.34.214 ॥
kimarthaṃ vasudevasya bhojaḥ kaṃso narādhipaḥ।
jaghāna putrān bālān vai tanno vyākhyātumarhasi ॥ 2.34.215 ॥
śrṛṇudhvaṃ vai yathā kaṃsaḥ putrānānakadundubheḥ।
jātāñjātāñciśūn sarvvān niṣpipeṣa vṛthāmatiḥ ॥ 2.34.216 ॥
bhayādyathā mahābāhurjātaḥ kṛṣṇo vivāsitaḥ।
tathā ca goṣu govindaḥ saṃvṛddha- puruṣottamaḥ ॥ 2.34.217 ॥
uktaṃ hi kila devakyā vasudevasya dhīmataḥ ।
sārathyaṃ kṛtavān kaṃso yuvarājastadā'bhavat ॥ 2.34.218 ॥
tato'ntarikṣe vāgāsīddivyā bhūtasya kasyacit।
yāmetāṃ vahase kaṃsa rathena parakāraṇāt।
asyā yaḥ saptamo garbhaḥ sa te mṛtyurbhaviṣyati ॥ 2.34.220 ॥
tāṃ śrutvā vyathito vāṇīṃ tadā kaṃso vṛthāmatiḥ।
niṣkramya khaḍgaṃ tāṃ kanyāṃ hantukāmo'bhavattadā ॥ 2.34.221 ॥
tamuvāca mahābāhurvasudevaḥ pratāpavān।
ugrasenātmajaṃ kaṃsaṃ sauhṛdātpraṇayena ca ॥ 2.34.222 ॥
nastriyaṃ kṣatriyo jātu hantumarhati kaścana।
upāyaḥ paridṛṣṭo'tra mayā yādavanandana ॥ 2.34.223 ॥
yo'syāḥ sambhavate garbhaḥ saptamaḥ pṛthivī pate।
tamahante prayacchāmi tatra kuryyā yathākramam ॥ 2.34.224 ॥
tvaṃ tvidānīṃ yatheṣṭatvaṃ vartethā bhūridakṣiṇa।
sarvānasyāstu vai garbhān satyaṃ neṣyāmi te vaśam ॥ 2.34.225 ॥
evaṃ mithyā naraśreṣṭha vāgeṣā na bhaviṣyati।
evamukto'nunītaḥ sa jagrāha tanayāṃstadā ॥ 2.34.226 ॥
vasudevaśca tāṃ bhāryyāmavāpya mudito'bhavat।
kaṃsaścāsyāvadhīt putrān pāpakarmmā vṛthāmatiḥ ॥ 2.34.227 ॥
ka eṣa vasudevaśca devakī ca yaśasvinī।
nandagopastu kastveṣa yaśodā ca mahāyaśāḥ।
yo viṣṇuṃ janayāmāsa yā cainaṃ cābhyavarddhayat ॥ 2.34.228 ॥
puruṣāḥ kaśyapasyāsannādityāstu striyāstathā।
atha kāmān mahābāhurdevakyāḥ samavarddhayat ॥ 2.34.229 ॥
acarat sa mahīṃ devaḥ praviṣṭo mānuṣīṃ tanum।
mohayan sarvabhūtāni yogātmā yogamāyayā ॥ 2.34.230 ॥
naṣṭe dharmme tadā jajñe viṣṇurvṛṣṇikule svayam।
kartuṃ dharmmavyavasthānamasurāṇāṃ praṇāśanam ॥ 2.34.231 ॥
āhṛtā rukmiṇī kanyā satyā nagnajitastadā।
sātrājitī satyabhāmā jāmbavatyapi rohiṇī ॥ 2.34.232 ॥
evamādīni devānāṃ sahasrāṇi ca ṣoḍaśa।
caturddaśa tu ye proktā gaṇāścāpsarasāṃ divi ।
vicintya devaiḥ śakreṇa viśiṣṭāstviha preṣitāḥ ॥ 2.34.234 ॥
patnyarthaṃ vāsudevasya utpannā rājaveśmasu।
etāḥ patnyo mahābhāgā viṃṣvaksenasya viśrutāḥ ॥ 2.34.235 ॥
pradyumnaścārudeṣṇaśca sudeṣṇaḥ śarabhastathā।
cāruśca cārubhadraśca bhadracārustathā'paraḥ ॥ 2.34.236 ॥
cāruvindhyaśca rukmiṇyāṃ kanyā cārumatī tathā।
sānurbhānustathākṣaśca rohito mantrayastathā ॥ 2.34.237 ॥
catasro jajñire teṣāṃ svasāro garuḍadhvajāt ॥ 2.34.238 ॥
bhānurbhaumarikā caiva tāmraparṇī jarandhamā।
satyabhāmāsutānetāñjāmbavatyāḥ prajāḥ śrṛṇu ॥ 2.34.239 ॥
bhadraśca bhadraguptaśca bhadravindrastathaiva ca।
saptabāhuśca vikhyātaḥ kanyā bhadrāvatī tathā।
sambodhanī ca vikhyātā jñeyā jāmbavatīsutāḥ ॥ 2.34.240 ॥
saṃgrāmajicca śatajit ta na ca sahasrajit।
ete putrāḥ sudevyāśca viṣvaksenasya kīrttitāḥ ॥ 2.34.241 ॥
vṛko vṛkāśvo vṛkajidvṛjinī ca surāṅganā।
mitrabāhuḥ sunīthaśca nāgnajityāḥ prajāstviha ॥ 2.34.242 ॥
evamādīni putrāṇāṃ saha srāṇi nibodhata।
prayutantu samākhyātaṃ vāsudevasya ye sutāḥ ॥ 2.34.243 ॥
ayutāni tathāṣṭau ca śūrā raṇaviśāradāḥ।
janārdanasya vaṃśo vaḥ kīrttito'yaṃ yathātatham ॥ 2.34.244 ॥
kanyā sā bṛhaducchasya śauneyasya mahātmanaḥ ॥ 2.34.245 ॥
tasyāḥ putrāstu vikhyātā strayaḥ samitiśobhanāḥ ।
aṅgadaḥ kumudaḥ śvetaḥ kanyā śvetā tathaiva ca ॥ 2.34.246 ॥
avagāhaśca citraśca śūraścitravaraśca yaḥ।
citrasenaḥ sutaścāsya kanyā citravatī tathā ॥ 2.34.247 ॥
tumbaśca tumbabāṇaśca janastambaśca tāvubhau।
upāṅgasya smṛtau dvau tu vajrāraḥ kṣipra eva ca ॥ 2.34.248 ॥
bhūrīndraseno bhūriśca gaveṣasya sutāvubhau ।
tisraḥ koṭyastu putrāṇāṃ yādavānāṃ mahātmanām ॥ 2.34.251 ॥
ihotpannā manuṣyeṣu bādhante sarvvamānavān ।
teṣāmutsādanārthantu utpannā yādave kule ॥ 2.34.253 ॥
sarvvamakakulaṃ yadvadvarttate vaiṣṇave kule ॥ 2.34.254 ॥
viṣṇusteṣāṃ pramāṇe ca prabhutve ca vyavasthitaḥ ।
nideśasthāyibhistasya baddhyante sarvamānuṣāḥ ॥ 2.34.255 ॥
iti prasūtirvṛṣṇīnāṃ samāsavyāsayogataḥ।
kīrttitā kīrttanāccaiva kīrttisiddhimabhīpsitām ।। 34.257 ।।
manuṣyaprakṛtīn devān kīrtyamānānnibodhata ।
saṅkarṣaṇo vāsudevaḥ pradyumnaḥ sāmba eva ca ॥ 2.35.1 ॥
aniruddhaśca pañcaite vaṃśavīrāḥ prakīrttitāḥ।
saptarṣayaḥ kuberaśca yakṣo maṇivarastathā ॥ 2.35.2 ॥
śālakī badaraścaiva vidvān dhanvantaristathā।
nandinaśca mahādevaḥ śālaṅkāyana ucyate।
ādidevastadā jiṣṇurebhiśca saha daivataiḥ ॥ 2.35.3 ॥
viṣṇuḥ kimarthaṃ sambhūtaḥ smṛtāḥ sambhūtayaḥ kati।
bhaviṣyāḥ kati vānye tu prādurbhāvā mahātmanaḥ ॥ 2.35.4 ॥
brahmakṣetre yugānteṣu kimarthamiha jāyate ।
punaḥ punarmmanuṣyeṣu tannaḥ prabrūhi pṛcchatām ॥ 2.35.5 ॥
vistareṇaiva sarvāṇi karmmāṇi ripughātinaḥ।
śrotumicchāmahe samyag dehaiḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ ॥ 2.35.6 ॥
karmmaṇāmānupūrvyañca prādurbhāvāśca ye prabho ।
yā cāsya prakṛtiḥ sūta tāścāsmān vaktumarhasi ॥ 2.35.7 ॥
kathaṃ sa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sureṣvariniṣūdanaḥ।
vasudevakule dhīmān vāsudevatvamāgataḥ ॥ 2.35.8 ॥
amaraiḥ sūta kiṃ puṇyaṃ puṇyakṛdbhiralaṃkṛtam।
devalokaṃ samutsṛjya martyalokamihāgataḥ ॥ 2.35.9 ॥
devamānuṣayornetā bhūrbhuvaḥprasavo hariḥ।
kimarthaṃ divyamātmānaṃ mānuṣe samaveśayat ॥ 2.35.10 ॥
yaścakraṃ vartayatyeko manuṣyāṇāṃ manomayam।
manuṣye sa kathaṃ buddhiṃ cakre cakrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ ॥ 2.35.11 ॥
gopāyanaṃ yaḥ kurute jagatāṃ sārvvalaukikam।
sa kathaṃ gāṃ gato viṣṇurgopamanvakarotprabhuḥ ॥ 2.35.12 ॥
mahābhūtāni bhūtātmā yo dadāra cakāra ha।
śrīgarbhaḥ sa kathaṃ garbhe striyā bhūcarayā dhṛtaḥ ॥ 2.35.13 ॥
sthāpitā jagato mārgāstrivargapravarāstrayaḥ ॥ 2.35.14 ॥
dadau jittvā vasumatīṃ surāṇāṃ surasattamaḥ ॥ 2.35.16 ॥
yena saiṃhaṃ vapuḥ kṛtvā dvidhākṛtvā ca yatpunaḥ।
pūrvvadaityo mahāvīryyo hiraṇyakaśipurhataḥ ॥ 2.35.17 ॥
yaḥ purā hyanalo bhūtvā aurvvaḥ saṃvarttako vibhuḥ।
pātālastho'rṇavagataḥ papau toyamayaṃ haviḥ ॥ 2.35.18 ॥
sahasracaraṇaṃ devaṃ sahasrāṃśuṃ sahasraśaḥ।
sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ yamāhurvai yuge yuge ॥ 2.35.19 ॥
nābhyāraṇyāḥ samudbhūtaṃ yasya paitāmahaṃ gṛham।
ekārṇavagate loke tatpaṅkajamapaṅkajam ॥ 2.35.20 ॥
yena te nihatā daityāḥ saṃgrāme tārakāmaye।
sarvvadevamayaṃ kṛtvā sarvāyudhadharaṃ vapuḥ ॥ 2.35.21 ॥
garuḍasthena cotsiktaḥ kālanemirnipātitaḥ।
uttarāṃśe samudrasya kṣīrodasyāmṛtodadheḥ।
yaḥ śete śāśvataṃ yogamāsthāya timiraṃ mahat ॥ 2.35.22 ॥
purāṇī garbhamadhatta divyaṃ tapaḥprakarṣādaditiḥ purā yam।
śakrañca yo daityagaṇāvaruddhaṃ garbhāvamānena bhṛśaṃ cakāra ॥ 2.35.23 ॥
yadānilo lokapadāni hṛtvā cakāra daityān salileśayāṃstān ।
kṛtvādidevastridivasya devāṃścakre sureśaṃ puruhūtameva ॥ 2.35.24 ॥
gārhapatyena vidhinā anvāhāryyeṇa karmmaṇā।
agnimāhavanīyañca vediñcaiva kuśasravam ॥ 2.35.25 ॥
prokṣaṇīyaṃ sruvañcaiva avabhṛthaṃ tathaiva ca।
atha trīniha yaścakre havyabhāga pradānmakhe ॥ 2.35.26 ॥
havyādāṃśca surāṃścakre kavyādāṃśca pitṝnapi।
bhogārthaṃ yajñavidhinā yo yajño yajñakarmmaṇi ॥ 2.35.27 ॥
yūpān samitsruvaṃ somaṃ pavitraṃ paridhīnapi।
yajñiyāni ca dravyāṇi yajñīyāṃśca tathānalān ॥ 2.35.28 ॥
sadasyān yajamānāṃśca aśvamedhān kratūttamān।
kṣaṇā nimeṣāḥ kāṣṭāśca kalāstraikālameva ca ॥ 2.35.30 ॥
muhūrttāstithayo māsā dinasaṃvatsarāstathā।
ṛtavaḥ kālayogāśca pramāṇaṃ trividhantathā ॥ 2.35.31 ॥
āyuḥ kṣetrāṇyupacayaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ rūpasauṣṭhavam।
medhā vittaṃ ca śauryyañca śāstrasyaiva ca pāraṇam ॥ 2.35.32 ॥
trayo varṇāstrayo lokāstraividyaṃ pāvakāstrayaḥ।
traikālyaṃ trīṇi karmmāṇi tisro māyāstrayo guṇāḥ ॥ 2.35.33 ॥
sṛṣṭā lokāḥ surāścaiva yenātyantena karmmaṇā।
sarvvabhūtagaṇāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ sarvvabhūtagaṇātmanā ॥ 2.35.34 ॥
nṛṇāmindriyapūrvveṇa yogena ramate ca yaḥ ।
gatāgatānāṃ yo netā sarvvatra vividheśvaraḥ ॥ 2.35.35 ॥
yo gatirdharmayuktānāmagatiḥ pāpakarmmaṇām।
cāturvarṇyasya prabhavaścāturvarṇyasya rakṣitā ॥ 2.35.36 ॥
cāturvidyasya yo vettā caturāśramasaṃśrayaḥ।
digantaraṃ nabho bhūmirāpo vāyurvibhāvasuḥ ॥ 2.35.37 ॥
candrasūryyadvayaṃ jyotiryugeśaḥ kṣaṇadācaraḥ।
yaḥ paraḥ śrūyate devo yaḥ paraṃ śrūyate tapaḥ ॥ 2.35.38 ॥
yaḥ parantapasaḥ prāhuryaḥ paramparamātmavān।
ādityādistu yo devo yaśca daityāntako vibhuḥ ॥ 2.35.39 ॥
yugānteṣvantako yaśca yaśca lokāntakāntakaḥ।
seturyo lokasetūnāṃ medhyo yo medhyakarmmaṇām ॥ 2.35.40 ॥
vedyo yo vedaviduṣāṃ prabhuryaḥ prabhavātmanām।
somabhūtastu bhūtānāmagnibhūto'gnivarcasām ॥ 2.35.41 ॥
manuṣyāṇāṃ manobhūtastapobhūtastapasvinām ।
vinayo nayatṛptānāṃ tejastejasvināmapi ॥ 2.35.42 ॥
vigraho vigrahāṇāṃ yo gatirgatimatāmapi।
ākāśa prabhavo vāyurvāyuprāṇā hutāśanaḥ ॥ 2.35.43 ॥
divā hutāśanaprāṇāḥ prāṇo'gnermadhusūdanaḥ।
raso'bhavacchoṇitaṃ vai śoṇitānmāṃsamucyate ॥ 2.35.44 ॥
māṃsāttu medaso janma medaso'sthi nirūpyate।
asthnā majjā samabhavanmajjātaḥ śukrasambhavaḥ ॥ 2.35.45 ॥
śukrādgharbhaḥ samabhavadrasamūlena karmmaṇā।
tatrāpi prathamañcāpastāḥ saumyarāśirucyate ॥ 2.35.46 ॥
garbhoṣmasambhavo jñeyo dvitīyo rāśirucyate।
śukraṃ somātmakaṃ vidyādārttavaṃ pāvakātmakam ॥ 2.35.47 ॥
bhāvau rasānugāvetau vīryye ca śaśipāvakau।
kaphavarge'bhavacchukraṃ pittavarge ca śoṇitam ॥ 2.35.48 ॥
kaphasya hṛdayaṃ sthānaṃ nābhyāṃ pittaṃ pratiṣṭitam।
dehasya madhye hṛdayaṃ sthānantu manasaḥ smṛtam ॥ 2.35.49 ॥
nābikoṣṭāntaraṃ yattu tatra devo hutāśanaḥ।
manaḥ prajāpatirjñeyaṃ kaphaḥ somo vibhāvyate ॥ 2.35.50 ॥
pittamagniḥ smṛtāvetāvagnisomātmakaṃ jagat।
vāyuḥ praveśanaṃ cakre saṅgataḥ paramātmanā।
sa pañcadhā śarīrastho vidyate varddhayet punaḥ ॥ 2.35.52 ॥
prāṇāpānau samānaśca udāno vyāna eva ca।
prāṇo'sya paramātmānaṃ varddhayan parivarttate ॥ 2.35.53 ॥
apānaḥ paścimaṃ kāyamudānorddhvaśarīragaḥ।
vyāno vyānasyate yena samānaḥ sarvvasandhiṣu ॥ 2.35.54 ॥
bhūtāvāptistatastasya jāyatendriyagocarā।
pṛthivī vāyurākāśamāpo jyotiśca pañcamam ॥ 2.35.55 ॥
sarvvendriyā niviṣṭāstaṃ svaṃ svaṃ yogaṃ pracakrire।
pārthivaṃ dehamāhustaṃ prāṇātmānaṃ ca mārutam ॥ 2.35.56 ॥
chidrāṇyākāśayonīni jalāsrāvaṃ pravarttate ।
saṅgrāmā viṣayāścaiva yasya vīryyātpravarttitāḥ ॥ 2.35.57 ॥
ityetān puruṣaḥ sarvvān sṛjaँllokān sanātanaḥ।
naidhane'smin kathaṃ loke naratvaṃ viṣṇurāgataḥ ॥ 2.35.58 ॥
eṣa naḥ saṃśayo dhīmanneṣa vai vismayo mahān ।
kathaṃ gatirgatimatāmāpanno mānuṣīṃ tanum ॥ 2.35.59 ॥
śrotumicchāmahe viṣṇoḥ karmmāṇi ca yathākramam।
āścaryyāṇi paraṃ viṣṇurvedadevaiśca kathyate ॥ 2.35.60 ॥
viṣṇorutpattimāścaryyaṃ kathayasva mahāmate।
etadāścaryyamākhyānaṃ kathyatāṃ vai sukhāvaham ॥ 2.35.61 ॥
prakhyātabalavīryyasya prādurbhāvā mahātmanaḥ।
karmmaṇāścaryyabhūtasya viṣṇoḥ sattvamihocyatām ॥ 2.35.62 ॥
ahañca kīrttayiṣyāmi prādurbhāvaṃ mahātmanaḥ।
yathā sa bhagavāñjāto mānuṣeṣu mahātapāḥ ॥ 2.35.63 ॥
jāyate ca yugānteṣu devakāryyarthasiddhaye ॥ 2.35.64 ॥
tasya divyatanuṃ viṣṇorgadato me nibodhata।
yugadharmme parāvṛtte kāle ca śithile prabhuḥ ॥ 2.35.65 ॥
kartuṃ dharmmavyavasthānaṃ jāyate mānuṣeṣviha।
bhṛgoḥ śāpanimittena devāsurakṛtena ca ॥ 2.35.66 ॥
kathaṃ devāsurakṛte adhyāhāramavāpnuyāt।
etadveditumicchāmo vṛttaṃ daivāsuraṃ katham ॥ 2.35.67 ॥
daivāsuraṃ yathāvṛttaṃ bruvatastannibodhata।
hiraṇyakaśipurdaityastrailokyaṃ prāk praśāsati ॥ 2.35.68 ॥
balinādhiṣṭitaṃ rāṣṭraṃ punarlokatraye kramāt।
sakhyamāsītparaṃ teṣāṃ devānāmasuraiḥ saha ॥ 2.35.69 ॥
nideśasthāyinaścaiva tayordevāsurābhavan ॥ 2.35.70 ॥
devāsurāṇāṃ ca tadā ghorakṣayakaro mahān ॥ 2.35.71 ॥
teṣāṃ dāyanimittaṃ vai saṃgrāṇā bahavo'bhavan।
vārāhe'smin daśa dvau ca ṣaṇḍāmārkottarāḥ smṛtā ॥ 2.35.72 ॥
nāmatastu samāsena śrṛṇudhvaṃ tān vivakṣataḥ।
prathamo nārasiṃhastu dvitīyaścāpi vāmanaḥ ॥ 2.35.73 ॥
tṛtīyaḥ sa tu vārāhaścaturtho'mṛtamandhanaḥ।
saṃgrāmaḥ pañcamaścaiva sughorastārakāmayaḥ ॥ 2.35.74 ॥
ṣaṣṭo hyāḍībakasteṣāṃ saptamastraipuraḥ smṛtaḥ।
andhakāro'ṣṭamasteṣāṃ dhvajaśca navamaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.35.75 ॥
vārttaśca daśamo jñeyastato hālā halaḥ smṛtaḥ।
smṛto dvādaśamasteṣāṃ ghorakolāhalo'paraḥ ॥ 2.35.76 ॥
hiraṇyakaśipurdaityo narasiṃhena sūditaḥ।
vāmanena balirvaddhastrailokyākramaṇe kṛte ॥ 2.35.77 ॥
hiraṇyākṣo hato dvandve prativāde tu daivataiḥ।
mahābalo mahāsattvaḥ saṃgrāmeṣvaparājitaḥ ॥ 2.35.78 ॥
prāhlādo nirjito yuddhe indreṇāmṛtamanthane ॥ 2.35.79 ॥
virocanastu prāhlādirnityamindravadhodyataḥ।
indreṇaiva sa vikramya nihatastārakāmaye ॥ 2.35.80 ॥
bhavādavadhyatāṃ prāpya viśeṣāstrādibhistu yaḥ।
sañjabho nihataḥ ṣaṣṭe śakrāviṣṭena viṣṇunā ॥ 2.35.81 ॥
nihatā dānavāḥ sarve tripurastryambakeṇa tu ॥ 2.35.82 ॥
jitadevamanuṣyaistu pitṛbhiścaiva saṅgatān ॥ 2.35.83 ॥
saṃvṛtān dānavāṃścaiva saṅgatān kṛtsnaśaśca tān ।
dhvaje lakṣyaṃ samāviśya vipravarttirmahābhujaḥ ॥ 2.35.85 ॥
daityāṃśca dānavāṃścaiva saṃhatān kṛtsnaśaśca tān।
rajiḥ kolāhale sarvān devaiḥ parivṛto'jayat।
ete daivāsurā vṛttāḥ saṃgrāmā dvādaśaiva tu।
devāsurakṣayakarāḥ prajānāmaśivāya ca ॥ 2.35.87 ॥
hiraṇyakaśipū rājā varṣāṇāmarbudaṃ babhau।
tathā śatasahasrāṇi hyadikāni dvisaptatiḥ ।
aśītiṃ ca sahasrāṇi trailokyasyeśvaro'bhavat ॥ 2.35.88 ॥
paryāye tasya rājā'nu balirvarṣārbudaṃ punaḥ ।
ṣaṣṭiṃ caiva sahasrāṇi triṃśataṃ niyutāni ca ॥ 2.35.89 ॥
bale rājyādhikārastu yāvatkālaṃ babhūva ha।
indrāstrayaste vikhyātā asurāṇāṃ mahaujasaḥ ।
daityasaṃsthamidaṃ sarvamāsīddaśayugaṃ kila ॥ 2.35.91 ॥
asapatnaṃ tataḥ sarvaṃ rāṣṭraṃ daśayugaṃ purā।
prahlādasya tataścādastrailokyaṃ kālaparyayāt ।
paryāyeṇa ca saṃprāpte trailokye pākaśāsanaḥ ॥ 2.35.93 ॥
tato'surān parityajya yajñe devā upāgaman ।
yajñe devānatha gate kāvyaṃ te hyasurābruvan ॥ 2.35.94 ॥
kṛtaṃ no miṣatāṃ rāṣṭraṃ tyaktvā yajñaṃ punargatāḥ।
sthātuṃ na śaknumo hyadya praviśāmo rasātalam ॥ 2.35.95 ॥
evamukto'bravīdetān viṣaṇṇaḥ sāntvayan girā।
mābhaiṣṭa dhārayiṣyāmi tejasā svena cāsurāḥ ॥ 2.35.96 ॥
vṛṣṭiroṣadhayaścaiva rasā vasu ca yadvayam।
kṛtsnā mayi ca tiṣṭhanti pādasteṣāṃ sureṣu vai।
yuṣmadarthaṃ pradāsyāmi tatsarvaṃ dhāryate mayā ॥ 2.35.97 ॥
tato devāsurān dṛṣṭvā dhṛtān kāvyena dhīmatā।
amantrayaṃstadā te vai saṃvignā vijigīṣayā ॥ 2.35.98 ॥
eṣa kāvya idaṃ sarvaṃ vyāvarttayati no balāt ।
sādhu gacchāmahe tūrṇaṃ kṣīṇānnāpyāyayasva tān ।
prasahya hatvā śiṣṭān vai pātālaṃ prāpayāmahe ॥ 2.35.99 ॥
tato devāḥ susaṃrabdhā dānavānabhisṛtya vai।
jadhnustai rvadhyamānāste kāvyamevābhidudruvuḥ ॥ 2.35.100 ॥
tataḥ kāvyastu tāndṛṣṭvā tūrṇaṃ devairabhidrutān।
samare'ktrakṣatārttāṃstān devebhyastān diteḥ sutān ॥ 2.35.101 ॥
kāvyo dṛṣṭvā sthitān devān tatra devo'bhyacintayat।
tānuvāca tato dhyātvā pūrvavṛttamanusmaran ॥ 2.35.102 ॥
trailokyaṃ vijitaṃ sarvaṃ vāmanena tribhiḥ kramaiḥ ।
balirbaddho hato jambho nihataśca virocanaḥ ॥ 2.35.103 ॥
mahārheṣu dvādaśasu saṃgrāmeṣu surairhatāḥ।
taistairupāyairbhūyiṣṭā nihatā ye pradhānataḥ ॥ 2.35.104 ॥
kiñcicchiṣṭāstu vai yūyaṃ yuddheṣvantyeṣu vai svayam।
nītiṃ vo hi vidhāsyāmi kālaḥ kaścitpratīkṣyatām ॥ 2.35.105 ॥
yāsyāmyahaṃ mahādevaṃ mantrārthe vijayāya vaḥ।
agnimāpyāyayeddhotā mantraireva bṛhaspatiḥ ॥ 2.35.106 ॥
tato yāsyāmyahaṃ devaṃ mantrārthe nīlalohitam।
yuṣmānanugrahīṣyāmi punaḥ paścādihāgataḥ ॥ 2.35.107 ॥
yūyaṃ tapaścaradhvaṃ vai saṃvṛtā valkalairvane।
na vai devā vadhiṣyanti yāvadāgamanaṃ mama ॥ 2.35.108 ॥
apratīpāṃstato mantrān devāt prāpya maheśvarāt।
yotsyāmahe punardevāṃstataḥ prāpsyatha vai jayam ॥ 2.35.109 ॥
tataste kṛtasaṃvādā devānūcustato'surāḥ।
nyastavādā vayaṃ sarve lokān yūyaṃ kramantu vai ॥ 2.35.110 ॥
vayaṃ tapaścariṣyāmaḥ saṃvṛtā valkalairvane।
prahlādasya vacaḥ śrutvā satyavyāharaṇaṃ tu tat ॥ 2.35.111 ॥
tato devā nivṛttā vai vijvarā muditāśca ha।
nyastaśastreṣu daityeṣu svān vai jagmuryathāgatān ॥ 2.35.112 ॥
tatastānabravītkāvyaḥ kañcitkālamupāsyatām।
nirutsukaistapoyuktaiḥ kālaṃ kāryārthasādhakaiḥ।
sa sandiśyāsurān kāvyo mahādevaṃ prapadya ca।
praṇamyenasuvācātha jagatprabhavamīśvaram ॥ 2.35.114 ॥
mantrānicchāmyahaṃ deva me nasanti bṛhaspatau।
parābhavāya devānāmasureṣvabhayāvahān ॥ 2.35.115 ॥
evamukto'bravīddevo mantrānicchasi vai dvija।
vrataṃ cara mayo ddiṣṭaṃ brahmacārī samāhitaḥ ॥ 2.35.116 ॥
pūrṇaṃ varṣasahasraṃ vai kuṇḍadhūmamavākśirāḥ।
yadyupāsyasi bhadrante matto mantramavāpsyasi ॥ 2.35.117 ॥
tathokto deva devena sa śukrastu mahātapāḥ।
pādau saṃspṛśya devasya bāḍhamityabhyabhāṣata ॥ 2.35.118 ॥
vrataṃ carāmyahaṃ śeṣaṃ yathoddiṣṭo'smi vai prabho।
tato niyukto devena kuṇḍadhāro'sya dhūmakṛt ॥ 2.35.119 ॥
asurāṇāṃ hitārthāya tasmiñchukre gate tadā।
mantrārthaṃ tatra vasati brahmacarye maheśvaraḥ ॥ 2.35.120 ॥
tadbuddhvā nātipūrvantu rājyaṃ nyastaṃ tadāsuraiḥ।
tasmiñchidre tadāmarṣā devāstān samabhidravan।
niśitāttāyudhāḥ sarve bṛhaspatipurogamāḥ ॥ 2.35.121 ॥
dṛṣṭvāsuragaṇā devān pragṛhītāyudhān punaḥ।
utpetuḥ sahasā sarve santrastāste tato'bhavan ॥ 2.35.122 ॥
nyastaśastre jaye datte ācāryavratamāsthite।
santyajya. samayaṃ devāste sapatnajighāṃsavaḥ ॥ 2.35.123 ॥
anācāryāstu bhadraṃ vo viśvastāstapasi sthitāḥ।
cīravalkājinadharā niṣkriyā niṣparigrahāḥ ॥ 2.35.124 ॥
raṇe vijetuṃ devān vai naśakṣyāmaḥ kathañcana।
aśuddhena prapadyāmaḥ śaraṇaṃ kāvyamātaram ॥ 2.35.125 ॥
prāpadyanta tato bhītāstadā caiva tadā'bhayam ॥ 2.35.127 ॥
dattanteṣāntu bhītānāṃ daityā nāmabhayārthinām।
abhijagmuḥ prasahyaitānavicārya balābalam।
tāṃstrastān vadhyamānāṃśca devairdṛṣṭvāsurāṃstadā ॥ 2.35.130 ॥
devī kruddhābravīdenānanindratvaṃ karomyaham।
saṃstabhya śīghraṃ saṃrambhādindraṃ sā'bhyacarattataḥ ॥ 2.35.131 ॥
tataḥ saṃstambhitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śakraṃdevāstu yūpavat।
vyadravanta tato bhītā dṛṣṭvā śakraṃ vaśīkṛtam ॥ 2.35.132 ॥
gateṣu surasaṅgheṣu viṣṇurindramabhāṣata।
māṃtvaṃ praviśa bhadrante neṣyāmi tvāṃ sureśvara ॥ 2.35.133 ॥
evamuktastato viṣṇuṃ praviveśa purandaraḥ।
viṣṇunā rakṣitaṃ dṛṣṭvā devī kruddhā vaco'vadat ॥ 2.35.134 ॥
eṣā tvāṃ viṣṇunā sārddhaṃ dahāmi maghavāniva।
miṣatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ dṛśyatāṃ me tapobalam ॥ 2.35.135 ॥
tayābhibhūtau tau devāvindraviṣṇū jajalpatuḥ।
kathaṃ mucyeva sahitau viṣṇurindramabhāṣata ॥ 2.35.136 ॥
indro'bravījjahi hyenāṃ yāvannau na dahedvibho।
viśeṣeṇābhibhūto'hamatastvañca hi mā ciram ॥ 2.35.137 ॥
tataḥ samīkṣya tāṃ viṣṇuḥ strīvadhaṃ karttumāsthitaḥ।
abhidhyāya tataścakramāpannaḥ satvaraṃ prabhuḥ ॥ 2.35.138 ॥
tasyāḥ satvaramāṇāyāḥ śīghrakārī surārihā।
striyā viṣṇustato devyā krūraṃ buddhvā cikīrṣitam।
kruddhastadastramāviddhya śiraściccheda mādhavaḥ ॥ 2.35.139 ॥
taṃ dṛṣṭvā strīvadhaṃ ghoraṃ cukopa bhṛgurīśvaraḥ।
tato'bhiśasto bhṛguṇā viṣṇurbhāryāvadhe tadā ॥ 2.35.140 ॥
yasmātte jānatā dharmānavadhyā strī niṣūditā।
tasmāttvaṃ saptakṛtvo vai mānuṣeṣu prapatsyasi ॥ 2.35.141 ॥
tatastenābhiśāpena naṣṭe dharme punaḥ punaḥ।
loke sarvahitārthāya jāyate mānuṣeṣviha ॥ 2.35.142 ॥
anuvyāhṛtya viṣṇuṃ sa tadādāya śiraḥ svayam।
samānīya tataḥ kāye apo gṛhyedamabravīt ॥ 2.35.143 ॥
eṣa tvāṃ viṣṇunā satye hatāṃ saṃjīvayāmyaham ।
yadi kṛtsno mayā dharmaścarito jñāyate'pi vā।
tena satyena jīvasva yadi satyaṃ bravīmyaham ॥ 2.35.144 ॥
satyābhivyāhṛtā tasyā devī saṃjīvitā tadā।
tadā tāṃ prokṣya śītābhiradbhirjīveti so'bravīt ॥ 2.35.145 ॥
tatastāṃ sarvabhūtāni dṛṣṭvā suptotthitāmiva।
sādhu sādhvityadṛśyānāṃ vācastāḥ sasvarurdiśaḥ ॥ 2.35.146 ॥
dṛṣṭvā sañjīvitāmevaṃ devīṃ tāṃ bhṛguṇā tadā।
miṣatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tadadbhutamivābhavat ॥ 2.35.147 ॥
asaṃbhrāntena bhṛguṇā patnīṃ sañjīvitāṃ tataḥ।
dṛṣṭvā śakro na lebhe'tha śarma kāvyabhayāttataḥ ॥ 2.35.148 ॥
prajāgare tataścendro jayantīmātmanaḥ sutām।
provāca matimān vākyaṃ svāṃ kanyāṃ pākaśāsanaḥ ॥ 2.35.149 ॥
eṣa kāvyo hyanindrāya carate dāruṇaṃ tapaḥ।
tenāhaṃ vyākulaḥ putri kṛto dhṛtimatā dṛḍham ॥ 2.35.150 ॥
gaccha sambhāvayasvainaṃ śramāpanayanaiḥ śubhaiḥ।
taistairmanonukūlaiśca hyupacārairatandritā ॥ 2.35.151 ॥
devī sā hīndratuhitā jayantī śubhacāriṇī।
pitrā yathoktaṃ kāvyaṃ sā kāvye kṛtavatī tadā।
gīrbhiścaivānukūlābhiḥ stuvatī valgubhāṣiṇī ॥ 2.35.153 ॥
gātrasaṃvāhanaiḥ kāle sevamānā sukhāvahaiḥ ।
śuśrūṣantyanukūlā ca uvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ ॥ 2.35.154 ॥
pūrṇe dhūmavrate cāpi ghore varṣasahasrike ।
vareṇa cchandayāmāsa kāvyaṃ prīto'bhavattadā ॥ 2.35.155 ॥
evaṃ bruvaṃstvayaikena cīrṇaṃ nānyena kenacit।
tasmāttvaṃ tapasā buddhyā śrutena ca balena ca ॥ 2.35.156 ॥
tejasā cāpi vibudhān sarvānabhibhaviṣyasi।
yacca kiñcinmama brahman vidyate bhṛgunandana ॥ 2.35.157 ॥
sāṅgañca sarahasyañca yajñopaniṣadāntathā।
pratibhāsyati te sarvaṃ taccādyantaṃ na kasyacit ॥ 2.35.158 ॥
sarvābhibhāvī tena tvaṃ dvijaśreṣṭo bhaviṣyasi।
evaṃ dattvā varāṃstasmai bhārgavāya punaḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.35.159 ॥
ajeyatvaṃ dhaneśatvamavadhyatvaṃ ca vai dadau।
etān labdhvā varān kāvyaḥ samprahṛṣṭatanūruhaḥ ॥ 2.35.160 ॥
harṣāt prādurbabhau tasya devastotraṃ maheśvaram।
tadā tiryaksthitastvevaṃ tuṣṭuve nīlalohitam ॥ 2.35.161 ॥
namo'stu śitikaṇṭāya surāpāya suvarcase।
ririhāṇāya lopāya vatsarāya jagatpate ॥ 2.35.162 ॥
kapardine hyūrddhvaromṇe hayāya karaṇāya ca।
saṃskṛtāya sutīrthāya devadevāya raṃhase ॥ 2.35.163 ॥
uṣṇīṣiṇe suvakrāya sahasrākṣāya mīḍhuṣe।
vasuretāya rudrāya tapase cīravāsase ॥ 2.35.164 ॥
hrasvāya muktakeśāya senānye rohitāya ca ॥ 2.35.165 ॥
kavaye rājavṛddhāya takṣakakrīḍanāya ca।
suvṛttāya suhastāya dhanvine bhārgavāya ca ॥ 2.35.166 ॥
sahasrabāhave caiva sahasrāmalacakṣuṣe।
sahasrakukṣaye caiva sahasracaraṇāya ca ॥ 2.35.167 ॥
sahasraśirase caiva bahurūpāya vedhase।
bhavāya viśvarūpāya śvetāya puruṣāya ca ॥ 2.35.168 ॥
niṣaṅgiṇe kavacine sūkṣmāya kṣapaṇāya ca।
tāmrāya caiva bhīmāya ugrāya ca śivāya ca ॥ 2.35.169 ॥
mahādevāya śarvvāya viśvarūpaśivāya ca ॥ 2.35.170 ॥
hiraṇyāya ca śiṣṭāya śreṣṭāya madhyamāya ca ।
pinākine ceṣumate citrāya rohitāya ca ॥ 2.35.171 ॥
dundubhyāyaikapādāya arhāya buddhaye tathā।
mṛgavyādhāya sarpāya sthāṇave bhīṣaṇāya ca ॥ 2.35.172 ॥
bahurūpāya cogrāya trinetrāyeśvarāya ca।
kapilāyaikavīrāya mṛtyave tryambakāya ca ॥ 2.35.173 ॥
vāstoṣpate vinākāya śaṅkarāya śivāya ca।
āraṇyāya guhasthāya yatine brahmacāriṇe ॥ 2.35.174 ॥
sāṅkhyāya caiva yogāya dhyānine dīkṣitāya ca।
antarhitāya śarvvāya mānyāya māline tathā ॥ 2.35.175 ॥
buddhāya caiva puṇyāya dhārmikāya śubhāya ca।
rodhase cekitānāya brahmiṣṭāya maharṣaye ॥ 2.35.176 ॥
catuṣpādāya medhyāya dharmiṇe śīghragāya ca।
śikhaṇḍine kapālāya daṃṣṭriṇe viśvamedhase ॥ 2.35.177 ॥
apratīghātāya dīptāya bhāskarāya sumedhase।
krūrāya vikṛtāyaiva bībhatsāya śivāya ca ॥ 2.35.178 ॥
śucaye rerihāṇāya sadyojātāya mṛtyave।
piśitāśāya kharvāya medhāya vaidyutāya ca ॥ 2.35.181 ॥
dakṣāya ca jaghanyāya lokānāmīśvarāya ca।
śreṣṭāya vāmadevāya īśānāya ca dhīmate।
mahākalpāya dīptāya rādenāya hasāya ca ॥ 2.35.190 ॥
vṛtadhanvane kavicine rathine ca varūthine।
bhṛgunāthāya śukrāya vahniriṣṭāya dhīmate ॥ 2.35.191 ॥
aghāya aghaśaṃsāya vipriyāya priyāya ca ।
digvāsaḥkṛttivāsāya bhagaghnāya namo'stu te ॥ 2.35.192 ॥
paśūnāṃ pataye caiva bhūtānāṃ pataye namaḥ।
praṇane ṛgyajuḥsāmne svadhāyai ca sudhāya ca ॥ 2.35.193 ॥
vaṣaṭkāratamāyaiva tubhyamantātmane namaḥ ।
sraṣṭre dhātre tathā hotre hartre ca kṣapaṇāya ca ॥ 2.35.194 ॥
bhūtabhavyabhavāyaiva tubhyaṃ kālātmane namaḥ।
vasave caiva sādhyāya rudrādityāśvināya ca ॥ 2.35.195 ॥
viśvāya marute caiva tubhyandevātmane namaḥ।
agnisomartvigijyāya paśumantrauṣadhāya ca ॥ 2.35.196 ॥
dakṣiṇāvabhṛthāyaiva tubhyaṃ yajñātmane namaḥ ।
tapase caiva satyāya tyāgāya ca śamāya ca ॥ 2.35.197 ॥
ahiṃsāyāpyalobhāya suveśāyātiśāya ca।
sarvabhūtātmabhūtāya tubhyaṃ yogātmane namaḥ ॥ 2.35.198 ॥
pṛthivyai cāntarikṣāya divāya ca mahāya ca।
janastapāya satyāya tubhyaṃ lokātmane namaḥ ॥ 2.35.199 ॥
avyaktāyātha mahate bhūtāyaivondriyāya ca ।
tanmātrāya mahāntāya tubhyaṃ tattvātmane namaḥ ॥ 2.35.200 ॥
nityāya cārthaliṅgāya sūkṣmāya cetanāya ca।
śuddhāya vibhave caiva tubhyaṃ nityātmane namaḥ ॥ 2.35.201 ॥
namaste triṣu lokeṣu svarānteṣu bhavādiṣu।
satyānteṣu mahānteṣu caturṣu ca namo'stu te ॥ 2.35.202 ॥
namaḥstotre mayā hyasmin sadasadvyāhṛtaṃ vibho।
madbhakta iti brahmaṇya sarvantat kṣantumarhasi ॥ 2.35.203 ॥
evamārādhya deveśamīśānaṃ nīlalohitam।
brahmeti praṇatastasmai prāñjalirvākyamabravīt ॥ 2.36.1 ॥
kāvyasya gātraṃ saṃspṛśya hastena prītimān bhavaḥ।
nikāmaṃ darśanaṃ dattvā tatraivāntaradhīyata ॥ 2.36.2 ॥
tataḥ so'ntarhite tasmin deveśānucare tadā।
tiṣṭhantīṃ prāñjalirbhūtvā jayantīmidamabravīt ॥ 2.36.3 ॥
kasya tvaṃ subhage kā vā duḥkhite mayi duḥkhitā।
mahatā tapasā yuktaṃ kimarthaṃ māñjugopasi ॥ 2.36.4 ॥
anayā satataṃ bhaktyā praśrayeṇa damena ca।
snehena caiva suśroṇi prīto'smi varavarṇini ॥ 2.36.5 ॥
kimicchasi varārehe kaste kāmaḥ samṛdhyatām।
taṃ te saṃpūrayāmyadya yadyapi syāt sudurlabham ॥ 2.36.6 ॥
evamuktā''bravīdanaṃ tapasā jñātumarhasi।
cikīrṣitaṃ me brahniṣṭhatvaṃ hi vettha yathātatham ॥ 2.36.7 ॥
evamukte'bravīdenāṃ dṛṣṭvā divyena cakṣuṣā।
māhendrī tvaṃ varārohe maddhitārthamihāgatā ॥ 2.36.8 ॥
mayā saha tvaṃ suśroṇi daśa varṣāṇi bhāmini।
adṛśyaṃ sarvabhūtaistu saṃprayogamihecchasi ॥ 2.36.9 ॥
devendrānalavarṇābhe varārohe sulocane।
imaṃ vṛṇīṣva kāmaṃ te matto vai valgubhāṣiṇi ॥ 2.36.10 ॥
evaṃ bhavatu gacchāmo gṛhān vai mattakāśini ।
tataḥ svagṛhamāgamya jayantyā sahitaḥ prabhuḥ ॥ 2.36.11 ॥
sa tayā saṃ va saddevyā daśa varṣāṇi bhāgaśaḥ।
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ māyayā saṃvṛtastadā ॥ 2.36.12 ॥
kṛtārthamāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā kāvyaṃ sarve diteḥ sutāḥ ।
abhijagmurgṛhaṃ tasya muditāste didṛkṣavaḥ ॥ 2.36.13 ॥
gatā yadā na paśyanto jayantyā saṃvṛtaṃ gurum।
dākṣiṇyaṃ tasya tadbudhvā pratijagmuryathāgatam ॥ 2.36.14 ॥
bṛhaspatistu saṃruddhaṃ jñātvā kāvyaṃ cakāra ha।
pitrarthe daśa varṣāṇi jayantyā hitakāmyayā ॥ 2.36.15 ॥
buddhvā tadantaraṃ so'tha daityānāmiva coditaḥ।
kāvyasya rūpamāsthāya so'surānsamabhāṣata ॥ 2.36.16 ॥
tataḥ samāgatān dṛṣṭvā bṛhaspatiruvāca tān।
svāgataṃ mama yājyānāṃ saṃprāpto'smi hitāya ca ॥ 2.36.17 ॥
ahaṃ vo'dhyāpayiṣyāmi prāptā vidyā mayā hi sā।
tataste hṛṣṭamanaso vidyārthamupapedire ॥ 2.36.18 ॥
pūrṇakāmastadā tasmin samaye daśavārṣike।
buddhiṃ cakre tataścāpi yājyānāṃ pratyavekṣaṇe ॥ 2.36.20 ॥
devi gacchāmahe draṣṭuṃ tava yājyān śucismite।
vibhrāntaprekṣite sādhvi trivarṇāyatalocane ॥ 2.36.21 ॥
evamuktā'bravīddevī bhaja bhaktān mahāvrata।
eṣa brahman satāṃ dharmo na dharmaṃ lopayāmi te ॥ 2.36.22 ॥
tato gatvāsurān dṛṣṭvā devācāryeṇa dhīmatā।
vāñcitān kāvyarūpeṇa vedhasā'suramabravīt ॥ 2.36.23 ॥
vañcitā bata yūyaṃ vai mayi śakte tu dānavāḥ ॥ 2.36.24 ॥
śrutvā tathā bruvāṇantaṃ sambhrāntā ditijāstataḥ।
sampramūḍhāḥ sthitāḥ sarve prāpadyanta na kiñcana।
tatasteṣu pramūḍheṣu kāvyastān punarabravīt ॥ 2.36.26 ॥
ācāryyo vo hyahaṃ kāvyo devācāryo'yamaṅgirāḥ।
anugacchata māṃ sarve tyajatainaṃ bṛhaspatim ॥ 2.36.27 ॥
tadā'surā viśeṣantu na vyajānaṃstayordvayoḥ ॥ 2.36.28 ॥
bṛhaspatiruvācaitānasambhrānto'yamaṅgirāḥ।
kāvyo'haṃ yo gururdaityā madrūpo'yaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ ॥ 2.36.29 ॥
sa mohayati rūpeṇa māmakenaiṣa vo'surāḥ।
śrutvā tasya tataste vai saṃmantryārthavaco'bruvan ॥ 2.36.30 ॥
ayanno daśa varṣāṇi satataṃ śāsti vai prabhuḥ।
eṣa vai gururasmākamantarepsurayaṃ dvijaḥ ॥ 2.36.31 ॥
tataste dānavāḥ sarve praṇipatyābhivādya ca।
vacanaṃ jagṛhustasya cirābhyāsena mohitāḥ ॥ 2.36.32 ॥
ūcustamasurāḥ sarve kruddhāḥ saṃraktalocanāḥ.
ayaṅgururhite'smākaṃ gaccha tvaṃ nāsi no guruḥ ॥ 2.36.33 ॥
bhārgavo'ṅgiraso vāyaṃ bhavatvevaiṣa noguruḥ।
sthitā vayaṃ nideśe'sya gacchatvaṃ sādhu mā ciram ॥ 2.36.34 ॥
evamuktvāsurāḥ sarve prāpadyanta bṛhaspatim।
yadā na pratipadyante tenoktaṃ tanmahaddhitam ॥ 2.36.35 ॥
cukopa bhārgavasteṣāmavalepena vai tadā।
bodhitā hi mayā yasmānna māṃ bhajata dānavāḥ ॥ 2.36.36 ॥
tasmāt pranaṣṭa saṃjñāṃ vai parābhavaṅgamiṣyatha।
idi vyāhṛtya tān kāvyo jagāmātha yathāgatam ॥ 2.36.37 ॥
kṛtārthaḥ sa tadā hṛṣṭaḥ svaṃ rūpaṃ pratyapadyata।
buddhvā'surāṃstadā bhraṣṭān kṛtārtho'ntaradhīyata ॥ 2.36.38 ॥
tataḥ pranaṣṭe tasmiṃste vibhrāntā dānavāstadā।
aho dhig vañcitāḥ smeha parasparamathābruvan ॥ 2.36.39 ॥
pṛṣṭhato vimukhāścaiva tāḍitā vedhasā vayam।
dagdhāścaivopayogācca svesve cārtheṣu māyayā ॥ 2.36.40 ॥
tato'surāḥ paritrastā devebhyastvaritā yayuḥ।
prahlādamagrataḥ kṛtvā kāvyasyānugamaṃ punaḥ ॥ 2.36.41 ॥
tataḥ kāvyaṃ samāsādya abhitasthu ravāṅmukhāḥ।
tānāgatān punardṛṣṭvā kāvyo yājyānuvāca ha ॥ 2.36.42 ॥
mayāpi bodhitāḥ kāle yato māṃ nābhinandatha।
tatastenāvalepena gatā yūthaṃ parābhavam ॥ 2.36.43 ॥
prahlādastamathovāca mānaṃ tvaṃ tyaja bhārgava।
svān yājyān bhajamānāṃśca bhaktāṃścaiva viśeṣataḥ ॥ 2.36.44 ॥
tvayā pṛṣṭā vayaṃ tena devācāryeṇa mohitāḥ।
bhaktānarhasi nastrātuṃ jñātvā dīrgheṇa cakṣuṣā ॥ 2.36.45 ॥
yadi nastvaṃ na kuruṣe prasādaṃ bhṛgunandana।
apadhyātā stvayā hyadya pravekṣyāmo rasātalam ॥ 2.36.46 ॥
jñātvā kāvyo yathātattvaṃ kāruṇyenānukampayā ।
evamukto'nunītaḥ sa stutaḥ kopaṃ nyayacchata ॥ 2.36.47 ॥
uvācedanna bhetavyaṃ na gantanyaṃ rasātalam।
avaśyambhāvī hyartho'yaṃ prāpto vo mayi jāgrati ॥ 2.36.48 ॥
na śakyamanyathā kartuṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hi balavattaram ।
saṃjñā pranaṣṭā yā vo'dya kāmaṃ tāṃ pratilapsyatha ॥ 2.36.49 ॥
prāptaḥ paryyāyakālo va iti brahmā'bhyabhāṣata।
matprasādācca yuṣmābhirbhuktaṃ trailokyamūrjjitam ॥ 2.36.50 ॥
yugākhyo daśa saṃpūrṇo devānākramya mūrddhani।
tāvantameva kālaṃ vai brahmā rājyamabhāṣata ॥ 2.36.51 ॥
sāvarṇike punastubhyaṃ rājyaṃ kila bhaviṣyati।
lokānāmīśvaro bhāvī pautrastava punarbaliḥ ॥ 2.36.52 ॥
evaṃ kilamahaṃ proktaḥ pautraste brahmaṇā svayam।
tathāhṛteṣu lokeṣu tapo'sya na kilābhavat ॥ 2.36.53 ॥
yasmāt pravṛttayaścāsya na kāmānabhisandhitāḥ।
tasmādajena prītena dattaṃ sāvarṇike'ntare ॥ 2.36.54 ॥
devarājyaṃ balerbhāvyamiti māmīśvaro'bravīt।
tasmādadṛśyo bhūtānāṃ kālākāṅkṣī sa tiṣṭhati ॥ 2.36.55 ॥
prītena cāmaratvaṃ vai dattaṃ tubyaṃ svayambhuvā।
tasmānnirutsu kastvaṃ vai paryyāyaṃ saha mākulaḥ ॥ 2.36.56 ॥
na ca śakyaṃ mayā tubhyaṃ purastādvai visarpitum ।
brahmaṇā pratiṣiddho'smi bhaviṣyaṃ jānatā prabho ॥ 2.36.57 ॥
imau ca śiṣyau dvau mahyaṃ tulyāvetau bṛhaspateḥ ।
daivataiḥ saha saṃrabdhān sarvvān vo dhārayiṣyataḥ ॥ 2.36.58 ॥
evamuktastu daiteyāḥ kāvyenākliṣṭakarmmaṇā।
tatastābhyāṃ yayuḥ sārddhaṃ prahlādapramukhāstadā ॥ 2.36.59 ॥
avaśyambhāvamarthatvaṃ śrutvā śukrācca dānavāḥ।
sakṛdāśaṃsamānāste jayaṃ kāvyena bhāṣitam ॥ 2.36.60 ॥
daṃśitāḥ sāyudhāḥ sarve tato devān samāhvayan।
atha devāsurān dṛṣṭvā saṃgrāme samupasthitān ॥ 2.36.61 ॥
tataḥ saṃvṛttasannāhā devāstān samayodhayan।
daivāsure tatastasmin varttamāne śataṃ samāḥ।
ajayannasurā devān bhagnā devā amantrayan ॥ 2.36.62 ॥
ṣaṇḍāmārkaprabhāvaṃ na jānīmastva surairvayam।
tasmādyajñaṃ samuddiśya kāryyaṃ cātmahitañca yat ॥ 2.36.63 ॥
athopāmantrayan devāḥ ṣaṇḍāmārkau tu tāvubhau ॥ 2.36.64 ॥
grahaṃ taṃ vā grahīṣyāmo hyanujitya tu dānavān ॥ 2.36.65 ॥
evaṃ tatyajatustau tu ṣaṇḍāmārkau tadāsurān ।
tato devā jayaṃ prāptā dānavāśca parābhavam ॥ 2.36.66 ॥
devāsurān parābhāvya ṣaṇḍāmārkāvupāgaman।
kāvyaśāpābhibhūtāśca hyanādhārāśca te punaḥ ॥ 2.36.67 ॥
vadhyamānāstadā devairviviśuste rasātalam।
evaṃ nirudyamāste vai kṛtāḥ śakreṇa dānavāḥ।
tataḥ prabhṛti śāpena bhṛgunaimittikena ca ॥ 2.36.68 ॥
jajñe punaḥ punarviṣṇuryajñe ca śithile prabhuḥ।
karttuṃ dharmmavyavasthānamadharmmasya ca nāśanam ॥ 2.36.69 ॥
prahlādasya nideśe tu ye'surā na vyavasthitāḥ।
manuṣyavadhyāṃstān sarvvān brahmā vyāhārayat prabhuḥ ॥ 2.36.70 ॥
dharmmānnārāyaṇastasmān sambhūtaścākṣuṣe'ntare।
yajñaṃ pravartayāmāsa caitye vaivasvate'ntare ॥ 2.36.71 ॥
prādurbhāve tadānyasya brahmaivāsīt purohitaḥ।
caturthyāntu yugākhyāyāmāpanneṣvasureṣvatha ॥ 2.36.72 ॥
sambhūtaḥ sa samudrāntarhiraṇyakaśiporvadhe।
dvitīyo narasiṃṅo'bhūdrudraḥ surapurassaraḥ ॥ 2.36.73 ॥
yajamānantu daityendramadityāḥ kulanandanaḥ।
dvijo bhūtvā śubhe kāle baliṃ vairocanampurā ॥ 2.36.75 ॥
trailokyasya bhavān rājā tvayi sarvvaṃ pratiṣṭitam।
dātumarhasi me rājan vikramāṃstrīniti prabhuḥ ॥ 2.36.76 ॥
dadāmītyeva taṃ rājā balirvairocano'bravīt।
vāmanantaṃ ca vijñāya tato'numuditaḥ svayam ॥ 2.36.77 ॥
sa vāmano divaṃ khaṃ ca pṛthivīṃ ca dvijottamāḥ।
tribhiḥ kramairviśvamidaṃ jagadākrāmata prabhuḥ ॥ 2.36.78 ॥
atyaricyata bhūtātmā bhāskaraṃ svena tejasā।
prakāśayan diśaḥ sarvvāḥ pradiśaśca mahāyaśāḥ ॥ 2.36.79 ॥
śuśubhe sa mahābāhuḥ sarvvalokān prakāśayan।
āsurīṃ śriyamāhṛtya trīṃllokāṃśca janārdanaḥ।
saputrapautrānasurān pātālatalamānayat ॥ 2.36.80 ॥
namuciḥ śambaraścaiva prahlādaścaiva viṣṇunā।
krūrā hatā vinirddhūtā diśaḥ saṃpratipedire ॥ 2.36.81 ॥
mahābhūtāni bhūtātmā saviśeṣāṇi mādhavaḥ।
kālañca sakalaṃ viprāṃstatrādbhutamadarśayat ॥ 2.36.82 ॥
tasya gātre jagatsarvamātmānamanupaśyati ।
na kiñcidasti lokeṣu yadavyāptaṃ mahātmanā ॥ 2.36.83 ॥
tadvai rūpamupendrasya devadānavamānavāḥ।
dṛṣṭvā sammumuhuḥ sarve viṣṇutejovimohitāḥ ॥ 2.36.84 ॥
baliḥ silo mahāpāśaiḥ sabandhuḥ sasuhṛdgaṇaḥ।
virocana kulaṃ sarvaṃ pātāle sanniveśitam ॥ 2.36.85 ॥
tataḥ sarvāmaraiśvaryaṃ dattvendrāya mahātmane।
mānuṣeṣu mahābāhuḥ prādurāsījjanārdanaḥ ॥ 2.36.86 ॥
etāstisraḥ smṛtāstasya divyāḥ sambhūtayaḥ śubhāḥ।
mānuṣyāḥ sapta yāstasya śāpajāṃstānnibodhata ॥ 2.36.87 ॥
tretāyuge tu daśame dattātreyo babhūva ha।
naṣṭe dharme caturthaśca mārkaṇḍeyapuraḥsaraḥ ॥ 2.36.88 ॥
pañcamaḥ pañcadaśyāṃ tu tretāyāṃ sambabhūva ha।
māndhātuścakravarttitve tasthau tathyapuraḥsaraḥ ॥ 2.36.89 ॥
jāmadagnyastathā ṣaṣṭo viśvāmitrapuraḥsaraḥ ॥ 2.36.90 ॥
caturviṃśe yuge rāmo vasiṣṭena purodhasā।
saptamo rāva ṇasyārthe jajñe daśarathātmajaḥ ॥ 2.36.91 ॥
aṣṭamo dvāpare viṣṇuraṣṭāviṃśe parāśarāt ।
vedavyāsastato jajñe jātūkarṇapuraḥsaraḥ ॥ 2.36.92 ॥
tathaiva navamo viṣṇuradityāḥ kaśyapātmajaḥ।
devakyāṃ vasudevāttu brahnagārgyapuraḥsaraḥ ॥ 2.36.93 ॥
aprameyo niyojyaśca yatra kāmacaro vaśī।
krījate bhagavāँ lloke bālaḥ krījanakairiva ॥ 2.36.94 ॥
na pramātuṃ mahābāhuḥ śakyo'sau madhusūdanaḥ।
paraṃ paramametasmādviśvarūpānna vidyate ॥ 2.36.95 ॥
aṣṭāviṃśa time tadvaddvāparasyāṃśasaṅkṣaye।
naṣṭe dharme tadā jajñe viṣṇurvṛṣṇikule prabhuḥ ॥ 2.36.96 ॥
karttuṃ dharmavyavasthānamasurāṇāṃ praṇāśanam।
mohayan sarvabhūtāni yogātmā yogamāyayā ॥ 2.36.97 ॥
praviṣṭo mānuṣīṃ yoniṃ pracchannaścarate mahīm।
vihārārthaṃ manuṣyeṣu sāndīpanipuraḥsaram ॥ 2.36.98 ॥
yatra kaṃsañca śālvañca dvividañca mahāsuram।
ariṣṭaṃ vṛṣabhañcaiva pūtanāṃ keśinaṃ hayam ॥ 2.36.99 ॥
nāgaṃ kuvalayāpīḍaṃ mallarājagṛhādhipam।
daityān mānuṣadehasthān sūdayāmāsa vīryavān ॥ 2.36.100 ॥
chinnaṃ bāhusahasrañca bāṇasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ ।
narakaśca hataḥ saṅkhaye yavanaśca mahābalaḥ ॥ 2.36.101 ॥
hṛtāni ca mahīpānāṃ sarvaratnāni tejasā।
durācārā śca nihatāḥ pārthivā ye rasātale ॥ 2.36.102 ॥
ete lokahitārthāya prādurbhāvā mahātmanaḥ।
asminneva yuge kṣīṇe sandhyā śliṣṭe bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.36.103 ॥
kalkirviṣṇuyaśā nāma pārāśaryaḥ pratāpavān।
daśamo bhāvyasambhūto yājñavalkyapuraḥsaraḥ ॥ 2.36.104 ॥
anukarṣan sarvasenāṃ hastyaśvarathasaṅkulām।
pragṛhītāyudhaurviprairvṛtaḥ śatasahasraśaḥ ॥ 2.36.105 ॥
nātyarthaṃ dhārmikā ye ca ye ca dharmadviṣaḥ vkacit।
īdīcyānmadhyadeśāṃśca tathā vindhyāparāntikān ॥ 2.36.106 ॥
tathaiva dākṣiṇātyāṃśca dravijān siṃhalaiḥ saha।
gāndhārān pāradāṃścaiva pahlavān yavanāñchakān ॥ 2.36.107 ॥
lampākānandhakān rudrān kirātāṃścaiva sa prabhuḥ ॥ 2.36.108 ॥
pravṛttacakrobalavān mlecchānāmantakṛdbalī।
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ pṛthivīṃ vicariṣyati ॥ 2.36.109 ॥
mānavaḥ sa tu saṃjajñe devasyāṃśena dhīmataḥ ।
pūrvajanmani viṣṇuryaḥ pramitirnāma vīryavān ॥ 2.36.110 ॥
gātreṇa vai candrasamaḥ pūrṇe kaliyuge'bhavat।
ityetāstasya devasya daśa sambhūtayaḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.36.111 ॥
taṃ taṃ kālañca kāryañca tattaduddiśya kāraṇam।
aṃśena triṣu lokeṣu tāstā yonīḥ prapatsyate ॥ 2.36.112 ॥
pañcaviṃśotthite kalpe pañcaviṃśati vai samāḥ।
vinighnan sarvvabhūtāni mānuṣāneva sarvvaśaḥ ॥ 2.36.113 ॥
kṛtvā bījāvaśeṣāntu mahīṃ krūreṇa karmmaṇā।
saṃśātayitvā vṛṣalān prāyaśastānadhārmmikān ॥ 2.36.114 ॥
tataḥ sa vai tadā kalkiścaritārthaḥ sasainikaḥ।
karmaṇā nihatā ye tu siddhāste tu punaḥ svayam ॥ 2.36.115 ॥
akasmāt kupitānyonyaṃ bhaviṣyanti ca mohitāḥ ।
kṣapayitvā tu tān sarvān bāvinārthena coditān ॥ 2.36.116 ॥
gaṅgāyamunayormadhye niṣṭāṃ prāpsyati sānugaḥ।
tato vyatīte kalkau tu sāmānyaiḥ saha sainikaiḥ ॥ 2.36.117 ॥
nṛpeṣvatha vinaṣṭeṣu tadā tvapragrahāḥ prajāḥ।
rakṣaṇe vinivṛtte tu hatvā cānyonyamāhave ॥ 2.36.118 ॥
purāṇi hitvā grāmāṃśca tulyāstā niṣparigrahāḥ ॥ 2.36.119 ॥
pranaṣṭaśrutidharmāśca naṣṭadharmāśramāstathā।
saritparvatasevinyaḥ patramūlaphalāśanāḥ।
cīra patrājinadharāḥ saṅkaraṃ ghoramāsthitāḥ ॥ 2.36.121 ॥
alpāyuṣo naṣṭavārttā bahvābādhāḥ suduḥkhitāḥ।
evaṃ kaṣṭamanuprāptāḥ kalisandhyaṃśake tadā ॥ 2.36.122 ॥
prajāḥ kṣayaṃ prayāsyanti sārddhaṃ kaliyugena tu ।
kṣīṇe kaliyuge tasmin pravṛtte ca kṛte punaḥ ॥ 2.36.123 ॥
prapatsyante yathānyāyaṃ svabhāvādeva nānyatā।
ityetat kīrtitaṃ sarvaṃ devāsuraviceṣṭitam ॥ 2.36.124 ॥
yaduvaṃśaprasaṅgena mahadvo vaiṣṇavaṃ yaśaḥ ।
turvasostu pravakṣyāmi pūrordruhyoranostathā ॥ 2.36.125 ॥
turvasostu suto vahnirvahnergobhānurātmajaḥ।
gobhānostu suto vīrastrisānuraparājitaḥ ॥ 2.37.1 ॥
karandhamastrisānostu maruttasya na cātmajaḥ।
anyastvavīkṣito rājā maruttaḥ kathitaḥ purā ॥ 2.37.2 ॥
anavatyo maruttastu sa rājāsīditi śrutam।
duṣkṛtaṃ pauravaṃ cāpi sarve putramakalpayan ॥ 2.37.3 ॥
evaṃ yayādiśāpena jarāyāḥ saṃkrameṇa tu ।
turvasoḥ pauravaṃ vaṃśaṃ praviveśa purā kila ॥ 2.37.4 ॥
duṣkṛtasya tu dāyādaḥ śarūtho nāma pārthivaḥ।
śarūthāttu janāpīḍaścatvārastasya cātmajāḥ ॥ 2.37.5 ॥
pāṇḍyaśca keralaścaiva colaḥ kulyastathaiva ca।
teṣāṃ janapadāḥ kulyāḥ pāṇḍyāścolāḥ sakeralāḥ ॥ 2.37.6 ॥
druhyostu tanayau vīrau babhruḥ setuśca viśrutau।
aruddhaḥ setuputrastu bābhravo ripurucyate ॥ 2.37.7 ॥
yauvanāśvena samiti kṛcchreṇa nihato balī।
yuddhaṃ sumahadāsīttu māsān pari caturdaśa ॥ 2.37.8 ॥
aruddhasya tu dāyādo gāndhāro nāma pārthivaḥ।
khyāyate yasya nāmnā tu gāndhāraviṣayo mahān ॥ 2.37.9 ॥
gāndhāradeśajāścāpi turagā vājināṃ varāḥ।
gāndhāraputro dharmmastu ghṛtastasya suto'bhavat ॥ 2.37.10 ॥
ghṛtasya durdamo jajñe pracetāstasya cātmajaḥ ।
pracetasaḥ putraśataṃ rājānaḥ sarva eva te ॥ 2.37.11 ॥
mleccharāṣṭrādhipāḥ sarve hyudīcīṃ diśamāśritāḥ।
anoḥ putrā mahātmānastrayaḥ paramadhārmmikāḥ ॥ 2.37.12 ॥
sabhānarasya putrastu vidvān kālānalo nṛpaḥ ॥ 2.37.13 ॥
kālānalasya dharmmātmā sṛñjayo nāma dhārmikaḥ ।
sṛñjayasyābhavat putro vīro rājā purañjayaḥ ॥ 2.37.14 ॥
āsīdindrasamo rājā pratiṣṭitayaśā divi।
mahāmanāḥ sutastasya mahā śālasya dhārmikaḥ ॥ 2.37.16 ॥
saptadvīpeśvaro rājā cakravarttī mahāyaśāḥ।
mahāmanāstu putrau dvau janayāmāsa viśrutau ॥ 2.37.17 ॥
uśīnarañca dharmajñaṃ titikṣuñcaiva dhārmikam।
uśīnarasya patnyastu pañca rājarṣivaṃśajāḥ ॥ 2.37.18 ॥
mṛgā kṛmī navā darvā pañcamī ca dṛṣadvatī।
uśīnarasya putrāstu pañca tāsu kulodvahāḥ।
tapasā te sumahatā jātavṛddhāśca dhārmikāḥ ।। 37.19।
mṛgāyāstu mṛgaḥ putro navāyā nava eva tu।
kṛmyāḥ kṛmistu darvāyāḥ suvrato nāma dhārmikaḥ ॥ 2.37.19 ॥
dṛṣadvatīsutaścāpi śivirauśīnaro dvijāḥ।
śiveḥ śivapuraṃ khyātaṃ yaudheyantu mṛgasya tu ॥ 2.37.20 ॥
navasya navarāṣṭrantu kṛmestu kṛmilā purī।
suvratasya tathā vṛṣṭā śiviputrānnibodhata ॥ 2.37.21 ॥
śivestu śivayaḥ putrāścatvāro lokasammatāḥ।
vṛṣadarbhaḥ suvīrastu kekayo madrakastathā ॥ 2.37.22 ॥
teṣāñjanapadāḥ sphītāḥ kekayā mādrakāstathā।
vṛṣadarbhāḥ sūcidarbhāstitikṣoḥ śrṛṇuta prajāḥ ॥ 2.37.23 ॥
taitikṣurabhavadrājā pūrvasyāndiśi viśrutaḥ।
uśadratho mahābāhustasya hemaḥ suto'bhavat ॥ 2.37.24 ॥
hemasya sutapā jajñe sutaḥ sutayaśā balī ।
jāto manuṣyayonyāṃ vai kṣīṇe vaṃśe prajepsayā ॥ 2.37.25 ॥
mahāyogī sa tu balirbaddho yaḥ sa mahāmanāḥ।
putrānutpādayāmāsa cāturvarṇyakarān bhuvi ॥ 2.37.26 ॥
aṅgaṃ sa janayāmāsa vaṅgaṃ suhlaṃ tathaiva ca।
puṇḍraṃ kaliṅgañca tathā bāleyaṃ kṣatramucyate ॥ 2.37.27 ॥
bāleyā brāhmaṇāścaiva tasya vaṃśakarāḥ prabhoḥ।
balestu brahmaṇā dattā varāḥ prītena dhīmate ॥ 2.37.28 ॥
mahāyogitvamāyuśca kalpāyuḥparimāṇakam।
saṃgrāme cāpyajeyatvaṃ dharme caiva prabhāvanā ॥ 2.37.29 ॥
trailokyadarśanañcaiva prādhānyaṃ prasave tathā।
bale cāprati matvaṃ vai dharmatattvārthadarśanam ॥ 2.37.30 ॥
caturo niyatān varṇān tvaṃ vai sthāpayiteti ca।
ityukto vibhunā rājā baliḥ śāntimparāṃ yayau ॥ 2.37.31 ॥
kālena mahatā vidvān svaṃ vai sthānamupāgataḥ।
teṣāṃ janapadāḥ sphītā vaṅgāṅgasuhlakāstathā ॥ 2.37.32 ॥
puṇḍrāḥ kaliṅgāśca tathā teṣāṃ vaṃśaṃ nibedhata।
tasya te tanayāḥ sarve kṣetrajā munisambhavāḥ।
sambhūtā dīrghatamasaḥ sudeṇṇāyāṃ mahaujasaḥ ॥ 2.37.33 ॥
kathaṃ baleḥ sutāḥ pañca janitāḥ kṣetrajāḥ prabho।
ṛṣiṇā dīrghatamasā etanno brūhi pṛcchatām ॥ 2.37.34 ॥
aśijo nāma vikhyāta āsīddhīmā nṛṣiḥ purā।
bhāryā vai samatā nāma babhūvāsya mahātmanaḥ ॥ 2.37.35 ॥
aśijasya kanīyāṃstu purodhā yo divaukasām।
bṛhaspatirbṛhattejā mamatāṃ so'bhyapadyata ॥ 2.37.36 ॥
uvāca mamatā tantu bṛhaspatimanicchatī।
antarvatnyasmi te bhrāturjyeṣṭhasyāṣṭamitā iti ॥ 2.37.37 ॥
ayaṃ hi me mahāgarbho rodate'ti bṛhaspate।
aśijaṃ brahmacābhyasya ṣaḍaṅgaṃ vedamudgiran ॥ 2.37.38 ॥
amogharetāstvañcāpi na māṃ bhajitamarhasi।
asminneva gate kāle yathā vā manyase prabho ॥ 2.37.39 ॥
evamuktastayā samyag bṛhattejā bṛhaspatiḥ।
kāmātmānaṃ mahātmā ca nātmānaṃ so'bhyadhārayat ॥ 2.37.40 ॥
sambabhūvaiva dharmātmā tayā sārddhaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ।
utsṛjantaṃ tadā reto garbhasthaḥ so'bhyabhāṣata ॥ 2.37.41 ॥
amogharetāstvañcāpi pūrvañcāhamihāgataḥ ॥ 2.37.42 ॥
śaśāpa taṃ tadā kruddha evamukto bṛhaspatiḥ।
āśijantaṃ sutaṃ bhrāturgarbhasthaṃ bhagavānṛṣiḥ ॥ 2.37.43 ॥
yasmāttvamīdṛśe kāle sarvabhūtepsite sati।
māmevamuktavān mohāttamo dīrghaṃ pravekṣyasi ॥ 2.37.44 ॥
tato dīrghatamā nāma śāpādṛṣirajāyata।
athāśijo bṛhatkīrttirbṛhaspatirivaujasā ॥ 2.37.45 ॥
ūrddhvaretāstataścāpi nyavasadbhrāturāśrame।
godharmaṃ saurabheyāttu vṛṣabhācchrutavān prabho ॥ 2.37.46 ॥
tasya bhrātā pitṛvyastu cakāra bhavanaṃ tadā।
tasmin hi tatra vasati yadṛcchābhyāgato vṛṣaḥ ॥ 2.37.47 ॥
darśārthamāhṛtān darbhāṃścacāra surabhīvṛtaḥ।
jagrāha taṃ dīrghatamā visphurantañca śrṛṅgayoḥ ॥ 2.37.48 ॥
sa tena nigṛhītastu na cacāla padātpadam।
tato'bravīdvṛṣastaṃ vai muñca māṃ balināṃ vara ॥ 2.37.49 ॥
na mayāsāditastāta balavaṃstvadvidhaḥ kvacit।
tryambakaṃ vahatā devaṃ yato jāto'smi bhūtale ॥ 2.37.50 ॥
muñca māṃ balināṃ śraṣṭha prītaste'haṃ varaṃ vṛṇu।
evamukto'bravīdenaṃ jīvastvaṃ me kva yāsyasi ॥ 2.37.51 ॥
tena tvāhaṃ na mokṣyāmi parasvāhaṃ catuṣpadam।
tatastaṃ dīrghatamasaṃ sa vṛṣaḥ pratyuvāca ha ॥ 2.37.52 ॥
nāsmākaṃ vidyate tāta pātakaṃ steyameva vā।
bhakṣyābhakṣyaṃ na jānīmaḥ peyāpeyañca sarvaśaḥ ॥ 2.37.53 ॥
kāryākāryaṃ na vai vijho gamyāgamyaṃ tathaiva ca।
na pāpmāno vayaṃ vipra dharmo hyeṣāṃ gavāṃ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.37.54 ॥
gavāṃ nāma sa vai śrutvā saṃbhrāntastvanumucya tam।
bhaktyā cānuśravikayā goṣu taṃ vai prasāda yat ॥ 2.37.55 ॥
manasaiva tadādatte tanniṣṭhastatparāyaṇaḥ ॥ 2.37.56 ॥
tato yavīyasaḥ patnīmautathyasyābhyamanyata।
viceṣṭamānāṃ rudatīṃ daivāt sa mūḍhacetanaḥ ॥ 2.37.57 ॥
avalepantu taṃ matvā śaradvāṃstasya nākṣamat।
godharmaṃvai balaṃ kṛtvā snuṣāṃ sa samamanyata ॥ 2.37.58 ॥
viparyayantu taṃ dṛṣṭvā śaradvān pratyacintayat।
bhaviṣyamarthaṃ jñātvā ca mahātmā ca na mṛtyutām ॥ 2.37.59 ॥
provāca dīrghatamasaṃ krodhāt saṃrakta locanaḥ।
gamyāgamyaṃ na jīnīṣe godharmāt prārthayat snuṣām ॥ 2.37.60 ॥
durvṛttastvaṃ tyajāmyeva gaccha tvaṃ svena karmaṇā।
yasmāttvamandho vṛddhaśca bharttavyo duranuṣṭitaḥ।
tenāsi tvaṃ parityakto durācāro'si me matiḥ ॥ 2.37.61 ॥
karmaṇyasmistataḥ krūre tasya buddhirajāyata।
nirbhatsya caiva bahuśo bāhubhyāṃ parigṛhya ca।
koṣṭe samudre prakṣipya gaṅgāmbhasi samutsṛjat ॥ 2.37.62 ॥
uhyamānaḥ samudrastu saptāhaṃ srotasā tadā।
taṃ sastrīko balirnāma rājā dharmārthatattvavit।
apaśyanmajjamānantu srotasābhyāśamāgatam ॥ 2.37.63 ॥
taṃ gṛhītvā sa dharmātmā balirvairocanastadā।
antaḥpure jugopainaṃ bhakṣyairbhojyaiśca tarpayan ॥ 2.37.64 ॥
prītaḥ sa vai vareṇātha cchandayāmāsa vai balim।
sa ca tasmādvaraṃ vavre putrārthaṃ dānavarṣabhaḥ ॥ 2.37.65 ॥
santānārthaṃ mahābhāga bhāryayā mama mānada।
putrān dharmārthasaṃyuktānutpādayitumarhasi ॥ 2.37.66 ॥
evamuktastu tenarṣistathāstvityuktavān hi tam ।
sudeṣṇāṃ nāma bāryāṃ vai rājāsmai prāhiṇottadā ॥ 2.37.67 ॥
andhaṃ vṛddhañca taṃ dṛṣṭvā na sā devī jagāma ha ।
svāñca dhātreyakīṃ tasmai bhūṣayitvā vyasarjayat ॥ 2.37.68 ॥
kakṣīvacakṣuṣau tasyāṃ śūdrayonyāmṛṣirvaśī।
janayāmāsa dharmātmā putrāvetau mahojasau ॥ 2.37.69 ॥
kakṣivacakṣuṣau tau tu dṛṣṭvā rājā balistadā।
prādhītau vidhivatsamyagīśvarau brahmavādinau ॥ 2.37.70 ॥
siddhau pratyakṣadharmāṇau buddhau śreṣṭhatamāvapi।
mamaitāviti hovāca balirvairocanastvṛṣim ॥ 2.37.71 ॥
netyuvāca tatastantu mamaitāviti cābravīt।
utpannau śūdrayonau tu bhavacchadmā surottamau ॥ 2.37.72 ॥
anadhaṃ bṛddhaṃ ca māṃ matvā sudeṣṇā mahiṣī tava।
prāhiṇodavamānāya śūdrāṃ dhātreyakīṃ mama ॥ 2.37.73 ॥
tataḥ prasādayāmāsa punastamṛṣisattamam।
balirbhāryāṃ sudeṣṇāṃ ca bhartsayāmāsa vai prabhuḥ ॥ 2.37.74 ॥
punaścaināmalaṃkṛtya ṛṣaye pratyapādayat।
tāṃ sa dīrghatamā devīmabravīdyadi māṃ śubhe ॥ 2.37.75 ॥
dadhnā lavaṇamiśreṇa svabya(vya)ktaṃ nagnakaṃ tathā।
lihiṣyasyajugupsantī hyāpādatalamastakam ॥ 2.37.76 ॥
tatastvaṃ prāpsyase devi putrāṃśca manasepsitān।
tasya sā tadvaco devī sarvaṃ kṛtavatī tathā ॥ 2.37.77 ॥
apānañca samāsādya jugupsantī nyavarjayat।
tāmuvāca tataḥ sarṣiryatte parihṛtaṃ śubhe।
vināpānaṃ kumāraṃ tvaṃ janayiṣyasi pūrvajam ॥ 2.37.78 ॥
tatastaṃ dīrghatamasaṃ sā devī pratyuvāca ha।
nārhasi tvaṃ mahābhāga putraṃ dātuṃ mamedṛśam ॥ 2.37.79 ॥
tavāparādho devyeṣa nānyathā bhavitānu vai ।
devī dānīñca te putramahaṃ dāsyāmi suvrate ॥ 2.37.80 ॥
tasyāpānaṃ vinā caiva yogyābhāvo bhaviṣyati।
tāṃ sa dīrghatamāścaiva kukṣau spṛṣṭvedamabravavīt ॥ 2.37.81 ॥
prāśitaṃ dadhi yatte'dya mamāṅgādvai śucismite ।
tena te pūrito garbhaḥ paurṇamāsyāmivodadhiḥ ॥ 2.37.82 ॥
bhaviṣyanti kumārāste pañca devasutopamāḥ।
tejasvinaḥ parākrāntā yajvāno dhārmikāstathā ॥ 2.37.83 ॥
tatoṅgastu sudeṣṇāyā jyeṣṭhaputro vyajāyata।
vaṅgastasmātkaliṅgastu puṇḍro brahmastathaiva ca ॥ 2.37.84 ॥
vaṃśabhājastu pañcaite baleḥ kṣetre'bhavaṃstadā।
ityete dīrghatamasā balerdattāḥ sutāḥ purā ॥ 2.37.85 ॥
prajāstvapahatāstasya brahmaṇā kāraṇaṃ prati।
apatyā mātyadāreṣu sveṣu mā bhūnmahātmanaḥ ॥ 2.37.86 ॥
tato manuṣyayonyāṃ vai janayāmāsa sa prajāḥ।
surabhirdīrghatamasamatha prīto vaco'bravīt ॥ 2.37.87 ॥
vicārya yasmādgodharmmaṃ tvamevaṃ kṛtavānasi ।
tasmāttava tamo dīrghaṃ nistudāmyadya paśya vai।
bārhaspatyañca yatte'nyatpāpaṃ santiṣṭhate tanau ॥ 2.37.89 ॥
jarāmṛtyubhayañcaiva āghrāya praṇudāmi te।
hyāghrātamātraḥ so'paśyata sadyastamasi nāśite ॥ 2.37.90 ॥
āyuṣmāṃśca yuvā caiva cakṣuṣmāṃśca tato'bhavat।
gavā dīrghatamāḥ so'tha gautamaḥ samapadyata ॥ 2.37.91 ॥
kakṣīvāṃstu tato gatvā saha pitrā giriprajām।
yathoddiṣṭaṃ hi pitrarthe cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ ॥ 2.37.92 ॥
tataḥ kālena mahatā tamasā bhāvitaḥ savai।
vidhūya manujo doṣān brahmaṇyaṃ prāptavān prabhuḥ ।। 37.94।
tato'bravīt pitā cainaṃ putravānasmyahaṃ prabho।
satputreṇa tvayā tāta kṛtārtho'smi yaśasvinā ॥ 2.37.93 ॥
yuktātmā hi tataḥ so'tha prāptavān brahmaṇā kṣayam।
brahmaṇyaṃ prāpya kakṣīvān sahasramasṛjat sutān ॥ 2.37.94 ॥
kṛṣṇāṅgā gautamāste vai smṛtāḥ kakṣīvataḥ sutāḥ।
ityeṣa dīrghatamaso balervairocanasya vai ॥ 2.37.95 ॥
samāgamaḥ samākhyātaḥ santānañcobhayostayoḥ।
balistānabiṣicyeha pañca putrānakalmaṣān ॥ 2.37.96 ॥
kṛtārthaḥ so'pi yogātmā yogamāśritya ca prabhuḥ।
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ kālākāṅkṣī caratyuta ॥ 2.37.97 ॥
tatrāṅgasya tu rājarṣe rājāsīddadhivāhanaḥ।
sāparādhasudeṣṇāyā anapāno'bhavanṛpaḥ ॥ 2.37.98 ॥
anapānasya putrastu rājā divirathaḥ smṛtaḥ।
putro divirathasyāsīdvidvān dharmaratho nṛpaḥ ॥ 2.37.99 ॥
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca pūrostu śrṛṇuta prajāḥ ॥ 2.37.113 ॥
raudrāśvasya ghṛtācyāṃ vai daśāpsarasi sūnavaḥ ॥ 2.37.117 ॥
rudrā śūdrā ca madrā ca śubhā jāmalajā tathā ॥ 2.37.119 ॥
talā khalā ca saptaitā yā ca gopajalā smṛtā।
tathā tāmrarasā caiva ratnakūṭī ca tādṛśī ॥ 2.37.120 ॥
yasmānmāmīdṛśe kāle sarvabhūtepsite sati।
tena te marutastasya marutsomena toṣitāḥ।
bṛhatkṣatrasya dāyādaḥ suhotro nāma dhārmikaḥ।
tapaso'nte sumahato rājño vṛddhasya dhārmikāḥ ॥ 2.37.161 ॥
vibhrājasya tu dāyādastvaṇuho nāma pārthivaḥ।
cyavanastasya putrastu rājā dharmārthakovidaḥ।
jahnustvajanayatputraṃ surathaṃ nāma bhūmipam।
imaṃ codāharantyatra ślokaṃ prati mahābhiṣam ॥ 2.37.231 ॥
subhadrāyāṃ rathī pārthādabhimanyurajāyata।
anāgatāni sarvāṇi bruvato me nibodhata।
kṣemakaṃ prāpya rājānaṃ saṃsthāṃ prāpsyati vai kalau।
ete aikṣvākavāḥ proktā bhavitāraḥ kalau yuge।
śūrāśca kṛtavidyāśca satyasandhā jitendriyāḥ ॥ 2.37.285 ॥
atrānuvaṃśaśloko'yaṃ bhaviṣyajñairudāhṛtaḥ।
ikṣvākūṇāmayaṃ vaṃśaḥ sumitrānto bhaviṣyati।
sumitraṃ prāpya rājānaṃ saṃsthāṃ prāpsyati vai kalau।
ityetanmānavaṃ kṣetramailañca samudāhṛtam ॥ 2.37.286 ॥
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi māgadheyānbṛhadrathān।
jarāsandhasya ye vaṃśe sahadevānvaye nṛpāḥ ॥ 2.37.287 ॥
atītā varttamānāśca bhaviṣyāśca tathā punaḥ।
prādhānyataḥ pravakṣyāmi gadato me nibodhata ॥ 2.37.288 ॥
saṃgrāme bhārate tasmin sahadevo nipātitaḥ।
somādhistasya tanayo rājarṣiḥ sagirivraje ॥ 2.37.289 ॥
pañcāśataṃ tathāṣṭau ca samā rājyamakārayat।
śrutaśravāḥ catuḥṣaṣṭisamāstasya suto'bhavat।
ayutāyustu ṣaḍviṃśaṃ rājyaṃ varṣāṇyakārayat।
samāḥ śataṃ nirāmitro mahīṃ bhuktvā divaṅgataḥ ॥ 2.37.290 ॥
pañcāśataṃ samāḥ ṣaṭ ca sukṛttaḥ prāptavānmahīm।
trayoviṃśaṃ bṛhatkarmā rājyaṃ varṣāṇyakārayat ॥ 2.37.291 ॥
senājitsāmprataṃ cāpi etāṃ vai bhujyate samāḥ।
śrutañjayastu varṣāṇi catvāriṃśadbhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.292 ॥
pañcatriṃśattu varṣāṇi mahīṃ pālayitā nṛpaḥ ॥ 2.37.293 ॥
aṣṭapañcā śataṃ cābdān rājye sthāsyati vai śuciḥ।
aṣṭāviṃśatsamāḥ pūrṇāḥ kṣemo rājā bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.294 ॥
bhuvatastu catuḥṣaṣṭīrājyaṃ prāpsyati vīryyavān।
pañcavarṣāṇi pūrṇāni dharmanetro bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.295 ॥
bhokṣyate nṛpatiścaiva hyaṣṭapañcāśataṃ samāḥ।
aṣṭātriṃśatsamā rājyaṃ suvratasya bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.296 ॥
catvāriṃśaddaśāṣṭau ca dṛḍhaseno bhaviṣyati।
trayastriṃśattu varṣāṇi sumatiḥ prāpsyate tataḥ ॥ 2.37.297 ॥
catvāriṃśatsamā rājā sunetro bhokṣyate tataḥ ॥ 2.37.298 ॥
satyajitpṛthivīrājyaṃ tryaśītiṃ bhokṣyate samāḥ।
prāpyemāṃ vīrajiccāpi pañcatriṃśadbhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.299 ॥
arīñjayastu varṣāṇi pañcāśatprāpsyate mahīm।
dvātriṃśacca nṛpā hyete bhavitāro bṛhadrathāḥ ॥ 2.37.300 ॥
pūrṇaṃ varṣasahasraṃ vai teṣāṃ rājyaṃ bhaviṣyati।
bṛhadratheṣvatīteṣu vītahotreṣu vartiṣu ॥ 2.37.301 ॥
munikaḥ svāminaṃ hatvā putraṃ samabhiṣekṣyati।
miṣatāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ hi pradyoto muniko balāt ॥ 2.37.302 ॥
sa vai praṇatasāmanto bhaviṣye nayavarjjitaḥ ।
trayoviṃśatsamā rājā bhavitā sa narottamaḥ ॥ 2.37.303 ॥
caturviṃśatsamā rājā pālako bhavitā tataḥ।
viśākhayūpo bhavitā nṛpaḥ pañcāśatīṃ samāḥ ॥ 2.37.304 ॥
ekatriṃśatsamā rājyamajakasya bhaviṣyati।
bhaviṣyati samā viṃśattatsuto varttivarddhanaḥ ॥ 2.37.305 ॥
aṣṭātriṃśacchataṃ bhāvyāḥ prādyotāḥ pañca te sutāḥ।
hatvā teṣāṃ yaśaḥ kṛtsnaṃ śiśunāko bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.306 ॥
vārāṇasyāṃ sutastasya saṃprāpsyati girivrajam।
śiśunākasya varṣāṇi catvāriṃśadbhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.307 ॥
śakavarṇaḥ sutastasya ṣaṭ‌triṃśacca bhaviṣyati।
tatastu viṃśatiṃ rājā kṣemavarmā bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.308 ॥
ajātaśatrūrbhavitā pañcaviṃśatsamā nṛpaḥ।
catvāriṃśatsamā rājyaṃ kṣatraujāḥ prāpsyate tataḥ ॥ 2.37.309 ॥
aṣṭāviṃśatsamā rājā vivisāro bhaviṣyati।
pañcaviṃśatsamā rājā darśakastu bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.310 ॥
udāyī bhavitā tasmāttrayastriṃśatsamā nṛpaḥ।
sa vai puravaraṃ rājā pṛthivyāṃ kusumāhvayam।
gaṅgāyā dakṣiṇe kūle caturthe'bde kariṣyati ॥ 2.37.311 ॥
dvācatvāriṃśatsamā bhāvyo rājā vai nandivarddhanaḥ।
catvāriṃśattrayañcaiva mahā nandī bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.312 ॥
aikṣvākavāścaturviṃśatpāñcālāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ।
kālakāstu caturvviṃśaccaturvviṃśattu haihayāḥ ॥ 2.37.315 ॥
dvātriṃśadvai kaliṅgāstu pañcaviṃśattathā śakāḥ।
kuravaścāpi ṣaḍviṃśadaṣṭāviṃśati maithilāḥ ॥ 2.37.316 ॥
śūrase nāstrayoviṃśadvītihotrāśca viṃśatiḥ।
tulyakālaṃ bhaviṣyanti sarva eva mahīkṣitaḥ ॥ 2.37.317 ॥
mahānandisutaścāpi śūdrāyāṃ kālasaṃvṛtaḥ।
utpatsyate mahāpadmaḥ sarvakṣatrāntare nṛpaḥ ॥ 2.37.318 ॥
tataḥprabhṛti rājāno bhaviṣyāḥ śūdrayonayaḥ।
ekarāṭ sa mahāpadma ekacchatro bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.319 ॥
aṣṭā viṃśativarṣāṇi pṛthivīṃ pālayiṣyati।
sarvakṣatrahṛtoddhṛtya bhāvino'rthasya vai balāt ॥ 2.37.320 ॥
sahasrāstatsutā hyaṣṭau samā dvādaśa te nṛpāḥ।।
mahāpadmasya paryāye bhaviṣyanti nṛpāḥ kramāt ॥ 2.37.321 ॥
uddhariṣyati tān sarvān kauṭilyo vai dviraṣṭabhiḥ।
bhuktvā mahīṃ varṣaśataṃ nandenduḥ sa bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.322 ॥
candraguptaṃ nṛpaṃ rājye kauṭilyaḥ sthāpayiṣyati।
caturviṃśatsamā rājā candragupto bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.323 ॥
bhavitā bhadra sārastu pañcaviṃśatsamā nṛpaḥ।
tasya putraḥ kunālastu varṣāṇyaṣṭau bhaviṣyati।
kunāla sūnuraṣṭau ca bhoktā vai bandhupālitaḥ ॥ 2.37.325 ॥
bandhupālitadāyādo daśamānīndrapālitaḥ।
bhavitā saptavarṣāṇi devavarmmā narādhipaḥ ॥ 2.37.326 ॥
rājā śatadharaścāṣṭau tasya putro bhaviṣyati।
bṛhadaśvaśca varṣāṇi sapta vai bhavitā nṛpaḥ ॥ 2.37.327 ॥
ityete nava bhūpā ye bhokṣyanti ca vasundharām।
saptatriṃśacchataṃ pūrṇaṃ tebhyastu gaurbhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.328 ॥
puṣpamitrastu senānīruddhṛtya vai bṛhadratham।
kārayiṣyati vai rājyaṃ samāḥ ṣaṣṭiṃ sadaiva tu ॥ 2.37.329 ॥
puṣpamitrasutāścāṣṭau bhaviṣyanti samā nṛpāḥ।
bhavitā cāpi tajjyeṣṭhaḥ saptavarṣāṇi vai tataḥ ॥ 2.37.330 ॥
vasumitraḥ suto bhāvyo daśavarṣāṇi pārthivaḥ।
tato dhrukaḥ samā dve tu bhaviṣyati sutaśca vai ॥ 2.37.331 ॥
bhaviṣyanti samāstasmāttisra eva pulindakāḥ।
rājā ghoṣasutaścāpi varṣāṇi bhavitā trayaḥ ॥ 2.37.332 ॥
tato vai vikramitrastu samā rājā tataḥ punaḥ।
dvātriṃśadbhavitā cāpi samā bhāgavato nṛpaḥ ॥ 2.37.333 ॥
bhaviṣyati sutastasya kṣemabhūmiḥ samā daśa।
daśaite tuṅgarājāno bhokṣyantīmāṃ vasundharam ॥ 2.37.334 ॥
śataṃ pūrṇaṃ daśa dve ca tebhyaḥ kiṃ vā gamiṣyati।
apārthivasudevantu bālyādvyasaninaṃ nṛpam ॥ 2.37.335 ॥
devabhūmistato'nyaśca śrṛṅgeṣu bhavitā nṛpaḥ।
bhaviṣyati samā rājā nava kaṇṭāyanastu saḥ ॥ 2.37.336 ॥
bhūtimitraḥ sutastasya caturvviṃśadbhaviṣyati।
bhavitā dvādaśa samāstasmānnārāyaṇo nṛpaḥ ॥ 2.37.337 ॥
suśarmmā tatsutaścāpi bhaviṣyati samā daśa।
kaṇṭāyanamathoddhṛtya suśarmmāṇaṃ prasahya tam।
sindhuko hyandhrajātīyaḥ prāpsyatīmāṃ vasundharām ॥ 2.37.340 ॥
trayoviṃśatsamā rājā sindhuko bhavitā tvatha।
śrīsātakarṇirbhavitā tasya putrastu vai mahān।
pañcāśataṃ samāḥ ṣaṭ ca sātakarṇirbhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.342 ॥
āpādabaddho daśa vai tasya putro bhaviṣyati।
caturvviṃśattu varṣāṇi ṣaṭ samā vai bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.343 ॥
tataḥ saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇaṃ hālo rājā bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.344 ॥
bhāvyaḥ putrikaṣeṇastu samāḥ so'pyekaviṃśatim ॥ 2.37.345 ॥
sātakarṇirvarṣamekaṃ bhaviṣyati narādhipaḥ।
aṣṭāviṃśattu varṣāṇi śivasvāmī bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.346 ॥
rājā ca gautamīputra ekaviṃśatsamā nṛṣu।
ekonaviṃśatiṃ rājā yajñaśrīḥ sātakarṇyatha ॥ 2.37.347 ॥
ṣaḍeva bhavitā tasmādvijayastu samā nṛpaḥ।
daṇḍaśrīḥ sātakarṇī ca tasya putraḥ samāstrayaḥ ॥ 2.37.348 ॥
ityete vai nṛpāstriṃśadandhrā bhokṣyanti ye mahīm ॥ 2.37.349 ॥
samāḥ śatāni catvāri pañca ṣaḍvai tathaiva ca।
andhrāṇāṃ saṃsthitāḥ pañca teṣāṃ vaṃśāḥ samāḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.37.350 ॥
saptaiva tu bhaviṣyanti daśābhīrāstato nṛpāḥ।
sapta gardabhinaścāpi tato'tha daśa vai śakāḥ ॥ 2.37.351 ॥
yavanāṣṭau bhaviṣyanti tuṣārāstu caturdaśa।
trayodaśa maruṇḍāśca maunā hyaṣṭādaśaiva tu ॥ 2.37.352 ॥
andhrā bhokṣyanti vasudhāṃ śate dve ca śataṃ ca vai।
śatāni trīṇyaśītiñca bhokṣyanti vasudhāṃ śakāḥ ॥ 2.37.353 ॥
aśītiñcaiva varṣāṇi bhoktāro yavanā mahīm।
pañcavarṣaśatānīha tuṣārāṇāṃ mahī smṛtā ॥ 2.37.354 ॥
śatānyarddhacaturthāni bhavitārastrayodaśa।
maruṇḍā vṛṣalaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhāvyānyā mlecchajātayaḥ ॥ 2.37.355 ॥
śatāni trīṇi bhokṣyanti mlecchā ekādaśaiva tu।
tataḥ kolikilebhyaśca vindhyaśaktirbhaviṣyati।
samāḥ ṣaṇṇavatiṃ trātvā pṛthivīṃ ca sameṣyati ॥ 2.37.357 ॥
śeṣasya nāgarājasya putraḥ svarapurañjayaḥ ॥ 2.37.358 ॥
bhogī bhaviṣyate rājā nṛpo nāgakulodvahaḥ।
sadācandrastu candrāṃśo dvitīyo nakhavāṃstathā ॥ 2.37.359 ॥
dhanadharmā tataścāpi caturtho viṃśajaḥ smṛtaḥ।
bhūtinandastataścāpi vaideśe tu bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.360 ॥
tasya bhrātā yavīyāṃstu nāmnā nandiyaśāḥ kila ॥ 2.37.361 ॥
tasyānvaye bhaviṣyanti rājānaste trayastu vai।
dohitraḥ śiśuko nāma purikāyāṃ nṛpo'bhavat ॥ 2.37.362 ॥
vindhyaśaktisutaścāpi pravīro nāma vīryavān ।
bhokṣyanti ca samāḥ ṣaṣṭiṃ purīṃ kāñcanakāñca vai ॥ 2.37.363 ॥
yakṣyanti vājapeyaiśca samāptavaradakṣiṇaiḥ।
tasya putrāstu catvāro bhaviṣyanti narādhipāḥ ॥ 2.37.364 ॥
vindhyakānāṃ kule'tīte nṛpā vai bāhlikā strayaḥ।
supratīko nabhīrastu samā bhokṣyati triṃśatim ॥ 2.37.365 ॥
śakyamā nāma vai rājā māhiṣīnāṃ mahīpatiḥ।
puṣpamitrā bhaviṣyanti paṭṭamitrāstrayodaśa ॥ 2.37.366 ॥
mekalāyāṃ nṛpāḥ sapta bhaviṣyanti ca sattamāḥ।
komalāyāntu rājāno bhaviṣyanti mahābalāḥ ॥ 2.37.367 ॥
meghā iti samākhyātā buddhimanto navaiva tu।
naiṣadhāḥ pārthivāḥ sarvve bhaviṣyantyāmanukṣayāt ॥ 2.37.368 ॥
nalavaṃśaprasūtāste vīryavanto mahābalāḥ।
māgadhānāṃ mahāvīryo viśvasphānirbhaviṣyati ॥ 2.37.369 ॥
utsādya pārthivān sarvvānso'nyān varṇān kariṣyati।
kaivarttān pañcakāṃścaiva pulindān brāhmaṇāṃstathā ॥ 2.37.370 ॥
sthāpayiṣyanti rājāno nānādeśeṣu tejasā।
viśvasphānirmahāsattvo yuddhe viṣṇusamo balī ॥ 2.37.371 ॥
viśvasphānirnarapatiḥ klībā kṛtirivocyate।
utsādayitvā kṣatrantu kṣatramanyat kariṣyati ॥ 2.37.372 ॥
navanākāstu bhokṣyanti purīṃ campāvatīṃ nṛpāḥ ॥ 2.37.374 ॥
mathurāñca purīṃ ramyāṃ nāgā bhokṣyanti sapta vai।
anugaṅgaṃ prayāgañca sāketaṃ magadhāṃstathā।
etāñjanapadān sarvvān bhokṣyante guptavaṃśajāḥ ॥ 2.37.375 ॥
niṣadhān yadukāṃścaiva śaiśī tān kālatopakān।
etāñjanapadān sarvvān bhokṣyanti maṇidhānyajāḥ ॥ 2.37.376 ॥
kośalāṃścāndhrapauṇḍrāṃśca tāmraliptān sasāgarān।
campāṃ caiva purīṃ ramyāṃ bhokṣyanti devarakṣitām ॥ 2.37.377 ॥
kāliṅgā mahiṣāścaiva mahendranilayāśca ye।
etāñjanapadān sarvvān pālayiṣyati vai guhaḥ ॥ 2.37.378 ॥
strīrāṣṭraṃ bhakṣyakāṃścaiva bhokṣyate kanakāhvayaḥ।
tulyakālaṃ bhaviṣyanti sarve hyete mahīkṣitaḥ ॥ 2.37.379 ॥
alpaprasādā hyanṛtā mahākrodhāḥ hyadhārmikāḥ।
bhaviṣyantīha yavanā dharmataḥ kāmato'rthataḥ ॥ 2.37.380 ॥
naiva mūrddhābhiṣiktāste bhaviṣyanti narādhipāḥ।
yugadoṣadurācārā bhaviṣyanti nṛpāstu te ॥ 2.37.381 ॥
strīṇāṃ balavadhenaiva hatvā caiva parasparam।
bhaviṣyantīha paryāye kālena pṛthivīkṣitaḥ ॥ 2.37.383 ॥
vihīnāstu bhaviṣyanti dharmmataḥ kāmato'rthataḥ।
tairvimiśrā janapadā mlecchācārāśca sarvaśaḥ ॥ 2.37.384 ॥
viparyyayena varttante nāśayiṣyanti vai prajāḥ।
lubdhānṛtaratāścaiva bhavitārastadā nṛpāḥ ॥ 2.37.385 ॥
teṣāṃ vyatīte paryāye bahustrīke yuge tadā।
lavāllavaṃ bhraśyamānā āyūrūpabalaśrutaiḥ ॥ 2.37.386 ॥
tathā gatāstu vai kāṣṭāṃ prajāsu jagatīśvarāḥ ।
rājānaḥ sampraṇaśyanti kālenopahatāstadā ॥ 2.37.387 ॥
adhārmikāśca te'tyarthaṃ pāṣaṇḍāścaiva sarvaśaḥ ॥ 2.37.388 ॥
pranaṣṭe nṛpaśabde ca sandhyāśliṣṭe kalau yuge।
kiṃñcicchiṣṭāḥ prajāstā vai dharmme naṣṭe'parigrahāḥ ॥ 2.37.389 ॥
anāvṛṣṭihatāścaiva parasparavadhena ca ॥ 2.37.390 ॥
anāthā hi paritrastā vārttāmutsṛjya duḥkhitāḥ।
tyaktvā purāṇi grāmāṃśca bhaviṣyanti vanaukasaḥ ॥ 2.37.391 ॥
evaṃ nṛpeṣu naṣṭeṣu prajāstyaktvā gṛhāṇi tu।
naṣṭe snehe durāpannā bhraṣṭasnehāḥ suhṛjjanāḥ ॥ 2.37.392 ॥
varṇāśramaparibhraṣṭāḥ saṅkaraṃ ghoramāsthitāḥ।
saritparvatasevinyo bhaviṣyanti prajāstadā ॥ 2.37.393 ॥
saritaḥ sāgarānūpān sevante parvatāni ca।
aṅgān kaliṅgān vaṅgāṃśca kāśmīrān kāśikośalān ॥ 2.37.394 ॥
ṛṣikāntagiridroṇīḥ saṃśrayiṣyanti mānavāḥ।
kṛtsnaṃ himavataḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ kūlaṃ ca lavaṇāmbhasaḥ ॥ 2.37.395 ॥
araṇyānyabhipatsyanti hyāryyā mlecchajanaiḥ saha।
mṛgairmīnairvihaṅgaiśca śvāpadaistakṣubhistathā।
madhuśākaphalairmūlairvarttayiṣyanti mānavāḥ ॥ 2.37.396 ॥
cīraṃ parṇañca vividhaṃ valkalānyajināni ca।
svayaṃ kṛtvā vivatsyanti yathā munijanāstathā ॥ 2.37.397 ॥
bījānnāni tathā nimnesvīhantaḥ kāṣṭhaśaṅkubhiḥ।
ajaiḍakaṃ kharoṣṭrañca pālayiṣyanti yatnataḥ ॥ 2.37.398 ॥
nadīrvatsyanti toyārthe kūlamāśritya mānavāḥ।
pārthivān vyavahāreṇa vibādhantaḥ parasparam ॥ 2.37.399 ॥
bahumanyāḥ prajāhīnāḥ śaucācāravivarjitāḥ।
evaṃ bhaviṣyanti narāstadādharmme vyavasthitāḥ ॥ 2.37.400 ॥
hīnāddhīnāṃstathā dharmmān prajāḥ samanuvarttate।
āyustadā trayoviṃśaṃ na kaścidativarttate ॥ 2.37.401 ॥
durbalā viṣayaglānā jarayā saṃpariplutāḥ।
patramūlaphalāhārāścīrakṛṣṇājināmbarāḥ ॥ 2.37.402 ॥
vṛttyarthamabhilipsantaścariṣyanti vasundharām।
etatkālamanuprāptāḥ prajāḥ kaliyugāntake ॥ 2.37.403 ॥
kṣīṇe kaliyuge tasmin divye varṣasahasrake।
niḥśeṣāstu bhaviṣyanti sārddhaṃ kaliyugena tu।
sasandhyāṃśe tu niḥśeṣe kṛtaṃ vai pratipatsyate ॥ 2.37.404 ॥
yadā candraśca sūryyaśca tathā tiṣyabṛhaspatī।
ekarātre bhariṣyanti tadā kṛtayugaṃ bhavet ॥ 2.37.405 ॥
eṣa vaṃśakramaḥ kṛtsnaṃ kīrtito vo yathākramam।
atītā varttamānāśca tathaivānāgatāśca ye ॥ 2.37.406 ॥
mahādevābhiṣekāttu janma yāvatparikṣitaḥ।
etadvarṣasahasrantu jñeyaṃ pañcādaśaduttaram ॥ 2.37.407 ॥
pramāṇaṃ vai tathā coktaṃ mahāpadmāntaraṃ ca yat।
antaraṃ tacchatānyaṣṭau ṣaṭ‌triṃśacca samāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.37.408 ॥
etatkālāntaraṃ bhāvyā andhrāntā ye prakīrttitāḥ।
bhaviṣyaistatra saṅkhyātāḥ purāṇajñaiḥ śrutarṣibhiḥ ॥ 2.37.409 ॥
saptarṣayastadā prāhuḥ pratīpe rājñi vai śatam।
saptaviṃśaiḥ śatairbhāvyā andhrāṇāṃ te tvayā punaḥ ॥ 2.37.410 ॥
saptaviṃśatiparyyante kṛtsne nakṣatramaṇḍale।
saptarṣayastu tiṣṭhanti paryāyeṇa śataṃ śatam।
saptarṣīṇāṃ yugaṃ hyetaddivyayā saṅkhyayā smṛtam ॥ 2.37.411 ॥
tebhyaḥ pravarttate kālo divyaḥ saptarṣibhistu taiḥ ॥ 2.37.412 ॥
saptarṣīṇāntu ye pūrvā dṛśyante uttarādiśi।
tato madhyena ca kṣetraṃ dṛśyate yatsamaṃ divi ॥ 2.37.413 ॥
tena saptarṣayo yuktā jñeyā vyomni śataṃ samāḥ।
nakṣatrāṇāmṛṣīṇāñca yogasyaitannidarśanam ॥ 2.37.414 ॥
saptarṣayo maghāyuktāḥ kāle pārikṣite śatam।
andhrāṃśe sa caturvviśe bhaviṣyanti mate mama ॥ 2.37.415 ॥
imāstadā tu prakṛtirvyāpatsyanti prajā bhṛśam।
anṛtopahatāḥ sarvā dharmataḥ kāmato'rthataḥ ॥ 2.37.416 ॥
śrautasmārtte praśithile dharme varṇāśrame tadā।
śaṅkaraṃ durbalātmānaḥ pratipatsyanti mohitāḥ ॥ 2.37.417 ॥
saṃsaktāśca bhaviṣyanti śūdrāḥ sārddhaṃ dvijātibhiḥ।
brāhmaṇāḥ śūdrayaṣṭāraḥ śūdrā vai mantrayonayaḥ ॥ 2.37.418 ॥
upasthāsyanti tān viprāstadā vai vṛttilipsavaḥ ।
lavaṃ lavaṃ bhrasyamānāḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ krameṇa tu ॥ 2.37.419 ॥
kṣayameva gamiṣyanti kṣīṇaśeṣā yugakṣaye।
yasmin kṛṣṇo divaṃ yātastasminneva tadā dine ॥ 2.37.420 ॥
pratipannaḥ kaliyugastasya saṅkhyāṃ nibodhata।
sahasrāṇāṃ śatānīha trīṇi mānuṣasaṅkhyayā।
ṣaṣṭiṃ caiva sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāmucyate kaliḥ ॥ 2.37.421 ॥
divye varṣasahasrantu tatsandhyāṃśaṃ prakīrttitam।
niḥśeṣe ca tadā tasmin kṛtaṃ vai pratipatsyate ॥ 2.37.422 ॥
aila ikṣvākuvaṃśaśca saha bhedaiḥ prakīrttitau।
ikṣvākostu smṛtaḥ kṣatraḥ sumitrāntaṃ vivasvataḥ ॥ 2.37.423 ॥
ailaṃ kṣatraṃ kṣemakāntaṃ somavaṃśavido viduḥ।
ete vivasvataḥ putrāḥ kīrttitāḥ kīrttivarddhanāḥ ॥ 2.37.424 ॥
atītā varttamānāśca tathaivānāgatāśca ye।
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāścaivānvaye smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.37.425 ॥
yuge yuge mahātmānaḥ samatītāḥ sahasraśaḥ।
bahutvānnāmadheyānāṃ parisaṃkhyā kule kule ॥ 2.37.426 ॥
punaruktā bahutvācca na mayā parikīrttitā।
vaivasvate'ntare hyasmin nimivaṃśaḥ samāpyate ॥ 2.37.427 ॥
evāyāntu yugākhyāyāṃ yataḥ kṣatraṃ prapatsyate ।
tathā hi kathayiṣyāmi gadato me nibodhata ॥ 2.37.428 ॥
devāpiḥ pauravo rājā ikṣvākoścaiva yo mataḥ।
mahāyogabalopetaḥ kalāpagrāmamāsthitaḥ ॥ 2.37.429 ॥
suvarccāḥ somaputrastu ikṣvākostu bhaviṣyati।
etau kṣatrapraṇetārau caturviṃśe caturyuge ॥ 2.37.430 ॥
na ca viṃśe yuge somavaṃśasyādirbhaviṣyati।
devāpirasapatnastu ailādirbhavitā nṛpaḥ ॥ 2.37.431 ॥
kṣatraprāparttakau hyetau bhaviṣyete caturyuge।
evaṃ sarvatra vijñeyaṃ santānārthe tu lakṣaṇam ॥ 2.37.432 ॥
kṣīṇe kaliyuge tasmin bhaviṣye tu kṛte yuge।
saptarṣibhistu taiḥ sārddhamādye tretāyuge punaḥ ॥ 2.37.433 ॥
gotrāṇāṃ kṣatriyāṇāñca bhaviṣyete pravarttakau।
dvāparāṃśe na tiṣṭhanti kṣatriyā ṛṣibhiḥ saha ॥ 2.37.434 ॥
bījārthante bhaviṣyanti brahmakṣatrasya vai punaḥ ॥ 2.37.435 ॥
evameva tu sarveṣu tiṣṭhantīhāntareṣu vai ।
saptarṣayo nṛpaiḥ sārddhaṃ santānārthaṃ yuge yuge ॥ 2.37.436 ॥
kṣatrasyaiva samucchedaḥ sambandho vai dvijaiḥ smṛtaḥ।
manvantarāṇāṃ saptānāṃ santānāśca śrutāśca te ॥ 2.37.437 ॥
paramparā yugānāñca brahmakṣatrasya codbhavaḥ।
yathā pravṛttisteṣāṃ vai pravṛttānāṃ tathā kṣayaḥ ॥ 2.37.438 ॥
saptarṣayo vidusteṣāṃ dīrghāyuṣṭvākṣayantu te।
etena kramayogena ailekṣvākvanvayā dvijāḥ ॥ 2.37.439 ॥
utpadyamānāstretāyāṃ kṣīyamāṇe kalau punaḥ।
anuyānti yugākhyāṃ tu yāvanmanvantarakṣayaḥ ॥ 2.37.440 ॥
jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa kṣatre niravaśeṣite।
kṛte vaṃśakulāḥ sarvāḥ kṣatriyairvasudhādhipaiḥ।
dvivaṃśakaraṇāścaiva kīrttayiṣye nibodhata ॥ 2.37.441 ॥
ailasyekṣvākunandasya prakṛtiḥ parivarttate।
rājānaḥ śreṇibaddhāstu tathānye kṣatriyā nṛpāḥ ॥ 2.37.442 ॥
ailavaṃśasya ye khyātāstathaivaikṣvākavā nṛpāḥ ।
teṣāmekaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ kulānāmabhiṣekinām ॥ 2.37.443 ॥
tāvadeva tu bhojānāṃ vistāro dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
bhajate triṃśakaṃ kṣatraṃ caturdhā tadyathādiśam ॥ 2.37.444 ॥
teṣvatītāḥ samānā ye bruvatastānnibodhata।
śataṃ vai prativindhyānāṃ śataṃ nāgāḥ śataṃ hayāḥ ॥ 2.37.445 ॥
dhṛtarāṣṭrāścaikaśatamaśītirjanamejayāḥ।
śatañca brahmadattānāṃ śīriṇāṃ vīriṇāṃ śatam ॥ 2.37.446 ॥
tataḥ śataṃ puromānāṃ śvetakāśakuśādayaḥ ।
tato'pare sahasraṃ vai ye'tītāḥ śatabindavaḥ ॥ 2.37.447 ॥
ījire cāśvamedhaiste sarve niyutadakṣiṇaiḥ ।
evaṃ rājarṣayo'tītāḥ śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ ॥ 2.37.448 ॥
manorvaivasvatasyāsmin varttamāne'ntare tu ye ।
teṣāṃ nibodhatotpannā loke santatayaḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.37.449 ॥
tatpūrvāparayogena vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi ॥ 2.37.450 ॥
aṣṭāviṃśadyugākhyāstu gatā vaivasvate'ntare।
etā rājarṣibhiḥ sārddhaṃ śiṣṭā yāstā nibodhata ॥ 2.37.451 ॥
catvāriṃśacca ye caiva bhaviṣyāḥ saha rājabhiḥ।
yugākhyānāṃ viśiṣṭāstu tato vaivasvatakṣaye ॥ 2.37.452 ॥
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvvaṃ samāsavyāsayogataḥ।
punaruktaṃ bahutvācca na śakyantu yugaiḥ saha ॥ 2.37.453 ॥
ete yayātiputrāṇāṃ pañcaviṃśā viśāṃ hitāḥ।
kīrttitāścāmitā ye me lokān vai dhārayantyuta ॥ 2.37.454 ॥
labhate ca vareṇyañca durlabhāniha laukikān।
āyuḥ kīrttiṃ dhanaṃ putrān svargaṃ cānantyamaśnute ॥ 2.37.455 ॥
ityeṣa vo mayo pādastṛtīyaḥ kathito dvijāḥ।
vistareṇānupūrvvī ca kimbhūyo varttayāmyaham ॥ 2.37.456 ॥
śrutvā pādaṃ tṛtīyantu krāntaṃ sūtena dhīmatā।
tataścaturthaṃ papracchuḥ pādaṃ vai ṛṣisattamāḥ ॥ 2.38.1 ॥
pādaḥ krāntastṛtīyo'yamanuṣaṅgeṇa yastvayā।
caturthaṃ vistarātpādaṃ saṃhāraṃ parikīrttaya ॥ 2.38.2 ॥
manvantarāṇi sarvāṇi pūrvāṇyevāparaiḥ saha।
saptarṣīṇāmathaiteṣāṃ sāmpratasyāntare manoḥ ॥ 2.38.3 ॥
vistarāvayavañcaiva nisargasya mahātmanaḥ।
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca sarvameva bravīhi me ॥ 2.38.4 ॥
bhavatāṃ kathayiṣyāmi sarvametadyathātatham।
pādaṃ tvimaṃ sasaṃhāraṃ caturthaṃ munisattamāḥ ॥ 2.38.5 ॥
manorvaivasvatasyemaṃ sāṃpratasya mahātmanaḥ।
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca nisargaṃ śrṛṇuta dvijāḥ ॥ 2.38.6 ॥
manvantarāṇāṃ saṃkṣepaṃ bhaviṣyaiḥ saha saptabhiḥ।
pralayañcaiva lokānāṃ bruvato me nibodhata ॥ 2.38.7 ॥
etānyuktāni vai samyak saptasaptasu vai mayā।
manvantarāṇi saṃkṣepācchṛṇutānāgatāni me ॥ 2.38.8 ॥
sāvarṇasya pravakṣyāmi manorvaivasvatasya ha।
bhaviṣyasya bhaviṣyanti samāsāttu nibodhata ॥ 2.38.9 ॥
anāgatāśca saptaiva smṛtāstviha maharṣayaḥ।
kauśiko gātavaścaiva jāmadagnyaśca bhārgavaḥ ॥ 2.38.10 ॥
dvaipāyano vasiṣṭhaśca kṛpaḥ śāradvatastathā।
ātreyo dīptimāṃścaiva ṛṣyaśrṛṅgastu kāśyapaḥ ॥ 2.38.11 ॥
bhāradvājastathā drauṇiraśvatthāmā mahāyaśāḥ।
ete sapta mahātmāno bhaviṣyāḥ paramarṣayaḥ ॥ 2.38.12 ॥
sutapā ścāmitābhāśca sukhāścaiva gaṇāstrayaḥ।
teṣāṃ gaṇāstu devānāṃ ekaiko viṃśakaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.38.13 ॥
nāmatastu pravakṣyāmi nibodhadhvaṃ samāhitāḥ।
ritastapaśca śukraśca dyutirjyotiḥ prabhākarau ॥ 2.38.14 ॥
prabhāso bhāsakṛddharmmastejoraśmiṛturvirāṭ।
arciṣmān dyotano bhānuryaśakīrttirbudho dhṛtiḥ।
viṃśatiḥ sutapā hyete nāmabhiḥ parikīrtitāḥ ॥ 2.38.15 ॥
prabhurvibhurvibhāsaśca jetā hantā'rihā rituḥ।
sumatiḥ pramatirdīptiḥ samākhyāto mahomahān ॥ 2.38.16 ॥
deho munirnayo jyeṣṭhaḥ samaḥ satyaśca viśrutaḥ।
ityete hyamitābhāstu viṃśatiḥ parikīrttitāḥ ॥ 2.38.17 ॥
damo dātā vidaḥ somo vittavaidyau yamo nidhiḥ।
homaṃ havyaṃ hutaṃ dānaṃ deyaṃ dātā tapaḥ śamaḥ ॥ 2.38.18 ॥
dhruvaṃ sthānaṃ vidhānañca niyamaśceti viṃśatiḥ।
mukhyā hyete samākhyātāḥ sāvarṇe prathame'ntare ॥ 2.38.19 ॥
mārīcasyaiva te putrāḥ kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ।
sāvarṇasya manoḥ putrā bhaviṣyanti navaiva tu ॥ 2.38.22 ॥
nava cānyeṣu vakṣyāmi sāvarṇeścāntareṣu vai।
sāvarṇamanavaścānye bhaviṣyā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ ॥ 2.38.23 ॥
dakṣasya te hi dauhitrāḥ priyāyā duhituḥ sutāḥ ॥ 2.38.24 ॥
mahatā tapasā yuktā merupṛṣṭe mahaujasaḥ।
brahmādibhiste janitā dakṣeṇaiva ca dhīmatā ॥ 2.38.25 ॥
maharlokagatāvṛtya bhaviṣyā merumāśritāḥ।
mahābhāvāttu te pūrvaṃ jajñire cākṣuṣe'ntare ॥ 2.38.26 ॥
jajñire manavaste hi bhaviṣyānāgatāntare ॥ 2.38.29 ॥
prācetasasya dakṣasya dauhitrā manavastu ye।
sāvarṇā nāmataḥ pañca catvāraḥ paramarṣijāḥ ॥ 2.38.30 ॥
saṃjñāputrastu sāvarṇa eko vaivasvatastathā।
jyeṣṭhaḥ saṃjñāsuto nāma manurvaivasvataḥ prabhuḥ ॥ 2.38.31 ॥
vaivasvate'ntare prāpte samutpattistayoḥ śubhā।
caturddaśaite manavaḥ kīrttitāḥ kīrttivarddhanāḥ ॥ 2.38.32 ॥
vede śrutau purāṇe ca sarve te prabhaviṣṇavaḥ।
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve bhūtānāṃ patayaḥ sthitāḥ ॥ 2.38.33 ॥
tairiyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā saparvatā।
pūrṇaṃ yugasahasraṃ vai paripālyā nareśvaraiḥ ॥ 2.38.34 ॥
prajābhistapasā caiva vistaraṃ teṣu vakṣyate।
caturddaśaiva te jñeyāḥ sargāḥ svāyambhuvādayaḥ ॥ 2.38.35 ॥
manvantarādhikāreṣu vartante ca sakṛt sakṛt।
vinivṛttādhikārāste maharlokaṃ samāśritāḥ ॥ 2.38.36 ॥
samatītāstu ye teṣāmaṣṭau ṣaṣṭāstathāpare।
pūrveṣu sāmprataścāyaṃ śāntirvaivasvataḥ prabhuḥ ॥ 2.38.37 ॥
ye śiṣṭāstān pravakṣyāmi saha devarṣidānavaiḥ।
saha prajānisargeṇa sarvvāṃstvanāgatān dvijān ॥ 2.38.38 ॥
vaivasvatanisargeṇa teṣāṃ jñeyastu vistaraḥ।
anyūnā nātiriktāste yasmāt sarvve vivasvataḥ ॥ 2.38.39 ॥
punaruktā bahutvāttu vakṣye na teṣu vistaram।
manvantareṣu bhāvyeṣu bhūteṣvapi tathaiva ca ॥ 2.38.40 ॥
kule kule nisargāṃstu tasmādbhūyo vibhāgaśaḥ ।
teṣāmeva hi śiṣṭārthaṃ vistareṇa krameṇa ca ॥ 2.38.41 ॥
dakṣasya kanyā dharmiṣṭā suvratā nāma viśrutā।
gṛhītvā tāṃ pitā kanyāṃ jagāma brahmaṇo'ntike ॥ 2.38.42 ॥
vairājastamupāsīnaṃ dharmeṇa ca bhavena ca।
bhavadharmasamīpasthaṃ dakṣaṃ brahmābyabhāṣata ॥ 2.38.43 ॥
dakṣa kanyā taveyaṃ vai janayiṣyati suvratā।
caturo vai manūn putrāṃścāturvarṇyakarāñchubhān ॥ 2.38.44 ॥
brahmaṇo vacanaṃ śrutvā dakṣo dharmo bhavastadā।
tāṃ kanyāṃ manasā jagmustrayaste brahmaṇā saha ॥ 2.38.45 ॥
satyābhidhyāyināṃ teṣāṃ sadyaḥ kanyā vyajāyata।
sadṛśānurūpāṃsteṣāṃ caturo vai kumārakān ॥ 2.38.46 ॥
saṃsiddhāḥ kāryakaraṇe sambhūtāste śriyānvitaḥ।
upabhogasamarthaiśca sadyojātaiḥ śarīrakaiḥ ॥ 2.38.47 ॥
te dṛṣṭvā tān svayambuddhvā brahmā vyāhāhiṇastadā।
saṃrabdhā vai vyakarṣanta mama putro mametyuta ॥ 2.38.48 ॥
abhidhyānānmanotpannānūcurvai te parasparam।
yo yasya vapuṣā tulyo bhajatāṃ sa tu taṃ sutam ॥ 2.38.49 ॥
yasya yaḥ sadṛśaścāpi rūpe vīrya ca nāmataḥ।
taṃ gṛhṇātu subhadraṃ vo varṇato yasya yaḥ samaḥ ॥ 2.38.50 ॥
dhruvaṃ rūpaṃ pituḥ putraḥ so'nurudhyati sarvadā।
tasmādātmasamaḥ putraḥ piturmātuśca jāyate ॥ 2.38.51 ॥
evaṃ te samayaṃ kṛtvā savarṇān jagṛhuḥ sutān।
cākṣuṣasyāntare'tīte prāpte vaivasvatasya ha।
ruceḥ prajāpateḥ putro raucyo nāmābhavatsutaḥ ॥ 2.38.54 ॥
bhūtyāmutpādito yastu bhautyo nāmābhavatsutaḥ।
vaivasvate'ntare rājā dvau manū tu vivasvatoḥ ॥ 2.38.55 ॥
vaivasvato manuryaśca sāvarṇo yaśca viśrutaḥ।
jyeṣṭhaḥ saṃjñāsuto vidvān manurvaivasvataḥ prabhuḥ ॥ 2.38.56 ॥
savarṇāyāḥ sutaścānyaḥ smṛto vaivasvato manuḥ ।
savarṇā manavo ye ca catvārastu maharṣijāḥ ॥ 2.38.57 ॥
tapasā sambhṛtātmānaḥ sveṣu manvantareṣu vai।
bhaviṣyeṣu bhaviṣyanti sarvakāryārthasādhakāḥ ॥ 2.38.58 ॥
prathamaṃ merusāvarṇerdakṣaputrasya vai manoḥ।
putrā marīcigarbhāśca suśarmāṇaśca te trayaḥ ।
sambhūtāśca mahātmānaḥ sarve vaivasvate'ntare ॥ 2.38.59 ॥
dakṣaputrasya putrāste rohitasya prajāpateḥ।
bhaviṣyasya bhaviṣyastu ekaiko dvādaśo gaṇaḥ ॥ 2.38.60 ॥
aiśvaryasaṃgrāho rāho bāhuvaśastathaiva ca।
pārā dvādaśa vijñeyā uttarāṃstu nibodhata ॥ 2.38.61 ॥
vājiyo vājijiccaiva prabhṛtiśca kakudyatha।
dadhikrāvāyapakvāśca praṇīto vijayo madhuḥ ॥ 2.38.62 ॥
tejasmānnathavo dvau tu dvādaśaite marīcayaḥ।
suśarmmāṇastu vakṣyāmi nāmatastu nibodhata ॥ 2.38.63 ॥
varṇastathāpyaṅgaviśvau muraṇyo vrajano mataḥ।
amito dravaketuśca jambhosthājasraśakrakāḥ ॥ 2.38.64 ॥
sunemirdyutapāścaiva suśarmmāṇaḥ prakīrttitāḥ।
teṣāmindrastadā bhāvyo hyadbhuto nāma nāmataḥ ॥ 2.38.65 ॥
skandaḥ somapratīkāśaḥ kārtikeyastu pāvakaḥ।
māghātithiśca paulastyo vasuḥ kāśyapa eva ca ॥ 2.38.66 ॥
jyotiṣmān bhārgavaścaiva dyutimānaṅgirāstathā।
vasitaścaiva vāsiṣṭha ātreyo havyavāhanaḥ ॥ 2.38.67 ॥
sutapāḥ paulavaścaiva saptaite rohitāntare।
dhṛtiketudīptiketuśāpahastā nirāmayaḥ ॥ 2.38.68 ॥
pṛthuśravāstathā nāko bhūridyumno bṛhadrathaḥ।
prathamasya tu sāvarṇernava putrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ॥ 2.38.69 ॥
daśame tvatha paryāye dharmaputrasya vai manoḥ।
dvitīyasya tu sāvarṇerbhāvyasyaivāntare manoḥ ॥ 2.38.70 ॥
sukhāmanā viruddhāśca dvāveva tu gaṇau smṛtau।
tviṣivantaśca te sarve śatasaṅkhyāśca te samāḥ ॥ 2.38.71 ॥
prāṇā nāyacchataḥ prokta ṛṣibhiḥ puruṣeṣu vai।
devāste vai bhaviṣyanti dharmaputrasya vai manoḥ ॥ 2.38.72 ॥
teṣāmindrastathā vidvān bhaviṣyaḥ śāntirucyate।
haviṣmān paulahaḥ śrīmān sukīrtiścāpi bhārgavaḥ ॥ 2.38.73 ॥
āpomūrtistathātreyo vasiṣṭhaścāpi yaḥ smṛtaḥ।
paulastyaḥ pratipaścāpi nābhāgaścaiva kāśyapaḥ।
abhimanyuścāṅgirasaḥ saptaite paramarṣayaḥ ॥ 2.38.74 ॥
sukṣetraścottamaujāśca bhūriṣeṇaśca vīryavān।
śatānīko nirāmitro vṛṣaseno jayadrathaḥ ॥ 2.38.75 ॥
bhūridyumnaḥ suvarccāśca daśaite mānavāḥ smṛtāḥ।
ekādaśe tu paryyāye sāvarṇe vai tṛtīyake ॥ 2.38.76 ॥
nirmmāṇaratayo devāḥ kāmajā vai manojavāḥ।
gaṇāstvete trayaḥ khyātā devatānāṃ mahātmanām ॥ 2.38.77 ॥
ekaikaṃ triṃśatasteṣāṃ gaṇāstu tridivaukasām।
māsasyāhāni triṃśattu yāni vai kavayo viduḥ ॥ 2.38.78 ॥
nirmmāṇaratayo devā rātrayastu vihaṅgamāḥ।
gaṇāste vai trayaḥ proktā devatānāṃ bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.38.79 ॥
manojavā muhūrttāstu iti devāḥ prakīrttitāḥ ।
ete hi brahmaṇaḥ putrā bhaviṣyā manavaḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.38.80 ॥
teṣāmindro vṛṣo nāma bhaviṣyaḥ surarāṭ tataḥ।
teṣāṃ saptarṣayaścāpi kīrttyamānānnibodhata ॥ 2.38.81 ॥
haviṣmān kāśyapaścāpi vapuṣmān yaśca bhārgavaḥ।
vāruṇiścaiva cātreyo vāsiṣṭo bhaga eva ca ॥ 2.38.82 ॥
puṣṭiścāṅgiraso jñeyaḥ paulastyo niścarastathā।
paulaho hyagnitejāśca devā hyekādaśe'ntare ॥ 2.38.83 ॥
sarvvavegaḥ sudharmmā ca devānīkaḥ purovahaḥ।
kṣemadharmā gṛheṣuśca hyādarśaḥ pauṇḍrako manaḥ ॥ 2.38.84 ॥
sāvarṇasya tu te putrāḥ prājāpatyasya vai manoḥ।
dvādaśe tvatha paryāye rudraputrasya vai manoḥ ॥ 2.38.85 ॥
caturthe ṛtusāvarṇe devāstasyāntare śrṛṇu।
pañcaiva tu gaṇāḥ proktā devatānāmanāgatāḥ ॥ 2.38.86 ॥
haritā rohitāścaiva devāḥ sumanasastathā।
parvatānucaraścaiva hyapoṃ'śuśca manojavaḥ।
urjjā svāhā svadhā tārā daśaite rohitāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.38.89 ॥
tapojānirbhṛtiścaiva vācā bandhuśca yaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
rajaścaiva tu rājaśca svarṇapādastathaiva ca ॥ 2.38.90 ॥
vyuṣṭirvidhiśca vai devo daśaite rohitāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
uṣitādyāstu ye devāstrayastriśatprakīrtitāḥ ॥ 2.38.91 ॥
suparvā vṛṣabhaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kṛpidyumnau vipaścitaḥ ॥ 2.38.92 ॥
vikramaśca kramaścaiva nibhṛtaḥ kānta eva ca।।
varyyoditastathā jiṣṭo varcasvī dyutimān haviḥ।
śubho havikṛtātprāptirvyāpṛtho daśamastathā ॥ 2.38.94 ॥
supārā mānasāstvete devā vai samprakīrttitāḥ।
teṣāmindrastu vijñeya ṛtadhāmā mahāyaśāḥ ॥ 2.38.95 ॥
kṛtirvasiṣṭhaputrastu hyātreyaḥ sutapāstathā।
tapomūrtiścāṅgirasastapasvī kāśyapastathā ॥ 2.38.96 ॥
tapo'śayānaḥ paulastyaḥ pulahaśca taporatiḥ।
bhārgavaḥ saptamastveṣāṃ vijñeyastu tapomatiḥ ॥ 2.38.97 ॥
ete saptarṣayaḥ siddhā anye sāvarṇike'ntare।
devavānupadevaśca devaśreṣṭo vidūrathaḥ ॥ 2.38.98 ॥
mitravān mitrabinduśca mitraseno hyamitrahā।
mitrabāhuḥ suvarcāśca dvādaśaite manoḥ sutāḥ ॥ 2.38.99 ॥
trayo daśe tu paryāye bhāvyā raucyāntare punaḥ।
traya eva gaṇāḥ proktā devānāntu svayambhuvā ॥ 2.38.100 ॥
brahmaṇo mānasāḥ putrāste hi sarve mahātmanaḥ।
sutrāmāṇaḥ sudharmmāṇaḥ sukarmmāṇaśca te trayaḥ ॥ 2.38.101 ॥
tridaśānāṃ gaṇāḥ proktā bhaviṣyāḥ somapāyinaḥ।
trayastriṃśaddevatā yāḥ prābhaviṣyanta yājñikaiḥ ॥ 2.38.102 ॥
ājyena pṛṣadājyena grahaśreṣṭena caiva hi।
devairdevāstrayastriṃśatpṛthaktvena nibodhata ॥ 2.38.103 ॥
sutrāmāṇaḥ prayājyāstu hyādyājyāstu sāmpratam।
sukarmaṇo'nuyājyāstu pṛṣadājyāśinastu ye ॥ 2.38.104 ॥
upayājyāḥ sudharmāṇa iti devāḥ prakīrttitāḥ ।
divaspatirmahāsattvasteṣāmindro bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.38.105 ॥
pulahātmajaputrāste vijñeyāstu ruceḥ sutāḥ ।
aṅgirāścaiva dhṛtimān paulastyaḥ pathyavāṃstu saḥ ॥ 2.38.106 ॥
paulahastattva darśī ca bhārgavaśca nirutsakaḥ।
niṣprakampastathātreyo nirmohaḥ kaśyapastathā ॥ 2.38.107 ॥
svarūpaścaiva vāsiṣṭhaḥ saptaite tu trayodaśe।
citraseno vicitraśca tapo dharmadhṛto bhavaḥ ॥ 2.38.108 ॥
raucyasyaite manoḥ putrā hyantare tu trayodaśe ॥ 2.38.109 ॥
caturddaśe tu paryāye bhautasyāpyantare manoḥ ।
devatānāṃ gaṇāḥ pañca proktā yetu bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.38.110 ॥
vācāvṛddhāśca ityete pañca devagaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.38.111 ॥
bṛhadādyāni sāmāni kaniṣṭān sapta tān viduḥ।
sapta lokāḥ paritrāste bhājirāḥ sapta sindhavaḥ ॥ 2.38.112 ॥
vācāvṛddhānṛṣīn viddhi manoḥ svāyambhuvasya vai।
sarve manvantarendrāśca vijñeyāstulyalakṣaṇāḥ ॥ 2.38.113 ॥
tejasā tapasā buddhyā balaśrutaparākramaiḥ।
trailokye yāni sattvāni gatimanti dhruvāṇi ca।
sarvaśaḥ svairguṇaistāni indrāste'bhibhavanti vai ॥ 2.38.114 ॥
bhūtāpavādino hṛṣṭā madhyasthā bhūtavādinaḥ।
bhūtānuvādinaḥ saktāstrayo vedāḥ pravādinām ॥ 2.38.115 ॥
agnidhraḥ kāśyapaścaiva paulastyo māgadhaśca yaḥ।
bhārgavo hyagnibāhuśca śucirāṅgirasastathā।
ojasvī subalaścaiva bhautyasyaite manoḥ sutāḥ ॥ 2.38.116 ॥
savarṇā manavo hyete catvāro brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ।
eko vaivasvataścaiva sāvarṇo manurucyate ॥ 2.38.117 ॥
raucyo bhautyaśca yau tau tu manoḥ paulahabhārgavau।
bhautyasyaivādhipatye tu pūrṇaḥ kalpastu pūryyate ॥ 2.38.118 ॥
niḥśeṣeṣu ca sarveṣu tadā manvantareṣviha।
ante'nekayuge tasmin kṣīṇe saṃhāra ucyate ॥ 2.38.119 ॥
saptaite bhārgavā devā ante manvantare tadā।
bhuktvā trailokyamadhyasthā yugākhyāṃ hyekasaptatim ॥ 2.38.120 ॥
anādhāramidaṃ sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ vai bhaviṣyati ॥ 2.38.122 ॥
tataḥ sthānāni śūnyāni sthānināṃ tāni vai dvijāḥ।
prabhraśyanti vimuktāni tārāṛkṣagrahaistathā ॥ 2.38.123 ॥
tatasteṣu vyatīteṣu trailokyasyeśvareṣviha।
sendrāṣṭeṣu maharlokaṃ yasmiṃste kalpavāsinaḥ ॥ 2.38.124 ॥
manvantareṣu sarvveṣu devāste vai mahaujasaḥ ॥ 2.38.125 ॥
tatasteṣu gateṣūrddhvaṃ sāyojyaṃ kalpavāsinām।
saśarīrāśca śrūyante janalokaṃ sahānugāḥ ॥ 2.38.127 ॥
evaṃ deveṣvatīteṣu maharlokājjanaṃ prati।
bhūtādiṣvavaśiṣṭeṣu sthāvarānteṣu cāpyuta ॥ 2.38.128 ॥
śūnyeṣu lokasthāneṣu mahānteṣu bhūrādiṣu।
deveṣu ca gateṣūrddhvaṃ sāyojyaṃ kalpavāsinām ॥ 2.38.129 ॥
saṃhṛtya tāṃstato brahmā devarṣipitṛdānavān।
