saṃsthāpayati vai sargaṃ mahadṝṣṭyā yugakṣaye ॥ 2.38.130 ॥
tatra yugasahasrāntamaharyardbrahmaṇo viduḥ।
rātriṃ yugasahasrāntāmahorātravido janāḥ ॥ 2.38.131 ॥
naimittikaḥ prākṛtiko yaścaivātyantiko'rthataḥ।
trividhaḥ sarvvabhūtānāmityeṣa pratisañcaraḥ ॥ 2.38.132 ॥
brāhmo naimittikastasya kalpadāhaḥ prasaṃyamaḥ।
pratisarge tu bhūtānāṃ prākṛtaḥ karaṇakṣayaḥ ॥ 2.38.133 ॥
jñānāccātyantikaḥ proktaḥ kāraṇānāmasambhavaḥ ।
tataḥ saṃhṛtya tān brahmā devāṃstrailokyavāsinaḥ ॥ 2.38.134 ॥
aharante prakurute sargasya pralayaṃ punaḥ।
suṣupsurbhagavān brahmā prajāḥ saṃharate tadā ॥ 2.38.135 ॥
tato yugasahasrānte saṃprāpte ca yugakṣaye।
tatrātmasthāḥ prajāḥ karttuṃ prapede sa prajāpatiḥ ॥ 2.38.136 ॥
tadā bhavatyanāvṛṣṭistadā sā śata vārṣikī।
tathā yānyalpasārāṇi sattvāni pṛthivītale ॥ 2.38.137 ॥
tānyevātra pralīyante bhūmitvamupayānti ca।
saptaraśmiratho bhūtvā hyudatiṣṭhadvibhāvasuḥ ॥ 2.38.138 ॥
asahyaraśmirbhagavān pibannambho gabhastibhiḥ।
haritā raśmayastasya dīpyamānāstu saptabhiḥ ॥ 2.38.139 ॥
bhūya eva vivartante vyāpnuvanto vanaṃ śanaiḥ।
bhaumaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ dhanaṃ tejo bhṛśamadbhistu dīpyate ॥ 2.38.140 ॥
tasmādudakaṃ sūryyasya tapato'ti hi kathyate।
nāvṛṣṭyā tapate sūryo nāvṛṣṭyā pariviṣyate ॥ 2.38.141 ॥
nāvṛṣṭyā paricinvanti vāriṇā dīpyate raviḥ।
tasmādapaḥ piban yā vai dīpyate ravirambare ॥ 2.38.142 ॥
tasya te raśmayaḥ sapta pibantyambho mahārṇavāt।
tenāhāreṇa sandīptaḥ sūryyaḥ sapta bhavatyuta ॥ 2.38.143 ॥
tataste raśmayaḥ sapta sūryyabhūtāścaturdiśam।
caturlokamimaṃ sarvaṃ dahanti śikhinastadā ॥ 2.38.144 ॥
prāpnuvanti ca bhābhistu hyūrddhaṃ cādhaśca raśmibhiḥ।
dīpyante bhāskarāḥ sapta yugāntāgniḥ pratāpinaḥ ॥ 2.38.145 ॥
te vāriṇā ca saṃdīptā bahusāhasraraśmayaḥ।
khaṃ samāvṛtya tiṣṭhanti nirdahanto vasundharām ॥ 2.38.146 ॥
tatasteṣāṃ pratāpena dahyamānā vasundharā।
sādrinadyarṇavā pṛthvī visnehā samapadyata ॥ 2.38.147 ॥
dīptābhiḥ santatābhiśca citrābhiśca samantataḥ।
adhaścordhvaśca tiryak ca saṃruddhaṃ sūryaraśmibhiḥ ॥ 2.38.148 ॥
sūryyagnīnāṃ pravṛddhānāṃ saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ parasparam।
ekatvamupayātānāmekajvālaṃ bhavatyuta ॥ 2.38.149 ॥
sarvalokapraṇāśañca so'gnirbhūtvā tu maṇḍalī।
caturlokamidaṃ sarvaṃ nirdahatyāśu tejasā ॥ 2.38.150 ॥
tataḥ pralīyate sarvvaṃ jaṅgamaṃ sthāvaraṃ tadā।
nirvṛkṣā nistṛṇā bhūmiḥ kūrmapṛṣṭhasamā bhavet ॥ 2.38.151 ॥
ambarīṣamivābhāti sarvaṃ māriṣitaṃ jagat।
sarvameva tadārcirbhiḥ pūrṇaṃ jajvālyate nabhaḥ ॥ 2.38.152 ॥
pātāle yāni bhūtāni mahotadhigatāni ca ।
tatastāni pralīyante bhūmitvamupayānti ca ॥ 2.38.153 ॥
dvīpāśca parvatāścaiva varṣāṇyatha mahodadhiḥ।
sarvvaṃ tadbhasmasāccakre sarvvātmā pāvakastu saḥ ॥ 2.38.154 ॥
samudrebhyo nadībhyaśca pātālebhyaśca sarvataḥ।
pibannapaḥ samiddho'gniḥ pṛthivīmāśrito jvalan ॥ 2.38.155 ॥
tataḥ saṃvarttakaḥ śailānatikramya mahāṃstathā।
lokān saṃharate dīpto ghoraḥ saṃvarttako'nalaḥ ॥ 2.38.156 ॥
tataḥ sa pṛthivīṃ bhittvā rasātalamaśoṣayat।
nirdahya tāṃstu pātālānnāgalokamathādahat ॥ 2.38.157 ॥
adhastātpṛthivīṃ dagdhvā hyūrddhvaṃ sa dahate divam।
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi hyayutānyarbudāni ca ॥ 2.38.158 ॥
udatiṣṭhañchikhāstasya bahvayaḥ saṃvarttakasya tu।
gandharvāṃśca piśācāṃśca samahoragarākṣasān ।
tadā dahati sandīpto golakaṃ caiva sarvvaśaḥ ॥ 2.38.159 ॥
bhūrlokantu bhuvarlokaṃ svarlokañca mahastathā।
ghoraṃ dahati kālāgnirevaṃ lokacatuṣṭayam ॥ 2.38.160 ॥
vyāpteṣu teṣu lokeṣu tiryagūrddhvamathāgninā।
tattejaḥ samanuprāptaṃ kṛtsnaṃ jagadidaṃ śanaiḥ।
ayoguḍanibhaṃ sarvvaṃ tadā hyevaṃ prakāśate ॥ 2.38.161 ॥
tato gajakulākārāstaḍidbhi samalaṃkṛtāḥ।
uttiṣṭhanti tadā ghorā vyomni saṃvarttakā ghanāḥ ॥ 2.38.162 ॥
kecinnīlotpalaśyāmāḥ kecitkumudasannibhāḥ।
kecidvaiḍhūryasaṃkāśā indranīlanibhā'pare ॥ 2.38.163 ॥
śaṅkhakundanibhāścānye jātyañjananibhāstathā ।
dhūmra varṇā ghanāḥ kecitkecitpītāḥ payodharāḥ ॥ 2.38.164 ॥
kecidrāsabhavarṇābhā lākṣāraktanibhāstathā।
manaḥśilābhāstvapare kapotābhāstathāmbudāḥ ॥ 2.38.165 ॥
indragopanibhāḥ keciduttiṣṭhanti ghanā divi।
kecitpuradharākārāḥ kecidgajakulopamāḥ ॥ 2.38.166 ॥
ke citparvatasaṃkāśāḥ kecitsthalanibhā ghanāḥ।
kuṇḍāgāranibhāḥ kecitkecinmīnakulopamāḥ ॥ 2.38.167 ॥
bahurūpā ghorarūpā ghorasvaraninādinaḥ।
tadā jaladharāḥ sarve pūrayanti nabhaḥsthalam ॥ 2.38.168 ॥
tataste jaladā ghorā navīnā bhāskarātmikāḥ।
saptadhā saṃvṛtātmānastamagniṃ śamayantyuta ॥ 2.38.169 ॥
tataste jaladā varṣaṃ muñcanti ca mahodyamam।
sughoramaśivaṃ sarvvaṃ nāśayanti ca pāvakam ॥ 2.38.170 ॥
pravṛṣṭaiśca tathātyarthaṃ vāribhiḥ pūryyate jagat।
adbhistejo'bhibhūtañca tadāgniḥ prāviśatyapaḥ ॥ 2.38.171 ॥
naṣṭe cāgnau varṣaśate payodāḥ pākasambhavāḥ।
plāvayanti jagatsarvaṃ bṛhajjālaparisravaiḥ ॥ 2.38.172 ॥
dhārābhiḥ pūrayantīmaṃ codyamānāḥ svayambhuvā।
anye tu salilaughaistu velāmabhibhavantyapi।
saṃveṣṭayati ghorātmā divi vāyuḥ samantataḥ ॥ 2.38.177 ॥
tasminnekārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame।
pūrṇe yugasahasre vai niḥśeṣaḥ kalpa ucyate ॥ 2.38.178 ॥
athāmbhasā vṛte loke prāhurekārṇavaṃ budhāḥ।
atha bhūmitalaṃ khañca vāyuścaikārṇave tadā।
pārthivāstvatha sāmudrā āpo haimāśca sarvvaśaḥ।
prasarantyo vrajantyekaṃ salilākhyāṃ bhajantyuta ॥ 2.38.180 ॥
āgatāgatikaṃ caiva tadā tatsalilaṃ smṛtam।
pracchādya tiṣṭhati mahīmarṇavākhyaṃ ca tajjalam ॥ 2.38.181 ॥
ābhānti yasmāttā bhābhirbhāśabdavyāptidīptiṣu।
bhasma sarvvamanuprāpya tasmādambho nirucyate ॥ 2.38.182 ॥
nānātve caiva śīghre ca dhāturvai ara ucyate।
ekārṇave tadā yo vai na śīghrāstena tā narāḥ ॥ 2.38.183 ॥
tasmin yugasahasrānte divase brahmaṇo gate।
tāvantaṃ kālamevaṃ tu bhavatyekārṇavaṃ jagat।
tadā tu sarvvavyāpārā nivarttante prajāpateḥ ॥ 2.38.184 ॥
evamekārṇave tasminnaṣṭe sthāvara jaṅgame।
tadā sa bhavati brahmā sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt ॥ 2.38.185 ॥
sahasraśīrṣā sumanāḥ sahasrapāt sahasracakṣurvadanaḥ sahasravāk।
sahasrabāhuḥ prathamaḥ prajāpatistrīyapathe yaḥ puruṣo nirucyate ॥ 2.38.186 ॥
ādityavarṇo bhuvanasya goptā hyapūrvva ekaḥ prathamasturāṣāṭ ।
hiraṇyagarbhaḥ puruṣo mahān vai saṃpadyate vai tamasaḥ parastāt ॥ 2.38.187 ॥
caturyugasahasrānte sarvataḥ salilaplute।
suṣupsuraprakāśāṃ svāṃ rātriṃ tu kurute prabhuḥ ॥ 2.38.188 ॥
caturvidhā yadā śete prajāḥ sarvvāṇḍamaṇḍitāḥ।
paśyante taṃ mahātmānaṃ kālaṃ sapta maharṣayaḥ ॥ 2.38.189 ॥
janalokavivarttantastapasā labdhacakṣuṣaḥ।
bhṛgvādayo mahātmānaḥ pūrvve vyākhyātalakṣaṇāḥ ॥ 2.38.190 ॥
satyādīn saptalokān vai te hi paśyanti cakṣuṣā।
brahmāṇaṃ te tu paśyanti mahābrāhmīṣu rātriṣu ॥ 2.38.191 ॥
saptarṣayaḥ prapaśyanti saptakālaṃ svarātriṣu।
kalpānāṃ parameṣṭitvāttasmādādyaḥ sa paṭyate ॥ 2.38.192 ॥
sa yaṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ kalpādiṣu punaḥ punaḥ।
evamāveśayitvā tu svātmanyeva prajāpatiḥ ॥ 2.38.193 ॥
athātmani mahātejāḥ sarvamādāya sarvakṛt।
tataste vasate rātriṃ tamasyekārṇave jale ॥ 2.38.194 ॥
tato rātrikṣaye prāpte pratibuddhaḥ prajāpatiḥ।
manaḥ sisṛkṣayā yuktaṃ sargāya nidadhe punaḥ ॥ 2.38.195 ॥
evaṃ saloke nirvṛtte upaśānte prajāpatau।
brahmanaimittike tasmin kalpite vai prasaṃyame ॥ 2.38.196 ॥
dehairviyogaḥ satvānāṃ tasmin vai kṛtsnaśaḥ smṛtaḥ।
tato dagdheṣu bhūteṣu sarvveṣvādityaraśmibhiḥ।
devarṣimanuvaryyeṣu tasmin saṅkalane tadā ॥ 2.38.197 ॥
gandharvādīni satvāni piśācāntāni sarvvaśaḥ।
kalpādāvaprataptāni janamevāśrayanti vai ॥ 2.38.198 ॥
tadā tānyapi dagdhāni dhutapāpāni sarvvaśaḥ।
jane tānyupapadyante yāvatsaṃplavate jagat ॥ 2.38.199 ॥
vyuṣṭāyāntu rajanyāṃ tu brahmaṇe'vyaktayonaye।
jāyante hi punastāni sarvvabhūtāni kṛtsnaśaḥ ॥ 2.38.200 ॥
ṛṣayo manavo devāḥ prajāḥ sarvvaścaturvidhāḥ।
teṣāmapīha siddhānāṃ nidhanotpattirucyate ॥ 2.38.201 ॥
yathā sūryasya loke'sminnudayāstamanaṃ smṛtam।
tathā janmanirodhaśca bhūtānāmiha dṛśyate ॥ 2.38.202 ॥
ābhūtasaṃplavāttasmādbhavaḥ saṃsāra ucyate ।
yathā sarvvāṇi bhūtāni jāyante hi varṣāsviha ॥ 2.38.203 ॥
sthāvarādīni sattvāni kalpe kalpe tathā prajāḥ।
yathārttāvṛtuliṅgāni nānārūpāṇi paryyaye ॥ 2.38.204 ॥
dṛśyante tāni tānyeva tathā brahmāttarātriṣu ।
pratyāhāre ca sarge ca gatimanti dhruvāṇi ca ॥ 2.38.205 ॥
niṣkramante viśante ca prajākāraṃ prajāpatim।
brahmāṇaṃ sarvabhūtāni mahāyogaṃ maheśvaram ॥ 2.38.206 ॥
saṃsraṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ kalpādiṣu punaḥ punaḥ।
vyaktā vyakto mahādevastasya sarvamidaṃ jagat ॥ 2.38.207 ॥
yenaiva sṛṣṭāḥ prathamaṃ prayātā āpo hi mārgeṇa mahītale'smin।
pūrvaprayātena tathā hyapo'nyāstenaiva tenaiva tu saṃvrajanti ॥ 2.38.208 ॥
yathā śūbhena tvaśubhena caiva tatraiva tatraiva vivarttamānāḥ।
martyāstu dehāntarabhāvitattvādravervaśādūrddhvamadhaścaranti ॥ 2.38.209 ॥
ye cāpi devā manavaḥ prajeśā anye'pi ye svargagatāśca siddhāḥ।
sadbhāvitākhyātivaśācca dharmmyāḥ punarnisargeṇa bhavanti sattvāḥ ॥ 2.38.210 ॥
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi kālamābhūtasaṃplavam।
manvantarāṇi yāni syurvyākhyātāni mayā dvijāḥ।
saha prajñānisargeṇa saha devaiścaturddaśa ॥ 2.38.211 ॥
sa yugākhyā sahasraṃ tu sarvāṇyevāntarāṇi vai ।
asyāḥ sahasre dve pūrṇe niḥśeṣaḥ kalpa ucyate ॥ 2.38.212 ॥
etadbrāhmamaho jñeyaṃ tasya saṃkhyāṃ nibodhata।
nimeṣastulya mātrā hi kṛto laghvakṣareṇa tu ॥ 2.38.213 ॥
mānuṣākṣinimeṣāstu kāṣṭā pañcadaśa smṛtā।
lavaḥ kṣaṇāstu pañcaiva viṃśatkāṣṭā tu te trayaḥ ॥ 2.38.214 ॥
prasthaḥ saptodakāścaiva sādhikāstu lavaḥ smṛtaḥ।
lavāstriṃśatkalā jñeyai muhūrtastriṃśataḥ kalāḥ ॥ 2.38.215 ॥
muhūrttāstu punastriṃśadahorātramiti sthitiḥ।
ahorātraṃ kalānāntu vyadhikāni śatāni ṣaṭ ॥ 2.38.216 ॥
tāścaiva saṃkhyāyā jñeyaṃ candrādityagatiryathā।
nimeṣā daśa pañcaiva kāṣṭāstāstriṃśataḥ kalā ॥ 2.38.217 ॥
triṃśatkalā muhūrttastu daśabhāgaḥ kalā smṛtā।
catvāriṃśatkalānāntu muhūrtta iti saṃjñataḥ ॥ 2.38.218 ॥
muhūrttāśca lavāścāpi pramāṇajñaiḥ prakalpitāḥ।
tatsthāne nāmbhasāścāpi palānyatha trayodaśa ॥ 2.38.219 ॥
māgadhenaiva mānena jalaprastho vidhīyate।
ete cāpyudakaprasthāścatvāro nāliko dhaṭaḥ ॥ 2.38.220 ॥
hemamāṣaiḥ kṛtacchidrai ścaturbhiścaturaṅgulaiḥ.
samāhani ca rātrau ca muhūrtto vai dvinālikau ॥ 2.38.221 ॥
ravergativiśeṣeṇa sarveṣu nṛṣu nityaśaḥ।
tadaharmānuṣaṃ jñeyaṃ nākṣatrantu daśādhikam।
sāvanena tu māsena hyabdo'yaṃ mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.38.223 ॥
etaddivyamahorātramiti śāstraviniścayaḥ।
ahnā'nena tu yā saṃkhyā māsartvayanavārṣikī ॥ 2.38.224 ॥
tadā baddhamidaṃ jñānaṃ saṃjñā yā hyupalakṣyatām।
kalānāṃ suparīmāṇātkāla ityabhidhīyate ॥ 2.38.225 ॥
yadaharbrahmaṇaḥ proktaṃ divyā koṭī tu tat smṛta।
śatānāñca sahasrāṇi daśadviguṇatāni ca।
navatiñca sahasrāṇi tathaivānyāni yāni tu ॥ 2.38.226 ॥
etacchrutvā tu ṛṣayo vismayaṃ paramādbhutam।
saṃsthāsambhajanaṃ jñānamapṛcchannantarantadā ॥ 2.38.227 ॥
saṃplāvanasya kālantu mānuṣeṇaiva sammatam।
mānena śrotumicchāmaḥ saṃkṣepārthapadākṣaram ॥ 2.38.228 ॥
teṣāṃ śrutvā sa devastu vāyurlokahite rataḥ।
saṃkṣepāddivyacakṣuṣmān provāca bhagavān prabhuḥ ॥ 2.38.229 ॥
ete rātryahanī pūrvaṃ kīrttite tviha taukike।
tāsāṃ saṅkhyāya varṣāgraṃ brāhyaṃ vakṣyāmyahaḥkṣaye ॥ 2.38.230 ॥
koṭiśatāni catvāri varṣāṇi mānuṣāṇi tu।
dvātriṃśacca tathā koṭyaḥ saṅkhyātāḥ saṅkhyayā dvijaiḥ ॥ 2.38.231 ॥
tathā śatasahasrāṇi ekonanavatiḥ punaḥ।
āśītiśca sahasrāṇi eṣa kālaḥ plavasya tu ॥ 2.38.232 ॥
mānuṣākhyeṇa saṅkhyātaḥ kālo hyābhūtasaṃplavaḥ।
sapta sūryyāstadā'greṣu tadā lokeṣu teṣu vai ॥ 2.38.233 ॥
mahābhūteṣu līyante prajāḥ sarvvāścaturvidhāḥ ।
salilenāplute loke naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame ॥ 2.38.234 ॥
vinivṛtte ca saṃhāre upaśānte prajāpatau।
nirāloke pradagdhe tu naiśena tu samāvṛte ।
īśvarādhiṣṭite hyasmiṃstadā hyekārṇave tadā ।। 38.235
tāvadekārṇavo jñeyo yāvadāsīdahaḥ prabhoḥ ।
rātristu salilāvasthā nivṛttau cāpyahaḥ samṛtam ॥ 2.38.235 ॥
ahorātrastathaivāsya krameṇa parivarttate।
ābhūtasaṃplavo hyeṣa ahorātraḥ smṛtaḥ prabhoḥ ॥ 2.38.236 ॥
trailokye yāni satvāni gatimanti dhruvāṇi ca।
ābhūtebhyaḥ pralīyante tasmādābhūtasaṃplavaḥ ॥ 2.38.237 ॥
ābhūtaḥ plavate caiva tasmādābhūtasaṃplavaḥ ॥ 2.38.238 ॥
atītā varttamānāśca tathaivānāgatāḥ prajāḥ।
divyasaṅkhyā prasaṅkhyātā hyaparārdhaguṇīkṛtā ॥ 2.38.239 ॥
parārdhadviguṇañcāpi paramāyuḥ prakīrttitam।
etāvān sthitikālastu hyajasyeha prajāmateḥ।
sthityante pratisargasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭinaḥ ॥ 2.38.240 ॥
yathā vāyupravegena dīpārcirupaśāmyati।
tathaivaṃ pratisargeṇa brahmā samupaśāmyati ॥ 2.38.241 ॥
tathā hyapratisaṃsṛṣṭe mahadādau maheśvare ।।
mahatpralīyate'vyakte guṇasāmyaṃ tato bhavet ॥ 2.38.242 ॥
ityeṣa ca samākhyāto mayā hyābhūtasaṃplavaḥ।
brahmanaimittiko hyeṣa saṃprakṣālanasaṃyamaḥ ॥ 2.38.243 ॥
samāsena samākhyāto bhūyaḥ kiṃ varttayāmi vaḥ।
ya idaṃ dhārayennityaṃ śrṛṇuyādvāpyabhīkṣṇaśaḥ ।
kīrttanācchravaṇāccāpi mahatīṃ siddhimāpnuyāt ॥ 2.38.244 ॥
asādhāraṇavṛttaistu hutaśeṣādibhirdvijaiḥ|
dharmmavaiśeṣikaiścaiva hyācūrṇasūkṣmadarśibhiḥ || 39.1 ||
te devaiḥ saha tiṣṭhanti maharlokanivāsinaḥ|
caturddaśaite manavaḥ kīrttitāḥ kīrttivardhanāḥ || 39.2 ||
atītā varttamānāśca tathaivānāgatāśca ye|
ṛṣibhi rdaivataiścaiva saha gandharvarākṣasaiḥ || 39.3 ||
sarvve hyapi kramātītā maharlokaṃ samāśritāḥ|
brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyairvaiśyairdhārmikaiḥ sahitaiḥ surāḥ || 39.4 ||
sarvve hyapi kramātītā maharlokaṃ samāśritāḥ|
brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyairvaiśyairdhārmikaiḥ sahitaiḥ surāḥ || 39.5 ||
taistathyakāribhiryuktaiḥ śraddhāvadbhiradarpitaiḥ|
varṇāśramāṇāṃ dharmmeṣu śrautasmārtteṣu saṃsthitaiḥ|
vinivṛttādhikārāste yāvanmanvantarakṣayaḥ || 39.6 ||
maharloketi yatproktaṃ mātariśvaṃstvayā vibho|
pratiloke ca karttavyamanekaiḥ samadhiṣṭitāḥ || 39.7 ||
provāca madhuraṃ vākyaṃ yathātattvena tattvavit || 39.9 ||
caturddaśaiva sthānāni varṇitāni maharṣibhiḥ|
lokākhyāni tu yāni syuryeṣu tiṣṭhanti mānavāḥ || 39.10 ||
sapta teṣu kṛtānyāhurakṛtāni tu sapta vai|
bhūrādayastu saṅkhyātāḥ sapta lokāḥ kṛtāstviha || 39.11 ||
akṛtāni tu saptaiva prākṛtāni tu yāni vai|
sthānāni sthānibhiḥ sārddhaṃ kṛtāni tu nibandhanam || 39.12 ||
pṛthivīṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca divyaṃ yacca mahaḥ smṛtam|
sthānānyetāni catvāri smṛtānyārṇavakāni ca || 39.13 ||
kṣayātiśayayuktāni tathā yuktāni vakṣyate|
yāni naimittikāni syustiṣṭhantyābhūtasaṃplavam || 39.14 ||
janastapaśca satyañca sthānānyetāni trīṇi tu|
aikāntikāni sattvāni tiṣṭhantīhāprasaṃyamāt || 39.15 ||
vyaktāni tu pravakṣyāmi sthānānyetāni sapta vai|
bhūrlokaḥ prathamasteṣāṃ dvitīyastu bhuvaḥ smṛtaḥ || 39.16 ||
svastṛtīyastu vijñeyaścaturtho vai mahaḥ smṛtaḥ|
janastu pañcamo lokastapaḥ ṣaṣṭo vibhāvyate || 39.17 ||
satyantu saptamo loko nirālokastataḥ param|
bhūriti vyāhṛte pūrvaṃ bhūrlokaśca tato'bhavat || 39.18 ||
dvitīyaṃ bhuva ityukta antarikṣaṃ tato'bhavat|
tṛtīyaṃ svaritītyukte divaṃ prādurbabhūva ha || 39.19 ||
vyāhāraistribhiretaistu brahmalokamakalpayat|
tato bhūḥ pārthivo loka antarikṣaṃ tato'bhavat|
tṛtīyaṃ svaritītyukte divaṃ prādurbabhūva ha || 39.20 ||
svarloko vai divaṃ hyetatpurāṇe niścayaṃ gatam|
bhūtasyādhipatiścāgnistato bhūtapatiḥ smṛtaḥ || 39.21 ||
vāyurbhuvasyādhipatistena vāyurbhuvapatiḥ|
bhavyasya sūryo'dhipatistena sūryo divaspatiḥ || 39.22 ||
maheti vyāhṛtenaivaṃ maharlokastato'bhavat|
vinivṛttādhikārāṇāṃ devānāṃ tatra vai kṣayaḥ || 39.23 ||
janastu pañcamo lokastasmājjāyanti vai janāḥ |
tāsāṃ svāyaṃbhuvādyānāṃ prajānāṃ jananājjanaḥ || 39.24 ||
yāstāḥ svāyambhuvādyā hi purastātparikīrttitāḥ|
kalpadagdhe tadā loke pratiṣṭhanti tadā tapaḥ || 39.25 ||
ṛbhuḥ sanatkumārādyā yatra santyūrddhvaretasaḥ |
tapasā bhāvitātmānastatra santīti vā tapaḥ || 39.26 ||
satyeti brahmaṇaḥ śabdaḥ sattāmātrastu saḥ smṛtaḥ|
brahmalokastataḥ satyaṃ saptamaḥ sa tu bhāskaraḥ || 39.27 ||
gandharvāpsaraso yakṣā guhyakāstu sarākṣasāḥ|
sarvabhūtapiśācāśca nāgāśca saha mānuṣaiḥ|
svarlokavāsinaḥ sarve devā bhuvinivāsinaḥ || 39.28 ||
maruto mātariśvāno rudrā devāstathāśvinau|
aniketāntarikṣāste bhuvarlaukyā divaukasaḥ || 39.29 ||
ādityā ṛbhavo viśve sādhyāśca pitarastathā|
ṛṣayo'ṅgirasaścaiva bhuvarllokaṃ samāśritāḥ || 39.30 ||
ete vaimānikā devāstārāgrahanivāsinaḥ|
ityete kramaśaḥ proktā brahmavyāhārasambhavāḥ || 39.31 ||
bhūrlokaprathamā lokā mahadantāśca te smṛtāḥ|
ārabhyante tu tanmātraiḥ śuddhāsteṣāṃ parasparam || 39.32 ||
śukrādyāścākṣuṣāntāśca ye vyatītā bhuvaṃ śritāḥ|
maharlokaścaturthastu tasmiṃste kalpavāsinaḥ || 39.33 ||
bhūrlokaprathamā lokā mahadantāśca ye smṛtāḥ|
tān sarvān sapta sūryāste arccirbhirnidahanti vai || 39.34 ||
marīciḥ kaśyapo dakṣastathā svāyambhuvo'ṅgirāḥ |
bhṛguḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kraturityevamādayaḥ || 39.35 ||
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve varttante tatra taiḥ saha|
niḥsattvā nirmamāścaiva tatra te hyūrddhvaretasaḥ || 39.36 ||
ṛbhuḥ sanatkumārādyā vairājyāste tapodhanāḥ|
manvantarāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ sāvarṇānāṃ tataḥ smṛtāḥ |
caturddaśānāṃ sarveṣāṃ punarāvṛttihetavaḥ || 39.37 ||
yogaṃ tapaśca satyañca samādhāya tadātmani|
ṣaṣṭe kāle nivarttante tattadāharviparyaye || 39.38 ||
satyantu saptamo loko hyapunarmārgagāminām|
brahmalokaḥ samākhyāto hyapratīghātalakṣaṇaḥ || 39.39 ||
paryāsapārimāṇyena bhūrlokaḥ samitiḥ smṛtaḥ |
bhūmyantaraṃ yadādityādantarikṣaṃ bhuvaḥ smṛtam || 39.40 ||
sūryadhruvāntaraṃ yacca svargaloko divaḥ smṛtaḥ|
dhruvājjanāntaraṃ yacca maharlokastaducyate || 39.41 ||
vikhyātāḥ saptalokāstu teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi siddhayaḥ|
bhūrlokavāsinaḥ sarve hyannādāstu ramātmakāḥ || 39.42 ||
bhuve svarge ca ye sarve somapā ājyapāśca te|
caturthe ye'pi varttante maha rlokaṃ samāśritāḥ || 39.43 ||
vijñeyā mānasī teṣāṃ siddhirvai pañcalakṣaṇā|
sadyaścotpadyate teṣāṃ manasā sarvvamīpsitam || 39.44 ||
ete daivā yajante vai yajñaiḥ sarvaiḥ parasparam|
prathamānantarairiṣṭvā hyantarāḥ sāmprataiḥ punaḥ|
nivarttatītyāsambandho'tīte devagaṇe tataḥ || 39.46 ||
vinivṛttādhikārāṇāṃ siddhisteṣāntu mānasī|
teṣāntu mānasī jñeyā śuddhā siddhiparamparā || 39.47 ||
uktā lokāśca catvāro janasyānuvidhistathā|
samāsena mayā viprā bhūyastaṃ varttayāmi vaḥ || 39.48 ||
marīciḥ kaśyapo dakṣo vasiṣṭhaścāṅgirā bhṛguḥ|
pulastyaḥ pulahaścaiva kraturityevamādayaḥ || 39.49 ||
pūrvaṃ te saṃprasūyante brahmaṇo manasā iha|
tataḥ prajāḥ pratiṣṭāpya janamevāśrayanti te || 39.50 ||
kalpadāhapradīpteṣu tadā kāleṣu teṣu vai|
bhūrā diṣu mahānteṣu bhṛśaṃ vyāpteṣvathāgninā || 39.51 ||
śikhā saṃvarttakā jñeyā prāpnuvanti sadā janāḥ|
yāmādayo gaṇāḥ sarve maharlokanivāsinaḥ || 39.52 ||
maharlokeṣu dīpteṣu janamevāśrayanti te|
sarve sūkṣmaśarīrāste tatrasthāstu bhavanti te || 39.53 ||
teṣāṃ te tulyasāmarthyāstulyamūrttidharāstathā |
jana loke vivarttante yāvatsaṃplavate jagat || 39.54 ||
vyuṣṭāyāntu rajanyāṃ vai brahmaṇo'vyaktayoninaḥ|
aharādau prasūyante pūrvavatkramaśāstviha || 39.55 ||
svāyambhuvādayaḥ sarve marīcyantāstu sādhakāḥ|
devāste vai punasteṣāṃ jāyante nidhaneṣviha || 39.56 ||
yāmādayaḥ krameṇaiva kaniṣṭādyāḥ prajāpateḥ|
pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ prasūyante paścime paścacimāstathā|
devānvaye devatā hi sapta sambhūtayaḥ smṛtāḥ|
vyatītāḥ kalyajāsteṣāṃ tisraḥ śiṣṭāstathā pare || 39.58 ||
āvarttamānā devāste krameṇaite na sarvvaśaḥ|
gatvā javantavībhāvandaśakṛtvaḥ punaḥ punaḥ || 39.59 ||
tataste vai gaṇāḥ sarvve dṛṣṭvā bhāveṣvanityatām|
bhāvino'rthasya ca balāt puṇyākhyātibalena ca || 39.60 ||
nivṛttavṛttayaḥ sarve svasthāḥ sumanasastathā|
tato'nyenaiva kālena nityayuktāstapasvinaḥ|
kathanāccaiva dharmasya teṣāṃ te jajñire'nvaye || 39.62 ||
īhotpannāstataste vai sthānā āpūrayantyuta|
devatve ca ṛṣitve ca manuṣyanve ca sarvaśaḥ || 39.63 ||
evaṃ devagaṇāḥ sarve daśakṛtvo nivarttya vai|
vairājeṣūpapannāste daśa tiṣṭhantyupaplavān || 39.64 ||
pūrṇe pūrṇe tataḥ kalpe sthitvā vairājake punaḥ|
brahmaloke vivarttaṃte pūrvvapūrvvakrameṇa tu || 39.65 ||
etasmin brahmaloke tu kalpe vairājake gate|
vairājaṃ punarapyeke kalpasthānamakalpayan || 39.66 ||
evaṃ pūrvvānupūrvyeṇa brahmalokagatena vai|
vairāje tūpapadyante daśakṛtvo nivarttate || 39.67 ||
evaṃ devayugānīha vyatītāni sahasraśaḥ|
nidhanaṃ brahmaloke tu gatānāmṛṣibhiḥ saha || 39.68 ||
na śakyamānupūrveṇa teṣāṃ vaktuṃ pravistaram|
anāditvācca kālasya hyasaṃ khyānācca sarvaśaḥ|
evameva na sandeho yathāvatkathitaṃ mayā || 39.69 ||
tadupaśrutya vākyārthamṛṣayaḥ saṃśayānvitāḥ|
sūtamāhuḥ purāṇajñaṃ vyāsaśiṣyaṃ mahā matim || 39.70 ||
vairājāste yadāhārā yatsattvāśca yadāśrayāḥ|
tiṣṭhanti caiva yatkālaṃ tanno brūhi yathātatham || 39.71 ||
taduktamṛṣibhirvākyaṃ śrutvā lokārthatattvavit|
sūtaḥ paurāṇiko vākyaṃ vinayenedamabravīt || 39.72 ||
tataḥ prāpyanta te sarvve śuddhiśuddhatamāśca ye|
ābhūta saṃplavāstatra daśa tiṣṭhanti tejanāḥ || 39.73 ||
sarve sūkṣmaśarīrāste vidvāṃso ghanamūrttayaḥ|
sthitalokāsthitatvācca teṣāṃ bhūtaṃ na vidyate || 39.74 ||
ūcuḥ sanatkumārādyāḥ siddhāste thogadharmiṇaḥ|
evameva mahābhāgāḥ praṇavaṃ sampraviśya ha|
brahmaloke pravarttānastannaḥ śreyo bhaviṣyati || 39.77 ||
evamuktvā tadā sarve brahmānte vyavasāyinaḥ|
yojayitvā tadā sarvve varttante yogadharmmiṇaḥ || 39.78 ||
tatraiva sampralīyante śāntā dīpārciṣo yathā|
brahmakāyamavarttanta punarāvṛttidurllabham ||. 39.79 ||
lokaṃ taṃ samanuprāpya sarvve te bhāvanāmayam|
ānandaṃ brahmaṇaḥ prāpya hyamṛtatvāya te gatāḥ || 39.80 ||
vairājebhyastathaivorddhvamantare ṣaḍguṇe tataḥ|
brahmalokaḥ samākhyāto yatra brahmā purohitaḥ || 39.81 ||
te sarve praṇavātmāno buddhaśuddhatapāstathā|
ānandaṃ brahmaṇaḥ prāpyāmṛtatvañca bhajantyuta || 39.82 ||
dvandvaiste nābhibhūyante bhāvatrayavivarjjitāḥ|
ādhipatyaṃ vinā tulyā brahmaṇaste mahaujasaḥ || 39.83 ||
prabhāvavijayaiśvaryyasthitivairāgyadarśanaiḥ|
tebrahmalaukikāḥ sarve gatiṃ prāpya vivarttanīm || 39.84 ||
brahmaṇā saha devaiśca samprāpte pratisañcare|
tapaso'nte kriyātmāno buddhāvasthā manīṣiṇaḥ|
avyakte saṃpralīyante sarve te kṣaṇadarśinaḥ || 39.85 ||
ityetadamṛtaṃ śukraṃ nityamakṣayamavyayam|
devarṣayo brahmasatraṃ sanātanamupāsate || 39.86 ||
apunarmārgagādīnāṃ teṣāṃ caivorddhvaretasām |
karmābhyāsakṛtā śuddhirvedānteṣūpalakṣyate || 39.87 ||
tatra te'bhyāsino yuktāḥ parāṃ kāṣṭāmupāsate|
hitvā śarīraṃ pāpmānamamṛtatvāya te gatāḥ || 39.88 ||
vītarāgā jitakrodhāḥ nirmohāḥ satyavādinaḥ|
śāntāḥ praṇihitātmāno dayāvanto jitendriyāḥ || 39.89 ||
niḥsaṅgāḥ śucayaścaiva brahmasāyujyagāḥ smṛtāḥ |
akāmayuktairye vīrāstapobhirddagdhakilbiṣāḥ|
teṣāmabhraṃśino lokā aprameyasukhāḥ smṛtāḥ || 39.90 ||
etadbrahmapadaṃ divyaṃ paramaṃ vyomni bhāsvaram|
gatvā na yatra śocanti hyamarā brahmaṇā saha || 39.91 ||
kasmādeṣa parārddhaśca kaścaiṣa para ucyate|
etadveditumicchāmastanno nigada sattama || 39.92 ||
śrṛṇudhvaṃ me parārddhañca parisaṃkhyāṃ parasya ca|
evaṃ daśa śatañcaiva sahasrañcaiva saṅkhyayā || 39.93 ||
vijñeyamāsahasrantu sahasrāṇi daśāyutam|
ekaṃ śatasahasrantu niyutaṃ procyate budhaiḥ || 39.94 ||
tathā śatasahasrāṇāmarbudaṃ koṭirucyate|
arbudaṃ daśakoṭyastu hyabjaṃ koṭiśataṃ viduḥ || 39.95 ||
sahasramapi koṭīnāṃ kharvamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ|
daśakoṭisahasrāṇi nikharvamiti taṃ viduḥ || 39.96 ||
śataṃ koṭisahasrāṇāṃ saṅkurityabhidhīyate|
koṭi sahasra srāṇāṃ koṭīnāṃ daśadhā punaḥ|
guṇitāni samudraṃ vai prāhuḥ saṃkhyāvido janāḥ || 39.97 ||
koṭikoṭisahasrāṇiṃ parārddha iti kīrtyate |
parārddhadviguṇañcāpi paramāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ || 39.99 ||
śatamāhuḥ paridṛḍhaṃ sahasraṃ paripadmakam|
vijñeyamayutaṃ tasmānniyutaṃ prayutaṃ tataḥ || 39.100 ||
arbudaṃ nirbudañcaiva kharbudañca tataḥ smṛtam|
kharvañcaiva nikharvañca śaṅkuḥ padmaṃ tathaiva ca || 39.101 ||
samudraṃ madhyamañcaiva parārddhamaparaṃ tataḥ|
evamaṣṭādaśaitāni sthānāni gaṇanāvidhau || 39.102 ||
śatānīti vijānīyāt saṃjñitāni maharṣibhiḥ|
kalpasaṃkhyā pravṛttasya parārddhaṃ brahmaṇaḥ smṛtam || 39.103 ||
tāvaccheṣo'pi kālo'sya tasyānte pratisṛjyate|
para eṣa parārddhañca saṃkhyātaḥ saṃkhyayā mayā || 39.104 ||
yasmādasya paraṃ vīryaṃ paramāyuḥ parantapaḥ|
parā śaktiḥ paro dharmmaḥ parā vidyā parā dhṛtiḥ || 39.105 ||
paraṃ brahma paraṃ jñānaṃ paramaiśvaryameva ca|
tasmātparataraṃ bhūtaṃ brahmaṇo'nyanna vidyate || 39.106 ||
pare sthito hyeṣa paraḥ sarvārtheṣu tataḥ paraḥ|
saṃkhyātastu paro brahmā tasyārddhaṃ tu parārddhatā || 39.107 ||
saṃkhyeyaṃ cāpyasaṃkhyeyaṃ satataṃ cāpi taṃ trikam|
saṃkhyeyaṃ saṃkhyayā dṛṣṭamapārārddhādvibhāṣyate || 39.108 ||
rāśau dṛṣṭe na saṃkhyāsti tadasaṃkhyasya lakṣaṇam|
ānantyaṃ sikatākhyeṣu dṛṣṭavān pañcalakṣaṇam || 39.109 ||
īśvaraistatprasaṃkhyātaṃ śuddhatvāddivyadṛṣṭibhiḥ|
evaṃ jñānapratiṣṭhatvāt sarvvaṃ brahmānupaśyati || 39.110 ||
etacchrutvā tu te sarve naimiṣeyāstapasvinaḥ|
bāṣpaparyyākulākṣāstu praharṣādghadghadasvarāḥ || 39.111 ||
papracchurmātariśvānaṃ sarvve te brahmavādinaḥ|
brahmalokastu bhagavan yāvanmātrāntaraḥ prabho || 39.112 ||
yojanāgreṇa saṃkhyātaḥ sādhanaṃ yojanasya tu|
krośasya ca parīmāṇaṃ śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ || 39.113 ||
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā mātariśvā vinītavāk|
uvāca madhuraṃ vākyaṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathākramam || 39.114 ||
etadvo'haṃ pravakṣyāmi śrṛṇudhvaṃ me vivakṣitam|
avyaktādvyaktabhāgo vai mahāsthūlo vibhāṣyate || 39.115 ||
daśaiva mahatāṃ bhāgā bhūtādiḥ sthūla ucyate|
daśabhāgādhikaṃ cāpi bhūtādiḥ paramāṇukaḥ || 39.116 ||
paramāṇuḥ susūkṣmastu bāvagrāhyo na cakṣuṣā|
yadabhedyatamaṃ loke vijñeyaṃ paramāṇu tat || 39.117 ||
jālāntaragataṃ bhānoryatsūkṣmaṃ dṛśyate rajaḥ|
prathamaṃ tatpramāṇānāṃ paramāṇuṃ pracakṣate || 39.118 ||
aṣṭānāṃ paramāṇūnāṃ samavāyo yadā bhavet |
trasareṇuḥ samākhyātastatpadmaraja ucyate || 39.119 ||
trasareṇavaśca ye'pyaṣṭau rathareṇustu sa smṛtaḥ |
te'pyaṣṭau samavāyasthā bālāgraṃ tatsmṛtaṃ budhaiḥ || 39.120 ||
bālāgrāṇyaṣṭa likṣā syādyūkā taccāṣṭakaṃ bhavet|
yūkāṣṭakaṃ yavaṃ prāhuraṅgulantu yavāṣṭakam || 39.121 ||
dvādaśāṅgulaparvvāṇi vitastisthānamucyate|
ratniścāṅgulaparvāṇi vijñeyo hyekaviṃśatiḥ || 39.122 ||
catvāri viṃśatiścaiva hastaḥ syādaṅgulāni tu|
kiṣkurdviratnirvijñeyo dvicatvāriṃśadaṅgulaḥ || 39.123 ||
ṣaṇṇavatyaṅgulañcaiva dhanurāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ|
etadgavyūtisaṃkhyāyāṃ pādānāṃ dhanuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ || 39.124 ||
dhanurdaṇḍo yugaṃ nālī tulyānyetānyathāṅgulaiḥ|
dhanuṣastriśataṃ nalvamāhuḥ saṃkhyāvido janāḥ || 39.125 ||
dhanuḥsahasre dve cāpi gavyūtirupadiśyate|
aṣṭau dhanuḥsahasrāṇi yojanantu vidhīyate || 39.126 ||
etena dhanuṣā caiva yojanaṃ tu samāpyate|
etatsahasraṃ vijñeyaṃ śakrakrośāntarantathā || 39.127 ||
yojanānāntu saṃkhyātaṃ saṃkhyājñānaviśāradaiḥ|
etena yojanāgreṇa śrṛṇudhvaṃ brahmaṇo'ntaram || 39.128 ||
mahītalātsahasrāṇāṃ śatādūrddhvaṃ divākaraḥ|
divākarātsahasreṇa tāvadūrddhvaṃ niśākaraḥ || 39.129 ||
pūrṇaṃ śatasahasrantu yojanānāṃ niśākarāt|
nakṣatramaṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnamupariṣṭātprakāśate || 39.130 ||
śataṃ sahasraṃ saṃkhyāto merurdviguṇitaṃ punaḥ|
grahāntaramathaikaikamūrddhvaṃ nakṣatramaṇḍalāt || 39.131 ||
tārāgrahāṇāṃ sarvveṣāmadhastāccarate budhaḥ|
tasyorddhvañcarate śukrastasmādūrddhvaṃ ca lohitaḥ || 39.132 ||
tato bṛhaspatiścorddhvaṃ tasmādūrddhvaṃ śanaiścaraḥ|
ūrddhvaṃ śatasahasrantu yojanānāṃ śanaiścarāt || 39.133 ||
saptarṣimaṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnamupariṣṭātprakāśate|
ṛṣibhistu sahasrāṇāṃ śatādūrddhvaṃ vibhāvyate || 39.134 ||
yo'sau tārāmaye divye vimāne hrasvarūpake|
uttānapādaputro'sau meḍhibhūto dhruvo divi || 39.135 ||
trailokyasyaiṣa utsedho vyākhyāto yojanairmayā|
manvantareṣu devānāmijyā yatraiva laukikī || 39.136 ||
varṇāśramebhya ijyā tu loke'sminyā pravarttate|
sarveṣāṃ devayonīnāṃ sthitihetuḥ savai smṛtaḥ || 39.137 ||
trailokyametadvayākhyātamata ūrddhvaṃ nibodhata|
dhruvā dūrddhvaṃ maharloko yasmiste kalpavāsinaḥ|
ekayojanakoṭī sā ityevaṃ niścayaṃ gatam || 39.138 ||
dve koṭyau tu maharlokādyasmiṃste kalpavāsinaḥ|
yatra te brahmaṇaḥ putrā dakṣādyāḥ sādhakāḥ smṛtāḥ || 39.139 ||
vairājā yatra te devā bhūtadāhavivarjitāḥ || 39.140 ||
ṣaḍguṇantu tapolokātsatyalokāntaraṃ smṛtam|
apunarmārakāmānāṃ brahmalokaḥ sa ucyate || 39.141 ||
yasmānna cyavate bhūyo brahmāṇaṃ sa upāsate |
ekakoṭiryojanānāṃ pañcāśanniyutāni tu || 39.142 ||
ūrddhvaṃ bhāgastato'ṇḍasya brahmalokātparaḥ smṛtaḥ|
caturaścaiva koṭyastu niyutāḥ pañcaṣaṣṭi ca || 39.143 ||
eṣo'rddhaṃśapracāro'sya gatyantaścāparaḥ smṛtaḥ|
dhravāgrametadvayākhyātaṃ yojanāgrādyathāśrutam || 39.144 ||
adhogatīnāṃ vakṣyāmi bhūtānāṃ sthānakalpanām|
gacchanti ghorakarmmāṇaḥ prāṇino yatra karmmabhiḥ || 39.145 ||
narako rauravo rodhaḥ sūkarastāla eva ca|
taptakumbho mahājvālaḥ śabalo'tha vimocanaḥ || 39.146 ||
kṛmī ca kṛmibhakṣaśca lālābhakṣo viśaṃsanaḥ |
adhaḥśirāḥ pūyavaho rudhirāndhastathaiva ca || 39.147 ||
tathā vaitaraṇaṃ kṛṣṇamasipatravanaṃ tathā|
agnijvālo mahāghoraḥ saṃdaṃśo'tha śvabhojanaḥ ||39.148 ||
tamaśca kṛṣṇasūtraśca lohaścāpyasijastathā|
apratiṣṭo'tha vīcyaśvanarakā hyevamādayaḥ || 39.149 ||
tāmasā narakāḥ sarve yamasya viṣaye sthitāḥ|
yeṣu duṣkṛtakarmāṇaḥ patantīha pṛthakpṛthak || 39.150
bhūmeradhastātte sarve rauravādyāḥ prakīrttitāḥ|
raurave kūṭasākṣī tu mithyā yaścābhiśaṃsati|
krūragrahe pakṣavādī hyasatyaḥ patate naraḥ || 39.151 ||
rodhe goghno brūṇahā ca hyagnidātā purasya ca|
sūkare brahmahā majjetsurāpaḥ svarṇataskaraḥ || 39.152 ||
tāle patetkṣatriyahā hatvā vaiśyañca durgatim|
brahamahatyāñca yaḥ kuryādyaśca syādgurutalpagaḥ || 39.153 ||
taptakumbhī svasāgāmī tathā rājabhaṭaśca yaḥ|
sādhvīvikrayakarttā ca yastu bhaktaṃ parityajet|
mahājvāle duhitaraṃ snuṣāṃ gacchati yastu vai || 39.155 ||
gurūṃścaivāvamanyante vākkrośaistāḍayanti ca || 39.156 ||
agamyagāmīca naro narakaṃ śabalaṃ vrajet|
vimohe patite caure maryādāṃ yo bhinatti vai || 39.157 ||
duradhvaṃ kurute yastu kīṭalohaṃ prapadyate|
devabrāhmaṇavidveṣṭā gurūṇāñcāpyapūjakaḥ|
ratnaṃ dūṣayate yastu kṛmibhakṣyaṃ prapadyate || 39.158 ||
paryyaśnāti ya eko'nyo brāhmaṇīṃ suhṛdaḥ sutām|
lālābhakṣe sa patati durgandhe narake gataḥ || 39.159 ||
kāṇḍakarttā kulālaśca niṣkaharttā cikitsakaḥ|
ārā meṣvagnidātā yaḥ patate sa viśaṃsane || 39.160 ||
asatpratigrahī yaśca tathaivāyājyayājakaḥ|
nakṣatrairjīvito yaśca naro gacchatyadhomukham || 39.161 ||
yaḥ kukkuṭāni badhnāti mārjārānsūkarāṃśca tān|
pakṣiṇaśca mṛgāñchāgānso'pyenaṃ narakaṃ vrajet || 39.163 ||
ājīviko māhiṣakastathā cakradhvajī ca yaḥ|
raṅgopajīviko vipraḥ śākunigrāma yājakaḥ || 39.164 ||
agāradāhī garadaḥ kuṇḍāśī somavikrayī|
surāpo māṃsabhakṣaśca tathā ca paśughātakaḥ || 39.165 ||
viśa(śva)stā mahiṣādīnāṃ mṛga hantā tathaiva ca|
parvakāraśca sūcī ca yaśca syānmitraghātakaḥ|
rudhirāndhe patantyete evamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ || 39.166 ||
patanti narake ghore viṅ‌bhuje nātra saṃśayaḥ || 39.167 ||
mṛṣāvādī naro yaśca tathā prākrośako'śubhaḥ|
patettu narake ghoro mūtrākīrṇe sa pāpakṛt || 39.168 ||
madhugrāhābihantāro yanti vaitaraṇīṃ narāḥ|
unmattāścittabhagnāśca śaucācāravivarjjitāḥ || 39.169 ||
krodhanā duḥkhadāścaiva kuhakāḥ kṛṣṭagāminaḥ|
asi patravane chedī tathā hyaurabhrikāśca ye|
karttanaiśca nikṛṣyante mṛgavyādhāḥ sudāruṇaiḥ || 39.170 ||
āśramapratyavasitā agnijvāle patanti vai|
bhaujyante śyāma śabalairayastuṇḍaiśca vāyasaiḥ || 39.171 ||
ijyāyāṃ vratamālopātsandaṃśe narake patet|
skandante yadi vā svapne vratino brahmacāriṇaḥ || 39.172 ||
putrairadhyāpitā ye ca putrairājñāpitāśca ye|
tesarve narakaṃ yānti niyatantu śvabhojane || 39.173 ||
varṇāśramavirūddhāni krodhaharṣasamanvitāḥ|
karmāṇi ye tu kurvanti sarve nirayagāminaḥ || 39.174 ||
upariṣṭātsito ghora uṣṇātmā rauravo mahān|
sudāruṇastu śītātmā tasyādhastāttapaḥ smṛtaḥ || 39.175 ||
evamādi krameṇaiva varṇyamānānnibodhata|
bhūmeradhastātsaptaiva narakāḥ parikīrtitāḥ || 39.176 ||
adharmasūnavaste syurandhatāmisrakādayaḥ|
rauravaḥ prathamasteṣāṃ mahā raurava eva ca || 39.177 ||
asyādhaḥ punarapyanyaḥ śītastapa iti smṛtaḥ|
tṛtīyaḥ kālasūtraḥ syānmahāhavividhiḥ smṛtaḥ || 39.178 ||
apratiṣṭha ścaturthaḥ syādavīcī pañcamaḥ smṛtaḥ|
lohapṛṣṭhastamasteṣāmavidheyastu saptamaḥ || 39.179 ||
ghoratvādrauravaḥ proktaḥ sāmbhako dahanaḥ smṛtaḥ|
sudāruṇastu śītātmā tasyādhastāttapo'dhamaḥ || 39.180 ||
sarpo nikṛntanaḥ proktaḥ kālasūtreti dāruṇaḥ|
apratiṣṭe sthitirnāsti bhramastasminsudāruṇaḥ || 39.181 ||
avīcirdāruṇaḥ prokto yantrasaṃpīḍanācca saḥ|
tasmātsudāruṇo lohaḥ karmmaṇāṃ kṣayaṇācca saḥ || 39.182 ||
tathābhūto śarīratvādavidhibhyastu sa smṛtaḥ|
pīḍabandhavadhāsaṅgādapratīkāralakṣaṇaḥ || 39.183 ||
ūrddhvaṃ sailamitāste tu nirālokāśca te smṛtāḥ|
duḥkhotkarṣastu sarveṣu hyadharmasya nimittataḥ || 39.184 ||
ūrddhvaṃ lokaiḥ samāvetau nirālokau ca tāvubhau|
kūṭāṅgārapramāṇaiśca śarīrī mūtranāyakaḥ || 39.185 ||
upabhogasamarthaistu sadyo jāyanti karmabhiḥ|
duḥkha prakarṣaścogratvaṃ teṣu sarveṣu vai smṛtaḥ || 39.186 ||
yātanāścāpyasaṃkhyeyā nārakāṇāṃ tathā smṛtāḥ|
duḥkhotkarṣastu sarveṣu hyadharmasya nimittataḥ || 39.187 ||
tiryagyonau prasūyante karmaśeṣe gate tataḥ|
devāśca nārakāścaiva hyūrddhvaṃ cādhaśca saṃsthitāḥ || 39.188 ||
dharmādharmanimittena sadyo jāyanti mūrttayaḥ|
upabhogārthamutpattiraupapattikakarmataḥ || 39.189 ||
paśyanti nārakāndevā hyadhovakrān hyadhogatān|
nārakāśca tathā devān sarvānpaśyantyadho mukhān || 39.190 ||
anagramūlatā yasmāddhāraṇāśca svabhāvataḥ|
tasmādūrddhvamadhobhāvo lokāloke na vidyate || 39.191 ||
eṣā svābhāvikī saṃjñā lokāloke pravarttate|
athābruvanpunarvāyuṃ brāhmaṇāḥ satriṇastadā || 39.192 ||
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ lokālokanivāsinām|
saṃsāre saṃsarantīha yāvantaḥ prāṇinaśca tān || 39.193 ||
sahkhyayā parisaṅkhyāya tataḥ prabrūhi kṛtsnaśaḥ|
ṛṣīṇāṃ tadvacaḥ śrutvā māruto vākyamabravīt || 39.194 ||
na divyacakṣuṣā jñātuṃ śakyā jñānena vā punaḥ|
cakṣuṣā vai prasaṃkhyātumato hyante narādhipaḥ || 39.196 ||
anādhyānādavedyatvānnaiva praśno vidhīyate|
brahmaṇā saṃjñitaṃ yattu saṃkhyayā tannibodhata || 39.197 ||
yaḥ sahasratamo bhāgaḥ sthāvarāṇāṃ bhavediha|
pārthivāḥ kṛmayastāvatsaṃsekādyeṣu sambhavāḥ || 39.198 ||
saṃsekajānāmbhāgena sahasreṇaiva sammitāḥ|
audakā jantavaḥ sarve niścayāttadvicāritam || 39.199 ||
sahasreṇaiva bhāgena satvānāṃ salilaukasām |
vihaṅgamāstu vijñeyā laukikāste ca sarvaśaḥ || 39.200 ||
yaḥ sahasratamo bhāgasteṣāṃ vai pakṣiṇāṃ bhavet|
paśavastatsamā jñeyā laukikāstu catuṣpadāḥ || 39.201 ||
catuṣpadānāṃ sarveṣāṃ sahasreṇaiva saṃmatāḥ |
sahasreṇaiva bhāgena dhārmmikebhyo divaṅgatāḥ|
yaḥ sahasratamo bhāgo dhārmmikāṇāṃ bhaveddivi|
saṃmitāstena bhāgena mokṣiṇastāvadeva hi || 39.204 ||
svargopapādakaistulyā yātanā sthānavāsinaḥ|
patitā ścūrṇamuddeśāddurātmāno mriyanti ye|
raurave tāmase hyete śītoṣṇaṃ prāpnuvanti te || 39.205 ||
vedanākaṭukāstabdhā yātanā sthānamāgatāḥ|
uṣṇastu rauravo jñeyastejo ghorarasātmakaḥ || 39.206 ||
tato ghanātmikaścāpi śītātmā satataṃ tapaḥ|
evaṃ sudurlabhāḥ santaḥ svarge ca dhārmmikā narāḥ || 39.207 ||
eṣā saṃkhyā kṛtā saṃkhyā īśvareṇa svayambhuvā|
gaṇanā vinivṛttaiṣā saṅkhyā brāhmī ca mānuṣī || 39.208 ||
maho janastapaḥ satyaṃ bhūto bhāvyo bhavastathā|
uktā hyete tvayā lokā lokānāmantareṇa ca|
lokāntarañca yādṛgvai tanno brūhi yathātatham || 39.209 ||
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā ṛṣīṇāmūrddhvaretasām|
sa vāyurdṛṣṭatattvārtha idantattvamuvāca ha || 39.210
vyaktaṃ tarkeṇa paśyanti yogātpratyakṣadarśinaḥ|
pratyāhāreṇa dhyānena tapasā ca kriyātmanaḥ || 39.211 ||
ṛbhuḥ sanatkumārādyāḥ sambuddhāḥ śuddhabuddhayaḥ|
vyapetaśokā virajāḥ santo brahmevasattamāḥ || 39.212 ||
akṣayāḥ prītisaṃyuktā brahme tiṣṭanti yoginaḥ|
ṛṣīṇāṃ vālakhilyānāṃ tairyathāddṛtamīśvaraiḥ || 39.213 ||
yathā caiva mayā dṛṣṭaṃ sānnidhyantatra kurvatā|
anahyasatkṛtārthānāmālayaṃ ceśvarasya yat || 39.214 ||
īśvaraḥ paramāṇutvādbhāvagrāhyo manīṣiṇām |
jñānaṃ vairāgyamaiśvaryantapaḥ satyaṃ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ || 39.215 ||
draṣṭṛtvamātmasambandhamadhiṣṭānatvameva ca|
avyayāni daśaitāni tasmiṃstiṣṭhati śaṅkare || 39.216 ||
vibutvātkhalu yogāgnirbrahmaṇo'nugraherataḥ|
sa lokavigraho bhūtvā sāhāyyamupatiṣṭhate || 39.217 ||
akṣaraṃ dhruvamavyagramaṣṭamantvaupasargikam|
tasyeśvarasya yanmātrasthānaṃ māyāmayaṃ param || 39.218 ||
māyayā kṛtamācaṣṭe māyī devo maheśvaraḥ|
devānāmupasaṃhārastatpramāṇaṃ hi kīrttyate || 39.219 ||
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca bruvato me nibodhata|
trayodaśaiva koṭyastu niyutā daśa pañca ca|
bhūrlokādbrahmaloko vaiyojanaiḥ samprakīrttyate || 39.220 ||
ekayojanakoṭī tu pañcāśanniyutāni ca|
ūrddhvaṃ bhāgavatāṇḍantu brahmalokātparaṃ smṛtam || 39.221 ||
eṣorddhvagapracārastu gatyantañca tataḥ smṛtam |
nityā hyaparisaṃkhyeyāḥ parasparaguṇāśrayāḥ || 39.222 ||
sūkṣmāḥ prasavadharmiṇyastataḥ prakṛtayaḥ smṛtāḥ|
yebhyo'dhikarttā saṃjajño kṣetrajño brahmasaṃjñitaḥ || 39.223 ||
tāsu prakṛtimatsūkṣmamadhiṣṭātṛtvamavyayam|
anutpādyaṃ parandhāma paramāṇu pareśayam || 39.224 ||
akṣayaścāpyanuhyaśca amūrttirmūrttimānasau|
prādurbhāvastirobhāvaḥ sthitiścaivāpyanugrahaḥ || 39.225 ||
vidhiranyairanaupamyaḥ paramāṇurmaheśvaraḥ|
satejā eṣa tamaso yaḥ parastātprakāśakaḥ || 39.226 ||
yadaṇḍamāsītsauvarṇaṃ prathamantvaupasargikam|
bṛhataṃ sarvatovṛttamīśvarādvyavajāyata || 39.227 ||
īśvarādbījanirbhedaḥ kṣetrajño bīja īṣyate|
yoniṃ prakṛtimācaṣṭe sā ca nārāyaṇātmikā || 39.228 ||
viburlokasya sṛṣṭyarthaṃ lokasaṃsthānameva ca|
sannisargaḥ sa tanvā ca lokadhāturmahātmanaḥ || 39.229 ||
purastādbrahmalokasya hyaṇḍādarvākca brahmaṇaḥ|
tayormadhye puraṃ divyaṃ sthānaṃ yasya manomayam || 39.230 ||
tadvigrahavataḥ sthānamīśvarasyāmitaujasaḥ|
śivaṃ nāma puraṃ tatra śaraṇaṃ janmabhīruṇām || 39.231 ||
sahasrāṇāṃ śataṃ pūrṇaṃ yojanānāṃ dvijottamāḥ|
abhyantare tu vistīrṇaṃ mahīmaṇḍalasaṃsthitam || 39.232 ||
madhyāhnārkaprakāśena paratejo'bhimardinā|
śātakaumbhena mahatā prākāreṇārkavarcasā || 39.233 ||
dvāraiścaturbhiḥ sauvarṇairmuktādāmavibhūṣitaiḥ|
tapanīyanibhaiḥ śubhrairgāḍhaṃ sukṛtaveṣṭanam || 39.234 ||
taccākāśe puraṃ ramyaṃ divyaṃ ghaṇṭādināditam|
sahasrāṇāṃ śataṃ pūrṇaṃ yojanānāṃ diśo daśa || 39.236 ||
sahasra pādaḥ prāsādastapanīyamayaḥ śubhaḥ|
anupameyai ratnaiśca sarvataḥ sa vibhūṣitaḥ || 39.248 ||
sphaṭikaiścandrasaṅkāśairvaiḍhūryaiḥ somasaṃprabhaiḥ|
bālasūryyaprabhaiścaiva sauvarṇaiścāgnisaṃprabhaiḥ || 39.249 ||
nityā hyaparisaṅkhyātāḥ parasparaguṇāśrayāḥ |
tasya śākho viśākhaśca naigameyaśca cāṣṭavān|
śrūyatāṃ devadevasya bhaviṣyāścaryamuttamam || 39.284 ||
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā vāyurvākyaṃ jagāda ha |
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi ye tatra prati vāsinaḥ|
ramye puravaraśreṣṭe tasminvaihāyabhūmiṣu || 39.301 ||
nānāratnavicitreṣu patākābahuleṣu ca|
sarvakāmasamṛddheṣu vanopavanaśobhiṣu || 39.302 ||
rājateṣu mahānteṣu śātakaumbhamayeṣu ca|
sandhyābhrasannikāśeṣu kailāsapratimeṣu ca || 39.303 ||
iṣṭaiḥ śabdādibhirbhāgairye bhavasyānusāriṇaḥ |
prāsādavara puṣpeṣu teṣu modanti suvratāḥ || 39.304 ||
brahmaghoṣairaviratāḥ kathāśca vividhāḥ śubhāḥ |
gītavāditraghoṣāśca saṃstavāśca samantataḥ || 39.305 ||
saṃhatāścaivamatulā nānāśrayakṛtāstathā|
evamādīni varttante teṣāṃ prāsādamūrddhani || 39.306 ||
sahasrapādaḥ prāsādastapanīyamayaḥ śubhaḥ|
anaupamyairvarai ratnaiḥ sarvataḥ paribhūṣitaḥ || 39.307 ||
sphaṭikaiścandrasaṅkāśairvaiḍhūryamaṇisamprabhaiḥ|
bālasūryamayaiścāpi sauvarṇaiścāgnisamprabhaiḥ || 39.308 ||
cukruśuṛṣayaḥ śrutvā naimiṣeyāstapasvinaḥ|
āpannasaṃśayāścemaṃ vākyamūcuḥ samīraṇam || 39.309 ||
ke tu tatra mahātmāno ye bhavasyānusāriṇaḥ|
anugrāhyatamāḥ samyak pramodante purottame|
ṛṣīṇāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā vāyurvākyamathābravīt || 39.310 ||
śrūyatāṃ devadevasya bhaktiryairanukalpitā|
hrīmantaḥ sūrjitā dāntāḥ śauryayuktā hyalolupāḥ || 39.311 ||
karmaṇā manasā vācā viśuddhenāntarātmanā|
ananyamanaso bhūtvā prapannā ye maheśvaram || 39.313 ||
tairlabdhaṃ rudrasālokyaṃ śāśvataṃ padamavyayam|
bhavasya rūpasādṛśyaṃ nītāścaiva hyanuttamam || 39.314 ||
vaiśvānaramukhāḥ sarve viśvarūpāḥ kaparddinaḥ |
nīlakaṇṭāḥ sitagrīvāstīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāstrilocanāḥ || 39.315 ||
arddhacandrakṛto'ṇīṣā jaṭāmukuṭadhāriṇaḥ |
sarve daśabhujā vīrāḥ padmāntara sugandhinaḥ || 39.316 ||
taruṇādityasaṅkāśāḥ sarve te pītavāsasaḥ |
pinākapāṇayaḥ sarvve śvetagovṛṣavāhanāḥ || 39.317 ||
śriyānvitāḥ kuṇḍalino muktāhāravibhūṣitāḥ|
tejaso'bhyadhikā devaiḥ sarvajñāḥ sarvadarśinaḥ || 39.318 ||
vibhajya bahudhātmānaṃ jarāmṛtyuvivarjitāḥ|
krīḍante vividhairbhāvairbhogān prāpya sudurlabhān || 39.319 ||
svacchandagatayaḥ siddhāḥ siddhaiścānyaurvibodhitāḥ|
ekādaśānāṃ rudrāṇāṃ koṭyo'nekamahātmanām || 39.320 ||
ebhiḥ saha mahātmā hi devadevo maheśvaraḥ|
bhaktānukampī bhagavānmodate pārvatīpriyaḥ || 39.321 ||
nāhanteṣāntu rudrāṇāṃ bhavasya ca mahātmanaḥ|
nānātvamanupaśyāmi satyametadbravīmi vaḥ || 39.322 ||
atha te ṛṣayaḥ sarve divākarasamaprabhāḥ|
śrutvemāṃ paramāṃ puṇyāṃ kathāṃ traiyambakīṃ tataḥ || 39.323 ||
bhṛśañcānugrahaṃ prāpya harṣaṃ caivāpyanuttamam|
sambhāvayitvā cāpyenāṃ vāyumūcurmahābalam || 39.324 ||
samīraṇa mahābhāga hyasmākaṃ ca tvayā vibho|
īśvarasyottamaṃ puṇyamaṣṭamantvaupasargikam || 39.325 ||
tasya sthānaṃ pramāṇañca yathāvatparikīrttitam|
yo gandhena samṛddhaṃ vai paramaṃ paramātmanaḥ || 39.326 ||
mahādevasya māhātmyaṃ durvijñeyaṃ surairapi |
svena māhātmyayogena sahasrasyāmitaujasaḥ || 39.327 ||
yasya bhakteṣvasaṃmoho hyanukampārthameva ca|
brāhmalakṣmyā svayaṃ juṣṭā yā sāpratimaśālinī || 39.328 ||
vibhūtirbhrājate'tyarthaṃ devadevasya veśmani || 39.329 ||
mahādevasya tulyānāṃ rudrāṇāntu mahātmanām|
tatsarvaṃ nikhilenedaṃ vaktrādamṛtanisravam || 39.330 ||
apītvā khalu sarvasya bhaktyāsmābhistu suvratāḥ|
nāsti kiñcidavijñeyamanyaccaivānugāminaḥ|
praśnaṃ devavara prāṇa yathāvadvaktumarhasi || 39.331 ||
sa khalūvāca bhagavānkiṃ bhūyo varttayāmyaham|
kiṃ mayā caiva vaktavyaṃ tadvadiṣyāmi suvratāḥ || 39.332 ||
ādityāḥ pāripārśveyāḥ siṃhā vai krodhavikramāḥ|
vaiśvānarā bhūtagaṇā vyāghrāścaivānugāminaḥ || 39.333 ||
ābhūtasaṃplave ghore sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ kṣaye|
kimavasthā bhavantyete tanno brūhi yathārthavat || 39.334 ||
vijñāteśvarasadbhāvamavyaktaṃ prabhavaṃ tathā || 39.336 ||
tatra pūrvagatāsteṣu kumārā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ|
sanakaśca sanandaśca tṛtīyaśca sanātanaḥ || 39.337 ||
voḍhuśca kapilasteṣāmāsuriśca mahāyaśāḥ|
muniḥ pañcaśikhaścaiva ye cānye'pyevamādayaḥ || 39.338 ||
tataḥ kāle vyatikrānte kalpānāṃ paryaye gate|
mahābhūtavināśānte pralaye pratyupasthite || 39.339 ||
anekarudrakoṭyastu yāḥ prasannā maheśvarī |
śabdādīnviṣayānbhogānsatyasyāṣṭavidhaśrayāt || 39.340 ||
praviśya sarvabhūtāni jñānayuktena tejasā|
vaihāyapadamavyagraṃ bhūtānāmanukampayā || 39.341 ||
tatra yānti mahātmānaḥ paramāṇuṃ maheśvaram|
taranti sumahāvarttāṃ janmamṛtyūdakāṃ nadīm || 39.342 ||
tataḥ paśyanti śarvāṇaṃ paraṃ brahmāṇameva ca|
devyā vai sahitāḥ sapta yā devyaḥ parikīrttitāḥ || 39.343 ||
yattatsahasraṃ siṃhānāmādityānāṃ tathaiva ca|
vaiśvānarabhūtabhavyavyāghrāścaivānugāminaḥ || 39.344 ||
āveśyātmani tānsarvānsaṃkhyāyopadravāṃstathā|
lokān sapta imānsarvvānmahābhūtāni pañca ca || 39.345 ||
viṣṇunā saha saṃyuktaṃ karoti vikaroti ca|
sa rudro yaḥ sāmamayastathaiva ca yajurmayaḥ || 39.346 ||
sa eṣa otaḥ protaśca bahirantaśca niścayāt|
eko hi bhagavānnātho hyanādiścāntakṛddvijāḥ || 39.347 ||
tataste ṛṣayaḥ sarve divākarasamaprabhāḥ|
karmaṇā manasā vācā viśuddhenāntarātmanā |
ananyamanaso bhūtvā prapadyante maheśvaram || 39.349 ||
vratopavāsaniratāḥ sarvabhūtadayāparāḥ|
yogaṃ hyanupamandivyaṃ prāptaṃ taiśchinnasaṃśayaiḥ || 39.350 ||
prapadya parayā bhaktyā jñānayuktena cetasā|
tairlabdhaṃ rudrasālokyaṃ śāśvataṃ padamavyayam || 39.351 ||
yaḥ paṭettapasā yukto vāyuproktāmimāṃ stutim|
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vāpi vaiśyo vā svakriyāparaḥ || 39.352 ||
amadyapaśca yaḥ śūdro bhavabhakto jitendriyaḥ || 39.353 ||
ābhūta saṃplavasthāyī hyapratīghātalakṣaṇaḥ|
gāṇapatyaṃ sa labhate sthānaṃ vā sarvakāmikam || 39.354 ||
madyapo madyapaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhūtasaṅghaiśca modate|
so'rcyamāno mahīpṛṣṭo marttyānāṃ varado bhavet|
iti hovāca bhagavānvāyurvākyamidaṃ varaḥ || 39.355 ||
pratyāhāraṃ pravakṣyāmi parasyānte svayambhuvaḥ।
brahmaṇaḥ sthitikāle tu kṣīṇe tasmiṃstadā prabhoḥ ॥ 2.40.1 ॥
yathedaṃ kurute'dhyātmaṃ susūkṣmaṃ viśvamīśvaraḥ ।
avyaktāngrasate vyaktaṃ pratyāhāre ca kṛtsnaśaḥ ॥ 2.40.2 ॥
paraṃ tadanukalpānāmapūrṇe kalpasaṅkṣaye।
upasthite mahāghore hyapratyakṣe tu kasyacit ॥ 2.40.3 ॥
ante drumasya yamprāpte paścimasya manostadā ।
ante kaliyuge tasminkṣīṇe saṃhāra ucyate ॥ 2.40.4 ॥
samprakṣāle tadā vṛtte pratyāhāre hyupasthite।
pratyāhāre tadā tasmin bhūtatanmātrasaṃkṣaye ॥ 2.40.5 ॥
mahadādervikārasya viśeṣāntasya saṃkṣaye।
svabhāvakārite tasminpravṛtte pratisañcare ॥ 2.40.6 ॥
āpo grasanti vai pūrvvaṃ bhūmergandhātmakaṃ guṇam।
āttagandhā tato bhūmiḥ pralayatvāya kalpate ।
praviṣṭe gandhatanmātre toyāvasthā dharā bhavet ॥ 2.40.7 ॥
āpastadā pranaṣṭā vai vegavatyo mahāsvanāḥ।
sarvamāpūrayitvedaṃ tiṣṭhanti vicaranti ca ॥ 2.40.8 ॥
apāmasti guṇo yastu jyotiṣe līyate rasaḥ।
naśyantyāpastadānte ca rasatanmātrasaṅkṣayāt ॥ 2.40.9 ॥
tejasā saṃhṛtarasā jyotiṣṭvaṃ prāpnuvantyuta ।
graste ca salile tejaḥ sarvvatomukhamīkṣyate ॥ 2.40.10 ॥
athāgniḥ sarvato vyāpta ādatte tajjalantadā।
sarvamāpūryyate'rcirbhistadā jagadidaṃ śanaiḥ ॥ 2.40.11 ॥
arcirbhiḥ santate tasmiṃstiryagūrddhvamadhastataḥ ।
jyotiṣo'pi guṇaṃ rūpaṃ vāyuranti prakāśakam।
pralīyate tadā tasmindīpārciriva mārute ॥ 2.40.12 ॥
pranaṣṭe rūpatanmātre hṛtarūpo vibhāvasuḥ।
upaśāmyati tejo hi vāyunā dhūyate mahat ॥ 2.40.13 ॥
nirāloke tadā loke vāyubhūte ca tejasi।
tatastu mūlamāsādya vāyuḥ sambhavamātmanaḥ ॥ 2.40.14 ॥
ūrddhvaṃ cādhaśca tiryakca dodhavīti diśo daśa ।
vāyorapi guṇaṃ sparśamākāśaṃ grasate ca tat ॥ 2.40.15 ॥
praśāmyati tadā vāyuḥ khantu tiṣṭhatyanāvṛtam।
arūpamarasasparghamagandhaṃ na ca mūrtimat ॥ 2.40.16 ॥
sarvamāpūrayannādaiḥ sumahattatprakāśate।
śabdamātraṃ tadākāśaṃ sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati।
tantu śabdaguṇantasya bhūtādiṃ grasate punaḥ ॥ 2.40.18 ॥
bhūtendriyeṣu yughapadbhūtādau saṃsthiteṣu vai।
abhimānātmako hyeṣa bhūtādistāmasaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.40.19 ॥
bhūtādiṃ grasate cāpi mahānvai buddhilakṣaṇaḥ।
mahānātmā tu vijñeyaḥ saṃkalpo vyavasāyakaḥ ॥ 2.40.20 ॥
buddhirmanaśca liṅgaśca mahānakṣara eva ca।
paryāyavācakaiḥ śabdaistamāhustattvacintakāḥ ॥ 2.40.21 ॥
sampralīneṣu bhūteṣu guṇasāmye tamomaye।
vinivṛtte tadā sarge prakṛtyāvasthitena vai ।
tadādyantaparokṣatvā dadṛṣṭatvācca kasyacit ॥ 2.40.23 ॥
anākhyānādabodhatvādajñānājjñānināmapi।
āgatāgatikatvācca grahaṇaṃ tanna vidyate ॥ 2.40.24 ॥
bhāvagrāhyānumānācca cintayitvedamucyate।
sthite tu kāraṇe tasminnitye sadasadātmike ॥ 2.40.25 ॥
anirddeśyā pravṛttirvai svātmikā kāraṇe na tu।
evaṃ saptādayo'bhyastātkramātprakṛtayastu vai ॥ 2.40.26 ॥
pratyāhāre tadā sarge praviśyanti parasparam।
yenedamāvṛtaṃ sarvaṃ maṇḍalantu pralīyate ॥ 2.40.27 ॥
saptadvīpasamudrāntaṃ saptalokaṃ saparvatam।
udakāvaraṇaṃ yacca jyotiṣāṃ līyate tu tat ॥ 2.40.28 ॥
yattaijasaṃ cāvaraṇamākāśaṃ grasate tu tat।
yadvāyavyaṃ cāvaraṇamākāśaṃ grasate tu tat ॥ 2.40.29 ॥
ākāśāvaraṇaṃ yacca bhūtādirgrasate tu tat।
bhūtādiṃ grasate cāpi mahānvai buddhi lakṣaṇaḥ ॥ 2.40.30 ॥
mahāntaṃ grasate'vyaktaṃ guṇasāmyaṃ tataḥ param।
etau saṃhāravistārau brahmāvyaktau tataḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.40.31 ॥
sṛjate grasate caiva vikārānsargasaṃyame।
saṃhārakāryakaraṇāḥ saṃsiddhā jñāninastu ye ॥ 2.40.32 ॥
gatvā javañjavībhāve sthāneṣveṣu prasaṃyamān।
pratyāhāre viyujyante kṣetrajñāḥ karaṇaiḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.40.33 ॥
avyaktaṃ kṣetramityāhurbrahma kṣetrajña ucyate।
sādharmyavaidharmmakṛtasaṃyogo'nādimāṃstayoḥ ॥ 2.40.34 ॥
evaṃ sargeṣu vijñeyaṃ kṣetrajñeṣviha brāhmaṇāḥ ।
brahmaviccaiva vijñeyaḥ kṣetrajñānātpṛthakpṛthak ॥ 2.40.35 ॥
viṣayāviṣayatvañca kṣetrakṣetrajñayoḥ smṛtam।
brahmā tu viṣayo jñeyo'viṣayaḥ kṣetramucyate ॥ 2.40.36 ॥
kṣetrajñādhiṣṭitaṃ kṣetraṃ kṣetrajñārthaṃ pracakṣate।
bahutvācca śarīrāṇāṃ śarīrī bahudhā smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.40.37 ॥
avyūhā śaṅkarāccaiva jyotirvacca vyavasthitaḥ।
yasmātpratiśarīraṃ hi sukhaduḥkhopalabdhitā।
tasmātpuruṣanānātvaṃ vijñeyaṃ tu vijānatā ॥ 2.40.38 ॥
yadā pravarttate caiṣāṃ bhedānāṃ caiva saṃyamāḥ।
svabhāvakāritāḥ sarve kālena mahatā tadā ॥ 2.40.39 ॥
nivarttate tadā tasya sthitirāgaḥ svayambhuvaḥ।
sahasā yojyakaiḥ sarvairbrahmaloka nivāsibhiḥ ॥ 2.40.40 ॥
vinivṛtte tadā rāge sthitāvātmanivāsinām।
tatkālavāsināṃ teṣāṃ tadā taddoṣadarśinām ॥ 2.40.41 ॥
utpadyate'tha vairāgyamātmavāda praṇāśanam।
bhojyabhoktṛtvanānātve teṣāṃ tadbhavadarśinām ॥ 2.40.42 ॥
pṛthagjñānena kṣetrajñāstataste brahmalaukikāḥ।
prakṛtau karaṇā nītāḥ sarve nānāpradarśinaḥ ॥ 2.40.43 ॥
svātmanyevāvatiṣṭhante praśāntā darśanātmakāḥ।
śuddhā nirañjanāḥ sarve cetanācetanāstathā ॥ 2.40.44 ॥
tatraiva parinirvāṇāḥ smṛtā nāgāminastu te।
nirguṇatvānirātmānaḥ prakṛtyante vyatikramāt ॥ 2.40.45 ॥
ityevaṃ prākṛtaḥ proktaḥ pratisargaḥ svayambhuvaḥ।
bhidyante sarvabhūtānāṃ karaṇāni prasaṃyame ॥ 2.40.46 ॥
ityeṣa saṃyamaścaiva tattvānāṃ karaṇaiḥ saha।
tattvaprasaṃyamo hyeṣa smṛto hyāvarttako dvijāḥ ॥ 2.40.47 ॥
dharmādharmau tapo jñānaṃ śubhe satyānṛte tathā।
ūrddhva bhāvo hyadhobhāvo sukhaduḥkhe priyāpriye ॥ 2.40.48 ॥
sarvametatprayātasya guṇamātrātmakaṃ smṛtam।
nirindriyāṇāṃ ca tadā jñānināṃ yacchubhāśubham ॥ 2.40.49 ॥
prakṛtyāṃ caiva tatsarvaṃ puṇyaṃ pāpaṃ pratiṣṭhati।
jantūnāṃ pāpapuṇyantu prakṛtau yatpratiṣṭitam ।
avyakta sthāni tānyeva puṇyapāpāni jantavaḥ।
ye jayanti punardehe dehānyatve tathaiva ca ॥ 2.40.51 ॥
dharmādharmau tu jantūnāṃ guṇamātrātmakāvubhau ।
karaṇaiḥ svaiḥ pracīyete kāyatveneha jantubhiḥ ॥ 2.40.52 ॥
sucetanāḥ pralīyante kṣetrajñādhiṣṭitā guṇāḥ।
sarge ca pratisarge ca saṃsāre caiva jantavaḥ।
saṃyujyante viyujyante karaṇaiḥ sañcaranti ca ॥ 2.40.53 ॥
rājasī tāmasī caiva sātvikī caiva vṛttayaḥ।
guṇamātrāḥ pravarttante puruṣādhiṣṭitāstridhā ॥ 2.40.54 ॥
ūrddhvaṃ devātmakaṃ sattvamadhobhāgātmakaṃ tamaḥ।
tayoḥ pravarttakaṃ madye ihaivāvarttakaṃ rajaḥ ॥ 2.40.55 ॥
ityevaṃ parivarttante trayaḥ srotoguṇātmakāḥ।
lokeṣu sarvabhūtānāṃ tanna kāryaṃ vijānatā ॥ 2.40.56 ॥
avidyāpratyayārambhā ārabhyante hi mānavaiḥ ।
etāstu gatayastisraḥ śubhāḥ pāpātmikāḥ smṛtāḥ ॥ 2.40.57 ॥
tama sābhibhavājjanturyāthātathyaṃ na vindati।
atatddarśanātso'tha trividhaṃ badhyate tataḥ ॥ 2.40.58 ॥
prākṛtena ca bandhena tathā vaikārikena ca।
dakṣiṇābhistṛtīyena baddho'tyantaṃ vivarttate ॥ 2.40.59 ॥
ityete vai trayaḥ proktā bandhā hyajñānahetukāḥ।
anitye nityasaṃjñā ca duḥkhe ca sukhadarśanam ॥ 2.40.60 ॥
asve svamiti ca jñānamaśucau śuciniścayaḥ।
yeṣāmete manodoṣā jñānadoṣā viparyyayāt ॥ 2.40.61 ॥
rāgadveṣanivṛttiśca tajjñānaṃ samudāhṛtam।
ajñānaṃ tamaso mūlaṃ karmmadvayaphalaṃ rajaḥ।
karmmajastu punardeho mahāduḥkhaṃ pravarttate ॥ 2.40.62 ॥
śrotrajā netrajā caiva tvagjihvāghrāṇatastathā।
punarbhavakarī duḥkhā karmmaṇāṃ jāyate tu sā ॥ 2.40.63 ॥
satṛṣṇo'bhihito bālaḥ svakṛtaiḥ karmmaṇaḥ phalaiḥ।
tailapālīkavajjīvastatraiva pari varttate ॥ 2.40.64 ॥
tasmātsthūlamanarthānāmajñānamupadiśyate ।
taṃ śaktamavadhāryyaikaṃ jñāne yatnaṃ samācaret ॥ 2.40.65 ॥
jñānādvijayate sarvaṃ tyāgād‌buddhirvirajyate।
vairāgyācchuddhyate cāpi śuddhaḥ sattvena mucyate ॥ 2.40.66 ॥
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi rāgaṃ bhūtāpahāriṇam।
abhiṣaṅgāya yo yasmādviṣayo'pyavaśātmanaḥ ॥ 2.40.67 ॥
aniṣṭamabhiṣaṅgaṃ hi prītitāpaviṣādanam।
duḥkhalābhe na tāpañca sukhānusmaraṇaṃ tathā ॥ 2.40.68 ॥
ityeṣa vaiṣayo rāgaḥ sambhūtyāḥ kāraṇaṃ smṛtam।
brahmādau sthāvarānte vai saṃsāre hyādhibhautike।
ajñānapūrvakaṃ tasmādajñānantu vivarjayet ॥ 2.40.69 ॥
yasya cārṣaṃ na pramāṇaṃ śiṣṭācāraṃ tathaiva ca।
varṇāśramavirodhī yaḥ śiṣṭaśāstravirodhakaḥ ॥ 2.40.70 ॥
eṣa mārgo hi niradhitiryagyonau ca kāraṇam।
tiryagyonigatañcaiva kāraṇaṃ sa nirucyate ॥ 2.40.71 ॥
vividhā yātanā sthāne tiryagyonau ca ṣaḍvidhe।
kāraṇe viṣaye caiva pratighātastu sarvaśaḥ ॥ 2.40.72 ॥
anaiśvaryyantu tatsarvaṃ pratighātātmakaṃ smṛtam ।
ityeṣā tāmasī vṛttirbhūtādīnāṃ caturvidhā ॥ 2.40.73 ॥
sattvasthamātrakaṃ cittaṃ yathā sattvapradarśanāt।
tattvānāñca tathā tattvaṃ dṛṣṭvā vai tattvadarśanāt ॥ 2.40.74 ॥
sattvakṣetrajñanānātvametajjñānārthadarśanam।
nānātvadarśanaṃ jñānaṃ jñānādvai yogamucyate ॥ 2.40.75 ॥
tena baddhasya vai bandho mokṣo muktasya tena ca ।
saṃsāre vinivṛtte tu mukto liṅgena mucyate ॥ 2.40.76 ॥
niḥsambandho hyacaitanyaḥ svātmanyevāvatiṣṭhate।
svātmavyavasthitaścāpi virūpākhyena likhyate ॥ 2.40.77 ॥
ityetallakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ samāsājjñānamokṣayo।
sa cāpi trividhaḥ prokto mokṣo vai tattvadarśibhiḥ ॥ 2.40.78 ॥
pūrvaṃ viyogo jñānena dvitīyo rāgasaṃkṣayāt।
liṅgābhāvāttu kaivalyaṃ kaivatyāttu nirañjanam ॥ 2.40.79 ॥
nirañjanatvācchuddhastu tato netā na vidyate।
tṛṣṇākṣayāttṛtīyastu vyākhyātaṃ mokṣakāraṇam ॥ 2.40.80 ॥
nimittamapratīghāte iṣṭaśabdādilakṣaṇe।
aṣṭāvetāni rūpāṇi prākṛtāni yathākramam ॥ 2.40.81 ॥
kṣetrajñeṣvavasajyante guṇamātrātmakāni tu।
ata urddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi vairāgyaṃ doṣadarśanāt ॥ 2.40.82 ॥
divye ca mānuṣe caiva viṣaye pañcalakṣaṇe।
apradveṣo'nabhiṣvaṅgaḥ karttavyo doṣadarśanāt ॥ 2.40.83 ॥
tāpaprītiviṣādānāṃ kāryyantu parivarjanam।
evaṃ vairāgyamāsthāya śarīrī nirmamo bhavet ॥ 2.40.84 ॥
anityamaśivaṃ duḥkhamiti buddhyānucintya ca।
paripavkakaṣāyo hi kṛtsnāndoṣānprapaśyati।
tataḥ prayāṇakāle hi doṣairnaimittikaistathā ॥ 2.40.86 ॥
ūṣmā prakupitaḥ kāye tīvravāyusamīritaḥ।
sa śarīramupāśritya kṛtsnāndoṣānruṇaddhi vai ॥ 2.40.87 ॥
prāṇasthānāni bhindanhi chindanmarmāṇyatītya ca।
śaityātprakupito vāyurūrddhvantu kramate tataḥ ॥ 2.40.88 ॥
sa cāyaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ prāṇasthāneṣvavasthitaḥ।
samāsātsaṃvṛte jñāne saṃvṛteṣu ca karmmasu ॥ 2.40.89 ॥
sa jīvo'nabhyadhiṣṭānaḥ karmmabhiḥ svaiḥ purākṛtaiḥ।
aṣṭāṅgaprāṇavṛttīrvai sa vicyāvayate punaḥ ॥ 2.40.90 ॥
śarīraṃ prajahaṃso vai nirucchvāsastato bhavet।
evaṃ prāṇaiḥ parityakto mṛta ityabhidhīyate ॥ 2.40.91 ॥
yatheha loke khadyotaṃ nīyamānamitastataḥ ।
tṛṣṇākṣayastṛtīyastu vyākhyātaṃ mokṣalakṣaṇam।
śabdādye viṣaye doṣaviṣaye pañcalakṣaṇe ॥ 2.40.93 ॥
apradveṣo'nabhiṣvaṅgaḥ prītitāpavivarjanam ।
vairāgyakāraṇaṃ hyete prakṛtīnāṃ layasya ca ॥ 2.40.94 ॥
aṣṭau prakṛtayo jñeyāḥ pūrvoktā vai yathākramam।
avyaktādyastu vijñeyā bhūtāntāḥ prakṛterlayāḥ ॥ 2.40.95 ॥
varṇāśramācārayuktāḥ śiṣṭāḥ śāstrāvirodhinaḥ।
varṇāśramāṇāṃ dharmmo'yaṃ devasthāneṣu kāraṇam ॥ 2.40.96 ॥
brahmādīni piśācāntānyaṣṭau sthānāni devatā।
aiśvaryyamaṇimādyaṃ hi kāraṇaṃ hyaṣṭalakṣaṇam ॥ 2.40.97 ॥
nimittamapratīghāta iṣṭe śabdādilakṣaṇe।
aṣṭāvetāni rūpāṇi prākṛtāni yathākramam ॥ 2.40.98 ॥
kṣetrajñeṣvanusajyante gaṇamātrātmakāni tu।
prāvṛṭ‌kāle pṛthaktvena paśyantīha na cakṣuṣā ॥ 2.40.99 ॥
paśyantyevaṃvidhaṃ siddhā jīvaṃ divyena cakṣuṣā।
tiryyagūrddhvamadhastācca dhāvato'pi yathākramam।
jīvaprāṇāstathā liṅgaṃ kāraṇañca catuṣṭayam ।।. 40.101 ।।
paryyāyavācakaiḥ śabdairekārthaiḥ so'bhilikhyate।
vyaktāvyakte pramāṇo'yaṃ sa vai rūpaṃ tu kṛtsnaśaḥ ॥ 2.40.101 ॥
avyaktānta gṛhītaṃ ca kṣetrajñādhiṣṭitañca yat ।
evaṃ jñātvā śucirbhūttvā jñānādvai vipramucyate ॥ 2.40.102 ॥
naṣṭañcaiva yathā tattvaṃ tattvānāṃ tattvadarśanam।
yatheṣṭaṃ pariniryyāti bhinne dehe sunirvṛte ॥ 2.40.103 ॥
bhidyate karaṇañcāpi hyavyaktājñāninastataḥ।
mukto guṇaśarīreṇa prāṇādyena tu sarvaśaḥ ॥ 2.40.104 ॥
nānyaccharīramādatte dagdhe bīje yathāṅkuraḥ।
jñānāccaturddaśācchuddhaḥ prakṛtiṃ so'nuvarttate।
prakṛtiṃ satyamityāhu rvikāro'nṛtamucyate ॥ 2.40.106 ॥
tatsadbhāvo'nṛtaṃ jñeyaṃ sadbhāvaḥ satyamucyate।
anāmarūpakṣetrajñanāmarūpaṃ pracakṣate ॥ 2.40.107 ॥
yasmātkṣetraṃ vijānāti tasmātkṣetrajña ucyate।
kṣetrapratyayato yasmātkṣetrajñaḥ śubha ucyate ॥ 2.40.108 ॥
kṣetrajñaḥ smaryyate tasmātkṣetraṃ tajjñairvibhāṣyate।
kṣetratvapratyayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kṣetrajñaḥ pratyayī sadā ॥ 2.40.109 ॥
kṣayaṇāt karaṇāccaiva kṣatatrāṇāttathaiva ca।
bhojyatvādviṣayatvācca kṣetraṃ kṣetravido viduḥ ॥ 2.40.110 ॥
mahadādyaṃ viśeṣāntaṃ savairūpyaṃ vilakṣaṇam।
vikāralakṣaṇaṃ tadvai sākṣarakṣarameva ca ॥ 2.40.111 ॥
tameva ca vikārantu yasmādvai kṣarate punaḥ।
tasmācca kāraṇāccaiva kṣaramityabhidhīyate ॥ 2.40.112 ॥
sukhaduḥkhamohabhāvā bhojyamityabhidhīyate।
acetatvāddhi viṣayastaddhi dharmmavibhuḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.40.113 ॥
na kṣīyate na kṣarati vikāraprasṛtantu tat।
akṣaraṃ tena cāpyuktamakṣīṇatvāttathaiva ca ॥ 2.40.114 ॥
yasmātpuryyanuśete ca tasmātpuruṣa ucyate।
purapratyayiko yasmātpūruṣetyabhidhīyate ॥ 2.40.115 ॥
puruṣaṃ kathayasvātha kathantajjñairvibhāṣyate।
śuddho nirañjanābhāso jñānājñānavivarjitaḥ ॥ 2.40.116 ॥
asti nāstīti so'nyo vā baddho mukto gataḥ sthitaḥ।
nairhetikāntanirddeśyasūktastasminna vidyate ॥ 2.40.117 ॥
śuddhatvānna tu deśyo vai dṛṣṭatvātsamadarśanaḥ।
bhāvagrāhyamanumānyaṃ cintayanna pramuhyate ॥ 2.40.118 ॥
yadā paśyati jñātāraṃ śāntārthaṃ darśanātmakam।
dṛśyādṛśyeṣu nirddeśyaṃ tadā taduddharaṃ varam ॥ 2.40.119 ॥
vijñātā na ca dṛśyeta pṛthaktveneha sarvvaśaḥ ॥ 2.40.121 ॥
svenātmānaṃ tamātmānaṃ kāraṇātmā niyacchati।
prakṛtau kāraṇe caiva svātmanyevopatiṣṭhati ॥ 2.40.122 ॥
asti nāstīti so'nyo vā ihāmutreti vā punaḥ।
ekatvaṃ vā pṛthaktvaṃ vā kṣetrajñapuruṣeti vā ॥ 2.40.123 ॥
ātmavān sa nirātmā vā cetano'cetano'pi vā।
karttā vā so'pyakarttā vā bhoktā vā bhojyameva vā ॥ 2.40.124 ॥
yajjñātvā na nivarttante kṣetrajñe tu nirañjane।
avācyaṃ tadanākhyānādagrāhyatvādahetuni ॥ 2.40.125 ॥
apratarkyamacintyatvādavāpyatvācca sarvaśaḥ।
kṣetrejñe nirguṇe śuddhe śānte kṣīṇe nirañjane।
vyape(ye)tasukhaduḥkhe ca niruddhe śāntimāgate ॥ 2.40.127 ॥
nirātmake punastasminvācyāvācyo na vidyate।
etau saṃhāravistārau vyaktāvyaktau tataḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.40.128 ॥
sṛjate grasate caiva grastaḥ paryavatiṣṭhate।
kṣetrajñādhiṣṭitaṃ sarvaṃ punaḥ sarvaṃ pravarttate ॥ 2.40.129 ॥
adhiṣṭānapravṛttena tasya te buddhipūrvakam।
sādharmyavaidharmyakṛtasaṃyogo vidhitastayoḥ।
anādimān sa saṃyogo mahāpuruṣajaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.40.130 ॥
yāvacca sargapratisargakālastāvacca tiṣṭhati susannirudhya।
pūrvaṃ hitavye tadabuddhipūrvaṃ pravarttate tatpuruṣārthameva ॥ 2.40.131 ॥
eṣā nisargapratisargapūrvaṃ pradhānikī ceśvarakāritā ca।
anādyanantā hyabhimānapūrvakaṃ vitrāsayantī jagadabhyupaiti ॥ 2.40.132 ॥
ityeṣa prākṛtaḥ sargastṛtīyo hetulakṣaṇaḥ।
ukto hyasmiṃstadātyantaṃ kavibhistatpramucyate ॥ 2.40.133 ॥
ityeṣa pratisargovastrividhaḥ kīrttito mayā।।
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca bhūyaḥ kiṃ varttayāmyaham ॥ 2.40.134 ॥
sūta sumahadākhyānaṃ bhavatā parikīrtitam।
prajānāṃ manubhiḥ sārddhaṃ devānāmṛṣibhiḥ saha ॥ 2.41.1 ॥
pitṛgandharvabhūtānāṃ piśācoragarakṣasām।
daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca yakṣāṇāmeva pakṣiṇām ॥ 2.41.2 ॥
atyadbhutāni karmmāṇi vidhimāndharmmaniścayaḥ।
vicitrāśca kathāyogā janma cāgryamanuttamam ॥ 2.41.3 ॥
tatkathyamānamasmākaṃ bhavatā ślakṣṇayā girā।
manaḥkarmasukhaṃ saute prīṇātyābhūtasambhavam ॥ 2.41.4 ॥
evamārādhya te sūtaṃ satkṛtya ca maharṣayaḥ ।
papracchuḥ satriṇaḥ sarve punaḥ sargapravarttanam ॥ 2.41.5 ॥
kathaṃ sūta mahāprājña punaṃ sargaḥ prapatsyate।
bandheṣu sampralīneṣu guṇasāmye tamomaye ॥ 2.41.6 ॥
vikāreṣvavisṛṣṭoṣu hyavyakte cātmani sthite।
apravṛttau brahmaṇastu mahāsāyujyagaistadā ।
kathaṃ prapatsyate sargastannaḥ prabrūhi pṛcchatām ॥ 2.41.7 ॥
evamuktastataḥ sūtastadāsau lomaharṣaṇaḥ ।
vyākhyātumupacakrāma punaḥ sargapravarttanam ॥ 2.41.8 ॥
ahaṃ vau varttayiṣyāmi yathā sargaḥ prapatsyate।
pūrvavatsa tu vijñeyaḥ samāsāttaṃ nibodhata ॥ 2.41.9 ॥
dṛṣṭaṃ caivānumeyañca tarkaṃ vakṣyāmi yuktitaḥ।
tasmādvāco nivarttante hyaprāpya manasā saha ॥ 2.41.10 ॥
avyaktavat parokṣatvādghrahaṇaṃ taddurāsadam।
vikāraiḥ pratisaṃdṛṣṭe guṇasāmye nivarttate ॥ 2.41.11 ॥
pradhānaṃ puruṣāṇāñca sādharmmyeṇaiva tiṣṭhati।
dharmmādharmmau pralīyete avyaktau prāṇināṃ sadā ॥ 2.41.12 ॥
sattvamātrātmako dharmmo guṇasattve pratiṣṭitaḥ।
tamomātrātmako'dharmmo guṇe tamasi tiṣṭhati ॥ 2.41.13 ॥
avibhāgavatāvetau guṇasāmyasthitāvubhau।
sarvakāryye buddhipūrvaṃ pradhānasya prapatsyate ॥ 2.41.14 ॥
abuddhipūrvaṃ kṣetrajña adhiṣṭāsyati tān guṇān।
evaṃ tānabhimānena prapatsyeta purastadā ॥ 2.41.15 ॥
yadā pravarttitavyantu kṣetrakṣetrajñayordvayoḥ।
bhojyabhoktṛtvasambandhaṃ prapatsyete yutāvubhau ॥ 2.41.16 ॥
tasmāccharaṇamavyaktaṃ sāmye sthitvā guṇātmakān।
kṣetrajñādhiṣṭitaṃ tacca vaiṣamyaṃ bhajate tu tat ॥ 2.41.17 ॥
tataḥ prapatsyate vyaktaṃ kṣetrakṣetrajñayordvayoḥ।
kṣetrajñādhiṣṭitaṃ sattvaṃ vikāraṃ janayiṣyati ॥ 2.41.18 ॥
mahadādyaṃ viśeṣāntaṃ caturviṃśaguṇātmakam।
kṣetrajñasya pradhānasya puruṣasya prapatsyate ॥ 2.41.19 ॥
ādi devaḥ pradhānasyānugrahāya pravakṣyate ॥ 2.41.21 ॥
anādyau svayamutpannāvubhau sūkṣmau tu tau smṛtau ।
anādisaṃyogayutau sarvakṣetrajñameva ca ॥ 2.41.22 ॥
abuddhi pūrvakaṃ yuktau maśakau tu varau tadā।
apratyayamanādyaṃ ca sthitāvudakamapsyaśaḥ ॥ 2.41.23 ॥
pravṛtte pūrvataḥ pūrvaṃ punaḥ sarge prapatsyate।
ajñāguṇaiḥ pravarttante rajaḥsattvatamātmakam ॥ 2.41.24 ॥
pravṛttikāle rajasābhipannamahattvabhūtādiviśeṣyatāñca।
viśeṣatāṃ cendriyatāñca yānti guṇāvasāne patibhirmanuṣyāḥ ॥ 2.41.25 ॥
satyābhidhyāyinastasya dhyāyinaḥ sannimittakam।
rajaḥsattvatamā vyaktā vidharmmāṇaḥ parasparam ॥ 2.41.26 ॥
ādyante saṃprapatsyante kṣetratajjñāstu sarvaśaḥ।
saṃsiddhakāryyakaraṇā utpadyante'bhimāninaḥ ॥ 2.41.27 ॥
sarve satvāḥ prapadyante hyavyaktātpūrvameva ca।
prasūte yā ca suvahāḥ sādhikāścāpyasādhikā ॥ 2.41.28 ॥
saṃsarantastu te sarve stānaprakaraṇaiḥ saha।
kāryyāṇi pratipatsyante utpadyante punaḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.41.29 ॥
guṇamātrātmakāścaiva dharmmādharmmau parasparam।
ārapsantīha cānyonyaṃ vareṇānugraheṇa ca ॥ 2.41.30 ॥
sarve tulyāḥ prasṛṣṭārthaṃ sarggadau yānti vikriyām।
guṇāstatpratidhāvante tasmāttattasya rocate ॥ 2.41.31 ॥
guṇāste yāni sarvāṇi prāk dṛṣṭeḥ pratipedire।
tānyeva pratipadyante sṛṣṭamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ॥ 2.41.32 ॥
hiṃsrāhiṃsre mṛdukrūre dharmmādharmmāvṛtānṛte।
tadbhāvitāḥ prapadyante tasmāttattasya rocate ॥ 2.41.33 ॥
mahābhūteṣu nānātvamindriyārtheṣu mūrttiṣu।
viprayogāśca bhūtānāṃ yuṇobhyaḥ saṃpravarttate ॥ 2.41.34 ॥
ityeṣa vo mayā khyātaḥ punaḥ sargaḥ samāsataḥ।
samāsādeva vakṣyāmi brahmaṇo'tha samudbhavam ॥ 2.41.35 ॥
avyaktātkāraṇāttasmānnityātsadasadātmakāt।
pradhāna puruṣābhyāntu jāyate ca maheśvaraḥ ॥ 2.41.36 ॥
sa punaḥ sambhāvayitā jāyate brahmasaṃjñitaḥ।
sṛjate sa punarlokānabhimānaguṇātmakān ॥ 2.41.37 ॥
ahaṅkārastu mahatastasmādbhūtāni cātmanaḥ।
yugapat sampravarttante bhūtānyevendriyāṇi ca।
bhūtabhedāśca bhūtebhya iti sargaḥ pravarttate ॥ 2.41.38 ॥
vistarāvayavasteṣāṃ yathāprajñaṃ yathāśrutam।
kīrttitaṃ vo yathā pūrvaṃ tathaivābhyupadhāryyatām ॥ 2.41.39 ॥
etacchrutvā naimiṣeyāstadānīṃ lokotpattiṃ saṃsthitiṃ ca vyayañca।
tasmin satre'vabhṛthaṃ prāpya śuddhāḥ puṇyaṃ lokamṛṣayaḥ prāpnuvanti ॥ 2.41.40 ॥
yathā yūyaṃ vidhivaddevatādīniṣṭvā caivāvabhṛthaṃ prāpya śuddhāḥ।
tyaktvā dehānāyuṣo'nte kṛtārthānpuṇyāँllokānprāpya yatheṣṭaṃ cariṣyatha ॥ 2.41.41 ॥
ete te naimiṣeyā vai iṣṭvā sṛṣṭvā ca vai tadā।
jagmuścāvabhṛdhasnātāḥ svargaṃ sarve tu satriṇaḥ ॥ 2.41.42 ॥
viprāstathā yūyamapi ceṣṭvā bahuvidhairmakhaiḥ ।
āyuṣo'nte tataḥ svargaṃ gantāraḥ stha dvijottamāḥ ॥ 2.41.43 ॥
prakriyā prathame pāde kathāvastuparigrahaḥ।
anuṣaṅga upodvāta upasaṃhāra eva ca ॥ 2.41.44 ॥
evametaccatuṣpādaṃ purāṇaṃ lokasammatam।
uvāca bhagavān sākṣādvāyurlokahite rataḥ ॥ 2.41.45 ॥
naimiṣe satramāsādya munibhyo munisattamāḥ ।
tatprasādādasaṃdigdhaṃ bhūtotpattilayāni ca ॥ 2.41.46 ॥
prādhānikīmimāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ tathaiveśvarakāritām।
samyagviditvā medhāvī na mohamadhigacchati ॥ 2.41.47 ॥
idaṃ yo brāhmaṇo vidvānitihāsaṃ purātanam।
śrṛṇuyācchrāvayedvāpi tathādhyāpayate'pi ca ॥ 2.41.48 ॥
sthāneṣu sa mahendrasya modate śāśvatīḥ samāḥ।
brahmasāyujyago bhūtvā brahmaṇā saha mokṣyate ॥ 2.41.49 ॥
teṣāṃ kīrttimatāṃ kīrttiṃ prajeśānāṃ mahātmanām।
prathayanpṛthivīśānāṃ brahmabhūyāya gacchati ॥ 2.41.50 ॥
dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ vedaiśca sammatam।
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanenoktaṃ purāṇaṃ brahmavādinā ॥ 2.41.51 ॥
manvantareśvarāṇāṃ ca yaḥ kīrtiṃ prathayedimām।
devatānāmṛṣīṇāñca bhūridraviṇatejasām।
sa sarvairmucyate pāpaiḥ puṇyañca mahadāpnuyāt ॥ 2.41.52 ॥
yaścedaṃ śrāvayedvidvānsadā parvaṇi parvaṇi।
dhūtapāpmā jitasvargo brahmabhūyāya kalpate ॥ 2.41.53 ॥
yaścedaṃ śrāvayecchrāddhe brāhmaṇānpādamantataḥ।
akṣayaṃ sārvakāmīyaṃ pitṝṃstaccopatiṣṭhati ॥ 2.41.54 ॥
yasmātpurā hyanantīdaṃ purāṇaṃ tena cocyate।
niruktamasya yo veda sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ॥ 2.41.55 ॥
tathaiva triṣu varṇeṣu ye manuṣyāḥ pradhānataḥ।
itihāsamimaṃ śrutvā dharmāya vidadhe matim ॥ 2.41.56 ॥
yāvantyasya śarīreṣu romakūpāṇi sarvaśaḥ।
tāvatkoṭi sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ divi modate।
brahmasāyujyago bhūtvā daivataiḥ saha modate ॥ 2.41.57 ॥
sarvvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ pavitrañca yaśasvi ca।
brahmā dadau śāstramidaṃ purāṇaṃ mātariśvane ॥ 2.41.58 ॥
tasmāccośanasā prāptaṃ tasmāccāpi bṛhaspatiḥ।
bṛhaspatistu prevāca savitre tadanantaram ॥ 2.41.59 ॥
savitā mṛtyave prāha mṛtyuścendrāya vai punaḥ।
indraścāpi vasiṣṭāya so'pi sārasvatāya ca ॥ 2.41.60 ॥
sārasvatastridhāmne ca tridhāmā ca śaradvate।
śaradvatastriviṣṭāya so'ntarikṣāya dattavān ॥ 2.41.61 ॥
varṣiṇe cāntarikṣo vai so'pi trayyāruṇāya ca।
trayyāruṇo dhanañjaye sa ca prādātkṛtañjaye ॥ 2.41.62 ॥
kṛta ñjayāttṛṇañjayo bharadvājāya so'pyatha।
gautamāya bharadvājaḥ so'pi niryyantare punaḥ ॥ 2.41.63 ॥
niryantarastu provāca tathā vājaśravāya ca।
sa dadau somaśūṣmāya sa dadau tṛṇabindave ॥ 2.41.64 ॥
tṛṇabindustu dakṣāya dakṣaḥ provāca śaktaye।
śakteḥ parāśaraścāpi garbhasthaḥ śrutavānidam ॥ 2.41.65 ॥
parāśarājjātukarṇastasmāddvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ।
dvaipāyanātpunaścāpi mayā prāptaṃ dvijottamāḥ ॥ 2.41.66 ॥
mayā vai tatpunaḥ proktaṃ putrāyāmitabuddhaye।
ityeva vācā brahmādiguruṇā samudāhṛtā ॥ 2.41.67 ॥
namaskāryyaśca guravaḥ prayatnena manīṣibhiḥ।
dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvārthasādhakam ॥ 2.41.68 ॥
pāpaghnaṃ niyamenedaṃ śrotavyaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ sadā।
nāśucau nāpi pāpāya nāpyasaṃvatsaroṣite ॥ 2.41.69 ॥
nāśraddadhānāviduṣe nāputrāya kathañcana।
nāhitāya pradātavyaṃ pavitramidamuttamam ॥ 2.41.70 ॥
avyaktaṃ vai yasya yoniṃ vadanti vyaktaṃ dehaṃ kālamantargatañca ।
vahniṃ vakraṃ candra sūryyau ca netre diśaḥ śrotre ghrāṇamāhuśca vāyum ॥ 2.41.71 ॥
vāyo vedāṃścāntarikṣaṃ śarīraṃ kṣitiṃ pādau tārakā romakūpān ।
taṃ devadevaṃ jananaṃ janānāṃ sarvveṣu lokeṣu pratiṣṭitañca।
varaṃ varāṇāṃ varadaṃ maheśvaraṃ brahmāṇamādiṃ prayato namasye ॥ 2.41.73 ॥
akṣaraṃ paramaṃ brahma paramātmā paraṃ padam।
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi gayāmāhātmyamuttamam।
yojanānāṃ sapādañca śataṃ tasyocchrayaḥ smṛtaḥ ॥ 2.44.4 ॥
            sanatkumāra uvāca।।
yadituṣṭāḥ stha me devā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ।
āsīddharmmo mahātejāḥ sarvvavijñānapāragaḥ।
brahmaṇo mānasaḥ putro marīcirnāma viśrutaḥ ।
etasminneva kāle tu prabuddho bhagavānajaḥ।
akṣayantu bhavecchrāddhaṃ japahomatapāṃsi ca।
bharatasyāśrame puṇye nityaṃ puṇyatamairvṛtam।
mataṅgasya padaṃ tatra dṛśyate sarvamānuṣaiḥ ॥ 2.46.25 ॥
sthāpitaṃ dharmasarvasvaṃ lokasyāsya nidarśanāt।
bharatasyāśrame puṇye nityaṃ puṇyatamairvṛtam।
mataṅgasya padaṃ tatra dṛśyate sarvamānuṣaiḥ ॥ 2.46.35 ॥
gayāyāṃ cākṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ japahomatapāṃsi ca।
           sanatkumāra uvāca।।
            sanatkumāra uvāca।।
           ।।sanatkumāra uvāca।।
pitā pitāmaha ścaiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ।
mātā pitāmahī caiva tathaiva prapitāmahī ॥ 2.48.23 ॥
asipatravane ghore kumbhīpākeṣu ye gatāḥ।
atra snāto divaṃ yāti svaśarīreṇa mānavaḥ ॥ 2.49.6 ॥
madhye kanakhalaṃ tīrthaṃ triṣulokeṣu viśrutam।
ātmānaṃ tārayetsadyo daśa pūrvāndaśāparān ॥ 2.49.23 ॥
gayāyāṃ dharmmapṛṣṭe ca sarasi brahmaṇasta thā ॥ 2.49.97 ॥
pitṝnpitāmahāṃścaiva tathaiva prapitāmahān ॥ 2.50.16 ॥
tatra snāto divaṃ yāti svaśarīreṇa mānavaḥ ॥ 2.50.52 ॥
tatpaṅgajavanaṃ puṇyaṃ puṇyakṛdbhirniṣevitam ॥ 2.50.53 ॥
